nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। āsūryakiraṇākrāntājjagato janagocarāt । puṇyadhāmni kurukṣetre samāyāteṣu rājasu ।।
ekībhūteṣu sainyeṣu kurupāṇḍavasaṃgare । vṛddhabālāvaśeṣāsu dikṣu yātāsu śūnyatām ।। dāruṇeṣu nimitteṣu prādurbhūteṣu sarvataḥ । mitho dṛṣṭipathaṃ yāte patākābhirbaladvaye ।।
sotsāhaṃ dadhmatuḥ śaṅkhaṃ hṛṣīkeśadhanaṃjayau । yayorgambhīraghoṣeṇa bhuvanāni cakampire ।। viṣamastho na hantavyo na ca senāvinirgataḥ । na nivṛtte raṇe ceti maryādāṃ cakrire nṛpāḥ ।।
atrāntare samabhyetya pārāśaryo munīśvaraḥ । viṣaṇṇaṃ mandiragataṃ dhṛtarāṣṭramabhāṣata ।। vīrāṇāṃ bhūmipālānāmaśeṣe asminsamāgame । kṣattrasya saṃkṣayo rājanviṣamaḥ samupasthitaḥ ।।
divyaṃ gṛhāma nayanaṃ svayaṃ yuddhaṃ vilokaya । ityukte muninā rājā jagādākulitāśayaḥ ।। bhagavānbandhunidhanaṃ nāhaṃ draṣṭuṃ samutsahe । bhāvyasyāvaśyabhāvitvānna ca vārayituṃ kṣamaḥ ।।
ityuktavati bhūpāle saṃjayaṃ varado muniḥ । vidhāya divyanayanaṃ punaḥ kṣitipamabhyadhāt ।। ayaṃ te nikhilaṃ yuddhaṃ kathayiṣyati saṃjayaḥ । nāsya kiṃcidavijñātaṃ divyadṛṣṭerbhaviṣyati ।।
kṛtānto jṛmbhate rājñāṃ dhṛtarāṣṭra tavānayāt । dṛśyante durnimittāni kṣayakarṇejapāni yat ।। saureṇa pīḍitā gāḍhaṃ rohiṇī jvalitā diśaḥ । viparītā prasūtiśca kabandhenāvṛto raviḥ ।।
kravyādairāvṛtaṃ vyoma meghā varṣanti śoṇitam । kimanyadrājamahiṣī hā mahī na bhaviṣyati ।। pradakṣiṇaśikho vahniḥ prasādo manasastathā । lakṣavyaktaṃ jayasyaitaddharmo yatrāsti tatra saḥ ।।
śatānyekena jīyante naiko jeyaḥ śatairapi । taralā hyasidhāreyaṃ niścayo nātra gaṇyate ।। ityuktvāntarhite kṣipraṃ munīndre saṃjayaṃ nṛpaḥ । papraccha dvīpasaṃsthānaṃ sa ca pṛṣṭho abhyabhāṣata ।।
rājanviśāle śītāṃśormaṇḍale darpaṇākṛtau । sphāraṃ sudarśanaṃ dvīpaṃ nikhilaṃ pratibimbitam ।। ekataḥ pippalācchāyamanyataḥ śaśakākṛti । dvīpe asminmaṇlākāre lavaṇāmbudhiveṣṭite ।
karṇikevāmbuje prāṃśurmadhye kanakaparvataḥ ।। śayānā bhṛdharāścānye pārśvayostasya bhūbhṛtaḥ । sthitā himālayamukhāḥ spṛśantaḥ pūrvapaścimam ।। himavānhemakūṭaśca niṣadaśceti dakṣiṇe ।
uttare śṛṅgavānnīlaḥ śvetaśceti mahābalāḥ ।। eṣāṃ ratnavicatrāṇāmantare varṣabhūmayaḥ । karmabhūrbhārataṃ varṣamanyāśca phalabhūmayaḥ ।। harivarṣamukheṣveva prajāsargaḥ smaropamaḥ ।
sthānaṃ sukṛtināṃ yatra vikhyātā gaṇḍikā iti ।। jambūkhaṇḍaṃ tathā meroradho yatphalavisrutā । jātā jambūnadī śubhrā jāmbunadavidhāyinī ।। uttarāḥ kuravaḥ pītvā tāmeva gatamṛtyavaḥ ।
divaspṛśastarestasya nāmnedaṃ dvīpamucyate ।। ityuktvā saṃjayo gatvā kurukṣetre rāṇāṅgaṇe । sametya dhṛtarāṣṭrāya śaśaṃya svabhaṭakṣayam ।। jambūkhaṇḍanirmāṇam ।।
śṛṇu rājanhatānantasāmantaḥ śantanoḥ sutaḥ । vidadhe pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ yathā vijayasaṃśayam ।। vajrasūcīmukhākhyābhyāṃ pyūhābhyāṃ rājakuñjaraiḥ mitho vyūḍheṣvanīkeṣu gāṅgeyenārjunena ca ।। tasminkṣattrakṣayakṣetre sarvakṣattrasamāgame ।
duryodhane atisaṃrabdhe pṛthusainyābhimānini ।। gāṅgeyaśaṅkhanādena samudbhūte balārṇave । śaṅkhaśabdena pārthānāṃ pāñcajanyānuyāyinā ।। pūrite bhuvanābhoge dikṣu visphūrjitāsviva ।
sarvasenāśrayaḥ śrīmānvijayo acyutasārathiḥ ।। dadarśa kurusenāsu gurusaṃbandhibāndhavān । nijapratāpadahane sa teṣāṃ śalabhāyitam । matvā jagāda govindaṃ viṣaṇṇaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ ।।
aho vata vimūḍhānāṃ rājyaleśe sukhāya naḥ । kṛṣṇa bandhuvadhe apyasminsasaṃrambho ayamudyamaḥ ।। avatīrya sadācārastutikramyakulasthitim । kathaṃ guruvadhaprāpyāṃ bhajedasmadvidhaṛ śriyam ।।
ityuktvā sāsrunayano bībhatsuḥ kṛpayā rathe । karādutsṛjya gāṇḍīvaṃ niṣasāda viṣādavān ।। śrīmadbhagavadgītāsu prathamo adhyāyaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā śokavivaśaṃ jagāda madhusūdanaḥ ।
akāṇḍe dhairyasārasya keyaṃ kātaratā tava ।। tarasvī kṣatriyo mānī prāṇairapi yaśaḥkrayī । nijāṃ kulasthitiṃ pārtha na dharmyāṃ hātumarhasi ।। saṃyuktaṃ vā viyuktaṃ vā nityaṃ dehena dehinam ।
viśvamāyāprapañce asmanko anuśocati tattvadhīḥ ।। sukhādyavasthā dehasya kāle kāle yathāvidhāḥ । dehino asya tathā dehāḥ sataḥ sattāvivarjitāḥ ।। viṣayendriyasaṃyogānkṣayino harṣaśokadān ।
sahate yo viluptātmā nirvāṇaṃ tasya śāśvatam ।। ajasya purāṇasya dehino asyāvināśinaḥ । jīrṇaparṇaparāvṛttitulyeyaṃ dehakalpanā ।। ādimadhyāvasāneṣu vyaktāvyaktasvarūpiṇaḥ ।
sata evāsya satataṃ na virāmaḥ śarīriṇaḥ ।। ayaśasyamatastyaktvā saṃkocaṃ vipulāśayaḥ । jayājayau samaṃ matvā viśa svargonmukho raṇam ।। āsthāya yaugikīṃ buddhiṃ karmabandhavivarjitaḥ ।
śuṣkavedakriyāhīnaṃ guṇātītaṃ padaṃ bhuja ।। sarvavedeṣu viduṣāmetadeva prayojanam । jalāśayeṣu pūrṇeṣu yathā salilahāriṇām ।। niḥsaṅgaḥ phalasaṃnyāsī kuru karma sadoditaḥ ।
parameśvaramevāhi vāṇijyaṃ hi phalārthinām ।। yadā te vītamohasya buddhiryāsyati nirvṛtim । kṛtī bhaviṣyasi tadā śruteṣvartheṣvanādaraḥ ।। iti bruvāṇaḥ pārthena sthitaprajñasya lakṣaṇam ।
pṛṣṭaḥ samādhisaktasya bhagavānityabhāṣata ।। īśvarādaparo nāhamiti svānandanirbharaḥ । nirastākhilasaṃkalpaḥ sthitaprajño abhidhīyate ।। āste kūrma ivāṅgāni kāmānsaṃvṛtyayaḥ śrayam ।
viṣayādhyānavirahātsthitadhīrna sa naśyati ।। kaṣṭaistapobhirviṣayāḥ śuṣyantyeva rasaṃ vinā । anādaraviraktānāṃ sadāpyadhyātmadarśinām ।। nidrārlubhūtakāleṣu prabuddhistimireṣu yaḥ ।
sa mahābdhirivākṣobhyaḥ sthitiṃ brāhmīṃ prapadyate ।। śrīgītāsu dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ ।। śrutvaitadarjunaḥ kṛṣṇamuvācākulitāśayaḥ । kathamevaṃ vadanghore samare asminyunakṣi mām ।।
karmaṇaḥ śreyasī buddhirityuktvāpi svayaṃ vibho । karma durmatiyogyaṃ māṃ praśaṃsasi vimohayan ।। śreyo vadetyuktavati śvetāśve keśavo abravīt । niṣṭhā prajñānakarmabhyāṃ mayoktā sāṃkhyayogayoḥ ।।
anārambhānna ca tyāgātkarmaṇo mucyate janaḥ । śrotrādayo balādasya dhāvantyeva svakarmasu ।। smaranti manasā sarvaṃ ruddhakarmendriyā api । mithyācārānatvasaktāḥ karmiṇo niyatāntarāḥ ।।
śreyo hyakarmaṇaḥ karma na yajñaḥ karmaṇā vinā । yajñaśeṣāśinaḥ puṇyadrumāḥ kevalabhoginaḥ ।। karmasthito api niḥsaṃjño yadā prāpnoti mānavaḥ । ātmārāmadaśāstuṣṭhastadā kāryānnivartate ।।
karmaṇaiva gatāḥ siddhiṃ janakapramukhāḥ purā । tanmā kāryānnivartasva lokastvāmanuvartatām ।। mamāpi kṛtakṛtyasya karmedaṃ sthitirakṣiṇaḥ । vinasyatyanyathā loko matpramāṇaviśṛṅkhalaḥ ।।
pātraṃ sarvajñayogyeṣu nādareṣu pṛthagjanaḥ । tasmānnotsāhayedetānpaṅgūnvegagatāniva ।। yudhyasva sarvakarmāṇi mayi saṃnyasya nirvṛtaḥ । taranti hi tamo ghoraṃ nityaṃ manmatavartinaḥ ।।
prakṛterucitaṃ sarvaṃ svadharmanirataḥ kuru । rāgadveṣau parityajya priyāpriyasamudbhavau ।। śrutvaitadarjuno avādītpreritaḥ kena pātakam । caratyanīśvaraḥ prāṇī balādiva vaśīkṛtaḥ ।।
iti pṛṣṭo hṛṣīkeśo jagāda jagatāṃ patiḥ । rajoguṇasamutthena harṣaśokādidāyinā ।। lokasaṃhāraśīlena kāmena krodhabandhunā । ahaṃkāreṇa balinā ghoreṇānena vairiṇā ।।
śevālenaiva salilaṃ rajasevāmalaṃ nabhaḥ । āvṛto malinonātmā meghenaivodito raviḥ ।। manobuddhisamāyuktaṃ sthānamindriyapañjaram । yasya taṃ duḥsahaṃ śatruṃ kāmarūpa vināśaya ।।
śrīgītāsu tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ ।। sūryeṇāptaḥ purā matto yogo ayaṃ manunā tataḥ । ya eva kālenotsannastubhyamadya mayoditaḥ ।। anekajanmasākṣī tvaṃ bhaktaḥ sahacaro api me ।
na tatsmṛtipathaṃ yātaṃ kiṃtu te prāktanaṃ vapuḥ ।। ahaṃ tu nityadharamasya sthitaye guptaye satām । yuge yuge bhavāmyeṣa vināśāya dṛrātmanām ।। akṛtaṃ dharmakartāraṃ karmaitannāvṛṇoti mām ।
tvamapyasakto niṣkāmaḥ kuru karma kulocitam ।। durjñeyaḥ pravibhāgastu karmākarmavikarmaṇām । svocitaṃ phalahīnaṃ ca viruddhaṃ ceti bhedataḥ ।। karmaṇaḥ phalasaṃnyāsādyo anupaśyatyakarmatām ।
jānātyakarmaṇaḥ pāpātkarma yaśca sa buddhimān ।। jñānāgninā dagdhakarmā nityānando nirāśrayaḥ । nirāśīrnirahaṃkāro yajvā brahmaṇi līyate ।। brahmārpaṇena brahmagnau hutvā brahmamayaṃ haviḥ ।
prāṇayajñarato yāti brahma brahmasamādhinā ।। saṃyamāgnāvindriyāṇi viṣayānindriyānale । tatkarmāṇyātmayogāgnau hutvā yānti parāṃ gatim ।। ye api dravyatapoyogasvādhyāyajñānayājinaḥ ।
prāṇāpānādiha viṣo dhṛtvā nāḍīṣu dhāraṇam ।। samarpayanti nikhilaṃ jñānaṃ vigatakalmaṣāḥ । te prayānti paraṃ dhāma yajñaśiṣṭāmṛtāśinaḥ ।। tadvidhāḥ praṇipātena sevitā jñāninastvayā ।
ayatnāttvāṃ vidhāsyanti svātmanyakhiladarśinam ।। jñānāgninā dagdhapāpaḥ pavitreṇa bhaviṣyasi । kālena śraddadhānānāṃ svayaṃ jñānaṃ prasīdati ।। naśyanti saṃśayajuṣo mūḍhā na tvastasaṃśayāḥ ।
jñāninaḥ saṃśayaṃ tvasmātsthitvottiṣṭha vibhūtaye ।। śrīgītāsu caturtho adhyāyaḥ ।। niśamya tatpunaḥ pārthaḥ papraccha madhusūdanam । saṃnyāsakarmayogābhyāṃ śreyo brūhi janārdana ।।
iti pṛṣṭo avadacchaurirubhāvetau vimuktaye । karmayogastu saṃnyāsādviśiṣṭa iti me matiḥ ।। śṛṇvanto api vadanto api spṛśanto api svakarmaṇi । saktā api na sajjanti paṅke ravikarā iva ।।
tadeva vihitaṃ kiṃcitpuṃsāṃ sukṛtaduṣkṛtam । ajñānapihite jñāne kiṃ tveṣā karmavāsanā ।। jñānenotsāritā jñānāḥ parāṃ niṣṭhāmupāgatāḥ । brāhmaṇe vā śvapāke vā vibudhāḥ samadṛṣṭayaḥ ।।
bāhye sukhe viraktānāṃ duḥkhajanmani naśvare । antaḥsukhārāmatayā paraṃ jyotiḥ prasīdati ।। bahiḥ sparśānsamutsṛjya bhrūmadhyanihitekṣaṇaḥ । nāsāntare samau dhṛtvā prāṇāpānau vimuktaye ।।
kāmarāgamadadveṣabhayakrodhavivarjitaḥ । ahantā jñānatamasāṃ śāntiṃ vindatyamatsaraḥ ।। śrīgītāsu pañcamo adhyāyaḥ ।। kriyāvānaphalākāṅkṣī nijaṃ karma karoti yaḥ ।
ārurukṣudaśātīto yogārūḍho vimatsaraḥ ।। kūṭastho jñānatṛptaśca paśyatyātmānamātmanā । samāsanaḥ samākāro nistaraṅga ivodadhiḥ ।। ghrāṇāgradarśī śāntātmā māmupaiti samādhinā ।
yuktāhārādiceṣṭasya nityaṃ niṣkampacetasaḥ ।। ātmalābho bhavatyeva tyaktakāmasya yoginaḥ । manaḥ saṃyamya paśyanti sravatyetadyato yataḥ ।। ātmānaṃ māṃ ca sarvatra mamātmani tathākhilam ।
manasaścañcalasyāsya vairāgyeṇaiva saṃyamaḥ ।। tathābhyāsena balinā vātasyeva pramāthinaḥ । etadākarṇya kaunteyaḥ punaḥ papraccha keśavam ।। lolatvānmanaso deva yogādbhraṣṭasya kā gatiḥ ।
arjuneneti bhagavānpunaḥ pṛṣṭo abhyabhāṣata ।। yogabhraṣṭo api puruṣaḥ śubhakṛttu bhaviṣyati । ciraṃ bhuktvā sukhaṃ divyaṃ sa kalyāṇapuraḥ saraḥ ।। bhogināṃ yogināṃ vāpi saṃbhūto mahatāṃ kule ।
pūrvābhyastaṃ punardhīmāñjanmabhiḥ pratipadyate । tapo jñānādhikaṃ yogaṃ tasmādyogī bhavārjuna ।। śrīgītāsu ṣaṣṭho adhyāyaḥ ।। mayi nyastamanā nityaṃ bhaktyā māṃ vetti mānava ।
aṣṭamūrtirahaṃ sarvaṃ jīvabhūtaścarācare ।। utpattisthitisaṃhārakāraṇaṃ māṃ vidurbudhāḥ । sarve matprāṇitā bhāvā mayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। devīṃ māyāṃ dadhānaṃ māṃ na jānāti vimohitaḥ ।
ye tu jānanti māṃ māyāṃ bhavanti kṛtinaḥ sadā ।। arthī jijñāsurārto vā jñānī vā māṃ prapadyate । priyaḥ priyasya satataṃ jñāninastvasmi gocare ।। ananyadevatābhaktāḥ śraddhāvanto visaṃśayāḥ ।
vāsudevaḥ sarvamiti yajante māṃ mumukṣavaḥ ।। te brahmādhyātmakarmākhyaṃ sādhibhūtaṃ vidanti mām । sādhidaivādhiyajñaṃ ca dehavyuparameṣvapi ।। śrīgītāsu saptame adhyāyaḥ ।।
acyutenetyabhihite śakrasūnurabhāṣata । kimetadbrahma bhagavannadhiyajñaḥ kimucyate ।। iti pṛṣṭo hṛṣīkeśo babhāṣe śvetavāhanam । anaśvaraṃ parabrahma bhāvo adhyātmā tathātmanaḥ ।।
niḥsaṅgo bhavakṛtkarma naśvareṣvadhibhūtatā । adhidaivo ahamevātra hyadhiyajño apyahaṃ vibhuḥ ।। antakāle smaranto māṃ praviśantyeva bhāvitāḥ । paryante bhāvatulyā hi nṛṇāṃ janmāntarasthitiḥ ।।
kaviṃ purāṇaṃ śāstāramaṇīyāṃsamaṇorapi । parastāttamaso nityaṃ ye smaranti raviprabham ।। bhrūmadhye vihitaprāṇā brahmarandhravibhedinaḥ । omityekākṣaraṃ brahma japanto yānti te param ।।
brahmādibhirbhūtasargaścakravatparivartate । paraṃ māṃ pratipannāste na bhavanti bhave punaḥ ।। vairañce asminnahorātre bhavanti na bhavanti ca । bhūtānyekastu bhagavānavyakto na vinaśyati ।
tejomayamahaḥ śuklo mokṣāyaivottarāyaṇam ।। śrīgītāsvaṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ ।। rājaguhyamidaṃ cānyatpavitraṃ śṛṇu phalguṇa । aśraddadhāno nāpnoti māṃ saṃsāravaśīkṛtaḥ ।।
sarvakartari bhūtāni mayi santi na teṣvaham । lokāḥ sthitā na sthitāśca mayi vyomnīva vāyavaḥ ।। adhiṣṭhitaiṣā prakṛtirmayā sūte carācaram । asaktaṃ māṃ na jānanti malināmoghadarśinaḥ ।।
sarvaṃ sarvagataṃ yajñaṃ vedyaṃ bījaṃ bhavābhavam । vidanti māṃ sukutinaḥ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam ।। trayīdharmajuṣaḥ svargabhogalābhakṣayākulāḥ । na prāpnuvanti māṃ śuṣkakriyāpāśavaśīkṛtāḥ ।।
madekaśaraṇā nityaṃ kṛtino ananyayājinaḥ । apyanyayonisaṃbhūtāḥ svayamāyānti yatpadam ।। śrīgītāsu navamo adhyāyaḥ ।। bhūyo api me śṛṇu sakhe prītyā yatpratibodhyase ।
na tattvenāmaragaṇā munayo vā vidanti mām ।। carācare asminpravaraṃ yadyatpaśyasi bhūtimat । tadahaṃ sarvabhūtātmā na hi kiṃcinmayā vinā ।। ahaṃ viṣṇurahaṃ sūryaścandro ahaṃ maghavānaham ।
śaṃkaro ahaṃ dhaneśaśca vahniḥ suragurustathā । akṣaro ahamahaṃ kālo jayo ahaṃ bhūtirapyaham ।। śrīgītāsu daśamo adhyāyaḥ ।। śrutvaitadavadatpārtho jāne tvāṃ sarvamacyuta ।
kiṃtu viśvamayaṃ rūpaṃ draṣṭumicchami te vibho ।। ityuktaḥ pāṇḍuputreṇa bhagavānkaiṭabhāntakaḥ । viśvāviṣkārakalayā viśvarūpamadarśayat ।। tasyānantaśironetrasahasrabhujaśālinaḥ ।
dehe jagannivāsasya līnaṃ viśvamadṛśyata ।। atisūryāgnimahasā tejasā pūritāmbaram । dṛṣṭvā pulakitaḥ pārthastamuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। paśyāmyudagragīrvāṇagrāmavyāptoruvigraham ।
tvāṃ yena pūritaṃ sarvamanavacchinnavarṣmaṇā ।। brahmarudramarudvahnimunīndrabhujagākulam । draṣṭuṃ tadeva paryantarahitaṃ notsahe vapuḥ ।। bhīṣmadroṇamukhānvīrānpraviṣṭānvadanāni te ।
daṃṣṭrotkaṭāni paśyāmi kālasyeva yugakṣaye ।। ko bhavānsarvasaṃhārāraudreṇa vapuṣāsūdanaḥ । akāṇḍe dagdhumakhilānsvayaṃ lokānsamudyataḥ ।। ityuktavati kaunteye jagāda madhusūdanaḥ ।
ahaṃ jagatkṣayotkṣopadīkṣitaḥ kṣitipāntakaḥ ।। kurusenāgragānvīrānpūrvaṃ vinihatānmayā । hatvā yaśaḥśriyā jṛṣṭamavāpnuhi kulocitam ।। tacchrutvā kāliyārātervacaḥ pārthaḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ ।
uvāca kampitamanāḥ praṇato gadgadasvanaḥ ।। kīrtyā jaganti hṛṣyanti stutayā siddhacāraṇaiḥ । dīptyā dravanti rakṣāṃsi sthāne tava janārdana ।। naumi tvāṃ jagadāvāsaṃ viśvarūpamadhokṣajam ।
anantaṃ śāśvataṃ dhāma sarvātmānaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।। kṣamyatāṃ tatsuhṛditi svayaṃ yatpraṇatapriyaḥ । ukto asi kṛṣṇa govinda yādaveti purā mayā ।। ugraṃ tadevaṃ bhagavandṛṣṭvā rūpamahaṃ mahat ।
cakrārūḍhamivāśeṣaṃ paśyāmi nikhilaṃ jagat ।। prasīda darśaya vibho vapuḥ saumyaṃ tadeva me । śāntiṃ me yāti sahasā nānyatā vyathitaṃ manaḥ ।। iti prasāditaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ praṇatena kirīṭinā ।
adarśayannijaṃ rūpaṃ tadevātha caturbhujam ।। devā api na paśyanti mamedaṃ sarvagaṃ vapuḥ । ityuktvāśvāsayāmāsa kaunteyaṃ kamalādhavaḥ ।। śrīgītāsvekādaso adhyāyaḥ ।।
athārjuno avadatkṛṣṇaṃ ye bhaktāstvāmupāsate । avyaktamakṣaraṃ ye ca teṣāṃ ke adhikayoginaḥ ।। pārtheneti hariḥ pṛṣṭo vihitānugraho avadat । madbhaktāḥ śraddhayopetāḥ sarvathā yogino adhikāḥ ।।
kleśenaiva tu matprāptiravyaktākṣarasevanāt । sūkṣmasthūlagatirduḥkhaṃ tattvajñairapyavāpyate ।। madbhaktāstvacirādeva prāpnuvanti paraṃ padam । atastvaṃ manmanā nityamananyanirato bhava ।।
vaśe yadi na te cittamabhyāsena gṛhāṇa tat । tatrāpyaśakto matkarmā satataṃ śreyase bhava ।। athavā phalasaṃnyāsaṃ karmaṇāṃ kuru matparaḥ । jñānaṃ hi paramābhyāsājjñānāddhyānamihottamam ।।
dhyānācca phalasaṃnyāsastataḥ śāntirviśiṣyate । adveṣṭā karuṇāsindhuḥ sukhaduḥkhasamaḥ śamī ।। udāsīnaḥ śucirdakṣaḥ kṣamī bhaktaḥ priyo mama । śrīgītāsu dvādaśo adhyāyaḥ ।।
śarīraṃ kṣetramityāhuḥ kṣetrajñaṃ māṃ vidurbudhāḥ । kṣetraṃ tatsavikāraṃ tu māyā bhūtādi ca sthitam ।। śāntānāṃ dṛṣṭadoṣāṇāṃ jñānināṃ na vimohanam । mānadambhamadakrodhatyāgo guruniṣevaṇam ।।
asaktirnaśvare nityaṃ jñānamajñānamanyathā । jñeyaṃ tu manmayaṃ brahma śuddhaṃ sadasatoḥ param ।। sarvataḥ pāṇivadanaṃ sarvākāramanāmayam । prakṛtiḥ puruṣaśceti kṣetrakṣetrajñasaṃgamaḥ ।।
prakṛtiḥ karaṇe heturbhoktā tu puruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ । ekasthānaṃ pṛthagbhāvaṃ bhūtānāṃ yo anupaśyati ।। tatsaṃgamācca vistāraṃ sa yāti brahma śāśvatam । paramātmā guṇātīto nityatvādayamavyayaḥ ।
bhautike api sthitaḥ kāye sarvavyāpī na lipyate ।। śrīgītāsu trayodaśo adhyāyaḥ ।। sarvajñānamidaṃ bhūyaḥ śrūyatāṃ surasevitam । yadyogo brahmagarbhe asminsaṃbhavanmūrtisaṃbhavaḥ ।।
sattvādayastadudbhūtā vibhāntyete guṇāstrayaḥ । vaicitryādaniśaṃ yeṣāṃ saṃsaranti śarīriṇaḥ ।। sattvaṃ prakāśakaṃ jñeyaṃ yadutthaiḥ stambhakaṃ rajaḥ । tamo hyāvaraṇaṃ mohapramādādyasya saṃbhavaḥ ।।
satataṃ saṃkareṇaiṣāṃ nyūnādhikyavibhedataḥ । guṇadoṣāśca dṛśyante te te kila śarīriṇām ।। madbhaktāḥ śāntamanaso jīvanmuktidaśāṃ śritāḥ । guṇairetaiḥ parityaktā bhajante sukhamakṣayam ।।
śrīkītāsu caturdaśo adhyāyaḥ ।। ūrdhvamūlaṃ bhavāśvatthamābrahmasadanoditam । lokāntarānekaśākhaṃ vicitraviṣayāṅkuram ।। guṇakarmaprabuddhānāṃ śubhāśubhaphalodayam ।
svabhāvabhūmāvavṛtaṃ jānīte yaḥ sa vedavit ।। tamasaṅgakuṭhāreṇa cchittvā yānti padaṃ mama । nirastamohaṃ vaimalyādatisūryendupāvakam ।। yadaṃśo jīvaloke asmiñjīvaścarati sarvagaḥ ।
vāyurgandhamivādāya yo yātīndriyavāsanāḥ ।। tadvidhaṃ guṇayuktānāṃ sarvāvasthāsu nirguṇam । paśyanti jñāninaḥ sarvajagatāṃ jīvanaṃ param ।। bhūtasargāmivāgatya akṣaro ahaṃ sanātanaḥ ।
manmayā dhṛtimanto māṃ bhajante puruṣottamam ।। śrīgītāsu pañcadaśo adhyāyaḥ ।। abhīḥ sattvaṃ śucirjñānaṃ damo dānaṃ tapaḥ kratuḥ । ahiṃsāyā guṇāścānye jāyante divyasaṃpadām ।।
dambhamānamadakrodhapāruṣyājñānacāpalaiḥ । āsurī sūcyate saṃpanmohasokavivardhinī ।। yukto api satataṃ divyasaṃpadā mā śucaḥ sakhe । āsuraṃ bhāvamāpannā bhajante yonimāsurīm ।।
sattvādibhirguṇairbaddho jñāyate ceṣṭitairjanaḥ । manobhojanamācāro guṇatulyo hi dehinām ।। śrīgītāsu ṣoḍaśo adhyāyaḥ ।। ākarṇyaitadathovāca phalgunaḥ punaracyutam ।
saṃnyāsatyāgayostatvaṃ jñātumicchāmyahaṃ vibho ।। ukte pāṇḍusuteneti bhagavānabhyabhāṣata । kāmyakarmaphalatyāgaṃ saṃnyāsaṃ saṃpracakṣate ।। sarvakarmaphalatyāgastyāga ityabhidhīyate ।
ma tkarma na parityājyaṃ tyājyaṃ tu vidhigarhitam ।। nityakarmaparityāgo mohāttāmasa ucyate । kleśaduḥkhabhayāttyāgo rājaso niṣphalaḥ smṛtaḥ । kurvatāmapyasaktānāṃ tyāgaḥ sattvocito mataḥ ।।
śrīgītāsu saptadaśo adhyāyaḥ ।। karma kartā ca buddhiśca trividhā guṇabhedataḥ । dhṛtiḥ sukhaṃ ca traiguṇyāttrividhaṃ dehināṃ matam ।। yathoktasevī niḥsaṅgaḥ kuru karma nijaṃ sakhe ।
madbhakto matstutiparaḥ paraṃ padamavāpsyasi ।। idaṃ bhaktāya te jñānamupadiṣṭaṃ mayā svayam । yaḥ śroṣyati sa saṃsāraduḥkhānyatitariṣyati ।। kaccinmoho vinaṣṭaste kaccidetacchrutaṃ tvayā ।
keśaveneti kathite babhāṣe śakranandanaḥ ।। bhagavanvītamoho ahaṃ kariṣye tava śāsanam । uktveti vīro gāṇḍīvamācakarṣa raṇotsukaḥ ।। śrīgītāsvaṃṣṭādaśo adhyāyaḥ ।।
athodatiṣṭhadgambhīrajaladadhvānamantharaḥ । yuyutsuṃ pārthamālokya sainyānāṃ harṣaniḥsvanaḥ ।। pūrvaṃ tataḥ subhaṭakaṅkaṭapātikhaṅgaṭāṅkāranādamukhareṣu baleṣu rājñām । dharmātmajaḥ kavacacāpaśarānvimucya devavratābhimukhamutsukadhīḥ sasarpaḥ ।।
dhigdhiṅnṛpaṃ kṛpaṇaceṣṭa manuṣyasaṃjñaṃ bhūruṃ yudhiṣṭhiramalīkakṛtābhidhānam । yācñā kṛtāñjalirupaiti parānyadeṣa śūrāstadiṅgitajaḍāḥ pṛthagityavocan ।। so apyacchakīrtiratha bhīṣmamukhānupetya prahvaḥ śarīrapaṇasaṃśritadhārtarāṣṭrān । tatpādalagnamukuṭaḥ prakaṭaṃ praṇamya lebhe tadāśiṣamaśeṣamahīpajaitrīm ।।
abhyāhataṃ ca raṇaraṅgamṛdaṅgatūrye pārthānguṇaikarasiko guṇavānyuyutsuḥ । abhyāyayau tava sutaḥ svakurūnnirasya dhāvanti tulyagumameva nṛṇāṃ manāṃsi ।। asminmahākṣayamukhe karavālapaṭṭasaṃrakṣitapratimukhe raṇaraṅganāṭye । vyākīrṇakīrtikusumāñjalirarjunāgranāndīmivāpaṭhadamandadhanurninādaiḥ ।।
atrāntare nṛpaticakrakirīṭakoṭisaṃpātajātavabuśākulavisphuliṅga । jaitrī triśūlakaraśiṣyamunerudagrā gāṅgeyaśātaviśisvāvalirullalāsa ।। saṃtrāsasaṃkucitaniścalakarṇatāladikkuñjarākalitakampitasarvalokam । kṣubhyatkṣayāmbudharabhairavabhīmanādaṃ bhīmaṃ niśamya bhayamāvirabhūdbhaṭānām ।।
atha bhīmaṃ samabhyāyātsvayaṃ rājā suyodhanaḥ । bhrātṛbhiḥ sahito vīrairdhunāno vipulaṃ dhanuḥ ।। tataḥ pravṛtte saṃgrāme durlakṣye śaravṛṣṭibhiḥ । svayaṃ śāntanavaḥ śrīmānabhyadhāvaddhanaṃjayam ।।
sātyakiṃ kṛtavarmā ca hyabhimanyuṃ bṛhadbalaḥ । duḥśāsano api nakulaṃ sahadevaṃ ca durmukhaḥ ।। yudhiṣṭhiraṃ tathā śalya ācāryo drupadātmajam । somadattaśca vairāṭiṃ bāhlikaścedibhūpatim ।।
rakṣasāṃ pravaraṃ vīraṃ ghaṭotkacamalumbusaḥ । śikhaṇḍinaṃ droṇasuto matsyaṃ prāgjyotiṣeśvaraḥ ।। kṛpaḥ kekayabhūpālaṃ drupadaṃ ca jayadrathaḥ । sutasomaṃ vikarṇaśca bhīmasenasutaṃ balī ।।
cekitānaḥ vikarṇaśca praaitivindhyaṃ ca saubalaḥ । irāvataśca vikrāntaṃ śatāyuḥ phalguṇātmajam ।। vindānuvindāvāvantyau kuntibhojaṃ yaśasvinam । kauravo vīrabāhuśca virāṭasutamuttaram ।।
anye ca vīrā rājāno rājasiṃhāḥ prahāriṇaḥ । utsāhasattvasaṃpannāḥ sasainyāḥ yamupādravan ।। teṣāṃ kaṅkaṇaratnāṃśupaṭalāḥ karanirgatāḥ । hemapuṅkhā śarāścakrurvahnivyāptaṃ digantaram ।।
athopuṅkhā rajasā gajavājirathākulam । vīrāṇāṃ tumulaṃ yuddhaṃ nirmaryādamavartata ।। tataḥ śirobhirvīrāṇāṃ patitotphullitairmuhuḥ । amandakandukakrīḍā babhūveva raṇaśriyaḥ ।।
tataḥ pāṇḍavasainyeṣu bhīṣmacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ । vidāriteṣa bahuśaḥ samuttasthau mahāravaḥ ।। athābhimanyurabhyetya śatamanyusutātmajaḥ । bhīṣmamabhyādravadvīro miṣatāṃ sarvabhūbhujām ।।
kṛtavarmaprabhṛtibhiḥ sahitaṃ bhīṣmamojasā । ayodhayatsa viśiśvairdhvajamasya cakarta ca ।। hematāle nipatite saṃrabdho atha pitāmahaḥ । divyāsravarṣī sāvegaṃ saubhadraṃ samupādravat ।।
tato vṛkodaramukhā vinadanto mahārathāḥ । sānugaṃ śantanusutaṃ samantātparyavārayan ।। bhīṣmo api sātyakiṃ viddhvā dhvajaṃ pavanajanmanaḥ । unmamātha śarāgreṇa haimaṃ kesariṇaṃ rathāt ।।
atrāntare giriprāṃśumāruhya madakuñjaram । ayodhyanmadrarājaṃ hṛṣṭo vairāṭiruttaraḥ ।। sa kuñjarendraḥ śalyasya pādena caturo hayān । jaghānākṛṣya hastena garjañjaladaniḥsvanaḥ ।।
tato madrādhipaḥ kruddhaḥ śaktiṃ śaktimatāṃ varaḥ । pradīptāṃ prāhiṇodvegāduttarāyeṣuvarṣiṇe ।। sa tayā bhinnahṛdayaḥ papāta galitāyudhaḥ । karṇikāra iva bhraṣṭaḥ karīndrācalaśekharāt ।।
uttaraṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā śaṅkhastasyānujaḥ krudhā । cakāra śalyamabhyetya śarairjaṭilavigraham ।। tasya śalyo atha gadayā vidārya dalaśo ratham । unnanādābhavanyena diśaḥ śakalitā iva ।।
śaṅkho hatāśvaḥ sahasā phalguṇasya rathaṃ yayau । bhīṣmo atha pāṇḍavacamūṃ vyagāhata nṛpāntakaḥ ।। matsyakekayāpāñcālacedisenāsu sarvaśaḥ । bhīṣmabāṇavibhinnāsu sūryo astaśikharaṃ yayau ।।
tato nivṛtte saṃgrāme śibirāṇi nareśvarāḥ । bhejire pratisaṃsanto vipulaṃ bhīṣmavikramam ।। prathame yuddhadivase uttaravadhaḥ ।। dinānte dīrṇapṛtanaḥ śokārto dharmanandanaḥ ।
saṃhāraṃ nijasainyānāṃ pradadhyau bhīṣmavikramam ।। sa rājamadhye govindamuvāca karuṇākulaḥ । kṣīyamāṇasya samare satyaṃ śreyastapo mama ।। alaṃ yuddhena me kṛṣṇa pṛthivīkṣayakāriṇā ।
ko mucyeta raṇe prāpya bhīṣmaṃ bhīṣmaparākramam ।। iti bruvāṇaṃ rājānamuvāca madhusūdanaḥ । dhruvaste vijayo rājanyasya yoddhā dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। sātyakirdrupadaḥ śaibyaḥ sikhaṇḍī pañca kekayāḥ ।
saubhadraśca raṇe kruddho hanyādeva gaṇānapi ।। ukte janārdaneneti tīvraṃ bhīṣmaparākramam । mithaḥ kathayatāṃ teṣāṃ sā jagāma vibhāvarī ।। athodite sahasrāṃśau vihite pāṇḍunandanaiḥ ।
kruñcavyūhe mahotsāhairvyūhamanye api cakrire ।। tataḥ pravṛtte samare tīvre bhīrubhayaṃkare । hṛdayākampane nājñāṃ tālaketuradṛśyata ।। gambhīradhīrasaṃrambho varjayansa pṛthagjanam ।
cakarta bhūbhujāmeva śirāṃsi laghuvikramaḥ ।। bhīṣmeṇālolite vyūhe vātoddhūta ivārmave । tamabhyadhāvatsaṃrabdhaḥ śvetāśvo acyutasārathiḥ ।। tamāpatantaṃ viśakhairbhīṣmaḥ kṣipramapūrayat ।
droṇaduryodhanamukhāḥ sarve cānye mahārathāḥ ।। pārtho api sāyakaiścakre samantātkuruvāhinīm । tatpakṣapavanasphārairdīrṇāmiva sahasradhā ।। duryodhanaprerito atha svayaṃ śantanunandanaḥ ।
nindannijaṃ kṣatradharmamabhyadāvaddhanaṃjayam ।। nirviśeṣaṃ tayostatra suciraṃ yudhyamānayoḥ । niruddhāṃ śarajālena nādṛśyanta diśo daśa ।। na dadarśa tayoḥ kaścidantaraṃ kṣipatoḥ śarān ।
dhārāsāraprabalayornadatoriva meghayoḥ ।। tato droṇamukhā vīrā dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamaiḥ । ayudhyantābhavanyena surāḥ pulakitā divi ।। bhībhasenaḥ kaliṅgānāṃ praviśyātha varuthinīm ।
pātayankuñjarāṃścakre niḥsaṃcārāṃ vasuṃdharām ।। bhīmanirbhinnamattebhakumbhodbhūtāsṛgambhasām । pravāhairyayurākaṇṭhaṃ turaṅgāḥ kṛcchagāminaḥ ।। nihatya kuñjarānīkaṃ kaliṅgānāṃ prahāriṇām ।
ketumantaṃ narapatiṃ jaghāna sapadānugam ।। niḥśeṣitakaliṅgasya bhīmasenasya nādataḥ । ghanagambhīranādena pṛthivī samakampata ।। tato bhīṣmaḥ samabhyetya dṛṣṭvā dīrṇāmanīkinīm ।
vidhāya virathaṃ bhīmaṃ śaineyāśvānapothayat ।। duryodhanasutaṃ vīraṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ śauryalakṣaṇam । abhimanyuḥ śitairbāṇaiḥ kṣiprahastamapothayat ।। gocare patitaṃ putraṃ saubhadrasya pramāthinaḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā duryodhano rājā sānugaḥ svayamādravat ।। kuruvīraiḥ parivṛtaṃ vilokya sutamarjunaḥ । maṇḍalīkṛtagāṇḍīvastūrṇaṃ pratyudyayau parān ।। lāghavādabhitastasya sāyakāścitrayodhinaḥ ।
jahnuḥ śirāṃsi śūrāṇāṃ phalānīva mahīruhām ।। ākhaṇḍalabhuvā caṇḍagāṇḍīvapreritaiḥ śaraiḥ । vidāriteṣvanīkeṣu vidhvastarathasādiṣu ।। rudhireṇeva gagane saṃdhyārāgema pūrite ।
avahāraṃ raṇe cakre vāsarānte pitāmahaḥ ।। ditīyo yuddhadivasaḥ ।। anyedyurgāruḍaṃ vyūhaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīṣmeṇa kalpitam । ardhacandraṃ prativyūhaṃ cakrire pāṇḍunandanāḥ ।।
tataḥ pravṛte samare bhīrūṇāṃ dhṛtikhaṇḍane । ārūḍheva mahīvyoma rajasā samalakṣyata ।। asṛkpravāhaiḥ sahasā praśānte reṇumaṇḍale । sughoraḥ saṃprahāro abhūnnṛpāṇāṃ tridaśekṣitaḥ ।।
bhīṣmadroṇamukhairvīraiḥ। phalguṇapramukhā raṇe । saṃsaktāḥ samadṛśyanta pūrvadevairivāmarāḥ ।। bāṇajālena mahatā saṃhatānāṃ samantataḥ । arjunena niruddhāsu ripūṇāṃ śastravṛṣṭiṣu ।। akampitau kuruvyūhe bhīmasenaghaṭotkacau ।
praviśya cakraturvīrau vyākulāṃ paravāhinīm ।। tāvabhyadhāvatsaṃrambhādamarṣī dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ । kurvannājasamājena mauliradnāruṇā diśaḥ ।। haiḍambabāṇanihatā vīrāstasya padānugāḥ ।
mahāvātasamākrāntā drumā iva cakampire ।। duryodhanapreritānāṃ śarāṇāṃ dīptatejasām । vṛṣṭimabhyudgatāṃ ghorāṃ cicchedāśu vṛkodaraḥ ।। bhīmotsṛṣṭena pṛthunā pṛṣaṅke nātha kauravaḥ ।
hṛdi viddho nimagnena mumoha bhṛśavihvalaḥ ।। tasminsārathinā nīte rathenākulaketunā । dudrāva sainyaṃ tatsarvaṃ paśyatordreṇabhīṣmayoḥ ।। mahārathairvārite api kīrṇe tasminbalārṇave ।
pratyudyayau samāśvasya tūrṇaṃ rājā suyodhanaḥ ।। pārthasātyakisaubhadraiḥ sa dṛṣṭvā bahuśaścamūm । vidrāvitāṃ samabhyetya pitāmahamabhāṣata ।। dāritaṃ paśya me sainyaṃ labdhalakṣairarātibhiḥ ।
pāṇḍuputreṣu kṛpayā tvayi mādhyasthyamāśrite ।। alaṃ dromasahāyasya paristhātuṃ purastava । madabhāgyavaśānna syādyadi pārtheṣu vaḥ kṛpā ।। etatsuyodhanenoktaṃ śrutvā surasaritsutaḥ ।
īṣatsmitasudhādhautakapolaphalako avadat ।। ukto asi bahuśo rājannajeyāḥ pāṇḍavā iti । yattu śakyaṃ mayā kiṃcidvṛddhenādya karomi kim ।। ityuktvā cāpamākṛṣya tālamātraṃ mahābhujaḥ ।
mandāyamāne divase samamabhyudyayau parān ।। tato bhīṣmarathodīrṇaiḥ śaraiḥ sūryakaraprabhaiḥ । vidāritānyanekāni tamāṃsīva kṣayaṃ yayuḥ ।। tomareṣvātapatreṣu śarīreṣu ca bhūbhujām ।
petuḥ punarabhāvāya bhīṣmanāmāṅkitāḥ śarāḥ ।। adṛṣṭapuṅkhavadanairghanaśreṇīkṛtairmuhuḥ । tatsāyakairadṛśyābhūtpāṇḍavānāmanīkinī ।। taṃ yudhyamānaṃ dīptāstraṃ varjayanto api saṃgare ।
dikṣu bhīṣmasahasrāṇi dadṛśuḥ sarvapārthivāḥ ।। vrajatsu rājacakreṣu bhīṣmānalapataṅgatām । ekenaikena bāṇena bhinneṣu triṣu dantiṣu ।। yāte sahasradhā sainye pāṇḍavānāṃ tarasvinām ।
anayatphalguṇarathaṃ gāṅgeyāntikamacyutaḥ ।। tato abhavadbhīṣmaśarairbhāsvaraiḥ savyasācinaḥ । kṣaṇaṃ pañcānanasyeva cārukāñcanapañjaraḥ ।। niruddhaśarasaṃcāro yatnena śatamanyujaḥ ।
vicitrairvicaranmārgairyuyudhe kṛṣṇasārathiḥ ।। tasyātimānuṣaṃ dhairyamāsthitasya pitāmahaḥ । sādhu putreti saṃhṛṣṭaḥ parākramamapūjayat ।। tatkaṅkapattrinirbhinnau kṛṣṇāvekarathe sthitau ।
raktāśokāvivotphullau babhatuḥ kṣatajokṣitau ।। tato nirantarairbāṇairbhīṣmakārmukanirgataiḥ । ākrāntabhuvanābhogairnādṛśyanta diśo daśa ।। bhīṣme pṛthuśarajvāle kālānala ivodyate ।
dudrāva pāṇḍavacamūḥ paścādabhisṛtā paraiḥ ।। bhagneṣu bhaṭamukhyeṣu babhāṣe kaiṭabhāntakaḥ । kva nu mānadhanā yūyamapārayaśaso raṇe । parityajya kulācāraṃ yātāḥ kātaratāmimām ।।
ityuktvā tānsamālokya vidrutāneva keśavaḥ । uvāca sātyakiṃ vīraṃ yudhyamānaṃ prayatnataḥ ।। tiṣṭhantu yāntu vā sarve sātyake pṛtanāgragāḥ । eṣa svayaṃ nihanmyadya sānugaṃ śantanoḥ sutam ।।
ityuktvā caṇḍamārtaṇḍamaṇḍalāgraṃ sudarśanam । svayamudyamya kaṃsāriḥ syandanāgrādavātarat ।। kruddhasya tasya kalpāntakarālānalarociṣaḥ । na rūpaṃ sehire draṣṭuṃ surā api divi sthitāḥ ।।
saṃrambhodbhrāntadordaṇḍavilasatpītavāsasā । śobhāṃ bheje sa nīlādreḥ sarpatsaṃdhyābhraśālinaḥ ।। tamantakamivāyāntaṃ jagatsaṃhāradīkṣitam । dhīraḥ śāntanavo dṛṣṭvā dhunāno dhanurabhyadhāt ।।
ehyehi bhagavanviṣṇo jiṣṇo tridaśavidviṣām । cakreṇa me śiraśchindhi bhavakleśakṛśānunā ।। bhavatā nābhijāmbhojasamuddhūtasvayaṃbhuvā । hato jagannivāsena dhanyatāṃ yātvayaṃ janaḥ ।।
siddhasindhusuteneti bhāṣite natamaulinā । avaruhya radhāttūrṇamarjunaḥ kṛṣṇamanvagāt ।। sa niṣpīḍya balātpādau purastātkāliyadviṣaḥ । uvāca saṃhara vibho kopaṃ viśvakṣayocitam ।।
kṣapayāmi ripūnsarvānyudhi satyena te śape । iti prasādya taṃ pārtho rathamāropayatpunaḥ ।। tato gāṇḍīvaghoṣeṇa pāñcajanyaraveṇa ca । cakrāte rājacakrāṇāṃ kṛṣṇau kṛṣṇāmbudabhramam ।।
tato nirvivarairbāṇaiḥ śalyabhiriśravaḥśalāḥ । avākiranbhīṣmamukhāḥ phalguṇaṃ śastravṛṣṭibhiḥ ।। tāmāyudhamahāvṛṣṭiṃ chittvā sapadi pāṇjavaḥ । māhendramastraṃ vidadhe sarvalokakṣayakṣamam ।।
tasminnudīrṇe sahasā mahāstre dīptatejasi । caṇḍavātavikīrṇeva cakampe kuruvāhinī ।। vadhyamāneṣu saineṣu kṣipraṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā । naranāgāśvadehotthā sasarpa rudhirāpagā ।।
chattrācchaphenapaṭalāṃ calaccāmarasārasām । keśaśevālaśabalāṃ piśācāstāṃ siṣevire ।। ghore nṛpakṣaye tasminvartamāne raṇotsave । saṃdhyayā dikṣu jātāsu śoṇitena bhṛtāsviva ।।
yāte astaṃ caṇḍakiraṇe pratyagrarudhiratviṣi । māṃsapiṇḍa iva graste ghoreṇa dhvāntarakṣasā ।। vidhvastacāpakavacā viprakīrṇarathadhvajāḥ । avahāramakurvanta pāṇḍavāḥ śastravikṣatāḥ ।।
tṛtīyo yuddhadivasaḥ ।। punaḥ prabhāte saṃrabdhā niryayuḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ । vinadanto mahotsāhā vyāḍavyūhāgravartinaḥ ।। atha pravṛtte samare pṛthivīkṣayaśaṃsini ।
saubhadrapramukhā vīrānbhīṣmamukhyānayodhayan ।। tataḥ śaraśatāsārasaṃpūritadigantaraḥ । mahārathānatītyānyānbhīṣmor'junamupādravat ।। nirviśeṣaṃ tayoḥ kṣipraṃ pīrayoryudhyamānayoḥ ।
eko droṇimukhānvīrānabhimanyurayodhayat ।। chinnavarmadhvajarathānsa vidhāya mahārathān । śiraḥprakaramucchinnaṃ rājñāṃ kṣipramapātayat ।। droṇaprabhṛtibhiḥ sarvairdṛṣṭvā saubhadramāvṛtam ।
dhṛṣṭadyumnaścamūnāthaścakartābhyetya kauravān ।। sa hatvā cāmaraṃ śūraḥ pauravyatanayaṃ nṛpam । śiraḥsaṃyamaneḥ kāyājjahārākulakuṇḍalam ।। atrāntare gajānīkairvipulaiśca gajādhipaḥ ।
bhīmaduryodhanādiṣṭo gadāpāṇiḥ samādravat ।। bhīmaseno atha rabhasādavaruhya rathādgajān । garjannurugadāghātairjaghāna ghanavikramaḥ ।। gadāprahārābhihatairvajrabhinnairivācalaiḥ ।
patadbhirmattamātaṅgaiścakampe cakiteva bhūḥ ।। nihate kuñjarānīke bhīmena bhayadāyinā । tamabhyadhāvansaṃkruddhāḥ sarve duryodhanādayaḥ ।। suyodhanaśarāghātamūrchito atha vṛkodaraḥ ।
samāśvāsya parānīkaṃ rathena kupito aviśat ।। viśvasaṃhārasaṃkruddhaṃ taṃ kṛtāntamivotthitam । prāpyānujāḥ kurupateścaturdaśa yayuḥ kṣayam ।। senāpatiṃ suṣeṇaṃ ca jayasaṃdhaṃ sulocanam ।
bhīmamugraṃ bhīmarathaṃ bhīmabāhumalolupam ।। samaṃ vavitsuṃ kaṭakaṃ durmukhaṃ duṣpradarśanam । hatvaināmakarotsenāṃ kauravāṇāṃ sahasradhā ।। tamabhyadhāvanmattena supratīkena dantinā ।
gambhīraghoraghoṣeṇa bhagadattaḥ sahānugaiḥ ।। gajodayācalaraveḥ śaraistīkṣṇairivāṃśubhiḥ । pratāpadhāmnastasyārātsa ca kopārivāhinī ।। tatsāyakena viddho atha hṛdi marmāvabhedinā ।
dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samālambya tasthau bhīmo atimūrchitaḥ ।। tato ghaṭotkacaḥ kruddho dṛṣṭvā janakamākulam । bhagadattamabhidrutya ghorāṃ māyāṃ samādade ।। airāvaṇagataḥ so atha prabhinnairdigdvipaiḥ saha ।
apīḍayatsupratīkaṃ dīptābhiḥ śastravṛṣṭibhiḥ ।। tasya nirbhidyamānasya kuñjarendrasya garjataḥ । śabdena tasthurālīya sarve saṃkucitā gajāḥ ।। ghaṭotkacena saṃsaktaṃ dṛṣṭvā prāgjyotiṣeśvaram ।
saha droṇādibhirvīrairbhīṣmastaṃ deśamādravat ।। ghaṭotkacaṃ kālarūpaṃ nadantaṃ vīkṣya bhairavam । saṃdhyāyāṃ durjayaṃ matvā bhīṣmastaṃ bhīmavikramam ।। avahāraṃ susainyānāṃ vidadhe dhīmatāṃ varaḥ ।
yenābhavankālavaktrānniṣkrāntā iva kauravāḥ ।। caturtho yuddhadivasaḥ ।। tato niśāyāmabhyetya kururājaḥ pitāmaham । papraccha pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ duḥkhito jayakāraṇam ।।
tamabravīcchāntanavo rājannukto asi sarvadā । devena viṣṇunā guptā na jeyāḥ pāṇḍavā iti ।। purā bhūbhāraśāntyarthaṃ svayaṃbhūrmunisaṃsadi । prādurbhūtaṃ svayaṃ viṣṇuṃ tuṣṭāva sahasāṃ nidhim ।।
jaya viśveśa viśvātmanviśvaksena sudhānidhe । amandaciddhanānanda saṃvitsamarasadyute ।। namastubhyaṃ jagatsargasthitisaṃhārakāriṇe । trivikramāya mahate triguṇāya trimūrtaye ।।
namaḥ pracaṇḍacakrāgraprabhābāsurabāhave । daityāndhakārasaṃhārakāriṇe mohadāriṇe ।। avatīrṇā bhuvaṃ nātha dānavā ye hatāstvayā । teṣāṃ vadhāya dṛptānāṃ mānuṣī tanumāviśa ।।
iti stutāḥ padmabhuvā devo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ । nareṇa sākaṃ bhūbhāraśāntyai kṣitimavātarat ।। sa eṣa kṛṣṇo bhagavāñjāto yādavanandanaḥ । naraśca vijayo dhīraḥ pravaraḥ sarvadhanvinām ।।
devau kṛṣṇārjunāvetau na jeyau tridaśairapi । iti jñātvā śamaḥ putra kriyatāṃ pāṇḍunandanaiḥ ।। viśvepākhyānam ।। atha prabhāte makaraśyenavyūhāgravartinaḥ ।
bhīṣmabhīmamukhā yuddhaṃ cakrire pāṇḍunandanāḥ ।। hatānāṃ hanyamānānāṃ ghnatāṃ ca samare mithaḥ । patatāṃ tatra vīrāṇāṃ niḥsvastumulo abhavat ।। bhīmaphalguṇasaubhadramatsyasātyakipārṣataiḥ ।
bhīṣmamukhyaiśca te sene bhinne saṃśayamāpatuḥ ।। kabandhatāṇḍavaścaṇḍe mattavetālasaṃkule । tasminnāyodhane ghore bhūtānāmutsavo abhavat ।। dhanvināṃ śarajālena divamutpatatāṃ muhuḥ ।
ravau saṃchādite rājñāṃ vyartho abhūcchastrasaṃgrahaḥ ।। bīreṇa bhūriśravasā saṃsaktaṃ vīkṣya sātyakim । abhyādrabandhanvinastaṃ deśaṃ sātyakisūnavaḥ ।। teṣāmāpatatāṃ pūrṇaṃ sṛjatāṃ śaradurdinam ।
bhūriśravāḥ śirāṃsyārāduścakarta śitaiḥ śaraiḥ ।। hateṣu teṣu kupitaḥ pradīptāstro dhanaṃjayaḥ । cakāra kurusenānāṃ saṃhāraṃ harisārathiḥ ।। hate lakṣacaturbhāge bhūbhujāmanivartinām ।
gāmḍīvadhanvanā sainyaṃ vāsarānte nyavartata ।। pañcamo yuddhadivasaḥ ।। punaḥ prabhāte saṃnaddhā niryayuḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ । alakṣyabhedāvyūhābhyāṃ krauñcena makareṇa ca ।।
tataḥ pramathya sahasā bhīmaseno arivāhinīm । viveśa bhṛśasaṃkruddhaḥ samaṃ drupadasūnunā ।। tābhyāṃ vidārite vyūhe kupitāḥ kurunandanāḥ । vimukhaiḥ kuñjarānīkaistau tūrṇaṃ paryavārayan ।।
bhīmasenagadāghātaniṣpiṣṭavapuṣāṃ raṇe । abhūdvyatikaro ghoraḥ patatāṃ gajayodhinām ।। yudhyamāneṣu sainyeṣu bhīmena bhujaśālinā । abhyādravatsānugastaṃ svayaṃ rājā suyodhanaḥ ।।
chāditaṃ kauravairdṛṣṭvā bhīmaṃ viśikhavarṣibhiḥ । vimohaṃ vidadhe teṣāṃ mohanāstreṇa pārṣanaḥ ।। droṇena svayamabhyetya jñānāstreṇa vināśite । mohanāstre kurupatiṃ bhīmastūrṇamupādravat ।।
madāndha kvādhunā jīvanmayi jīvati yāsyasi । ityuktvā te śaraśatairvajravegairavākiran ।। bhīmacāpacyutairbāṇaiḥ so atha kṛttarathadhvajaḥ । hṛdi nirdārito bheje mūrchāṃ vyathitamānasaḥ ।।
atrāntare bhīṣmaśarairhanyamāneṣu rājasu । ghoro babhūva saṃmardaḥ kṛtāntasamarotsavaḥ ।। draupadeyeṣu vīreṣu yudhyamāneṣu kauravaiḥ । avartata raṇo ghoro gajavājirathakṣayaḥ ।।
athāvahāraṃ sainyānāṃ cakre śantanunandanaḥ । rājasevāvṛte sūrye yāte astaṃ rudhirāruṇe ।। ṣaṣṭho yuddhadivasaḥ ।। anyedyurmaṇḍalavyūhe bhīṣmeṇa vihite svayam ।
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sa durbhedyaṃ vajravyūhamakalpayat ।। tataḥ pravṛtte samare bhīṣaṇe bhīṣmapārthayoḥ । virāṭa ādravaddroṇaṃ gariṣṭhaṃ sarvadhanvinām ।। dromastaṃ bāṇavarṣeṇa saṃchādya śaravarṣiṇam ।
unnanāda dhanadhvāno rathamasya jaghāna ca ।। sa hatāśvaṃ samutsṛjya rathaṃ putrasya saṃbhramāt । āruroha hatānīkaṃ śaṅkhasyārūḍhadhanvinaḥ ।। droṇo atha tau pitāputrau vilokyaikarathe sthitau ।
śaṅkhāya prāhiṇoddhoraṃ mṛtyudaṇḍopamaṃ śaram ।। sa tena bhinnahṛdayaḥ papāta kṣatajokṣitaḥ । vātenonmathitaḥ śailādutphulla iva kiśukaḥ ।। tataḥ śikhaṇḍinaṃ droṇaḥ śarairviśikhavarṣiṇam ।
hatāśve sātyakirathaṃ samārūḍhe śikhaṇḍini । alambuso rākṣasendraḥ krūrakarmā tamādravat ।। māyayā yudhyamānaṃ taṃ garjantaṃ rākṣaseśvaram । cakāra vimukhaṃ kopādraurdreṇāstreṇa sātyakiḥ ।।
śaineyena jite tasminnirāvānarjunātmajaḥ । vindānuvindāvabhyāyājjambhārisamavikramaḥ ।। ghaṭotkacamathāyāntaṃ kṛtāntamiva bhairavam । avārayadgajendreṇa bhagadatto nṛpāgraṇīḥ ।।
vīraṃ sa hatvā haiḍambaṃ pāṇḍavānāmanīkinīm । darpādviloḍayāmāsa gajendro nalinīmiva ।। mādrīsutau tataḥ śalyaṃ vidhāya virathaṃ śaraiḥ । cakraturvimukhaṃ saṃkhye rājacakrasya paśyata ।।
svayaṃ yudhiṣṭhiro rājā nṛpaṃ jitvā śrutāyudham । vigāhya kauravānīkaṃ vidadhe vimukhaṃ śaraiḥ ।। cekitānena vijite gautame dhanvināṃ gurau । bhīṣmaścakāra kadanaṃ rājñāmanyatra cārjunaḥ ।।
yudhiṣṭhiragirā vīkṣya bhīṣmāya samabhidravat । śikhaṇḍinaṃ madrarājo divyairastrairavārayat ।। bhīṣmeṇa hanyamāneṣu bhūpāleṣvanivartiṣu । pārthena ca trigarteṣu jagāmāstaṃ divākaraḥ ।।
tamobhirāvṛte loke raṇe raktāsavākule । pramattairiva vetālaiḥ śibirāṇi yayurnṛpāḥ ।। saptamo yuddhadivasaḥ ।। bhīṣmeṇa sāgaravyūhe prātarviracite punaḥ ।
śṛṅgāṭakaṃ mahāvyūhaṃ cakre drupadanandanaḥ ।। vidīrṇeṣviva sainyeṣu bhīṣmacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ । babhūvābhimukhaḥ kopādeka eva vṛkodaraḥ ।। sa hatvā sārathiṃ bāṇaistūrṇaṃ śantanujanmanaḥ ।
droṇasya ca samudbhrāntapatākaṃ vidadhe ratham ।। labdhalakṣyastato bhīmaḥ sapta duryodhanānujān । jaghāna madasaṃrabdhānpañcānana iva dvipān ।। bahvāśinaṃ kuṇḍadhāraṃ viśālākṣaṃ sudurjayam ।
mahodaraṃ maṇḍitakaṃ sunābhaṃ ca nihatya tān ।। vidrāvya kauravacamūṃ nanādāsphālayandiśaḥ । kṣayāya sarvajagatāṃ devai rudra ivoditaḥ ।। irāvānatha vikrānto viveśa kuruvāhinīm ।
ulūpī nāgalalanā phalgunādyamajījanat ।। kāryaṃ samārasāhāyyaṃ svayamityarjunena saḥ । uktaḥ purā surapure tāṃ yuddhabhuvamāyayau ।। ratnakāñcanasaṃnāhaiḥ sa pātālaturaṅgamaiḥ ।
uhyamānaḥ śaraiścakre phaṇilokamivāparam ।। sa gatvā vipulānīkāngāndhārānhayayodhinaḥ । śakunestanayānsapta jaghāna ghanavikramān ।। tato duryodhanādiṣṭo māyāvī rākṣasādhipaḥ ।
alambusaḥ samabhyāyādirāvantaṃ raṇotkaṭaḥ ।। irāvanatha khaṅgena chittvā sapadi rakṣasaḥ । sa niṣaṅgaṃ dhanurdīptaṃ nanāda balināṃ varaḥ ।। tato māyāṃ samāśritya mahatīṃ mohanīṃ nṛṇām ।
yuyudhāte samāviśya tau nabho bhīmavikramau ।। irāvatā nijāstraughairhanyamānasya rakṣasaḥ । ghoraḥ samudabhūnnādaḥ sarvaprāṇibhayaṃkaraḥ ।। atha sāhāyyakaṃ cakrurbhujaṅgā bhujagībhuvaḥ ।
tadvamanto viṣaṃ tīkṣṇaṃ bhogānbhogabhṛtāṃ varāḥ ।। rākṣaso atha bhṛśaṃ kruddho rūpamāsthāya gāruḍam । bhakṣayitvākhilānsarpānbhīmaṃ svaṃ vapurādade ।। māyāvimohitasyātha khaṅgenārādirāvataḥ ।
jahāra rākṣasaṃ kāyācchirastalakuṇḍalam ।। hate dhanaṃjayasute haiḍambaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ । rurāva yena vasudhā cacāla sakulācalā ।। tamabhidrutamālokya rājā duryodhanaḥ svayam ।
saha sarvairnijānīkairmahāmāyamayodhayat ।। vidyujjihvaṃ vegavantaṃ mahāraudraṃ pramāthinam । haiḍimbānucarānghorānsa jaghāna niśācarān ।। śaktiṃ ghaṭotkacenātha preritāṃ kurubhubhūje ।
mahāgajena jagrāha vaṅgānāmadhipaḥ puraḥ ।। nāge nipatite tasminrakṣite ca suyodhane । saṃhāraṃ purusainyānāṃ cakāra piśitāśanaḥ ।। bhagadatto atha vidrāvya pāṇḍavānāmanīkinīm ।
supratīkena nāgena ghaṭotkacamayodhayat ।। tanayaṃ nihataṃ śrutvā kupitaḥ śatamanyujaḥ । śirobhirbhūmipālānāṃ durgamāṃ vasudhāṃ vyadhāt ।। bhīmo api krodhasaṃtapto bhrātuḥ putre nipātite ।
suyodhanānujānvīrānprāhiṇodyamamandiram ।। anādhṛṣṭiṃ kuṇḍalinaṃ kuṇḍabhediṃ sulocanam । virāṭaṃ dīrghabāhuṃ ca subāhuṃ kanakadhvajam ।। hatvaitānkauravānīkaṃ kabandhaśatasaṃkulam ।
vidadhe mattavetālanandane dinasaṃkṣaye ।। visrastacāpakavace bhagnasyandanakuñjare । raṇe avahāraṃ sainyānāṃ tataścakrurmahārathāḥ ।। aṣṭame yuddhadivase irāvadvadhaḥ ।।
tato niśāyāmanujaiḥ saha rājā suyodhanaḥ । karmamānāyya pārthānāṃ parābhavamacintayat ।। vaikartanastamavadatkriyatāṃ madvacaḥ sakhe । śastraṃ nyāsaya gāṅgeyamahaṃ jeṣyāmi pāṇḍavān ।।
eṣa vṛddho nirīhaśca sapakṣaśca dhanaṃjaye । tvayā nyasto atibhāro asminnavicāryaiva kevalam ।। etadākarṇya karṇoktaṃ harṣātkarmaśatairiva । utthāya bhīṣmaśibiraṃ pratasthe bhrātṛbhiḥ saha ।।
maṇidīpasahasrāṃśupiṅgīkṛtadigantaraḥ । naktaṃ dīptauṣadhivanaḥ sakulādririvābabhau ।। ratnakuṇḍalakeyūrakirīṭadyutinirjitāḥ । puro niṣpratibhā dīpāstasyāsaṃllajjitā iva ।।
praṇatāndṛktrimodāraiḥ bhūmipālānvilokayan । nāmabhirvikrabhāgena sūcitānvetrimaṇḍalaiḥ ।। sa babhau gatilolena hāreṇa tuhinātviṣā । sudhākallolajālena pādadāreṇa manmathaḥ ।।
śrīmānsaṃprāpya śibiraṃ śubhraṃ śantanujanmanaḥ । śayānaṃ ratnaparyaṅke praṇanāma vilokya tam ।। rājñeti pūjitastena kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ । duryodhanaḥ kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā pitāmahamabhāṣata ।।
ayaṃ jetā bhṛgubhuvaḥ kārmukapramayī tava । bhujastrailokyavijaye paryāpta iti me matiḥ ।। kāruṇyādānṛśaṃsyādvā rakṣyāste yadi pāṇḍavāḥ । tatkarṇamanujānīhi yuddhāya raṇakarkaśam ।।
ityuktaḥ kururājena marmaṇīva samāhataḥ । prabhāte drakṣyasītyuktvā niḥśvasankṣmāmalokayat ।। kauravo api tamāmantrya nijaṃ śibiramāyayau । diśaḥ śabalayankṣiptaṃ dīpadīptaurvibhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।
atha prabhāte bhīṣmeṇa droṇadrauṇimukhaiḥ saha । vihite sarvatobhadre vyūhe vyūhāgravartinā ।। prativyūheṣvanīkeṣu nadadbhiḥ pāṇḍunandanaiḥ । abhimanyuḥ kurucamūragre vīro vyadārayat ।।
śarāṃśuśataduṣprekṣyaṃ nidāghārkamivodyatam । na sehire taṃ bhūpālā māninaḥ saṃhatā api ।। duryodhanaprerito atha rakṣaḥpatiralambusaḥ । tamabhyadhāvadbibhrāṇo māyāṃ trailokyamohinīm ।।
tasya nādena mahatā jagatpralayaśaṃsinā । nipetuḥ sahasā yodhā bahavo vigatāsavaḥ ।। draupadeyaiḥ puraḥ prāptaiḥ sa vidhāya raṇaṃ kṣaṇam । abhimanyuradhaṃ bāṇaiḥ samaṃ dehamivākarot ।।
śaranirdāritenātha vihitāṃ tena rakṣasā । saubhadrastāmasīṃ māyāṃ cicchedārkāstratejasā ।। atha drauṇiprabhṛtibhiḥ sātyakipramukhā yudhi । saṃsaktā gaganaṃ cakrurdivyāstradahanākulam ।।
arjuno droṇamabhyetya mahāstragrāmaduḥsaham । vāyavyāstreṇa vidadhe jagatāṃ kṣokṣavibhramam ।। samudīrya ca śailāstraṃ drauṇena kṣapite anale । dhanaṃjayaḥ kurucamūṃ śarajālairapūrayat ।।
bhīmabhīmagadāghātanirbhinne gajamaṇḍale । susrāva śoṇitanadī patākāphenamālinī ।। tasminnākulasaṃgrāme vartamāne bhayaṃkare । vetāladattatāleṣu nṛtyatsu cchinnamūrdhasu ।।
bhīṣmaḥ pṛthuśarajvālāduḥsahaḥ subhaṭendhanaḥ । jajvāla cāpakreṅkāramantrapūta ivānalaḥ ।। tadbhujapreritāḥ kṣipraṃ sāyakā viviśurnupān । vihaṅgā iva sāyāhne ghanacchāyānmahīruhān ।।
khadyotā iva vṛkṣeṣu śalabhā iva śāliṣu । bhīṣmabāṇā narendreṣu peturhaṃsāḥ sahaḥsviva ।। nikṛttaiścāmaroṣṇīṣaiśchannāśca pṛthivībhujām । cakāra samare bhīṣmaḥ svayaśoviṣadā diśaḥ ।।
rājñāṃ śirobhiḥ pṛthivīmāstīrya pulakojjvalaḥ । raṇalakṣmyāḥ sa vidadhe kelipadmākarāniva ।। śirastraśaranirgharṣajātā vahnikaṇā babhuḥ । rājñāṃ hatānāṃ bhīṣmeṇa jīvā iva nabhaścarāḥ ।।
ghanena śarajālena grastā lokena sarvataḥ । sa cakre sarvasainyānāmakaṇḍarajanībhramam ।। vidīrṇe pāṇḍavabale chinnavarmarathadhvaje । gajānīkeṣu bhagneṣu bhāghaśeṣeṣu rājasu ।।
lajjāmutsṛjya yāteṣu tyaktacāpeṣu keśavaḥ । satyasaṃdhaṃ raṇe bhīṣmaṃ jahītyarjunamabravīt ।। dhanaṃjayo atha niḥśvasya viṣaṇṇavadanāmbujaḥ । nindanmuhuḥ kṣattradharmaṃ pitāmahamupādravat ।।
dṛṣaṭvā gāṇḍīvadhanvānamudyataṃ śaravarṣiṇam । bale tūrṇamupāvṛtte punaryuyudhire bhaṭāḥ ।। bhīṣmacāpacyutairbāṇaiśchāditaṃ vīkṣya phalguṇam । rathamutsṛjya kaṃsāristamadhāvadbhujāyudhaḥ ।।
vilokya kupitaṃ bhīṣmaḥ svayaṃ kṛṣmamabhidrutam । uvāca dhanyatāmānī pulakālaṃkṛtākṛtiḥ ।। puṇyabhājāmahaṃ dhuryo bhagavankṛtināṃ varaḥ । yasya tvaṃ jagatāṃ nātho vadhāya svayamudyataḥ ।।
iti vādini gāṅgeye rathāttūrṇaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ । avaruhya tataḥ kṛṣṇamānināya rathaṃ punaḥ ।। athārjunaśarāsārairākīrṇe kurukānane । punaḥ śāntanavaścakre saṃhāraṃ pṛthivībhujām ।।
ghore vyatikare tasminbhagne subhaṭamaṇḍale । avahāramakurvanta dinānte pāṇḍunandanāḥ ।। navamo yuddhadivasaḥ ।। tato rājanyāṃ vijane dharmarājo janārdanam ।
jagāda rājakaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhinnaṃ bhīṣmeṇa duḥkhitaḥ ।। paśya kṛṣṇa prabuddhena gāṅgeyavaḍavāgninā । sainyāmbudhiraparyante mama nīto alpaśeṣatām ।। maṇḍalīkṛtacāpasya sahasrāṃśuśatatviṣaḥ ।
bhīṣmasyākhaṇḍalopyagre satyaṃ paribhāvāspadam ।। alaṃ rājyena me tāvaditi vādini dharmaje । uvāca śauriryotsye ahaṃ svayaṃ śantanunandanam ।। nākārya me bhavatkāryamutsṛṣṭasamayo adhunā ।
pālayāmi raṇe bhīṣmaṃ paśyatāṃ jagatībhujām ।। etadākarṇya kṛṣṇoktaṃ babhāṣe pāṇḍavāgrajaḥ । na mithyāvādinaṃ kāmāttvāṃ kuryāmahamacyuta ।। jayopāyamito gatvā bhīṣmaṃ pṛcchāmi bhūtale ।
sa hi māmāśiṣā pūrvaṃ vātsalyātsamayojayat ।। iti niścitya kṛṣṇena bhrātṛbhiśca sahāśu kṛt । jagāma bhīṣmaśibiraṃ gūḍhacārī yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। sa pramamyānujasakhaḥ śauryarāśiṃ pitāmaham ।
papraccha vijayopāyaṃ sa ca pṛṣṭastamabravīt ।। na taṃ paśyāmi lokeṣu vīro māṃ vijayeta yaḥ । jayalābhe ca yuṣmākaṃ mayi jīvati kā kathā ।। na viśastrena saṃtraste na strīpūrve mameṣavaḥ ।
patanti tasmātklīvena māṃ ghātaya śikhaṇḍinā ।। ukte devavrateneti lajjāvinamitānanaḥ । akāma iva duḥkhena yayau svaśibiraṃ nṛpaḥ ।। tataḥ prabhāte vyūheṣu sainyeṣu subhaṭairmithaḥ ।
śikhaṇḍipramukhā vīrā parānīkamupādravan ।। tato bhīṣmaśaraśreṇīlulite rājamaṇḍale । śikhaṇḍī dhutakodaṇḍaścaṇḍakopastamabhyadhāt ।। tamabravīcchāntanavaḥ kāmaṃ prahara pārṣata ।
nanāma bhīṣmaviśikhāḥ patantyanujane jane ।। iti vādinamabhyetya maṇḍalīkṛtakārmukaḥ । śikhaṇḍī niḥśvasankopādāpageyamabhāṣata ।। jetāraṃ bhārgavasyāpi jānāmi tvāṃ mahaujasam ।
yudhi yudhyasva vā mā vā na me jīvangamiṣyasi ।। uktvaitadbāṇajālena pārṣataḥ samapūrayat । rakṣyamāṇaḥ samabhyetya paścādgāṇḍīvadhanvanā ।। bhīṣmo api tamanādṛtya viddhvā kṛṣṇārjunau śaraiḥ ।
viveśa pāṇḍavacamūṃ rājaveṇuvanānalaḥ ।। dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhairvīraiḥ kauravāṇāṃ tarasvinām । dāruṇo atha prahāro abhūdrajaḥpihitadiḍbhukhaḥ ।। tato droṇiprabhṛtayo vīrā droṇasya śāsanāt ।
rakṣantaḥ samare bhīṣmaṃ dhanaṃjayamayodhayan ।। tataḥ śāntanavo rājñāṃ śarairaśanigauravaiḥ । mauliratnāṃśuśabalaṃ samunmathya virocanam ।। ākrīḍamiva kālasya vidhāya kadanaṃ raṇe ।
abravītkūṇitamanā dūrādeva yudhiṣṭhiram ।। vadhāya kuru kaunteya yatnaṃ me nṛpatikṣayāt । viṣaṇṇo ahaṃ bhṛśaṃ putra raudreṇānena karmaṇā ।। iti vādini gāṅgeye śithilīkṛtakārmuke ।
sṛñjayāḥ saha pāñcālaiḥ somakaiśca sahādravan ।। tataḥ kurucamūvīrāḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ mahārathān । āvārya bhīṣmarakṣāyai dvandvaṃ yuddhāni cakrire ।। atha gāṅgeyaviśikhairaprayatnojjhitairapi ।
avartata mahāraudro rājajīvitasaṃkṣayaḥ ।। tamabhyadhāvadākarṇākṛṣṭakodaṇḍalaḥ । śikhaṇḍī khaṇḍaparaśuprabhāvaṃ phalguṇeritaḥ ।। svayaṃ duryodhanenātha preritāṃ vīkṣya vāhinīm ।
tasminsvabhaṭasaṃhāre vartamāne pitāmahaḥ ।। udīrya ghoraṃ divyāstramabhyadhāvaddhanaṃjayam । athārjunasyāgrametya śikhaṇḍini puraḥsthite ।। vimānā iva gāṅgeyo mahāstraṃ saṃjahāra tat ।
brahmalokābikāmeṣu yudhyamāneṣu rājasu ।। vīrāṇāṃ bhīṣmaviśikhairayuteṣu patatsu ca । dārayantaṃ parānīkaṃ tametya vasavo abruvan ।। bhīṣma saṃnyāsakālo ayaṃ tavāsmadabhikāṅkṣitaḥ ।
tataḥ ślathodyame tasminprasanne bhuvanatraye ।। arjunapramukhāḥ sarve sāyakaistamapūrayan । chidyamāneṣu bāleṣu tasya tūrṇaṃ kirīṭinā ।। śikhaṇḍī prāhiṇottasmai hemapuṅkhaśarāvalīm ।
śaikhaṇḍīṃ śaramālāṃ tāṃ śairoṣīmiva peśalām ।। jagrāha prahasanbhīṣmaḥ kṣaṇaṃ sthagitakārmukaḥ । duryodhanasamādiṣṭānbhīṣmasya ratharakṣiṇaḥ ।। mohayanbāṇajālena phalguṇastamavākirat ।
vidāryamāṇo nīrandhrairgāṇḍīvānniḥsṛtaiḥ śaraiḥ ।। duḥśāsanaṃ pārśvagataṃ bhīṣmaḥ sasmitamabravīt । naite śikhaṇḍino bāṇāḥ śilāsaṃghātabhedinaḥ ।। viśanti mama marmāṇi bilaṃ viṣadharā iva ।
ete te vajrasaṃsparśā nivātakavacacchidaḥ ।। śarīrahāriṇo ghorāḥ kirātaraṇasākṣiṇaḥ । ityuktvā pāṇḍuputrāya śaktiṃ cikṣepa śaktimān ।। tāṃ ca śakrasutastūrṇaṃ cakāra viśikhaistridhā ।
sarvāyudheṣu cchinneṣu tato gāṇḍīvadhanvanā ।। kṣaṇādbabhūva durlakṣyo bhīṣmo nirvivaraiḥ śaraiḥ । yudhyamāneṣu vīreṣu bhūtāviṣṭeṣvivākulam ।। dārume tumule tasminnirvibhāge baladvaye ।
aparāhṇe rathādbhīṣmaḥ sahasrāṃśurivāparaḥ ।। aspṛṣṭabhūmirviśikhaiḥ papāta mahasāṃ nidhiḥ । tasminnipatite vīre ketau sarvadhanuṣmatām ।। mahatāmapi vīrāṇāṃ hṛdayāni cakampire ।
tato nivṛtte saṃgrāme hāhākāre nabhaḥspṛśiḥ ।। divyaṃ bheje nijaṃ bhāvamaluptātmā pitāmahaḥ । ākampamāne bhuvane vāguvācāśarīriṇī ।। bhīṣma kālaṃ pratīkṣasva yogavānuttarāyaṇam ।
sarvajña dhāraya prāṇānsvacchandanidhano hṛdi ।। śrutvaitatparamaṃ yogamāsasāda suravrataḥ । tatastridaśavāhinyā visṛṣṭa haṃsarūpiṇaḥ ।। tamevārthaṃ samabhyetya munayo bhīṣmamabruvan ।
sthito asmīti ca gāṅgeyo nigadya yaśasāṃ nidhiḥ ।। iratalpe gataḥ sarvānkurūnbhītānasāntvayat । praṇatānatha saṃprāptānpunaḥ kauravapāṇḍavān ।। aśrupūrṇekṣaṇānūce saṃbhāvya kurupuṃgavaḥ ।
dhāraṇaṃ lambamānasya śiraso me vidhīyatām ।। śrutvaitadupadhāneṣu samānīteṣu rājabhiḥ । jagrāha śāsanāttasya tribhiḥ pārthaḥ śaraiḥ śiraḥ ।। bhīṣmastatkarmatuṣṭo atha praśaśaṃsa dhanaṃjayam ।
pāṇḍavaiḥ kriyatāṃ saṃdhirityuvāca ca kauravam ।। daśamo yuddhadivasaḥ ।। tato rajanyāṃ yātāyāmupāviṣṭeṣu rājasu । sevyamāno munijanairbhīṣmo jalamayācata ।।
maṇikāñcanacitreṣu kalaśeṣvamalāmbhasaḥ । samānīteṣu bhūpālairvyadhānmeghāstramarjunaḥ ।। tadudbhūtena payasā gāṅgeyastena tarpitaḥ । narāvatāraṃ prītātmā sādaraṃ tamapūjayat ।।
mahāratheṣu yāteṣu samāmantryāpagāsutam । karṇaḥ prasādayāmāsa tadabhyarcya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। tamuvāca prasannātmā vītamanyuḥ pitāmahaḥ । bhajasva pārtheṣu śamaṃ vīrāste bhrātarastava ।।
vaikartanastadākarṇya jagāda vinatānanaḥ । jāne sarvamavaśyaṃ tu bhavitavyamidaṃ prabho ।। kiṃtu duryodhanasyārthe suhṛdo mānakāriṇaḥ । anujānīhi māṃ tāta samarāya samudyatam ।।
iti bruvāṇo bhīṣmeṇa so anujñāto varūthinīm । prayayau kuruputrāṇāṃ rathena ghananādinā ।। atha kuruvṛṣabāṇāmaṅgarājotsukānāṃ paraparibhavadīkṣābhagnamānādarāṇām । patihitamanīkaṃ sāmyamāpa drutānāṃ sarayapavanapānīkampitānāṃ vanānām ।।
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। suravrataṃ hataṃ śrutvā dhṛtarāṣṭro atiduḥkhitaḥ । muhurmuhuryaśorāśiṃ tamaśocadariṃdamam ।।
punaḥ saṃgrāmamālokya samāyāto atha saṃjayaḥ । pṛṣṭo vaicitravīryeṇa vīrasaṃhāramabhyadhāt ।। tato bhīṣmehate rājankuravo bhṛśaduḥkhitāḥ । abdhau bhagne pravahaṇe vaṇijaḥ patitā iva ।।
vāñchitaṃ samare śarma dadṛśuḥ karṇamāgatam । vikrītāḥ paradeśeṣu snigdhaṃ bandhumivāpadi ।। tato duryodhanaḥ śokaṃ saṃstambhya dhṛtisāgaraḥ । karṇasyānumate cakre droṇaṃ senāsu nāyakam ।।
tenābhiṣikto vidhivadguruḥ sarvadhanuṣmatām । sa babhau śaktimānvīro mahāsena ivāparaḥ ।। vṛddhasya svayaśaḥśubhraṃ chattraṃ tasya vyarocata । dugdhodadheriva śrīmaccandramaṇḍalamudyatam ।।
āmuktahemakavacaḥ sa dīptaḥ kiraṇairbabhau । upasthitaiḥ kṛtyakāle divyāstrairiva sevitaḥ ।। praṇetā sarvavīrāṇāṃ sadṛśaḥ prājyatejasā । sākṣādiva dhanurvedaḥ saṃhārasyāgamāvadhiḥ ।।
reje rathena raukmena śoṇāśvena patākinā । saṃdhyājuṣā nirjhariṇā meruṇeva divākaraḥ ।। virarāja rathe tasya śātakaumbhaḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ । śauryoṣmaṇā pratigataḥ pratāpa iva piṇḍitaḥ ।।
ākarṇapalitaḥ śyāmo dhaureyaḥ sarvadhanvinām । dadau varaṃ śriyā juṣṭaḥ sa rājñā svayamarthitaḥ ।। jīvagrāhaṃ samādāya rājānaṃ te yudhiṣṭhiram । haterjune pradāsyāmi paśyatāṃ sarvabhubhujām ।।
etadguruvaco rājā pratigṛhya kṛtāñjaliḥ । viśrāvya nijasenāsu tūryanādotsavaṃ vyadhāt ।। tacca dharmasuto jñātvā saha gāṇḍīvadhanvanā । krauñcavyūhaṃ samādhāya saṃnaddho yoddhumudyayau ।।
dromena śakaṭavyūhe nirmite bhṛśasaṃhate । avartata mahadyuddhaṃ vīrāṇāṃ dehaśātanam ।। tataḥ sṛñjayapāñcālamatsyasenāsu duḥsahāḥ । śarīrahāriṇaḥ peturdreṇanāmāṅkitāḥ śarāḥ ।।
bhidyamāneṣu sainyeṣu nipatadgajavājiṣu । raktakallolinīvegairnīteṣu syandaneṣvapi ।। yudhiṣṭhiramukhānvīrānkopāddroṇamabhidrutān । avārayansusaṃrabdhāndroṇikarṇakṛpādayaḥ ।।
abhimanyurathākṛṣya rathātkeśeṣu pauravam । apātayatkṛpāṇena paśyatāṃ sarvadhanvinām ।। tatkopātkhaṅgamādāya jayadrathamupāgatam । śalyaṃ ca virathaṃ vīro vidadhe balināṃ varam ।।
tataḥ śalyo gadāpāṇiḥ padbhyāṃ saubhadramādravat । gadayā vīravārinyā bhīmaśca tamavārayat ।। tayoḥ parasparāghātakīrṇavahnikaṇākulam । nṛṇāṃ vimohanaṃ ghoraṃ gadāyuddhamavartata ।।
maṇḍalāni carantau tau samadāviva kuñjarau । abhipatya padānyaṣṭau gadābhyāṃ jaghnaturmithaḥ ।। gāḍhaprahārasaṃjātamūrchāvihvalamānasau । tau dṛṣṭvā patitau vīrāḥ saṃnipetuḥ prahāriṇaḥ ।।
nīte madrādhipe tūrṇaṃ rathena kṛtavarmaṇā । bhīmasenaḥ samādāya kurusenāmadārayat ।। karṇasūnoratha śarairdṛṣasenasya pāṇḍavāḥ । ākīrṇāndraupadīputrānvilokya tamupādravan ।।
tato rukmaratho droṇaḥ svayaṃ pāñcālavāhinīm । praviśya bāṇairvidadhe viprakīrṇāṃ sahasradhā ।। śikhaṇḍisātyakimukhānsa vidārya mahārathān । yudhiṣṭhiramabhiprekṣuḥ kurvannarapatikṣayam ।।
yugaṃdharaṃ vyāghradattaṃ sihasenaṃ ca pārthivam । nināya mṛtyusadana śarairaśanidāruṇaiḥ ।। tiṣṭha sthito aha yuddhasva hato asīti muhurmuhuḥ । droṇāgre yudhyamānānāṃ bhūbhujāmabhavadraṇaḥ ।।
droṇena yudhyamānānāṃ niśamya śvetavāhanaḥ । kolāhalaṃ svasainyānāṃ tūrṇaṃ taṃ deśamāyayau ।। sa nihatyāstrajālena vīraḥ kuruvarūthinīm । vidadhe raktataṭinīmāvartahṛtakuñjarām ।।
tato avahāraṃ sainyānāṃ pārthasāyakapīḍitāḥ । yāte astaṃ tigmakiraṇe cakrire kurupuṃgavāḥ ।। droṇābhiṣekaḥ prathamo yuddhadivasaśca ।। niśāyāṃ saṃniviṣṭeṣu śibire sarvarājasu ।
lajjamāna ivācāryo duryodhanamabhāṣata ।। uktameva mayā rājanrahitaṃ savyasācinā । yudhiṣṭhiraṃ grahīṣyāmi durjayo hi dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। iti bruvāṇe vailakṣyādācārye rājasaṃnidhau ।
trigarvarājaḥ provāca kṛtavairaḥ kirīṭinā ।। vayaṃ saṃśaptakagaṇairmālavaistuṇḍilaistathā । vīrairmadrakakāmbojalalitaiśca prahāribhiḥ ।। rathāyutaistribhiḥ pārthamāhūya pṛthagāsthitaḥ ।
yotsyāmahe suprakṛtairiti satyaṃ śapāmahe ।। ityukte śapathaṃ kṛtvā trigartā vahnisākṣiṇaḥ । pratyūṣe niryayurvīrāḥ suśarmapramukhā nṛpāḥ ।। te turaṅgakharoddhūtadhūligrastanabhastalāḥ ।
cakrire phalguṇāhvānaṃ nādaiḥ pralayaśaṃsibhiḥ ।। tānvyūhenārdhacandreṇa same deśe vyavasthitān । dṛṣṭvā pārthastadāhūto yudhiṣṭhiramabhāṣata ।। anujānātu māmāryastrigartānāṃ vadhaṃ prati ।
ete māmabhivāñcanti yoddhuṃ saṃgharṣaśālinaḥ ।। ayaṃ te satyajidvīraḥ pāñcālyaḥ pravaro rathaḥ । goptā droṇābhisaraṇe śakratulyaparākramaḥ ।। ityuktvā caṇḍagāṇḍīvaghoṣaghaṇṭitadiktaṭaḥ ।
pralayāmbhodasaṃrabdhastānyayau kapiketanaḥ ।। te api pāṇḍavamāyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā pramadanirbharāḥ । phullasālamivādṛśyaṃ cakruḥ kṣipraṃ śilīmukhaiḥ ।। tataḥ śauryāmbudheḥ phenamaṭṭahāsaṃ raṇaśriyaḥ ।
dadhmau dhanaṃjayaḥ śaṅkhaṃ kandaṃ nijayaśastaroḥ ।। tasya śabdena mahatā tatsainyaṃ bhayakāriṇā । abhūnnivṛttamātaṅgaṃ stimitāṅgaturaṅgamam ।। atha sāyakajālena jīvamatsyāpahāriṇā ।
trigartavāhinīṃ pārthaḥ samantātparyavārayat ।। tataḥ saṃśaptakagaṇotsṛṣṭairavivaraiḥ śaraiḥ । pihite bhuvanābhoge babhūvākālaśarvarī ।। tataḥ pravidadhe tvāṣṭraṃ mahāstraṃ vajrinandanaḥ ।
yenārjunasahasrāṇi dadṛśuste sasaṃbhramāḥ ।। jahārākarṇakṛṣṭena bhallena ca mahaujasaḥ । sphuranmauliprabhājālaṃ śiraḥ kāyātsudhanvanaḥ ।। tatpreṣitāṃ śastravṛṣṭiṃ pavanāstreṇa hāriṇā ।
vidhūya tacchiraḥpuñjairadṛśyāṃ vidadhe mahīm ।। chinnacchattradhvajarathaṃ patadbhujabhaṭānanam । trigartakadanaṃ pārtho ghoramāyodhanaṃ vyadhāt ।। saṃśaptakayuddham ।।
asminkṣaṇe vainateyavyūhe droṇena nirmite । vyūhena nirmitārdhena pāṇḍuputrāḥ samudyayuḥ ।। tataḥ pravṛtte saṃgrāme kṣaye caiva mahībhujām । dhṛṣṭadyumnaprabhṛtayo droṇamukhyānayodhayan ।।
rajobhiḥ pihite vyomni dikṣu ruddhāsu sāyakaiḥ । avibhāgamamaryādaṃ ghoraṃ yuddhamavartata ।। abhidrute tato droṇe dharmarājajighṛkṣayā । ghoro halahalāśabdaḥ sainyānāmudabhūtkṣaṇam ।।
kālāgnitejasaṃ vīraṃ dhaureyaṃ sarvadhanvinām । avārayitumabhyetya satyajitsatyavikramaḥ ।। yudhyamānaṃ tato hatvā vṛkaṃ rājasutaṃ guruḥ । śaraiḥ satyajitaṃ cakre kīrṇāṃśumiva bhāskaram ।।
hemanāmāṅkitairbāṇairmuhūrtādatha satyajit । dīptairapūrayaddroṇaṃ khadyotairiva pādapam ।। tataḥ satyajitaḥ kāyādācāryaḥ śauryaśālinaḥ । śiro jahāra bhallena caṇḍatāṇḍavakuṇḍalam ।।
nipātite satyajiti pravare sarvadhanvinām । vidrute dharmatanaye vyadīryate varūthinī ।। satyajidvadhaḥ ।। hṛtvānujaṃ virāṭasya śatānīkaṃ prahāriṇam ।
dṛḍhasenaṃ kṣatradevaṃ vasudānaṃ ca pārthivam ।। nighnanrukmarathaścedimatsyapāñcālasṛñjayān । vidadhe rudhirāvartaiḥ kṛtāntodyānavāhinīm ।। vidrute pāṇḍavabale pīḍite droṇasāyakaiḥ ।
karṇaduryodhanamukhā bhāradvājamapūjayan ।। punarāvartite sainye bhīmena bhujaśālinā । saṃhatāḥ pṛthivīpālāḥ kopāddroṇamupādravan ।। ṛṣyavarṇairhayairbhīmaḥ sātyakiḥ sphāṭikaprabhaiḥ ।
pārāvataprabhaiścāśvairdhṛṣṭadyumnaścamūpatiḥ ।। nakulaḥ sahadevaśca śukatittirisaprabhaiḥ । abhimanyuḥ piśaṅgābhaiḥ pāṇḍyaiśca tuhinaprabhaiḥ । dantaprabhaiḥ kṛṣṇavālaiḥ svayaṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।।
anye tu vividhacchāyaiścitravarmāmbaradhvajaiḥ । parivārya raṇe droṇaṃ cakrurbāṇamayaṃ jagat ।। mṛdaṅganādakau rājño dhvajo nandopanandakau । divyayantreṇa vihitau babhaturdharmajanmanaḥ ।।
dharmānilendrāśvināṃ ca pratimā draupadībhuvām । tumule yudhyamānānāṃ rejire kāñcanojjvalāḥ ।। āvṛtaṃ droṇamālokya rājabhiḥ krūrayā dhiyā । duryodhanādayo vīrānbhīmamukhyānsamāpatan ।।
teṣu śalyapradhāneṣu yudhiṣṭhirapurogamaiḥ । dvandvaddhaniṣakteṣu samarotsavarājiṣu ।। kṛtabāhau subāhau ca hate vīre yuyutsunā । vaṅgarāje samātaṅge bhīmasenena pātite ।।
vidrute kauravabale nihateṣvabhimāniṣu । nirālokeṣu lokeṣu rajastimiramaṇḍalaiḥ ।। prerito bhagadattena saṃvartakaghanaprabhaḥ । supratīko madoddāmaḥ pāṇḍusenāṃ vyagāhata ।।
daityasaṃgrāmasāhāyye jambhāribhavanasthitaḥ । airāvaṇaghaṭābandhaḥ pramāṇaṃ yasya varṣmamaḥ ।। śaśiśubhrairnakhairudyādekapātsa kṣaṇaṃ babhau । svamahīpīḍanaruṣā daṣṭaḥ seṣaśatairiva ।।
itaścandrārkamukhyānāṃ prabhavaḥ sarvatejasām । iti nakṣatramālābhirudayādririvāśritaḥ ।। digvāraṇaraṇāvāptiṃ vinā vyarthamidaṃ balam । itīva pṛthuśūtkārairniḥśaśvāsa madālasaḥ ।।
etā āyāntu vaiklavyaṃ matpratāpoṣmaṇā diśaḥ । itīva karṇatālābhyāṃ muhurmuhuravījayat ।। caṇḍīśaḍamaroccaṇḍaḍiṇḍimadhvānaniḥsvanaiḥ । helayonmīlayankiṃcillocane pracacāla saḥ ।।
bhagadattāstraniṣkṛttavīravaktrāñcitāṃ mahīm । gatvā pade pade paśyansasmāra kamalākarān ।। sa vāhinīṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ praviśya nibiḍaṃ gajaḥ । gajavājiratānpiṃṣanvasākardaminīṃ vyadhāt ।।
mṛdyamānāḥ karīndreṇa tāḥ senāḥ kauravadviṣām । saṃkocamāpuḥ sahasā darpeṇeva vibhūtayaḥ ।। tena mandaratulyena gajenānīkavāridheḥ । samākrāntasya nistriṃśakālakūṭacchaṭā babhuḥ ।।
kuṇḍalīkṛtaśuṇḍāgraḥ so abhyadhāvadvṛkodaram । ākṛṣṭaṃ pāśahastena yena taṃ menire janāḥ ।। saṃśaye patitaṃ bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā tūrṇaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । saha sarvairmahīpālairbhagadattaṃ samabhyadhāt ।।
sa taiḥ parivṛto vīrairhatvā dāśārṇabhūpatim । unmamātha rathaṃ vegātsupratīkena sātyake ।। tasya śīkariṇā ghoraśītkṛtenātha dantinaḥ । bhīmasenamukhā dūraṃ jahrustrastāsturaṅgamān ।।
sā senā bhagadattena kuñjarasthena pīḍitā । janatā kṛnṛpeṇeva na lebhe śaraṇaṃ kvacit ।। gajānāṃ patyamānānāṃ rathānāṃ sphuṭatāmapi । hāhākāraiśca bhītānāṃ niḥsvanastumulo abhavat ।।
sveṣāmākrandamākarṇya vajrāstreṇendranandanaḥ । trigartānsānugānhatvā bhagadattamathāpatat ।। dṛṣṭvā gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ tārkṣyavattarṇamāgatam । prerito bhagadattena kruddho adāvaddvipādhipaḥ ।।
tamantakamivāyāntamapasavyena keśavaḥ । rathena moghasaṃrambhaṃ kṛtvā punarabhūtpuraḥ ।। viddhvā śarasahasreṇa pārthaṃ prāgjyotiṣeśvaraḥ । nārāyaṇāstramasṛjattacca jagrāha keśavaḥ ।।
arjunaṃ rakṣatastūrṇaṃ tadastraṃ kaiṭabhadviṣaḥ । niṣaktaṃ vakṣasi prāpa hemasragdāmavibhramam ।। tasminviphalatāṃ yāte mahāstre dīptatejasi । vailakṣyādarjunaḥ kṛṣṇamuvācāsphālayandhanuḥ ।।
nūnaṃ yuddheṣvayogyo ahaṃ yenāstraṃ dhṛtavānasi । śrutvaitadavadatpārthaṃ mānayangaruḍadhvajaḥ ।। caturmūrtimṛtā pūrvaṃ pṛthivīvacasā mayā । vitīrṇaṃ narakāyaitannijāstraṃ bhūmisūnave ।।
amoghamāptavāṃstasmāddetyātso asau narādhipaḥ । gṛhītaṃ tanmayā divyaṃ jahyenamadhunā nṛpam ।। ukte janārdaneneti savyasācī sakuñjaram । ūrdhvavaktraiḥ śaraiḥ kṣipraṃ bhagadattamapūrayat ।।
girivarṣma gajārūḍho bāṇaiḥ prāgjyotiṣeśvaraḥ । adūravidrutāmartyavimānamakaronnabhaḥ ।। tataḥ karṇāntakṛṣṭena kumbhayoḥ kuñjareśvaram । āpucchagāminā pārtho nārācenākulaṃ vyadhāt ।।
sa phalguṇeṣunirbhinnaḥ patindviradabhūdharaḥ । jaghāna mahītaṃ senāṃ patitāḥ pātayanti yat ।। kruddhastator'dhacandreṇa hṛdi viddhaḥ kirīṭinā । muktāṅkuśadhanurbāṇo bhagadatto abhavadvyasuḥ ।।
bhagadattavadhaḥ ।। tasminnipatite vīre kakude sarvabhūbhujām । vijaye kurusenānāmāśābandhaḥ ślatho abhavat ।। vidrute kauravānīke saubalau vṛṣakācalau ।
gāndhārau dhanvināṃ dhuryai dhanaṃjayamayudhyatām ।। tau bāṇavarṣiṇau pārthaśareṇaikena saṃhatau । syūtāvapātayatprītyā yāto bhāruṇḍatāmiva ।। vṛṣabhakācalavadhaḥ ।।
anujau nihatau dṛṣṭvā śakuniḥ kopakampitaḥ । kalpayanvipulāṃ māyāṃ savyasācināmādravat ।। astraiśca krūrasatvaiśca tamobhiścabhito vṛtaḥ । nākampata raṇe pārthastasya māyāśatairapi ।।
saureṇāstreṇa tanmāyāṃ chittvā kātaramohinīm । prāhiṇotsāyakānyena śakuniḥ prayayau bhayāt ।। yāter'junamayaṃ lokaṃ manyamāne atha saubale । na lebhe śaraṇaṃ trāsādvidrutā kuruvāhinī ।।
tato droṇaḥ sahānīkairyudhiṣṭhirajighṛkṣayā । haranvaktrāṇi vīrāṇāṃ pāñcālānsamupādravat ।। vadhyamāneṣvanīkeṣu śoṇāśvena sahasraśaḥ । raktāsavamadeneva cakampe vasudhāvadhūḥ ।।
tūrṇaṃ praharata droṇaṃ tūrṇaṃ rakṣata saṃgare । pāṇḍavānāṃ pareṣāṃ ca babhūveti mahādhvaniḥ ।। pāñcāleṣvatha bhagneṣu sṛñjayeṣu ca sarvataḥ । ayodhayatkurucamūṃ nīlo māhiṣmatīpatiḥ ।।
taṃ dahantamanīkāni divyāstrairvahnitejasam । pratyudyayau dhairyanidhirdraiṇireko dhanurdharaḥ ।। ācāryasūnustasyātha vajrasāreṣuvarṣiṇaḥ । chattraṃ dhvajaṃ kārmukaṃ ca bhallaiściccheda nirvyathaḥ ।।
avaruhya rathāttūrṇaṃ nīlaścitraparākramaḥ । kṛpāṇena śiro hartuṃ drauṇeḥ śyena ivāpatat ।। bhāradvājasutastasya bhallenojjvalakuṇḍalam । kāntaṃ śiro aharattārāyugayuktamivoḍupam ।।
nīlavadhaḥ ।। nīle hate pāṇḍavānāṃ bhagne subhaṭamaṇḍale । hatvā saṃśaptakānpārtho javārtāṃ bhuvamāyayau ।। bhīmaphalguṇasaubhadramatsyacaidyamukhaistataḥ ।
bhidyamāne parānīke niḥsvanastumulo abhavat ।। tataḥ karṇaprabhṛtibhisteṣāṃ samaraśālinām । ghoro babhūta saṃmardaḥ sarvalokabhayaṃkaraḥ ।। nirmaryāde raṇe tasminrūdhirāvartadustare ।
bhinnāṃ kurucamūṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ pārthamayodhayat ।। sor'junaṃ pāvakāstreṇa sātyakipramukhāṃstathā । cakāra ghoradigdāhapiṅgalāniva bhūdharān ।। tato dhanaṃjayamukhā hatvāstrairastramutkaṭam ।
karṇaṃ śaraśataiścakrurghanavetravanopamam ।। śatruṃjayaṃ vipāṭaṃ ca vīraṃ cāvarajaṃ śaraiḥ । karṇānujānyamapuraṃ prāhiṇotkapiketanaḥ ।। karṇānujavadhaḥ ।।
atha droṇamukhāḥ sarve kauravāṇāṃ mahārathāḥ । karṇapārśvaṃ samājagmurdīptāstragrāmaduḥsahāḥ ।। te sātyakiprabhṛtibhiḥ saṃsaktā dhanvināṃ varāḥ । cakrire samaraṃ ghoraṃ gajavājirathakṣayam ।।
tator'junaśarāsārairbhinneṣu bhujaśāliṣu । vāsarānte nyavartanta pārthivā bhṛśapīḍitāḥ ।। dvītīyo yuddhadivasaḥ ।। tataḥ prātaḥ samabhyetya guruṃ duryodhano abravīt ।
karṇayanbhṛśasaṃtaptaḥ pāṇḍavānāṃ parākramam ।। aho nu puṇyahīnasya bhavatāpi pratiśrutaḥ । vīro niṣphalatāṃ yāto dharmajagrahaṇe mama ।। śaktimanta- praṇayināmabhijātā yaśasvinaḥ ।
vṛthā manorathaṃ kartuṃ śikṣitā na bhavadvidhāḥ ।। śrutvā suyodhanenoktaṃ jagāda kalaśodbhavaḥ । durgrahyaḥ pāṇḍavo rājangupto gāṇḍīvadhanvanā ।। tathāpyadya karomyeṣa yathāśakti hitaṃ tava ।
saṃśaptakāḥ punaryāntu ratādākṛṣya phalguṇam ।। ācāryeṇeti gadite saṃśaptakagaṇāḥ punaḥ । samāhūyārjunaṃ ninyurdakṣiṇāśāṃ yuyutsavaḥ ।। rāmaśiṣyastato droṇaḥ kṣatriyakṣayadīkṣitaḥ ।
saṃsāracakradurbhedyaṃ cakravyūhaṃ vinirmame ।। arīṇāmayute tasminrājaputrāyutaṃ babhau । vyomanirjhariṇīsvacchapatākālaṃkṛtairbhujaiḥ ।। nābhimanye svaya śrīmānrājā tasthau suyodhanaḥ ।
gajānīkena mahatā vṛtaḥ sarvairmahārathaiḥ ।। jayadrathena sahito droṇo vyūhamukho abhavat । triṃśatā tridaśākaraistathā duryodhanānujaiḥ ।। tadapāraṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā vyūhaṃ vikramaśālibhiḥ ।
droṇanirdāritānīkaḥ pradadhyau dharmanandanaḥ ।। sa saubhadraṃ raṇe matvā kaṃsārisamavikramam । babhāṣe saṃnidhau rājñāṃ trailokyavijayakṣamam ।। abhimanyo tava pitā yātaḥ saṃśaptakānprati ।
tadvoḍhurmahasi dhuraṃ tvamimāṃ tadguṇādhikaḥ ।। kṛṣṇor'juno raukmiṇeyastvaṃ vā vajriparākramaḥ । pragalbhaḥ pañcamo nāsti cakravyūhavibhedine ।। śrutvaitadūce saubhadraḥ praharṣotphullalocanaḥ ।
eṣa vyūhaṃ vidāryādya praviśāmi tvadājñayā ।। nirgantumanabhijñaṃ māmanuyāntu mahārathāḥ । ukter'junasuteneti yudhiṣṭhiramukhairnṛpaiḥ ।। tathetyabhihite sūtaṃ saubhadraḥ samacodayat ।
sa muktaśaiśvo vīraḥ kesarīva trihāyanaḥ ।। manyamāno raṇamukhe varākaṃ sarvarājakam । kāntaḥ kankasaṃnāho baddhasvaṅgo vibhūṣitaḥ ।। kautukātkṣmāmivāyāto vīraḥ surakumārakaḥ ।
akaṭhoratarākāro vīro jaraṭhavikramaḥ ।। droṇānīkaṃ śaraiścakre kṣubhitāmbhodhivibhramam । tataḥ pravṛtte samare mahatāmapi mohane ।। vidārya vyūhamaviśatsaubhadrastīkṣṇavikramaḥ ।
lāghave sauṣṭhave citre yātamekamanekatām ।। dṛṣṭvā praviṣṭaṃ taṃ sarve kuruvīrāḥ samādravan । ayaṃ gṛhīto yāto ayaṃ hato ayaṃ hantyayaṃ bahūn ।। iti rājñāṃ ninādo abūdabhimanyurathaṃ prati ।
saratnamukuṭaiḥ śīrṣaiḥ saprāsāsiśaraiḥ karaiḥ ।। sahemakavacaiḥ kāyaiḥ sakeyūrāṅgadairbhujaiḥ । turaṅgaiḥ kṛttasāraṅgairbhinnakumbhaiśca kumbhibhiḥ ।। nipatadbhiraviśrāntaśchannāṃ cakre sa medinīm ।
vadhyamānaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā saubhadreṇa prahāriṇā ।। tamādravansasaṃrabdhāḥ drauṇikarṇakṛpādayaḥ । tānbāṇavarṣiṇo vīrānvidhāya vimukhāñśaraiḥ ।। śiro jahāra bhallena saubhadro aśmakabhūpateḥ ।
bhagne tato kurubale droṇakarṇakṛpāḥ punaḥ ।। drauṇihārdikyagāndhāraśaraśalyabṛhadbalāḥ । bhūribhūriśravaścitraduḥśāsanasuyodhanāḥ ।। anye cābhyetya bhūpālāḥ sāyakaistamavākiran ।
kṣipraiḥ śilīmukhaisteṣāṃ saṃcchannor'junanandanaḥ ।। vasantasamaye kāntaḥ karṇikāra ivābabhau । tasya pārthakumārasya kumārasyeva dānavāḥ ।। śaktyā śaktimato yuddhe nirjitāste pradudruvuḥ ।
madrarājānujaṃ hatvā sa tūrṇaṃ bhīmavikramam ।। karṇasya bhrātaraṃ śūraṃ jaghāna ghanagarjitam । krameṇaikaikaśo jitvā saṃhatāṃśca punaḥ punaḥ ।। karṇaduḥśāsanamukhānsa cakre bhūbhujāṃ kṣayam ।
parasainyāntarasthasya dikṣu sarvāsu bhūmipāḥ ।। hemacāpasahasrāṇi dadṛśustasya lāghavāt । gajavājirathānīke dārite tena pattribhiḥ ।। cāmaroṣṇīṣahāsāṅkā prasasarpāsravāhinī ।
utthiteṣu kabandheṣu bhagne subhaṭamaṇḍale ।। dadhmau pārthasutaḥ śaṅkhaṃ diśaḥ śakalayanniva । atrāntare pāṇḍusutānpraveṣṭuṃ vyūhamudyatān ।। avārayadbhargavarāddṛpto rājā jayadrathaḥ ।
sa kṛṣṇāharaṇe pūrvaṃ vijitastairmaheśvarāt ।। varaṃ tapaḥ kṛśo lebhe tajjayaṃ phalgumaṃ vinā । sa babhau pāṇḍutanayānvārayansapadānugān ।। velācala ivoddhūtānvārivegānmahodadheḥ ।
haimaṃ varāhaṃ bibhrāṇo dhvaje vaiśvānaraprabham ।। dadāha pāṇḍavacamūṃ saindhavo rudratejasā । tenaikena niruddheṣu prasabhaṃ pāṇḍusūnuṣu ।। abhimanyurviśanrājñāmuccakarta śirovanam ।
vṛṣasenaṃ sa vidrāvya vīro vaikartanātmajam ।। jahāra lulitoṣṇīṣaṃ kāmbojanṛpateḥ śiraḥ । tasminvimarde tumule dikṣu ruddhāsu pāṃsubhiḥ ।। asūcyanta mahīpālā ratnābharaṇaraśimabhiḥ ।
tato vijayadāyādaḥ kesarīva madadvipam ।। jagrāha satyaśravasaṃ rājānamatulaujasam । abhimanyorvaśaṃ yāte tasminbhūmibhṛtāṃ vare ।। śalyātmajo rukmarathastaṃ garjansamupādravat ।
sa teṣāṃ bhrukuṭīdhūmalakṣyakopāgnisaṃpadām ।। gāndharvāstreṇa sahasā vidadhe kīrtiśeṣatām । tena tulyavayoveśe rājaputraśate hate ।। rambhākāṇḍavane bhagne prabhinneneva dantinā ।
vidrute bhūbhujāṃ cakre bhagnāmānaḥ suyodhanaḥ ।। niḥśaśvāsa hriyā namraḥ saubhadraśaradāritaḥ । tato duryodhanasuto lakṣmaṇo lakṣmaṇopamaḥ ।। abhimanyuṃ samabhyetya prāhiṇodviśikhāvalīm ।
lakṣmīlatākisalayaṃ saṃbhogatarukandaram ।। taṃ rājaputraṃ saubhadraḥ kṣaṇaṃ tulyamayodhayat । tasya muktāvalītārāpaṅktisevitamānanam ।। śaśāṅkamiva bhallena kaṇṭhamūlājjahāra saḥ ।
kauravendrastataḥ kruddhaḥ priye putre nipātite ।। saubhadramādravadvīraḥ saha sarvairmahārathaiḥ । nṛpavaikartandroṇadrauṇihārdikyagautamān ।। śarairvidrāvya tarasā vṛndārakamapātayat ।
kopādāpatataḥ so atha kosalādhipateḥ śiraḥ ।। bṛhadbalasya ciccheda bhallenākulakuṇḍalam । tataḥ karṇamabhidrutya śarairaśanidāruṇaiḥ ।। nināya saṃśayatulāṃ mṛtyudaṃṣṭrāṅkurairiva ।
nipātya karṇasacivānrājaputrānprahāriṇaḥ ।। jaghāna mārtikaṃ bhojaṃ tathā kuñjarekatanam । dauḥśāsaniṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pṛṣatkena parāṅbhukham ।। vidhāya virathaṃ śalyaṃ śarajālairamohayat ।
śatruṃjayaṃ meghavegaṃ candraketuṃ suvarcasam ।। sūryabhāsaṃ ca hatvaitāngāndhārāṇāṃ kṣayaṃ vyadhāt । vidrāvya bhinnasarvāṅgaṃ śakuniṃ kṣatajokṣitam ।। śiraḥphaloccayaṃ cakre rājacūtavaneṣu saḥ ।
hemapuṅkheṣujālena janakaspardhayeva saḥ ।। cakāra kauravānīkaṃ jvalatsvāṇḍavavibhramam । sa babhau bimbito rājñāṃ svaṅgeṣu kavaceṣu ca ।। eko viśvakṣayāyeva prayāto viśvarūpatām ।
taṃ dahantamanekāni dṛṣṭvā śaraśatārciṣam ।। ācāryametya rādheyo gāḍhaviddhaḥ samabhyadhāt । bālo apyabālacaritaḥ kākutsthamavikramaḥ ।। aśeṣaṃ kṣapayatyeṣa sainyaṃ vajrisutātmajaḥ ।
vidhīyatāmatra nītirdurjayo ayamupekṣitaḥ ।। tvadadhīnā hi yuddhe asminkauravāṇāṃ jayaśriyaḥ । śrutvaitatsasmito droṇaḥ sūtaputramabhāṣata ।। satyaṃ hinasti pṛtanāṃ muhurtenārjunātmajaḥ ।
asya dhairyamamaryādaṃ dṛṣṭvā prauḍhaṃ ca vikramam ।। romāñjakañcukaḥ kāyaḥ kasya nāma na jāyate । sakārmuko na śakyo ayaṃ sakhaṅgarathakaṅkaṭaḥ ।। sacakro vā raṇe jetuṃ bhāsvaraistridaśairapi ।
tadasya kriyatāṃ yatnaḥ sarvāyudhavināśane ।। paracakrāntarasthasya yuṣmābhiryadi śakyate । tato droṇaḥ samābhāṣya karṇena sahito yayau ।। saubhadraṃ drāvitānīkaṃ saha sarvairmahārathaiḥ ।
sa tānāpatato vīrānmaṇḍalīkṛtakārmukaḥ ।। śaraiścakāra vimukhānnadīvegānivācalaḥ । tataściccheda pārśvena karṇastasyānataṃ dhanuḥ ।। rathaṃ jaghāna hārdikyaḥ sārathiṃ tasya gautamaḥ ।
virathaṃ chinnadhanvānaṃ droṇamukhyāstamādravan ।। sa dīptaṃ svaṅgamādāya carma cānekatārakam । maṇḍalāni caranvīro durlakṣyaḥ samapadyata ।। carantaṃ vyomni bāhulyātsahasrāṃśumivābhitaḥ ।
patitaṃ menire mūrdhni tulyaṃ sarve mahārathāḥ ।। prahāriṇaḥ kṣurapreṇa droṇastasyākaroddvidhā । khaṅgaṃ bhinnebhakumbhāgrasaktamauktikadanturam ।। chinnakhaṅgaḥ samādāya cakraṃ vikramalācchanaḥ ।
sa cakre rājacakrāṇāṃ kṣayaṃ cakrāyudhabhramam ।। tataste saṃhatāḥ sarve droṇamukhyā mahārathāḥ । taccakraṃ tilaśaścakruḥ śaraiḥ saṃhāraśaṅkitāḥ ।। hemāṅgadagadāpāṇiḥ so atha bhīma ivāparaḥ ।
subalasyātmajaṃ vīraṃ kālikeyaṃ jaghāna saḥ ।। gāndhārarājaputrāṇāṃ sa hatvā saptasaptatim । nṛpānbrahmavasātīyāngadayāpātayaddaśa ।। niṣpiṣṭakekayaratho gajānīkaṃ cakāra saḥ ।
vajrapātavinirbhinnaśailamaṇḍalasaṃnibham ।। rathaṃ dauḥśāsaneḥ sāśvaṃ sa niṣpiṣya sasārathim । gadayā gajaghātinyā gadāpāṇiṃ tamādravat ।। maṇḍalāni carantau tāvanyonyamabhijaghnatuḥ ।
gadābhyaṃ bhīṣaṇāghātajātavahnikaṇākulau ।। guruprahārābhihatau petatustau mahābhujau । saubhadraṃ patitaṃ dūrādbāṇairjaghnurmahārathāḥ ।। sāyakāñcitasarvāṅgaṃ vikīrṇākulakuntalam ।
dauḥśāsanistamutthāna gadayā mūrdhnyatāḍayat ।। tasminnipatite vīre vālacūta ivānilaiḥ । vītaśobhamabhūtsarvaṃ jagadudyānamākulam ।। praśāntamapi taṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣatraveṇuvanānalam ।
punaruttiṣṭhatītyāsīdbhūbhujāṃ hṛdayabhramaḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā candravadanaṃ kumāraṃ bhūmipātitam । vyomagā mumucurbāṣpaṃ suravidyādharāṅganāḥ ।। bālo lūnadhanuṣsvaṇḍaḥ śrānto vihatavāhanaḥ ।
hato mahārathaiḥ sarvairityabhūddivi niḥśvanaḥ ।। tataḥ prahṛṣṭaiḥ kurubhirlabdhalakṣyaiḥ samantataḥ । garjadbhirnirjitāḥ senā dudruvurdharmanandanam ।। tṛtīye dine abhimanyuvadhaḥ ।।
sahasrapattranayane saubhadre yudhi pātite । śokārta iva raktāṃśuḥ papātāstādrikandarāt ।। tato yudhiṣṭhiramukhāḥ saṃmukhaṃ hatamāhave । aśocyaṃ śuśucuḥ snehājjambhāritanayātmajam ।।
samāyayau tato jiṣṇuḥ śibiraṃ vimanā iva । prāyaḥ pūrvaṃ manāṃsyeva kathayanti śubhāśubham ।। sa nijaṃ sainyamālokya dhvastacchāyamadhomukham । bhrātṝṃśca viṣanārācanirbhinnāniva marmasu ।।
divasaproṣitaṃ putraṃ draṣṭumutkaṇṭhitāśayaḥ । mūkībhūtāniva śucā tānapṛcchatsasaṃbhramaḥ ।। kaccinna droṇavihitaṃ cakravyūhaṃ mamātmajaḥ । praviṣṭo nidhanaṃ nītaḥ kurubhiḥ kūṭayodhibhiḥ ।।
praveśaṃ śikṣito vyūhe mayā bālo na nirgamam । dhruvaṃ sa nihataḥ pāpaurvīro rājīvalocanaḥ ।। uktveti śokadanakvāthyamāno dhanaṃjayaḥ । śrutvā tanayavṛttāntaṃ mohātsthāṇurivābhavat ।
yaśomayīṃ praviṣṭo asau vīraḥ kalpasthirāṃ tanum ।। ityucyamānaḥ kṛṣṇena labdhasaṃjño jagāda saḥ । aho nu nābhavatkaścinmatputraṃ yo arimadhyagam ।। rarakṣa madhye yuṣmākaṃ mithyāśastraparigrahaḥ ।
taṃ samagraguṇārāmaṃ tanayaṃ rāmavikramam ।। drakṣyāmi kva punaḥ kāntaṃ svapnalabdhamivepsitam । vyaktaṃ ripubhirākīrṇaḥ patansasmāra māṃ sutaḥ ।। svasrīyaḥ keśava tvāṃ vā luptadhairyo athavā na saḥ ।
hatā subhadrā rahitā putreṇāmṛtavarṣiṇā ।। sarvātiśayalāvaṇyaguṇavikramaśālinā । manye taṃ manyate kāntaṃ tārāpatinibhānanam ।। navaṃ manmathamāyātaṃ divi devavadhūjanaḥ ।
pariṣvajasva hā putra kva yāto asi vihāya mām ।। ityuktvā mūlanirlūno bhuvi tāla ivāpatat । pratilabhya punaḥ saṃjñāṃ śrutvā hetuṃ jayadratham ।। sutakṣayaprakopāgnipītaśokārṇavo avadat ।
hantāhaṃ saindhavaṃ pāpaṃ tridaśairapi rakṣitam ।। anastano tigmakare paśyatāṃ sarvabhūjām । ye caranti gurudrohaṃ sādhūnparivadanti ye ।। viśvastānghnanti ye svairaṃ nikṣepaṃ bhakṣayanti ye ।
nindanti ye striyaṃ bhuktvā ye ca śāstrārthavarjitāḥ ।। ācaranti niṣiddhaṃ ye vihitaṃ ca tyajanti ye । lokanvrajeyaṃ tattulyānhanyā yadi na taṃ yudhi ।। asamāpte ahni nikhile na hataścejjayadrathaḥ ।
tatpravekṣyāmi dahanaṃ hūṣaṇānṛtaśāntaye ।। bhuvi vā diva pātāle merumandarakandare । api sthitaṃ taṃ madbāṇā dārayiṣyantyavāritāḥ ।। ityuktvā kopatāmrākṣaḥ samaṃ kāliyavidviṣā ।
dadhmau śaṅkhaṃ mahī yena cakampe sakulācalā ।। arjunapratijñā ।। asminnavasare cārairvijñāyārjunabhāṣitam । bhīto duryodhanāyaitya saindhavastannyavedayat ।।
kauravastaṃ samādāya dromamabhyetya sānugaḥ । pratijñāmavadaddhorāṃ saindhave savyasācinaḥ ।। jayadratho vadatyeṣa dinamekamalakṣitaḥ । gacchāmi pārthivāḥ sarve māṃ vā rakṣantu saṃhatāḥ ।।
iti duryodhanenokte bhāradvājastamabravīt । śvaḥ kartāsmi mahāvyūhaṃ durbhedyaṃ tridaśairapi ।। ahaṃ dhanaṃjayaṃ vīraṃ vārayiṣyāmi sāyakaiḥ । saindhavārthinamāyāntaṃ velaśaila ivodadhim ।।
ukte śoṇahayeneti prahṛṣṭāḥ kurupuṃgavāḥ । hataṃ pārthamamanyanta pratijñābhaṅgavahninā ।। adhunaivākhilāṃ senāmekaḥ kruddho vināśayet । rātrāvityarjunabhayātkuravastasthurutthitāḥ ।।
atrāntare putraśokavyathātāpralāpinīm । subhadrāṃ yājñasenīṃ ca śauriḥ sāntvayituṃ yayau ।। āśvāsitā keśavena subhadrā bāṣpagadgadam । vilalāpa muhuḥ kaṇṭhe snuṣāmālambya mūrcchitām ।।
hā putra nayanānanda mandirāmṛtadīdhite । kva nu te padmapattrākṣaṃ drakṣyāmi vadanaṃ punaḥ ।। iyaṃ te matsyaduhitā navoḍhā mahiṣī priyā । martumāhitasaṃkalpā rakṣyate garbhagauravāt ।।
nāthe pitari kṛṣṇe ca bhīme ca balināṃ vare । raṇe reṇubhirakīrṇaḥ śeṣe kathamanāthavat ।। brahmaṇyānāṃ vadānyānāṃ yajvanāṃ puṇyakarmiṇām । sadācāravratajuṣāṃ gatimāpnuhi putraka ।।
iti pralāpamukharāṃ tāṃ samāśvāsya mādhavaḥ । tūrṇaṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ vītanidramupāyayau ।। kṛṣṇājñayā japaparo vidhivatparikalpite । pavitre śayane nidrāṃ lebhe śakrasutastataḥ ।।
so apasyadvyomagaḥ svapne viṣṇunā saha saṃyutaḥ । divyaparvatamārūḍho devaṃ candrārdhasekharam ।। taṃ govindasakho dṛṣṭvā praṇamya racitāñjaliḥ । bhaktyā tuṣṭāva varadaṃ vareṇyaṃ harṣanirbharaḥ ।।
namo bhavāya bhuvanaprabhavāpyāyakāriṇe । namaḥ śarvāya niḥśeṣaduṣkarmaviṣahāriṇe ।। namo rudrāya daityendradrāvitendrabhayacchide । namaḥ śivāya bhīmāya śrīkaṇṭhāya kapāline ।।
ugrāya śreyasāṃ dhāmne vāmārdhāyordhvaretase । vyālākulāya sevyāya niṣkalāya kalābhṛte ।। triguṇāya trinetrāya tryambakāya trimūrtaye । saṃkalpakalpavṛkṣāya namastubhyaṃ triśūline ।।
iti rudraḥ stutaḥ svapne mahābhujagavigraham । dhanurastraṃ ca pārthāya sasthānakamadarśayat ।। pūrvalabdhaṃ mahāstraṃ taddṛṣṭvā pāśupataṃ jayaḥ । manttraṃ ca prāpya caṇḍīśātkṛtakṛtyo vyabudhyata ।।
tataḥ prabhāte kṛṣṇāya tannivedya dhanaṃjayaḥ । pratijñābhāramakhilaṃ hṛṣṭaḥ svalpamamanyata ।। atha snātāḥ kṛtāvaśyakaraṇīyā hutāgnayaḥ । raṇāṅgaṇaṃ mahotsāhā niryayuḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ ।।
tato vyūhaṃ vyadhāddroṇaḥ pṛthucakrapariṣkṛtam । śakaṭaṃ vikaṭāṭopaṃ guptaṃ subhaṭakoṭibhiḥ ।। mahādalaṃ ca tanmadhye padmaṃ nṛpatikesaram । turaṅgarathamātaṅgasahasrāyutakarṇikam ।।
kṛtavarmamukhaiḥ kṛtvā sūcivyūhaṃ tadantare । jayadrathaṃ vṛtaṃ vīraiḥ sūcīpāśe nyavedayat ।। evaṃ vyūḍheṣvanīkeṣu guruṇādbhutakāriṇā । gāṇḍīvadhanvā senāgre dīptaketuradṛśyata ।।
tasya caṇḍakarasyeva śararaśmisahasriṇaḥ । sehire na mahīpālā draṣṭuṃ tejo mahaujasaḥ ।। ākampite atha bhuvane durnimittaśatākule । śvetāśve syandane kṛṣṇau śubhrau śaṅkhau pradadhmatuḥ ।।
tayoḥ śabdena pavanaskandasaṃghaṭṭakāriṇā । akāṇḍapralayārambhasarvabhūtāni menire ।। tato militayostūrṇaṃ mithaḥ senāsamudrayoḥ । vyālanīlavalatasvaṅgātaraṅgaḥ saṃgaro abhavat ।।
śirobhiratha śūrāṇāṃ bāhubhiśca sabhūṣaṇaiḥ । mahīmācchādayanpārtho droṇānīkamathāviśat ।। sa praṇamya guruṃ vṛddhamanumānya prasādya ca । pūrvotsṛṣṭaśaraṃ dīptaiḥ śarajālairavākirat ।।
tato jayadrathākāṅkṣī tūrṇamacyutasārathiḥ । droṇaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya praviśyānilaraṃhasā ।। lāghavāddroṇamṛtsṛjya praviṣṭe śvetavāhane । cakrarakṣau viviśaturyudhāmanyūttamaujasau ।।
tato mandarasaṃrabdhakṣubhitāmbhodhivibhramaḥ । vyūhasyādīryamāṇasya nirghoṣastumulo abhavat ।। prasaktaṃ vrajatastasya puraḥ kuñjarabhedinaḥ । babhuḥ padmavanānīva patitairbhūbhujāṃ mukhaiḥ ।।
vṛto gato hato labdho hantyeṣa patitā vayam । ityabhūddārumaḥ śabdo yatra yatra dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। tūrṇaṃ praviśatastasya sindhurājavadhepsayā । pralayāmbudharadhvānadhīro abhūtasyandansvanaḥ ।।
ajayyaṃ samare droṇaṃ tyaktvā dhīmati phalguṇe । praviṣṭe śaravarṣābhre cakampe kurukānanam ।। kṛtavarmamukhānvīrāṃstatastūrṇamabhidrutān । jitvā yavanakāmbojaṃ jaghāna śatamanyujaḥ ।।
droṇaḥ paścādathābhyetya brahmāstreṇa dhanaṃjayam । rundhānaḥ samare cakre jvālājālajaṭaṃ nabhaḥ ।। brahmāstreṇaiva sahasā hatvāstraṃ śakranandanaḥ । parivarjya guruṃ prāyādbhojānīkaṃ manojavaḥ ।।
vidhāya vimukhaṃ bhojaṃ prayāntaṃ savyasācinam । abhyudyayau vāripateḥ suto rājā śrutāyudhaḥ ।। śaraistenāyutotsṛṣṭairviddho dhairyamahodadhiḥ । rathaṃ hatvāsya vidadhe pārthaḥ sarvāyudhakṣayam ।।
varuṇena purā pitrā sa dattāmādade gadām । ayodhe pātitā mohāttamevaitya nihanti yā ।। sa tayā keśavaṃ mūḍho mṛtyudūtyeva ghorayā । atāḍayanmahāvegī vicacāla na cācyutaḥ ।।
tayā pratīpamabhyetya sa niṣpiṣṭo nareśvaraḥ । papāta bhagnakaṭako vajreṇeva kulācalaḥ ।। saritastanaye vīre varṇamāyāḥ śrutāyudhe । hate pārtharathasyābhūdabhagnapraṇayā gatiḥ ।।
śrutāyudhavadhaḥ ।। jayoddhūtapatākāgraṃ vrajantaṃ vānaradhvajam । vegadīrghīkṛtasmerakirīṭābharaṇaprabham ।। taḍitāṃ maṇḍaleneva piṅgaṃ gāṇḍīvatejasā ।
rājā sudakṣiṇo abhyāyātkāmbojaḥ kurudakṣiṇaḥ ।। tasyāstravarṣiṇastūrṇaṃ chitvā kārmukamarjunaḥ । cakarta śaktiṃ tanmuktāṃ ghanaghaṇṭāvirāviṇīm ।। so atha pārthaśarāsāraviśarārutanurnṛpaḥ ।
papāta hemamālāṅko vidyādhara ivāmbarāt ।। sudakṣimavadhaḥ ।। kāmboje nihate vīre bhajyamāne balārṇave । sahācyutāyuṣā rājñā śrutāyuḥ pārthamādravat ।।
śrutāyuṣā tomarema śūlenānyena cāhataḥ । tulyaṃ bāṇasahasraiśca mumoha kapiketanaḥ ।। labdhasaṃjño atha śakrāsraṃ samudīrya dhanaṃjayaḥ । sāśvasūtau supatrau ca kathāśeṣau cakāra tau ।।
śrutāyurvadhaḥ ।। aṅgānvaṅgānkaliṅgāṃśca dākṣiṇātyāṃśca pāṇḍavaḥ । hatvā jaghāna vipulaṃ kuñjarānīkamāśugaiḥ ।। daratturaṣkacīnānāṃ mlecchānāṃ ca varūthinīm ।
śarairnipātya vidadhe ghorāṃ raktataraṅgiṇīm ।। ambaṣṭhādhipateśchitvā mauliratnojjavalaṃ śiraḥ । avāritagatirvīro viveśācyutasārathiḥ ।। atha droṇaṃ samabhyetya babhāṣe kauraveśvaraḥ ।
ācārya paśya pārthena bhūbhujāṃ kadanaṃ kṛtam ।। kathaṃ nu laṅghayedvīra varākastvāṃ pṛthāsutaḥ । śiṣyānurodho yadi te na syātsaralacetasaḥ ।। dattābhayo adya bhavatā helayaiva jayadrathaḥ ।
praveśitaḥ svayaṃ kālakarālavadanodare ।। ko hi gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ tvayāpi samupekṣitam । carantaṃ mama sainyeṣu sāmānyo vārayiṣyati ।। ityukte kururājena bhāradvājo jagāda tam ।
tārkṣyavego yuvā pārtho vṛddhamullaṅghya cāgataḥ ।। vyūhadvāre mayā ruddhā bhīmasātyakipārṣatāḥ । praviśantyeṣa bībhātsuṃ vrajāmi yadi pṛṣṭhataḥ ।। idaṃ tu te karomyadya hitaṃ lokeṣu duṣkaram ।
bhaviṣyasi raṇe yena devānāmapi durjayaḥ ।। ghore vṛtraraṇe rudraḥ surendrāya dadau purā । divyaṃ mantramayaṃ varma durbhedyo yena so abhavat ।। tadetanmantrasaṃyuktaṃ prāptaṃ gurumukhānmayā ।
badhnāmi brahmasūtreṇa tava śatrunibarhaṇam ।। ityuktvā tasya mantreṇa bhāsvatkanakakaṅkaṭam । prasthitasyārjunaṃ jetuṃ babandha kurubhūpateḥ ।। āmuktadivyakavaco guruṇā kauraveśvaraḥ ।
gajavājirathānīkaiḥ prayayau pārthamojasā ।। asminnavasare yuddhe vyūhasya pramukhe abhavan । droṇaśalyaśalādīnāṃ dhṛṣṭadyumnapurogamāḥ ।। pāṇḍavā draupadeyāśca rākṣasaśca ghaṭotkacaḥ ।
sātyakirdrupado matsyaḥ kuntibhojasca kekayāḥ ।। vīrāścānye mahīpālāḥ samabhidrutya saṃhatāḥ । divyāstravittamā vīrā jalasandhaṃ narādhipam ।। duḥśāsanaṃ vikarṇaṃ ca citrasenaṃ viviṃśatim ।
alāyudhaṃ rākṣasendramalambumamalambusam ।। bāhlikaṃ śakuniṃ droṇiṃ vṛṣasenaṃ ca gautamam । muhurmuhārathāṃścanyānvyūhagarbhavinirgatān ।। avākiranhemapuṅkhairnijanāmāṅkitaiḥ śaraiḥ ।
mitho rathāgre kurvāṇā rudhirāvartadurgamam ।। te cakrurvikramodārā ghorābhiḥ śastravṛṣṭibhiḥ । kabandhatāṇḍavoccaṇḍasaṃrambhalalitā diśaḥ ।। atrāntare śvetahayaḥ praviśankuruvāhinīm ।
cakāra nipatacchatrurājahaṃsāvalīsitām ।। śarāṇāmarjunabhujotsṛṣṭānāmāśugāminām । krośadvayaṃ yayāvagre sa kṛṣṇaprerito rathaḥ ।। te hayā hemasaṃnāhā gāhamānā ivāmbaram ।
javadīrghaiḥ prabhājālaiścakruḥ pallavitā diśaḥ ।। hato gajo rathaśchinnaḥ patito ayaṃ narādhipaḥ । ityabhūnniḥsvanastatra ceruryatrārjuneṣavaḥ ।। vindānuvindāvāvantyāvabhidrutyātha pāṇḍavam ।
adṛśyaṃ cakraturnānāśastravarṣaiḥ sakeśavam ।। tayoḥ pārtho rathau hatvā chitvā ca dhanuṣī śaraiḥ । jahāra śirasī yābhyāṃ dvicandrevābhavanmahī ।। vindānuvindavadhaḥ ।।
sasainyo rājaputrau tau hatvā vipulavikramau । nijāśvānvyathitānvīkṣya babhāṣe kṛṣṇamarjunaḥ ।। kṛṣṇārtānvājinaḥ klāntāndasyuśastraśarakṣatān । pāyayoddhṛtaśalyāṃstvaṃ muktvaitānsalilaṃ vibho ।।
uktveti so avatīryaśu pādacārī nareśvarān । idamantaramityāptānekaḥ sarvānayodhayat ।। tataḥ pārthāstrajālānāṃ tadastrāṇāṃ ca saṃghaśaḥ । nigharṣaniḥsṛtajvālākarālamabhavannabhaḥ ।।
arjunena kṛte kṣipraṃ śarapañaajaramandiram । tadastrabhinnavasudhāsaṃjātavimalodake ।। parivṛttānsamākṛṣṭaśalyānāghrātabhūtalān । pāyayitvā hayānkṛṣṇo hṛṣṭānpunarayojayat ।।
te kṛṣṇāvavahanvāhā jātadviguṇaraṃhasaḥ । āruhanta ivākāśaṃ śakrāśvivijigīṣayā ।। atha svalpāvaśeṣe ahni tūrṇaṃ saindhavakāṅkṣiṇaḥ । cakampe kauravacamūḥ sāyakaiḥ savyasācinaḥ ।।
vidruteṣu narendreṣu bhagne gajaghaṭāvane । droṇānubaddhakavacaḥ kauravendraḥ samāyayau ।। vilokya vipulānīkaṃ tamāyāntaṃ mahaujasam । uvāca kaiṭabhārātirnivātakavacāntakam ।।
ayaṃ sa kartā darpāndho nikārāṇāṃ sthavīyasām । prāpto mūlamanarthānāṃ jahyenaṃ kulakaṇṭakam ।। ityukte puṣkarākṣeṇa vīrau jiṣṇusuyodhanau । kṣaṇaṃ vilokya cakrāte surendranamuciprabham ।।
