preritā kururājena śubhrapakṣā kirīṭinam । krauñcādrimiva haṃsālī viveśa viśikhāvalī ।। gāṇḍīvadhanvano bāṇānvandhyāndṛṣṭvā suyodhane । kimetaditi govindo jagāda pṛthuvismayaḥ ।।
dhanaṃjayastamavadatsmitadhautādharadyutiḥ । jñātaṃ kṛṣṇa mayā yena pāpo ayaṃ pratibhāṃ śritaḥ ।। varmāsya guruṇā baddhaṃ vidyayā vajrasaṃnibham । pratiyogaṃ ca jāne ahaṃ kṛtsnametadvināśane ।।
ityuktvāstraṃ mahaddivyaṃ kavacocchittaye vyadhāt । tacca dūrānmahāstreṇa droṇaputro vyadārayat ।। dviṣprayojyaṃ na divyāstramityuktvā pāṇḍunandanaḥ । cakre suyodhanaṃ chinnarathasārathikārmukam ।।
hastayośca śarairasya cakārāprāptavarmaṇoḥ । lakṣyābhyāsamivāsaktaṃ yenāsau vimukho abhavat ।। tato drauṇiprabhṛtayaḥ pārthaṃ sarve mahārathāḥ । abhyādravansusaṃrabdhā vicitrakavacadhvajāḥ ।।
śikhidhvajaḥ karṇasutaḥ sīrāṅko madrabhūpatiḥ । maṇināgadhvajaḥ śrīmānsvayaṃ rājā suyodhanaḥ ।। bhūriśravā yūpaketurante ca vividhadhvajāḥ । hemadīptāyudhadharā ghoraṃ yuyudhire nṛpāḥ ।।
teṣāmāpatatāṃ tūrṇaṃ laghuhasto dhanaṃjayaḥ । ciccheda bāṇairmarmāṇi chattrāṇi ca dhanūṃṣi ca ।। śarairvivarmaṇāṃ teṣāṃ padmagarbhanibhāni saḥ । bālātapāruṇānīva vapūṃṣi rudhirairvyadhāt ।।
vadhyamāneṣu vīreṣu jiṣṇunā sarvarājasu । valatsvaṅgabhujaḥ kālo nanarteva nijotsave ।। atrāntare dharmasutaṃ droṇo vyūhamukhe sthitaḥ । mahārathaiḥ parivṛtaṃ jighṛkṣustūrṇamādravat ।।
sa kṛtvā matsyapāñcālacedisṛñjayakekayān । alpāvaśeṣānrājānaṃ cakāra virathaṃ śaraiḥ ।। hatāśvaṃ kṛttacāpaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā sarve yudhiṣṭhiram । hṛto hṛto nṛpa iti sphāratāraṃ pracukruśuḥ ।।
tataḥ pāṇḍusutaḥ śaktiṃ prāhiṇotprāṇahāriṇīm । brahmastreṇa ca tāṃ droṇo bhasmasādakarotkṣaṇāt ।। chinnasarvāyudho viddhaḥ śaraiḥ kuliśadāruṇaiḥ । saha devarathenāśu muktvā droṇaṃ yayau nṛpaḥ ।।
vidrute dharmatanaye bhāradvājo ruṣā jvalan । dadāha pāṇḍavacamūṃ śaraśreṇīśikāśataiḥ ।। kekayo atha bṛhatkṣatraḥ pāṇḍavānīkanāyakaḥ । droṇānugaṃ kṣemadhūtiṃ mahīpālamapātayat ।।
traigartaṃ vīradhanvānaṃ dhṛṣṭaketuṃ mahāratham । vidhāya cchinnamūrdhānaṃ kabandhaṃ vidadhe kṣaṇam ।। nirapatyaṃ hātamitraṃ sahadevo avadhīdyudhi । sātyakirvyāghradattaṃ ca rājaputramapātayat ।।
vidhyamānaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhāradvājasutaḥ paraiḥ । śiraḥkūṭāvaseṣāṇi pāṇḍusainyānyakalpayat ।। rākṣaso atha bakabhrātā bhīmasenamalambusaḥ । yodhayitvā śaraśataistatsenāṃ māyayāvadhīt ।।
pravartitāṃ rākṣasena bhīmo dṛṣṭvāsṛgāpagām । tvāṣṭreṇāstreṇa tanmāyāṃ chitvāramajayatkṛtī ।। vadhāya bhīmasenasya rakṣastatpunarāgamat । avārayanmahākāyaṃ mahākāyo ghaṭotkacaḥ ।।
sa rathādrathamutsṛjya kālaḥ kāla ivonnadan । ākṛṣyālambusaṃ vegānniṣpiṣya vidadhe vyasum ।। alambusavadhaḥ ।। ghaṭotkacena nihate rākṣase jambhavikrame ।
bhayamāvirabhūddhoraṃ samare sarvabhūbhujām ।। atrāntare dharmasuto dūrasthasya kirīṭinaḥ । aśṛṇvañśaṅkhanirghoṣaṃ kimapyāśaṅkito abhavat ।। bhīto abhimanyuvṛktāntādviṣaṇṇo bhrātṛvatsalaḥ ।
uvāca sātyakiṃ matvā sa dhuryaṃ sarvadhanvinām ।। sātyake paśya bandhūnāṃ gurūṇāṃ suhṛdāṃ tathā । dordarpasya ca saṃprāptaḥ kālo ayamucitastava ।। sa te guruḥ sakhā bandhuḥ kirīṭi śatrumadhyagaḥ ।
na jñāyate praṇaṣṭe atra śaṅkhaśabde kathaṃ sthitaḥ ।। ṛte tvāmujjvalācāraṃ pravaraṃ śauryaśālinām । bhāraḥ kasminnasahyo ayaṃ dhuraṃdhara nidhīyatām ।। pātre vitaratāṃ pṛthvīṃ rakṣatāṃ śaraṇāgatam ।
mittrārthe tyajatāṃ prāṇānsamānaṃ śrūyate phalam ।। dhanyā bhavadvidhā eva kriyate yaiḥ sthiraṃ yaśaḥ । pavanākampikadalīdalālolairnijāsubhiḥ ।। tvayi yāter'junaṃ draṣṭuṃ droṇagrahaṇajaṃ bhayam ।
bhīmapārṣataguptasya satyaṃ me na bhaviṣyati ।। ukta yudhiṣṭhireṇeti sātyakiḥ satvasāgaraḥ । sajjo abhavattathetyuktvā parānīkabibhitsayā ।। sa hemakavacaḥ sragvī śubhrāśvaṃ rathamāsthitaḥ ।
dīptasaṃhadhvajaḥ śrīmānghananirghoṣakārmukaḥ ।। dātā hutānalo hṛṣṭo nṛpamāntrya sānujam । bhīme rakṣāṃ nidhāyāsya maṅgalālaṃkṛto yayau ।। sa bhāradvājamāsādya vainateya ivāśugaḥ ।
cakre rājabhujaṅgānāṃ kṣaṇamākampavibhramam ।। tato yuddhamabhūddhoramācāryayuyudhānayoḥ । mohanaṃ sarvalokānāṃ skandatārakayoriva ।। droṇaṃ sa durjayaṃ matvā dhīmānsātyakirabravīt ।
guro śiṣyaṃ tavānveṣṭuṃ phalguṇaṃ prasthitasya me । asminnalpāvaśeṣe ahni na vighnaṃ kartumarhasi ।। śrutvaitaccāpamākṛṣya babhāṣe kumbhasaṃbhavaḥ । na praveṣṭuṃ tvayā śakyaṃ mayi jīvati sātyake ।।
iti bruvāṇaṃ śaineyo mano mārutaraṃhasā । rathena vañcayitvā taṃ parāhūtaṃ samāviśat ।। sa vrajandurjayāñjitvā kṛtavarmamukhānraṇe । ghorānmlecchānkirātāṃśca kāmbojāṃśca nyapātayat ।।
sānugānpāṇḍutanayānbhettuṃ vyūhāgramudyatān । nirgatyāvārayansarvānkṛtavarmā dhanurdhanaḥ ।। javena praviśantaṃ ca sātyakiṃ subhaṭāśanim । bhindānaṃ kuñjaraghaṭā rundhānaṃ sāyakairdiśaḥ ।।
śastravṛṣṭiṃ tadutsṛṣṭāṃ śarairvikṣipya sātyakiḥ । ciccheda jalasaṃdhasya śakrāyudhanibhaṃ dhanuḥ ।। kupitaśchinnacāpāstraḥ kṛtvā sarvāyudhavyayam । sāvegaṃ preritagajaḥ so atha sātyakimādravat ।।
javādāpatatastasya śaineyaścandanokṣitau । chitvā bhujau jahārāśu saratnamukuṭaṃ śiraḥ ।। tasminhate sa nāgendro yuyudhānaśarārditaḥ । vidrutaḥ kauravacamūṃ pipeṣālambi kaṅkaṭaḥ ।।
jalasaṃdhavadhaḥ ।। vidārya māgadhānīkaṃ praviśanvṛṣṇipuṃgavaḥ । duryodhanamukhānvīrānayodhayadasaṃbhramaḥ ।। parāṅmukhīkṛtāśeṣasubhaṭaḥ so atha māninaḥ ।
sudarśanasya nṛpateścakarta ruciraṃ śiraḥ ।। śabarānyavanānbhojānbarbarāṃstāmraliptikān । śakānmuṇḍānkuvindāṃśca harandūrānmataṅgajān ।। dasyusaṃghāṃśca vividhānsa hatvā krūravikramān ।
cakre karabhakuṭṭākaḥ kṣitaṃ mastiṣkakardamām ।। duḥśāsano atha niśitairviddhaḥ sātyakinā śaraiḥ । vihāya samaraṃ tūrṇaṃ bhāradvājāntikaṃ yayau ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā vihvalaṃ droṇo babhāṣe pārśvartinam ।
ko ayaṃ te saṃbhramo vīra gatvā rakṣa yajadratham ।। aho na sātyakiśarairbhinnāṃ dṛṣṭvā varūthinīm । kṛtavairaśca mānī ca yoddhavye vidruto asi kim ।। etattāvatkṛtaṃ karma śaineyenātimānuṣam ।
ato bahuguṇaṃ vīrau bhīmapārthau kariṣyataḥ ।। naiṣā sabhā sā pāñcālī yatra tvaṃ kṛṣṭavānasi । imāḥ prāṇapaṇaprāpyā yaśovikramabhūmayaḥ ।। adyāpi rocatāṃ saṃdhiryuṣmākaṃ pāṇḍunandanaiḥ ।
antaṃ na yātā vīrāṇāṃ saṃpratyarjunasāyakāḥ ।। yudhyasva tūrṇamathavā śātravairaparāṅmukhaḥ । bhagnapradhānā hi camūrvāryamāṇāpi dīryate ।। iti rukmarathenokto vailabhyātkṣmāṃ vilokayan ।
nighnansāhāyyakaṃ cakre mṛtyoriva jagatkṣate ।। vīraketuṃ sudhanvānaṃ citraketuṃ ca pārthivam । tathā citrarthaṃ vīraṃ pāñcālānavadhīdyudhi ।। dhṛṣṭadyumnastataḥ kruddhaḥ sarvābharaṇabhedibhiḥ ।
viddhvā droṇamasaṃbhrāntaḥ śaraiḥ senāmadārayat ।। ācāryaṃ bhṛśamākīrṇaṃ śarairmūrchāmupāgatam । khaḍgapāṇirabhidrāvya pārṣato hantumudyayau ।। labdhasaṃjñastato droṇaḥ śarairāsannapātibhiḥ ।
kiṣkupramāṇairvaitastairvaṃśotthaistamapūrayat ।। vṛścikairiva tairvyāpto dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ parāṅmukhaḥ । prayayau guruṇā paścāddāritaḥ pṛthusāyakaiḥ ।। tataḥ śoṇahayaḥ kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavānāmanīkinīm ।
dārayanbhūmipālānāṃ śirobhiḥ kṣmāmapūrayat ।। duḥśāsanamathāyāntaṃ sātyakiḥ śaravarṣiṇam । cakāra cchinnavarmāṇaṃ virathadhvajasāyakam ।। saṃtyaktaṃ vidrutairmlecchaiḥ prahāraśakalīkṛtaiḥ ।
rakṣanpratijñāṃ bhīmasya vimukhaṃ nāvadhīdgatam ।। atrāntare rukmaratho viśanpāñcālavāhinīm । droṇāya prāhiṇoddīptāṃ śiśupālasuto balī ।। tasya tūrṇaṃ śitairbāṇairguruḥ kṛtvā yudhi kṣayam ।
cakāra mauliratnāṃśucchuritoṣṇīṣamānanam ।। dhṛṣṭaketau vinihate jalasaṃdhasuto balī । bāṇavarṣī kṣaṇātprāpa droṇānalapataṅgatām ।। kekayadhṛṣṭaketuvadhaḥ ।।
dhṛṣṭadyumnasutaṃ hatvā kṛtavarmāṇamāśugaiḥ । droṇo jaghāna pāñcālānhehayāniva bhārgavaḥ ।। bhagnāsu pāṇḍusenāsu ghore tasminmahāhave । nininda krūravarmāṇamācāryaṃ vyathito janaḥ ।।
sātyakipraveśaḥ ।। cirapraviṣṭe śeneye śaṅkito dharmajaḥ punaḥ । lambamāne ravau bhīmaṃ samabhyetyābhyabhāṣata ।। yathā na śrūyate bhīma śaṅkhaśabdaḥ kirīṭinaḥ ।
tathā manye kimapyasya kṛtaṃ sarvairmahārathaiḥ ।। taṃ vīramamarārātitamovidhvaṃsabhāskaram । vinā tavānujaṃ bhīma kathaṃ jīvitumutsahe ।। nirghoṣaḥ śrūyate ghoraḥ pāñcajanyasya duḥsahaḥ ।
jāner'junavadhakrodhānmādhavo yoddhumudyataḥ ।। tadgatvā vīra jānīhi vṛttāntaṃ savyasācinaḥ । paśyāmi timirākrāntāḥ kaśmalābhihato diśaḥ ।। ukte yudhiṣṭhireṇeti taṃ jagāda vṛkodaraḥ ।
rājandhanaṃjaye śaṅkāṃ na mithyā kartumarhasi ।। ko nāma vibudhārātivadhūvaidhavyadāyinaḥ । pragalbhate dhuraṃ dhatte yudhi gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ ।। tathāpyadya gṛhītvāhaṃ śirasā tava śāsanam ।
carāmi padavīṃ jiṣṇordārayankuruvāhinīm ।। ityuktvā mārutasutaḥ syandanenābhranādinā । hemacitratanutrāṇaḥ pattrirāja ivādravat ।। sa rukmarathamāruhya rukmapuṅkhaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ ।
apūrayatkuruvanaṃ ratnadīptairivāhibhiḥ ।। praveṣṭukāmamācāryastamabhyetyābravīttataḥ । māmanirjitya kaunteya bhettuṃ śakyā na vāhinī ।। tvadvidhaiḥ kururājasya saṃrambhaṃ mā kṛthā vṛthā ।
ityuktvā pāṇḍavaṃ droṇaḥ śaravarṣairavākirat ।। tadbāṇajālanirbhinno babhāṣe ca vṛkodaraḥ । yathā tvaṃ manyase droṇa nedānīṃ no gururbhavān ।। pūjayatyarjuno mānyānbhīmo ahaṃ paśya māmiti ।
ityuktvā prāhiṇottasmai gadāmaśanigauravām ।। tayā droṇaparityakto rathaḥ śakalatāṃ yayau । apakrānte kṣaṇaṃ droṇe sānujaṃ kauraveśvaram ।। śarairapūrayadbhīmo bhīmasāyakavarṣiṇam ।
kṣuraprotkṛttavadanānsa jaghānātha kauravān ।। vṛndārakaṃ dīrghanetraṃ suṣeṇaṃ durvimocanam । raudrakarmāṇamabhayaṃ citrakāntiṃ sudarśanam ।। nipātyaitāngadābhinnasainyaścakre talasvanam ।
vidrutaṃ svabalaṃ dṛṣṭvā taṃ dromaḥ punarādravat ।। rathenākālajaladadhvanigambhīranādinā । saṃprahārastataḥ kṣipraṃ dāruṇo droṇabhīmayoḥ ।। yayau bhārgavakākutstharaṇasmaraṇahetutām ।
syandanādavaruhyātha krūrakarmā vṛkodaraḥ ।। cikṣepa dorbhyāmutkṣipya dūradūre rathaṃ guroḥ । bhagnacakradhvajahayādvikīrṇayugakūbarāt ।। avaplutya yayau tasmāddroṇo garuḍavikramaḥ ।
athāntaraṃ samāsādya dārayanvaravāraṇān ।। pothayanraṇasaṃghātānviveśa pavanātmajaḥ । pātayanrājavaktrāṇi punaḥ sasmāra mārutiḥ ।। nirlūnanālanalināṃ kuberanalinīṃ muhuḥ ।
sa vrajanbojakāmbojānvijitya vijayāgrajaḥ ।। viveśākulitaṃ tūrṇaṃ karṇānīkamanākulaḥ । tasya nādaṃ parijñāya dūrātkṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau ।। ākarṇya kārmukaravaṃ nanāda pramadākulaḥ ।
tasya nādaṃ parijñāya dūrātkṛṣṇadhanaṃjayau ।। mandaroddhūtadugdhābdhighoṣau saṅkhau pradadhmatuḥ । tena diktaṭasaṃghaṭṭapaṭṭaṭāṅkāraśālinā ।। śabdena sādhvasakṛtā bhuvanāni cakampire ।
ākarṇya kṛṣṇayostulyaṃ śaṅkhanādaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। hṛṣṭo mene samuttīrṇamarjunaṃ ripusāgarāt । bhajyamānaṃ balaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmena bhujaśālinā ।। kopādabhyāyayau karṇaḥ kurvanbāṇamayaṃ jagat ।
tamāyāntaṃ śarairviddhvā nadatpavananandanaḥ ।। cakāra vimukhaṃ kṛttadhvajasyandanakārmukam । bhagne samiti rādheye dhaureye dhairyaśālinām ।। uvāca droṇamāgatya mlānamānaḥ suyodhanaḥ ।
arjunaste priyaḥ śiṣyastvāmullaṅghya gato yadi ।। tatkiṃ praviṣṭau prasabhaṃ yuyudhānavṛkodarau । kimanyadvidhivaimukhyaṃ satyamasmāsu jṛmbhate ।। yatra velāmatikrānto bhavānvīryamahodadhiḥ ।
ityuktaḥ kururājena babhāṣe kumbhasaṃbhavaḥ ।। sainyaṃ puraśca paścācca gṛhītaṃ dhāryate katham । rakṣyamāṇamito yatnātpurataḥ pravidīryate ।। avāritā viśantyeva sarve pāñcālasṛñjayāḥ ।
sainyadvāramito yatnādrakṣyaṃ sarvātmanā mayā ।। bhavānkarṇamukhaiḥ sārdhamebhiḥ sarvairmahārathaiḥ । pārthasātyakibhīmānāṃ paryāptaḥ kiṃ na vāraṇe ।। asminmuhūrtaśeṣe ahni gatvā rakṣa jayadratham ।
adhunā tatpaṇāveva raṇadyūte jayājayau ।। ityukto guruṇā rājā gatvā pāñcālanandanau । sarvaiścakāra virathau cakrarakṣau kirīṭinaḥ ।। atrāntare punaḥ karṇaḥ samāgatya vṛkodaram ।
hemupuṅkhaiḥ śaraiścakre jvalitānalasaṃnibham ।। tato bhīmabhujotsṛṣṭaiḥ pattribhirgiribhedibhiḥ । viddhaśchinnāyudharatho raṇaṃ tatyāja sūtajaḥ ।। tato bhagne kurubale nadantaṃ vāyunandanam ।
karṇo mānī samāśvasya rathena punarādravat ।। ghore pravṛtte samare suciraṃ karṇabhīmayoḥ । babhūva viśikhavrātairnaranāgarathakṣayaḥ ।। bhīmo atha sūtaputrasya cchitvā tālopamaṃ dhanuḥ ।
jaghāna ghananirghoṣaṃ rathaṃ saha manorathaiḥ ।। virathaṃ karṇamālokya yudhyamānaṃ prayatnataḥ । ādiṣṭaḥ kururājena durjayastamupādravat ।। duryodhanānujaṃ vīramāyāntaṃ śaravarṣiṇam ।
taṃ hatvā vinadanbhīmaḥ śaraiḥ karṇamapūrayat ।। punaḥ syandanamāsthāya sūtapūtro vṛkodaram । abhyadhāvatpṛthuśarajvālājaṭilakārmukam ।। tadbāṇadāritatanuḥ pāvaniḥ kopakampitaḥ ।
gurvī gadāṃ visṛjyāsya niṣpipeṣa rathaṃ javāt ।। bhuvi sthitaṃ śarairbhinnaṃ karṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā suyodhanaḥ । ādideśānujaṃ kopāddurmukhaṃ karṇaguptaye ।। vegātkauravamāyāntaṃ taṃ śastrāśaniduḥsaham ।
rathādapātayadbhīmo nirbhinnahṛdayaṃ śaraiḥ ।। āruhya durmukharathaṃ karṇo duḥkhānalākulaḥ । bhīmāya prāhiṇodbāṇāñjvalitāniva duḥsahān ।। tato bhīmabhujotsṛṣṭāḥ saniḥśvāsā ivoragāḥ ।
aṅgarājaṃ vinirbhidya śarāḥ pātālamāviśan ।। sa gāḍhaviddho dudrāva javavyālolaketunā । rathena kurusenānāṃ dhṛtimunmūlayanniva ।। abhyadhāvaṃstato bhīmaṃ pañca duryodhanānujāḥ ।
jagaduḥ śalyadurgrāhyāḥ sadurdarśanaduṣprabhāḥ ।। yudhyamānānsa tānbāṇairmahārhābharaṇojjvalān । apātayanmahāvāta iva sendrāyudhānghanān ।। hateṣu teṣu rādheyo dhunāno vipulaṃ dhanuḥ ।
ayodhayatpunarbhīmaṃ mahākāle apyasaṃbhramaḥ ।। tasya bhīmo dhanuśchitvā rathaṃ ca guruvikramaḥ । nardankare abhyo vīrāṇāmāyudhāni nyapātayat ।। viṣame vartamānasya rādheyasya suyodhanaḥ ।
saptānujānsahāyārthaṃ preṣayāmāsa satvaram ।। citrākṣaścitravarmā ca citrabāṇaḥ śarāsanaḥ । upacitraḥ sacitraśca cārucitraśca te samam ।। āyānta eva vimukhāstulyābharaṇavāsasaḥ ।
śaraibharmibhujotsṛṣṭaiḥ pretāḥ peturmahītale ।। tānvīkṣya patitānvīrānkṣīṇapuṇyāniva grahān । karṇo asrupūrṇanayano rathamanyaṃ samādade ।। krodhādadhikasaṃrambo yudhyamāno vṛkodaraḥ ।
taṃ nirvikāro viśikhairvajravegairapūrayat ।। karṇamācchāditaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ । vyādideśānujānsapta tadguptyai kauraveśvaraḥ ।। citrāyudhaḥ śatrusahaḥ śatruḥ śatruṃjayastathā ।
citrāsuścitrasenaśca vikeśaśceti tāndrutam ।। vīrānabhimukhānbāṇaviddhānpavananandanaḥ । unmamātha ratāgrebhyaḥ śailebhyaḥ pādapāniva ।। hateṣu rājaputreṣu teṣu vikramaśāliṣu ।
bhīmakarṇaśaraiḥ kṣipraṃ babhūva janasaṃkṣayaḥ ।। bhīmabāṇavinirbhinnaḥ saṃstambhyādhirathirvyathām । maṇḍalīkṛtakodaṇḍaścakre bāṇamayaṃ nabhaḥ ।। tataḥ karṇaśarāścakrurvyaśvasūtadhanurdhvajam ।
ekībhūtā iva javādbhīmaṃ vismayakāriṇaḥ ।। sarvāyudhāni saṃrabdho virathasyopasarpataḥ । vaikartanaścakartāsya saṃvartaka ivonnadan ।। kṣīṇāyudho atha dviradānhayāṃśca pavanātmajaḥ ।
prāhiṇotsūtaputrāya śaraiściccheda tāṃśca saḥ ।। viṣamasthaṃ raṇe karṇo na jaghāna vṛkodaram । vīraḥ kuntīvacaḥ smṛtvā satyaśīlā hi sādhavaḥ ।। taṃ spṛśanniva cāpena provāca vinadannṛpaḥ ।
mahadbhirmūḍhamā yuddhamakṛtāstraḥ punaḥ kṛthāḥ ।। haṃho bahubhujo neyamucitā tava yuddhabhūḥ । māṃsāstikūṭakuṭṭāka sūdaśālāsu śobhase ।। athavā bhārayogyasya śarīrasyāsya te paśoḥ ।
yuktāstūvarakāḥ sphītāḥ kānane labdhavṛttayaḥ ।। iti bruvāṇe rādheye bhīmaṃ kṛcchradaśāśritam । vilokya dūrātkaṃsāriḥ phlaguṇāya nyavedayat ।। tato muhūrtagaṇane hemarekhānukāriṇī ।
tūrṇaṃ bāṇāvalī karṇaṃ gāṇḍīvapatitāviśat ।। khāṇḍavānalasaṃkrāntaśikhayeva bhṛto bhṛśam । vyāpto dudrāva rādheyo jayoddhūtadhvajāṃśukaḥ ।। bhīmasenapraveśaḥ ।।
ārūḍhe sātyakirathaṃ kopatapte vṛkodare । karṇāya prāhiṇotpārtho nārācaṃ vyomavartmanā ।। vajratulyaṃ tamāyāntaṃ dāruṇaṃ sarvabhūbhujām । dūrādalakṣito drauṇiścicchedāśu patatribhiḥ ।।
athārjuno bāṇaśatairdreṇātmajamapūrayat । so api tatsāyakairbhinnaḥ senāsaṃgaramāviśat ।। tataḥ kanakapṛṣṭhānāṃ śarāṇāṃ dhanuṣāṃ tathā । raśmibhiḥ koparacanā raṭantamiva rājakam ।।
vidārayannāsasāda sūcivyūhaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ । āste mahārathairgupto yatra pāpo jayadrathaḥ ।। atrāntare śarajvālīñakṣitipakānanam । alambiṣo ghanadhvāno garjansātyakimādravat ।।
taṃ rājavaramāyāntaṃ pūrayantaṃ śarairdiśaḥ । avārayanmahānīkaṃ sātyakiḥ satyapauruṣaḥ ।। tayoḥ kāñcanapuṅkhābhiḥ śaramālābhirāvṛtāḥ । siktā vīraraseneva diśaḥ pallavitā babhuḥ ।।
tataścakarta bhallena śirastasyāśu sātyakiḥ । mauliśoṇamaṇicchāyācchuritena samāharan ।। nihatyālambipaṃ vīraṃ pravarāṇāṃ prahāriṇām । śatāni rājaputrāṇāṃ nyavadhītpañca sātyakiḥ ।।
kṣapayantaṃ kurucamūṃ taṃ raṇe dīptavikramam । abhyadhāvadvīraketurvīro bhūriśravāḥ svayam ।। tayorvicitradhanuṣoḥ śaradurdinameghayoḥ । garjitaṃ cakitāḥ sarve rājahaṃsā na sehire ।।
tau mithaḥ śarasaṃpātanirgharṣaṇasamutthitaiḥ । virejatuḥ sphuliṅgaughaiḥ kīṭaratnaurivācalau ।। chitvā parasparaṃ cāpaṃ syandanaṃ saṃpramathya ca । khaṅgacarmadharau vīrau yuyudhāte cirāya tau ।।
javādalakṣyavapuṣościtramaṇḍalacāriṇoḥ । tayoḥ sthagitasaṃgrāmā vīrāḥ prekṣakatāṃ yayuḥ ।। tataḥ sātyakimākṛṣya mālyavadbhiḥ śiroruhaiḥ । hatvā vakṣasi pādena saumadattirapātayat ।।
khaḍgena sātyakiśiraśchettuṃ dṛṣṭvā tamudyatam । uvāca sahasā pārthaṃ saṃbhrāntaḥ kaiṭabhāntakaḥ ।। preṣitaṃ dharmarājena tvadarthaṃ vṛṣṇipuṃgavam । paśya śatruvaśaṃ yātaṃ śrāntaṃ sātyakimāhave ।।
anityau sarvathā nūnaṃ subhaṭānāṃ jayājayau । yadimāṃ sātyakirapi prāptaḥ klībocitāṃ daśām ।। eṣa bhūriśravāstūrṇaṃ khaḍgenākhaṇḍavikramaḥ । samudyataḥ śiro hartuṃ śiṣyasya tava sātyakeḥ ।।
ukte janārdaneneti prahārābhimukhaṃ bhujam । bhallena bhūriśravaso jahāra kapiketanaḥ ।। kṛtte dūrādadṛśyena bhujastambhe kirīṭinā । kālavaktrānnipatitaṃ sātyakiṃ menire janāḥ ।।
patansa bhuvi dordaṇḍaḥ kaṅkaṇāvaliniḥsvanaḥ । ninādairiva kaunteyaṃ tāratārairatarjayat ।। tasmiñjayadvipālāne viśrāntisadane kṣiteḥ । pratāpamandirastambhe bhuje bhuvi nipātite ।।
tyaktvā vāmakarākṛṣṭāṃ sātyakermūrdhajāvalīm । uvācānalpasaṃkalpo yūpaketurdhanaṃjayam ।। aho vīravrataṃ pārtha kīdṛśaṃ darśinaṃ tvayā । yenānyaraṇasaktasya cchadmanā me hato bhujaḥ ।।
ucitaṃ vā tavaivaitanmantrī yasya janārdanaḥ । jātā hṛdyārthalobhena kūṭayuddhavigdhatā ।। ityuktvā vāmahastena śaraśayyāṃ vidhāya saḥ । upaviśya viśannantaḥ sahitaḥ svarśavṛttibhiḥ ।।
hutvā prāṇānalaṃ bāṇairbhrumadhye nihitekṣaṇaḥ । tejaḥ pravidadhe mūrdhni śaśisūryānalottaram ।। tato bībhatsuravadannindāmukharitānnṛpān । vihvalo viṣamātmā ca rakṣitaḥ sātyakirmayā ।।
hantā śiṣyasya sakhyuśca kṛttahastaḥ kṛto yadi । tatra kiṃ nāma manyadhvaṃ nirdeṣā yūyamāhave ।। eko abhimanyurnihataḥ samāyaiḥ sarvapārthivaiḥ । śrāntaśchinnadhanuḥkhaḍgastatkiṃ nāma vadanti naḥ ।।
ityuktavati kaunteye labdhasaṃjño atha sātyakiḥ । yayāce praṇataḥ pūrvaṃ raṇaṃ prāyajuṣo ripoḥ ।। khaḍgena yajñaśīlasya vīrasya yaśasāṃ nidheḥ । vaktraṃ muktāvalībhābhirjātahāsamivāharat ।।
sa kṛṣṇena ca bhūpālairvāryamāṇena saṃbhramāt । krodhādajñātavṛttena tasminsātyakinā hate ।। dhikśabdaḥ sarvavīrāṇāmuttasthau sthagitāmbaraḥ । saumadatteśca caritaṃ praśaśaṃsuḥ surā divi ।।
bhūriśravaso vadhaḥ ।। sa tena nirjitaḥ pūrvaṃ somadatto atimanyunā । ārādhya tapasā devaṃ rūdraṃ tripuradāraṇam ।। lebhe sātyakijetāraṃ bhūriśravasamātmajam ।
śekharaṃ sarvavīrāṇāṃ vadānyaṃ bahuyājinam ।। tasminnipatite vīre jayadrathavadhotsukaḥ । tūrṇaṃ viveśa śvetāśvo nibiḍaṃ rājamaṇḍalam ।। astādricūḍāmaṇitāṃ gantumicchati bhāskare ।
dadarśa saindhavaṃ pārtho guptaṃ sarvairmahārathaiḥ ।। ākarṇāñcitagāṇḍīvastaṃ dūrādduḥsahāgamam । dṛśaiva kopāruṇayā tasya dāhamivākarot ।। tato vilulite sainye parāvṛtta ivāmbudhau ।
hato hataḥ sindhurājo babhūveti mahāsvanaḥ ।। atha karṇakṛpadrauṇiduḥśāsanasuyodhanāḥ । saha sarvairmahīpālairdhanaṃjayamayodhayat ।। tānvidhāya śaraistūrṇaṃ dvastavarmarathadhvajān ।
pātayanrājavaktrāṇi jiṣṇuḥ saindhavamādravat ।। jayadratho api vijayaṃ vilokyācyutasārathim । sa niṣkṛṣyāsakṛttaistaiḥ sāyakaistamapūrayat ।। tato abravīnmadhuripurdinānte savyasācinam ।
chindhi sindhupateḥ kṣipraṃ śiro divyena patriṇā ।। vṛddhakṣattraḥ pitā prādādvaramasya kṣitau śiraḥ । pātayiṣyati yastulyaṃ tasyāpi nipatiṣyati ।। samantapañcakābhyarṇe pitāsya tapasi sthitaḥ ।
tadaṅke pātaya ripoḥ sirastasmātprayātu gām ।। ityukte śauriṇā jiṣṇuśchittvā sindhuśiro javāt । śareṇa saṃdhyādhyānasthajanakāṅke nyapātayat ।। aṅkādajñāsavṛttasya kṣipatastacchiraḥ kṣitau ।
vṛddhakṣattrasya sahasā papātāgre nijaṃ śiraḥ ।। jayadrathavadhaḥ ।। tasminnipatite vīre trailokyāścaryakāriṇā । gāṇḍīvadhanvanā kṛṣṇo nanādāsphoṭayandiśaḥ ।।
tato vighaṭite vyūhe kururājavarūthinī । naurivābdhermahāvātairbabhrāmāvartanartitā ।। bhīmo nanarda taṃ nādaṃ hataṃ matvā jayadratham । prahṛṣṭaḥ pratijagrāha nānāvādyaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।।
akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta hatvā hataḥ pārthena saindhavaḥ । nūnaṃ na durgaṃ daivasya kiṃcidityūcire janāḥ ।। nirvibhāge tato yuddhe pravṛtte nṛpatikṣaye । droṇaṃ kṛpaṃ ca vidadhe śarairjiṣṇuḥ parāṅmukham ।।
bhīmasāyakanirbhinnajihvākarṇaṃ ca sātyakiḥ । āruroha rathaṃ vīro vitīrṇa hariṇā nijam ।। māruteravamānaṃ ca kalayañśatamanyujaḥ । punaḥ pratijñāṃ karṇasya vṛṣasenavadhe vyadhāt ।।
tato yudhiṣṭhiraṃ prāpya tau ca sātyakiphalguṇau । mithaḥ śaśaṃsuḥ pramadādabhinandya parākramam ।। kṛṣṇāvatha pariṣvajya mānandaṃ dharmanandanaḥ । tuṣṭāva jagatāṃ nāthaṃ viṣṇuṃ vijayakāraṇam ।।
bāṣpākulastato rājā droṇametya suyodhanaḥ । ūce tvayā kṛtāśvāso nihataḥ sa jayadrathaḥ ।। śrutvaitadavadaddroṇo nidhanāyaiva dīkṣitaḥ । tyakṣyāmi kavacaṃ rājannāhatvā tava vairiṇaḥ ।।
ācāryeṇetyabhihite sarve duryodhanānugāḥ । prāṇahavye raṇamakhe tasthurābaddhaniścayāḥ ।। athāṃśumati yāte astaṃ dinakṛtkamalatviṣi । śoṇacchatra ivākṛṣṭe saṃdhyāraktasaritplavaiḥ ।।
nakṣatraistārataralaiḥ kopakampajuṣāṃ raṇe । hatānāṃ bhūbhunāṃ jīvairiva vyāpte nabhastale ।। tamobhirāvṛte vyomni kṛpāṇavanameckaiḥ । divyāstradagdhairmātaṅgairiva tridivagāmibhiḥ ।।
visphuranmaulikeyūrahemasāyakakārmukāḥ । cakrire samaraṃ ghoraṃ duryodhanamukhāḥ paraiḥ ।। arjunadhvānagarjābhiḥ siṃhanādaiśca māruteḥ । droṇakārmukanirghoṣaiḥ pṛthivī samakampata ।।
aśrāntaṃ yudhyamānānāṃ kurupāṇḍavabhūbhujām । babhau sākṣādivāyātā kālarātrirvibhāvarī ।। prāpustamāṃsi vaipulyaṃ khaḍgeṣu dviradeṣu ca । prāpustamāṃsi dāridryaṃ chattreṣu vyajaneṣu ca ।।
gṛdhrabhūtotsave tasminvikarālā vasuṃdharā । avartamānamānena tamaseva vidāritā ।। dattavetālatālo abhūdakāṇḍadhṛtikhaṇḍanaḥ । kabandhoddaṇḍadordaṇḍatāṇḍavāḍambarotsavaḥ ।।
śirastrakaṅkaṭāpātiśastrajvālājaṭā babhuḥ । tamaḥpiśācasaṃghānāṃ piṅgāḥ śmaśrusaṭā iva ।। tatra droṇo mahāstraughaiḥ kṣapayanrājamaṇḍalam । ādīptaratnamukuṭaṃ proccakarta śineḥ śiraḥ ।।
bhīmaseno api kāliṅgaṃ rājaputraṃ tarasvinam । rathādrathamabhiplutya nijaghānāśu muṣṭinā ।। tasya muṣṭihatasyājau peturasthīni bhūtale । phalgunyaśmahatasyeva cirapakvasya śākhinaḥ ।।
kaliṅgakulasaṃhāraṃ kṛtvā tūrṇaṃ vṛkodaraḥ । dhruvaṃ ca jaladhāraṃ ca rājaputrāvadārayat ।। vidhāya vimukhaṃ karṇaṃ bhīmo duryodhanānujam । niṣpipeṣa padā hatvā vīro duṣkaradurmadaḥ ।।
somadattasya tanayaṃ śalaṃ hatvātha sātyakiḥ । taṃ putraśokavidhuraṃ cakāra vimukhaṃ śaraiḥ ।। dārayantaṃ kurucamūṃ sātyakiṃ śaravarṣiṇam । diśaḥ saṃpūrayanbāṇairaśvatthāmā samādravat ।।
kṣapayantamanīkāni dṛṣṭvā rudramivāparam । niśīthe dviguṇotsāhastamadhāvaddhaṭotkacaḥ ।। tasya nādena mahatā diśaḥ samabhipūritāḥ । sphuṭitā yatra dalaśastadāścaryamivābhavat ।।
aśvatthāmni prabhādhāmni bāṇograkiraṇe raṇe । kurvanghaṭotkaco reje rāhujṛmbhāvijṛmbhitam ।। śarāṇāṃ drauṇimuktānāṃ divyānāṃ samare rucaḥ । na kūṇitāni netrāṇi rātrau bhūtāni sehire ।।
akṣauhiṇīṃ rākṣasānāṃ haiḍambavaśavartinām । taṭāyudhāni dalayanneko drauṇirayodhayat ।। chittvā ghaṭotkaṭo hṛṣṭaṃ cakraṃ kālānalaprabham । jaghānāñjanaparvāṇaṃ tatputraṃ ghoravikramam ।।
tato vimohanīṃ māyāṃ drauṇiḥ kruddhasya rakṣasaḥ । chittvā jaghāna visikhairdhṛmnānujānraṇe ।। kuntibhojasutānhatvā sahasrāṇi prahāriṇām । jaghāna rājaputrāṇāṃ drauṇiḥ kāla ivākulaḥ ।।
atrāntare bhīmaseno bāhlikādhipateḥ śiraḥ । gadayā vīraghātinyā niṣpipeṣāśu maulinaḥ ।। tato jaghāna saṃrabdhāndaśa duryodhanānujān । vīrabāhuṃ dṛḍharathaṃ nāgadantamayobhujam ।।
pramāthinaṃ virajasaṃ suhastaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ tathā । hatvaitānsapta gāndhārānavadhītsubalātmajān ।। nighnantaṃ kauravacamūṃ svayaṃ yudhi yudhiṣṭhiram । aindravāruṇavāyavyairastrairdreṇo apyayodhayat ।।
tataḥ prayuktaṃ brahmāstraṃ guruṇā tajjihīrṣayā । avārayadasaṃrambho brahmāstreṇaiva dharmajaḥ ।। sānugaiḥ pāṇḍutanayairgajairiva sarojinīm । mṛdyamānāṃ camūṃ dṛṣṭvā karṇamūce suyodhanaḥ ।।
karṇākarṇaya saṃgrāme jayibhiḥ pāṇḍusūnubhiḥ । virāvaṃ vadhyamānānāṃ sainyānāṃ ca tarasvinām ।। tumule asminnirāloke viṣame samupasthite । tejasāmāśrayaḥ śūra tvamevaikaḥ parāyaṇam ।।
praṇayāditi rādheyo bhūbhujā svayamarthitaḥ । uvāca pāṇḍusenāsu kṣipanniva śaravalīḥ ।। vīraśayyāsthite bhīṣme śekhare sarvadhanvinām । rājanbhāraḥ kramāyāto mamaivāyaṃ kimucyate ।।
adya vīravrataharaṃ harasyāpi kirīṭinam । pātayāmyeṣa samare śaktyā vāsavadattayā ।। ityukte sūtaputreṇa provāca prahasankṛpaḥ । loke sūtyamavīre asminnekastvaṃ vīratāṃ gataḥ ।।
aho nu mithyā rādheya kathitena tāvamunā । satataṃ sarvavīrāṇāṃ śravaṇau badhirīkṛtau ।। kutastvamaśrutodanta ivāyātaḥ parākramī । yadā hataḥ sindhupatiḥ kṛtavānna bhavāṃstadā ।।
dṛṣṭasārā vayaṃ sarve tava pāṇḍusutasya ca । balānusāraṃ yudhyasva vṛthā ślāghāṃ tu mā kṛtāḥ ।। iti śāradvatenokte kopādvaikartano abravīt । garjanti saphalaṃ vīrāḥ prāvṛṣeṇyā ivāmbudāḥ ।।
tvaṃ tu vṛddha nirācāro mohādevaṃ prabhāṣase । anyapakṣāśrayaḥ ko hi bandīvānyānpraśaṃsati ।। brahmabandho punardveṣādyadyevamabhidhāsyati । chetasyāmi jihvāṃ kaṭukāṃ tadanenāsinā tava ।।
iti karṇena saṃrambhātkopitaṃ vīkṣya mātulam । karavālamathākṛṣya krudhyaṃstaṃ drauṇirādravat ।। rudratulyaṃ tamāyāntaṃ trijagatpralayakṣamam । nyavārayatsvayaṃ rājā nayavāgbhiḥ sagautamam ।।
droṇikarṇau prasādyātha kururāje raṇonmukhaḥ । viveśa pāṇḍavacamūṃ saha sarvairmahārathaiḥ ।। ākarṇāñcitakodaṇḍamuktaiḥ karṇaśaraistathā । abhūdyaudhiṣṭhiraṃ sainyaṃ viprakīrṇaṃ samantataḥ ।।
śaratvālākarālaṃ taṃ karṇapāvakamutkaṭam । abhyetya pārthajalado bāṇadhārābhirāvṛṇot ।। kṣaṇādathārjunaśaracchinnacāparathadhvajaḥ । karṇaḥ kṛpasyāruhoha rathaṃ bhagnamanorathaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaṃ vīraṃ yudhyamānamarātibhiḥ । jaghāna pāñcālacamūṃ drauṇirāhavadurmadaḥ ।। sahasraśo vadhyamānāḥ kṣatrakānanavahninā । pāñcālā droṇaputreṇa hataśeṣā diśo yayuḥ ।।
dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ tato jitvā vīraṃ hatvāsya cānugān । drauṇirāyodhanaṃ cakre kṛtāntodyānavibhramam ।। bhīmārjunābhyāṃ sahitaḥ svayaṃ rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । vidrāvya kauravīṃ senāṃ droṇaśeṣāmivākarot ।।
somadattamathāyāntaṃ sātyakiḥ pṛthuvikramam । ayodhavadasaṃbhrāntaḥ kumāra iva tārakam ।। tadbāṇaśatanirbhinno vyathāṃ saṃstambya sātyakiḥ । śareṇāśanitulyena vidārya tamapātayat ।।
tato droṇārjunaraṇe divyāstragrāmaduḥsahe । babhau raktāmbaravatī kālarātrīva śarvarī ।। tataḥ kirīṭipramukhairdraiṇikṛperitaiḥ । sainyānāṃ bhajyamānānāṃ babhūva bhayado ravaḥ ।।
tato duryodhanādeśādgāḍhe tamasi saṃtataiḥ । dīpairyuyudhire vīrā gajāśvetsaṅgasaṅgibhiḥ ।। te sene dīpanikarairabhito babhatuḥ kṣaṇāt । hatānāṃ kaṇaśo yātaistejobhiriva bhūbhujām ।।
virejustānyanīkāni dīpaiḥ khaḍgeṣu bimbitaiḥ । jvalitāni vanānīva naktamoṣadhimaṇḍalaiḥ ।। dīpadīptā narendrāṇāṃ ratnābharaṇarociṣaḥ । tamaḥkaṣaṇapāṣāṇe hemalekhā ivābabhuḥ ।।
tato vimardanaṣṭeṣu teṣu dīpeṣu saṃgare । niśītho yauvanaṃ prāpa vairāṇyapanayairiva ।। nirvibhāge tato yuddhe pravṛtte śauryaśālini । svayaṃ jite dharmajena sānuge kauraveśvare ।।
mṛtyuvīthīmapi prāptaṃ sahadevamavārayat । na jaghāna raṇe karṇaḥ smarankuntīvaco muhuḥ ।। tataḥ karṇasuto vīro vṛṣaseno arivāhinīm । viveśāstrāvalījvālālīḍhakṣattriyakānanaḥ ।।
vidrāviteṣu vīreṣu vṛṣasenena sāyakaiḥ । kupito draupado roṣātkurusainyaṃ vyadārayat ।। vartamāne raṇe ghore bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ । dhṛṣṭadyumno avadhīdvīraṃ drumasenaṃ narādhipam ।।
tato duryodhanagirā droṇakarṇau mahībhujām । kṛttaiḥ śirobhiścakrāte bhuvi padmākarāniva ।। dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhāñjitvā kṣapitānīkanāyakaḥ । vidrāvya pāṇḍavacamūṃ karṇaścakre nṛpakṣayam ।।
taṃ karṇaṃ sāyakānena kirantaṃ tejasāṃ nidhim । na sehire pare draṣṭuṃ raṇe tapanasaṃbhavam ।। bhajyamāneṣvanīkeṣu karṇena raṇaśālinā । jayāśā pāṇḍuputrāṇāṃ sakalā tanutāṃ yayau ।।
atha kṛṣṇasya vacanātkṛṣṇarātrau ghaṭotkacaḥ । avadhīttvaritaṃ karṇaṃ kṛṣṇākopa ivāpatan ।। tasminnabhyudgate dīptaśmaśrujihvāvilocane । vāhinyaḥ śatadhā jagmuḥ pratāpapatitā iva ।।
sa tadā jaladacchāyo bhrukuṭī vidyudutkaṭaḥ । sphārābhiḥ śatadhārābhiḥ pārthaḥ karṇamapūrayat ।। āsthitastaptahemāṅgaṃ caturhastaśataṃ ratham । sarvākārasya lagnāgnernīlādrerupamākṣamam ।।
daśahastaparīṇāhaṃ dadhāno bhāsuraṃ dhanuḥ । dāvānalaprajvalitaṃ mahāsālamivānalaḥ ।। visphuratsphāramukuṭo dīptajāmbūnadāṅgadaḥ । tamaḥśailaśikhāsajjo babhau vighaṭayanniva ।।
aṭṭahāsapaṭurnādastasyābhūttamasāmiva । taṃ dṛṣṭvā vikaṭājvālaṃ pāṭitānāṃ vyathāravaḥ ।। vidruteṣvarisainyeṣu saṃbhogārheṣu rājasu । rādheyagirirevāsya jagrāha śaradurdinam ।।
athāṅgarājarakṣāyai jaṭāsurasuto balī । kauraveśvaramāmantrya samabhyāyādalambusaḥ ।। tatastasyābhavaddhoraḥ saṃprahāraḥ prahāriṇā । ghaṭotkacena saśtrāstraśilāpāvakavarṣiṇaḥ ।।
tayormāyāmayāścaryakūṭaprakaṭayodhinoḥ । ūrjitaiḥ śataśo yodhā garjitairvyasavo abhavat ।। rathādrathamabhidrutya tato bhaimiralambusam । dorbhyāṃ mittramivāliṅgya gāḍhagāḍhamapīḍayat ।।
tasya niṣpīḍyamānasya niryayuḥ srotasāṃ mukhaiḥ । sadhūmāḥ sānalajvālāḥ saśabdaṃ śoṇitacchaṭāḥ ।। tato bhuvi viniṣpiṣya rāviṇaṃ taṃ ghaṭotkacaḥ । uddhṛtya tacchiro vegādduryodhanamathāyayau ।।
tamuvāca hato ayaṃ te mayā bandhurniśācaraḥ । priyasya pātaya śiraḥ punareva nṛpādham ।। uktvaitatkarṇamabhyāyādvinadanrajanīcaraḥ । caṇḍānilasamuddhūtaḥ kālameva ivākulaḥ ।।
alambusavadhaḥ ।। tataḥ pravṛtte samare ghore rādheyarakṣasoḥ । rāmarāvaṇasaṃgrāmamasmaranvibudhā divi ।। stambhapramāṇairviśakhairjvalitairulmukairiva ।
viddho api rakṣasā karṇo na cacāla mahāśayaḥ ।। atha krodhavinirmuktairvipulaiḥ karṇasāyakaiḥ । nirbhinno rākṣasaścakraṃ prāhiṇotkarṇapāvakam ।। prekṣya cāyatsahasrāraṃ tejaḥpiñjaritāmbaram ।
cakāra khaṇḍaśaścakraṃ karṇaḥ sāvegamāśugaiḥ ।। tato ghaṭotkacaḥ kopānmāyāṃ kṛtvā vimohanīm । piṣṭvā sūtadhjarathaṃ viśālamaviśannabhaḥ ।। śāntatejomaye vahnau tārā tārāsthisaṃkule ।
vyoma śmaśāne tasyāsanmattavetālakoṭayaḥ ।। muhurgajo muhuḥ siṃhaḥ kṣaṇaṃ meghaḥ kṣaṇaṃ giriḥ । sarvabhūtamahākāyo varṣansa vipulāḥ śilāḥ ।। bhuvo vahniṃ divaḥ śastraṃ digbhyo rākṣasamaṇḍalam ।
visṛjankurusenāsu vaikartanamayodhayat ।। tato vidhūya tāṃ māyāṃ karṇo divyāstratejasā । nirdahanpāṇḍavacamūṃ rakṣo vivyādha sāyakaiḥ ।। heḍihanpāṇḍava yātudhānānsahasraśaḥ ।
karṇo dhanuṣmatāṃ dhuryo vibabhau rāmavikramaḥ ।। aṣṭāṣṭacakrāmaśaniṃ kālajihvavibhīṣaṇām । bhaimaḥ sasarja karṇāya svayaṃ rudreṇa nirmitām ।। visṛṣṭā rākṣasendreṇa śailasaṃghapramāthinī ।
sā bhasmasānmahāghoṣā rathamādhirathervyadhāt ।। tato aparaṃ samāsthāya syandanaṃ sūtanandanaḥ । piśācavadanānanyāñjaghāna piśitāśinaḥ ।। virathaḥ kopahutabhugjvālāvalayitekṣaṇaḥ ।
ghaṭotkaco mahāmāyaḥ punarantaradhīyata ।। atrāntare rākṣasendro bakasya dayitaḥ sakhā । suyodhanābhyanujñāto bīmamāyādalāyudhaḥ ।। hayānāṃ hastikarṇānāṃ piśācamukhavarcasām ।
yukte śatena gambhīranirghoṣe syāndane sthitam ।। taṃ bhīmaḥ pratijagrāha saṃrambhagurugarjitam । siddhamantra ivākampo vīro vetālamutthitam ।। ākīryamāṇo ghoreṇa śilaśastrastravarṣiṇā ।
rākṣasena gadāṃ bhīmaḥ prāhiṇottadvadhāśayā ।। tāṃ gadāṃ gadayā rakṣo hatvā jāmbūnadāṅgadām । nadannakālajaladadhvānadhīraḥ khamāviśat ।। alāyudhena saṃsaktaṃ rajanyāṃ kūṭayodhinā ।
bhīmaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃdehākulito abhavat ।। tataḥ śaurergirā vīraḥ pravaro raudrakarmaṇām । alāyudhaṃ samabhyāyāttyaktvā karṇaṃ ghaṭotkacaḥ ।। tayoḥ saṃrabdhayorvyomni saṃnipāto ghanasvanaḥ ।
abhūdbhṛśaṃ śilāśastranirgharṣoddhūtapāvakaḥ ।। citāgnipaṅgalaśmaśrujaṭābhīṣaṇayostayoḥ । dantaniṣpeṣasaṃjātāḥ sphuliṅgā iva babhramuḥ ।। agnikuṇḍopamānābhyāṃ kuṇḍalābhyāṃ virājitam ।
alāyudhasyāśu śiraściccheda ca ghaṭotkacaḥ ।। alāyudhavadhaḥ ।। taṃ hatvā vinadanghoraṃ haiḍimbo ghoravikramaḥ । drutaṃ karṇaṃ samabhyetya śilavarṣairatāḍayat ।।
vaikartano api pārthānāṃ kṣapayitvā varūthinīm । ghaṭotkacasaṃbhrāntaḥ śarajālairapūrayat ।। athāstreṇa rathaṃ hatvā karṇasya rajanīcaraḥ । trijaganmohanīṃ māyāṃ samādāyāviśannabhaḥ ।।
ulmukairāyudhairvṛkṣaiḥ śilābhiḥ parvataistathā । sa jaghāna mahāghoṣaḥ kauravāṇāmanīkinīm ।। niśīthe sarvavīreṣu yudhyamāneṣu rakṣasā । dudruvuḥ pṛthivīpālā bhagnasyandanakuñjarāḥ ।।
saṃhāre sarvayodhānāṃ tasminnatibhayaṃkare । niṣkampaḥ samare karṇaḥ sāyakaiḥ khamapūrayat ।। gagane vidhyamānānāṃ śilānāṃ karṇamārgaṇaiḥ । jvālājālajaṭālānāmabhūccaṭacaṭāravaḥ ।।
tataḥ parighanistriṃśaśataghniprāsamudgarāḥ । satriśūlagadācakrabhusuṇḍiśaratomarāḥ ।। karṇānane rākṣasena prāsta viṣamayodhinā । cakrire kauravānīkaṃ hataṃ kālaśatairiva ।।
vidrute ca tathā sainye raktakulyāvarohini । vidyamāne nirādhāre rādheye dhairyaśālini ।। svastītyuktvā prayāteṣu vyomnaḥ siddhasurarṣiṣu । akampata jagatsarvaṃ rākṣasendrasya māyayā ।।
yudhyamānaṃ tato vīraṃ karṇamabhyetya kauravaḥ । avadatsarvasaṃhārasaṃtrāsāyāsakātaraḥ ।। tvayārjunavadhe śaktirdhāryate kimanarthakā । asminniśīthe ko hyasmānmucyate yaḥ punarjayet ।।
etadākarṇya rādheyaḥ śakradattāṃ mahāprabhām । ekavīravadhāyattāṃ suciraṃ parirakṣitām ।। dāraṇīṃ daityasaṅghānāmutsasarja nabhastale । yasyā jvālāvalīdhāmnā sīmantitamivābhavat ।।
tejasvino rākṣasasya dṛḍhaṃ vakṣo vidārya sā । jagāma tridivaṃ dīptā prāṇaśaktirivāparā ।। dagdhamāyastadā kṣipraṃ haiḍimbo mandarākṛtiḥ । patannirbhinnahṛdayaḥ pipeṣa kuruvāhinīm ।।
rātriyuddhe ghaṭotkacavadhaḥ ।। hate ghaṭotkace vīre daśakaṇṭhaparākrame । prahṛṣṭāḥ kuravaḥ karṇaṃ rāmopamamapūjayan ।। śaktihīne tataḥ karṇe nadatkāliyasūdanaḥ ।
viṣṇo pāṇḍavānīke nanartānandanirbharaḥ ।। valatpītāṃśukāstasya nṛtyato vibabhurbhujāḥ । sphūrjatikañjalkapaṭalā vātalolā iva drumāḥ ।। tamūce nindayanpārtho haiḍimbavadhaduḥkhitaḥ ।
ko ayaṃ viṣādasamaye praharṣaste janārdana ।। śrutvaitadabravītkṛṣṇo jitaḥ karṇo adhunā sakhe । haiḍimbavapuṣaḥ prāṇaścintācapalacetasaḥ ।। śaktiśca karṇadordaṇḍātsamaṃ yātā jayāya vaḥ ।
ekalavyajarāsaṃdhaśiśupālādayo mayā ।। purā yuddhamidaṃ jñātvā durjayāḥ śaktibhirhatāḥ । evameva raṇe karṇo na jeyastridaśairapi ।। kiṃ punarghorayā pārtha śaktyā vāsavadattayā ।
tvayi notsṛṣṭavāñśaktiṃ satataṃ mohito mayā । karṇa pratiniśaṃ pāpaiḥ preryamāṇo api kauravaiḥ ।। ityuktavati dāśārhe siddhavīravadhārditāḥ । nirvibhāgaṃ yuyudhire krodhāndhāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ ।।
haiḍimbe nihate rājā śokatapto yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । āśvāsitaḥ keśavena kupittaḥ karṇamādravat ।। nṛpairanugataḥ sarvaiḥ praviṣṭaḥ kuruvāhinīm । abhyetya bhagavānvyāso dharmarājamabhāṣata ।।
diṣṭyā nādhiratheḥ śaktyā kṛtaṃ jagadanarjunam । adhunā vīra yudhyasva niḥsaṃrambhamanākulaḥ ।। itaścaturbhirdivasairna bhaviṣyanti bhūmipāḥ । dharmavīra tjaja krodhaṃ sadā dharmānugo jayaḥ ।।
ityuktvāntarhite vyāse bhīmārjunayudhiṣṭhirāḥ । cakrire samaraṃ ghoraṃ droṇakarṇakṛpādibhiḥ ।। sā kālarātriḥ śūrāṇāmutsavo yakṣarakṣasām । sahasrayāmatāṃ yātā triyāmābūnmahībhujām ।।
tato nidrākule sainye śānte śastrakṛtakṣate । dṛṣṭvā jagāda kāruṇyācchvetāśvo yaśasāṃ nidhiḥ ।। muhurte asminnirāloke khinnāḥ sarve mahārathāḥ । kṣaṇaṃ bhajantu viśrāntiṃ nidrāmukulitekṣaṇāḥ ।।
ityukte sainikāḥ sarve praśaṃsanto dhanaṃjayam । kṣaṇaṃ gajarathaskandaniṣṇṇāstatyajuḥ śramam ।। niḥsyandanāgaturagā niscalacchatracāmarāḥ । aṅkanyastāyudhabhāṭāstāḥ senā niścalā bhabhuḥ ।।
athodyayau vyomakṛpāṇapaṭṭadantatsaruḥ kāntisarinmarālaḥ । candro jagatkuñjarakarṇaśaṅkho digaṅganāmaṇḍanadarpaṇaśrīḥ ।। tataḥ samastavīrāṇāṃ saṃmukhāhavapātinām । yaśobhiriva śītāṃśuraṃśubhirdyāmapūrayat ।।
tuṣārahararuciraiḥ kiraṇairamṛtatviṣaḥ । cāmarairiva bhūpālā vījyamānāḥ kṣaṇaṃ babhuḥ ।। śareṣvaṅkuritaścandraḥ sāndraṃ pallavitomiṃṣu । hareṣu phullito rājñāṃ śaṅkheṣu phalito abhavat ।।
pratibimbagato raktataṭinīṣu niśākaraḥ । babhau saṃdhyāsaveneva ghūrṇamānāruṇacchaviḥ ।। tataḥ kṣīṇe kṣapākāle dhvajinī rājayakṣmaṇi । udyayau śoṇitātāmro bhagavānvāsareśvaraḥ ।।
caturthadivase rātriyuddham ।। duryodhanena vākyalyairarditaḥ kumbhasaṃbhavaḥ । tato dadāha divyāstrairanastrajñānapi krudhā ।। punaḥ pravṛtte samare nirmaryāde jagatkṣaye ।
droṇena vadhyamānānāmānandastumulo abhavat ।। tasminnakālakalpānte rudraḥ kiṃ vāpuṣāmunā । saṃhartumudyato lokānityūcurvyomacāriṇaḥ ।। cedisomakapāñcālamatsyakekayasṛñjayāḥ ।
na śarma lebhire vīrāḥ pīḍitā droṇasāyakaiḥ ।। tato virāṭadrupadau bhāradvājaṃ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ । saṃcchādya cakratuḥ kṣipraṃ vismayaṃ tava dhanvinām ।। droṇo atha pārṣatasutānhatvā vipulavikramān ।
kaṇṭhāñjahāra bhallābhyāṃ virāṭadrupadau samam ।। virāṭadrupadavadhaḥ ।। matsyapāñcālasenāsu bhagnāsu pavanātmajaḥ । dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhaiḥ sārdhaṃ droṇānīkamupādravat ।।
karṇasaubalahārdikyaduḥśāsanamukhāstataḥ । bhīmapārṣatasaineyaphalgunādyānayodhayan ।। saṃghaṭṭaḥ sarvavīrāṇāṃ tumule saṃprahāriṇi । āyātsollolakīlālakulyā kallolamālinī ।।
pāñcālacedimatsyānāṃ kurvāṇāṃ kadanaṃ raṇe । droṇaṃ vilokya kaṃsārirbabhāṣe pāṇḍunandanam ।। jāmadagnyasya śiṣyo ayaṃ pravṛddhaḥ kṣatriyānalaḥ । divyāstraduḥsahaśikhaḥ soḍhuṃ naḥ kena pāryate ।।
sarvātmanā yudhyamāno durjayaḥ sāyudho guruḥ । udyataḥ kartumadyaiva jāne niṣpāṇḍavaṃ jagat ।। putraṃ tu nihataṃ śrutvā dhruvameṣa na yotsyate । tasmādyuktimupāśritya jaye nītirvidhīyatām ।।
śrutvaitadarjune karṇau pidhāyādhomukhasthite । kathaṃcidabhyupagamānmūke pāṇḍavabhūpatau ।। aśvatthāmābhidhaṃ hatvā gadayā madakuñjaram । uccaiḥ putravadhaṃ bhīmo droṇamaśrāvayatpuraḥ ।।
lajjamānena bhīmena vyāhṛtaṃ bhṛśamapriyam । durjayaṃ tanayaṃ matvā droṇo mene na tattathā ।। sa praviśyātha pāñcālāndhṛṣṭadyumnajighāṃsayā । jaghāna vīrayodhānāṃ rathānāmayutāni ṣaṭ ।।
cedipāñcālamatsyānāṃ brahmastreṇogravikramaḥ । prayutānyadahatkruddho droṇo rudra ivāparaḥ ।। nighnanprabhadrakānvīrānsomakāśca prahāriṇaḥ । caturvarṣaśato darpādyuveva vicacāra saḥ ।।
ṛṣayo atha samabhyetya taṃ krūratarakāriṇam । tasmādavārayanghorāllokasaṃhāravaiśasāt ।। munisaṃghe gate vyomnā droṇo bhīmavacaḥ smaran । yudhiṣṭhiraṃ śaṅkitadhīrapṛcchatsatyavikramam ।।
govindenārthito yatnāllokasaṃhāraśāntaye । yudhiṣṭhirastadevoktvā svairaṃ hastītyabhāṣata ।। aspṛśanto hayā bhūmimavahanye yudhiṣṭhiram । te nīcagāminastūrṇamasatyaguravo abhavan ।।
tataḥ saviṣanārācairnirbhinna iva marmasu । niścityātmavadhaṃ droṇaścitrārpita ivābhavat ।। taṃ jihvādīptaviśikho dhṛṣṭadyumno avadaddrutam । aho tanu brāhmaṇo bhūtvā piśitāśīva niṣkṛpaḥ ।
karoṣi kaluṣaṃ karma nihate api priye sute ।। tacchrutvā sahasā droṇastyaktvā cāpaṃ saha krudhā । dattvā sarvābhayaṃ maunī dadarśa jyotirāntaram ।। tasya ṣaṭkośasaṃghasya saṃpuṭatrayapātanāt ।
brahmarandhraviniṣkrāntaṃ jyotirvyoma samāviśat ।। atrāntare samākṛṣya dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śiroruhaiḥ । krodhāndhaḥ pāṇḍutanayairvāryamāṇo api saṃbhramam ।। gurorakṛṣṭaśastrasya dhāmni saṃkrāntatejasaḥ ।
śiro jahāra khaḍgena dhikkṛtaḥ sravarājabhiḥ ।। droṇavadhaḥ ।। hate rukmarathe vīre gurau sarvadhanuṣmatām । saṃbhrāntā dudruvuḥ sarve kauravāṇāṃ mahārathāḥ ।।
bhagnaṃ kurubalaṃ dṛṣṭvā śaṅkito droṇanandanaḥ । kimetaditi papraccha sāśrunetraṃ suyodhanam ।। tasminnadhomukhe duḥkhāddhoraṃ vaktumanīśvare । tatpreritaḥ pitṛvadhaṃ gautamo asmau nyavedayat ।।
śrutvā sa vaiśasaṃ ghoraṃ chadmanā vihitaṃ gurau । pāñcālyena nṛśaṃsena jajvāla krodhavahninā ।। tasya niḥśvasataḥ kopātkālasyeva didhakṣataḥ । saṃrambhaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ babhūvātibhayaṃkaraḥ ।।
niṣpiṣyapāṇinā pāṇiṃ so abravītsāśrulocanaḥ । aho mamāpi janakaḥ keśagrahaṇamāptavān ।। ghātayitvā mṛṣāvādī guruṃ rājā bakavrataḥ । mayi jīvati kaunteyaḥ kathaṃ prāpsyati medinīm ।।
adya matkopanirdagdhe pāṇḍuputre sarājake । bhārgavasya smariṣyanti vīrāḥ kṣattrakulacchidaḥ ।। kṛtvādya pārṣatapaśuṃ krodhāgnerupahāratām । akṛṣṇapārthāṃ pṛthivīmeṣo ahaṃ kartumudyataḥ ।।
purā mahyaṃ pitā prādādastraṃ nārāyaṇoditam । tenādya saṃhṛtāṃllokānmayā paśyantu khecarāḥ ।। ityuktvā saṃdadhe dhīptaṃ tadastraṃ niyataḥ śuciḥ । yenāśvatthadalālolā vicacālajagattrayī ।।
tato nanāda manthādrikṣubhitāmbhodhiniḥsvanam । drauṇiryena diśaḥ sarvā yayuḥ śakalatāmiva ।। tato vyathitamālokya svasainyaṃ śvetavāhanaḥ । jagāda dharmatanayaṃ śvasannanuśayākulaḥ ।
vyājādvibhavalubdhena śiṣyeṇa nihato guruḥ ।। iti pralāpamukhare surarājasute guroḥ । kopādātāmranayanaḥ provāca pavanātmajaḥ ।। na nāma munivatpārtha kṣattriyo vaktumarhasi ।
ghorāpakāre kaḥ śatrau raṇe nyāyamupekṣate ।। asminmama bhuje vīre gadāpraṇayini sthite । tvayi kṛṣṇe ca kiṃ nāma drauṇiślāghābhinandyate ।। ityukte bhīmasenena pārṣator'junamabravīt ।
lokāntako vikarmastho brahmabandhurhato mayā ।। brahmāstreṇa hato yena muktavarmā pṛthagjanaḥ । sarvopāyaiḥ sa hantavyo asuravadviśvakaṇṭakaḥ ।। tvayā hataḥ kathaṃ bhīṣmaḥ sa ca prāgjyotiṣeśvaraḥ ।
pituḥ sakhā kimetena gahanā vīravṛttayaḥ ।। dhṛṣṭadyumnavacaḥ śrutvā tiryagjihmīkṛtekṣaṇaḥ । niḥśvasya kopasaṃtapto dhigdhigityarjuno abravīt ।। lajjānate dharmasute mūkībhūteṣu rājasu ।
sātyakiḥ kopasaṃtapto dhṛṣṭadyumnamabhāṣata ।। bata pāpa vayaṃ sarve ye gurughnaṃ puraḥ sthitam । svastivatpratibhāṣante hantavyaṃ tvāṃ prayatnataḥ ।। ityuktavati śaineye jagāda drupadātmajaḥ ।
aho nu paradoṣajño nirdeṣa iva bhāṣase ।। bhūriśravāḥ prāyagataḥ kṛttabāhuḥ kirīṭinā । nṛśaṃsa patitācāra kenānyena nipātitaḥ ।। naitadvācyaṃ tvayā bhūpo bāṇaistvāmanyathā śitaiḥ ।
karomi śikṣāgurubhirvinayāvanivartinam ।। iti bruvāṇau saṃrambhāttau mitho hantumudyatau । ni vārayatkṛṣṇagirā bhīmasenaḥ sahānujaiḥ ।। tataḥ kṣaṇātsamāvṛtte kururājabalārṇave ।
droṇātmajāstrapihitā nālakṣyanta diśo daśa ।। nārāyaṇāstraniḥsṛtaiḥ pradīptāyudhamaṇḍalaiḥ । badhyamānālpaśeṣābhūtpāṇḍavānāmanīkinī ।। tasminnāyudhasaṃgharṣajātajvālāśatākule ।
ghore subhaṭasaṃhāre trasto rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। uvāca pārṣatamukhānvīkṣamāṇaḥ kirīṭinam । palāyantāmitaḥ sarve mahadbhayamupasthitam ।। mādhyasthyamāsthito jiṣṇuḥ kopito nidhanādguroḥ ।
yenābhimanyurvṛddhena vyājādbālo nipātitaḥ ।। satyajitpramukhā yena hatāste te mahārathāḥ । durbhedyaṃ kavacaṃ prādāddivyaṃ duryodhanāya yaḥ ।। kriyatāṃ nādhunā yuddhaṃ svasti pārthāya dhīmate ।
evaṃ vahniṃ pravekṣyāmi drauṇiṃ kālaṃ saheta kaḥ ।। ityukte dharmarājena bhujāvutkṣipya keśavaḥ । uccairuvāca bhūpālāñjvalitānstratejasā ।। bho bhoḥ śastraṃ parityajya rathebhyo vrajata kṣitim ।
astreṇānena hanyante na viśastrā bhuvi sthitāḥ ।। iti bruvāṇe saṃrambhātsāvegaṃ kaiṭabhadviṣi । bhīmo babhāṣe bhūpālānabhayaṃ kartumarhatha ।। eṣo ahaṃ samayaprakhyāṃ gadāmādāya daṃśitaḥ ।
drauṇimabhyudyato hantuṃ paśyantu kurupāṇḍavāḥ ।। iti garjantamāyāntaṃ pāvaniṃ droṇanandanaḥ । hasanmūḍho ayamityuktvā śarajālairapūrayat ।। tato nārāyaṇāstreṇa dahyamānāḥ samantataḥ ।
avātaranvāhanebhya śastrāṇyutsṛjya bhūmipāḥ ।। rathe sthitaṃ yudhyamānaṃ bhīmasenamasaṃbhramāt । astrajvālāvalīcakramekībhūtaṃ samāpatat ।। prajavāgniśikhākūṭasaṃghaṭṭantaritaṃ kṣaṇāt ।
arjuno bhīmamālokya varuṇāstramavāsṝjat ।। nārāyaṇāstradahanaistadastramabhito hatam । modhīkṛtaṃ kṣaṇenābhūdaprayuktamivāmbare ।। mahāstrasaṃkaṭe ghore vartamānaṃ vṛkodaram ।
avaruhya rathātkṛṣṇau drāgbhujābhyāṃ vikṛṣya tam ।। śastraṃ hṛtvā balādvīraṃ nītvāśu syandanādbhuvam । vīrau citrojjvalau hṛṣṭau tasthātuḥ kṛṣṇapāṇḍavau ।। astre tataḥ svayaṃ śānte prasanne bhuvanatraye ।
ūce duryodhano drauṇiṃ punarastraṃ prayujyatām ।। dviṣprayojyaṃ na divyāstramityuktvā drauṇirākulaḥ । śaraiśvakāra pāñcālamatsyakekayasaṃkṣayam ।। sa sātyakiṃ pārṣataṃ ca jitvā vidrāvya vāhinīm ।
jaghāna pauravaṃ vīraṃ rājānaṃ ca sudarśanam ।। pāṇḍusainyeṣu bhagneṣu drauṇiṃ paścādabhidrutam । avārayatsvayaṃ kruddho bāṇavarṣairdhanaṃjayaḥ ।। prāduścakre tato ghoraṃ jvālāvalayitāmbaram ।
āgneyamastraṃ lokānāṃ kṣayāya drauṇirudyataḥ ।। atha kāñcanasaṃnāhauriva sarve samāvṛtāḥ । mahāstratejasā vyāptāḥ peturbhūmibhṛtāṃ varāḥ ।। astreṇākṣauhiṇīṃ dagdhāṃ vahnivyāpto dhanaṃjayaḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā prāduścakārograṃ brahmāstraṃ tatpraśāntaye ।। astre tirohite tasminvimuktau keśavārjunau । dṛṣṭvā droṇasutaḥ kruddho dhigastrāṇītyabhāṣata ।। atrāntare jñānasahasraraśmirapāravedāmṛtasindhusetuḥ ।
sarasvatīmānasarājahaṃsaḥ kṛṣṇo apyakṛṣṇo munirājagāma ।। rathaṃ samutsṛjya tamugrakarmā praṇamya papraccha gurostanūjaḥ । astrāṇi divyānyaphalāni kasmātpārthe sakṛṣṇe bhagavangatāni ।। pṛṣṭaḥ kopākuleneti tamuvāca munīśvaraḥ ।
vīrau kṛṣṇārjunāvetau naranārāyaṇāvṛṣī ।। ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi tapaḥ kṛtvā pinākinam । nārāyaṇastoṣayitvā lebhe tattulyatāṃ purā ।। sa eṣa durjayaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ svayaṃ liṅgārcanavrataḥ ।
drauṇe tvamapi rudrāṃśastasmānmā vikriyāṃ gamaḥ ।। etadvyāsavacaḥ śrutvā śāntamanyurguroḥ sutaḥ । dhiyā rudraṃ namaskṛtya devau kṛṣṇāvamanyata ।। tato avahāre sainyānāṃ vihite kurupāṇḍavaiḥ ।
nivṛttaḥ samarātpārthaḥ pathi vyāsaṃ vyalokayat ।। taṃ namaskṛtya papraccha bhagavansamare puraḥ । dṛṣṭo mayā śūlahastaḥ puruṣo dahanadyutiḥ ।। tacchūlinaḥsṛtairdīptairasaṃkhyaiḥ śūlamaṇḍalaiḥ ।
kurusenā mayā dṛṣṭā dahyamānā samantataḥ ।। krośārdhaspṛṣṭavasudho raudro rudra ivāparaḥ । pṛṣṭo dhanaṃjayeneti hṛṣye dvaipāyano abravīt। ।। sa devastripurārātirgajāsuravimardanaḥ । rudraḥ kṛtāntadahanastrijagatpralayakṣamaḥ ।।
yaṃ namaskṛtya varadaṃ rājante divi devatāḥ । astambhayadbujastambhaṃ jambhārāteḥ smitānanaḥ ।। smaraharamasurāriṃ taṃ smara smerakāntiṃ haramajaramajayyaṃ śāśvataṃ viśvarūpam । viṣamadṛśamanīśaṃ śāntamīsānamīśaṃ taruṇataraṇimālāsphāratejaḥprakāram ।।
kṣapitadinakarākṣaṃ dakṣadīkṣāvighātaṃ bhavamabhavamabhedaṃ svacchabhāvopalabhyam । śivamacalamacintyaṃ bālacandrāvataṃsaṃ giriparivṛḍhaputrīdyūtagoṣṭhīgariṣṭham ।। hatyāgrahātparamamāgrahamindrasūnoḥ prītyā vidhāya munimaulimaṇau prayāte । bhūpāḥ praviśya śibirāṇi dināvasāne cakruḥ kathāḥ pravaravīrakathānubaddhāḥ ।।
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। hate droṇe kurukṣetre punarabhyetya saṃjayaḥ । rājñe nyavedayadyuddhamāścaryaṃ karṇapārthayoḥ ।।
tato duryodhanaḥ karṇaṃ cittasaṃkalpaśālinam । cakre drauṇigirā hṛṣṭaḥ śūraṃ senāsu nāyakam ।। abhiṣikto maṇimayaiḥ kalaśairyaśasāṃ nidhiḥ । manorathasudhāvarṣī so abhavatkurubhūpateḥ ।।
vidhāya makaravyūhaṃ sthito vairikuleṣu saḥ । cakrire pāṇḍavā vyūhamardhacandramatandritam ।। tataḥ śastrāstrasaṃgharṣakīrṇavahnikaṇākule । ghore pravṛtte samare nirdhoṣastumulo abhavat ।।
bhīmo atha kuñjarārūḍho mattamātaṅgamāsthitam । caturdantaṃ jaghānograṃ kulūtanṛpatiṃ raṇe ।। tataḥ karṇāntanirmuktaiḥ karṇacāpacyutaiḥ śaraiḥ । nirbhinnāḥ kuñjarāḥ petuśchinnapakṣā ivācalāḥ ।।
pārthasātyakipāñcāladraupadeyaśikhaṇḍinaḥ । kṛpadrauṇimukhaiścakruḥ paraṃ navamivāharam ।। pārthaḥ saṃśaptakānhatvā nināya bhrātarau nṛpau । daṇḍādhāraṃ sadaṇḍaṃ ca daṇḍādhārapuraṃ śaraiḥ ।।
atha pāṇḍyaḥ kurucamūṃ dārayañjagatībhujām । bhallaiḥ śirāṃsi ciccheda labdhalakṣyaḥ prahāriṇām ।। bhīṣmadroṇārjunaspardhāṃ darpajvarabhavāṃ nayaḥ । sahate nityamātmānaṃ manyamāno balādhikam ।।
dakṣiṇāpathanāthena karṇāṭīsmitakīrtinā । lāṭīnetraśitāstreṇa tena bāṇairnipīḍitā ।। drauṇinā sūtapūtreṇa saubalena kṛpeṇa ca । vāryamāṇāpi dudrāva kururājavarūthinī ।।
tamabhyetya javāddrauṇirviśikhāśanivarṣiṇam । ayodhayadasaṃbhrānto jambhāririva śambaram ।। tasya līlāvatīlolalocanabhramarāmbujam । drauṇiḥ śiro jahārātha bhallenāndelikuṇḍalam ।।
pāṇḍyasaṃjñe hate vīre mauliratne mahībhujām । pāṇḍusenā na śuśubhe śaśihineva śarvarī ।। pāṇḍyavadhaḥ ।। tato gāḍhaniṣakteṣu śastravṛṣṭiṃ pibatsiva ।
āviṣṭeṣviva vīreṣu yudhi māneṣvavāritam ।। miśrībhūteṣu bhūpānāṃ ratheṣu ca gajeṣu ca । naṣṭālokeṣu lokeṣu vapurgāḍhena pāṃsunā ।। mleccharājaṃ mahānīkaṃ nakulaḥ krūrayodhinam ।
jaghāna rākṣasācāraṃ sarvāyudhaviśāradam ।। vimarde nibiḍe tasminnakulaṃ vadhagocaram । smarankuntīvacaḥ karṇo nāvadhītsatyavikramaḥ ।। tataḥ karṇamukhairvīraiḥ kīrṇāḥ pāñcālasṝñjayāḥ ।
na lebhire paritrāṇaṃ kuravaścārjunādibhiḥ ।। hatavīreṣu bhagneṣu cchinnadhvajaratheṣu ca । gāḍhaviddhasravaddantighaṭāniṣpiṣṭapattiṣu ।। akāṇḍatāṇḍavāviddhakabandhākulavartmasu ।
viśālaśoṇitanadīmañjatkuñjaravājiṣu ।। hataśeṣeṣu sainyeṣu śrānteṣu kurupāṇḍavāḥ । avahāraṃ dināpāye cakruḥ śithilakārmukāḥ ।। prathamo yuddhadivasaḥ ।।
atha prabhāte saṃnaddhe saṃnikṛṣṭe baladvaye । ūce duryodhanaṃ karṇaḥ pāṇḍusenāṃ vyalokayan ।। tvatprasādapraṇayino mānasya vibhavasya ca । adyāhamanṛṇo bhūtvā raṇe gacchāmi nirvṛtim ।।
adya gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ hatvā sāraṃ bhavaddviṣām । saphalaṃ te karomyeṣa saṃkalpaṃ cirasaṃbhṛtam ।। nindyaṃ sarvātmanā loke satāṃ svaguṇakīrtanam । kiṃtu kartavyakāleṣu na praśaṃsanti mūkatām ।।
ahamabhyadhikaḥ pārthādvidyayā vikrameṇa ca । etāvadadhikaṃ kṛṣṇo yadanargho asya sārathiḥ ।। kṛṣṇādabhyadhikaḥ śalyo viditaḥ sarvabhūbhujām । tena sārathinā jiṣṇuṃ vijetumahamutsahe ।।
iti vaikartanenokte hṛṣṭo rājā suyodhanaḥ । tadevābhyetya vinayānmadrarājamabhāṣata ।। tato madrādhipaḥ kruddhaḥ saṃrambhalulitāṃśukaḥ । sāsūyaṃ vīkṣya rādheyaṃ kauravādhipamabhyadhāt ।।
aho saralatā rājannavamānāya kevalam । yadahaṃ dīrghasaṃghābhyāṃ sārathye gaditastvayā ।। kimahaṃ pāṇḍavānsarvānhantuṃ śakte na saṃgare । nṛpaṃ māṃ sūtaputrasya sūtaṃ kartuṃ yadicchasi ।।
uktveti sahasā śalye sānuge hantumudyate । prasādya taṃ kurupatirvaktuṃ samupacakrame ।। madrarāja ja saṃrambhamasthāne kartumarhasi । adhikastvaṃ hi govindādato asmābhirihārthyate ।।
arjunādadhikaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sārathirvihitaḥ paraiḥ । tvaṃ karṇādadhikastasmātsārathye mā haṭhaṃ kṛthāḥ ।। trailokyopaplave daityaiḥ prajāpativarorjitaiḥ । rājatāyasasauvarṇasvacchandapuravāsibhiḥ ।।
vadhyamāneṣu lokeṣu devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ । purā pinākinaṃ devaṃ śaṃkaraṃ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ ।। viśvatrāṇāya viśveśastridaśairarthitastataḥ । sarvadevamayaṃ kṛtvā rathaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca sāyakam ।।
uvāca devānsaṃnaddhaḥ sārathiḥ kalpyatāṃ mama । matprabhāvādhikaḥ kaścidyena hantāsmi dānavān ।। tataḥ śakramukhā devā vicārya suciraṃ dhiyā । brahmāṇaṃ viśvakartāraṃ sārathye paryakalpayan ।।
tenoṅkārapratodena gṛhīte syandane haraḥ । ekībhūtānpure daityāndadāha viśikhāgninā ।। tripuravadhopākhyānam ।। iti rudrasya dhātāpi svayaṃ sūto abhavatpurā ।
tathā tvamapi karmasya nāvajñāṃ kartumarhasi ।। aiśvaryasyābhijanyasya guṇānāṃ vikramasya ca । santaḥ phalaṃ hi manyante mitrapraṇayapūraṇam ।। ukte duryodhaneneti madrarājaḥ smitānanaḥ ।
svacchandavādī sūto ahaṃ bhaviṣyāmītyabhāṣata ।। śalyasārathyasvīkāraḥ ।। tataḥ svakalpitaiḥ śvetaisturaṅgairiva mātaliḥ । taptakāñcanasaṃnāhe karṇasya rucire rathe ।।
jagrāha helayā śalyo raśmimamālāṃ suśikṣitām । pratāpadhāmnaḥ sūryasya divīva garuḍāgrajaḥ ।। yuyutsuṃ karṇamālokya dhanvinaṃ śalyasārathim । jayaṃ hastagataṃ mene kururājaḥ sahānugaḥ ।।
nadastu kurusainyeṣu śaṅkhadundubhiniḥsvanaiḥ । maurvīmāsphālayankarṇo madrarājamabhāṣata ।। adya śakraḥ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā mayā nihatamarjunam । divyāstreṣu dṛśaḥ śaṅke sāsūyaṃ kṣipati kṣaṇāt ।।
adya madbāṇadalitaṃ pārthaṃ vīkṣya yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । bhīṣmadroṇavadhāyāsavaiphalyātparitapyatām ।। iti bruvāṇaṃ rādheyaṃ karṇa madrādhipo abravīt । mā sūtaputra mithyaiva pralāpaṃ śiśuvatkṛthāḥ ।।
gandharvasamare pūrvaṃ tvayi dhīmati vidrute । yena trailokyavīreṇa kauravāḥ parirakṣitāḥ ।। mānināmāttaśastrabhāṇāṃ tasmingograhavigrahe । yuṣmadvidhānāṃ sahasā hṛtā yenāṃśukāvalī ।।
ākhaṇḍalaḥ sānucaraḥ khāṇḍave yena nirjitaḥ । taṃ samutsahase jetuṃ karṇa karṇo asi kiṃ na vā ।। iti śalyena sahasā śalyenevārdito muhuḥ । saṃstambhya kopaṃ rādheyo drakṣyasīti tamabhyadhāt ।।
tato vyūheṣvanīkeṣu savyasāciraṇotsukaḥ । agresaro rathāgryāṇāṃ karṇaḥ papraccha sainikān ।। kvāsau jayadrathārātirvīro vānaraketanaḥ । taṃ vinā rabhasādete tāmyantyeva mameṣavaḥ ।।
vidhatte locanapathaṃ mama yastūrṇamarjunam । dadāmi tasmai vāsāṃsi citrāṇyābharaṇāni ca ।। rathānsamattamātaṅgāngāḥ suvarṇaṃ purāṇi ca । kāntāśca vividhaṃ cānyaddraviṇaṃ yāvadicchati ।।
etadākarṇya sotprāsaṃ babhāṣe madrabhūpatiḥ । hāso duḥkhāya jāyeta rādheya tvadviceṣṭitaiḥ ।। mūmūrṣuriva niṣputro draviṇaṃ cirasaṃbhṛtam । avicāryaiva kiṃ mohātpareṣu tyaktumicchasi ।।
svayamarjunamāyāntaṃ vaśaḥ sitasaṭābharam । draṣṭāsi bāṇanakharaiḥ kuraṅga iva kātaraḥ ।। śrutvaitatkupitaḥ karṇo jagāda bhrukuṭīmukhaḥ । nirguṇastvaṃ na jānīṣe na māṃ na ca dhanaṃjayam ।।
ahamevārjunaṃ jāne pratimallaṃ pinākinaḥ । sa ca māṃ vetti tattvena tvaṃ mithyā tu pragalbhase ।। ayaṃ mitropadhiḥ śatruḥ kenāpi preṣito asi naḥ । kudeśajasya vā naitattava kauṭilyamadbhutam ।।
madrakāḥ kutsitācārāḥ satyaśīlārjavojjhitāḥ । mānaṃ pracakṣate loke sarvavedavido janāḥ ।। nirlajjāḥ sarvagāminyo lobhamohamadākulāḥ । anāryā madrikāyāstāḥ svasāro mātaraśca te ।।
rādheyeneti saṃrambhādbhāṣito madrabhūpatiḥ । uvāca mūḍha bahuśo hitamuktaṃ na budhyase ।। smartāsi vigaladdarpo nirjitaḥ savyasācinā । hitopadeśavākyānāṃ śocannanuśayākulaḥ ।।
samudrakūlanilayaḥ purā vaiśyo mahādhanaḥ । bahvapatyo abhavadrājñā rakṣito nirupadravaḥ ।। tatputrāṇāmabhūtkākaḥ satatocciṣṭabhojanaḥ । puṣṭāṅgo yo dhanāḍhyānāṃ praṇayī putravatpriyaḥ ।।
tataḥ kadācidāyātā haṃsā mānasagāminaḥ । so avadajjātasaṃgharṣastulyā yūyaṃ na me jave ।। jāne pātaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ viḍīnoḍḍīnabhedataḥ । jñāyate tulyapātānme yuṣmākaṃ ca tarasvitā ।।
ityucchiṣṭabhujā tena rājahaṃsā vivalgitāḥ । āhūtā vihasanto antarvīrā no kiṃcidūcire ।। ekastu haṃso jaladhau vrajāva iti saṃvidā । kākena sārdhaṃ śaravannipapāta smitānanaḥ ।।
tena vātajavenābdhau vāyasaḥ khe vrajansamam । sa ca krośārdhamātre abhūddhastapakṣo ativihvalaḥ ।। tenaiva bhagnadarpo atha tīre nyastaḥ kṛpāvatā । raktaṣṭhīvī cirātprāpa saṃjñāṃ jñātakhagāntaraḥ ।।
haṃsakākīyam ।। evaṃ tvamapi rādheya kauravaiḥ parivāritaḥ । arjunaṃ samare prāpya hīnadarpo bhaviṣyasi ।। śrutvaitanmadrarājena kathitaṃ marmadāraṇam ।
ūce vaikartano vīraḥ pṛthukopo apyavikriyaḥ ।। yuṣmadvidhānāṃ vacasā jāyate na bhayaṃ mama । paśyārjunaṃ mayā śalya samare vinipātitam ।। lakṣyābhyāse mayā vatsaḥ purā bāṇena dāritaḥ ।
pracchannastarukhaṇḍena homadhenordvijanmanaḥ ।। tacchāpādrathacakraṃ me paryantaṃ sādhayiṣyati । ityetacchidramekaṃ me durjayo ahamato anyathā ।। tvaṃ tu kevalayānena nṛpeṇa vāhinā vṛtaḥ ।
mayā svayaṃ saṃnikarṣe dvijihvaḥ kuṭilo vṛtaḥ ।। madrakāṇāṃ kuvṛttānāṃ pāpadeśanivāsinām । tīrthācāravihīnānāmadhipo asi kimucyate ।। abhakṣyaṃ bhuñjate nityamapātavyaṃ pibanti ye ।
agamyāsu ramante ca te madrāstava bāndhavāḥ ।। sarvasādhāraṇā yoṣāḥ sarvabhakṣyā dvijātayaḥ । sarvapātakasaṃpṛktā madrā yeṣu bhavānnṛpaḥ ।। madrakutsanam ।।
iti karṇena gadite madrarājo apyabhāṣata । karṇa rājā tvamaṅgānāṃ mātulyatyāgapāpinām ।। vikrīyante sadā yatra dārāḥ putrāśca mānavaiḥ । tasminpraṇetā viṣaye naivaṃ me vaktumarhasi ।।
aṅgakutsanam ।। ityukte madrarājena coditāste turaṅgamāḥ । dārayanta iva kṣoṇīṃ jātapakṣā ivodyayuḥ ।। athādṛśyata śubhrāśvo jiṣṇuracyutasārathiḥ ।
agre samagrasainyānāṃ vyagraḥ śatrunibarhaṇe ।। tataḥ pravṛtte vīrāṇāṃ samare prāṇahāriṇi । dhanuṣāṃ kūjatāṃ śabde chādite tūryaniḥsvanaiḥ ।। uvāca śalyo rādheyaṃ dhanaṃjayaraṇotsukam ।
paśya gāṇḍīvadhanvānaṃ bhindānaṃ kuruvāhinīm ।। ete saṃśaptakāḥ pārthaśaraśreṇīśatārditāḥ । hatadvipaghaṭākūṭakuṭīṣu nibhṛtaṃ sthitāḥ ।। paśyārjunaśarotkṛttakaṇṭhānāṃ mauktikāvalī ।
patitā bhūmipālānāmaśrumālā iva śriyaḥ ।। iti madrādhipenokte kva yāsyati dhanaṃjayaḥ । madbāṇagocaraṃ yāto harṣādityavadannṛpaḥ ।। tato vaikartanaśaraiḥ pūrite bhuvanodare ।
cakampe pāṇḍavānīkaṃ vātairiva mahadvanam ।। dhṛṣṭadyumnamukhānvīrānkurvāṇo virathānmuhuḥ । ayutāni kṣaṇātkarṇo vīrāṇāmavadhīddaśa ।। cedimāgadhapāñcālasainye bhagne yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।
mahārathairanugataḥ svaṃya rādheyamādravat ।। rājavallabha vāgyuddhaṃ nedaṃ yatra pragalbhase । ityuktvā dharmatanayaḥ śaraiḥ karṇamapūrayat ।। atha karṇo narapateścakrarakṣau mahārathau ।
hatvā śarairunmamātha dhvajaṃ cāpaṃ cakarta ca ।। tataḥ śaktiṃ niśātāgrāṃ kāladaṃṣṭrāmivotkaṭām । prāhiṇotsūtavṛtrāya sa nirhnādāṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। bhittvā vaikartanaḥ śaktiṃ tāṃ ghaṇṭākrandinīṃ muhuḥ ।
jātarūpamayaṃ varma cakarta nṛpateḥ śaraiḥ ।। muhūrtaṃ taṃ samāpūrya cchinnavarmāṇamāśugaiḥ । dantavarṇāñjaghānāsya kṛṣṇabālāṃsturaṅgamān ।। vidrutaṃ dharmatanayaṃ dṛṣṭvā krodhī vṛkodaraḥ ।
karṇaṃ parāṅmukhaṃ cakre śarairaśanidāruṇaiḥ ।। duryodhanānujānvīrānāyātānbhrāturajñayā । vidadhe vipulairbāṇairbhīmaḥ pretapurāśrayān ।। nandopanandau durdharṣaṃ dhanurgrāhaṃ mahābhujam ।
jarāsaṃdhaṃ śrutarvāṇaṃ durdinaṃ saniṣaṅgiṇam ।। pāśahastaṃ kavacinaṃ krodhaṃ ca sa mahābhujam । hatvā praviśya pṛtanāṃ nāgānīkamapothayat ।। tataḥ sātyakipāñcālamādrīsutayudhiṣṭhirāḥ ।
ayodhayankarṇamukhyāṃstasminsubhaṭasaṃkṣaye ।। vṛṣasenamukhairvīrairbhidyamāne balārṇave । udabhūccaṇḍagāṇḍīvadhvanirāghaṭṭitāmbaraḥ ।। hatvā saṃśaptakānsarvānpratyāvṛtte dhanaṃjaye ।
āvartanartitevābhūtsahasā kuruvāhinī ।। bhagne suśarmapramukhe pārthāstrairnṛpamaṇḍale । karṇaḥ pāṇḍavasainyeṣu kālalīlāyitaṃ vyadhāt ।। ayutāni gajendrāṇāṃ sapta hatvā tarasvinām ।
tāvantyeva rathānāṃ ca cakre bhūmibhujāṃ kṣayam ।। vyāghraketuṃ jayaṃ śaṅkuṃ rudramugrāyudhaṃ param । siṃhasenaṃ rocamānaṃ śuktaṃ citrāyudhaṃ harim ।। devāpiṃ jiṣṇukarmāṇaṃ śalabhaṃ citradaṇḍakau ।
anyāṃśca bhūmipānhatvā pāñcālakadanaṃ vyadhāt ।। vadhyamāne atha karṇena vidīrṇe ca sahasradhā । babhūva pāṇḍave sainye ghoro vyatikaro navaḥ ।। karṇena droṇaputreṇa kṛpeṇa kṛtavarmaṇā ।
kirīṭinā pārṣatena śaineyena śikhaṇḍinā ।। kupitena ca bhīmena te sene pravidārite । babhūvaturviprakīrṇe vidhvastakavacāyudhe ।। divyāstravarṣiṇaṃ drauṇiṃ divyāstreṇaiva phalguṇaḥ ।
jitvā dadarśa karṇena vadhyamānānmahārathān ।। tamabravīnmadhuripurvismitaḥ karṇāvikramāt । paśya kaunteya karṇāstravahnidagdhāṃ varūthinīm ।। paśya kālakaṭākṣeṇa lakṣitaḥ sūtanandanaḥ ।
kaṭākṣeṇa madādhmātaḥ sārathye māṃ yadaikṣata ।। kṣaṇena nikhilāṃ syūtāṃ tāṃ senāṃ kurute nṛpaḥ । paśyāsya śarajālena nīrandhreṇāvṛtā diśaḥ ।। ityuktvā keśavastūrṇaṃ rathena ghananādinā ।
nināya śakratanayaṃ bhīmasenarathāntikam ।। tato bhīmagirā dhyātvā dharmarājaṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ । karṇasāyakanirbhinnaṃ prayātaṃ śibiraṃ śanaiḥ ।। niḥśvasanbhṛśasaṃtaptaḥ kesarīva talāhataḥ ।
prayayau bhrātaraṃ draṣṭuṃ saha kāliyavidviṣā ।। sa hemapuṅkhairnirbhinnaṃ karṇanāmāṅkitaiḥ śaraiḥ । śayānaṃ dharmatanayaṃ dadarśa cchinnakaṅkaṭam ।। tasyābhivādya caraṇau niṣaṇṇau keśavārjunau ।
cintāsaṃtāpitatanū tasthatuḥ kṣaṇamākulau ।। yudhiṣṭhirastaṃ vijñāya karṇaṃ hatvā samāgatam । utthāya nirvyatho harṣājjayādapṛthuvismayaḥ ।। prāyo niḥśeṣitāḥ senā yenāstradahanena naḥ ।
sa diṣṭyā samare pārtha tvayā karṇo nipātitaḥ ।। vīrāḥ sa vidviṣāṃ hantā dhaureyaḥ sarvadhanvinām । rāmaśiṣyastvayā brūhi kathaṃ vaikartano hataḥ ।। iti pṛṣṭo nṛpatinā babhāṣe śvetavāhanaḥ ।
yudhyamānasya suciraṃ drauṇinā rudratejasā ।। saṃśaptakaiśca vighano abhūnmama karṇanipātane । bhīmasenamavasthāpya pratyanīke mahābhujam ।। prahāravikṣataṃ deva tvāmahaṃ draṣṭumāgataḥ ।
adhunā tvadanujñātaḥ kauravāṇāṃ parāyaṇam ।। kathāśeṣaṃ karo apyeṣa karṇaṃ karṇāyataiḥ śaraiḥ । iti bruvāṇaṃ bibhatsuṃ moghasaṃkalpaduḥkhitaḥ ।। uvāca sāyakākīrṇaḥ kopatapto yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।
bhāraṃ vinyasya vipulaṃ bhīmasene dhanurdharaḥ ।। apayāto asi karṇasya satyaṃ dṛṣṭvā parākramam । mithyaiva kuntyā garbhe tvaṃ kṣatriyavyañjano dhṛtaḥ ।। pūrakaḥ putrasaṃkhyāyāṃ bāṇastṛṇamayo yathā ।
trayodaśa samāste te saṃkalpā vihitāstvayi ।। sarve prayātā vaiphalyamupakārā ivādhame । ka eva nāma jānīte karṇādbhīto dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। apayāsyati saṃgrāmādyo varteta tathā vidhim ।
etatprayaccha kasmaicidgāṇḍīvaṃ śauryaśāline ।। samare karṇasaṃtrāsaṃ yo asmākamapaneṣyati । etadākarṇya bībhatsurmarmaṇīva samāhataḥ ।। etadgirā dadau khaḍge kruddhaḥ sāśrulavā dṛśaḥ ।
taṃ kopasaṃkaṭo ghore duḥkhāgnau ca nirantare ।। patitaṃ vīkṣya govindaḥ sarvavyāpī tamabhyadhāt । jāne te hṛdgataṃ pārtha yena dolāyase muhuḥ ।। gāṇḍīvaṃ vitarānyasmai tvāṃ brūyādyaḥ sa te dhruvam ।
vadhya ityucitācāra pratijñā tava viśrutā ।। tadarthamasi kopāndho nihantuṃ kiṃsvidagrajam । ātmānaṃ vā vratabhraṃśabhayātkhaṅgaṃ nirīkṣase ।। śruyatāmatra satyena kevalena vimuhyase ।
dharmādharmau na jānīṣe satyamātradṛḍhavrataḥ ।। asatyaṃ dharmatāṃ yāti satyamāyātyadharmatām । kadācitkarmabhedena tadvicāryaṃ dhiyā budhaiḥ ।। dharmo api gahanaḥ sūkṣmo jñāyate na yathā tathā ।
purā babhūva vipine balāko nāma lubdhakaḥ ।। ghorasattvaṃ kadācitsa gobrāhmaṇagaṇāntakam । hatvā śareṇa sahasā śakralokamavāptavān ।। kauśiko nāma vipraḥ prāksatyavākyakṛtavrataḥ ।
vidrutāndhanikānpṛṣṭo dasyubhiḥ kva gatā iti ।। adarśayatsatyavādī sa tānguṇadayāśrayān । dṛṣṭāṃśca dasyavo jaghnustūrṇaṃ tāndraviṇāśayā ।। kauśiko apyatha kālena patito narakaṃ yayau ।
ityevaṃ gahanā pārtha pravṛttiḥ satyadharmayoḥ ।। tasmāttvamagraje rājñi dharmaniṣṭhe yudhiṣṭhire । mohādasāṃprataṃ kiṃcinna cintayitumarhasi ।। śrutvaitatkhaḍgamākṛṣya hantumātmānamudyatam ।
pratijñābhaṅganirbhinnaṃ pārthaṃ kṛṣṇo abravītpunaḥ ।। avamānena nihato gururbhavati sarvathā । bhavatyātmā ca nihataḥ ślāghayā gurusaṃsadi ।। rakṣanpratijñāmajñānaṃ nirasya krodhasaṃbhavam ।
tasmādetadvadhāyādya nivṛtto bhava phalguṇa ।। ityuktavati dāśārhe tathetyuktvā dhanaṃjayaḥ । bhīruḥ pramādī krūrastvamityuvāca yudhiṣṭhiram ।। mayaikena hatāḥ sarve saṃhatā daityadānavāḥ ।
dhuryo ahaṃ kārmukabhṛtāmityātmānamuvāca ca ।। tato dharmasutaṃ duḥkhātkānanaṃ gantumudyatam । yatnātprasādayāmāsa gṛhītvā caraṇau hariḥ ।। pārthaṃ ca pādapatitaṃ sāśrunetraṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।
rurodha gāḍhamāliṅgya vigalanmanyuviplavaḥ ।। kṛtaśaucau tato vīrau dharmarājadhanaṃjayau । rathāvāruhya saṃnaddhau jagmatuḥ samarāṅgaṇam ।। athārjunaśaravrātakṛttavaktrairnareśvaraiḥ ।
kṣaṇaṃ babhūva patitaiḥ sā kabandhamayīva bhūḥ ।। atrāntare bhīmaseno hatvā duryodhanānujān । duḥśāsanaṃ yudhyamānamāsasādebhavikramam ।। niṣpiṣya gadayā tasya rathaṃ sāśvāyudhadhvajam ।
ācakarṣa raṇe dhvastaṃ taṃ hiḍimbāpatirbalāt ।। priyāparibhavaṃ ghoraṃ smarannatha vṛkodaraḥ । prakoparākṣasāviṣṭaḥ koṣṇaṃ śoṇitamāpapau ।। ghoraṃ tatkarma bhīmasya dṛṣṭvā srastāsikārmukāḥ ।
trastā mahārathāḥ sarve mīlitākṣākampire ।। asṛkprasaragarvitaḥ pulakadaṇḍagaṇḍānano madādativiśṛṅkhalaḥ skhalitapādacārakramaḥ । babhau bhayadavibhramabhramitabhīmabhāsvadgadaḥ priyācikurasaṃyamodyatamatiḥ samīrātmajaḥ ।। apūrveṇaiva vidhinā hate duḥśāsane tathā ।
mahatāmapi bhūtānāmabhūtkaṇṭakitā tanuḥ ।। duḥśāsanavadhaḥ ।। atrāntare pāṇḍavānāṃ vṛṣasenaśarārdite । sainye babhūva nirghoṣaḥ patatāṃ gajavājinām ।।
saṃhatā api bhūpālā bhīmasātyakirakṣitāḥ । na sehire raṇe dīptaṃ karṇasūnoḥ parākramam ।। sa sātyakiṃ bhīmasenaṃ mādrīputrau kirīṭinam । dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ nṛpāścānyānvīrastulyamayodhayat ।।
āścaryayodhinastasya smayamāna ivārjunaḥ । bhujau śiraśca ciccheda kamalākamalopamam ।। vṛṣasenavadhaḥ ।। vṛṣasene hate karṇaḥ puro gāṇḍīvadhanvanā ।
sasmāra sāśrunayanaḥ saubhadraṃ bahubhirhatam ।। athāmarṣājyasiktena bhrukuṭīdhūmaketunā । krodhāgninā dahyamānaḥ karṇo adhāvaddhanaṃjayam ।। manorathaśatābhyaste pravṛtte samare tayoḥ ।
babhūva kautukāyātasurasiddhākulaṃ nabhaḥ ।। karṇārjunaraṇe tasminsvaputrajayaśaṃsinoḥ । jāte vivāde sahasā divi sūryasurendrayoḥ। ।। pṛṣṭo dvidhā sthitairdevairvṛṣāṅkakamalodbhavau । kṛṣṇo yatra jayastatretyūcaturniścitaṃ purā ।।
atha gambhīranirghoṣau śaṅkhau karṇakirīṭinau । dadhmatuḥ śauriśalyau ca yaiścakampe jagattrayī ।। tato dhavalapakṣāgrāḥ svayaśobhirivāṅkitāḥ । vaikartanaḥ pāṇḍavāya prāhiṇodviśikhāvalīḥ ।।
pārthadhvajenābhihataḥ karṇaketurakampata । kṛṣṇasya dṛktribhāgaśca śalyaṃ śalyamivāviśat ।। athārjunaśarairdikṣu pūryamāṇāsu saṃtatam । bāṇapātamatikramya tasthuḥ kauravasainikāḥ ।।
duryodhanaprayuktānāṃ rādheyaratharakṣiṇām । mahārathānāṃ vaktrāṇi jahārātha kapidhvajaḥ ।। asaṃbhrāntastataḥ karṇo muṣṭimūle kirīṭinaḥ । prayujyamānamasakṛcciccheda śaramaṇḍalam ।।
tato bhīmo abravītpārthamacyutaścātivismitaḥ । durjayaḥ samare karṇaḥ sthiro yudhyasva phalguṇa ।। kairāte khāṇḍave vīra kālakeyavadhe api vā । yo abhavattava saṃrambho gṛhāṇābhyadhikaṃ tataḥ ।।
etadākarṇya vijayo vellanmukharakaṅkaṇaḥ । gāḍhamākṛṣya gāṇḍīvaṃ divyāstrairdyāmapūrayat ।। bhārgavāstreṇa hatvā tāmastravṛṣṭiṃ kirīṭinaḥ । taṃ ca bhīmaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca karṇo bāṇairapūrayat ।।
tataḥ karṇaśarāsārairarjunāstraiśca sarvataḥ । pāṇḍukauravasenāsu babhūva vipulaḥ kṣayaḥ ।। atha sarpamukhaṃ dīptaṃ kīrṇacandanaśālinam । astraṃ karṇo mahābhogaṃ prāhiṇotsavyasācinaḥ ।।
visṛṣṭe bhujage tasminśalyo aṅgapatimabhyadhāt । nāyaṃ prāpnoti pārthasya kaṇṭhaṃ nāgastvayeritaḥ ।। punaḥ saṃdhānayogyaste rādheya yadi manyase । akarṇo asyatha vā karṇahitavākyeṣu sarvadā ।।
iti tejovadhāyoktaḥ śalyena tapanātmajaḥ । uvāca dvirna saṃdhatte karṇa ityamalāśayaḥ ।। karṇacyutaṃ mahāghoramāpatantaṃ viṣolbaṇam । vyālaṃ dṛṣṭvā hariścakre vapurmandaragauravam ।।
jānubhirvasudhāṃ yāte tato hayacatuṣṭaye । phaṇī jagrāha namrasya kirīṭāgraṃ kirīṭinaḥ ।। kirīṭakhaṇḍe patite muktāratnāṭṭahāsini । so aviśadvasudhāṃ sarpo vipralabdho viniḥśvasan ।।
tataḥ kṛṣṇārjunau vidhyankāladaṇḍopamaiḥ śaraiḥ । karṇaḥ karṇāyato asṛṣṭairunnanāda hasanmuhuḥ ।। atha śakrasutaḥ kopāddivyaratnavirājitam । varma ciccheda karṇasya śaraiścāpūrayadvapuḥ ।।
khāṇḍave kṛtavairaṃ taṃ khaṃ vrajantaṃ mahoragam । chittvā ṣaḍbhiḥ śaraiḥ pārthaḥ karṇaṃ punaratāḍayat ।। vaikartanena nihate brahmāstre śākramarjunaḥ । prāduścakre vighātāya vajrāśaniśatākulam ।।
hatvā tamastraṃ rādheyo jyāṃ ciccheda kirīṭinaḥ । kṣaṇādabhinavāṃ maurvī vidadhe ca dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। tato raudraṃ sphurajjvālājaṭālaṃ saṃdadher'junaḥ । astraṃ yenābhavadvyoma ghoradigdāhabhīṣaṇam ।।
atrāntare mahī svayaṃ rathacakraṃ vidhervaśāt । jagrāha samaye tasminnaṅgarājasya saṃgare ।। tatastaccakramuddhartumudyato viṣamasthitaḥ । uvāca karṇaḥ kaunteyaṃ muhūrtaṃ kṣamatāṃ bhavān ।।
uddhṛte asminmayā cakre mahāstraṃ muñca phalguṇa । vyasanasthe viśastre ca nahi śūrā bhavādṛśaḥ ।। etacchrutvāvadatkarṇaṃ hasankāliyasūdanaḥ । diṣṭyādya karṇa jānīṣe dharmaṃ vīravrate sthitaḥ ।।
bahubhirnihato bālaḥ saubhadraḥ kiṃ nu vismṛtaḥ । gaṇyatāṃ tacca yatkṛṣṇāṃ sabhāyāmuktavānasi ।। viṣavahnipradāneṣu cchinnadharmaḥ smṛtastvayā । nūnaṃ vipadi nīcānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ dharmavṛttayaḥ ।।
ukte janārdaneneti manyunā prajvalanniva । brahmāstraṃ karṇavihitaṃ brāhmeṇa vijayo avadhīt ।। āgneyamarjunotsṛṣṭaṃ vāruṇenāṅgabhūpatiḥ । astreṇāstraṃ samāhṛtya grastacakro vyalambata ।।
athonmamātha bāṇena dhvajaṃ kanakabhāsvaram । karṇasyākhaṇḍalasuto manorathamivonnatam ।। tato añjalikamādāya śaraṃ kāñcanabhūṣitam । abhimantrya samākṛṣya mṛtyudaṃṣṭrāsitānanam ।।
rudrādayo astraguravastuṣṭā me tapasā yadi । tadanena ripuṃ hanyāmityuktvāsṛjadarjunaḥ ।। nirbhinnastena sahasā kaṇṭhe hārapariṣkṛte । rādheyaḥ krakacotkṛttahematāla ivāpatat ।।
hate dhanuṣmatāṃ dhurye kauravānīkanāyake । karṇe drutaṃ yayau śalyaḥ śalyayanhṛdayānanam ।। prāptaṃ rathena śūnyena dṛṣṭvā madranareśvaram । hato duryodhanaḥ karṇo jīvatītyūcire nṛpāḥ ।।
duryodhano arjunaśarairaṅgarāje nipātite । uttamāṅga ivājñāsīnna kiṃcidvihatondriyaḥ ।। tejastatastaraladīdhitikarṇadehādabhyudgataṃ taraṇimaṇḍalamāviveśa । yenāvakāśaviśarāruvimānamāsījjvālākalāpajaṭilaṃ kṣaṇamantarikṣam ।।
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। evaṃ jambha ivendreṇa hate karṇe kirīṭinā । yuddhaṃ nyavedayadrājñe punarabhyetya saṃjayaḥ ।।
śekhare sarvavīrāṇāmarthināṃ kalpapādape । hate vaikartane rājansarvāśārajanīkṛti ।। tadātmanā gate kvāpi nijajīva ivākulaḥ । duryodhano nirucchvāso mene śūnyā diśo daśa ।।
cacāra rathināṃ madhye pāṇḍavānyoddhumudyataḥ । pareṇaiva śarīreṇa paralokagato naraḥ ।। tato drauṇigirā kṛtvā śalyaṃ senāpatiṃ nṛpaḥ । raṇaṃ vitara rājyārthe viveśa tridaśālayam ।।
rathānāmayutaṃ sāgraṃ tāvadeva ca dantinām । lakṣyadvayaṃ dvayānāṃ ca tisraḥ koṭyaḥ padātinām ।। sainyaśeṣamabhūdetatkururājasya saṃgare । ator'dhaṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca hataśeṣamabhūdbalam ।।
asminnāyodhane ghore rājñāṃ saṃhāramaṇḍale । mastiṣkakardamaluṭhatpattisyandanakuñjare ।। ākīrṇavaktrakamale raṅgodbhaṅgarathāṅgake । visrastārājaṃsaughe khaṅgakhaṇḍotpalākule ।।
keśaśevālajambālaśeṣakīlālapicchile । akālakālakariṇā sarasīva viloḍite ।। srastavarāśvakarṇāṅke bhagnabāṇāsanāvṛte । kadalīśakalālole vane vajrairivāhate ।।
utpalāvayavāpūrṇavyaktaśaktyāsavodite । udyāna iva kālasya kapālacaṣakākule ।। punaḥ pravṛtte samare śalyahārdikyasauvalāḥ । viviśuḥ pāṇḍavacamūṃ kṛpadrauṇisuyodhanāḥ ।।
pārthapārṣataśaineyadraupadeyaśikhaṇḍinaḥ । jaghnustrigartagāndhārakapināthavarūthinīḥ ।। amaryāde raṇe tasminkṣībā iva mahārathāḥ । kruddhā yuyudhire ghoraṃ hatabandhusuhṛdgaṇāḥ ।।
satyasenaṃ suṣeṇaṃ ca citrasenaṃ ca karṇajam । jaghāna nakulo vīrānkarṇatulyaparākramān ।। tataḥ śalyena balinā gajeneva sarojinī । mṛdyamānā sanirghoṣā cakampe pāṇḍuvāhinī ।।
śalyena ripuśalyenā vadhyamānāṃ varūthinīm । dṛṣṭvā bhīmo gadāpāṇirbhīmakopastamādravat ।। sa hatvā gadayā tasya rathaṃ rathaśatacchidaḥ । mumūrṣordaṇḍamudyamya tasthau kāla ivāgrataḥ ।।
ādāya madrarājo api gadāṃ cāmīkarāṅgadām । bhīmaṃ bhīmabalaḥ kopāddarpoddhatamayodhayat ।। maṇḍalāni carantau tāvabhipatya parasparam । ghātajātasphuliṅgābhyāṃ gadābhyāmabhijaghnatuḥ ।।
tayormūrcchitayoḥ kṣipraṃ mohātpatitayorbhuvi । sānugāstūrṇamājagmuḥ saṃrabdhāḥ kurupāṇḍavāḥ ।। saṃjñāmavāpya sahasā yathāvatsthitayostayoḥ । duryodhanamukhā vīrāḥ pārthamukhyānayodhayan ।।
brahmalokābhikāmeṣu yudhyamāneṣu rājasu । suyodhanaścekitānamavadhīdbhūbhujāṃ varam ।। madrarājastataḥ kruddhaḥ pāṇḍūputrānsahānugān । avārayadbalādekaḥ pūjyamāno nabhaścaraiḥ ।।
śastravṛṣṭiṃ tadutsṛṣṭāṃ chittvā bāṇairasaṃbhramaḥ । muhurtādvidadhe śalyastānadṛśyānpatatribhiḥ ।। chādite śarajālena sainye madramahībhujā । kruddho avadhītsahasre dve rathānāṃ dharmanandanaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvānugānhatānrājñā śalyo yudhi yudhiṣṭhiram । śilīmukhaśataiḥ pūrṇamathāśokamivākarot ।। pīḍite dharmatanaye nakulaḥ kopakampitaḥ । bhīmasātyakimukhyāśca śaraiḥ śalyamavākiran ।।
tataḥ śarāndhakāreṇa sthagayanbhuvanodaram । unmamāthaḥ ghanadhvānaḥ śalyaḥ pārthavarūthinīm ।। ākulaḥ samare tasmiñjiṣṇurdraiṇimayodhayat । duryodhanaṃ bhīmaseno nakulaḥ subalātmajam ।।
kṣapitāśeṣanṛpateḥ śalyasyātha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । chittvāyudhāni sarvāṇi tilaśo vidadhe ratham ।। aparaṃ rathamāsthāya madrarājaḥ krudhā jvalan । cakāra dharmatanayaṃ kṛttacāparathadhvajam ।।
bhīmaseno atha virathaṃ dṛṣṭvā rājānamākulaḥ । cakarta madrarājasya rathaṃ sarvāyudhaiḥ saha ।। khaḍgahastastataḥ śalyo nighnansyandanakuñjarān । cacārālakṣitatanurmargairgaruḍavikramaḥ ।।
atha jvālāyamānena śoṇapaṭṭena guṇṭhitām । bhrājiṣṇuratnakhacitāṃ mṛtyordantāvalīmiva ।। etadantaṃ kurubalaṃ yuddhamevaṃvidhaṃ kutaḥ । itīva ghaṇṭāpaṭalaiḥ krośantīmaśanisvanām ।।
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sahasraghniṃ dīptāṃ ṣaṇmukhavikramaḥ । prāhiṇonmadrarājāya śaktiṃ śaktimatāṃ varaḥ ।। sa tayā bhinnahṛdayaḥ papāta kṣmābhṛtāṃ varaḥ । śrotranāsāsyavivarasravadrudhiranirjharaḥ ।।
śalyavadhaḥ ।। śalye hate kauravāṇāmāśā śeṣāvalambane । rathino dudruvuḥ sarve bhagnamānamanorathāḥ ।। tataḥ śalyānujaḥ kruddho vicitrakavacābhidhaḥ ।
abhyāyāyau dharmarājaṃ dārayantamanīkinīm ।। pṛṣatkavarṣiṇastasya citraratnojjvalaṃ śiraḥ । rohaṇādrerivottuṅgaṃ śṛṅgaṃ ciccheda dharmajaḥ ।। tasminhate bhajyamānāṃ nāthahīnāṃ patākinīm ।
parāvṛtya kṛpadrauṇihārdikyāstūrṇamāyayuḥ ।। nadadbhiścedipāñcālairlabdhalakṣyairmahārathāḥ । te muhūrtaṃ yuyudhire prayātā bahutāmiva ।। tataḥ svāmivadhāmarṣādyudhiṣṭhiramabhidrutān ।
hatvā śeṣānaho madrānamadrāṃ pṛthivīṃ vyadhāt ।। atha bhīmo gadāpāṇirnipuṇaḥ kṣayakarmasu । niṣpiṣya mlecchānsarvāṃśca raṇaṃ śūnyamivākarot ।। tataḥ sātyakinā vīre satyarāje nipātite ।
svayaṃ duryodhano abhyetya pāṇḍuputrānayodhayat ।। na ratho na gajo nāśvo na yodhaḥ pāṇḍaveṣvabhūt । haimanāmāṅkitairvyāpto yo na duryodhaneṣubhiḥ ।। cakampe kuñjarakulaṃ tasya nārācavarṣiṇaḥ ।
maṇikāñcanajhāṅkāratāramaurvīravairmuhuḥ ।। duryodhane yudhyamāne labdhalakṣyairarātibhiḥ । āyayurdraiṇihārdikyasuśarmakṛpasaubalāḥ ।। ghore raṇavyatikare teṣāṃ nibiḍapātinām ।
nirāloko abhavalloko rajasā saṃvṛte ravau ।। kuñjarendrataṭāghātakṣame rajasi duḥsahe । vibhāgo nābhavatkaścitkalpāpāya ivāgate ।। kva drauṇiḥ kva ca gāndhāraḥ kva ca rājā suyodhanaḥ ।
ityabhūdvipulaḥ śabdaḥ pāṇḍusenāsu sarvataḥ ।। tasminmuhūrte pralayāvartasaṃkrāntagocare । jaghāna mārutasutaḥ śeṣānduryodhanānujān ।। mahābāhuṃ bhūribalaṃ jaitraṃ durdarśanaṃ śalam ।
sunādaṃ ca sa hatvā tānunnanāda kṣayocitān ।। tato māmagrahīdvīraḥ sātyakirvinarale raṇe । saṃjayo ayaṃ mayā labdho nigadyeti sasaṃbhramam ।। athārjunaḥ suśarmāṇaṃ saputraṃ sapadānugam ।
hatvā saṃśaptakānīkaṃ niḥśeṣaṃ viśikhairvyadhāt ।। dyūte raṇābhidhe tasminsāyakākṣānkṣipanmuhuḥ । sahadevor'dhacandreṇa jahāra śakuneḥ śiraḥ ।। śakunivadhaḥ ।।
ulūkaṃ tatsutaṃ hatvā gāndhārāṇāmanīkinīm । jaghāna mādrītanayo vanavāsadaśāṃ smaran ।। atha niḥśeṣite sainye śrānto nihatavāhanaḥ । apasṛtya raṇātprāyātpadbhyāṃ rājā suyodhanaḥ ।।
kṛtavarmakṛpadrauṇiśeṣe tasminmahāraṇe । kṣaṇādaśeṣatāṃ yāte bhūtavetālamaṇḍale ।। dhṛṣṭadyumnasya vacasā māṃ nihantuṃ samudyate । śaineye bhagavānvyāso rarakṣa karuṇānidhiḥ ।।
tato dinānte śokārtaḥ prasthito ahaṃ suyodhanam । apaśyaṃ vajrahṛdayaṃ prayāntaṃ cakravartinam ।। sa pādacārī māṃ dṛṣṭvā lajjākuṭilakandharaḥ । ūce saṃjayarājānaṃ brūyāstvaṃ janakaṃ mama ।।
tena karṇena suhṛdā taiśca vīrairvinā kṛtaḥ । hradaṃ praviṣṭaḥ putraste hīno duḥśāsanādibhiḥ ।। māmityuktvā sa saṃstambhya salilaṃ daityamāyayā । hradaṃ viveśa vipulaṃ prauḍhaśokānalākulaḥ ।।
taṃ stambhitorusalile sarasi praviṣṭaṃ jñātvā girā mama gurostanayaḥ kṛpaśca । bhojaśca bhūpatiśikhāmaṇilīḍhapādaṃ lakṣmīvilāsasadanaṃ śuśucustametya ।। akṣauhiṇīparivṛto atha visṛjya gehaṃ rātrau yuyutsumakhilaiḥ saha rājadāraiḥ । dharmātmajastamṛṇaśeṣamiva pradadhyau duryodhanaṃ saha dhanaṃjayabhīmamukhyaiḥ ।।
yatpādapadmanakhacandramarīcimālā mālā iva kṣitibhṛtāṃ babhuruttamāṅge । so apyeka eva kururājasutaḥ padātiryāto dhigāsthiravilāsavikāsi daivam ।। yasyā vaśādbata natonnatabhāñji bhāvacakrāṇi hanta viśarārudaśāṃ viśanti । saṃkrandanāni yativibhramamudritāni tasyai namo astu satataṃ bhavitavyatāyai ।।
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। tato drauṇimukhā vīrāḥ samabhyetya rathāstrayaḥ । hradaṃ praviṣṭaṃ rājānamūcurmānadhanaṃ śaraiḥ ।।
rājannuttiṣṭha saṃgrāme jahi śatruṃ dhanurdhara । sahāsmābhirayaṃ kālo vikramasya yaśobhuvaḥ ।। iti śrutvā kurupatiḥ praśaṃsaṃstatparākramam । ūce prātaḥ samāśvāsya mama kṣatrocitā gatiḥ ।।
iti teṣāṃ samālāpaṃ śrutvā jñātvā suyodhanam । śaśaṃsurbhīmasenāya lubdhakā dhanalubdhakāḥ ।। bhīmasenagirā rājā sasainyo atha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । kṛṣṇapradhānaiḥ sahitastaṃ deśaṃ tūrṇamāyayau ।।
garjadgajarathānīkaiḥ pārthānvīkṣya samāgatān । narendrasūcanabhayātprayayurgautamādayaḥ ।। tasya kṛṣṇasya vacasā dharmasūnuḥ suyodhanam । tataḥ sa salilāntaḥsthamuvāca kṣmābhṛtāṃ varaḥ ।।
rājanrajatakarpūrarajanīpatisundaram । aho vīra yaśaḥ śubhraṃ bhavatā malinīkṛtam ।। ghātayitvā narapatīṃllakṣmīkulagṛhānraṇe । prāṇarakṣāparo mānī kathaṃ jīvanna lajjase ।।
uttiṣṭha yuddhe svāṃ lakṣmīṃ tridivaṃ vā samāpnuhi । lākṣaḥ samo hi vīrāṇāṃ vijayo nidhanaṃ nu vā ।। iti yaudhiṣṭhiraṃ śrutvā vaco manyuviṣākulaḥ । prāha dūryodhanastoye stambheram iva śvasan ।।
evametadyathāttha tvaṃ śriyaṃ nidhanameva me । bandhusvajanahīnā tu lakṣmīḥ kasya manaḥ spṛśet ।। dhvajinī vīrahīnena goṣṭhīva budhavarjitā । svajanena vinā lakṣmīḥ kasya prīṇāti mānasam ।।
sa karṇaḥ suhṛdāmagryaḥ sa guruḥ sa pitāmahaḥ । vinā tapovanamaho sumuneḥ kasya vismaret ।। bandhumittraviyuktānāṃ bhūtayo hi viḍambanāḥ । andhānāmiva saundaryavicitrāścitramālikāḥ ।।
bhuṅkṣva bhuktāṃ mayā pṛthvīṃ vīraratnavivarjitām । vairāgyamuktābharaṇāṃ jaratīmiva yoṣitam ।। ityākarṇya pṛthāsūnurdhārtarāṣṭramabhāṣata । diṣṭyā tapovanaruciḥ śānto asi vasudhāpate ।।
sūcyagramapi na tyājyaṃ pāṇḍavānprati te bhuvaḥ । samagrāṃ pṛthivīmadya dātumicchasi kautukam ।। uttiṣṭha yuddhamekena tavāstu vijitaḥ sa cet । jitāḥ sarve tvayā rājanmā pralāpaiḥ kṛśo bhava ।।
udatiṣṭhanniśamyaitatpārthavākyaṃ nṛpaḥ krudhā । sāvalepaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā na sahante hi māninaḥ ।। hemāṅgadagadāpāṇiḥ sumeruriva śṛṅgavān । utthitaḥ sa babhau rājā daṇḍadhāra ivāparaḥ ।।
kṛṣṇavākyātsa saṃnaddho gadāpāṇirvṛkodaraḥ । tasya tasthau puraḥ kṛṣṇānikāragaṇanāparaḥ ।। duryodhanāvirbhāvaḥ ।। atrāntare haladharaḥ kurupāṇḍavasaṃkṣaye ।
bandhunāśabhayodvignastīrthayātrāgataḥ śanaiḥ ।। tadābhyetya kurukṣetraṃ tāvapaśyadgadāyudhau । śiṣyayoḥ samaraṃ paśyañśṛṇvanniva giro mithaḥ ।। sa pūjitaḥ kṛṣṇamukhyaiḥ pārthaiḥ śaśiśatadyutiḥ ।
upāviśannīlavāsā himavāniva sāmbudaḥ ।। ityākarṇya kathāpadhye papraccha janamejayaḥ । tīrthayātrāṃ halabhṛto vaiśampāyanamādarāt ।। so abravītprastute yuddhe kurupāṇḍavabhūbhujām ।
āmantrya kṛṣṇaṃ prayayau kṣayāśaṅkī pralambahā ।। puṣpeṇa nirgato rāmo dvijebhyaḥ sarvakāmadaḥ । sarasvatīmavāpyātha prabhāsaṃ śayanena saḥ ।। yatra tārāpatiṃ tārā rohiṇīsaktamānasam ।
khinnā nyavedayatpitre tacchāpātso abhavatkṣayī ।। kṣaṇena śāpātprakṣīṇe śaśalakṣmaṇi yakṣmaṇā । sarvakṣayabhayodvignairdaivairdiṣṭaṃ tadā yayau ।। tatprabhāsaṃ hasaṃstūrṇaṃ tatrāpi prāpa pūrṇatām ।
tatra bharādvajaḥ snātvā tritakūpaṃ samāyayau ।। upekṣitaḥ purā yatra bhrātṛbhyāṃ nṛpatistritaḥ । sa cakre mānasaṃ yajñaṃ tato devāḥ samabhyayuḥ ।। tato varātsakūpo abhūtsomapānaphalapradaḥ ।
tasminsarasvatītīre sasne rāmeṇa sādaram ।। tato vinaśanaṃ puṇyaṃ prāpa yatra sarasvatī । śūdrabhīrukavidviṣṭā vinaṣṭā duṣṭanāśinī ।। sa bhūmikaṃ tataḥ prāyādbalī yatrāpsaraḥsakhā ।
krīḍanti suragandharvā nṛtyagītavinodanaiḥ ।। durgasrotaḥ śaṅkhatīrthaṃ puṇyaṃ dvaitavanaṃ tathā । avāpya nagadhanvānaṃ vasatiryatra vāsukeḥ ।। viveśa naimiṣa rāmo yatra prācī sarasvatī ।
munīnāṃ darśanaṃ yatra naimiṣāraṇyavāsinām ।। sapta sārasvataṃ prāyādyatra caṅkaṇako muniḥ । nanarta gātrādālokya nijācchākarasaṃ srutam ।। nṛtyatastasya sāvegaṃ sakhelaṃ varakānanam ।
munestapaḥprabhāvena jagatsarvaṃ nanarta ca ।। devairathārthito abhyetya tasya śambaradarśanāt । svakarānniḥsṛtaṃ bhasma tenābhūnnirmado muniḥ ।। tasmai stutikṛte tuṣṭastapovṛddhiṃ dadau vibhuḥ ।
saptasārasvate tīrthe saṃnidhānaṃ ca śaṃkaraḥ ।। kapālamocanaṃ prāpa tīrthamauśanasaṃ balaḥ । yatra jaṅghāgrahānmukto munirghorānmahodaraḥ ।। rāghaveṣunikṛttasya rākṣasasya śiraḥ purā ।
mahodarasya jaṅghāyāṃ lagnaṃ kila visarpadam ।। sarvatīrthanimagno api tatraiva svāsthyamāpa saḥ । uttaṅkāśramamāsādya pṛthūdakamavāpa ca ।। vasiṣṭhena jitaḥ pūrvaṃ dhenuhṛdbrahmatejasā ।
rājanyavaṃśyo yatrāpa brahmatāṃ kauśiko muniḥ ।। tatra rāmo dadau bhūri dhanaṃ vārṣṇeyanandanaḥ । tataḥ sārasvate kuñje yatrendro namucervadhāt ।। brahmahatyākulo muktastaṃ prāpa dāruṇaṃ śanaiḥ ।
somatīrthaṃ tataḥ prāpa yatreṣṭamamṛtatviṣā ।। tārakakhyo hato yatra ṣaṇmukhena mahāsuraḥ । skandābhiṣekātsnātvātha vahnitīrthaṃ samāyayau ।। yatrānalo bhṛgoḥ śāpānnaṣṭo abhūnnirvṛtaḥ punaḥ ।
kauberamindratīrthaṃ ca yāmunaṃ cācyutāgrajaḥ ।। devalasyāśramaṃ prāpya jaijīṣavyaḥ suyogavit । yatra sarvagataṃ brahma devalāya jagau muniḥ ।। tataḥ sārasvataṃ tīrthamāsasāda halāyudhaḥ ।
apasarodarśanātpūrvaṃ śukraṃ nipatitaṃ jale ।। dadhīcasya munestena putraṃ lebhe sarasvatī । dadhīcasyāsthinicaye mahendrāyudhatāṃ gate ।। anāvṛṣṭyāṃ sa tanayastayā matsyāśanairvṛtaḥ ।
sārasvataḥ suto vedānsa sasmāra mahāmatiḥ ।। durbhikṣakarṣitā nāma vismṛte adhyayane tataḥ । sarveṣāṃ munimukhyānāṃ babhūva gururarthitaḥ ।। tasmiṃstīrthe balaḥ snātvā yayau yatra purā vapuḥ ।
sanatkumārī tapasā svargāya tyaktumudyatā ।। nāradaḥ prāha nodvāhaṃ vinā svargo bhavediti । sā gālavasutāyaiva dinabhogyāṃ tanuṃ dadau ।। kṛtvā lalitamākāraṃ tridivaṃ ca yayau tataḥ ।
tatra snātvā ca datvā ca plakṣaprasravaṇe tathā ।। avāpa kārapavanaṃ tīrthānyālokayañśanaiḥ । nāradāttatra śuśrāva kurukṣetre nṛpakṣayam ।। rāmatīrthayātrā ।।
pṛṣṭo atha dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa saṃjayo yuddhamabravīt । bhīmasenasya virathaṃ kauravasya ca māninaḥ ।। samantapañcakaṃ gatvā padbhyāmeva suyodhanaḥ । tasthāvakampo mahatāmadhikaṃ dhairyamāpadi ।।
tato duryodhano avādīddharmaputraṃ sahānugāḥ । upaviśya nirīkṣantāṃ bhavanto yudhyamānayoḥ ।। ajātaśatruḥ śrutvaitatsaha pāñcālasainikaiḥ । upāviśatkṛṣṇasakhaḥ parivārya halāyudham ।।
atha bhīmaṃ gadāpāṇiṃ baddhakakṣastarasvinam । ājuhāva vacoyuddhe pravṛtte kurunandanaḥ ।। tatastayorgadāghātajātā vahnikaṇāvalī । vidadhe saṃbhramāvṛttahemābharaṇavibhramam ।।
surairāpūrite vyomni yuddhadarśanalālasaiḥ । babhūva nākakāntānāṃ ko api kautukavibhramaḥ ।। ākṣepe varjane mokṣe rājavṛttau nivartake । dhāvane samavasthāne viplute samaviplute ।।
tau pragalbhatayā vīrau citramaṇḍalacāriṇau । sanirghoṣaṃ mahāvegaḥ pārśvadeśamatāḍayat ।। tato bhīmaḥ samādhūya gadāmaśaniniḥsvanām । bhrāmayāmāsa yenābhūddhoro gharagharāravaḥ ।।
tatastāṃ prahiṇodbhīmo girigurvīṃ gadāṃ javāt। akampitastāḍito api punarbhīmo asṛjadgadām । punarmoghīkṛtā rājñā sāpatatkampitāvaniḥ ।। atha vakṣastaṭe bhīmaḥ kauraveṇa samāhataḥ ।
na viveda kṣaṇaṃ kiṃcinmūrchāvyākulitāśayaḥ ।। pāñcālasṛñjayānīke saṃdehākulite tataḥ । śanairbhīmaḥ samāśvasya pārśve nṛpamatāḍayat ।। gāḍhaprahārābhihataḥ patitaḥ kauraveśvaraḥ ।
utthāya tūrṇamāhatya bhuvi bhīmamapātayat ।। athāpatatsurotsṛṣṭa puṣpavṛṣṭiryaśaḥsitā । sādhuvādāvalī mūrdhi sūnave kurubhūpateḥ ।। athotthite bhīmasene parimṛjyāśu śoṇitam ।
ko anayoradhiko yoddhā papracchetyarjuno harim ।। so abravīdbalavānbhīmo bhīmavīryaḥ kimucyate । upadeśe gadāyuddhe kiṃtu yuddhaparākrame ।। sa prayatnaḥ kurupatirbhīmasenādvilokyate ।
tasmānna dharmayuddhena bhīmaḥ śakto nipātane ।। māyayā nihatā daityā māyāvadhyā hi māyinaḥ । ūrubhaṅgamato bhīmo vidadhātvasya māyayā ।। anyathā durjayo rājā trayodaśasamāvyadhāt ।
eṣa lokabhayaṃ bhīmo vidhāya gadayā śramam ।। vyāyāmacaturo vegādūrdhvacārī suyodhanaḥ । mahāśaileyabhaṅgo asminsukaraśchidradarśanāt ।। ukte janārdaneneti bhīmaścikṣepa bhīṣaṇām ।
gadāṃ tāṃ kururājo api vilaṅghya tamatāḍayat ।। vyathāṃ saṃstambhya bhīmo atha ghūrṇamānatanuḥ kṣaṇam । gadāṃ randhraṃ vicintyāsmai prāhiṇotkanakāṅgadām ।। puṣpāyudhapurodārahemābharaṇavibhrame ।
ūruyugme bhujaṅgīva sā papāta mahīpateḥ ।। nirghātaghoraghanaghoṣagadānipātaniṣpeṣajarjarataratruṭitorusaṃdhiḥ । duryodhano atha nipapāta divaṃ vilokya vajrāvapātahatapakṣa ivādrirājaḥ ।। akṣauhiṇīpatinareśvaramauliratnaraśmicchaṭāpaṭalapāṭalapādapīṭhe ।
asminmahīparivṛḍhe patite ca bhūmau kairninditaṃ na bhavabhaṅgurabhaṅgi janma ।। gadāyuddham ।। tasminnekādaśacamūnāthe bhuvi nipātite । cakampe lolataṭinīraśanā vasudhāvadhūḥ ।।
babhūva bhayadairvyāptaṃ durnimittaśatairjagat । praśaṃsantaśca tadyuddhaṃ prayayurvyomacāriṇaḥ ।। bhīmo nikāragaṇanāṃ kurvankurupateḥ śiraḥ । caraṇenāspṛśallakṣmīvilāsasadanaṃ tataḥ ।।
