taṃ vilokya rurodeva patitaṃ cakravartinam । tvaṅgadgadāṅgadacchinnahāramuktāśrubhirmahī ।। bhīmaṃ nirasya garjantaṃ dharmarājaḥ suyodhanam । ūce rājaṃstavaivāyamanayātsuhṛdāṃ kṣayaḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā śiraḥ padā spṛṣṭaṃ bhīmena jagatībhujaḥ । prāhottālahalaḥ kopakarālastālalāñchanaḥ ।। pratāpatāpitaricoryaśaḥ śatruhṛtaśriyaḥ । śiro vyājahatasyāsya kaḥ spṛśedapaśuḥ padā ।।
ityuktvā krodhaśikhinā taṃ bhīmaṃ dagdhumudyatam । śamayāmāsa kaṃsāristaistairvinayabhāṣitaiḥ ।। viṣadyutāgnidoṣāṇāṃ prabhāvo asīti vādinam । kṛṣṇaṃ duryodhano avādītsaṃstambhya rujamutkaṭām ।।
gopālabāla mūrkhāṇāṃ saṃjñāṃ kṛtvāsmi vañcitaḥ । tvayā bhīṣmamukhā vīrāste vyājaireva pātitāḥ ।। bhuktaṃ suhṛdbhirvihṛtaṃ kāntābhirhutamagryajaiḥ । vadhaḥ kṣatrocitaḥ prāptaḥ ko anyo asti sadṛśo mayā ।।
bhrūbhaṅgena nivāsitā vanabhuvaṃ śuṣyanmukhāḥ śatravo dṛṣṭā śrīḥ svayamarpitāgryasuhṛdāmuṣṇīṣahārasmitā । saṃgrāme apyaparāṅmukhasya nidhanaṃ dikṣu prarūḍhaṃ yaśaḥ kartavya spṛhaṇīyamanyadicitaṃ yuktaṃ kimastyāyuṣaḥ ।। ityākarṇya vacastasya lajjitā iva māninaḥ । nṛpaiḥ saha yayuḥ pārthā nādayanto rathairjayam ।।
athāvaropya prathamaṃ phalguṇaṃ madhusūdanaḥ । rathādavātaratpascājjajvāla sa rathastataḥ ।। droṇakarṇāstradagdho ayamatyantaṃ jvalito rathaḥ । iti pṛṣṭo avadatpārthaṃ vismitaṃ kāliyāntakaḥ ।।
śrutveti saṃjayādrājā dāruṇaṃ mohavihvalaḥ । śuśoca putrānvākyāni vidurasya smaranmuhuḥ ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇamunau prāpte kuruveśma harirnṛpam । gāndhārīṃ cāvadatprāpya visṛṣṭo ajātaśatruṇā ।।
yācito apiśamaṃ naicchatkauravo nijadurnayāt । na ca dharmāccyutāḥ pārthāstena tena padaṃ ruṣaḥ ।। putrāste yuvayoradya pāṇḍuputrāḥ suratviṣaḥ । yuvābhyāmeva coktaṃ prāgyato dharmastato jayaḥ ।।
iti prasādya tau yāte vṛṣṇivīre ambikāsutaḥ । munāvāśvāsya yāte ca śeṣaṃ papraccha saṃjayam ।। so abravīdatha putraste veṣya māno mahītale । māmūce paśya sūdena māyayāhaṃ nipātitaḥ ।।
atrāntare samabhyetya drauṇihārdikyagautamāḥ । dadṛśuḥ kauravapatiṃ nītaṃ kālena tāṃ daśām ।। tato gurusutaḥ kopādviniṣpiṣya kare karam । niḥśeṣaśatrunidhane pratijñāṃ niḥśvasanvyadhāt ।।
atha vīraṃ tamāliṅgya cakre senāpatiṃ nṛpaḥ । na hyahaṃkāraśaithilyaṃ paryante apyabhimāninām ।। pralayāmbudanirghoṣaṃ vinadya droṇanandanaḥ । niśāyāṃ tāṃ rujā rājā viṣamāmagamaddaśām ।।
tato gautamahārdikyaguruputrā mahāvanam । viviśuḥ kalayanto antaḥ śriyaḥ kallolalolatām ।। nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।।
pratāpadhāmni yāte astaṃ ravau kamalinīpriye । śokāvakīrṇakeśena tamobhirabhavanmahī ।। kṣayaṃ kālena nīte ahni śānte saṃdhyācitānale । asthiśeṣairivāpūrṇaṃ tārakābhirabhūnnabhaḥ ।।
śyāmā pratyagraduḥkhena prasarattimirāñjanā । babhāra tārataralāṃ nakṣatrāśrukaṇāvalīm ।। ghore tasminniśāvaktre ghorasattvaghane vane । śramānnidrāmupagate kṛpe sa kṛtavarmaṇi ।।
dhyāyanduryodhanavadhaṃ manyuhālāhalākulaḥ । pratijñāṃ śatrunidhane drauṇireko vyacintayat ।। atrāntare dadarśoccanyagrodhaśikharāśrayam । vadhyamānamulūkena vāyasānāṃ ca maṇḍalam ।।
kākānkālabalenaitya dṛṣṭvā ghūkena pātitān । tāmeva pāṇḍavavadhe nītiṃ drauṇiracintayat ।। krudhā krūrāṃ dhiyaṃ kṛtvā kṛpabhojau vibodhya saḥ । uvāca niḥśvasandīrghaṃ dahyamāna iva krudhā ।।
rājā rājasahasrāṇāmekākī viṣamasthitiḥ । vyājādasmāsu jīvatsu bhīmasenena pātitaḥ ।। śastraṃ vahadbhirmithyaiva dṛṣṭo asmābhiḥ sa bhūtale । aśrupātapratīkārākṣamaiḥ klībatarairiva ।।
deśakālau samāśritya vadhyaḥ sarvātmanā ripuḥ । tasmātprasuptānadyaiva sānugānhanmi pāṇḍavān ।। śrutvaitatkūṇitamanāḥ prasuptavadhapātakam । kṛpaḥ kṛpākulo nindannabhāṣata sutaṃ svasuḥ ।।
dhigetatkutsitaṃ yuddhaṃ niśceṣṭo yatra hanyate । bhagnadhairye api no vīrāḥ praharanti yaśasvinaḥ ।। bhavānahaṃ ca bhojaśca kartāraḥ prātareva tat । punaryena na yāsyāmo duryodhanavadhavyathām ।।
surāṇāmapi paryāptāḥ saṃhatāḥ samare vayam । pravekṣyāmo vairivanaṃ jvalitā iva pāvakāḥ ।। gautamenetyabhihite saṃmate kṛtavarmaṇaḥ । niḥśvasansāśrunyanaḥ punardraiṇirabhāṣata ।।
māyopamā vidagdheṣu nikṛtyāvicarastu ye । spṛśantyadharmamaryādāṃ na te tatphalabhāginaḥ ।। arjunena hataḥ karṇaḥ sa ca śāntanavo yathā । tatkiṃ na viditaṃ loke śeṣaṃ vaktuṃ na pāryate ।।
adhunā svasti dharmāya racito asmai mayāñjaliḥ । parābhavamimaṃ tāvanna sahe marmadāraṇam ।। drauṇirdāruṇasaṃkalpamityuktvā kṛtaniścayaḥ । rathena tamasi prāyācchibiraṃ kauravadviṣam ।।
kṛṣṇasya śāsanātpūrvaṃ yāteṣu śibirāntaram । saha sātyakinā yodhaiḥ pāṇḍaveṣu vinānugaiḥ ।। kṛpabhojāvatikramya javāddrauṇirupāgataḥ । śibiradvāramāsādya mahadbhūtaṃ vyalokayat ।।
hariśmaśrujaṭānetraṃ jvālānāmiva saṃcayam । tamasāmiva saṃghātamañjanācalasaṃnibham ।। sahasraśīrṣanayanaṃ sahasracaraṇādbhutam। sarpayajñopavītāṅgaṃ sarpakeyūrakaṅkaṇam ।
bhayaṃkaraṃ bhayasyāpi kṛtāntasyeva daivatam ।। taddṛṣṭvā ghorasaṃrambho drauṇirdurjayavikramaḥ । sarvāyudhāvalī tasmai prāhiṇauddhairyabhūdharaḥ ।। tānyāyudhāni sahasā jvalitānyeva tejasā ।
bṛmbhamāṇaṃ mahadbhūtaṃ tadāsādya kṣayaṃ yayuḥ ।। drauṇistatastadākāramarīcibhyo vyalokayat । cakrāyudhasahasraṇi niḥsṛtāni sa vismayaḥ ।। kṣaṇādgrastāyudhastena gāḍhānuśayatāpitaḥ ।
prastutaṃ malinaṃ karma nininda svayamākulaḥ ।। sa rathādavatīryātha prayatastripurāntakam । śūlinaṃ śaraṇaṃ prāyāttatstotramukharānanaḥ ।। ātmopahāraṃ rudrāya tasmindātuṃ samudyate ।
jvālākulā hemavedī purastātpratyadṛśyata ।। tadudbhūtairgaṇairghorairnānāprāṇimukhodaraiḥ । nānāpraharaṇairdīptairvyoma kṣipramapūrayat ।। tato vedyāṃ mahāvahnau jvalite droṇanandanaḥ ।
bhaktyātmānaṃ trinetrāya nivedyābhyapatatsvayam ।। tuṣṭo atha bhagavānetya svayamandhakasūdanaḥ । tamuvāca svamevāṃśamuttiṣṭhāṅgirasāṃ vara ।। saṃsthānāya mayaitāvatkṛtaṃ kaiṭabhavidviṣaḥ ।
ātgānaṃ viddhi me kṛṣṇaṃ sa me bahumataḥ sadā ।। kālapakvāstu pāñcālā naiṣāṃ rakṣāsti kutracit । gṛhāṇa khaḍgametena dārayaitānaśaṅkitaḥ ।। ityuktvā bhairave dīptaṃ khaḍgaṃ datvā tirohite ।
tadā vikārādduṣprekṣyo drauṇiḥ śibiramāviśat ।। dvāri bhojakṛpau dhṛtvā vidrutānāṃ vadhāya saḥ । praviśya śayane śubhre dhṛṣṭadyumnaṃ vyalokayat ।। tārahārāṃśunakharaṃ dīptakesarisaṃnibham ।
ghūrṇamānaśikhairdīpairvismayādiva vīkṣitam ।। anekaraṇasaṃmardaśrāntairnidrāvimohitaiḥ । adhiṣṭhitaṃ bahubhaṭairmuktaparyāṇavāhanaiḥ ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā kopaśikhinā dahyamānaḥ smaranpituḥ ।
uttiṣṭha re gurughneti drauṇiruktvā padāspṛśat ।। bodhitaḥ sahasā tena saṃbhramasvīkṛtāyudhaḥ । droṇaputraṃ parijñāya cakampe drupadātmajaḥ ।। drauṇistamutthitaṃ vegānmālyavadbhiḥ śiroruhaiḥ ।
ākṛṣyāpātayatkaṇṭhe gāḍhaṃ niṣpīḍya vihvalam ।। niṣpiṣyamāṇaḥ saṃrambhādraktodgārākulānanaḥ । kupitvā pādayordraiṇiṃ nakhairdantaiśca visphuran ।। śastreṇa chindhi māṃ tūrṇaṃ mā padeneti gadgadam ।
kaṇṭharuddhasvaraḥ śvāsādasphuṭākṣaramabhyadhāt ।। tamabravīddroṇasutaḥ pāpa padbhyāṃ nihanyase । lokānāṃ śastrapūtānāṃ na pāpaṃ gurughātinām ।। ityuktvā caraṇāghātairjarjaraṃ tamapothayat ।
tasminhate tadvimardaśabdena bubudhe janaḥ ।। dhṛṣṭadyumnavadhaḥ ।। tato drauṇiṃ samālekya ripuraktacchaṭāṅkitam । pāñcālā draupadeyāśca kālo ayamiti menire ।।
nidrāśeṣāruṇadṛśāṃ śastrāṇyānayatāṃ mithaḥ । krośatāṃ varma varmeti teṣāmāsīnmahāsvanaḥ ।। kva gajaḥ kva rathaḥ kvāśvaḥ kva cāpaṃ kva śilīmukhāḥ । iti bruvāṇānkhaṅgena drauṇiściccheda tānkrudhā ।।
hatvottamaujasaṃ padbhyāṃ kaṇṭhe kaṭhinavikramaḥ । gadāhastaṃ yudhāmanyuṃ niṣpipeṣa virāviṇam ।। tataḥ khaṅgena śūrāṇāṃ śirāṃsi bhuvi pātayan । kālarātryāḥ sa vidadhe vinodaṃ kandukairiva ।।
kṛṣṇāsutānāpatato draupadeyānasaṃbhramāt । cakāra karavālena sa kālakavalocitān ।। prativindhye hate vīre sutasome nipātite । śrutakīrtai śatānīke chinne ca śrutavarmaṇi ।।
śikhaṇḍī kṛṣṭakodaṇḍaḥ śarairdraiṇimapūrayat । droṇaputro api khaḍgena kruddhastaṃ vidadhe dvidhā ।। draupadeyaśikhaṇḍivadhaḥ ।। kopādācāryaputreṇa vadhyamānāḥ prabhadrakāḥ ।
matsyasṛñjayapāñcālāḥ kālaṃ dadṛśurantike ।। asitaṃ raktavasanaṃ raktamālyānulepanam । hasantaṃ vīkṣya taṃ vīrāḥ saṃhāraṃ menire sphṛṭam ।। ghanāndhakāre vīrāṇāṃ rathakuñjaravājinām ।
yodhānāṃ ca kṣayaṃ dvāri cakraturbhojagautamau ।। evamakṣauhiṇīṃ hatvā vasāraktānulepanaḥ । niryayau raudracarito drauṇirbhairavavigrahaḥ ।। sa gatvā sahitastūrṇaṃ hārdikyena kṛpeṇa ca ।
dadarśa bhuvi rājānaṃ bhagnaśaktiṃ suyodhanam ।। vārayantaṃ gadāgreṇa muhuḥ kravyādamaṇḍalam । vyathayā marmadinyā bhakṣayantaṃ vasuṃdharām ।। śoṇitaṃ vadanodvāntaṃ parimṛjyāśu tasya te ।
sarvapāñcalasaṃhārakathayā vavṛṣuḥ sudhām ।। sa kiṃciccheṣajīvo api tacchrutvā vṛttakandharaḥ । paryantagrasitāvyaktabhāṣitaiḥ praśaśaṃsa tān ।। sa pariṣvajya yatnena drauṇiṃ sāśruvilocanam ।
punarnaḥ saṃgamaḥ svarge bhūyādityavadacchanaiḥ ।। aṅge vidhāya dayitāṃ sa gadāṃ sadaiva bhuktāṃ ciraṃ vasumatīmavagūhya dorbhyām । karṇāvalambitabalodgatajīvacāro vīraḥ śanaiḥ suravadhūpraṇayī babhūva ।। duryodhanasvargagamanam ।।
atrāntare prayātāyāṃ kṣapāyāṃ kṣapitārayaḥ । jajñire pāṇḍavāḥ karma dāruṇaṃ drauṇinā kṛtam ।। muktānmahābhayāttasmātkṛṣṇā śrutvā hatānsutān । anujāṃśca sapāñcālānpapāta bhuvi mūrcchitā ।।
śanakairlabdhasaṃjñā sā vilapantī sulocanā । pārthānāṃ śokavidhurā hṛdayāni vyadārayat ।। yāvanna viśikhaiḥ kṛttamuttamāṅgaṃ vikarmaṇaḥ । drauṇerdṛṣṭaṃ mayā tāvajjīvitasyāyamañjaliḥ ।।
ityuktvā draupadī duḥkhādvīkṣamāṇā vṛkodaram । novāca kiṃcitsaṃtāpānmaraṇe kṛtaniścayā ।। tato bhīmaḥ priyāśokaśūlenābhyāhato hṛdi । prayayau rathamāruhya droṇaputrajighāṃsayā ।।
vrajatastasya kālagneriva lokāndidhakṣataḥ । dhūmamālābhramaṃ cakre lalāṭe bhrukuṭiḥ kṣaṇam ।। raudro rudrāśrayo drauṇiḥ kruddhaśca pavanātmajaḥ । gacchāmaḥ pṛṣṭhatastasmādityūce pāṇḍavānhariḥ ।।
tataḥ kirīṭipramukhāḥ saha sātyakinā yayuḥ । rathinaḥ seṣavaḥ sarve pāṇḍuputrā yuyutsavaḥ ।। tataste drauṇimāsādya prasuptavadhapātakāt । dhvastacchāyaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ kopenākulatāṃ yayuḥ ।।
abhidrute bhīmasene drauṇiṃ nakulasārathau। pādacārī ghṛtābhyaktaḥ sarasvatyāstaṭe kṣaṇam । apāṇḍavaṃ jagatkartuṃ brahmaśīrṣāstramādade ।। tadvināśāya pārtho api brahmāstramasṛjatkṛtī ।
yenābhavandiśo vyāptāḥ kampātaṅkataraṅgitāḥ ।। atrāntare samabhyāyānnāradena saha svayam । muniḥ satyavatīsūnurbhagavānbhūtabhāvanaḥ ।। so abravīddroṇatanayaṃ jiṣṇuṃ ca kṣayaśaṅkitaḥ ।
ayaṃ divyāstrasaṃmarde hatavīraṃ jagaddahet ।। pārtha saṃhara divyāstraṃ tvaṃ ca drauṇe girā mama । akāṇḍe mā bhavantvete lokāḥ pralayabhāginaḥ ।। ityukte muninā kṣipraṃ saṃjahārāstramarjunaḥ ।
drauṇiḥ prayogakuśalo neśo abhūdastrasaṃhṛtau ।। tataḥ prajvalite loke vyathite suramaṇḍale । abhimanyuvadhūgarbhe drauṇirastramapātayat ।। bhūyastatpratiṣedhāya putrasaṃtānavāñchayā ।
nindandroṇasutaṃ pārthastadastraṃ kupito asṛjat ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇo avadajjiṣṇuṃ viṣaṇṇaṃ saṃtatikṣayāt । mā śuco dhairyajaladhe na te vaṃśo vinaṅkṣyati ।। jātvenaṃ jīvayiṣyāmi dagdhamapyastratejasā ।
uttarāyāḥ sthitaṃ garbhe saubhadratanayaṃ śiśum ।। iti bruvāṇe govinde pārthāstre jvalite bhuvi । uvāca droṇatanayaṃ vyāso devarṣiṇā saha ।। tyaja cūḍāmaṇiṃ rakṣa jīvaratnaṃ mahāstrataḥ ।
aśaktaśca pramādī ca jānīṣe na yathocitam ।। vatsarāṇāṃ sahasra tvaṃ visrarogī samāhitaḥ । durbhikṣavyañjako duḥkhī vijane vicariṣyasi ।। iti śapto gurusutaḥ kopādvyāsamabhāṣata ।
vyasane patitaḥ kasmātkṣipto ahaṃ saṃkaṭe tvayā ।। yatra yatra bhaviṣyāmi tatra tatra mamānugaḥ । tvamapi pratiśāpena mune nityaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। ityuktvāstropahārāya cūḍāratnaṃ vitīrya saḥ ।
prayayau droṇatanayo muniśca muninā saha ।। tataḥ praśānte brahmāstre pāṇḍavāḥ saha śauriṇā । cūḍāratnaṃ samādāya yājñasenyai nyavedayan ।। aiṣīkamastram ।।
evaṃ prasādya pāñcālīṃ śokārtāḥ pāṇḍunandanāḥ । pāñcālakadanaṃ ghoraṃ dhyāyanto na yayurvṛtim ।। saṃjayeneti kathite śrutvā rājāmbikāsutaḥ । papāta mūrcchito mohāllīnaśokānalaḥ kṣaṇam ।।
taṃ śītasalilāpūrairāśvāsyovāca saṃjayaḥ । mantriṇaśca priyānputrāñśocantaṃ vyathitendriyam ।। svapnamāyāvilasitaiḥ paryante śokamohadaiḥ । saṃsāravibhramairdhīrāḥ spṛśyante na manīṣiṇaḥ ।।
devaindrajālikakṛtaiśchāyākrīḍanakairiva । putrairdhanaiśca dāraiśca na muhyanti madāśayāḥ ।। upekṣitastvayaivāyaṃ durnayādbāndhavakṣayaḥ । vṛtte tasminnamithyaiva śokaṃ kartumihārhasi ।।
prabhāvaprabhavairbhāvairmāyāvibhavabhāvitaiḥ । abhāvaniṣṭhāparyantaiḥ satāṃ na kriyate bhramaḥ ।। svakarmamudrite loke niyatau pralayodadhau । kalayāmi na kālasya kaśca tāvati vartate ।।
ityādi saṃjayamukhā nṛpamugramohabhagnaṃ svayaṃ vihitadurnayadṛṣṭapāram । helāvalatkalabhacñcalakarṇatālalolāṃ bhavasthitikathāmasakṛttamūcuḥ ।। nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।।
gāndhārī dhṛtarāṣṭraśca rājā vyākulamānasau । hatāvatha sutāndraṣṭuṃ sotkaṇṭhāviva jagmatuḥ ।। tatra tau vilapantau ca kṣipantau ca tanuṃ bhuvi । bhagavānatha cābhyetya pārāśaryo vyalokayat ।।
sa dīnaṃ patitaṃ bhūmau hataputraṃ nareśvaram । vidureṇa sahovāca kṛṣṇena ca kṛpākulaḥ ।। abhāvaḥ prākca paścācca dehināṃ satataṃ sthitaḥ । teṣu madhyavikāreṣu kaḥ śnehaṃ kartumarhasi ।।
apāre asminbhavāmbhodhau bhavanti na bhavanti ca । jalabudbudavatsarve karmayogena jantavaḥ ।। satyaṃ bhūbhāraśāntyarthamajāyata suyodhanaḥ । sa ca yātastathā kṛtvā kastvaṃ tasya sa kastava ।।
narendra mā kṛthāḥ śokaṃ pravṛtte asminmahālaye । pratīpameti yātānāṃ kaṇikāpi na pārṣadām ।। āyāsāya prayāso ayaṃ śokavyasanasaṃbhavaḥ । adhunā duḥkhavṛkṣāṇāṃ sneho mūlaṃ nivāryatām ।।
namaḥ kālāya yaḥ ko api vidyate mṛtyunā vṛtaḥ । kāyo vārdhakamāyāti svayaṃ yena śarīriṇām ।। ātmāparādhātputrāste kālena kavalīkṛtāḥ । tasmānna pāṇḍaputrebhyaḥ kilbiṣātkroddhamarhasi ।।
dharmanityāḥ kṛtadhiyaste dharmeṇa kṣatāstava । pāṇḍavā bhrātaraṃ smṛtvā kāluṣyaṃ teṣu mā kṛthāḥ ।। gāndhārīṃ brūhi sahasā mohe majjati no yathā । eṣaivoktavatī pūrvaṃ jaye dharmo nibandhanam ।।
iti teṣāṃ girā kṣipraṃ samohaṃ kauraveśvaram । draṣṭumabhyāyayuḥ pārthā lajjānamraśirodharāḥ ।। āliliṅga tato rājā prajñācakṣuryudhiṣṭhiram । bhīmaṃ māyāmayaṃ paścātkṛṣṇabuddhyā vivardhitam ।।
āyayau mārutirdveṣādbhujābhyāṃ tena pīḍitaḥ । prayayau kaṇaśastena sarve vismayamāyayuḥ ।। dharmasūnustato vṛddhāṃ praṇanāma pativratām । gāndhārīṃ bhartṛsādṛśyātsadā vastrāvṛtekṣaṇām ।।
adho nipatitastasyāḥ pādayordharmanandanaḥ । dadāhāṅguṣṭhayugalaṃ dṛṣṭikopānalākulaḥ ।। tato hatānāṃ duḥkhārtā vallabhā jagatībhujām । raṇamadhyaṃ pratiyayurgāndhārī ca snuṣākulā ।।
vilapya karuṇaṃ tatra vihvalā subalātmajā । babhāṣe keśavaṃ sāsrā divyadṛṣṭiḥ pativratā ।। paśyaitānkṛṣṇa matputrānsīmantinyo raṇe hatān । śocanti yāḥ purā dṛṣṭā na sūryeṇa na cendunā ।।
paśyāntaḥpuracārībhirapsarobhirivāvṛtaḥ । saṃmukhaṃ nihataḥ śūro bhagnorustanayo mama ।। hatanāgāṃ hatāśvāṃ ca suyodhanavadhūriyam । kṣmāṃ sapatnīmivālokya paśya mūrcchāmupāgatā ।।
labdhasaṃjñā śanaireṣā parimṛjya rajaściram । rājarājasya mahiṣī paripṛcchati vallabham ।। utsaṅge māmivādāya ratnāṃśukavatīṃ gadām । dorbhyāṃ ca bhuvamāliṅgya kathaṃ supto asi bhūpate ।।
na te kanakaparyaṅke vilāsaśayane vṛtā । asminnarapate suptā raktakṣībā kathaṃ śivā ।। eṣaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ śete priyo ramyastavānujaḥ । nipītaṃ rākṣaseneva yasya bhīmena śoṇitam ।।
ayaṃ te dayitaḥ putro lakṣmaṇaḥ śatruṇā hataḥ । sajīva iva vaktuṃ tvaṃ nātha kiṃcitsamīhate ।। dantastambhāviva bhraṣṭāvanaṅgaṅganatoraṇau । saralau pātitāvatya manyete kāladantinā ।।
ayaṃ te maulirucitaściraṃ mūrdhni sukhoṣitaḥ । rociṣṇuriha vibhraṣṭaḥ spṛṣṭaḥ kāntiparikṣayāt ।। pādābhyāṃ rudhirārdrābhyāṃ raṇasaṃcāriṇastava । vānteva satatā pītā rājacūḍāmaṇicchaviḥ ।।
lokapāle tvayi divaṃ yāte nandanakautukāt । dhanyābhimānitevaikā kīrtistvadanuyāyinī ।। bhrājiṣṇuratnavalaye doṣṇi karpūrapāṇḍure । kasyānyasya mahī yātu śeṣaviśrāntinirvṛtim ।।
yaḥ sa kaṅkaṇjhāṅkārairvyajanairvijito nṛpaḥ । kravyādapakṣivātene so ayamadyāpi vījyate ।। iti duryodhanavadhūṃ krośantīṃ kauravastriyaḥ । samākṛṣya viveṣṭante patitāḥ paśya bhūtale ।।
itaḥ subhadrā saubhadraṃ putrakaṃ putravatsalā । parimārṣṭi rajodigdhaṃ stanau dātumivodyatā ।। aṅke śaśāṅkasadṛśaṃ kṛtveyaṃ patyuruttarā । vadanaṃ bāṣpadhārābhiḥ prakṣālya paripṛcchati ।।
ayi nātha tathā tattaduktvā praṇayapeśalam । bhūmimāliṅgya kiṃ śeṣe priyāmadya vihāya mām ।। gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ putraścakrapāṇeḥ svasuḥ sutaḥ । tvaṃ śakrasadṛśaḥ śaurye kathameko hataḥ paraiḥ ।।
idaṃ te vadanaṃ kāntaṃ kamalākamalopamam । nūnamāpāsyati smeraṃ dhanyaḥ svargavadhūjanaḥ ।। nanvanaṅgatayānaṅgastvayyabhūnnopamāspadam । so ayamaṅgavadhātkānta tvayādya saphalīkṛtaḥ ।।
śaśāṅkaśaṅkayā śaṅke tvayi tridivagāmini । karoti tārakāpaṅktiḥ kaṇṭhe muktāvalībhramam ।। yāhaṃ tvayā navavadhūḥ pratyālāpaṃ purārthitā । tvāṃ svayaṃ bhāṣyamāṇāṃ māṃ kathaṃ na pratibhāṣase ।।
kva nu sarvaguṇagrāmagaṇanīyasya te gatam । dākṣiṇyaṃ svargalalanāsakto yanmāmupekṣase ।। punaḥ kartumaśakye asmindhātuḥ saubhāgyavarṇane । prahṛtaṃ tvaccharīre yaurdhiktāndagdhavilocanān ।।
kusumāyudhatulyasya kusumāyudhataiva te । nūnaṃ raṇe abhūttvāṃ vīrāḥ sehire kathamanyathā ।। evaṃ vilāpinīṃ bālāṃ balādākṛṣya putrikām । virāṭapatnyo yāntyetā rudantyaḥ patyurantikam ।।
sānujaḥ sa sutāmātyo virāṭanṛpatirhataḥ । vadhūbhirāvṛto bhūmau divīvāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।। eṣā droṇaśacchinnaṃ sudoṣṇā bharturānanam । vilokya tāraṃ krośantī ruddhā sakhyeva mūrcchayā ।।
kravyādaluptāvayavaṃ paśya karṇaṃ vadhūjanaḥ । parāyaṇaṃ kauravāṇāmāliṅgyāliṅgya śocati ।। nāmni saṃkīrtite yasya prāpurnidrāṃ na śatravaḥ । sa tvamadya hataḥ śeṣe dhikkālasya durantatām ।।
jambhārirabhavadyasya varmakuṇḍalayācakaḥ । satyasaṃdhaḥ kathaṃ kaṇaḥ karṇaśeṣīkṛtaḥ khagaiḥ ।। nisargavisaraḥ sargaḥ sarvathā hatavedhasaḥ । kṛtvā yaḥ śakratulyatvaṃ na cakre kalpasākṣiṇam ।।
iti prakīrṇābharaṇāḥ krandantyaḥ karṇayoṣitaḥ । dārayanti kucābhogaṃ vṛṣasenasya mātaraḥ ।। paśya jāmātaraṃ kṛṣṇa hataṃ mama jayadratham । bālā śociti matputrī na ca jānāti śocitum ।।
eṣa śalyo hataḥ saṃkhye ripuśalyaparākramaḥ । śalyatāmadhunā yātaḥ paśyāntaḥpurayoṣitām ।। paśyāsya kṛṣyate jihvā madrarājasya vāyasaiḥ । rādheyasyaiṣa vidadhe yudhi tejovadhaṃ yayā ।।
paśya droṇasya samare vahneḥ śāntārciṣo yathā । saṃskāraḥ kriyate vipraiḥ krimīnutsārya mūrcchitān ।। eṣa bhūriśravā vīraḥ somadattasuto hataḥ । mahiṣyā śocyate vīraśchinnabāhuḥ kirīṭinā ।।
raṇayajñamahīyūpe yūpadhvajabhuje tava । nikṛte jiṣṇunā manye yaśo nirlūnamātmanaḥ ।। lakṣmīkareṇukālāne bhūbhārabhujageśvare । śivākṛṣṭe virautīva doṣṇi te kaṅkaṇāvalī ।।
candrikābharaṇe harmye tvatpremābharaṇāḥ striyaḥ । āliliṅga purā so ayaṃ vilāsābharaṇo bhujaḥ ।। arthikalpadrume doṣṇi cchinne asmiñśatruyoṣitām । vaidhavyadīkṣāgurutāṃ vīra yāsyati ko aparaḥ ।।
haṭhakaṇṭhagrahaḥ prauḍhaḥ ko nāma hariṇīdṛśām । keyūrakāntikalikāṃ karṇapūrīkariṣyati ।। iti pralāpinī vakti vihvalā kamaleśvaram । pravaraṃ bhūriyaśasaṃ bhūriśravasamātmanā ।।
hitopadeśavidveṣī śukuniḥ paśya bhakṣyate । śivābhiraśivācāro veśyābhiriva vittavān ।। pṛthivī kṣapitā kṣipraṃ kṣudraiḥ karṇāntagāmibhiḥ । itaḥ pūrvamanenākṣairito bāṇaiḥ kirīṭinā ।।
itaḥ sudakṣiṇasyaitāḥ priyāḥ kāmbojabhūpateḥ । hṛdayāni pralāpena dārayantyaśmanāmapi ।। saubhadraśaranirbhinnaṃ rājaputraṃ bṛhadbalam । etāḥ komalakāminyaḥ śotanti śaśirociṣam ।।
dhṛṣṭadyumnasutā dīptahemamālāvibhūṣitāḥ । bhāntyete droṇanihatā bhraṣṭā vidyādharā iva ।। kekayo dhṛṣṭaketuśca jayatsenaśca māgadhaḥ । vṛddhaśca rājā drupadaḥ sāmātyasutabāndhavaḥ ।।
alāyudho alambusaśca bhagadattaḥ śrutāyudhaḥ । vindānuvindāvāvantyau jalasaṃdhaḥ sulocanaḥ ।। pravarāḥ pārthivāścānye hatā vīrāḥ sahasraśaḥ । labdhajīvā ivābhānti kāntābhiḥ parivāritāḥ ।।
śaktenāpi tvayā kṛṣṇa yasmātkāmādupekṣitāḥ । sarvakṣayādvā dveṣādvā sarvajñena ca līlayā ।। ṣaṅviṃśe vatsare prāpte vṛṣṇīnāṃ samare mithaḥ । tasmāttāvāpi bhavitā vipulo bāndhavakṣayaḥ ।।
tavāpyanucitaḥ ko api vadhaheturbhaviṣyati । ityuktvā tārakaruṇaṃ ruroda subalātmajā ।। tāmuvāca hasankṛṣṇaḥ svecchāsṛṣṭalayodayaḥ । vidhinaitatpurādiṣṭaṃ punaruktaṃ tvayoditam ।।
avaśyabhāvini śucaṃ kṣaye asminmā vṛthā kṛthāḥ । avaśyaṃ kṣatriyasute hantāhaṃ kila vidviṣām ।। ityuktavati dāśārhe dhṛtarāṣṭro yudhiṣṭhiram । gatiṃ papraccha vīrāṇāṃ parimāṇaṃ ca saṃkṣaye ।।
tamabravīddharmarājo lakṣaṇāmadhuraṃ raṇe । viṃśatiśca sahasrāṇi koṭyaḥ ṣaḍadhikāśca ṣaṭ ।। vīrāṇāṃ gaṇanārhāṇāmasminnāyodhane hatāḥ । aprahṛṣṭā hatā ye ca te gandharvapuraṃ gatāḥ ।।
bhayātparāṅmukhā ye ca te yakṣatvamupāgatāḥ । ye tvakhaṇḍitasattvasthāste brahmabhuvanaṃ śritāḥ ।। merupārśvaṃ prayātāste ye padbhyāṃ vāhanairhatāḥ । prasādāllomaśasyaitanmuneḥ paśyāmi divyadṛk ।।
ityuktvā dharmatanayo hatānāṃ jagatībhujām । bandhūnāṃ cādideśāśu saṃskāraṃ vibhavocitam ।। indrasenamukhāḥ sūtāḥ saṃjayo vidurastathā । yuyutsuśca girā tasya teṣāmantyavidhau yayuḥ ।।
mālyairvastrairaṃlakārairbhūṣitāste mahārathāḥ । citānaleṣu nihitāḥ svapratāpamivāviśan ।। athodatiṣṭhannārīṇāṃ saṃhatānāmitastataḥ । mithaḥ kaṇṭhavilagnānāṃ karuṇo rodanadhvaniḥ ।।
dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa sahitaḥ sānugo atha yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । anuyāto nṛpastrībhiryayau snātumathāpagām ।। śrāvitaḥ karṇavṛttāntaṃ sa mātrā gūḍhasaṃbhavam । bhrātre duḥkhāddadau tasmai bāṣpamiśrāṃ jalāñjalim ।।
sa yathāvidhi bandhūnāṃ vidhāya svocitāṃ kriyām । ādideśa nṛpastrīṇāṃ kriyāyau paṭamaṇḍapān ।। tā bhūmipālalalanā saralāyatākṣyo netrāmbunirjharavinirjitatārahārāḥ । bhāgīrathīmatha yayuḥ kalahaṃsamañjukāñcīvirāvipulinorunitambabimbāḥ ।।
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। kṛtodakaṃ kṛtāśaucaṃ sthitaṃ surasarittaṭe । munayo abhyāyayurdraṣṭuṃ nāradādyā yudhiṣṭhiram ।।
teṣu prāptāsanārghyeṣu pūjiteṣu purodhasā । prītyā provāca devarṣiḥ pṛṣṭvā nṛpamanāmayam ।। diṣṭyā virājase rājankuśalī nihatāhitaḥ । diṣṭyā śalyādayo vīrā yātā vṛtrasamā kṣayam ।।
kacchinna bandhuvirahādavasthāṃ kātarocitām । mohādālambya dhairyaghnīṃ vijayaṃ nābhinandasi ।। ityukte divyamuninā niḥśvasyovāca dharmajaḥ । śmaśānasadṛśe rājye ko asminmodeta mādṛśaḥ ।।
guravaḥ suhṛdaḥ putrā bhṛtyāḥ saṃbandhibāndhavāḥ । śarīraśeṣairasmābhirghātitā vibhavārthibhiḥ ।। yadarthaṃ rājyamīhante rājāno hatakaṇṭakam । te hatāḥ svajanāḥ sarve gato niṣphalatāṃ śramaḥ ।।
idaṃ dahati me ceto yatkarṇo vinipātitaḥ । sa hi me kathitaḥ kuntyā bhrātā tapanasaṃbhavaḥ ।। purā vikārajaḥ krodhastasminmama puraḥsaraḥ । kuntyāḥ sadṛśapādo asāviti mārdavamāyayau ।।
aiśvaryalubdhairasmābhirnihataḥ sa sahodaraḥ । narakāparaparyāyaṃ dhigrājyamadhunā mama ।। asmadarthe raho mātrā yācitaḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ । kāle kāle rarakṣāsmānpatitānvadhagocare ।।
śrotumicchāmi bhagavaṃstasya śāpo yathābhavat । iti rājñā viṣaṇṇena pṛṣṭaḥ provāca nāradaḥ ।। yuṣmaddeṣātpurā karṇo bhāradvājamayācata । brahmāstraṃ tacca na dadau droṇo asmai phalguṇapriyāt ।।
jñātavyaṃ brāhmaṇenaitadityuktastena duḥkhitaḥ । vipraveṣaṃ vidhāyāśu jāmadagnyāśramaṃ yayau ।। anyevāsī bhṛgubhuvaḥ so atha brahmāstrayācakaḥ । vicacāra ciraṃ dhanvī mahendragirisānuṣu ।।
taṃ kadāciddijaḥ kaścidajñānāvāptakilbiṣam । śaśāpātyantakupito homadhenunikārataḥ ।। mohādapakṛtaṃ yasmāddhomadhenormama tvayā । saktasya śatruṇā tasmādbhūste cakraṃ grasiṣyati ।।
iti śaptaḥ sa vipreṇa dahyamāna ivāniśam । ārādhya rāmaṃ brahmāstramavāpa vipulaśramaḥ ।। tataḥ kadācitsaṃjātavisramavāpa bhṛgusaṃbhavaḥ । karṇasyāṅke śiraḥ kṛtvā suṣvāpa vratakarṣitaḥ ।।
atrāntare kṛmistīkṣṇadaṃṣṭroṣṭhacaraṇaḥ kṛśaḥ । adaśaddāruṇaḥ karṇamalarko nāma duḥsahaḥ ।। guruprabodhacakito yāvatsehe sa tadvyathām । tāvattadrudhirāsikto nidrāṃ tatyāja bhārgavaḥ ।।
kimetaditi saṃbhrāntaḥ śoṇitasparśakūṇitaḥ । daṣṭaṃ rādheyamālokya dadarśa vikṛtākṛtim ।। rāmeṇa dṛṣṭamātro atha bhasmībhūtaḥ kṛmiḥ kṣaṇāt । rākṣaso lohitagrīvaḥ pradīptākṣo babhūva saḥ ।।
so abravīdbhṛgubhāryāyāṃ cāpalādabhilāṣukaḥ । gṛdhro nāma surārātiḥ śapte ahaṃ muninā purā ।। tacchāpānnirayaṃ yātaḥ pāpāṃ yonimimāṃ vibho । tvatsaṃdarśanaparyantāṃ prapannaḥ kṣapitā ca sā ।।
ityuktvā rākṣase yāte karṇaṃ papraccha bhārgavaḥ । kastvaṃ nāsi dvijo nūnaṃ kṣattrastīvravyathāsahaḥ ।। śrutvaitaccakitaḥ karṇo nijaṃ tasmai nyavedayat । kulaṃ nāma ca yenāśu taṃ śaśāpa ruṣā guruḥ ।।
brāhmaṇaccadmanā yasmādbrahmāstraṃ prāptavānasi । tasmāttavaitatparyante vināśamupayāsyati ।। nirasto bhārgaveṇeti karṇaḥ prāpya suyodhanam । yuṣmatsaṃgharṣasauhārdāttenāṅgeṣu kṛtaḥ patiḥ ।।
citrāṅgadasya tanayāṃ kaliṅganṛpateḥ purā । tadbāhubalamāśritya jahāra dhṛtarāṣṭrajaḥ ।। tasminsvayaṃvare karṇaḥ kupitaṃ rājamaṇḍalam । yāte duryodhane pūrvameko darpadayodhayat ।।
jitvā samastabhūpālāñjarāsaṃdhaṃ yaśonidhiḥ । saṃdehadolāmanayanniyuddhena baloddhataḥ ।। jarāsaṃdho dadau tasmai mālinīṃ nagarīṃ jitaḥ । anye ca tatyajurvīrā bhāgaṃ bhāgaṃ nareśvarāḥ ।।
vañcitaḥ sa surendreṇa varmakuṇḍalahāriṇā । śaptaḥ pūrvaṃ dvijendreṇa guruṇā bhārgavena ca ।। prājñayāmantritaḥ kuntyā gāṅgeyena tiraskṛtaḥ । śalyena tejasaḥ śāntyai śrāvitaḥ paruṣā giraḥ ।।
hataḥ kṛṣṇadhiyā dhīro divyāstraiḥ śakrajanmanā । anyathā samare hanyātkastamūrjitavikramam ।। nāradeneti kathite śokārtaṃ dharmanandanam । uvāca kuntī dhairyeṇa vidhūya tanayavyathām ।।
raviṇāpyarthitaḥ saṃdhiṃ bubudhe na vidhervaśāt । yuṣmaddveṣī sa satataṃ mayā svayamupekṣitaḥ ।। yātaḥ sa sūryasadanaṃ saṃmukhaṃ samare hataḥ । mā śucaḥ prāptamadhunā bhuṅkṣva rājyamanākulaḥ ।।
na lebhe śarma vipulānkarṇasya kalayanguṇān । so abravīdgūhanānmāturajñāto asmābhiragrajaḥ ।। yasmāttasmādbhaviṣyanti cchinnasattvā sadā striyaḥ । bhaikṣyeṇa phalamūlairvā vṛttayaḥ santyavāritāḥ ।।
tāstyaktāḥ kathamasmābhirghoraḥ sarvakṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ । lobhāddharmaṃ parityajya prajñāhīnairabhikṣavat ।। dhyātvāsmābhiḥ kulācāraṃ vikrītā tridive gatiḥ । aho śvabhirivāsmābhirghoraḥ sarvakṣayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।।
aṅgakṣayāvadhi kṣudraiḥ kalaho vipulaḥ kṛtaḥ । mittrabanadhuviyogogragrāhasaṃsāravāridhim ।। saṃgatyāgaplavo naiṣa tarāmi vitaraspṛhaḥ । arjunaḥ pṛthivīṃ vīro rakṣatvasmāsu gauravāt ।।
tyajāmyāyāsavirasāmetāṃ kutsitajīvikām । ityuktvati saṃtapte dharmaputre dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। uvāca kopatāmrākṣaḥ kṣaṇamālokayankṣitim । aho nu devaśaptānāṃ duḥkhānyante sukhānyati ।।
tatsarveṣvapi śocanti sarvathā vidhivañcitāḥ । hāsāya sādhugoṣṭhīṣu saṃnyāso ayaṃ tavādhunā ।। naṣṭāmarthayamānasya prāptāṃ ca tyajataḥ śriyam । avasthāviparīteṣu klībakāryeṣu majjatām ।।
saṃnyāso dīrghasūtrāṇāmālasyamabhidhīyate । lajjākaramato loke kimanyatprājñagarhitam ।। yatsarvaṃ tyajati kṣipraṃ naraḥ kṣība ivāmbaram । apūrvamidamārabdhaṃ bhavatā vyasanādhikam ।।
na kadācicchruto asmābhiḥ kila bhikṣāśano nṛpaḥ । kramaprāptāmimāṃ lakṣmīṃ bhaja rājannavikriyaḥ ।। dhanināmeva dhanyānāṃ yajñadānādikāḥ kriyāḥ । yathā hi śocyastyaktārtho na tathā tyaktajīvitaḥ ।।
vyasurmuhūrtaṃ nidhano nirdhanastu sadā mṛtaḥ । imāṃ vasumatīṃ rājanmāndhātṛnahuṣopamaḥ ।। avāpya vividhairyajñairyajasva bahudakṣiṇaiḥ । iti śakrasutenokto dharmasūnurabhāṣata ।।
śrotumarhasi me pārtha hitvā grāmyasukhaspṛhām । śīrṇaparṇalavāhāraḥ samaḥ śāntapriyāpriyaḥ ।। sa brahmacārī vipine kuraṅgāṇāṃ vihāriṇām । dhiyā na cintaye kiṃcinmaunī vigalitāgrahaḥ ।।
nirāhāro bhaviṣyāmi saṃsārocchittaye muniḥ । iti bruvāṇaṃ rājānamabhyadhānmārutātmajaḥ ।। bata deva jaḍasyeva buddhiste durgrahe dṛḍhā । aghātayitvā pṛthivīṃ kiṃ naiṣā dhīstvayā kṛtāḥ ।।
kiṃ jalāhṛtayantreṇa nirdagdhe nagare agninā । rājanna paścimavayāḥ sarvatyāgī na śobhase ।। madhumāsu ivāśokaḥ sahasā śuṣkapallavaḥ । pāptāṃ pāṇapaṇenātha śrameṇa pṛthivīmimām ।।
tyajatastava sāvajñaṃ mohādanyatkimucyate । vidhūya vighnasaṃmardamāsthāya sa cirānnidhim ।। padā kṣipasi kiṃ rājangataṃ na prāpyate punaḥ । taistaiḥ prāṇaparityagaiḥ kāntamāhṛtya gatvarām ।।
madhumatto yathā śete tathā tvaṃ kartumudyataḥ । saṃnyāsavipralabdhātmā na sthitiṃ hātumarhasi ।। muktā vṛkṣā na dṛśyante mokṣaścettyaktakarmaṇām । kiṃ vānyatpatitāḥ sarve tadaiva vyasane vayam ।।
yadaiva tvaṃ grāmakāmastvaṃ dhātrā jyeṣṭhaḥ kṛto asi naḥ । purā vane grāmakāmastvaṃ grāme adya vanotsukaḥ ।। tiṣṭhatyaṅke na ca skanadhe kaṣṭaṃ bāla ivāturaḥ । sattvaśīlāḥ svakarmasthā mucyante gṛhamedhinaḥ ।।
vane kuraṅgamātaṅgā na tu dṛṣṭā divaṃ gatāḥ । ityukte bīmasenena punarūce dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। rājannasti gṛhe mokṣo dhanyānāṃ vighasāśinām । ajātaśmaśravo bālāḥ purā brāhmaṇaputrakāḥ ।।
akāle śritavairāgyā vanametya pravavrajuḥ । saṃjātakarumasteṣu pakṣirūpī puraṃdaraḥ ।। praśaśaṃsa tadabhyāse gṛhasthānvighasāśinaḥ । hiraṇmayasya śukaneste śrutvā bhāṣitaṃ dvijāḥ ।।
ātmānaṃ menire mūrkhāḥ prahṛṣṭā vighasāśinam । śakuniḥ so atha taiḥ pṛṣṭo jagāda vihasanniva ।। rūkṣāḥ kṛśā malādigdhā vipine kaṣṭavṛttayaḥ । duḥkhaikabhāgino nityaṃ na yūyaṃ vighasāsinaḥ ।।
sāyaṃ prātarvibhajyānnaṃ vidhivadgṛhamedhinaḥ । bhṛtyārthiśeṣaṃ ye aśnanti te dhanyā vighasāśinaḥ ।। teṣāṃ puṇyairaparyantairdivi lokāḥ sanātanāḥ । gṛhādāśramiṇaḥ sarve jīvantyabhrādiva prajāḥ ।।
evaṃ te bodhitā yuktvā svagarūpeṇa vajriṇā । vanavāsaṃ parityajya dvijāḥ svagṛhamāyayuḥ ।। gatijñaḥ sarvadharmāṇāmācāryāṇāṃ ca tattvavit । tvamapyevaṃ mahīpāla na sthitiṃ tyaktumarhasi ।।
arjuneneti kathite mādrīputrāvathocatuḥ । bhaja rājyamanāyāsamidamuddhṛtakaṇṭakam ।। sāmrājyavijayī yajvā pāhi bhūmipate prajāḥ । yamābhyāmityabhihite priyā praṇayinī priyam ।।
draupadī dharmatanayaṃ babhāṣe valguvādinī । tvadājñākāriṇo vīrā bhrātarastridaśatviṣaḥ ।। anutsāhena te paśya likhantyete mṛṣā bhuvam । yadetairduṣkaraṃ karma samare kṛtamojasā ।।
tadadya rājyabhāgena saphalaṃ kartumarhasi । adhomukhānāṃ śvasatāṃ niṣphalārambhaduḥkhinām ।। praṇayairmānayaiteṣāmabhinanadya parākramam । aklībacarito rājanrājyaṃ nijabhujārjitam ।।
bhajasva vijayotthānāṃ na klībāḥ saṃpadāṃ padam । ityukte kṛṣṇayā jiṣṇuḥ punarnṛpamabhāṣata ।। lokasya pālanātsamyagrājānaḥ svargagāminaḥ । svadharmeṣu pravartante rājadaṇḍabhayātprajāḥ ।।
mitho matsyā ivāśnanti janā daṇḍavivarjitāḥ । yatra saṃnihito daṇḍaḥ śyāmo lohitalocanaḥ ।। tatra vedaiśca yajñaiśca vardhante dharmasaṃpadaḥ । taistaistapobhirucitairyatphalaṃ śāntatojasām ।।
tadeva daṇḍadhārasya dharmabhrāturmahībhṛtaḥ । janakaṃ rājyavimukhaṃ yiyāsuṃ kānanaṃ purā ।। uvāca patnī praṇayānmadhuraṃ dharmavādinī । rājanvane na mokṣo asti bandho nāsti gṛheṣu ca ।।
svakarmaṇi pravṛttānāmapavargo vivekinām । amuṇḍitaspṛhā muṇḍā bahirantaḥ kaṣāyiṇaḥ ।। dambhadharmadhvajā loke kathyante dharmavādibhiḥ । tasmādrājye api bhavatā vartamānena sarvadā ।।
labhyaḥ satyamasaktena sukhinā saṃsṛtikṣayaḥ । ityukto maithilaḥ patnyā jīvanmuktadaśāṃ śritaḥ ।। yayāvatyaktarājyo api paramaṃ dhāma śāśvatam । phalguṇeneti kathite devasthāne praśaṃsati ।।
muniḥ pravṛttadharmaṃ ca kṛṣṇadvaipāyano abravīt । prajānāṃ pālanaṃ samyaksvadharmaste mahīpate ।। araṇyagamanaṃ rājñāmakāle sthitiviplavaḥ । siddhiṃ prakṛtino yātāḥ sudyumnapramukhā nṛpāḥ ।।
tapaḥkleśairasaṃspṛṣṭa yathāvaddaṇḍadhāraṇāt । bhrātarau prāḍmunivarau śrutismṛtiviśāradau ।। abhūtāṃ śaṅkhalikhitāvācāraniśitavratau । kadācidāśrame bhrātuḥ svayamādāya pādapāt ।।
phalāni likhito mohādbhuktavānpraṇayādiva । tamabhyetyābravīcchaṅkho dharmabhraṃśabhayākulaḥ ।। stainyametanna jānīṣe kasmātparaphalāśanam । gaccha pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ bhrātaḥ svayaṃ rājñe nivedaya ।।
ityukto likhitastena sudyamnaṃ vasudhādhipam । śrutvācacakṣe daṇḍārthīṃ sa svayaṃ phalabhakṣaṇam ।। tamabhyadhātkṣitipatirbhagavanvipulavratāḥ । yūyaṃ pramāṇaṃ dharmāṇāṃ śucirgaccha varānmama ।।
ityucyamāno rājñāpi daṇḍameva punaḥ punaḥ । so ayācata sadācārabhraṃśabhīrurnareśvaram ।। tatastasya karacchedamādideśa mahīpatiḥ । chinnahastaḥ sa ca yayau prahṛṣṭo bhrāturantikam ।।
tadgirā ca punardadyāṃ snātvā jātakaradvayaḥ । sa babhūva tapoyogātpraśāntānuśayajvaraḥ ।। sudyumno api prajānāthaḥ samyagdaṇḍasya dhāraṇāt । tapaḥsamucitāṃllokānavāpa yaśasāṃ nidhiḥ ।।
sudyumnopākhyānam ।। tasmātpālaya bhūpāla kṣattradharme sthitaḥ prajāḥ । kṣayaṃ kālakṛtaṃ vīkṣya mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ ।। bhūtvā bhūtvā pralīyante kālena kalitāḥ kila ।
lokāḥ kālakalājalaiścitraścāyaṃ bhavaśramaḥ ।। uktaṃ senajitā rājñā purā rājanvivekinā । duḥkhe dṛḍhaṃ manaḥ kuryānnartiśokagadauṣadham ।। śocatāṃ dhṛtihīnānāṃ na śāntirjāyate kvacit ।
duḥkhairāyānti duḥkhāni dhanānīva dhanairnṛṇām ।। dṛṣṭvā jagati jantūnāṃ kāle kāle bhavābhavam । phalānāmiva kālajñaḥ ko anuśocati tattvadhīḥ ।। janakena purā pṛṣṭo jagāda brāhmaṇo aśmakaḥ ।
svabhāvanaśvarānbhāvānna śocanti vivekinaḥ ।। na kaściddṛśyate atyetuṃ sthāvareṣu careṣu ca । śakto hyāyuṣi maryādāṃ yaḥ kālavihitāṃ bhavet ।। dhanamāyuḥ śarīraṃ ca jātistaruṇatā tathā ।
bhajante kālavaicitryānnānārūpaviparyayam ।। uccā nīcatvamāyānti viśīryante ca saṃhatāḥ । bhavanti kila kālena nimnānyucchrāyavanti ca ।। hīnavaṃśāḥ kulīnatvaṃ dhaninaśca daridratām ।
yānti mūrkhāśca vaiduṣyaṃ daurbhāgyaṃ subhagāstathā ।। svalpāyuṣaśca rājāno daridrāśca śatāyuṣaḥ । jarābhagnāśca dṛśyante rasāyanavicakṣaṇāḥ ।। dhanino vyādhisaṃtaptā daridrāśca nirāmayāḥ ।
āyurvedavido yānti taruṇā eva pañcatām ।। mūrkhāḥ sadācāraratāḥ paṇḍitā dharmavarjitāḥ । bhavanti kālavihataistaistaiḥ kila viparyayaiḥ ।। api trailokyakartārascaturmukhamukhāḥ surāḥ ।
na hi kālakaṭākṣeṇa lakṣitaṃ rakṣituṃ kṣamāḥ ।। śrīmatāṃ hīnavittānāṃ dhīmatāṃ jaḍacetasām । tulyaṃ niranurakto hi kālapaṇyagṛhe krayaḥ ।। kālānilavilolānāṃ dehināṃ bhavakānane ।
drumāṇāmiva jāyante mitho nityaṃ gamāgamāḥ ।। akasmātsaṃgato nāma yadyakasmādvinaśyanti । śokaḥ kiṃ tatra jantūnāṃ satataṃ hi gatāgatam ।। na viyogeṣu saṃtāpaḥ kāryaḥ kila vivekibhiḥ ।
abhāvānubhave bhāvā bhave hi kṣaṇabhaṅginaḥ ।। aśmakeneti kathitaṃ kathayitvā munīśvaraḥ । virarāma samālokya gāḍhaśoka yudhiṣṭhiram ।। aśmakagītā ।।
athārjunena praṇayātpreritaḥ puṣkarekṣaṇaḥ । bhagavānkaiṭabhārātirdharmasūnubhāṣata ।। viṣādaṃ mā vṛthā rājañśarīrocchoṣaṇaṃ kṛthāḥ । teṣāṃ hatānāṃ vīrāṇāṃ na śokātpunarāgamaḥ ।।
eke adya prātarapare paścādanye punaḥ pare । sarve niḥsīmni saṃsāre yānti kaḥ kena śocyate ।। nūnamakṣayamātmānaṃ mohātsarvo abhimanyate । yatpuraḥsthitanāśo api naṣṭañśocati naśvaraḥ ।।
te janāste prabhāvāśca tāśca prajvalitāḥ śriyaḥ । helayā kila kālena prāpitāḥ smṛtiśeṣatām ।। sṛñjayaṃ nāma bhūpālaṃ bhagavāneṣa nāradaḥ । kṛpayāśvāsayannūce putraśokākulaṃ purā ।।
rājanprāptāvadhiṃ putraṃ yātaṃ kimanuśocasi । sarvaṃ jagatsahāsmābhiḥ paryante na bhaviṣyati ।। matuttaḥ pṛthivīpālaḥ kālena nidhanaṃ gataḥ । yasyāsanbhuvi gīrvāṇāḥ sendrā yajñasabhāsadāḥ ।।
vavarṣa kanakaṃ yasmai vatsaraṃ pākaśāsanaḥ । abhūdbṛhaspatibhrātā saṃvarto yasya yājakaḥ ।। suhotraśca mahīnāthaḥ kathāśeṣatvamāgataḥ । yo yathārthāṃ vasumatīṃ cakre kāñcanavṛṣṭibhiḥ ।।
bṛhadrathaśca nṛpatiryāto astaṃ rathināṃ varaḥ । yasya yajñe surapatiḥ somaṃ pītvā mudaṃ yayau ।। śibirauśīnaraḥ pṛthvīmekacchatrāṃ śaśāsa yaḥ । sa dhuryaḥ sarvadāttṝṇāṃ prayātaḥ kīrtiśeṣatām ।।
sahasreṇāśvamedhānāṃ rājasūyaśatena ca । īje yaḥ so api bharataḥ kālena tridivaṃ gataḥ ।। sa ca dāśarāthī rāmo daśakaṇṭhakulāntakaḥ । yātaḥ paryantapadavīṃ gīyamānaguṇaḥ suraiḥ ।।
bhagīrathaśca bhūpālastapasā yas jāhnavī । avāpa śaṃkaraśiraḥ sa kālasyecchayā gataḥ ।। so api smṛtidaśāṃ prāpto dilīpaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ । yūpe hiraṇmaye yasya nanṛtustridivaukasaḥ ।।
ayonijaśca māṃdhātā sa sarvavijayī nṛpaḥ । gataḥ śakrādayo devā yasyāsankāntavikrame ।। yayātirapi kālena kṣmāpālaḥ pralayaṃ gataḥ । devāsuraraṇe vīro yo jaghānāmaradviṣaḥ ।।
yaśaḥ śarīramaviśatso ambarīṣaśca pārthivaḥ । yasya śāsanamamlānaṃ nṛpā mālyamivāvahan ।। śaśabindurnarapatiḥ so apyantapadamāśritaḥ । abhūtkoṭiśataṃ yasya putrāṇāṃ śakravarcasām ।।
gato gayaśca nṛpatiryaḥ kāñcanamayīṃ mahīm । pradadau yasya saṃkhyāṃ ca yajñānāṃ na pracakṣate ।। prayāto rantidevaśca yajñeṣu paśucarmabhiḥ । srutaiḥ pravartitā tena puṇyā carmaṇvatī nadī ।।
atītaḥ sa ca bhūpālaḥ sagaro yena sāgarāḥ । ṣaṣṭyā putrasahasrāṇāṃ kṛtāsturagarakṣiṇām ।। vainyaśca yo dhanuṣkoṭyā parvatānkarotpṛthak । so api śakrādhipo rājā priyaṃ tatyāja vigraham ।।
ete cānye ca bhūpālāḥ kālena kavalīkṛtāḥ । mā śacastava madvākyātputraḥ sṛñjaya jīvatu ।। ityuktvā nārado rājñaḥ kanakaṣṭhīvinaṃ sutam । taṃ sahasrāyuṣaṃ cakre jīvayitvā kṛpānidhiḥ ।।
ṣoḍaśarājakīyam ।। kathaṃ sa kāñcanaṣṭhīvī sṛñjayasya suto abhavat । pṛṣṭo dharmasuteneti punaruce caturbhujaḥ ।। sṛñjayasya kṣitipatestathā nāradaparvatau ।
devarṣī tasthaturgehe martyalokavihāriṇau ।। vaktavyaṃ hṛdgataṃ sarvaṃ mithastāviti saṃvidam । cakratustatra sahitau prītyā praṇayaśālinau ।। sṝñjayastatsaparyāyai kanyāṃ lāvaṇyabhūṣaṇām ।
yathārthanāmnīṃ tanayāṃ sukumārīṃ samādiśat ।। bālāṃ paricarantīṃ tāṃ hariṇīhārilocanām । nirvarṇayannanimiṣo nārado abūtsmarākulaḥ ।। taṃ tasya hṛdgataṃ bhāvaṃ gūhamānasya lajjayā ।
svasrīyaḥ parvataḥ kṣipraṃ bubudhe jñānacakṣuṣā ।। maryādābhraṃśakupitaḥ sa śaśāpātha mātulam । patirvānararūpo asyāḥ sukumāryā bhaviṣyasi ।। iti tena ruṣā śaptaḥ kopāttamapi nāradaḥ ।
śaśāpāśvargago bhūyādbhavāniti sutaṃ svasuḥ ।। vitīrṇāṃ sṛñjayenātha kanyāṃ kālena nāradaḥ । tāṃ prāpyodvāhasamaye kṣaṇāccāsīttathavidhaḥ ।। sāpi tadvidhamāsādya bhartāraṃ nāradaṃ satī ।
ananyamanasā mene taṃ netrāmṛtanirjharam ।। śamayitvā mithaḥ śāpaṃ praśānte manyuviplave । prītyā babhūvatuḥ svasthau tau parityajya vikriyām ।। tyaktavānararūpaṃ ca sukumārī pativratā ।
śaṅkitā nāradaṃ bheje cireṇa jñātatatkathā ।। ataḥ śeṣāṃ kathāmeṣa svayaṃ vadatu nāradaḥ । ityuktvā virate kṛṣṇe tamapṛcchadyudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। munistenābravītpṛṣṭastathāhaṃ parvatānugaḥ ।
uṣitvā sṛñjayagṛhe paritoṣamupāgataḥ ।। asmadvarāttato rājñaḥ sṛñjayasya suto gataḥ । yathārthaṃ kāñcanaṣṭhīvī na sehe taṃ śatakratuḥ ।। taṃ śiśuṃ jāhnavītīre kelisaktaṃ yadṛcchayā ।
aghātayatsurapatirvajreṇa vyāghrarūpiṇā ।। sṛñjayastaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā putraṃ rājīvalocanam । śuśoca viṣamāyāsamūrchāvihvalamānasaḥ ।। pralāpamukharaṃ kṣmāpaṃ taṃ vilokyāhamākulam ।
kṛpayājīvayaṃ tasya svarṇaṣṭhīvinamātmajam ।। madvarātsa sahasrāyurbhuktvā vasumatīmimām । kālena yātastridivaṃ sthāyino na hi dehinaḥ ।। svarṇaṣṭhīvyupākhyānam ।।
nāradeneti kathite vyāsenāpi muhurmuhuḥ । bodhito dharmatanayaḥ śokārtaḥ punarabravīt ।। lobhāndhaṃ patitaṃ dhiṅbhāmasminkilbiṣasaṃkaṭe । bhogāśayā kṛto yena gurubandhusutakṣayaḥ ।।
punaḥ punarimāṃ hutvā vahnau pātakinīṃ tanum । kṣayaṃ yāsyati manye no na bhīṣmavadhapātakam ।। iti śokānalakrāntaṃ vilapantaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram । uvāca lokasthitaye parāśarasuto muniḥ ।।
saṃgrāmajīvināṃ rājñāṃ dharmaḥ śatruvadhaḥ sadā । kṛtvā kulocitaṃ karma mā viṣādaṃ vṛthā kṛthāḥ ।। kīrtanairanutāpaiśca prāyaścittairmahābalaiḥ । dānaistīrthābhiṣekaiśca pāpānāmasti niṣkṛtiḥ ।।
nijadharmaparityāgāttvaṃ tu rājansakalmaṣaḥ । yajasva hayamedhena mithyā yadi viśaṅkase ।। prajāḥ pālaya visrabdhaṃ hatanāthāśca yoṣitaḥ । nihātārātiputrāṇāṃ putravatpaśya kanyakāḥ ।।
iti bruvāṇo bhagavānrājñā pṛṣṭo muniḥ punaḥ । uvāca sarvapāpānāṃ praśāntiṃ śāntaviplavaḥ ।। satkarmaṇāmakaraṇānninditānāṃ ca sevanāt । paścāttāpamanāsādya prāyaścittaṃ naror'hati ।।
kapālī dvādaśa samāścaranbhaikṣyamasaṃvṛtaḥ । brahmahatyābhayāttīvrādvratānte mucyate naraḥ ।। etattulyāni pāpāni yajñairvipuladakṣiṇaiḥ । gosahasrapradānaiśca taranti kila dehinaḥ ।।
surāpaiśceryata pāpaṃ pītvāgnisadṛśīṃ surām । vahnivarṇaśikhāśāyī mucyate gurutalpagaḥ ।। bhṛguvahninipātena mahāprasthānakena ca । mahīdānena dātṝṇāṃ kṣīyate gurupātakam ।।
prāyaścittaṃ na tu strīṇāṃ rajasā saṃvṛtā hitāḥ । mahaugheneva vāhinyo bhavanti vimalāśayāḥ ।। bhakṣyābhakṣyavicāreṇa kāryākāryavibhedataḥ । vihitāvihitodīrṇaḥ sūkṣmo ayaṃ dharmasaṃkaraḥ ।।
abhinandya nijaṃ rājyaṃ svīkṛtya prakṛtīstathā । gaccha śāntanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ sa te dharmānpravakṣyati ।। iti dvaipāyanenoktaḥ kṛṣṇena ca vibodhitaḥ । dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ puraskṛtya nagaraṃ sānugo aviśat ।।
pūjyamānaḥ prakṛtibhirgīyamānaśca māgadhaiḥ । rājadhānīṃ samāsādya viveśa rucirāṃ sabhām ।। upasthitānsvayaṃ tatra brāhmaṇānvipulāśiṣaḥ । apūjayatpuraskṛtya dhaumyaṃ dhuryaṃ purodhasām ।।
yudhiṣṭhiranagarapraveśaḥ ।। atrāntare tridaṇḍāṅkastriśikhaḥ kapaṭo muniḥ । suhṛdduryodhanasyāyāccārvāko nāma rāśrasaḥ ।। so abravīddharmajaṃ rājanvacmi tvāṃ brāhmaṇājñayā ।
bandhumittradruhaḥ kiṃ te rājyena dhvastatejasaḥ ।। iti bruvāṇe cārvāke viṣaṇṇe ca yudhiṣṭhire । brāhmaṇāste krudhāviṣṭā jajñire jñānacakṣuṣaḥ ।। sakhā duryodhanasyāyaṃ cārvāko nāma rākṣasaḥ ।
uktveti taṃ dvijāścakrur huṃkāreṇaiva bhasmasāt ।। tasminbrāhmaṇakopena nirdagdhe rajanīcare । uvāca vihasañśauriramṛtaṃ vikiranniva ।। avadhyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tapasvī vedhaso varāt ।
edho brāhmaṇakopāgnerbabhūvaiṣa niśācaraḥ ।। so ayaṃ diṣṭyā hataḥ pāpastejasā brahmavādinām । ityuktavati govinde sabhāyāmutsavo abhavat ।। cārvākanigrahaḥ ।।
athābhiṣeko divyena vidhinā dharmajanmanaḥ । avartata hate vṛtre devasyeva śatakratoḥ ।। sumeruvipule pīṭhe pariṣvakto jayaśriyā । pradīpasaṃdhyāruciro divākara ivābabhau ।।
dhṛtvā daivatavatpūrvaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ vadhūsakham । nidhāya mārutasutaṃ yauvarājye mahābhujam ।। viduraṃ mantrakāryeṣu digjayeṣu dhanaṃjayam । saṃjayaṃ vyayacintāsu nakulaṃ sainyapālane ।।
dhaumyaṃ brāhmaṇacintāsu sahadevaṃ ca saṃnidhau । uciteṣu ca kāryeṣu vṛddhāmātyānakalpayat ।। yudhiṣṭhirābhiṣekaḥ ।। tataḥ stutvā hṛṣīkeśaṃ duryodhananiveśanam ।
mahārharatnaruciraṃ dadau bhīmāya dharmajaḥ ।। vṛtaṃ dāsīsahasraiśca duḥśāsanagṛhaṃ nṛpaḥ । arjunāya dadau ratnakāñcanodāramandiram ।। anyebhyo api vilabhyaivaṃ kauravāvasathāvalīm ।
labdhapraśamanaṃ cakre cakrāyudhamate sthitaḥ ।। tato vidhāya bandhūnāṃ rājā śrāddhaṃ yathāvidhi । prapākūpanipānāṅkāstebhyo dharmānakalpayat ।। atha prabhāte bhūpālaḥ pūjayitvāmbikāsutam ।
gāndharīṃ svāṃ ca jananīṃ praṇamya racitāñjaliḥ ।। viśrāntaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ stitamarjunamandire । sānugaḥ prayayau druṣṭuṃ brahmaṇamiva vāsavaḥ ।। tamāsādya nabhaḥśyāmaṃ vyāptaṃ kaustubhakāntibhiḥ ।
dineśakiraṇodāravāsarārambhavibhramam ।। sumerukūṭavikaṭe niṣaṇṇaṃ kanakāsane । tatkāntivalayeneva saṃvītaṃ pītavāsasā ।। dhyāyantaṃ kimapi prahvo jagāda jagatīpatiḥ ।
taddarśanānandasudhāṃ dantakāntyā kiranniva ।। sukhena kaccidbhagavanvyatītā tava śarvarī । tvadyoganidrāsarasīvilāsramarāvalī ।। ityuktaḥ kamalākāntaḥ kimapi dhyānamāsthitaḥ ।
na jagāda yadā kiṃcittadā rājāvadatpunaḥ ।। aho na sarvabhūtātmandhyeyastvaṃ tattvadarśinām । vimalaṃ dhyānamālambya vismayaṃ vidadhāsi naḥ ।। kuśalaṃ jagatāṃ kacciditi vādini bhūpatau ।
īṣadunmīlya nayane viśvarūpī tamabhyadhāt ।। śaraśayyāgato bhīṣmaḥ pravṛttaḥ stotumadya mām । tamahaṃ manasā yāto mānyaṃ sarvamanīṣiṇām ।। sa me bahumataḥ śrīmānyoginaṃ cintayāmi tam ।
ye māṃ smaranti satataṃ dehatyāge smarāmi tān ।। uttarāśāpraṇayitāṃ yātaḥ prāyo divākaraḥ । devavratasya kāle ayaṃ mumukṣordehamuktaye ।। śrutvaitaddharmatanayaḥ praṇayāvartitāñjaliḥ ।
uvāca bhagavanbhīṣmastvatsaṃdarśanamarhati ।। tadehi sarve gacchāmastaṃ druṣṭuṃ tejasāṃ nidhim । aśeṣasaṃśayacchettā sa me jñānaṃ pravakṣyati ।। ityukto dharmarājena sahitaḥ phalguṇena ca ।
bhīmasātyakimukhyaiśca pratasthe syandane hariḥ ।। asminnavasare bhīṣmaḥ sarvairmunigaṇairvṛtaḥ । tuṣṭāva prayato dhyātvā viṣṇuṃ jiṣṇuṃ jagaddhiṣām ।। saṃsāramarusaṃtāpanirvāṇasuraśākhine ।
mohastambheramaghaṭāharaye haraye namaḥ ।। sphuratsaṃvinmaṇiśikhāṃ cittaprāṅganacandrikām । prapadye bhagavadbhaktimānandodyānavāhinīm ।। phullollasatsamutsāhaśaktivyāptajagattrayām ।
yā pūrvakoṭirbhāvānāṃ sattāṃ tāṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ namaḥ ।। pavanāghaṭṭitāmbhojavanaparyantalambinām । jalānāmiva jantūnāṃ sthairyameko hariḥ smṛtaḥ ।। namaḥ sūryātmane tasmai saṃvitkiraṇaśāline ।
hṛtkuśeśayakośaśrīsamunmeṣavidhāyine ।। namastasmai yamīkṣante jñānino gatamṛtyavaḥ । paramaṃ puruṣaṃ pāre tamasāṃ mahasāṃ tathā ।। yajñāya yajñahaviṣe yajñasomamayātmane ।
namaḥ sarasvatīvāhahaṃsāyākhilarūpiṇe ।। satyāya dharmanidhaye kṣetrajñāyāmṛtātmane । sāṃkhyayogapratiṣṭhāya namo mokṣaikahetave ।। ghorāya māyānidhaye sahasraśirase namaḥ ।
yoganidrātmane nābhipadmodbhūtajagatsṛje ।। namaḥ salilarūpāya kāraṇāya jagatsthitau । duṣṭakālāya valine jīvāya pavanātmane ।। kālāya dhāmne varṇānāṃ sarvalokamayātmane ।
lokaprāṇāya bhūtānāṃ namo viśvāya vedhase ।। tṛptāya siṃhavapuṣe daityasaṃhārakāriṇe । vīryāyānantamahase jagadbhārabhṛte namaḥ ।। saṃsārakartre mohāya jñānāya timiracchide ।
acityadhāmne guhyāya rudrāya jaṭine namaḥ ।। śāntāya śāntakallolakaivalyapadaśāyine । sarvabhāvātiriktāya namaḥ sarvamayātmane ।। indīvaravanaśyāsame sphuratkiñjilkavibhrame ।
bibhrāṇaṃ vāsasī viṣṇuṃ naumi netrarasāyanam ।। ityuktvā nirbharānandaḥ praṇamya manasā harim । dadhyau śāntanavaḥ sāstraiḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ ।। atha pāṇḍusutaiḥ sārdhaṃ rathairgambhīranādibhiḥ ।
āyayau sātyakisakhaḥ saṃjayādyaiśca keśavaḥ ।। āyātkṛṣṇaḥ kurukṣetraṃ tānpaśyanbhārgavahradān । yudhiṣṭhirāyākathayaddharmyaṃ rāmaparākramam ।। tataḥ surasaritsūnuṃ dadarśa śaraśāyinam ।
sānugaḥ śaurirabhyetya svāṃśujālairivāvṛtam ।। taruṇārkopamāpātraṃ vṛddhaṃ vṛddhena tejasā । ruddhaṃ siṃhamiva sphāraśarakāñcanapañjare ।। avaruhya rathātkṛṣṇaḥ sānugaśca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।
praṇamyopāviśansarve praśaṃsantaḥ pitāmaham ।। tato abravīcchāntanavaṃ śaraśreṇīvṛthākulam । sādaraṃ puṇḍarīkākṣo dṛśā nirvāpayannivaṣa ।। kañcitte vimalaṃ jñānaṃ paramaṃ brahmadarśanam ।
vajrāgradāruṇaśarasyūtasya na vilupyate ।। nidhānaṃ guṇaratnānāṃ śekharaṃ śauryaśālinām । dhanyatā māninī manye vahati tvāṃ vasuṃdharā ।। gāḍhānuśayasaṃtaptastvayi vīra śarārdite ।
vyathito dharmatanayo na kvāpi labhate dhṛtim ।। sarvajña dharmānakhilānkathayāsmai girā mama । prasannakaraṇajñānapaṭurbhava gatavyathaḥ ।। kṣīrodaśāyī bhagavānityuktvā garuḍadhvajaḥ ।
karāmṛtakarāluptavyathaṃ cakre suravratam ।। athāpatatpuṣpavṛṣṭirmūrdhni gāṅgeyakṛṣṇayoḥ । vyāsanāradamukhyāśca praśaśaṃsuḥ smayena tau ।। śvo vaktāsmyakhilāndharmānityukte atha janārdanaḥ ।
jāhvavīsutamāmantrya prataśthe pāṇḍavaiḥ saha ।। uṣitvā rajanīṃ śauriḥ pārthāśca nijaveśmani । rathaiḥ śāntanavaṃ druṣṭuṃ prātaḥ sarve samāyayuḥ ।। te vihāya rathāṃstūrṇaṃ praṇipatya pitāmaham ।
parivāryopaviviśuḥ sevyamānaṃ maharṣibhiḥ ।। tataḥ pṛṣṭo harirbhīṣmaṃ śāntavyathamanāmayam । uvāca kathyatāṃ didvansvadharmāndharmasūnave ।। bhavatprasādātsvartho ahaṃ vakṣyāmi tava śāsanāt ।
kiṃ tu pṛcchatu māṃ rājā dharmaniṣṭho yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। vṛtte kṣatrocite kārye na lajjā kartumarhati । ukte pitāmaheneti kṛṣṇavākyādyudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। abhyetya bhīṣmacaraṇau vavande hrīnatānanaḥ ।
sa tena mūrdhnyupāghrāya pṛccha māmiti coditaḥ ।। prajānāṃ pālane dharmaṃ pūrvaṃ papraccha dharmajaḥ । tato jagāda gāṅgeyaḥ praṇamya manasā harim ।। śṛṇu putra yathā rājye virājante nareśvarāḥ ।
paramaṃ saṃśayasthānamādhipatyaṃ pramādinām ।। atikaṅkaṇakeyūrahāraṃ rājñāṃ vibhūṣaṇam । nityaṃ dvijātimānyatvaṃ prajāpālanarañjanam ।। paramaṃ daivataṃ viprā nigrahānugrahāya ca ।
rājñāṃ śriyo hi tadvākyādbhavanti na bhavanti ca ।। jātaṃ brāhmaṇataḥ kṣattraṃ salilācca hutāśanaḥ । śastraṃ tathāśmato yāni kṣata mete svajanmasu ।। rājavṛttiriyaṃ pūrvā yanna tīvraṃ na mārdavam ।
rūḍhirviṣāmṛtasphārairbhīmaḥ sevyaśca sāgaraḥ ।। hitairmānyaiśca rakṣyante bhṛtyairnṛpatisaṃpadaḥ । tāneva nābhimanyante rājāno hi niraṅkuśāḥ ।। sunayo rājavṛttīnāṃ vinayo guṇasaṃpadām ।
lāvaṇyamiva nārīṇāṃ vibhūṣaṇamakṛtrimam ।। sa nṛpaḥ kamalākelidhāmakarṇābjaṣaṭpadaḥ । piśunairnābhimanyante yasminsaṃbhṛtavṛttayaḥ ।। siddhaye saṃyatadhiyāṃ sanmantrabalaśālinām ।
samastacittagrahaṇaṃ yogināmiva bhūbhujām ।। mṛduṃ bālamivādhairyaṃ vinodarasikaṃ sadā । rājānaṃ hāsyasaṃpannaṃ manyante sevakāstṛṇam ।। narmasācivyamāptāste bhūpaterlaghucetasaḥ ।
tāṃ tāmutkramya maryādāṃ vartante kāmacāriṇaḥ ।। rājasrīsaṃgamaṃ yānti rājatulyavibhūṣaṇāḥ । suṣiraṃ kurvate rājyaṃ svāṃ svaniṃ mūṣikā iva ।। hayaṃ rathaṃ gajaṃ vāso rājayogyaṃ tathāsanam ।
āruhya rājñā spardhante vismaranti ca bhṛtyatām ।। bahu dattaṃ na manyante yācante durlabhānyapi । nindanti svābhicaritaṃ bahirmantraṃ kiranti ca ।। rājadeyaṃ harantaśca lajjante nijakarmasu ।
prathayanti ca mithyaiva loke bhūpālavaśyatām ।। svāminā kelisaktena śanakairmarmadarśinaḥ । kimanyatpeśaladhiyā khelante rājavallabhāḥ ।। mantrairbhūtāni śāmyanti dānairmṛtyurnivartate ।
prajānāṃ dalane saktā na tu te rājasaṃmatāḥ ।। susahāyaḥ sthirārambho gūḍhamantraḥ sadodyataḥ । prajāhito apramattaśca rājā rājye virājate ।। ko hi paśyedimaṃ lokaṃ gāḍhena tamasā vṛtam ।
rājñaḥ śaśāṅkayaśasaḥ pratāpo yadi na sphuret ।। avaśyamekacaraṇo dharmo asminkalikardame । praskhaledbhūmipālānāṃ vinā daṇḍāvalambanam ।। arājake purā loke pravṛtte dharmaviplave ।
surārthitena vidhinā nayopāye pravartate ।। caturvargaphale śāstre bhāgairātte munīśvaraiḥ । asṛjanmānasaṃ jiṣṇuṃ tumulaṃ virajaṃ sutam ।। sa niyukto bhagavatā prajānāṃ paripālane ।
tacchāsanamanādṛtya saṃnyāsavirato abhavat ।। kīryāmāno api tatputrastathaiva tapase gataḥ । tatsutaḥ kardamākhyaśca viraktaḥ kānanaṃ yayau ।। anaṅganāmnastatsūnostanayo atibalastataḥ ।
rājābhūnmṛtyutanayāṃ munīnāṃ prāpa yaḥ priyām ।। venaṃ nāma sutaṃ tasyāṃ saṃprāpya tapase yayau । tataḥ krūro abhavadrājā venaḥ kopaviṣolbaṇaḥ ।। munayo mantrapūtaistaṃ jaghnurvajraśitaiḥ kuśaiḥ ।
tasyoruṃ dakṣiṇaṃ mantraiste nirmathya maharṣayaḥ ।। hrasvaṃ dehaṃ tadudbhūtaṃ dadṛśurvikṛtaṃ naram । sa tairukto niṣīdeti niṣādajanako abhavat ।। venasya dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇiṃ nirmathya munayaḥ punaḥ ।
apaśyanvainyamuditaṃ sāyudhaṃ śakravikramam ।। sa daṇḍanītimāsādya śaśāsa muniśāsanāt । prāptāṃ ratnapradāṃ sākṣātpṛthvīṃ sagirisāgarām ।। tamāviveśa bhagavāṃllokapālasakho hariḥ ।
naradevā iti khyātāstataḥ prabhṛti bhūmipāḥ ।। rājamānaguṇe tasminrājani kṣmāṃ praśāsati । svadharmaniratāstasthuḥ samyagdaṇḍabhayātprajāḥ ।। teneyaṃ vihitā rājñāṃ sthitaye daṇḍadhāratā ।
yathā lokāḥ prakāśante na sūryeṇa na cendunā ।। rājotpattiḥ ।। samyagvyavasite trātuṃ rājñi dharmapare prajāḥ । sthitayo na vilupyante cāturvarṇyavibhāgajāḥ ।।
yathāvidhiprayātānāmāśramādāśramāntaram । cāturāśramyavihitā siddhirvighnairna hanyate ।। māṃdhāturnṛpateḥ pūrvaṃ yajñadarśanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ । śakrarūpadharo viṣṇurbhagavānsvayamāyayau ।।
pṛṣṭo jijñāsayā tena sa rājā praṇipatya tam । uvāca sarvadharmāṇāṃ pratiṣṭhiḥ rājaśāntaye ।। rājanītyā pravartante khakarmasu sadā prajāḥ । śrutismṛtisadācāre kāraṇaṃ rājavṛttayaḥ ।।
trātā dharmagatasyāsya yasmātkila nareśvaraḥ । gauravādātmatulyaṃ taṃ svadharmasthamamanyata ।। pitā prajānāṃ nṛpatirjagatsīdatyarājakam । vastavyaṃ mlecchamadhye api sādhubhirna tvarājake ।।
durbalaṃ ghnanti balinaḥ sevante ca parastriyaḥ । māṃsaṃ mithaśca khādante rāṣṭre rājavivarjite ।। arājakāḥ prajāḥ pūrvaṃ nimagnāḥ sthitiviplave । cakrire rājabhāgārthaṃ manuṃ nimagnāḥ sthitiviplave ।
cakrire rājabhāgārthaṃ manuṃ vaivasvataṃ nṛpam ।। rājñā sumanasā pūrvaṃ kausalyena bṛhaspatiḥ । pṛṣṭo babhāṣe lokānāṃ daṇḍadhāraṃ parāyaṇam ।। nārājakeṣu rāṣṭreṣu havyaṃ vahati pāvakaḥ ।
na ca dharmāḥ pravartante na ca varṣati vāsavaḥ ।। kuto dhanaṃ kuto dārāḥ śarīraṃ ca kuto nṛṇām । sarvadevamayastrātā yāvanna vasudhādhipaḥ ।। sarvāvalokane sūryaḥ pāpānāṃ nigrahe yamaḥ ।
kubero bharaṇe rājā prāyaścitteṣu pāvakaḥ ।। ācchettā rājavittānāṃ hantā marṣayitāpi vā । sarve prayānti narakaṃ yathā brahmasvaharimaḥ ।। yajvanāṃ dharmaśīlānāṃ vairāgyanyastakarmaṇām ।
tulyamāpnoti bhūpālaḥ phalaṃ lokānupālanāt ।। iti devagurorvākyaṃ niśamya sa mahīpatiḥ । ciraṃ prajāḥ svadharmasthāḥ pālayitvā divaṃ yayau ।। kośedurgabalādīnāṃ kṣayaṃ śatruṣu nirdiśan ।
apramattaḥ sada rājā kuryātsaṃśrayamātmanaḥ ।। sarvato guptamantrāṇāṃ gūḍhapraṇidhicakṣuṣām । svasthaprakṛtisārāṇāṃ rājñāṃ lakṣmīranaśvarā ।। seveta dharmānadveṣastyajetprītimadāruṇaḥ ।
akarkaśo labhetārthānkāmī syādamadoddhataḥ ।। priyaṃ vadedadainyaśca vikrāntaścāvikatthanaḥ । dayādānamakāmaśca paṭuḥ syādakaṭurgirām ।। maittraḥ syādakhalāsaṅgī yudhyeta na tu bandhubhiḥ ।
viddhyeta śatrunnānāstraiḥ kuryātsarvamahiṃsakaḥ ।। jñānaṃ diśenna cāsatsu guṇāñślāgheta nātmanaḥ । haredarthānna sādhumbhaḥ saṃśrayeta na durjanam ।। daṇḍayennāvicāreṇa mantrasenna na saṃsadi ।
pūrayenna kadaryāṃstu viśvasenna ca vairiṣu ।। rakṣeddārānnahīrṣyāluḥ kalāvānsyādavañcakaḥ । bhajena kāntā nātyantamadyātsādhu na cāhitam ।। sevetārcyānna tu stabdho bhavecchiṣyo na māyayā ।
yajeta devānno dambhādicchedbhūtimaninditām ।। prītiṃ bhajennātinayo dakṣaścārabhaso bhavet । āśāṃ sṛjenna viphalāṃ vibhajeta na viṣṭhuram ।। prahartā stānna sarvatra hanyācchatrūnnaśeṣakṛt ।
prakupyenna tvadoṣebhyaḥ peśalaḥ syānna śatruṣu ।। etairyuktāḥ kila guṇaiḥ pārthivāḥ pṛthuvaṃśajāḥ । yaśaḥśubhrā prayāntyeva satataṃ hāratāṃ śriyaḥ ।। guṇaṣaṭriṃtraśakāḥ ।।
brāhmaṇāḥ sarvadā rājñā mūrdhni kāryā bubhūṣatā । brāhmeṇa tejasā yuktaṃ balaṃ kṣātraṃ hi duḥsaham ।। aiḍena bhūbhujā pṛṣṭaḥ purā provāca mārutaḥ । brāhmaṇānāmiyaṃ pṛthvī dhanaṃ vā jātu rakṣitam ।।
anivedya mahīṃ tasmādviprebhyaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ । svayamapyarjitaṃ vīro na kāmādbhoktumarhati ।। purodhasā brāhmaṇena saṃyuktaḥ śreyasāṃ nṛpaḥ । jetā bhavati śatrūṇāṃ sarvalokābhayaṃkaraḥ ।।
mucukundaḥ purā rājā vijitya sakalā diśaḥ । yayau vayasyaṃ rudrasya kuberaṃ jetumojasā ।। tataḥ pravṛtte samare guhyakā balavattarāḥ । pṛthunā mucukundasya tejasā ca kṣayaṃ yayuḥ ।
kṣaṇādalakṣyamantrasya vīrāste yakṣarākṣasāḥ ।। tataḥ prāptāḥ kubereṇa dattāṃ vasumatīṃ nṛpaḥ । tyaktvā parākrameṇaiva sa jagrāha balotkaṭaḥ ।। iti rājabalaṃ brahmabālānuprāṇitaṃ sadā ।
abhagnapraṇayāṃ dhatte trailokyavijayaśriyam ।। mucukundopākhyānam ।। brāhmaṇānpurataḥ kṛtvā prajā dharmeṇa pālayet । caturbhāgaharo rājā prajānāṃ puṇyapāpayoḥ ।।
tasya saṃvṛtamantrasya prajākāryāṇi paśyataḥ । vadānyasyānṛśaṃsasya kvaciddharmo na lupyate ।। viprāḥ pūjyāḥ sadā rājñā yathoktācāravartinaḥ । śūdravatkrūrakarmārhā daṇḍyāstvācāravarjitāḥ ।।
purā kekayabhūpālo gṛhīto rakṣasā vane । āśvāsayannijaṃ ceto jagāda dhṛtisāgaraḥ । na bhetavyaṃ tvayā citta rāṣṭre me nāsti viplavaḥ ।। nāyajvā na vikarmastho na pāpī na kulacyutaḥ ।
vidyate nagare kaścitkṣattradharme sthitasya me ।। iti bruvāṇaṃ nṛpatiṃ sa tatyāja niśācaraḥ । satyaśīlāḥ svadharmasthā labhante na parābhavam ।। viśvasen ca sarvatra na ca śaṅketa pārthivaḥ ।
viśvāsī cātiśaṅkī ca sarvathā vipadāṃ padam ।। āpteṣvapi na viśvāsaḥ kartavyaḥ kila bhūbhujā । na śarīrāṇi cetāṃsi sthirāṇi na hi dehinām ।। tasmātkośaśca mantraśca rakṣaṇīyaḥ prayatnataḥ ।
kāle kāle svayaṃ rājñā draṣṭavyaścāpramādinā ।। purā babhāṣe bhagavānnāradaṃ garuḍadhvajaḥ । vṛṣṇīnāmāhnikaṃ rājñāṃ cintābharamahaṃ sahe ।। guṇavikramasaṃpannāḥ sābhimānā matā na me ।
na śṛṇvanti na manyante girā māṃ vyathayanniva ।। etacchrutvā suramuniḥ keśavaṃ pratyabhāṣata । satvasārā vahantyeva gaṇakāryaṃ mahāśayāḥ ।। dānena kṣamayā śaktyā mārdavenārjavena ca ।
vaśe tiṣṭhanti dhīrāṇāṃ guṇabaddhā mahāguṇāḥ ।। ārjavaṃ na tu kośeṣu praśaṃsantyarthadarśinaḥ । śrutvaitannāradenoktaṃ tatheti harirabhyadhāt ।। harināradasaṃvādaḥ ।।
sarvātmanā viśuddheṣu saciveṣu nareśvaraḥ । cāraiḥ sadā tadācāraṃ jānankāryāṇi nikṣipet ।। kośādhyakṣaḥ svayaṃ rājā parirakṣyaḥ śuciḥ sadā । amātyā na sahante taṃ goptāraṃ kośahāriṇaḥ ।।
kosalādhipateḥ pūrvaṃ nagare kṣemadarśinaḥ । muniḥ kālakavṛkṣe yo yadṛcchābhyāgato avasat ।। pañjare kākamādāya sā rājā sarvapakṣiṇām । saṃcaranbubudhe sarvaṃ svavṛttaṃ rājajīvinām ।।
mantraśrāvamakāryaṃ ca kośalopaṃ ca mantriṇām । sa nivedya sadā rājñe pratyakṣaṃ samadarśayat ।। te sarve kaṇṭakaṃ matvā saṃhatya nṛpajīvinaḥ । suptaṃ taṃ vāyasaṃ rātrau jaghnurbāṇena nirjane ।।
kākaṃ nihatamālokya nṛpametyābravīnmuniḥ । svasti gacchāmi bhūpāla bhayāttvadanuvīvinām ।। sa tairme nihataḥ kākaḥ prāha yo māṃ bhava dvitam । kāko nipatito daivānmadarthaṃ preritaḥ śaraḥ ।
vibhedya pātayāmātyānityuktvā virarāma saḥ ।। rājāpi tadgirā kāle śoṣayitvā krameṇa tān । dānena bhedayitvā ca cakre niṣkaṇṭakāṃ śriyam ।। kākapañjarikā ।।
tasmātkramāgataṃ kuryāddraṣṭāraṃ nṛpatirhitam । bhavanti yadbhayātsarve kāyasthā bhinnasaṃhatāḥ ।। dāsādhipaśatasyaiko bhaveduparicintakaḥ । tatsahasrasya cādhyakṣaḥ sarvaṃ rājño nivedayet ।।
ghoṣaṃ grāmaṃ puraṃ rāṣṭraṃ bhakṣayantyadhikāriṇaḥ । kriyante yadi na prājñauruparyupari cintakāḥ । malopadānenārhāśca tīvrapākānivāriṇaḥ ।। śītkārakamalotkāraviparyastalipikramaiḥ ।
ka eṣāṃ bhṛtabhastrāṇāṃ cauryasyodbhāsane kṣamaḥ ।। teṣāṃ luṇṭhakavṛttīnāṃ jṛmbhārambhamṛjā juṣām । nagarāṇyeva culakaṃ galagartagaladgirām ।। tairghaṭyamānāṃ pṛthivīṃ rakṣedvetālaceṣṭitaiḥ ।
yeṣāṃ narakapākograparyante viṣamā sthitiḥ ।। yauvanāśvaṃ narapatiṃ prāgutathyo avadanmuniḥ । pṛthivīpālane rājankuru kaṇṭhakaśodhanam ।। anāthāndurbalānrakṣetkṛpaṇāṃścānulepayet ।
rājñāṃ hi kṛpaṇākrandairmūlānnaśyanti saṃpadaḥ ।। artho apyanarthatāṃ yāti bhūbhujāṃ janapīḍanāt । janāpavādaparaśuṃ sahate śrīlatā katham ।। vadānyaḥ sabhyavānvīraḥ kṛtajñaḥ satyavākpaṭuḥ ।
abhijāto bhavatyeva prajānāṃ sukṛtairnṛpaḥ ।। utathyeneti kathite māṃdhātā pṛthivīpatiḥ । tathā śaśāsa yaśasā yathā jīvanniva sthitaḥ ।। utathyagītāḥ ।।
uvāca kosalādhīśaṃ vāmadevaḥ purā muniḥ । dharmalopena bhūpānāṃ kṣīyante sahasā śriyaḥ ।। suhṛdbhiḥ praṇayakrītairmānakrītairmanīṣibhiḥ । dhanakrītaistathā bhṛtyairdhāryate śrīrmahībhujā ।।
śṛṇoti karuṇākrandaṃ śrutvā ca trāyate bhayat । nāvicārya sṛjeddaṇḍaṃ yaḥ sa sarvapriyo nṛpaḥ ।। nātaḥ parataraṃ kiṃcidrājñaḥ kilbiṣakāraṇam । prajā viraktatāṃ yānti yatkubharturivābalāḥ ।।
ityuktaṃ vāmadevena śrutvā sa vasudhādhipaḥ । vartamānaḥ svadharmeṇa prajānāmabhavatpriyaḥ ।। vāmadevagītāḥ ।। viṣamasthairasaṃnaddhaiḥ kṣīṇasainyairbhayārditaiḥ ।
na yudhyate kṣatriyo yaḥ sa dharmavijayī nṛpaḥ ।। tathā manye na śocyaḥ śvā mṛto viṇmūtrakardame । nihataḥ svajanasyāgre kṣatriyaḥ śayane yathā ।। parairvidārite sainye hate bhṛtyajane puraḥ ।
ye svayaṃ kṣemiṇo yānti dhiktānkṣatriyapāṃsanān ।। yasya pṛṣṭhaṃ na paśyanti yudhyamānasya śatravaḥ । sa hataḥ svargamāsādya śakreṇa spardhate nṛpaḥ ।। vijigīṣamāṇavṛttam ।।
ambarīṣaḥ purā rājā yajvā prāpya surālayam । sudevākhyaṃ camūnāthaṃ dadarśābhyadhikaṃ śriyā ।। uparyupari gacchantaṃ sarveṣāṃ puṇyaśālinām । taṃ dṛṣṭvā vismitaḥ śakraṃ paprāccha sa mahīpatiḥ ।।
yathādharmaṃ yathāśāstraṃ pālayitvā vasuṃdharām । iṣṭvā datvā ca taptvā ca prāpto ahaṃ tvatpurīmimām ।। mama senāpatirayaṃ sudevaḥ kena karmaṇā । prabhābhirabhibhūyāsmānuccaiḥ sūrya iva sthitaḥ ।।
iti rājñā surapatiḥ pṛṣṭastaṃ pratyabhāṣata । śṛṇu yenādhiko rājaṃstvatto ayaṃ pṛtanāpatiḥ ।। śastrānale raṇamakhe rudhirājye dhanuḥsrave । kabandhayūpe kṛtinā hutānena nijā tanuḥ ।।
so ayaṃ virājate vīrastejasā kṛtamaṇḍalaḥ । niṣkampaḥ samare kṛttasrastānāmabhayapradaḥ ।। śrutvaitadvismito rājā praśaṃsanvīravikramān । vismitaśca prahṛṣṭaśca manasā tamapūjayat ।।
śakrāmbarīṣasaṃvādaḥ ।। pṛṣṭaḥ purā surendreṇa rājanītiṃ bṛhaspatiḥ । uvāca śrīryathā rājñāṃ na karoti taḍidbhramam ।। vacasā madhureṇaiva kuryānmūlakṣayaṃ ripoḥ ।
ghoreṇa kalahenāpto jaghanyo hi jayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। saṃdehāyoddhṛtaṃ śastraṃ vāgyuddhaṃ kaṇṭhaśoṣaṇam । śatruṃ hanyātpriyālāpaiḥ kuraṅgamiva lubdhakaḥ ।। praṇameddeśakālajño balinaṃ ripumudyatam ।
tamevāpacite kāle hanyādeṣa nayakramaḥ ।। sāmnā seveta balinaṃ lubdhaṃ dānena sādhayet । bhedena kupitāmātyaṃ hīnaṃ daṇḍena pātayet ।। pramādinaṃ sahānīkaṃ kośadurgabalocitam ।
sarvopāyavihīnaṃ ca tūṣṇīṃ daṇḍena yojayet ।। sadā vibudhyeta nijānviraktānanujīvinaḥ । ātmanastāṃśca gūheta cchidraṃ yaccintayedareḥ ।। na bhāṣate vepate ca lakṣitaḥ kṣmāṃ nirīkṣate ।
na catuṣpatidānena viraktahṛdayo janaḥ ।। guruṇā kathitaṃ śrīmānniśamyaitatpuraṃdaraḥ । ātmaguptaḥ parānveṣī babhūvāvahitaḥ sadā ।। indrabṛhaspatisaṃvādaḥ ।।
daivādavāpto vipadaṃ na śocedvasudhādhipaḥ । anirvedena labhyante hāritā api saṃpadaḥ ।। muniḥ kālakavṛkṣīyaḥ kṣmābhujā kṣemadarśinā । vibhraṣṭena purā pṛṣṭo jagāda nayakovidaḥ ।।
vidyudvilāsataralāḥ surāṇāmapi saṃpadaḥ । rājanna nityamāyuśca yatkṛte śriyamīhase ।। tathāpi yadi te vāñchā sve rājye śatruṇā hate । gatvā tameva sevasva maunaṃ kṛtvā kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।
tāvacca sevako bhūtvā sarvathā vyasanālasam । yāvatkośe ca mitre ca śanakairupacīyase ।। praviśya ca manaḥ prītyā priyavādī yathā tathā । protsāhānāmakāryeṣu kurvīthā dusteraṣvareḥ ।।
tatastaṃ saṃśayāpannaṃ drutakośaṃ pramādinam । taistairupāyairdravyairvā kurvīthāḥ kṣaṇasādhanam ।। ityukte muninā rājā kutsitācārakūṇitaḥ । mānī naitatkaromīti jagādābhijanojjvalaḥ ।।
tasya satyavato bhāvamupalabhya munistataḥ । dūto bhūtvā svayaṃ saṃdhau tasya śatrumayo ajayat ।। saṃdhāya munivākyena vaidehaḥ kṣemadarśinā । vitatāra sutāṃ tasmai vibhavaṃ ca yathocitam ।।
kālakavṛkṣīyam ।। pālayetsvagaṇaṃ rājā pareṣāṃ bhedayedgaṇam । samyagvṛttena satyena vartante hi gaṇāḥ sadā ।। gaṇairvijayate rājā cintitaiḥ svabhṛtaistathā ।
upekṣitaiḥ saṃhataiśca tairevāśu vipadyate ।। praśāmyati bahiḥ kopo rājñāṃ sāmādibhiḥ kṣaṇāt । gūḍhastu veśmanīvāgnirnāntaḥ kopo gaṇodbhavaḥ ।। gaṇavṛttam ।।
daivataṃ pitaro yasya dharmo yasya prajāhitam । samyagdaṇḍo vrataṃ yasya sa rājā yajvanāṃ varaḥ ।। na satyaṃ kevalaṃ satyamanṛtaṃ na tathānṛtam । hitaṃ yatsarvalokasya tatsatyaṃ śeṣamanyathā ।।
anṛtenānṛtācāraścikitsyaḥ kila bhūbhujā । satyena satyaśīlaśca sevyo vibhavamicchatā ।। satyānṛtakam ।। yājinaḥ śuddhasaṃkalpāstyāginaḥ pātravarṣiṇaḥ ।
trātāraḥ sarvadharmāṇaṃ kartāraḥ puṇyakarmaṇām ।। śrotāraḥ sādhuvacasāṃ bhettāro dhanahāriṇām । taranti ghoradurgāṇi paratreha ca bhūmipāḥ ।। sadācārāstapoyuktāḥ praśāntāḥ satyavādinaḥ ।
saṃtaranti ca durgāṇi nārāyaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ।। durgātitaraṇam ।। asaumyāḥ saumyacaritā mṛdavaḥ krūrakāriṇaḥ । bhavanti puruṣā loke tāṃśca budhyeta bhūmipaḥ ।।
purā babhūva bhūpālaḥ prerakaḥ pūrikāpatiḥ । dārumaḥ puruṣaḥ kṣudraḥ piśitāśanaceṣṭitaḥ ।। kālena pañcatāṃ yātaḥ sa ca prāptaḥ śṛgālatām । janmāntarakṛtaiḥ puṇyairjātaṃ sasmāra duḥkhitaḥ ।।
āpannaḥ kutsitaṃ sargaṃ nirvedācchātamānasaḥ । parairapyāhṛtaṃ māṃsaṃ nādade phalabhojanaḥcha ।। śmaśānanilayaṃ kopāttaṃ vilokya śucivratam । ūtcurgomāyavaḥ sarve nindantastadviceṣṭitam ।।
vasatāpi śmaśāne asminhāritaṃ jaḍabuddhinā । tvayā mūḍhavratenedaṃ svādu māṃsarasāyanam ।। viparītamidaṃ sarvaṃ dunoti hṛdayaṃ satām । asminpitṛvane ghore śṛgālo yadamāṃsabhuk ।।
bhuṅkṣveti tairabhihitaḥ so avadadvimalāśayaḥ । na śīlakāraṇaṃ jātirnāśramaḥ puṇyakāraṇam ।। kimāśrame prāṇivadhaḥ pātakaṃ na pracakṣate । manaḥ śuddhikṛtaṃ sarvaṃ pramāṇaṃ karma dehinām ।।
iti bruvāṇaṃ taṃ sarve vijñāya dṛḍhaniścayam । nocuḥ kiṃcidamarśena kiṃtvatapyanta kevalam ।। tataḥ kadācittadvṛttaṃ śrutvā vyāghro abhipatya tam । uvāca mama sācivyaṃ śuddhātmā bhajatāṃ bhavān ।।
gomāyuratha tacchrutvā babhāṣe vinayānataḥ । svācchandyamamṛtaṃ tyaktvā kaḥ sevāṃ vikaṭāṃ śrayet ।। saṃtoṣadraviṇaṃ tyaktvā nirāyāsamanaśvaram । abhyarthayeta kaḥ sevāṃ daivyātaṅkakalaṅkitām ।।
athavā yadi nirbandhāttatkaromi bhavadvacaḥ । mayaivekena bhṛtyena bhavitavyaṃ sadā tvayā ।। tvadekasaṃśrayaṃ bhaktyā na ca saṃghātavāsinam । vināśayanti piśunā na yathā māṃ tathā kṛthāḥ ।।
evamuktvā śamamayaṃ niṣkāmaḥ pūjyagaurāvat । tatheti vādinastasya vyāghrasyāmātyatāṃ yayau ।। tamāśvāsya bhuvaṃ nītamekaṃ sarvādhipaṃ kṛtam । vyāghreṇa vīkṣya duḥkhābdhau petustadanujīvinaḥ ।।
vyāghrāya kalpitaṃ māṃsaṃ ninyurgomāyuketanam । kva māṃsamiti te pṛṣṭā vyāghreṇa kṣudrakāriṇaḥ । ūcuścauryeṇa tannītaṃ śucinā tava mantriṇā ।। mithyācāraṃ viditvā taṃ dṛṣṭvā māṃsaṃ ca tadgṛhe ।
krodhāndho hantukāmastaṃ vyāghraḥ saṃrambhamāyayau ।। tamabhyetyābravīnmātā vyāghrī piśunaśaṅkitā । śuddhāya tasmai bhṛtyāya vimohātputra mā krudhaḥ ।। bahavaḥ saṃhatā dhūrtāḥ saṃmataṃ sacivaṃ navam ।
mithyādoṣeṇa limpanti nirdeṣaṃ kṣudrapaṇḍitāḥ ।। svarūpaṃ vikṛto dveṣṭi śūraṃ bhūrurbudhaṃ jaḍaḥ । kulīnaṃ hīnajanmā ca duḥśīlā ca pativratām ।। evaṃ vibodhito mātrā tattvamanviṣya cārataḥ ।
śuddhaṃ vijñāya taṃ vyāghraḥ prasādyasīdvilajjitaḥ ।। tamabravīcchṛgālo atha svasti gacchāmyahaṃ vibho । vimānitastvayā vastuṃ notsahe tyaktasaṃvidā ।। gumavāniti saṃsatsu yaḥ stutaḥ sādhubhiḥ purā ।
satyapratijñairdeṣe api na sa vācyo anyathā punaḥ ।। bhinna tathāsminsaṃśleṣe punaḥ prītiḥ sudurlabhā । ityuktvā vyāghramāmantrya gomāyustapase yayau ।। sa kālena nirāhāraḥ śāntasaṃsāravāsanaḥ ।
vane kalevaraṃ tyaktvā tridivaṃ prayayau kṛtī ।। vyāghragomāyusaṃvādaḥ ।। āsthāya vaitasīṃ vṛttiṃ deśakālau samīkṣya ye । na santi tiṣṭhantyuccairvā na te yānti parābhavam ।।
sāgaraḥ saritaḥ sarvāḥ purā papraccha kautukāt । yuṣmatpravāheṣvakhilānpaśyāmyunmūlitāndrumān ।। ete viśanti māṃ vṛkṣā hṛtā kūlaṃkaṣairjalaiḥ । vetasaṃ na tu paśyāmi kasmādatra taṭodbhavam ।।
samudreṇeti pṛṣṭhāsu nadīṣu prāha jāhnavī । hriyamāṇaḥ sadāmbhobhirvinamatyeva vetasaḥ ।। hantuṃ na śakyāste vṛkṣā mahaughairvinamanti ye । truṭyanti trāsādevānye drumā mūrkhā ivoddhatāḥ ।।
etadgāṅgaṃ vacaḥ śrutvā tathetyūce saritpatiḥ । mene ca vaitasīṃ vṛttiṃ śreyase deśakālayoḥ ।। saritsāgarasaṃvādaḥ ।। rājñāṃ dhanaṃ nijā buddhirdākṣyaṃ cotsāhaśālinām ।
alasā buddhihīnāśca sarvathā vipadāṃ padam ।। uṣṭraḥ pareṇa tapasā prajāpativarātpurā । ālasyopahato grīvāmavāpa śatayojanīm ।। āsane copaviṣṭo atha tayā pīluvaneṣu saḥ ।
prāṇayātrāṃ sadā cakre manyamāno mahatsukham ।। durdinābhihate kāle kadācittasya jambukaiḥ । kṣutkṣāmairbhakṣitā grīvā dīrghā sā maṇḍalīkṛtā ।। uṣṭragrīvikam ।।
kulīnānviditācārānrājā karmasu yojayet । pade mahati vinyastāḥ saṃśayāyaiva durjanāḥ ।। uvāsa śvā kṛpāpātramāśrame kasyacinmuneḥ । sa dṛṣṭvā dvīpinaṃ ghoraṃ kadācidavadadbhayāt ।
bhagavanneṣa māṃ dvīpī kṣudhito hantumāgataḥ ।। pāhi pāhiti tenoktaḥ sa muniḥ karuṇānidhiḥ । etattulyo bhavetyuktvā taṃ cakre dvīpivigraham ।। so api śvā dvīpitāṃ prāptastrasto vyāghrātpunarmunim ।
trāyasvetyabhidhāyaiva vyāghrātāṃ tadgirā yayau ।। so api mattagajādbhītaḥ kālena madamantharāt । muninā kalpitāṃ prītyā prāptau mattagajendratām ।। so api pañcānanādbhītaḥ karālāttālakesarāt ।
yātastacchāsanādeva sahasā mṛgarājatām ।। aṣṭapādaṃ mahādaṃṣṭraṃ dṛṣṭvā śarabhamāgatam । sa viṣaṇṇo munigirā babhūva śarabhaḥ kṣaṇāt ।। kālena śarabhākāraḥ sarvaprāṇibhayaṃkaraḥ ।
sa jātadarpaḥ sahasā taṃ muniṃ hantumudyayau ।। apadhvastastatastena muninā huṃkṛtena saḥ । sa babhūva punardīnaḥ kṣaṇādaśucivigrahaḥ ।। ityavijñātaśīlebhyo hīnebhyo vitarañśriyam ।
kulācāramanālocya rājā patati saṃśaye ।। śvaṛṣisaṃvādaḥ ।। nayamevāṃvidhaṃ jñātvā rājadaṇḍena gāmimām । sarvakāmadughāṃ vīraḥ pālayenna tu pīḍayet ।।
vasuhomo aṅganṛpatirhimavicchikhare purā । avadadyauvanāśvena pṛṣṭo daṇḍasya saṃbhavam ।। dhṛto varśasahasraṃ prāṅbhūrdhnā garbhaḥ prājāsṛjā । kṣutena sahaso atsṛṣṭaḥ sa śrīmānkṣupa ityabhūt ।।
atrāntare jagatsarvamāśāsanamayantraṇam । nirmaryādaṃ vilokyedaṃ vyākulo abhūtprajāpatiḥ ।। athāsya vacasā rudraḥ prayayau daṇḍatāṃ svayam । daṃṣṭrī caturbhujo dīptaḥ śyāmoṣṭhacaraṇo jaṭī ।।
devastaṃ viṣṇave prādādviṣṇuraṅgirase dadau । so api śakramarīcibhyāṃ marīcirbhṛgave tataḥ ।। sa munibhyo dadau te api dikpatibhyo kṣupāya te । kṣupaśca manave prādāddaṇḍaṃ dharmasya guptaye ।।
tasminsamyakpraṇihite rakṣāyai pūtatejasi । labhante śāśvataṃ vīrā yaśaḥ svargaṃ ca bhūmipāḥ ।। ityuktamaṅgarājena māṃdhātā pṛthivīpatiḥ । niśamyotphullanayanaḥ sādaraṃ tamapūjayat ।।
vasuhomopākhyānam ।। kāmalobhodbhavaṃ pāpaṃ rājño brāhmamasevayā । punaścākaraṇāddānātkīrtanācca vinaśyati ।। trayī trātā tato dharmaṃ bhajate tyaktakilviṣaḥ ।
ityariṣṭena pṛṣṭaḥ prāṅbhuniḥ kāmardako abravīt ।। kāmandāriṣṭasaṃvādaḥ ।। śīlamābharaṇaṃ rājñāṃ saujanyaṃ viduṣāmiva । śīlena rājate lakṣmīrvasanteneva mañjarī ।।
rājasūye śriyaṃ dṛṣṭvā tava dveṣavipākulaḥ । duryodhanaḥ purā pitre dyūte kāmaṃ nyavedayat ।। dhṛtarāṣṭrastamavadatputra mā bhava viplutaḥ । pravartantāṃ tavāpyante yajñā vipulasaṃpadaḥ ।।
śīlavānprāpsyasi sadā lakṣmīṃ pāṇḍusutādhikaḥ । na hi śīlavataḥ kiṃcidvidyate bhuvi durlabham ।। śīlaṃ rājñāṃ diśāṃ canandrastāruṇyaṃ bahariṇīdṛśām । madhumāsaśca vṛkṣāṇāṃ manohāryaṃ vibhūṣaṇam ।।
videśeṣu dhanaṃ vidyā vyasaneṣu dhanaṃ matiḥ । paraloke dhanaṃ dharmaḥ śīlaṃ tu nikhilaṃ dhanam ।। śīlavittocitaṃ śakraḥ pradīptavibhavaṃ purā । bṛhaspatipuraḥ prāyātprahlādaṃ brāhmaṇākṛtiḥ ।।
śreyo vadeti vinayāddaityendrastena śiṣyavat । pṛṣṭo babhāṣe kālena prājākāryaikasaktadhīḥ ।। trailokyarājyaṃ saṃprāptaṃ mayā śīlavatā sadā । śṛṇoti vidyā viduṣāṃ kavīnāṃ saṃśaye vacaḥ ।।
anirṇītamasaṃspṛṣṭamanākhyātamacintitam । sahasā na bhajetkiṃcidapi svādu vicāradhīḥ ।। etadeva hitaṃ vipra sarveṣāmapi dehinām । varaṃ gṛhāṇa tuṣṭo ahaṃ tava praṇayasevayā ।।
ityukto dānavendreṇa tuṣṭaḥ provāca vṛtrahā । sarvaṃ dehi nijaṃ mahyāṃ śīlaṃ śīlavatāṃ vara ।। śrutvaitatsatyavāgdaityo dadānīti tamabravīt । śakro api tadgirā prāpya prayayau dvijaveśabhṛt ।।
gate tasminmahotsāhe chāyārūpo varākṛtiḥ । prahlādavigrahāttūrṇaṃ niryayau puruṣo bahiḥ ।। ko asīti pṛṣṭastenātha so avadaddaityabhūpatim । vitīrṇo adya tvayā kāmādahaṃ śīlābhidho guṇaḥ ।।
uktveti śakraṃ yāte asminnaparo niragāttataḥ । so api pṛṣṭo avadaddaityaṃ dharmo ahaṃ śīlamārgagaḥ ।। viniḥsṛtastṛtīyo api satyamaramītyuvāca tām । avadadvittamasmīti caturtho apyatha nirgataḥ ।
ahaṃ balamiti kṣipraṃ niryātaḥ pañcamo avadat ।। tataḥ kamalaparyaṅkasthitā kamalalocanā । prahlādavakrānnirgatya jagāda kamalā svayam ।। vrajāmyahaṃ hasasrākṣaṃ yaste śiṣyo abhavaddvijaḥ ।
tasmai tvayā vitīrṇaṃ hi śīlaṃ śīlavibhūṣaṇa ।। śīlādanugato dharmaḥ satyaṃ tadanuyāyi ca । yātaṃ vittaṃ ca tanmūlaṃ balaṃ caitannibandhanam ।। eteṣu surarājasya praviṣṭeṣu kramādvapuḥ ।
śīlāśrayāṃ śriyaṃ viddhi māmapi prasthitāṃ vibho ।। ityuktvā śakrasadanaṃ yayau lakṣmīrvihāya tam । evaṃ śīlodbhavāḥ sarvā duryodhanavibhūtayaḥ ।। ityukto apyāmbikeyena na śaśāma suyodhanaḥ ।
pūjyeṣu vimukhā mohātsarvathā hi mumūrṣavaḥ ।। śīlavarṇanam ।। etatpitāmahenoktaṃ śrutvā sarvaṃ nṛpocitam । smṛtvā duryodhanakathāṃ niḥśvasyovāca dharmajaḥ ।।
āśā mamābhūdvipulā satataṃ dhṛtarāṣṭraje । yathā vananivṛtteṣu sā māsmāsu vidhāsyati ।। sarvathā yuddharucinā pratyākhyāte janārdane । āśā viphalatāṃ nītā sā tena mama saṃvṛtā ।।
tasmādvaipulyamāyātāstadbhaṅge duḥsahāḥ śucaḥ । nivartante kathaṃ nāma kathyatāṃ me pitāmaha ।। pṛṣṭo yudhiṣṭhireṇeti punaḥ śāntanavo abravīt । āśā sumahatī pārtha daśā jīvitahāriṇī ।।
haihayo rājaputraḥ prāksumitro nāma kānane । javādanusasāraikaṃ kuraṅgaṃ vegavattaram ।। sameṣu tarukuñjeṣu śvabhreṣu viṣameṣu ca । mṛgānusārī sucirātsa dhanvī klamamāyayau ।।
tatastapovanaṃ prāpya dṛṣṭanaṣṭe mṛge punaḥ । āśāvināśasaṃtapto munīnāmaviśatsabhām ।। sa tānpraṇamya papraccha kaṣṭāmāśāṃ mahattamām । munistaṃ vṛṣabho nāma babhāṣe sasmitānanaḥ ।
rājaputra kṛśāmāśāṃ jahi duḥkhānubandhinīm ।। bhūridyumnaḥ purā rājā vīradyumnābhidhaṃ sutām । vicinvanhṛtamaśvena badaryāśramamāyayau ।। tatastapovanaṃ prāpya dṛṣṭanaṣṭe mṛge punaḥ ।
āśāvināśasaṃtapto munīnāmaviśatsabhām ।। sa tānpraṇamya papraccha kaṣṭāmāśāṃ mahattamām । munistaṃ vṛṣabho nāma babhāṣe sa smitānanaḥ ।। rājaputra kṛśāmāśāṃ jahi duḥkhānubandhinīm ।
bhūridyumnaḥ purā rājā vīradyumnābhidhaṃ sutam ।। tanurnāma munistatra prāṃśuḥ kṛśatarākṛtiḥ । duḥkhāntenāvadatpṛṣṭo mā rājanviklavo bhava ।। na vidyate janaḥ kaścidāśayā yo na hīyate ।
na ca paśyāmi taṃ loke yācakaṃ yo abhimanyate ।। kṛtaghneṣu nṛśaṃseṣu kuṭileṣvalaseṣu ca । āśādaurvalyamāyānti śaradīvālpanimnagāḥ ।। dhiktāṃ kṛśatarāmāśāṃ kāyaśoṣavidhāyinīm ।
pratiśrutamasaṃprāpya hṛdayātparivartate ।। putre mṛte vā naṣṭe vā piturekātmajasya vā । āśā dahati gātrāṇi sā kṛśāpi mahīyasī ।। vṛddhānāṃ putralābheṣu nityamāśā bhavanti yāḥ ।
sthāvire jīrṇakāyānāṃ tāḥ kṛśā api duḥsahāḥ ।। bhrāmayatyāptamātraiva śoṣayatyāyatī kṛśā । hanti magnā jaṭilyeva dhigāśāṃ mṛtyudāyinīm ।। ityuktvā tanayaṃ rājñe sa munirdivyalocanaḥ ।
adarśayatsvayaṃ cābhūtprakaṭaṃ dharmavigrahaḥ ।। ṛṣabhagītāḥ ।। āśāpāśānparityajya yogīva vijitendriyaḥ । pāturmahasi kaunteya pṛthvīṃ pṛthurivāparaḥ ।।
kośamūlaṃ balaṃ rājñāṃ tasminkṣīṇe yathā tathā । abrāhmaṇadhanaiḥ kāryāttadvṛddhirdharmasaṃpade ।। rājadharmāḥ ।। vaktāraṃ sarvadharmāṇāṃ siddhasindhusutaṃ nṛpaḥ ।
kṣīṇakośasahāyānāṃ vṛttiṃ papraccha bhūbhujām ।। balibhirvijito rājā bhinnamantro nirāśrayaḥ । nirutsāhatayā bhraṣṭaḥ kiṃ śreyaḥ saṃśrayediti ।। bhīṣmo avadannarapatiḥ kṣīṇaḥ saṃdhāya vairibhiḥ ।
śanaiḥ kośabalādīnāṃ yatnātkuryādvivardhanam ।। tūrṇaṃ varteta sāmnā vā tyaktātmā vāraṇaṃ vrajet । ubhayorantare tiṣṭhandīrghasūtro vinaśyati ।। vipadānāṃ mūlaghātī yo ayaṃ kośāparikṣayaḥ ।
utthānopahatāstena prabhavanti na tāḥ kila ।। gṛdhrāḥ prayāntyeva śavaṃ dagdhamaṅgārakāṣṭhakam । na tu dāridryasaṃspaṣṭaṃ kaścitspṛśati pūruṣam ।। api klinnasirājālaṃ pūtiryuṣitaṃ śavam ।
na tathā varjayantyārāddhanahīnaṃ yathā janam ।। viluptavibhavodbhrāntacetasāṃ viṣame pade । anaśvaramanākramyaṃ maryādā mānināṃ dhanam ।। apyanutsṛṣṭamaryādo dasyuḥ syānna viśṛṅkhalaḥ ।
maryādā saṃpadāṃ dhāma mūḍhatā vipadāmiva ।। purā dasyupatirvīraḥ kopavyo gurupūjakaḥ । aparityaktamaryādaḥ prāpa siddhimanuttamām ।। rakṣitā nyastaśastrāṇāṃ dvijānāṃ yoṣitāṃ tathā ।
niḥśeṣadānavasakhaḥ sa lebhe vipulaṃ yaśaḥ ।। kopavyacaritam ।। na tajjagati nāmāsti yadanākramyamāpadām । śarīrarakṣā prathamaṃ tāsāṃ buddhiśca bheṣajam ।।
prāptajño dīrghadarśī ca dīrghasūkṣatraśca sānugāḥ । bahuputrāḥ purā matsyā nyavasansalilāśaye ।। srāvyamāṇo jale tatra dhīrvaraistajjighṛkṣayā । dīrghadarśī parānūce gacchāmo mānasāntaram ।।
ityarthitau tena yadā tau vimohānna jagmatuḥ । dīrghadarśī tadā pūrvaṃ svayaṃ prāyātsaraḥ param ।। tataḥ srutajale dāśaiḥ kṛṣṭe matsyakadambake । lalambe kṛtakaṃ dhāmni prāptajño mṛtavatsvayam ।।
so aphālānakhilānmatsyānhatvā protānathāparān । jalāntare kṣālaṃnāya vikṣipurjālajīvinaḥ ।। nyasteṣu teṣu niḥśaṅkhairnadīṣvambhasi dhīvaraiḥ । alakṣito yayau tūrṇaṃ prāptajño dhīmatāṃ varaḥ ।।
ardhajīvastu vicalandīrghasūtro mahākṛtiḥ । vyapādyata niṣādena laguḍairjarjarīkṛtaḥ ।। dīrghadarśīyam ।। bahunāṃ gocaraṃ yāto vairiṇāṃ viṣame sthitaḥ ।
kuryādbalādhikaṃ tebhyo mitraṃ kiṃtvatiśaṅkitaḥ ।। nyagrodhamūlanilayaḥ pralayo mūṣikaḥ purāḥ । lomaśaṃ nāma mārjāraṃ jālabaddhaṃ vyalokayat ।। baddhe tasmingatāśaṅkaḥ sa jighraṃścapalānanaḥ ।
bhakṣyaṃ niśi cacārākhurvilikhannakharairmahīm ।। haritaṃ nāma so apaśyannakulaṃ lohitānanam । candrakākhyamulūkaṃ ca kūjantaṃ ghoralocanam ।। tau dṛṣṭvā balinau bhītaḥ saṃprāpte prāṇasaṃśaye ।
mūṣikaḥ kalayansarvā diśaḥ kṣaṇamacintayat ।। nakulolūkabhīto ahaṃ mārjāraṃ balināṃ varam । saṃśaye viṣamasthānāṃ saṃdhistrāṇaṃ hi śatruṇā ।। sa niścityeti tatpāśacchedāyodyatamānasaḥ ।
mārjāramavadannīlakācakācaralocanam ।। amitro mittratāṃ yāti mittramāyātyamitratām । kālena tasmācchetsyāmi pāśaṃ te mittratāṃ gataḥ ।। śrutvaitanmadhuraṃ hṛṣṭo mārjāraḥ suhṛdaṃ vyadhāt ।
gāḍhamaṅke pariṣvajya mūṣikaṃ vipadi sthitaḥ ।। taddṛṣṭvā nakulolūkau nirāśāvāśvabhakṣaṇe । babhūvaturbhugnamukhau balavatprītiśaṅkitau ।। śanaiḥ śanairmuṣiko atha ciccheda snāyubandhanam ।
taṃ tūrṇaṃ tūrṇamityūce mārjāraścirakāriṇam ।। svārthamuddiśya lambante ye kṣaṇaṃ prītitantubhiḥ । dhūrtāṃstānkāryaśeṣeṇa yāpayetkāryayācakān ।। etaddhyātvā dhiyaivākhurlubdhakāgamanāvanadhi ।
ekapāśāṃśaśeṣaṃ taṃ cakāra nayakovidaḥ ।। prātarghoratare prāpte caṇḍāle parighābhidhe । jālanikṣiptanayane saśastre pāśajīvini ।। pāśaśeṣaṃ cakartākhuśchitvā ca bilamāviśat ।
yāto vyādho nirāśaśca mārjāre vidrute drutam ।। tasmānmhābhayānmuktaḥ kālenābhyetya mūṣikam । antaḥsthitaṃ biladvārānmārjāraḥ praṇato avadat ।। ahaṃ sa te paraṃ mittramupakāravaśīkṛtaḥ ।
bhṛśamutkaṇṭhitāṃ prāptaḥ sakhe nirgamyatāmitaḥ ।। iti bruvāṇaṃ mārjāraṃ dṛṣṭvā bhakṣaṇadīkṣitam । śuklatīkṣṇādradaśanaṃ śmaśrusūcīcitānanam ।। jighrāntaṃ muṣikāmodamardhonmīlitalocanam ।
uccaikapādanibhṛtaṃ tamabhāṣata mūṣikaḥ ।। sauhārdenopayuktaḥ prāktava cāhaṃ bhāvaṃśca me । gamyatāṃ sa gataḥ kālo na bhūmirvañcaneṣvaham ।। yadbhavānmadhuraṃ vakti tanmahyaṃ nādya rocate ।
yācakaḥ kāryakālo asāvadhunā nāsti saṃgatam ।। nijaprayojanāpekṣāpeśalapriyabhāṣaṇaṇ । durbalaḥ krūramanasaṃ dhīraḥ dūrādevāryacetasam । na śreyo asti viruddho hi bhojyabhoktṛsamāgamaḥ ।।
kṛtajña bhavase mittraṃ dūrādevāryacetasam । na śreyo asti viruddho hi bhojyabhoktṛsamāgamaḥ ।। nirasya bahubhirvākyairmārjāramiti mūṣikaḥ । bilaṃ tatyājā kālena dṛṣṭaṃ dhūrtena śatruṇā ।।
mārjāramūṣikasaṃvādaḥ ।। evameṣa nayaḥ prājñairjñātavyaḥ śatrusaṃdhiṣu । na viśvasetpriyagirāṃ viśeṣeṇa kṛtāgasām ।। kāmpilye nagare pūrvaṃ brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ ।
uvāsa pūtanā nāma vihagī jīvajīvikā ।। sā rājabhavane jātavisrambhājījanatsutam । tatputratulyajanmā ca putro abhūttasya bhūbhujaḥ ।। vitīrya sāgaradvīpasaṃjātaṃ sā phaladvayam ।
svaputraṃ rājupatraṃ ca bālye api balinau vyadhāt ।। tataḥ kadācidvihagaṃ śiśuṃ rājasuto balī । ādāya kelisaṃsaktaṃ cakāra gatajīvitam ।। vilokya nihataṃ putraṃ samabhyetyātha pūtanā ।
tuṇḍena rājaputrasya kruddhā netre vyadārayat । pratikṛtya nikāreṇa duḥkhitā gantumudyayau ।। vrajantīṃ brahmadattastāṃ harmyādālokya saṃbhramāt । vidāritākṣaṃ putraṃ ca jagādācchādya vikriyām ।।
apakāre pratikṛte vairaṃ vaireṇa pātitam । kopaḥ sāmyādapakrānto mā gamaḥ putri pūtane ।। tacchrutvovāca vihagī nedānīmasti saṃgatam । kṛtapratikṛtaṃ vairamabhyāsāddviguṇaṃ bhavet ।।
śrutvā ca guruvṛddhebhyaḥ purāṇamapi vismṛtam । sahasā navatāṃ yāti vairaṃ koṭaravahnivat ।। kṛtāpakāre viśvāsaṃ mohādyo yāti bāliśaḥ । sa vismṛtātmā sahasā yāti kālavidheyatām ।।
gīteneva kuraṅgāṇamāmiṣeṇeva pakṣiṇām । baḍiśeneva matsyānāṃ viśvāsanavyathā nṛṇām ।। priyavādyairvibhinnānāṃ saṃśleṣaḥ kila durlabhaḥ । muktāphalānāṃ bhagnānāṃ jatuleśairna saṃdhayaḥ ।।
dhiktaṃ kudeśaḥ yatrātmā na śete aśāṅkitaḥ sukham । pravādaḥ kila satyo ayaṃ yadātmārthe mahīṃ tyajet ।। iti bruvāṇā sā rājñā prārthitāpi punaḥ punaḥ । aviśvāsabhayātprāyāttyaktvā praṇayagauravam ।।
brahmadattapūtanāsaṃvādaḥ ।। āpatkāle ghṛṇāṃ tyaktvā kṛtasneheṣu gauravaiḥ । pratikūleṣu varteta pratikūlataraṃ dhiyā ।। rājñā śatruntapākhyena vṛttiṃ nītiṃ ca bhūbhujām ।
kaṇiṅkanāmā nītijñaḥ purā pṛṣṭo abravīnmuniḥ ।। mūlacchedaṃ ripoḥ kuryādathavā na prakopayet । anyathāsau vināśāya pādaspṛṣṭa ivoragaḥ ।। janaṃ viśvasayedvācā śaucaṃ dambhena darśayet ।
pragāṇaiḥ śapathaiḥ śāstraiḥ śatruṃ seveta śambaraiḥ ।। atītaśāntaye snehai samaṃ jaḍamanāgataiḥ । pratyakṣairupapatraiśca piṇḍitaiḥ phalavarjitaiḥ ।। tūlavatsahasā kṣipraṃ jvaledavasare kvacit ।
mandapratāpo dhūmāṅko na bhaveddrumavahnivat ।। prayojanārthinaḥ kuryādāśābandhānsadā madā । na hi kaścitkṛte kārye kartāramanumanyate ।। lokāpavādādudvego mārdavaṃ cirakāritam ।
asaṃvṛttiḥ svamantre vā mūlacchedor'thasaṃpadām ।। prasupto badhiro andho vā kāle syātsvārthasiddhaye । prapātamadhuvattiṣṭeddurlabhaḥ sarvadehinām ।। dāruṇaḥ syānmukhe svādurguḍalipta ivopalaḥ ।
viśedantaśca śatrūṇāṃ madhudigdha iva kṣuraḥ ।। dīrghamāśāmiṣaṃ dātuṃ cintayejjñānasaṃgraham । āśāṃ nighnairnamittaiśca hetubhiśca tathā vadet ।। na yathā ratimāyāti saṃvatsaraśatairapi ।
atṛptijanakā prītirdadyātsvasyāntaraṃ nṛṇām ।। kākavatpariśaṅkena nāśayenmṛgamugdhatām । cārairbhavecca sarvajñaḥ praharedvyasane ripau ।। pūrvaṃ māyābhighātī syāddhataṃ śocetsvabandhuvat ।
na kuryānniṣphalaṃ vairaṃ na haredapyapuṣkalam ।। dantānāṃ śātanaṃ mithyā śuṣkāsthiparicarvaṇam । śṛṇavadvyādhivaccheṣaṃ na śatroḥ parivarjayet ।। api putraṃ svayaṃ hanyādarthavighnavidhāyinam ।
gṛdhravaddīrghadarśī syādbakavatkapaṭavrataḥ ।। śārdūlavanmahotsāhaḥ kuṭilaśca bhujaṅgavat । bhedanāya sadā kuryātpareṣāṃ paurasāntvanam ।। gaṇāṃścopajapetpūrvaṃ dhanairākṛṣya vallabhān ।
paṇḍitairvairamutpādya na niḥśaṅkaḥ sukhaṃ caret ।। etadbuddhvaiva nikhila nanu seveta sajjanam । suverarājaḥ śrutvaitadbhāradvājena bhāṣitam । kaṇiṅkakhyena muninā babhūva nayakovidaḥ ।।
kaṇiṅkopākhyānam ।। āpadaṃ kāladaurātmyāddevadoṣeṇa vā budhaḥ । saṃprāpto daivadiṣṭādvā dhiyā varteta saṃkaṭe ।। ayameva sadopāyo bhāvi kalyāṇasaṃpadām ।
trivargasādhanaṃ dehaṃ rakṣedāpatsu yadbudhaḥ ।। anāvṛṣṭihate kāle purā dvādaśavārṣike । kathāśeṣeṣu toyeṣu durbhikṣakṣapite jane ।। utsanne dharmasaṃtāne śavākīrṇe mahītale ।
tyaktvāgnidaivatāḥ sarve munayo luptasaṃyamāḥ ।। babhramurnaṣṭasaṃketā nirdagdhāśramakānanāḥ । viśvāmitro atha vicarannavāpa śvapacālayam ।। kṛttaprāṇivasāvisraṃ śuṣkamāṃsāsthibhālikam ।
āyāsaniyamāvāsaṃ śvacarmāstīrṇapakkaṇam ।। śoṇitāpūrṇapiṭharaṃ saramāsaṅgasaṃkulam । snāyupralambasaṃbādhaṃ kaṅkālaśakalākulam ।। kṣutkṣāmakukṣistatrāpi munirbhikṣāmayācata ।
arthamāno api sa yadā tato lobhena kiṃcana ।। tadā kṛcchrāṃ daśāṃ yātaḥ papāta bhuvi mūrchitaḥ । so acintayadaho kaṣṭamiyamāpadupasthitā ।। śvamāṃsaleśamathavā harāmi niśi cauravat ।
prāṇārthī sarvamādadyātsarvataḥ sthitiviplave ।। āpadi prāṇarakṣā hi dharmasya prathamāṅkuraḥ । etaccintayatastasya kṛṣṇarātriḥ pravartitā ।। śvapākavañcitānekakākapakṣairivāvṛtā ।
sa saktikāṃ snāyutattrīṃ lambamānāṃ vicintya saḥ ।। kuṭīdvāraṃ śanaiḥ prāpya sakampo hartumudyayau । antaḥ prasupto nirnidraḥ śleṣmavyālagnalocanaḥ ।। vṛddhaḥ śvajīvī provāca taṃ kāsoddhargharasvaraḥ ।
snāyurākṛṣyate kena nāsmi nidrāvaśaṃ gataḥ ।। eṣa śastreṇa sahasā hanyate yo atra lambate । viśvāmitro niśamyaitattamūce durbalasvaraḥ ।। kauśiko ahaṃ muniḥ prāṇarakṣāyai cauratāṃ gataḥ ।
alabdhabhaikṣaḥ kṣutkṣāmo harāmyenāṃ śvajāghanīm ।। adharmo nāturasyāsti ghoraṃ kṛcchraṃ gatasya ca । mūlaṃ ca jīvo dharmasya tasminnāpatsu rakṣyate ।। pravartante punaḥ sarvāḥ sadācārocitāḥ kriyāḥ ।
ityukto muninā vṛddhaḥ samutthāya jagāda saḥ ।। aho nu bhagavanprāṇalobhātpāpaṃ praśaṃsasi । yuṣmābhireva vihito bhakṣyābhakṣyeṣu nirṇayaḥ ।। sa kathaṃ jīvitabhraṃśabhayātpāpe pravartase ।
na vārayāmi te māṃsaṃ vitarāmi na te svayam ।। vaktāsi sarvadharmāṇāṃ mohānmā nirayaṃ gamaḥ । etatsa muninākarṇya jagāda praskhalanmuhuḥ ।। yasmiṃstapaśca satyaṃ ca svajñāna ca pratiṣṭhitam ।
śarīre rakṣite tasminsarvaṃ bhavati rakṣitam ।। abhakṣyaṃ bhakṣayitvāpi vimuktaḥ prāṇasaṃśayāt । vratatīrtheṣu puṇyena kṣapayiṣyāmi pātakam ।। ityuktvā tāṃ samādāya yayau tūrṇaṃ śvajāghanīm ।
asminnavasare meghā vavarṣuḥ sasyasaṃpadaḥ ।। ityevaṃ prāṇarakṣāyai munināpyatigarhite । śvamāṃse vihitā buddhistasmāttrāyeta jīvitam ।। viśvāmitraśvapacasaṃvādaḥ ।।
dharmasūnurniśamyaitadbhīṣmaṃ papraccha vismitaḥ । pitāmaha gatiṃ brūhi śaraṇāgatarakṣiṇām ।। etatpṛṣṭo nṛpatinā prāha śantanunandanaḥ । pṛṣṭaḥ pūrvaṃ jagādedaṃ mucukundena bhārgavaḥ ।।
vipule durdināyāse lubdhakaḥ kānane purā । śītasaṃpiṇḍito rātrau mūle suṣvāpa śākhinaḥ ।। skande viṭapinastasya kapotaḥ kṛtasaṃśrayaḥ । vāsarānte api nāyātāṃ smṛtvā bhāryāmatapyata ।।
vilalāpa sa saṃtaptaḥ priyāvirahakātaraḥ । kapotī tacca śuśrāva baddhā vyādhena pañjare ।। sā tamūce sukṛtino na prayānti viṣaṇṇatām । prathamaṃ sukṛtametaccharaṇāgatarakṣaṇam ।।
