lubdhako vṛkṣamūle asminsupto hyasmai yathocitam । pūjāṃ vidhatsva śītārtaḥ śaraṇaṃ hyeṣa vāñchati ।। prayasyā vacanaṃ śrutvā lubdhakaṃ vihago abravīt । bhadra madgṛhamāpto asi vitarāmi tavepsitam ।।
śītārditastadākarṇya lubdhakastamayācata । vahniṃ so api khagastūrṇaṃ mānināya divo antikam ।। tṛṇaparṇasusiddhe agnau jvalite lubdhakastataḥ । vinaṣṭaśītaḥ kṣutkṣāmastamayācata bhojanam ।।
māṃ bhakṣayeti kāruṇyānnigadya vihagaḥ svayam । viveśa vahniṃ tadaddṛṣṭvā vyādho apyanuśayaṃ yayau ।। sa tyaktvā kūṭayantrāṇi samutpāṭya ca pañjaram । viraktaḥ kānanaṃ prāyādvihitānaśanavrataḥ ।।
kapote tridivaṃ yāte vimānenārkavarcasā । bhartāramanuśocantī kapotī vahnimāviśat ।। tasyāṃ nivasamānāyāṃ bhartrā saha surālaye । dāvānale tanuṃ tyaktvā lubdhako api divaṃ yayau ।।
lubdhakakapotīyam ।। pāpamarjitamajñānātkathaṃ naśyati dehinām । pṛṣṭo yudhiṣṭhireṇeti punaḥ śāntanavo abravīt ।। indotākhyaṃ munivaraṃ rājā pārikṣitiḥ purā ।
brahmahatyākulaḥ prāyādviśvastaḥ śaraṇaṃ vane ।। muhustena nirasto api pāpasaṃsargabhīruṇā । nināya karuṇairvākyaistaṃ rājā karuṇārdratām ।। tasya kīrtayataḥ pāpaṃ taptasyānuśayāgninā ।
tīrthāplutasya śanakaiḥ sa muniryājako abhavat ।। aśvamedhena vidhivatpūtātmā so atha bhūpatiḥ । tāritaḥ kilbiṣāddhorādindotena kṛpālunā ।। indotapārikṣitīyam ।।
vyayasāyena buddhyā ca niścayena ca dehinaḥ । taranti narakaṃ bālaṃ śuśucurbāndhavāḥ purā ।। tānsametyābravīdgṛdhro gamyatāṃ tyajyatāṃ śiśuḥ । imāmavasthāṃ paryante ko nāma na gamiṣyati ।।
mā tiṣṭhata ciraṃ ghore śmaśāne pretabāndhavāḥ । iha martyasahasrāṇi yayuryāsyanti ca kṣayam ।। śrutvaitadbālakaṃ tyaktvā śanaistāngantumudyatām । uvāca jambuko abhyetya dhigyuṣmānnirghṛṇāśayān ।।
aho nu dāruṇā yūyaṃ tyaktvā gacchanti ye sutam । gatāsavo api jīvanti kadācitsuptabhautikāḥ ।। kiṃta vo bhayaṃ śmaśāne asminyāto astaṃ na divākaraḥ । tiraścāmapi bāle asmiñjāyate karuṇākaṇaḥ ।।
śṛgāleneti gadite punaḥ śavabhṛtaśca tān । gṛdhro jagāda citraṃ vo jambukasya girā bhramaḥ ।। jīvaratnabhṛto yūyaṃ kāṣṭhaloṣṭhopamākṛteḥ । snehena pātajīvasya śiśoḥ kiṃ yāta mūḍhatām ।।
vanaṃ vrajata vairāgyāttapaḥ kuruta vā mahat । viyogasāre saṃsāre satyānnānyatparāyaṇam ।। anyena vartmanā putraḥ pitā cānyena gacchati । svakarmabhiḥ pare loke tyajata snehavikriyām ।।
yāntyeva vṛddhāstaruṇā bālā garbhagatāstathā । kriyate kiṃ vicāro asti na kālasya pramāthinaḥ ।। bandhūnāmidamānṛṇyaṃ sthitijñānaṃ pracakṣate । mṛtaḥ pralāpaṃ bāṣpaṃ ca na śṛṇoti na paśyati ।।
vatsarāṇāṃ sahasraṃ me sāgraṃ jātasya vartate । nirgatāsurmayā dṛṣṭaḥ pralāpairnotthitaḥ kvacit ।। ityuktvā virate gṛdhre gomāyuḥ punarabravīt । dayāṃ kuruta kānte asminbāle kamalalocane ।।
śambukasya vadhātpūrvaṃ mṛto api brāhmaṇātmajaḥ । daśakaṇṭhadviṣo rājye jīvitaṃ prāpa durlabham ।। karābhyāṃ śiśunānena vitīrṇaṃ salilāñjalim । kadācitpāsyati pitā sukṛtī paralokagaḥ ।।
bhāṣite jambukeneti gṛdhraḥ punaruvāca tān । santaḥ śokāmaye nṝṇāṃ na praśaṃsanti bheṣajam ।। dinānte dāruṇatarā bhavatyeṣā śmaśānabhūḥ । kaṅkālamālākalitairbhūtavetālamaṇḍalaiḥ ।।
kṣaṇena hi na gīryante sahasrāṇi bhavādṛśām । mā kurudhvaṃ prayāse asminvyasane kalahe matim । vapuṣāṃ jīvitānāṃ ca gatānāmagamaḥ kutaḥ ।। iti gṛdhrasya vacasā nivṛttānvīkṣya bāndhavān ।
uvācābhyetya gomāyuḥ punaḥ svārthaikapaṇḍitaḥ ।। abāndhave asminnadhunā na saṃsāre matirmama । gacchanti kāṣṭhavattyaktvā putrakaṃ yatra mānuṣāḥ ।। vṛddhaḥ prayātyātmabhayādvijane tyajyate śiśuḥ ।
ko asminpratyayamādhattāṃ janaḥ svārthapare jane ।। ityūcatustau bhakṣyārthaṃ kṣutkṣāmau gṛdhrajambukau । divā gṛdhrasya bhojyaṃ yadrātrau gomāyukasya tat ।। atrāntare samabhyetya bhagavānambikāsutaḥ ।
svecchāvihārī varadastaṃ bālakamajīvayat ।। śatāyuṣaṃ skandavarātte yayuḥ prāpya taṃ sutam । prāpatuśceśvaradṛśā kuśalaṃ gṛdhrajambukau ।। ityanirvedaśīlānāṃ dhīmatāṃ vyavasāyinām ।
abhīpsitāni sahasā sidhyantīśvaraśāsanāt ।। gṛdhragomāyusaṃvādaḥ ।। na kuryādbalinā vairaṃ durbalo darpamāśritaḥ । vinaṣṭaḥ spardhayā vāyormahāñśalmalipādapaḥ ।।
vistīrṇaśākhāvipulaḥ saṃtaptādhvanyasaṃśrayaḥ । babhūva himavatprasthe śalmaliścumbitāmbaraḥ ।। papraccha nāradaḥ prītyā taṃ yadṛcchāgato muniḥ । aho nu tava nīrandhrāḥ pattrapuṣpaphalaśriyaḥ ।।
manye tava paraṃ mittraṃ vāyuryenāsi rakṣyase । taravastadbalākrāntā viśīryante patanti ca ।। śrutvaitadūce darpāndhaḥ śalmaliḥ skandabandhuraḥ । cittraṃ mune na jānīṣe bale tulyo na me anilaḥ ।।
katthanenetyabhihite bahuśastena śākhinā । tadeva nārado gatvā pavanāya nyavedayat ।। tadgirā krodhavidhuraḥ sphāraḥ pralayamārutaḥ । śvo draṣṭāsīti taṃ vṛkṣaṃ samabhyetya tadābravīt ।।
rajanyāmatha saṃtrāsātsa saṃcintyaiva śalmaliḥ । prabhañjanaṃ mahāvegaṃ dhīmānkhayamaśīryata ।। tataḥ prātaḥ śakalitāśeṣaśākhāsamākulam । apaśyadvāyurabhyetya viśīrṇaṃ śalmaliṃ svayam ।।
aho nu dhanyamantro asi buddhyā tvaṃ rakṣitastaro । ityuktvā vigatakrodho vāyuḥ prāyādyathāgatam ।। nāradaśalmalisaṃvādaḥ ।। lobhe eva mahatpāpaṃ jñānameva paraṃ mahaḥ ।
dama eva parā śāntistapa eva paraṃ padam ।। satyameva paraṃ puṇyaṃ śreyaḥ krodhābhinigrahaḥ । ānṛśaṃsyaṃ paro dharmaḥ sāro ayaṃ dharmavādinām ।। adhyāyaḥ ।।
śrutismṛtikṛtaistaistaiḥ prāyaścittaiḥ śarīriṇām । kīrtanāttīrthasevābhiḥ pāpaṃ dānaiśca naśyati ।। brahmahā dvādaśa samāḥ kapālāṅko vrataṃ caret । saṃmukhaḥ khaḍgalito bhrūṇahā mucyate yudhi ।।
brāhmaṇārthe hatāḥ pāpaṃ taranti gurutalpagāḥ । mucyante sarvapāpebhyo hayamedhena bhūmipāḥ ।। prāyāścittavidhiḥ ।। dharmātmajopadeśeṣu nakulena kathāntare ।
atha pṛṣṭo abravīdbhīṣmaḥ karavālasya saṃbhavam ।। asurābhihate kāle himavacchikhare purā । svayaṃbhūrbhagavānkhaṅgo dhātrā dhyātaḥ samāyayau ।। prāṃśurnīlotpalaśyāmo bhuvanāni vilokayan ।
sa babhūva trinetrasya brahmavākyātkarāgragaḥ ।। tena niṣkaṇṭakaṃ kṛtvā rudro raudreṇa katejasā । jagacchivākṛtiḥ paścādbabhūva śaśibhūṣaṇaḥ ।। taṃ khaḍgaṃ lebhire bhūpā manuprabhṛtayaḥ kramāt ।
yasya dhārānipātena punarjanma na dehinām ।। khaḍgotpattiḥ ।। śrutveti mandiraṃ pārtho gatvā bhīṣmagiraḥ smaran । vidureṇa kathāścakre dharmasarvasvavādinā ।।
teṣāṃ viduraṣaṣṭhānāṃ babhūvurvividhāḥ kathāḥ । śuddhapravṛttadharmāṇāṃ dharmakāmārthasaṃśrayāḥ ।। ṣaḍgītāḥ ।। samabhyetyātha papraccha punarbhīṣmaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।
sauhārdaṃ kena na calediti pṛṣṭo abravīcca saḥ ।। kṛtajñaiḥ sādhubhiḥ sabhyaiḥ kulīnairanapāyibhiḥ । satāṃ na naśyati prītirguṇādānaikatatparaiḥ ।। mitradruhaḥ kṛtaghnāṃśca varjayetkuṭilāśayān ।
kṛtaghnatāsamaṃ rājanna hi paśyāmi pātakam ।। darpavānmalinācāro vedādhyāpanavarjitaḥ । madhyadeśyo asitatanuḥ śīlācāraparāṅmukhaḥ ।। gautamo nāma kaluṣo brahmabandhurabhūtpurā ।
sa vasañśabarīsaktaḥ paryanteṣu dhanārthitām । bibhradbhrāntvā vasumatīṃ sārthabhraṣṭo aviśadvanam ।। tasminsnigdhatarucchāye prasannaharikuñjare । nyagrodhapādapasyāgre chāyārthī samupāviśat ।।
nāḍījaṅghābhidhastūrṇaṃ bakaḥ sugatasadvrataḥ । vilokya taṃ kṛpāviṣṭo durgataṃ vinato abravīt ।। brahmandāridryamunnidraṃ tavaitatpradahāmyaham । suhṛdaṃ me virūpākṣaṃ rākṣasendramito vraja ।।
kārtikyāṃ sa hi dātṝṇāṃ dhuryo dāsyati te dhanam । madīyamiti tacchrutvā sa gatvā karuṇākulāt ।। tasmātkanakamāsādya bahulaṃ tūrṇamāgataḥ । bakaṃ vilokya tatraiva dhanatuṣṭo vyacintayat ।।
na hyetadbhakṣyate hema vane vigatavikriye । sāṃprataṃ bakamevādya pātayāmi supīvaram ।। iti saṃcintya suciraṃ pātheyārthī dvijādhamaḥ । hemabhāranataḥ suptaṃ jaghāna saralāśayam ।।
adarśanena tasyātha khinno rākṣasabhūpatiḥ । śaṅkākulaścāracakraṃ visṛjya prāpa taṃ dvijam ।। hataṃ tena bakaṃ jñātvā nijagrāha tamutkaṭam । ākāśadhuniphenaiśca jīvitaṃ prāpa khecaraḥ ।।
aparādhahataṃ dṛṣṭvā nāḍījaṅgho api gautamam । ajīvayaddurācāraṃ na manyuradhame satām ।। evaṃ kṛghnacarito gautamaḥ sugatavratam । jaghāna pāpe pāpānāṃ niḥśaṅkaṃ ramate manaḥ ।।
nyāsāpahāriṇo dhenustrīgurubrāhmaṇāntakāḥ । dharmiṣṭhā iva yasyāgre sa kṛtaghno vicāryatām ।। āpaddharmāḥ ।। atha paprāccha dharmajñaṃ dharmarājaḥ pitāmaham ।
kathaṃ samāśrayeddharmaṃ vinaṣṭadhanabāndhavaḥ ।। sa tena pṛṣṭaḥ provāca śṛṇu senajitaṃ nṛpam । putraśokākulaṃ kaścijjñātvābhyetyāvadaddvijaḥ ।। abhāvāyaiva jāyante bhave asminsarvajantavaḥ ।
śocyastvamapi kālena kathaṃ śocasi pārthiva ।। yadṛcchayā saṃgataścetpratiyāto yadṛcchayā । saṃsārādhvani tatko ayaṃ viyoge mohavibhramaḥ ।। jāyate kṣaṇadṛṣṭeṣu sneho duḥkhāya dehinām ।
mamāyamiti mugdhānāṃ na sa teṣāṃ na tasya te ।। śocantyalubdhaṃ vāñchantaḥ prāptaṃ śocanti durbhagam । naṣṭaṃ śocanti duḥkhārtā jantavaḥ sukhinaḥ kadā ।। dhanaputrakalatreṣu na snihyanti vipaścitaḥ ।
avaśyaṃ viprayogo hi taiḥ paraiśca nṛṇāṃ sadā ।। ko nāma priyasaṃyogānna manyetāmṛtopamān । marmacchido viyogeṣu yadi na syurviṣotkaṭāḥ ।। piṅgalā dattasaṃketaṃ kāntaṃ vārāṅganā purā ।
anāgataṃ ciraṃ dhyātvā svayamekābravīnniśi ।। āgatenāpi kiṃ tena viyoge duḥkhadāyinā । bhaje kāntamihāntasthāmanaśvaramaśocakam ।। iti saṃtoṣapīyūṣaśāntā śāpāpavedanā ।
pratibuddhvaiva suṣvāpa parame dhāmni piṅgalā ।। senajidgītāḥ ।। asminpravāhavadyāti nṛṇāmāyuṣi kiṃ sukham । pṛṣṭo yudhiṣṭhireṇeti punarūce pitāmahaḥ ।।
medhāvinā purā pṛṣṭaḥ putreṇaitaddvijaḥ pitā । uvācādhyayanaṃ kṛtvā brahmacārī tato gṛhī ।। putraiḥ pitṝṇāmanuṇo bhūtvā pītvānilānvane । munistulyasuhṛddveṣyaḥ prayāti paramaṃ padam ।।
tacchrutvovāca tanayaḥ sarvametadaninditam । ślāghyāya śreyase karma yadi kālaḥ pratīkṣate ।। asamāptasvakāryāṇāmāyuḥ svalpamamudritam । ahorātragaṇaireva sravayetadalakṣitam ।।
muhūrtamapi jantūnāṃ kālo ayaṃ kalitākhilaḥ । sārthaḥ sudūragāmīva nārthito api vilambate ।। kṣaṇārdhamapi kāryeṣu na vilambeta paṇḍitaḥ । na jānīmaḥ kadā kasminkṛtānto nipatiṣyati ।।
na vātsalyānna kāruṇyānnopayogānna gauravāt । pratīkṣāṃ kṣamate kālaḥ kāryaśeṣeṣu dehinām ।। mṛtyunā yasya sauhārdaṃ yo na vettyāyuṣo avadhim । śvaḥ kartāsmīdamityeṣā vāṇī tasyaiva śobhate ।।
aho nu mohamugdhasya lokasyeyaṃ pramāditā । yadbālaṃ mṛtamālokya vṛddhastiṣṭhati nirbhayaḥ ।। nave vayasi bhogārhe naveṣu vibhaveṣu ca । navoḍheṣu ca dāreṣu hriyate mṛtyunā janaḥ ।।
tasmātkuśalamevādau kāryaṃ saṃsāraśāntaye । tarattaraṅgalolo hi dehidehasamāgamaḥ ।। pitāputrasaṃvādaḥ ।। dhanināṃ nirdhanānāṃ ca vibhāgaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।
pṛṣṭo atha dharmarājena punaḥ śāntanavo abravīt ।। śampāko nāmavānvipraḥ purā dhīmānabhāṣata । vitṛṣṇayātipīḍyante saṃtoṣo amṛtanirjharaḥ ।। bhayānabhijño niścinto nidrāvānrogavarjitaḥ ।
nirdhanaḥ sukhito nityaṃ yathāvāptakṛtakriyaḥ ।। sukhamāste sukhaṃ śete sukhaṃ ca pratibudhyate । saṃtoṣavānnirāyāso nirapāyo nirāmayaḥ ।। dhanino darpapūrṇasya bhrūbhaṅgādvakradarśinaḥ ।
kumbhīnyastadhanatrāṇacintāpāṇḍukṛśatviṣaḥ ।। cauro bhūpālabhītasya vṛddhyārthaṃ pāpakāriṇaḥ । ajīrṇarogagrastasya ṣṭhīvino bhojyakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। lobhaśuṣkakalatrasya duḥkhaikaphalabhāginaḥ ।
spardhākathaiva kā nityamākiṃcanyāmṛtāśibhiḥ ।। manyate tāvadātmānaṃ śakravaiśravaṇopamam । gṛhyate dhanavānyāvanna dasyunṛpamanyubhiḥ ।। dhanaṃ gamayatāṃ bhūri gṛhāṃśca suparicchadān ।
nirdhanāddhanināmeva kṛcchrādduḥkhaviṣūcikā ।। śampākagītāḥ ।। yāte vaiphalyamārambhe kiṃ kuryāddraviṇotsukaḥ । etatpṛṣṭaḥ kṣitibhujā dhyātvā śāntanavo avadat ।
śrūyatāṃ yadvinaṣṭārthasamaye duḥkhabheṣajam ।। maṅkirnāma dvijaḥ pūrvamīhamāno asakṛddhanam । prayatnairapi na prāpa vidhivaimukhyahelāya ।। kṣīṇārthaḥ sor'thaśeṣeṇa krītvā cātha vṛṣadvayam ।
svayamutkarṣaṇaṃ cakre kṣetre vipulavāhakaḥ ।। atrāntare pṛthugrīvo nidrābhaṅgātsamutthitaḥ । jahāroṣṭro mahākāyastau vṛṣau skandhalambinau ।। yugotkṣepāllambyamānau tau tena balaśālinā ।
vṛṣau vilokya śokārto vilalāpa dvijātmajaḥ ।। aho nu citravarṇāṅkau mama vatsatarau priyau । karṣanvibhāti karabho ratnāḍhyāviva bhūṣaṇau ।। ityuktvā jātanirvedagāḍhavairāgyavāsanaḥ ।
tṛṣṇāṃ nininda sahasā praśāntānuśayajvaraḥ ।। duḥkhāya bata jantūnāṃ tṛṣṇā paribhavāspadam । vipralabdho janaḥ sarvo yayā śocatyaharniśam ।। alabdhaṃ vāñchatāṃ vittaṃ labdhaṃ ca parirakṣatām ।
naṣṭaṃ ca śocatāṃ puṃsāṃ kadā duḥkhaṃ nivartate ।। kāmor'theṣu vipanmūlaṃ saṃtoṣaḥ paramaṃ sukham । niṣkāmaśca sakāmaśca matau me svastharogiṇau ।। sadhanaścintyate rājñā dasyunā svajanena ca ।
vikalaśceti lokena nirdhanaśca na gaṇyate ।। tasmātsaṃtyaktakāmānāṃ saṃtoṣadhanaśālinām । kṣayodayavyayāyāsairna cetaḥ paribhūyate ।। idaṃ labdhamidaṃ naṣṭamidaṃ lapsye punardhiyā ।
idaṃ cintayatāmeva jīrṇamāyuḥ śarīriṇām ।। adhunā lobhamunmūlya spṛhāṃ dūre nirasya ca । vītamoho bhavāmyeṣa munistulyapriyāpriyaḥ ।। tyāgo hi hanti vyasanaṃ tathā hi janakaḥ purā ।
dahyamāne api nagare nābhajadduḥkhavikriyām ।। iti dhyātvā ciraṃ maṅkirnirvedācchāntamānasaḥ । āśāpāśaṃ parityajya paraṃ padamavāptavān ।। maṅkigītāḥ ।।
etaddharmasutaḥ śrutvā punaḥ śantanunandanam । samabhyadhātkathaṃ janturvītaśokaścarediti ।। so abravīcchṛṇu bhūpāla prahlādo dānavādhipaḥ । nityānandaṃ purā vipramūce svacchandacāriṇām ।।
sukhaduḥkhaśatāvarte vipule asmindhanārṇave । aviluptaḥ kathaṃ brahmannityatuṣṭo abhilakṣyase ।। keyaṃ ślādhyatarā vṛttiḥ ko vāyaṃ vibhavo dhiyaḥ । krīḍāvihārī loke asminyadasakto na lipyase ।।
iti pṛṣṭo dvijastena babhāṣe vipulāśayaḥ । taṭasthaḥ sarvabhāveṣu nityatṛptaścarāmyaham ।। māyāvilasitaṃ sarvaṃ jānansaṃsāravibhramam । kṣayodayeṣu bhūtānāṃ na duḥkhaṃ na sukhaṃ bhaje ।।
āyuṣāṃ vibhavānāṃ ca bhāvānāṃ ca svabhāvataḥ । paśyannasāratāmetānnānuśocāmi nirvyathaḥ ।। bhuñjāno vividhānbhogānnirāhāro athavā kvacit । nagnaścīrāmbaro vāpi mahārhavasano api vā ।।
bhujopadhānaḥ kṣmāśāyī paryaṅkaśayano api vā । samaḥ śamadamābhyāṃ ca dharāmyājagaraṃ vratam ।। parāvarajño bhāvānāṃ kūṭastho vigataspṛhaḥ । tyaktamohabhayadveṣaścarāmyājagaraṃ vratam ।।
pāptaṃ giratyajagaraḥ kuraṅgaṃ mahiṣaṃ gajam । asaṃprāpteṣvanudvegaṃ vidhatte niścalasthitiḥ ।। etāmājagarīṃ vṛttimāśritya vimalāśayaḥ । na cintayāmi sattvastho lābhālābhau sukhāsukhe ।।
brāhmaṇeneti kathitaṃ śrutvā vismitamānasaḥ । jīvanmuktadaśāṃ tasya prahlādaḥ praśaśaṃsa tām ।। prahlādabrāhmaṇasaṃvādaḥ ।। etatpāṇḍusutaḥ śrutvā punarbhīṣmamabhāṣata ।
kulakarmārthabuddhīnāṃ pitāmaha kimuttamam ।। iti pṛṣṭo nṛpatinā babhāṣe jāhnavīsutaḥ । atikramya guṇānsarvānprajñaivopari vartate ।। vaiśyau dhanamadādhmātaḥ syandanena purā vrajan ।
apātayatkṛśataraṃ muniṃ vartmani kaśyapam ।। lalatkuṇḍalagaṇḍena sa tena bhuvi pātitaḥ । śocandaridramātmānaṃ niścayaṃ nidhane vyadhāt ।। taṃ pāṃsuśāyinaṃ dīnaṃ prāṇatyāgakṛtavratam ।
śakraḥ śṛgālarūpeṇa kṛpayā vaktumāyayau ।। so avadadbata saṃtoṣaḥ saṃsāre nāsti kasyacit । mune yadujjvalācāro nātmānaṃ bahu manyase ।। dhanyā manuṣyāḥ saṃsāre yaiḥ svahastena bhujyate ।
kaṇḍūrnivāryate kīṭakaṇṭakādirvikṛṣyate ।। aho sukṛtināṃ rājā tvaṃ yanmānuṣayonijaḥ । brāhmaṇaśca tapasvī ca spṛhaṇīyo asi kaśyapa ।। aho dhanyo asi yannāsvurna maṇḍūko na kukkuṭaḥ ।
na pukkaso na cāṇḍālo na kuṣṭī na jaḍo asi vā ।। dṛśyante dīrgharogārtā duḥkhādduḥkhataraṃ śritāḥ । śocantastāmasīṃ yonīṃ prapannāstānvilokaya ।। manuṣyaḥ paripūrṇāṅgo vyādhivyasanavarjitaḥ ।
brāhmaṇaśca tvamuditastvatto dhanyataro asti kaḥ ।। asaṃtoṣe matiṃ mohānmā kṛthā vibhavāśayā । prāpyendratāmapi janastato apyādhikyamīhate ।। tṛṣṇeyaṃ satatābhyāsādvardhamānā śarīriṇām ।
antrasnāyumayī tantrī kṛṣṭevāyāti dīrghatām ।। tasmātsvadharmanirataḥ spṛhaṇīyaḥ kulodgataḥ । parasya vibhavaṃ dṛṣṭvā na kāmānmartumarhasi ।। ahaṃ kutārkiko bhūtvā dhūmāgniprāyavādabhṛt ।
vedadveṣī nāstikaśca pāpayonimimāṃ śritaḥ ।। asmiñśarīre bahuśo nirviṇṇo api bhayādaham । na tyajāmi tanuṃ pāpa yonayaḥ santyato adhikāḥ ।। iti buddhyā surapatirvītaśokaṃ vidhāya tam ।
rūpaṃ ca darśayitvāsmai prayayau tridaśālayam ।। indrakaśyapasaṃvādaḥ ।। śrutvaitadūce kaunteyaḥ kena sṛṣṭamidaṃ jagat । jīvaśca kīdṛśo dehe sa ca yātaḥ kva tiṣṭhati ।।
bhīṣmo abravīdetadeva purā kailāsaśekhare । bhāradvājena muninā pṛṣṭo bhṛgurabhāṣata ।। pṛthivīpadmasaṃsthasya mānasasya prajāpateḥ । ākāśaḥ pūrvasargo ayaṃ viṣṇorvyaktākṛtispṛśaḥ ।
vṛkṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ ca samānaṃ pāñcabhautikam ।। tenaivāsminmahāsarge citrāśca vyaktayaḥ kṛtāḥ । prāṇāpānādirūpeṇa vāyunā sahito analaḥ ।। uttare himavatpārśve phalabhūmirnirāmayā ।
tāṃ puṇyakāriṇo yānti viparītā viparyayam ।। ihāpi loke dṛśyete sukhaharṣadhanādibhiḥ । dāridryakleśaduḥkhaiśca jantūnāṃ śubhaduṣkṛte ।। bhṛgubharadvājasaṃvādaḥ ।।
athābravītsadācāro rājñā pṛṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ । prātaḥ prabuddho vijane malaṃ tyaktvā śuciḥ sadā ।। devapūjārato hotā dātā monī ca bhojane । ṛtukālābhigāmī ca jyeṣṭhānāṃ praṇataḥ kṣamī ।
yo naraḥ sa sadācāraḥ prāpnoti padamuttamam ।। ācāravidhiḥ ।। punaḥ kṣitibhujā pṛṣṭaḥ kimadhyātmeti sarvavit । ūce śāntanavastattvaṃ dhyātvā hṛdi sanātanam ।।
kṣetrajñastriguṇaḥ kṣetre raśmivatprasṛtendriyaḥ । asaktaḥ saktavadbhāti cchanno vyavahitairapi ।। nivātadīpaniṣkampamānasaḥ śāntadhīḥ samaḥ । ayatnāttendriyo maunī sthāṇubhūtastamīkṣate ।।
brāhyavṛttinirodhena manaso niyamena ca । rāgaśokabhayadveṣatyāgātsadbhiḥ sa dṛśyate ।। taḍittaraṅgataralaṃ caratyāratacañcalam । cittaṃ vātavadudbhrāntaṃ bhavatyevāsamarthinām ।।
abhyāsena samībhūte nistaraṅga ivodadhau । cetasyacalatāṃ yāte praśāntāśeṣaviplave ।। prakāśatamasoḥ pāre puruṣaṃ śāśvataṃ śivam । dhyānenātyantasukhadaṃ paraṃ paśyanti yoginaḥ ।।
adhyātmasaṃkīrtanam ।। etadākarṇya kaunteyaḥ pitāmahamabhāṣata । pātakānāṃ phalāvāptiḥ kīdṛśī gatayaśca kāḥ ।। iti pṛṣṭaḥ kṣitibhujā gāṅgeyaḥ punarabravīt ।
abhidhyāsadṛśī puṃsāṃ phalāvāptirapāyinī ।। ahaṃkārapravṛttānāṃ bhaugaiśvaryasukhārthinām । nirayeṣveva nilayaḥ kāmināṃ kāmasaṃnibhaḥ ।। pārijātalatālolā mandārodārasaurabhāḥ ।
hemābjasarasī ramyā nākanāyakasevitāḥ ।। velladvimānasulabhāstāstāstridaśabhūmayaḥ । niyatāvadhayaḥ sarvā nirayaḥ saṃpracakṣate ।। anādinidhanaṃ dhāma guṇatrayavivarjitam ।
aspṛṣṭaṃ kālakalayā niṣkāmenaiva labhyate ।। prayataḥ saṃhitājāpī kāmarāgoñjhitaḥ purā । uvāsa brāhmaṇaḥ kaścitpāde tuhinabhūbhṛtaḥ ।। tasya parṣasahasrānte divyajñānasya jāpinaḥ ।
japavṛddhiṃ dadau tuṣṭā sāvitrī svayamāgatā ।। atha kālena bhagavāndharmo abhyetya tamabravīt । tyaktvā śarīramāgaccha divyaṃ divyavapuḥ padam ।। tacchrutvā so avadannaitāṃ tyaje ahaṃ sahajāṃ tanum ।
svargaspṛhā na me kāciddyaurmahī ca same mama ।। na vāñchā na ca me dveṣaḥ svarge apyastyavaśaṃ mayā । sarvathā yadi gantavyaṃ tatsadehena nānyathā ।। ityukte tena bhagavānyamo mṛtyuśca tāṃ bhuvam ।
kālaścābhyetya jagadurvipraṃ dharmo yaduktavān ।। asminnavasare śrīmānikṣvākuḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ । tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena tamāśramamupāyayau ।। sa taṃ jāpakamabhyetya babhāṣe tejasāṃ nidhim ।
gṛhaṇa me dhanaṃ vipra pātraṃ tvatsadṛśo asti kaḥ ।। tacchrutvā jāpako avādīnnivṛtto ahaṃ mahīpate । pravṛttadharmaniratā viprāḥ pātraṃ pratigrahe ।। samīhitamahaṃ tubhyaṃ dadānyevāvilambitam ।
brāhmaṇeneti kathite jagāda pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। japasyāsya phalaṃ dehi yattvayā samupārjitam । ityukto bhūbhujā vipro gṛhāṇeti tamabhyadhāt ।। rājāvadadvacoyuddhairajeyaḥ sattvavānbhavān ।
na mamaitajjapaphalaṃ tvaddattamupayujyate ।। iti bruvāṇo viproṇābhyarthito api sakṛnnṛpaḥ । na tajjagrāha dātāhaṃ bhūbhṛdityabhimānavān ।। atrāntare tamabhyetya kāmakrodhau vivādinau ।
virūpau vikṛtākārau nyāyaṃ papracchaturmudā ।। eko avadaddhenuphalaṃ deyamasmai dadāmyaham । dattaṃ mayā punargrāhyaṃ netyuvāca tathā paraḥ ।। rājā vicārya suciraṃ tayorvivadamānayoḥ ।
uvāca dīyamānaṃ yo na gṛhṇāsi jito atha saḥ ।। athābravīnnṛpaṃ viprastvaṃ na gṛhṇāsi kiṃ mama । paropadeśeṣvathavā sarvo bhavati paṇḍitaḥ ।। jāpakeneti gadite kāmakrodhau vilokya tau ।
saha bhoktavyamityuktvā jagrāha nṛpatiḥ phalam ।। tataḥ svarge sa vibudhe prāpte sa brahmaṇi svayam । viveśa jāpakastyāgasamādhiṃ bhūbhujā saha ।। prāṇe manaḥ samāveśya paśyannāsāpuṭadvayam ।
āpūrya vyoma ṣaṭkośaṃ prakāśenāntaraṃ nabhaḥ ।। bhrūmadhyanihitajyotiruddhāṭya brahmasaṃpuṭacam । kṣipramutkrāntasūryo abhūdatisūryānaladyutiḥ ।। tālurandhrasamutthaṃ tattejo dvijamahībhujoḥ ।
brahmāṇamaviśatsākṣātprādeśapuruṣākṛti ।। jāpakopākhyānam ।। jñānayogyasya vedānāṃ niyamasya ca bhūbhujā । phalaṃ svargaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ bhīṣmaḥ pṛṣṭo abravītpunaḥ ।।
prajāpatirmanuḥ pūrvametadūce bṛhaspatim । sukhaduḥkhādikaṃ karma heyopādeyalakṣaṇam ।। sukhamastyasukhaṃ yasmātpravṛttiriti karmaṇaḥ । sukhaduḥkhojjhitaṃ jñātaṃ kāmarāgavivarjitam ।।
śrautaṃ karma sukhāyaiva viruddhamasukhāya ca । śuddhāḥ samādhiniyamairbhānti dānādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।। narāḥ karmaphalaistaistaistattadākārabhedataḥ । sukhaduḥkheṣu sīdanti rāgamohavaśīkṛtāḥ ।।
māyeyaṃ jagadutpattisthitisaṃhārakāriṇī । kṛtā mahābhūtamayī chāyevākāśadarśinī ।। dṛṣṭvā śarīrāntarago mohādyairna vilokyate । sradhūma iva kāṣṭhāntaḥ sadā saṃnihito analaḥ ।।
hemnīva kaṭakāditvaṃ kāṣṭhe vā sālabhañjikā । ātmanyevākhilaṃ bhāti sadapyasadiva sthitam ।। jñānena gṛhyate jñānaṃ gajeneva vane gajaḥ । tadevāsya gatiṃ vetti sarpapādānivoragaḥ ।।
manubṛhaspatisaṃvādaḥ ।। svarūpaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ pārthenātha pitāmahaḥ । uvāca jñānanayanaiḥ kathitaṃ nāradādibhiḥ ।। bhagavānpuṇḍarīkākṣaḥ keśavo nābhipaṅkajāt ।
sṛṣṭvā caturmukhaṃ cakre jagannikhilamīśvaraḥ ।। hatvā madhumukhāndaityānvidadhe śāśvatīṃ sthitim । saṃkarṣaṇaḥ sarvaharaḥ pralaye yāti rudratām ।। sargasthitivināśānāmityeṣa kila kāraṇam ।
mṛṇālīlīlayā yena varāheṇoddhṛtā mahī ।। vāsudevaḥ paraṃ dhāma śāśvataṃ dhruvamavyayam । nivṛttadharmāya guruḥ śiṣyāyeti nyavedayat ।। vicitramāyayā viṣṇormohitāḥ kila jantavaḥ ।
rāgadveṣamadagrastāḥ punarāyānti yānti ca ।। śukraśoṇitasaṃbhūtā yānti saṃsāriṇastataḥ । tānmohayanti lalanā vipākaviṣamabhramāḥ ।। striyo hi nāma saṃsārakārāmandiraśṛṅkhalāḥ ।
rādadveṣaviṣādānāṃ saṃgatigranthirajjavaḥ ।। snehādvā kṣayamāyānti svāṅgajaiḥ kṛmibhiḥ sutaiḥ । jantavaḥ saṃtatimayāḥ klinnacarmalavā iva ।। yatendriyecchā mucyante saṃsārādbrahmacāriṇaḥ ।
mūlabījapariploṣā yeṣu kāmo na jāyate ।। saṃkalpajaṃ vahantyetāḥ sirāḥ śvabhraṃ manovahāḥ । tacchruṣyati virāgeṇa yeṣāṃ te paramaṃ gatāḥ ।। tṛṣṇātanturanādyanto bisānāmiva dehinām ।
sahajo antaḥsthito hantuṃ niḥśeṣaṃ ca na śakyate ।। samairyuktasamācārairviśuddhagaganaprabham । hṛdi nārāyaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā śāntiḥ śāntairavāpyate ।। vaiṣṇavādhyātma ।।
mokṣaṃ prayāto janakaḥ kathamityatha bhūbhujā । devavrato avadatpuṣṭo mithilādhipateḥ kathām ।। janakasyābhavatpūrvamācāryaśatasevinaḥ । guruḥ pañcaśikho nāma kapilo brahmanaiṣṭhikaḥ ।।
sa rājānamuvācedamācāryaśatasaṃnidhau । sphuranniḥsārasaṃsāravikāraparihāradhīḥ ।। sa galajjātinirbandhaḥ karmabaddho apyavāsanaḥ । viśarārusamāhārasarvagrahaparigrahaḥ ।।
ahaṃkāravikāreṣu mūlacchedavidhāyinām । avadhānalavādeva bhidyate bhavavibhramaḥ ।। mayi sarvamidaṃ bhāti sarvatrāhamavasthitaḥ । ityasaṃsāriṇāmeva satāṃ vṛttirmahīyasī ।।
satyaṃ saṃkṣayaniṣṭhānāṃ jarāmaraṇadharmiṇām । krameṇendriyavaikalyāccharīraṃ yāti pañcadhā ।। ete śabdādayaḥ pañca yeṣu tattvārthaniścayaḥ । avyayaṃ paramaṃ cakraṃ buddhiśceti paraṃ mahat ।।
asamyagdarśināmeṣāṃ duḥkhatatparamanyathā । tyāgā evaṃ paraṃ tattvaṃ muktānāṃ nyastakarmaṇām । mithyāprayātacittānāṃ phalanti hṛdayabhramāḥ ।। dravyatyāgaḥ karma hanti bhogatyāgo vratakriyām ।
sukhatyāgastapoyogaṃ sarvatyāgaptu śāntaye ।। guṇatrayavimukto asau kṣetrajñaḥ śāśvato avyayaḥ । yairdṛṣṭaste na lipyante paṅke śaśikarā iva ।। naṣṭe phale toṣajuṣi kṣīṇayoḥ puṇyapāpayoḥ ।
avyaṅgā gaganākārā mahatpaśyanti sūrayaḥ ।। caranmṛgaḥ śṛṅgamiva tvacaṃ vṛddhaṃ ivoragaḥ । pakṣīvonmathitaṃ sālaṃ bandhaṃ muñcati sāttvikaḥ ।। ityākarṇya vaco rājā janako mithilāṃ purā ।
dagdhāmadagdhāṃ nājñāsīttṛṣṇārāgavivarjitaḥ ।। janakarājānaṃ prati pañcaśikhācāryopadeśaḥ ।। sukhaṃ kimiti pārathena bhīṣmaḥ pṛṣṭo abravītpunaḥ । ihāmutra ca dāntānāṃ sukhaṃ saṃtoṣaśālinām ।।
damo dhṛtirdamastejo jamaḥ kīrtirdamo ratiḥ । puṃsāṃ damaprasaktānāṃ śatrurnāma na vidyate ।। dāntādhyāyaḥ ।। kiṃ tapo vā na vetyetadupavāsādikaṃ vratam ।
pṛṣṭaḥ provāca kaunteyaṃ punaḥ śantanunandanaḥ ।। bhuñjāno apyupavāsī syādyuktāhāro naraḥ sadā । upavāso hi mūrkhāṇāṃ kevalaṃ prāṇaśaṣaṇam ।। sadā rataḥ svadāreṣu brahmacārī bhavennaraḥ ।
yajñopayuktamāṃsāśī bhavenmāṃsavivarjakaḥ ।। atithidvijabhṛtyānāṃ śeṣamaśnāti yaḥ sadā । amṛtāśī sa vijñeyaḥ surā nāmnāmṛtāśinaḥ ।। amṛtaprāśikā ।।
naraḥ karmaphale kartā kiṃ na vetti kṣamābhujā । bhīṣmaḥ pṛṣṭo abravīcchakraḥ purā prahlādamabravīt ।। sthānāccyutastvaṃ daityendra hatāste bāndhavā mayā । śokasthānaṃ kathaṃ svastho nirākula ivekṣyase ।।
śrutveti daityastaṃ prāha śakra kiṃ katthase vṛthā । bhāvāḥ svabhāvacapalāḥ puruṣārtho nirarthakaḥ ।। mūrkho buddhimatāṃ dhuryaḥ surūpo rūpavarjitaḥ । pramattā nayasaṃpannā yāntyete heturatra kaḥ ।।
na hi śokaḥ sukhabhraṃśe kartavyo vṛddhasevibhiḥ । bhavedabhāvaḥ sadbhāve bhāvā bhrūbhaṅgabhaṅgurāḥ ।। iti śrutvā yayau śakrastatprajñānopadeśataḥ । prahṛṣṭā buddhisārāṇāmadveṣṭāro hi sādhavaḥ ।।
śakraprahlādasaṃvādaḥ ।। akālavahninā dagdhe rājñāmaiśvaryakānane । kiṃ dhairyamiti pṛṣṭo atha pārthenāha pitāmahaḥ ।। bhraṣṭarājyeṣu daityeṣu prāptaiśvaryaḥ śatakratuḥ ।
papraccha gatvā brahmāṇaṃ naṣṭe vairocanaṃ purā ।। vibhavaṃ lokapālānāmabhibhūya nijaśriyā । yo babhūva jagannāthaḥ sa baḍiḥ kvādya vartate ।। iti pṛṣṭaḥ surendreṇa jagāda kamalodbhavaḥ ।
śūnyāgāre kharo bhūtvā bhraṣṭaiśvaryo baḍiḥ sthitaḥ ।। śrutvaitanmuditaḥ śakrastūrṇa taṃ draṣṭumāyayau । airāvaṇaṃ samāruhya kailāsamiva jaṅgamam ।। sa gatvā śūnyanilaye dadarśa khararūpiṇam ।
tuṣāśinaṃ baliṃ ko vā vipadbhirnaiva pīḍyate ।। dṛṣṭvā tamūce trailokyanātho bhūtvaiśāsanaḥ । tvamimāṃ gatimāpannaḥ kathaṃ śocyāṃ na śocasi ।। lakṣmīvilāsahāsācchaṃ kva tacchatraṃ kva cāmaram ।
tālavyālolavalayaṃ gītamapsarāsaṃ kva tat ।। brahmadattā kva sā hemamālā maulimatastava । kṣapāsvapi yayā dikṣu babhurbālātapaśriyaḥ । athavā yānti cetāṃsi mahatāṃ saha bhūtibhiḥ ।।
api smarasi kiṃ daitya bhāsvatastava śāsanāt । akṛṣṭapacyā pṛthivī yadabhūdbhūriyājinaḥ ।। yaścātapatre yātrāyāṃ śītāṃśudhavale tava । gandharvāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi nanṛturhemamālinām ।।
airāvaṇagatasyeti śrutvā śakrasya bhāṣitam । avuluptamanāḥ prāha baḍi vāmanavañcitaḥ ।। taraṅgataralā lakṣmīryadyāyāti ca yāti ca । kṛtamasmābhiriti ki tatpranṛtyanti śatravaḥ ।।
na śocāmi svasatvastho nistaraṅga ivodadhiḥ । dṛṣṭvā kālena mahatā kathāśeṣīkṛtāḥ śriyaḥ ।। avaśyaṃ vidhidaurātmyādvipadantā hi saṃpadaḥ । lakṣmīṃ vinaśvaraḥ śocetkaḥ kālakavalīkṛtām ।।
anatikramaṇīyo ayaṃ kālaḥ sarvatra jṛmbhate । tuṣaiḥ kalpitavṛttiryatprayātaḥ svaratāmaham ।। vikośāśāpalāśe asminsaṃsārorusaroruhe । kālabhṛṅgaḥ pibatyeva janakiñjalkamañjasā ।।
jagadgrāsagariṣṭhasya tasya kālasya śāsanāt । smṛtiśeṣadaśāṃ śakra sameṣyati bhavānapi ।। kiṃ na viplavāyantyetā hariṇyaḥ śīghragāḥ kṣaṇam । sphītaphenasitacchattrāstaraṅgiṇyo vibhūtayaḥ ।।
prayāti taralā lakṣmīḥ sravatyāyuralakṣitam । iti vastusvabhāve asminko nu śocati madvidhaḥ ।। āyuḥ kenākṣayaṃ labdhaṃ viyogaḥ kasya vā priyaḥ । kasminvā capalā lakṣmīrniṣaṇṇā caravīkṣitā ।।
alīkalīlācaṭulaiḥ saṃgamairdṛṣṭanaṣṭayā । anayā sarvagāminyā kiyanto na viḍambitāḥ ।। aiśvaryasaurabhabharānguṇabhṛṅgasaṅgānkāntālatāvalayitānabhimānavṛkṣān । utphullakīrtikusumānphalapūritāśānsarvakaṣo harati kālamahāpravāhaḥ ।।
tasyaitadvadataḥ kāryāllalanaṃ lalitākṛtim । dadarśanirgatāṃ śakro dṛṣṭvāpṛcchacca vismitaḥ ।। līlāśikhaṇḍābharaṇā kā tvaṃ hariṇalocane । kimarthamasi niṣkrāntā daityādhipativigrahāt ।।
sā tacchrutvāvadacchakraṃ tvāmahaṃ samupasthitā । tyaktvainaṃ vismṛtācāramucchiṣṭaspṛṣṭasarpiṣam ।। ahaṃ subhaṭakhaḍgāgradhārājalanivāsinī । kamalāpūtamahgalyā kamalākaravāsinī ।।
etaduktvā curbhiḥ śrīrbhūmyambhovahnivāyuṣu । pādaiḥ saṃnidhimādāya sahasrākṣamupāyayau ।। śrīsaṃnidhānam ।। śrīvihīnaṃ purā śakro namuciṃ nāma dānavam ।
papraccha śokakāle asminkiṃ na śocasi dānava ।। iti pṛṣṭo avaddaityo niḥsyandodadhidhairyabhūḥ । naṣṭāḥ śokena naśyanti dviṣadānandadāyinaḥ ।। śokadagdhaśarīrāṇāṃ prarohaḥ kva punaḥ śriyaḥ ।
śokena naśyati prajñā prajñānāśo vipattaye ।। śokena spṛṣṭacittānāṃ naṣṭānāmudbhavaḥ kutaḥ । svakṛtaṃ bhujyate karma paripāke śubhāśubham । satāmamlānavaktrāṇāṃ nāntarajñāstu śatravaḥ ।।
śakranamucisaṃvādaḥ ।। bhūtimāsādya śakreṇa baḍiḥ svapadavicyutaḥ । punarevāvadatpṛṣṭo vyasane apyaviluptadhīḥ ।। avaśyameva śūrāṇāṃ sthitau jayaparājayau ।
karmāyattau na kartā tvaṃ kālaprāptamidaṃ bhaja ।। kālo na yāti yāsyanti sahasrāṇi bhavādṛśām । gantā tvamapi kālena kiṃ dhairyeṇa vikatthase ।। na tallokeṣu paśyāmi vicinvāno api sūkṣmadhīḥ ।
duṣprāpaṃ yadayatnena na līḍhaṃ kālajihvayā ।। kathāvaśeṣavibhavāḥ kālena bhuvanādhipāḥ । śrūyante vihitāste te kiṃ vṛthā śakra mādyasi ।। śakto asmi jetuṃ tvāmekaḥ sānugaṃ darpamohitam ।
kiṃtu na kṣamate kālo velevābdherbalaṃ mama ।। kālenāyānti vipadaḥ kālenāyānti saṃpadaḥ । puṃsāṃ svakarmamudrāṇāṃ śokasyāvasaro atra kaḥ ।। niśamyaitatsahasrākṣo virato amarṣasāhasāt ।
sa tamūce kālavaśaṃ tvaṃ yathāttha tathaiva tat ।। yadā lokā bhaviṣaayanti nirmaryādāḥ kalispṛśaḥ । tadā tvaṃ dāruṇaiḥ pāśairmuktaḥ svāsthyāṃ gamiṣyasi ।। baḍi vāsavasaṃvādaḥ ।।
śubhāśubhasya pṛṣṭo atha pūrvaṃ rūpaṃ mahībhujā । jagāda bhīṣmo jantūnāṃ vināśodayalakṣaṇam ।। ākāśataṭinītīre purā śakraḥ sanāradaḥ । vilokya lakṣmīṃ papraccha vikāsikamalānanām ।।
devi śaṃsa yathā tattvamihāgamanakāraṇam । iti pṛṣṭā mahendreṇa sāvadatkamalekṣaṇā ।। tyaktvā daityānahaṃ śakra naṣṭācārānviśṛṅkhalān । surāṇāṃ sadma sādhūnāṃ saṃprāptā tava cāntikam ।।
asurāḥ pūrvamabhavansadācāravibhūṣaṇāḥ । snātā hutāgnayaścāsannijitāḥ strībhirarcitāḥ ।। dātāro niḥspṛhāḥ kṣāntāḥ prabhāte ghṛtadarśinaḥ । na niśīthe na cotsaṅge dadhisaktubhujo abhavan ।।
avandhyaratisargāśca tenāhaṃ tānabhūṣayam । adya tūtsannamaryādāstyaktāste durmadā mayā ।। āyattāḥ patayaḥ strīṇāṃ śaṇṭīnāmadya tatpare । pratyutthānādikaṃ tāṃśca kurvantyuccairvadanti ca ।।
taruṇā dhūrtasacivā vṛddhānāṃ vacanaṃ vayaḥ । viḍambayanti darpāndhā helollolitakuntalāḥ ।। aśaucocchiṣṭasūdaiśca vihitaṃ bhakṣayanti te । guptodyāneṣu devārthibhṛtyasvajanavarjitāḥ ।।
dhānyaṃ payonnaṃ vivṛtaṃ svocchiṣṭaspṛṣṭasarpiṣam । gṛhe teṣāṃ na vīkṣante hāsakeliratāḥ striyaḥ ।। strīyogyaṃ puruṣo dhatte keśāṃśukavibhūṣaṇam । ācāragatisaṃlāpaṃ pauruṣaṃ strī bibharti ca ।।
itthaṃ teṣāṃ madāndhānāṃ vasatiṃ pāpināmaham । tyaktvāntikamavāptā tvāṃ satyaśīle mam sthitiḥ ।। āśā śraddhā dhṛtiḥ kṣāntiḥ kāntirvṛttirjitirmatiḥ । yuṣmāneva samāyātā devyo aṣṭau matpuraḥsarāḥ ।।
iti bruvāṇāṃ tāṃ śakraḥ prāpya prāyāttriviṣṭapam । nimittametatprathamaṃ subhāśubhaphalaṃ nṛṇām ।। śrīvāsavasaṃvādaḥ ।। rājñā brahmapadaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ punarūce pitāmahaḥ ।
asito devalaḥ pūrvaṃ jaigīṣavyamabhāṣata ।। vandito ninditaścāsi samastulyapriyāpriyaḥ । tyaktarāgabhayadveṣo lakṣyase kena hetunā ।। iti pṛṣṭo munīndreṇa jaigīṣavyaḥ svatantravit ।
uvāca śāntamanasaḥ satyaṃ jātamidaṃ mama ।। vidyānalasamudbhūtavivekavyastaviplavāḥ । na hṛṣyanti na śocanti santaḥ saṃtoṣanirbharāḥ ।। mānāvamānayostulyā na snigdhā na ca vairiṇaḥ ।
mamāyamiti no yeṣāmahamasyeti vā kvacit ।। mātsaryamanurāgo vā nirapāyasukhaspṛśām । sarvabandhavinirmuktā nirbhayāḥ saṃcaranti ye । prabuddhāḥ svapnamāyāsu labhante brahmaṇaḥ padam ।।
jaigīṣavyasaṃvādaḥ ।। priyaḥ sarvatra pūjyaśca ko astīti jagatībhujā । bhīṣmaḥ pṛṣṭo avadatkṛṣṇo yadāhāndhakabhūpatim ।। eka evāsti nikhilapriyaḥ pūjyaśca nāradaḥ ।
svacchandacārī sukhitaḥ sodyogo vijitendriyaḥ ।। asaṃniruddhaprasaro niḥsaṅgo bahusaṃgataḥ । krīḍāratirjagaddraṣṭā kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ ।। śrutveti pṛṣṭaḥ pārthena bhūtānāṃ prabhavo apyayam ।
kālasya ca gatiṃ bhīṣmo babhāṣe viśvatattvavit ।। purā śukena bhagavānvyāsaḥ pṛṣṭo abravīdidam । sargāsthitiṃ ca kālaṃ ca yacca kṛtyaṃ dvijanmanām ।। sahasrayugaparyanteṣvavyakto vyaktatāṃ gataḥ ।
brahma sṛjati śabdāttu vyomādikṣmāntapañcakam ।। tadudbhute punaḥ sarge kālenākāśaśeṣatām । gate vyomādi vilayaṃ prayātyavyaktasaṃjñake ।। ityayaṃ sargasaṃkṣepaḥ śṛṇu kṛtyaṃ dvijanmanām ।
saṃskṛto jātakarmādyairbrahmacārī bhavedgṛhī ।। ātmānamātmanā paśyanvānaprasthastato yatiḥ । brāhmaṃ karmeti kathitaṃ jñānināṃ vṛttirucyate ।। anādaravirakteccho vidyuttaralamātmanā ।
paśyannantaḥ paraṃ jyotiḥ sarvavyāpī samīravat ।। śūnyasthānaikanilayaḥ samo brahmaṇi līyate । karmaṇā yāti saṃsāraṃ niḥsaṃsārastu vidyayā ।। nijodbhavavilīnecchaḥ saṃvidvikacamānasaḥ ।
satataṃ svāntaviśrāntaḥ paramāmṛtamaśnute ।। vyāsaśukasaṃvādaḥ ।। śrutveti bhīṣmaṃ papraccha ya ete pṛthivīśvarāḥ । yātā mṛtyuvaśaṃ teṣāṃ ko mṛtyuriti pāṇḍavaḥ ।।
bhīṣmo abravītpurā prāha rājānamanukampakam । nāradaḥ putraśokārtaṃ śatrūṇāṃ vaśamāgatam ।। sarvametadvidhiḥ sṛṣṭvā prajā vipulatāṃ gatāḥ । āvartamāne bhuvane dṛṣṭvā krodhaṃ samāyayau ।।
tatkrodhāddīptaśikhinā dahyamāneṣu jantuṣu । kṛpāvāṃruyambako devaścaturmukhamayācata । śaṃbhunābhyarthito dhātā kopāgniṃ saṃjahāra tam ।। saṃhṛtātkrodhadahanātkanyā kamalalocanā ।
udatiṣṭhannabhaḥśyāmā raktāmbaravibhūṣaṇā ।। uvāca tāṃ tato brahmā tvaṃ śanaiḥ saṃhara prajāḥ । apsu pratiṣṭhitā hyeṣā bhūmirbhāreṇa majjati ।। tacchrutvā dāruṇaṃ dhātuḥ kṛpayā netrajaṃ jalam ।
nijaṃ jagrāha pāṇibhyāṃ nindantī janma duḥkhitā ।। kathaṃ tava sutā deva ghore karmaṇi madvidhā । yogyā bandhuviyuktānāṃ na sahe duḥkhināṃ giraḥ ।। ityuktvā vipulaṃ cakre duṣkaraṃ vividhaṃ tapaḥ ।
sā mṛtyuḥ sarvasaṃhārabhītā kāruṇyaśālinī ।। tasyai varaṃ dadau dhātā vyādhayaste aśrubindavaḥ । bhaviṣyanti janāntāya tvāṃ na jñāsyanti mohitāḥ ।। iti mṛtyuḥ purā sṛṣṭvā brahmaṇā sarvasaṃhṛtiḥ ।
mā śucaḥ pṛthivīpāla sā hi kaṃ nopasarpati ।। mṛtyuprajāpatisaṃvādaḥ ।। dharmatattvaṃ punaḥ pṛṣṭo dharmajena pitāmahaḥ । śaśaṃsa sāraṃ dharmasya satyaṃ parahitaṃ tathā ।।
gatirdharmasya vividhā sūkṣmā jñātuṃ na śakyate । viparītavicārāṇāmadharmo yāti dharmatām ।। antarjalatapāḥ pūrvamabhavajjājalirmuniḥ । jaṭāsu yasya viśvāsātkulāyāḥ pakṣibhiḥ kṛtāḥ ।।
sa dṛṣṭvā pakṣiṇāṃ mūrdhni nirvṛttāñśāvakāñśanaiḥ । babhūva dharmasaṃmattastamūcuratha rākṣasāḥ ।। tulādharasya samātāmanāsādyaiva kiṃ mune । mādyasi sphāratapasāṃ vyayaṃ kartumihodyataḥ ।।
iti śrutvā samanviṣya gatvā vārāṇasīṃ muniḥ । tulādharaṃ dadarśātha māṃsavikrayajīvitam ।। jñānadṛṣṭyā svayaṃ jñātvā tasyāgamanakāraṇaṇ । tulādharo abravīdbrahmandharmo hi gaganātmakaḥ ।।
abhītaiḥ sarvabhūtebhyo bhūtānāmabhayapradaiḥ । asaktaiḥ karmanipuṇairdharmasyāsādyate gatiḥ ।। ahiṃsā paramo yajñaḥ puṇyairyaṣṭuṃ sa śakyate । paśya pāpaṃ kṛśāprāpyaṃ gopaśuprāṇapīḍanāt ।।
ātmayajñāptapuṇyānāmātmatīrthaikasevinām । tyaktābhimānaspardhānāṃ naiva śocanti bāndhavāḥ ।। iti mānamahāmohaṃ jājaleḥ sa tulādharaḥ । nivāryāsaktakarmasthaḥ prayayau paramāṃ gatim ।।
tulādharajājalisaṃvādaḥ ।। gītaṃ vicaravnunā pūrvaṃ dharma'sminneva bhūbhujā । ahiṃsā paramo dharmaḥ kratuścādravyaḍambaraḥ ।। paśuprāṇairyajantyete kāmātmānaḥ phalepsavaḥ ।
māṃsamatsyamadhupraāyaṃ dhūrtairbhogāya kalpitam ।। lolupairdambhagurubhiḥ paśuyāgo adhigamyate । pūjyo hi bhagavānviṣṇuḥ so adbhiḥ puṣpaiśca tuṣyati ।। ralāniṃ śarīraṃ nāyāti yathā na maraṇaṃ bhavet ।
tathā karma pravartena śarīraṃ dharmasādhanam ।। vicaravnugītāḥ ।। kāryākāryavimarśāya rājñā pṛṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ । uvāca cirakārīti babhūvāṅgiraso muniḥ ।।
ciraṃ vicārya karmāmi sa karoti yadā tadā । alaso dīrghadarśī ca mūrkhairiti viḍambyate ।। sa kadācitsvayaṃ pitrā prerito jananīvadhe । ciraṃ nidadhyau saṃdehadolāviślathamānasaḥ ।।
avilaṅghyaṃ guruvaco duḥsaho jananīvadhaḥ । ityabhūdduḥkhakaluṣaḥ patito dharmasaṃśaye ।। tāvaccintāparaḥ so abhūdyāvattasya pitā svayam । paścāttāpamanuprāpto nijāmājñāmavārayat ।।
cirakārī vimarśena rarakṣeti svayaṃ muniḥ । mātaraṃ guruvākyaṃ ca vimarśo hi śubhāspadam ।। cirakāricaritam ।। rājā rakṣetsadācāraṃ kathaṃ lokānapīḍayan ।
iti pṛṣṭo narendreṇa punaḥ śāntanavo abravīt ।। dyumatsena purā putraṃ sālvarājo mahāmatiḥ । babhāṣe satyavānnāma vadhyānvīkṣyātipīḍitān ।। rājandharmagatiḥ sūkṣmā kimete dasyavastvayā ।
asāmarthyena viprāṇāṃ nigṛhyante yathā tathā ।। ekasya hi vadhenaiva te bhāryāputrabāndhavāḥ । hatā bhavanti bahavastasmāddaṇḍo vivecyate ।। dyumatseno niśamyeti prāha daṇḍyānadaṇḍayan ।
rājā kṣipatyagādhe asminprajā bhayamahāvaṭe ।। laghudaṇḍāḥ purābhūvanmṛdavo alpadruho janāḥ । adya kālaviparyāsādvadhyadaṇḍe apyasaṃyatāḥ ।। ityāsīdrājaputrasya rājñaśca paribhāṣaṇam ।
nivṛtte ca pravṛtte ca dharme dharmavidāṃ vara ।। dyumatsenopākhyānam ।। nivṛttaṃ ca pravṛttaṃ ca dharmaṃ pṛṣṭo atha bhūbhujā । vyājahārobhayostattvaṃ draṣṭā śantanunandanaḥ ।।
nahuṣasya purā saure sattre gāṃ yūpasaṃgatām । svecchācāro dvijo yogī vilokya kapilo abravīt ।। aho nu hiṃsā durvṛttairdharmāya parikalpitā । paropaghāte nandanti lubdhāḥ kāmaphalepsavaḥ ।।
ityākarṇya dvijastatra syūmaraśmiḥ praviśya gām । avadadvedavacanaprāmāṇyaṃ neṣyate tvayā ।। yajeta dadyādityeṣā na śrutā kiṃ śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ । gārhasthyalakṣaṇo dharmo yajñāṅgo hyakhilāśrayaḥ ।।
śrutveti kapilaḥ prāha śuddhajñānamayaḥ kratuḥ । tārayatyeva tamaso dravyayāgo hi bandhanam ।। syūmaraśmirniśamyaitatprovāca kriyayā punaḥ । viśuddhe acirmaṇau jñānaṃ pratimāmāśrayediti ।।
gaukāpilīyam ।। varaṃ dharmārthekāmānāṃ kimiti kṣmābhujā punaḥ । pṛṣṭo abravīcchāntanavastrivargagatikovidaḥ ।। dhanārthī brāhmaṇaḥ kaściddevānārādhya niṣphalaḥ ।
siṣeve kuṇḍadhārākhyaṃ bhaktyā jñānadharaṃ ciram ।। tuṣṭe tasmindadarśātha svapne vaiśravaṇālaye । maṇibhadraṃ dhanacayānvitarantaṃ yathocitam ।। kuṇḍadhārastamabhyetya brāhmaṇārthamayācata ।
kuṇḍadhārasya yogena brāhmaṇo hitakāriṇā ।। varānnirvedamāpanno dharmavāṃstapase yayau । nabhaścaro divyadṛṣṭiḥ so abhavattapasā kṛtī ।। evaṃ sārastrivargasya dharmaḥ śubhaphalapradaḥ ।
arthakāmaprasaktānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ narake sthitim । niśamya kuryātko nāma na dharmopārjane matim ।। kuṇḍadhāropākhyānam ।। ahiṃsā paramo dharmo nirvedo jñānadeśakaḥ ।
sarvatyāgaḥ parā śāntiḥ kāmināṃ tvanyathākhilam ।। asito devalaḥ pṛṣṭo nāradenābravītpurā । aṣṭādaśātmakaḥ soṣmā saṃgataḥ pāñcabhautikaḥ ।। kṣetrajñena punaryāti saṃgamaṃ vṛkṣapakṣivat ।
akṣīṇavāsanātanturbhinno api na vimucyate ।। vicchinnakarmā nirdvandvaḥ puṇyapāpavivarjitaḥ । dehī dehaviyoge svaṃ brahma gacchati nirguṇaḥ ।। nāradāsitasaṃvādaḥ ।।
prakṣīṇavāsanājālo māṇḍavyaṃ janako abravīt । dhuryo ahamasmi sukhināmeka evārthavarjitaḥ । dahyamāne api nagare yasya kiṃcinna dahyate ।। saṃsāramarutaptānāṃ tṛṣṇāmūrcchitacetasām ।
bheṣajaṃ paramaṃ nāma saṃtoṣāmṛtavāridaḥ ।। dhanena vardhane tṛṣṇā lāvaṇeneva vāriṇā । śoko vivṛddhatṛṣṇāyā goḥ śṛṅgamiva vardhate ।। tāṃ tyaktvā gatasaṃsargo nirduḥkhapadamāśritaḥ ।
kūrmāṅgavatsaṃhṛtecchaḥ svecchācārī vimucyate ।। janakasyeti vacasā māmḍavyaḥ srastasaṃsṛtiḥ । brahmaprakāśamaviśaddhruvaṃ śāntamanāmayam ।। māṇḍavyajanakasaṃvādaḥ ।।
yatendriyecchaḥ saṃnyāsī nirbhayo janitābhayaḥ । avajñāto avadhūtaśca śūnyācāro apyanāśrayaḥ ।। anirviṇṇaḥ prahṛṣṭaśca jñātā maunī ca mucyate । budha ityāha hārīto viśuddhajñānasaṃśrayaḥ ।।
hārītagītāḥ ।। bhraṣṭaiśvaryaḥ purā vṛtraḥ śukraṃ gurumabhāṣata । jīvānāṃ karmabandhānāṃ tiṣṭhatāṃ pāñcabhautike । paryāyeṇa bhavantyeva saṃpado vipadastathā ।।
niḥspṛho asmi na śocāmi bhaje sāmyamanaśvaram । na yāsyāmyadhunā rāgamavarṇo varṇasaṃgamāt ।। ityuktvā dānavapatiryadṛcchopagatānmuneḥ । sanatkumārādajñāsīdviṣṇuṃ kāraṇamavyayam ।।
sa vijñāyācyutaṃ devaṃ prayayau paramāṃ gatim । so ayaṃ nārāyaṇaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃbandhī tava pāṇḍava ।। vṛtragītāḥ ।। rājñā vṛtrakathāṃ pṛṣṭaḥ punaḥ prāha pitāmahaḥ ।
purā vṛtreṇa vijito raṇe jambhanisūdanaḥ ।। sa bodhito vasiṣṭhena garvajvaravimohitam । viṣṇutejo dadhadvajraṃ taṃ jaghāna mahākṛtim ।। hatasya kāyādvṛtrasya brahmahatyā vinirgatā ।
muktakeśī kṛśā ghorā maladigdhā kapālinī ।। sā vidrutaṃ sahasrākṣāṃ ciramanviṣya sarvataḥ । vilokya kaṇṭhe jagrāha niścalābhayakampitam ।। taṃ tayā gūḍhamākrāntaṃ cirāya caturānanaḥ ।
vilokya kṛpayā hatyāṃ yayāce śakramuktaye ।। viratā brahmaṇo vākyādbrahmahatyā sureśvaram । tatyāja sthitimāsādya caturdhā ghoradarśanā ।। yo agnau prajvalite yatnānna bījādikamarpayet ।
yaḥ parvakāle viṭapicchettā yaśca rajasvalām ।। kāmayecca jale yaśca kṣipecchleṣmamalādikam । sa padaṃ brahmahatyāyāḥ svayaṃbhūrityabhāṣata ।। vṛtravadhaḥ ।।
jvarotpattiṃ punaḥ pṛṣṭo bhīṣmaḥ pārthamabhāṣata । sumeruśṛṅge bhagavānsthito gaurīvapatiḥ purā । śuśrāva yajñaṃ dakṣasya devākīrṇaṃ prajāpateḥ ।। abhāgārhe asi kiṃ yajñeṣviti gaurīgirā haraḥ ।
anāhūtaścakārātha dakṣayajñakṣaye matim ।। kruddhasya tasya lālāṭasvedavārikaṇātkṣaṇāt । samudyayau jvaro dīptastriśirāstāmralocanaḥ ।। brahmaṇā duḥsaha so atha vinyastaḥ kila bhāgaśaḥ ।
teṣu teṣūtkaṭo yatnādekaḥ ko nu saheta tam ।। saṃtāpaṃ gajakumbheṣu parvateṣu śilājatu । nirmokapaṭṭaṃ sarpeṣu nīlikāṃ salileṣu ca ।। goṣu khorakaniḥśvāsamūṣiraṃ kṣetrabhūmiṣu ।
pādarogaṃ tathāśveṣu netrarogaṃ pikeṣu ca ।। meṣeṣu pittabhedaṃ ca hikkāśvāsaṃ śukeṣu ca । śikhābhedaṃ mayūreṣu śramaṃ pañcānaneṣu ca ।। janmanyante vivāhe ca manuṣyeṣu jvaraṃ tathā ।
bahudhāvasthitaṃ ghoraṃ satataṃ ca pracakṣate ।। rudro atha vīrabhadrākhyaṃ sasarja gaṇamutkaṭam । bhadrakālīṃ tathā devīṃ kālānalaśikhopamām ।। tau gatvā cakraturyajñaṃ bahudravyaṃ prajāpateḥ ।
bhinnabhinnāpaviddhāṅgaṃ nihatya mṛgarūpiṇam ।। tataḥ prajāpatiḥ pūrvaṃ devāhitavināśakam । virūpākṣamanekākṣaṃ tryakṣaṃ yakṣapatipriyam ।। sarvātmanā sarvagataṃ sarvākāramanāmayam ।
tuṣṭāva śaṃkaraṃ dakṣo gūḍhārthairdivyanāmabhiḥ ।। namo yajñāya vijñeyatattvānubhavaśāline । sarvavedamayoṅkāravācyāya vṛṣaketave ।। anavaccinnarūpāya vyāpine viśvamūrtaye ।
sarvataḥ pāṇiśirase namaḥ sarvāntarātmane ।। ugrāyodagramahase śarvāyāgarvaśāline । rudrāyodagrayaśase vandyāyendubhṛte namaḥ ।। tatastuṣṭe bhagavati tryambake tripurāntake ।
phalaṃ yajñasahasrasya dakṣo alabhata tadvarāt ।। dakṣayajñadhvaṃsaḥ ।। kathaṃ vijitalokānāṃ bhayaṃ mṛtyornivartate । iti prṛṣṭo narendreṇa vyājahāra pitāmahaḥ ।।
nāradena purā pṛṣṭaḥ samaṅgaḥ sarvatattvavit । prāṇendriyajayānnūnaṃ śoko mṛtyuśca naśyati ।। pañcendriyahitaṃ tuṣṭyai tuṣṭirutsekakāriṇī । utseko vinipātāya saṃsārasaraṇau sadā ।।
arāgamoho hṛṣṭātmā carāmyanupalakṣitaḥ । aśokaścāmṛtaścāhaṃ tena nārada paśya mām ।। samaṅganāradasaṃvādaḥ ।। śāstraniḥsaṃśayaṃ śreyo rājñā pṛṣṭo abravītpunaḥ ।
bhīṣmo yadgālavaṃ prāha nāradaḥ sarvadarśinam ।। hite varteta bhūtānāmahaṃkāraṃ parityajet । prakhyāpayenna saṃsatsu svotkarṣaṃ paranindayā ।। paiśunyaṃ laulyamālasyaṃ rātricaryāṃ ca varjayet ।
na darpādbahubhāṣī syānnendriyāṇāṃ hitaṃ caret ।। nānuśocetsukhabhraṃśe kāmayeta na durlabham । jānannapi na kurvīta kauṭilyaṃ na ca viśvaset ।। satāṃ saṅge matiṃ kuryātsadācārapure vaset ।
sahasā saṃtyajetpāpaṃ na kuryādanutāpadam ।। nāradagālavasaṃvādaḥ ।। muktiḥ śanaiḥ kathamiti bhīṣmaḥ pṛṣṭo abravītpunaḥ । ariṣṭanemiḥ sagaraṃ yadbabhāṣe vimuktaye ।।
āśālatāvalayitaṃ baddhamūlamavidyayā । na hi pātayituṃ śaktaḥ sukhena bhavapādapam ।। ko hi janmasahasroktāṃ vāsanābhyāsajāṃ nijām । prītitaṃ vārayituṃ śakto lalanādhanabandhuṣu ।।
samārūḍhaḥ śriyaṃ kāntāṃ lalanāmbhojaṣaṭūpadaḥ । tyajeti viṣasaṃkāśaṃ ko nāma vacanaṃ pibet ।। dhanaputrakalatreṣu svayamevārjiteṣvaho । avasannā vinaśyanti kṣudrāḥ kṣaudraraseṣviva ।।
śiśūnaṃ vṛttimālokya vyastāṃ devena kalpitām । ko hi tadvartanādānairātmānamavasādayet ।। paricchinnāśinaḥ kiṃ te koṭibhirbhūmisaṃcayaiḥ । na paśyasi mṛtaḥ kiṃcitko ayaṃ sarvagrahastava ।।
kāñcane loṣṭaśakale paryaṅke pāṃsusaṃstare । cīnāṃśuke valkale ca samānaḥ kila mucyate ।। antavatkalayansarvaṃ nirvedaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ । taṭasthaḥ sarvabhāveṣu bhavatyevābhavo naraḥ ।।
gaṇayandurdaśāmante samānaḥ kāñcanāśmanoḥ । avidyāgranthibhedena mucyate nirmamaḥ sukham ।। sagarāriṣṭanemisaṃvādaḥ ।। atha śukrakathāṃ pṛṣṭo rājñā prāha suravrataḥ ।
purā yogīśvaraḥ śukro bhṛgusūnurdhanaprabhoḥ । guhyakādhipaterdehaṃ praviśyākramya sarvataḥ ।। dhanaṃ bhūri jahārāśu tacca duḥkhāddhanādhipaḥ । pinākine dasyuvṛttaṃ vayasyāya nyavedayat ।।
kupitastripurārātirādāya bhṛgunandanam । papau sa codare śaṃbhorbabhrāma vipule ciram ।। sa rudradhāraṇāvahnidahyamāno antarasthitaḥ । ruddheṣu sarvasrotaḥsu tasya tuṣṭāva vallabhām ।।
tataḥ sa śukradvāreṇa nirgataḥ śukratāṃ yayau । satīsaṃrakṣito lebhe na ca vai pūrvavatsthitim ।। śukrotpattiḥ ।। śreyaḥ kimiti pṛṣṭo atha punarāha pitāmahaḥ ।
purā videhādhipatiṃ yaduvāca parāśaraḥ ।। manoratho ratho yasya saṃyataḥ śāntiraśmibhiḥ । na caratyavaṭe tasya karmaṇo api sukhaṃ sadā ।। ratyai bhogā vimūḍhānāṃ sā duḥkhāya viyoginām ।
tamase duḥkhamevaiṣāṃ bandhāya mahate tamaḥ ।। satāṃ bhogaviyogeṣu nirvedo nāma jāyate । nirvedastapase teṣāṃ tapaḥ saṃsāraśāntaye ।। sadācārapravṛttānāṃ yathāśāstrānusāriṇām ।
svakarmasaktamanasāṃ svayamāyānti saṃpadaḥ ।। parāśaragītāḥ ।। prajāpatirhaṃsarūpī rājñā pṛṣṭo abravītpurā । krodho mṛtyuḥ kujantūnāṃ svasukhādyadi nirgataḥ ।।
dagdhāḥ krodhena śocanti krodhānadhā nipatanati ca । jitakrodhaḥ śasukhaṃ śete grastarāgādibandhanaḥ ।। haṃsagītāḥ ।। pṛṣṭaḥ kimakṣaramiti prāha bhīṣmo nareśvaram ।
bhagavāñjanakaṃ pūrvaṃ vasiṣṭho yadabhāṣata ।। caturdaśavidhaḥ sargo guṇāḥ karmāṇi codanāḥ । sarvametatkṣaraṃ vidyādakṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam ।। akṣarakṣarasaṅgo ayaṃ dehidehasamāgamaḥ ।
dehatāmrakalādāhe hemavaddṛśyate abharam ।। vasiṣṭhajanakasaṃvādaḥ ।। punaḥ pṛṣṭo avadadbhīṣmo yājñavalkyo guruḥ purā । provāca śiṣyaṃ janakaṃ paramākṣaranirṇayam ।।
adhyātmacintāgantavyamadhibhūte ca kāraṇam । guṇatrayavinirmuktamakṣaraṃ vedyavarjitam ।। sāṃkhyayogoditaṃ śāntaṃ śāśvataṃ dhruvamavyayam । nistaraṅgodadhinibhi yuktāḥ paśyanti nirbhayāḥ ।।
sūryaprasādādvadanaṃ praviṣṭā me sarasvatī । tayāsmi vedakṛdbhūtvā sārameva padaṃ śritaḥ ।। ṣaṅviśo mucyate vyaktaṃ pralīnaṃ pañcaviṃśake । iti gandharvabhūpālo viśvāvasumabodhayat ।।
yājñavalkyajanakasaṃvādaḥ ।। tiṣṭhangṛhe ko nu muktaḥ pārtheneti suravrataḥ । pṛṣṭo babhāṣe sulabhā yadūce janakaṃ purā ।। tridaṇḍadhāriṇī muktā sulabhā nāma bhikṣukī ।
mithilāṃ janakaṃ draṣṭuṃ purā prāyādvihāyasā ।। yauvanābharaṇaṃ rūpaṃ dadhatī sā sumadhyamā । dadarśa janakaṃ kāntā lāvaṇyalalitākṛtiḥ ।। tāṃ vilokya sudhāsārasiktāṅga iva maithilaḥ ।
cakre samucitāṃ pūjāṃ tasmai pāpāsanādibhiḥ ।। tataḥ sukhoṣitā tatra muktāttaramupetya sā । sabhāyāṃ janakaṃ cakre raśmibhiḥ svīkṛtāntaram ।। netrābhyāṃ cārunayanā viśantī tamalakṣitā ।
antaraṅgā kṣaṇamabhūtsā supteva sudhānadī ।। tadbhāvaspṛṣṭabhāvo atha babhāṣe dantakāntibhiḥ । janako nirguṇāṃ kurvanvimuktāṃ hāravallarīm ।। ayi cittasudhāsindhucandrikā kāsi kasya vā ।
kutastvamanavadyāṅgi nayanāmṛtavarṣiṇī ।। śiṣyaḥ pañcaśikhasyāhaṃ sāṃkhyavedavido muniḥ । vivekāstravidāṃ śreṣṭho mokṣaṃ prāpto janādhipaḥ ।। kirīṭī kaṅkaṇadharaśchattravyajanavāhanaḥ ।
muṇḍitecchaḥ śamāraṇyo manaḥ karmaprasādanaḥ ।। svāntabodhakapāle asminpluṣṭaṃ pañcaśikhena me । jñānabījasya sāmarthyādviṣayeṣu na jāyate ।। naikāntavāsitā śāntyai na gehaṃ bandhanāya ca ।
sarvatra vihitā nāma muktirnirlepacetasām ।। antaḥpraveśaḥ kimayaṃ tvayā me yogataḥ kṛtaḥ । varṇagotrāśramādīnāṃ vibhedādeṣa saṃkaraḥ ।। jetumicchasi cedasmānsiddho mānastadeṣa te ।
ayaṃ svaśāstradoṣaśca tava spṛśasi yatparān ।। sarvāṅgasaṅgaṃ kuruṣe satī bhūtvā na lajjase । kāraṇaṃ brūhi subhage na mithyā vaktumarhasi ।। iti pṛṣṭātiparuṣaṃ na dhairyātsaṃcacāla sā ।
īṣadunnamitaikabhrūrhāsapallavitādharā ।। sā babhāṣe praviṣṭāpi cchāyeva purataḥ sthitā । pūrvāparahitaṃ vākyaṃ nadansajjanasaṃsadi । muktaśca bhedavaktā cetyaho rājanna rājase ।।
kāsi kasya kuto vā tvaṃ yadevamabhidhīyate । tatra kiṃ na śrutaṃ kāṣṭhajantuvadguṇabhautikam ।। triṃśadguṇakalākāro vyakto vyaktatvamāgataḥ । saṃghātastattvacakrasya so ayaṃ kasya na kasya vā ।।
śukrasekādyavasthāstā na lakṣyante jarāvadhi । dīpasyevārciṣo yātā yasya so ayaṃ kutaḥ katham ।। svāṅgairapi na saṃbandhaḥ saṃbandho jagatāmiva । kimutātmani nātmānaṃ muktaḥ paśyasi bimbavat ।।
vikalpaṃ pṛcchato naiṣā muktatā tava śobhate । samarārāvabhagnasya jayamāleva dantinaḥ ।। idaṃ rājyamaparyantaṃ tiṣṭhataste vimuktatā । na manye ahaṃ marutaṭe taptasyeva vitṛṣṇatā ।।
cāmarairlolayantyeva cchattrairācchādayanti ca । vivekaṃ madakallolairharanti ca nṛṇāṃ śriyaḥ ।। hatāḥ senāḥ punaryuddhe rājaputro nipātitaḥ । iti sādhāraṇairdeṣairbhūbhujāmeva duḥkhitā ।।
dhanaṃ kośe gajāḥ śāle svagṛheṣu ca mantriṇaḥ । śayyāvibhāge mahiṣī triyāmāyāṃ tvamekakaḥ ।। akaṅkaṇamahāraṃ ca śayyāyāṃ vartate vapuḥ । ucchvāsaśeṣo vimukhaḥ svapne dhāvasi cānyataḥ ।।
bhikṣukī śūnyanilayā śūnye asmiṃstava vigrahe । nivasāmi kṣapāmekāṃ kā nu te nṛpate kṣatiḥ ।। aspṛśantī vapuste ahaṃ praviṣṭā yadi yogataḥ । tatkathaṃ nṛpate muktaḥ sparśaṃ vetsi sarāgavat ।।
varṇasaṃkarabhīroste kathaṃ pañcaśikho guruḥ । vṛthā tadadhunā jātaṃ yattvayoktaṃ nareśvara ।। naivāṅkurasamarthaṃ me jñānabījaṃ prarohati । viṣayeṣviti tadrājansvayamuktaṃ na paśyasi ।।
avibhinnā vayaṃ sarve samāśrayisamāśrayāt । tarau latā tatra puṣpaṃ tasminṣaṭcaraṇā iva ।। sarvātmanā pṛthaktvaṃ cediti bhāgaṃ vipaśyasi । tadekāntavibhinnasya kasya kenātra saṃkaraḥ ।।
sa tvaṃ pravṛttivimukho na ca prāpto nivṛttatām । triśaṅkuriva madhyastho na divaṃ na bhuvaṃ śritaḥ ।। sarvametanmama na vā yatsarvamahameva vā । niṣṭhāmetāmanāsādya kathaṃ mukto asi pārthiva ।।
ityavāptopadeśārthaḥ sulabhāvacasā nṛpaḥ । na hṛṣṭo nāpahṛṣṭaśca tūṣṇīṃ nabha ivābhavat ।। sulabhājanakasaṃvādaḥ ।। rājñā śukasya vairāgyaṃ bhīṣmaḥ pṛṣṭo abravītpunaḥ ।
yaduvāca śukaṃ putraṃ parāśarasuto muniḥ ।। putra saṃsāramaraṇau saratāmavivekinām । paśya śītātapavyādhimaraṇāvadhiduḥsthitim ।। asminśarīrakusume bhṛṅgavajjīvite sthite ।
capaleṣu ca bāveṣu tāṭasthyaṃ putra nocitam ।। yathā likhitamevāyuḥ kṣaṇarātriṃ divaṃ tataḥ । koṭibhiḥ prāptakālānāṃ muhūrtamapi durlabham ।। vāsanākṣaudrapaṭale nānābhāvarasāhṛte ।
svayamutpādite magnaḥ kṣudraḥ ko nāma mucyate ।। aparyāptamanaḥsvecchāstyaktvā dārāndhanaṃ sutān । kālavyālasamākṛṣṭā hanta gacchanti jantavaḥ ।। asipattravanaṃ ghoraṃ taptā vaitaraṇī nadī ।
paratroṣṇakaṭāhāśca santi gehaṃ na bāndhavāḥ ।। na yāvadetattāruṇyaṃ galatyanupalakṣitam । na yāsi yāvatsaṃkocaṃ jarayā taptacarmavat ।। hikkāśvāsaviparyasto yāvatsvapnavilocanaḥ ।
kulālacakravadbhrānto na paśyasi diśo daśa ।। hiraṇyavarṇāṃ vasudhāṃ yāvadvīkṣya viśṛṅkhalam । na gacchasi tamo dīrghaṃ sūcyabhedyamabāndhavaḥ ।। yāvacchubhāśubhākrānto na hṛṣyasi virauṣi vā ।
tāvatsamādhivibudho vinivṛttabhavo bhava ।। śrutvetyavāptanirvedaḥ śukastyaktvā svamāśrayam । āmantrya pitarau yogī yayau śreyaḥsamādhaye ।। yāvatkam ।।
karmamūlaṃ niśamyātha nṛṇāṃ sukṛtaduṣkṛtam । rājñā śukakathāṃ paṣṭaḥ punarāha pitāmahaḥ ।। karṇikāravane meroḥ purā śītāṃśuśekharaḥ । vijahāra haro hāraphaṇiratnāṃśupiñjaraḥ ।।
tatrogratapasā yukto vyāsaḥ satyavatīsutaḥ । putrakāmo varaṃ prāpa dāsyamīti maheśvarāt ।। tataḥ kālena sa munirvahnyarthamaraṇīṃ svayam । mamanthāpsarasaṃ paśyandhṛtācīmagracāriṇīm ।।
tasya śukraṃ papātāśu śukībhūtāṃ vilokya tām । araṇyāmaratasyāpi tatrāsya tanayo abhavat ।। araṇyā garbhasaṃbhūtaḥ so abhūdvyāsasutaḥ śukaḥ । śukraḥ kamaṇḍaluṃ yasmai dyauśca daṇḍājinaṃ dadau ।।
vedānadhītya sākārānavāpya ca bṛhaspateḥ । tapasā brahmacaryeṇa mānyo abhūtsa divaukasām ।। upadeśaṃ pituḥ prāpya tadgirā janakaṃ yayau । mokṣadharmārthanipuṇaṃ draṣṭuṃ padbhyāṃ nabhaścaraḥ ।।
meruvarṣānatikramya mithilāṃ praviveśa saḥ । nivāryamāṇo apyakrodho dvāḥsthaiḥ paruṣavādibhiḥ ।। paraṃ janakarājasya kakṣyādvayamatītya saḥ । mantripraveśitastasthau pūjito antaḥpure muniḥ ।।
tataḥ paryacarankāntāstamutpalavilocanāḥ । yāsāṃ smitāmṛtaiḥ kāmaḥ śivadagdho api jīvati ।। varāhar śayane tatra yogī dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ । nināya rātriṃ prātaśca nṛpo draṣṭuṃ tamāyayau ।।
gurorvyāsasya tanayo janakena sa pūjitaḥ । ratnāsanopaviṣṭo atha paprāccha mithileśvaram ।। visṛṣṭo ahaṃ bhagavatā pitrā vyāsena te antikam । gurūpadeśasaṃbandhaṃ vada jñānamanāmayam ।।
janakaḥ prāha śanakaiḥ kriyāsopānapaṅktibhiḥ । āruhyoccaiḥ paraṃ dhāma visuddhaṃ śuddhacetasā ।। jñānānilahṛtāśeṣavikalpaghanaḍambaraḥ । dvandvatriyāmāviratau dṛśyate bodhabhāskaraḥ ।।
sarvamātmani sarvatra tamātmānaṃ vilokayan । guṇatrayavinirmukto muniścarati nirmamaḥ ।। tasyotsṛṣṭakalaṅkasya prasannāsaktacetasaḥ । sarvatra vijito mokṣaḥ sarvakartṛpadaspṛśaḥ ।।
spṛhāgranthiṃ puro muktvā tato rāgaṃ tataḥ śucam । ahaṃkāraparityāgādyogī brahmamayo bhavet ।। sarvāntarātmatāṃ yātaḥ sarvajñapadamāsthitaḥ । yukto vimiśratāṃ yāti śaileṣu salileṣu ca ।।
ahamityeva saṃsāro nāhamityeva tatkṣayaḥ । dehamānavirāme ca prāṇamānaṃ samāśrayet ।। bhāvasnehaṃ parityajya dehamānaṃ samāśrayet । dehamānavirāme ca prāṇamānaṃ samāśrayet ।।
nirasya prāṇamānaṃ ca viśvāhaṃkāramāśrayet । śūnyatāṃ cintayetpaścādyayā brahmaṇi līyate ।। ityādi mithilendrasya niśamya viśadaṃ vacaḥ । tamāmantrya kṛtī prāyācchukastuhinabhūdharam ।।
atrāntare suramunirnārado draṣṭumāyayau । himācalaṃ latālāsyavilāsamaṇimandiram ।। vidyādharaghaṭājuṣṭanirjharodārakandaram । hemapaṅkajinīkuñjakūjanmañjuvihaṅgamam ।।
śuko atha tatra pitaraṃ śiṣyānvinayaśālinaḥ । adhyāpayantamabhyetya svavṛttānta nyavedayat ।। sumantuḥ pailasahito vaiśampāyanajaiminī । te vyāsaśiṣyāḥ pramadātpariṣasvajire śukam ।।
kadācidatha yāteṣu kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ gurum । vaiśaṃpāyanamukhyeṣu samāmantrya mahītalam ।। eka eva śukastasthau tatra dhyānaparāyaṇaḥ । adhīyānaḥ paraṃ brahma vyastaṃ vyāsena dhīmatā ।।
atha pravāti pavane kṛte cādhyayane śukaḥ । samīraṇagatīstāstāḥ śuśrāva guruṇoditāḥ ।। divyo vāyuḥ samānākhyastasyodānaḥ suto balī । vyānaśca tasya tanayaḥ khyāto apānaśca tatsutaḥ ।।
tatsaṃbhavaḥ prāṇanāmā teṣāṃ sapta gatikramāḥ । karma caiṣāṃ bahuvidhaṃ nāmnā sadṛśamucyate ।। pravaho nāma tadrūpo dhūmābhraprerako anilaḥ । āvaho nāma pavanastaḍidvibhramakṛnmuneḥ ।।
jalaṃ vahati megheṣu yaścodīrayati grahān । udvaho nāma sa jñeyaḥ sarvasāgaraghasmaraḥ ।। vimānavāhī devānāṃ saṃgarjaḥ saṃvahābhidhaḥ । vyomagaṅgāmbudhartā ca nivahaḥ pañcamo anilaḥ ।।
pūrayatyamṛtenenduṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ parivahaḥ smṛtaḥ । antyo antakṛcca bhūtānāṃ ghoro vāyuḥ parāvahaḥ ।। sa eva vāyurniḥśvāso vahatsveteṣu no pate t । etaduktvā nabhogaṅgāṃ kṛṣṇadvaipāyane gate ।।
śukramekākinaṃ prītyā nāradaḥ samupāyayau । ādarādvyāsatanayastaṃ praṇamya sukhasthitam ।। apṛcchadaihikaṃ śreyaḥ pṛṣṭastena sa cābravīt । vidyācakṣustapaḥ satyaṃ tyāgarāgau sukhāsukhe ।।
krodhaśca mṛtyurityetadyo vetti na sa śocati । ahiṃsā dhāma dharmasya duḥkhasyāyatanaṃ spṛhā ।। saṅgatyāgaḥ padaṃ mukterbhogābhyāso gṛhaṃ śucaḥ । viprayoge mahāñśoṣastāpakṛdyaiḥ prajāyate ।।
āpātaramaṇīyāṃstānbhāvānsādhurna cintayet । bahu manyena na dhanaṃ saṃtoṣaṃ śamamāsthitaḥ ।। saṃsārasāravaicitryaṃ gaṇayanbahubādhakam । na vismayaṃ na saṃtāpaṃ vānurāgaṃ bhajeta ca ।।
alasā dīrghasūtrāśca dṛśyante vibhavairyutāḥ । īhamānāśca dakṣāśca na kvaciddhanabhāginaḥ ।। anicchatāṃ saṃtatiṃ ca jāyante bahavaḥ sutāḥ । labhante putrakāmāśca pātaṃ vā naiva vā sutam ।।
durjarāḥ sahasā yasmiñjīryante kṣipramāsthitāḥ । tasminnevodare garbho māsāndaśa vivardhate ।। vyādhidagdhā vipadyante narā vaidyaśatairvṛtāḥ । rogānatitarantyanye rathyākardamaśāyinaḥ ।।
rūpabuddhivihīnānāṃ dāsāḥ svākṛtayo budhāḥ । śocantyanyatra vidhavā gatabhāryāstathā kvacit ।। ityevaṃ vividhāṃ māyāṃ kalayannakhilāṃ dhiyā । bhavasvabhāvavairī syānna tu sajjeta paṇḍitaḥ ।।
nāradeneti kathitaṃ niśamya vyāsanandanaḥ । dhyāyansaṃsārasaraṇiṃ nirvedānna dhṛtiṃ yayau ।। sarvatyāgadhṛtodyogaḥ sa samāmantrya nāradam । vyāsametya sarittīre vavande harṣanirbhaḥ ।।
tasmai nivedya vinayānnirvedaṃ gatavāsanaḥ । pradakṣiṇīkṛtya guruṃ gantumabhyudyayau śukaḥ ।। kṣaṇaṃ putra pratīkṣakha yāvattvaddarśanāmṛtaiḥ । prīṇāmi nirbharaṃ cetastamityūce pitā tataḥ ।।
nirakṣepaḥ sa gatvātha samāruhya gireḥ śiraḥ । niḥśabdaḥ sa same deśe sarvajñaḥ samupāviśat ।। ullaṅghanākrameṇaiva granthibandhānvimucya saḥ । tejasyekarase tejo dhṛtvā hemnīva kāñcanam ।।
raviṃ vāyuṃ jalaṃ bhūmiṃ praviśya gaganaṃ tathā । viśvāviṣkārakalayā śūnyāśūnyasamāśrayaḥ ।। vihasyotpatya sahasā saśarīro apyadehavat । samīravadasaktāṅgaḥ khe yayau vainateyavat ।।
taṃ prāptaṃ paramāṃ siddhiṃ devagandharvayoṣitaḥ । avākiranpuṣpavarṣaiḥ sarve ca vyomacāriṇaḥ ।। so abravīddevatāḥ sarvā vicinvānasya māṃ pituḥ । pralāpinaḥ prativaco deyaṃ sarvābhirāśrame ।।
ityuktvā sa samullaṅghya kṣipramaṣṭavidhaṃ tamaḥ । tyaktvā rajaḥ saptavidhaṃ sattvaṃ cotsṛjya kevalam ।। ulkāpātaiḥ sa digdāhaiḥ kampite bhuvanatraye । nirvyañjanaṃ nirguṇaṃ ca brāhmaṃ tejaḥ samāviśat ।।
sa vrajanvipulāyāmaṃ dviśṛṅgaṃ divyabhūdharam । dvidhā vyadhādalagnāṅgastato devāḥ svayaṃ yayuḥ ।। atha mandākinītīre kacatkāñcanapaṅkaje । utphullodāramandārapārijātamanohare ।।
snānakelīratā loladṛśastridaśayoṣitaḥ । hemakumbhopamakucāḥ pīnoruśroṇimaṇḍalāḥ ।। śyāmaromalatākāntatanumadhyā vivāsasaḥ । vītarāgaṃ śukaṃ dṛṣṭvā tasthurvismayaniścalāḥ ।।
taṃ kāmakañcukottīrṇaṃ tāḥ samunmuktakañcukāḥ । kāntaṃ dadṛśurekāgramasaṃkocakuñcitāḥ ।। vātaskandhānatikramya yāte tasminsutapriyaḥ । tamanveṣṭuṃ samabhyāyādvyāsastūrṇaṃ vihāyasā ।।
hā putreti piturvācaṃ śrutvā sarvāntarātmatām । avāptaḥ śuddhacinmātro bhoḥśabdamakarocchukaḥ ।। śūnyākārasya śabdena tasya pratiravaṃ nagāḥ । cakruḥ saiva sthitirabhūtpratiśrutvā sa bhūbhṛtām ।।
līne tataḥ pare dhāmni śuke tanayavatsalaḥ । vyāso nyaṣīdaddyusarittīre hemaśilātale ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvāpsaraso vārikrīḍāsaktāḥ parasparam । gātre nidhāya vāsāṃsi hriyā saṃkocamāyayuḥ ।।
tataḥ śokasamākrāntaṃ tamapi jñānabhāskaram । sametyāśvāsya vidadhe vītaśokaṃ śivaḥ svayam ।। śukātipātanam ।। eka eva paro devaḥ ko vedya iti bhūbhujā ।
pṛṣṭo abravīcchāntanavo dhyātvā nārāyaṇaṃ hṛdi ।। nāradena purābhyetya badaryāśramamīśvaraḥ । nārāyaṇo darśanāya prārthitastamabhāṣata ।। viṣṇoravyaktarūpasya caturdhā vyaktarūpiṇaḥ ।
icchāmātrasamunmeṣo naraścāhaṃ ca nārada ।। ekāyanairekadevairakavratadharaiḥ sadā । sa vibhurdṛśyate yuktairjñānanirdhūtakalmaṣaiḥ ।। śvetadvīpamito gatvā viṣṇurūpānanāmayān ।
viṣṇudhyānaparāñśubhrānpaśya śrīvatsalakṣaṇān ।। iti śrutvā munirabhūttaccittastatparāyaṇaḥ । prayayau ca paraṃ draṣṭuṃ kāraṇaṃ viṣṇumavyayam ।। ekatena dvitenāpi tritena ca tapasvinā ।
vastrayajñasadasyairyaḥ śvetadvīpe purā stutaḥ ।। śvetadvīpaṃ samāsādya nārado rucirānnarān । dadarśa śaśikarpūratuṣārarajatāprabhān ।। tānprāṇamya sa sattvasthairmanasā taiśca vanditaḥ ।
divyairmantrapadairviṣṇuṃ tuṣṭāva racitāñjaliḥ ।। oṃ jaya ajita avyaya aprameya ananta acyuta aparimita acala acintya apratihata abhava mahāvibhava niratiśaya nirañjana nirlepa niṣprapañca nirupama nirvikāra nirguṇa nityodita viśva viśvarūpa viśveśvara viśvasamuddharaṇa śuddhasūkṣma dhrunava śāśvata śānta saṃvitsvarūpa paramānandamandira bhaktimandākinīmarāla svecchāśaktivyaktīkṛtanijaprasāra lakṣmīlatāvasanta madhuvadhūgaṇḍapāṇḍitākhaṇḍala kaustubhaprabhāracitakamalākucakuṅkumabhaṅga apariṣvaṅgasaṅgamākulīkṛtasvarbhānubhāminīloka daṃṣṭrendukalālekhāyitavasudhābhirāmamahāvarāha hiraṇyakaśipukānanadavānala vāmanalīlāsaṃpadavāmanīkṛtasuraiśvarya caraṇanakhamayūkhāyitasvarvāhinīpravāha kṣatrakṣayādhvaroddīpitakuṭhārānala daśavadanavadanakandukavinodānandita kāliyakulakamalinīkuñjara rukmiṇīkapoladantapattrīkṛtapāñcajanyaprabhāpura vidrumadrumāyitakaiṭabharudhirāruṇorustambha brahmapadmapadmākaraturagamukhakhalīnakhanakhanāyamānasāmavedoccāra । ityādibhiḥ stutiśatairdivyairguhyaiśca nāmabhiḥ । nānāvarṇaṃ tato apaśyajjayotīrūpaṃ sanātanam ।।
jitantādyena mantreṇa stūyamānaṃ sitairnaraiḥ । taṃ viśvavyāpinaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛtakṛtyo yayau muniḥ ।। ityevaṃ nāradādanyo na dadarśa tamīśvaram । so avyaktaḥ paramo viṣṇurbhūtānāṃ prabhavo avyayaḥ ।
anādinidhanaḥ śuddho vedyaḥ sūkṣmo nirañjanaḥ ।। nārāyaṇīyam ।। nivṛttadharmamākarṇya śāntaye dharmajanmanā । punarāśramiṇāṃ dharmaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ prāha suravrataḥ ।।
gaṅgātīre dvijaḥ kaścidatithiṃ gṛhamāgatam । kimagryaṃ sarvadharmāṇāmityapṛcchadudāradhīḥ ।। padmo nāma mahānnāgo naimiṣe gomatītaṭe । sa jānātīti vipreṇa sa pṛṣṭo atithirabravīt ।।
tatastadvacasā gatvā gomatītīramagryajaḥ । vāreṇa sūryarathagaṃ na dadarśa bhujaṅgamam ।। sthitvā tatra nirāhāro dināni katiciddvijaḥ । nāgaṃ dadarśa taṃ prāptaṃ dṛṣṭvā papraccha kautukam ।।
brūhi tāvadidaṃ nāga tvayā ravirathasthitau । divi dṛṣṭaṃ kimāścaryaṃ paścāddharma pravakṣyasi ।। ityākarṇyābravīnnāgo dṛṣṭaṃ mārtaṇḍavartmani । rathasya cakraṃ vāreṇa balena vahatā mayā ।।
aṃśuśākhāsahasreṣu raveḥ śakunayo yathā । tiṣṭhanti devāḥ siddhāśca munayaśceti kautukam ।। karairgṛhītvā tyajati payo bhūmau praviśya ca । paśyatyalakṣitaḥ sarvaṃ bhagavāniti kautukam ।।
sa bhittvā maṇḍalaṃ bhānostejasyeva samāviśat । tejastejasi saṃlīnaṃ dṛṣṭvāsmābhirdivākaraḥ । pṛṣṭaḥ ko ayamiti śrīmānharṣapūrṇo abravīdraviḥ ।। sa bhittvā maṇḍalaṃ bhānostejasyeva samāviśat ।
tejastejasi saṃlīnaṃ dṛṣṭvāsmābhirdivākaraḥ । pṛṣṭaḥ ko ayamiti śrīmānhar,pūrṇo abravīdraviḥ ।। uñchavṛttirayaṃ siddhaḥ kāpotīṃ vṛttimāśritaḥ । madīyaṃ dhāma yāto asāvityetadapi kautukam ।।
śrutveti nāgādvipro abhūtpraharṣavikacānanaḥ । avāntarakathāvāptasvābhidheyopadeśavāk ।। āmantrya pannagaṃ vipro vidhāya cyavanaṃ gurum । uñchavrato yayau siddhiṃ gīyamānaḥ surairdivi ।।
cyavanānnāradenaitattasmājjambhaladviṣā । śakrācca vasubhistebhyo mayā mattastvayā śrutam ।। mokṣadharmāḥ ।। śamaṃ vividhamākarṇya dharmarājaḥ pitāmaham ।
babhāṣe śokavivaśaścintayanbāndhavakṣayam ।। aho batāhaṃ saṃsāre dhuryaḥ kilbiṣakāriṇām । sarvasvajanasaṃhāre nīto daivena hetutām ।। jāyeta mādṛśaḥ ko anyaḥ sadṛśo mama duṣkṛtī ।
pitāmaha śarairyastvāṃ ghātayitvā nirīkṣate ।। dhanyaḥ suyodhanastāta dhiṅ māṃ puṇyairnirākṛtam । banadhūnāṃ tvatpradhānānāṃ yaḥ kṣaye sākṣitāṃ gataḥ ।। śaiśave kṣaumavasanaṃ yasyāṅke laḍatā mayā ।
mlāpitaṃ rājyalubdhena sa eva nihato bhavān ।। śrutvā yudhiṣṭhireṇaitadvaktuṃ śantanunandanaḥ । tamūce mā kṛthāḥ putra mithyaivānuśayavyathām ।। paratantramidaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsvayamanīśvaram ।
svakarmamudrito lokaḥ prāpnotyeva bhavābhavam ।। brāhmaṇī gautamī nāma putrakaṃ putravatsalā । daṣṭaṃ dadarśa sarpeṇa gatāsuṃ kānane purā ।। tāṃ dṛṣṭvā putraśokārtāṃ lubdhakor'junakābhidhaḥ ।
baddhvā taṃ sarpamādāya jagādābhyetya gautamīm ।। ayaṃ putrasya te hantā mayā baddho bhujaṅgamaḥ । brūhi yāvatkṣipāmyenaṃ vahnau śastreṇa hanmi vā ।। śrutvaitallubdhakavaco vivignā prāha gautamī ।
varākaḥ pannago nāyamajñānādvadharmahati ।। antavantyeva bhūtāni niyatāvadhi mudrayā । upayānti svayaṃ mṛtyuṃ hantā kaścinna kasyacit ।। tasmādasminna kopo me kutaḥ kope api nigrahaḥ ।
jaḍa vyādha vimuñcainaṃ hataḥ kālena me sutaḥ ।। ityukto apyasakṛdvyādhastayā sarpavadhe matim । na tatyāja yadā kopāttadā dīno avadatphaṇī ।। hato ayaṃ mṛtyunā bālo yo māṃ preritavānsvayam ।
asvatantrasya kā śaktistadā jñātikramānmama ।। pannagenetyabhihite lubdhakaḥ punarabravīt । kāraṇena tvayā sarpa nīto ayaṃ mṛtyunā śiśuḥ ।। na hi nāma svayaṃ kaścitkareṇākṛṣya mṛtyunā ।
nīto bhavadvidhā yāvadyātāḥ sarpa na hetutām । vadhyo asi sarvathā tasmādvināśe kāraṇaṃ śiśoḥ ।। iti bruvāṇe bahuśaḥ kopādvyādhe bhujaṅgamam । svayamanigrahānmṛtyurabhyetya tamabhāṣata ।।
nāhamasya śiśorhantā na cāyaṃ bhujago jaḍa । prerako bhagavānkālaḥ sarvaṃ kṣayati saṃkṣaye ।। kālena kalitāste te bhāvāstrailokyavartinaḥ । spṛśantyabhāvapadavīṃ bhavanti ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।
ityukte mṛtyunā kālaḥ svayametya tamabhyadhāt । nāhaṃ na mṛtyurno sarpaḥ prabhurbālanipātane ।। svakarmabhirayaṃ loko labhate nidhanodayau । karmasūtrairviceṣṭante narā yantramayā iva ।।
jāyate vardhate bhuṅkte prasūte modate punaḥ । jīryate kṣīyate vāpi na jantuḥ karmaṇā vinā ।। iti kālena kathite sarpaṃ tatyāja lubdhakaḥ । pṛthagyayuśca te sarve naṣṭaśokā ca gaiṃtamī ।।
ityevaṃ svakṛtaireva kṣīyante karmabhirjanāḥ । karmaṇā nidhanaṃ yātānmā śucaḥ pṛthivīdharān ।। gautamīsarpamṛtyulubdhakasaṃvādaḥ ।। gṛhāśrame kena mṛtyurvartamānena dharmataḥ ।
jitaḥ pāṇḍusuteneti pṛṣṭaḥ śāntanavo abravīt ।। ikṣvākuvaṃśajo rājā māhiṣmatyāmabhūtpurā । śrīmānsuyodhano nāma smarendradhanadopamaḥ ।। taṃ narmadā nadī dṛṣṭvā snātaṃ kamalalocanam ।
akāmayata kāmārtā vilāsalalitākṛtim ।। tasyāmajījanatkanyāṃ rājā rājīvalocanām । kāntāṃ sudarśanāṃ nāma nayanānandidarśanām ।। tāṃ yauvanavatīṃ kāle bhagavānvīkṣya pāvakaḥ ।
smarākulo narapati yayāce brāhmaṇākṛtiḥ ।। nirdhanāvajñayā tasmai tāṃ yadā na dadau nṛpaḥ । tadā tasya sa yajñe agniḥ prāyātkopādadarśanam ।। ṛtvigbhiratha saptārcirniyamena prasāditaḥ ।
svapne jagāda taṃ mahyaṃ kanyaiṣā dīyatāmiti ।। tataḥ pratyakṣavapuṣe tasmai rājā sudarśanāt । prahṛṣṭastanayāṃ prādātprāpya tatsaṃnidhiṃ makhe ।। rājñā tenārthito adyāpi māhiṣmatyāṃ hutāśanaḥ ।
āste sadā saṃnihitaḥ kṣapayansarvaviplavān ।। sudarśanāyāṃ nayo babhūvātha vibhāvasoḥ । kāntaḥ sudarśano nāma guṇaratnamahodadhiḥ ।। sutā moghavato rājñaḥ kāntāṃ moghavatīṃ yuvā ।
sa lebhe kṣīṇāvāṇasya navā śaktiṃ manobhuvaḥ ।। tayā saha kurukṣetre gṛhī dharmapade sthitaḥ । cakre mṛtyujaye yatnaṃ so arthikalpadrumastadā ।। abhagnapraṇayāḥ kāryāḥ sarvathārthimanorathāḥ ।
ityūce sa sadā jāyāṃ dharmasabrahmacāriṇīm ।। dharmādacyavatastasya cchidrapekṣī sadābhavat । pracchannaḥ sarvato mṛtyurna cāntaramavāptavān ।। tataḥ kadācididhmārthaṃ svayaṃ yāte sudarśane ।
atithiḥ kaścidabhyetya tadbhāryāṃ brāhmaṇo abravīt ।। ātithyaṃ kriyatāṃ subhru rājaputri mama tvayā । yadi dharmaḥ pramāṇaṃ te tanmāṃ bhaja sulocane ।। iti bruvāṇaḥ sa tayā vārito apyapairarvaraiḥ ।
tvāṃ ninā nārthaye kiṃcidityuvācāsakṛddvijaḥ ।। dharmyaṃ tataḥ sā vacanaṃ smṛtvā bhartuḥ pativratā । tathetyuktvākarotsarvaṃ brāhmaṇasya samīhitam ।। asminnavasare gehadvārametya sudarśanaḥ ।
ehītyāhūya dayitāṃ sotkaṇṭho api vyalambata ।। sā bhartrā sahasāhūtā na ca prāptā dvijāntikam । dolāvilolahṛdayā tasthau lajjākulā kṣaṇam ।। tato gṛhāntarādvipraḥ sudarśanamabhāṣata ।
iyaṃ mayā tava vadhūrarthitātithinā ratam ।। prāptā nādyāpi śayanaṃ prāptaśca tvaṃ gṛhādhipaḥ । kimatra manyase yuktamityuktvā virarāma saḥ ।। atrāntare channavapurmṛtyurādāya mudgaram ।
labdho avakāśa ityuktvā babhūvānandanirbharaḥ ।। tataḥ sudarśano vipramuvācāvikṛtāśayaḥ । niḥśaṅko madgirā brahmanramasva mama bhāryayā ।। ityukte vahniputreṇa gaganātsādhu sādhviti ।
śabdo babhūva vipulaḥ sahasā tridivaukasām ।। atithirviprarūpaṃ sa parityajya mahākṛtiḥ । uvāca mahasāṃ rāśiḥ prītyābhyetya sudarśanam ।। dharmo ahaṃ dampatī prāpto yuvāṃ jijñāsurāśrame ।
aṃkhaṇḍitaṃ ca yuvayordṛṣṭaṃ sattvamidaṃ mayā ।। adhṛṣṭa tejasā ceyaṃ tvadbhāryā kena laṅghyate । dvidhātmānaṃ vibhajyaiṣā yogenaughavatī nadī । bhaviṣyati kṣitau puṇyā nityaṃ tvāṃ cānuyāsyati ।।
ityuktvāntardadhe dharmo mṛtyuśca vimukho yayau । sa ca vīro divaṃ prāpa sabhāryaśca sudarśanaḥ ।। sudarśanopākhyānam ।। viśvāmitreṇa saṃprāptaṃ brāhmaṇyaṃ durlabhaṃ katham ।
pṛṣṭo yudhiṣṭhireṇeti gāṅgeyaḥ punarabravīt ।। kuśikasya purā rājñaḥ śrīmāngādhiḥ suto abhavat । putrī satyavatī nāma tasyābhūnmṛgalocanā ।। ṛcīkastāṃ munivaraḥ śulkalabhyāmavāptavān ।
hayānāṃ śyāmakarṇānāṃ sahasreṇenduvarcasām ।। sa tayā śīlaśālinyā yatnadārādhito muniḥ । yācitastu varaṃ tuṣṭaḥ putraṃ mātustathātmanaḥ ।। tvamaśvatthaṃ samāliṅgya tava mātāpyudumbaram ।
caruṃ ca prāpya maddattaṃ putriṇītyavadanmuniḥ ।। varamevaṃ samāsādya hṛṣṭā mātre nyavedayat । tadgirā vyatyayaṃ cakre vṛkṣayoḥ pāyase tathā ।। tacca jñātvā munirjāyāmuvāca jñānalocanaḥ ।
tvanmāturbrāhmaṇaḥ putraḥ kṣatrātmā te bhaviṣyati ।। tacchrutvā duḥkhasaṃtaptā yayāce sā muniṃ punaḥ । kṣatrācārastu me pautro mā putra iti mūrchitā ।। evamastviti tenokte lebhe satyavatī sutam ।
jamadagniṃ sutaścāsya rāmo abhūtkṣatriyocitaḥ ।। gādhipatnī ca kālena viśvāmitramajījanat । vṛkṣapāyasayoryo abhūdvyatyayādbrāhmaṇāgraṇīḥ ।। viśvāmitrotpattiḥ ।।
ānṛśaṃsyaguṇaṃ rājñā punaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ suravrataḥ । uvāca kānane pūrvaṃ ghanacchāyo abhavaddrumaḥ ।। sa viddho viṣadagdhena śarema mṛgagāminā । lubdhakena yayau śoṣaṃ spṛṣṭo dāvānalairiva ।।
taṃ parityajya yāteṣu niṣphalaṃ sarvapatriṣu । eka eva śukastaśthau sātaṃ prītiracañcalā ।। nidāghaploṣaparuṣe phalapumpavivarjite । sthitaṃ tatra śukaṃ vīkṣya śakro abhyetya tamabravīt ।।
svacchacchāyāphalādyeṣu vṛkṣeṣu vigatadyutiḥ । kiṃ tvayāyaṃ śritaḥ śākhī tyaktvainaḥ cara nirvṛtaḥ ।। athovāca śukaḥ śakraṃ nedaṃ sadṛśamucyate । samānā sukhaduḥkheṣu sajjanaiḥ saha saṃgatiḥ ।।
yatroṣitaṃ ca bhuktaṃ ca vihṛtaṃ ca yathāsukham । tasminkālahataiśvarye palāyante na sādhavaḥ ।। maghavānetadākarṇya toṣādvṛkṣaṃ sudhākaṇaiḥ । cakāra sahasoddīrṇapatrapuṣpaphalākulam ।।
ānṛśaṃsyātsa ca śukaḥ prayayau paramāṃ gatim । evaṃ dākṣiṇyasadṛśo nāparo vidyate guṇaḥ ।। śukaśakrasaṃvādaḥ ।। daivaṃ sapauruṣaṃ rājñā bhīṣmaḥ pṛṣṭo abravītpunaḥ ।
ubhayoḥ saṃgamaḥ siddhyai viyogo niṣphalo anayoḥ ।। anuptabīje kṛṣṭe api daivaṃ kṣetre karoti kim । pauruṣaṃ karma puruṣairyathā yatra yadā kṛtam । tathā tatra tadābhyetya visaṃvādo na dṛśyate ।।
dātṝṇāṃ puṇyaśīlānāṃ vratināṃ satyavādinām । dṛśyante dhanyatāstāstā rājyasvargatibhūtibhiḥ ।। daivapurukārīyam ।। ke pūjyā iti pārthena pṛṣṭo avādītsuravrataḥ ।
sadā dvijātayaḥ pūjyāste sarvatra parāyaṇam ।। narau janmāntare pūrvaṃ kapijambukatāṃ gatau । jātismarau dadṛśatuḥ śmaśānaṃ suhṛdau mithaḥ ।। tatroce vānaraḥ premṇā śṛgālaṃ svinnamānasaḥ ।
karmaṇā kena yāto asi śavamāṃsāśitāmiti ।। pratiśrutya mayā pūrvaṃ na vitīrṇaṃ dvijanmane । sārgālīṃ yonimāpannastenāhamiti so abravīt ।। etadeva śṛgālena pṛṣṭa provāca vānaraḥ ।
brāhmaṇānavamanyāhaṃ prayāntaḥ kapitāmiti ।। brāhmaṇātikrameṇaiva bhajante tāmasīṃ daśām । tasmātsarvātmanā viprāḥ pūjyāḥ kuśalamicchatā ।। brāhmaṇamāhātmyam ।।
asavarṇopadeṣṭāraḥ kiṃ na syuḥ śreyasāṃ padam । viprā iti punaḥ pṛṣṭo rājñā śāntanavo abravīt ।। purā vane śūdramunerbrahmarṣirabhavatsakhā । kadācitso arthitaḥ śrāddhe śūdreṇāgāttadāśramam ।।
pitṛkarmaṇi tasyāsau havyakavyopadeśakṛt । pūrvaṃ śeṣāṃ vṛsīmetāṃ kuruṣvetyavadanmuniḥ ।। tataḥ kālena mahatā kṣapayitvā kalevaram । karmaśeṣopabhogāya tau janmāntaramāpatuḥ ।।
sa sūdro abhūtkṣitipatiḥ sa brahmarṣiḥ purohitaḥ । tasya rājño abhavallaptajñāno naṣṭākhilasmṛtiḥ ।। svastipuṇyāhavādeṣu nṛpo jātismaraḥ satām । sadā jahāsa taccāsau nṛpaṃ papraccha lajjitaḥ ।।
pṛṣṭaḥ śapathadānena bhūpatirhāsakāraṇam । purohitaṃ rahaḥ prāha śūdro ahamabhavaṃ purā ।। brahmarṣiśca bhavānmahyamupadeśaṃ vyadhātsakṛt । tenādya suravandyo api prāpto asyanucitāṃ daśām ।।
śrutvaitatsahasā smṛtvā tapase sa yayau muniḥ । evaṃ naivopadeṣṭā syādavarāṇāṃ dvijottamaḥ ।। gurūpadiṣṭam ।। kaḥ śriyo bhājanamiti kṣmābhujā jāhnavīsutaḥ ।
pṛṣṭaḥ prāha hareragre rukmiṇīṃ śrīḥ purābhyadhāt ।। subhageṣu pragalbheṣu dakṣeṣūjjvalakarmasu । jitendriyeṣu vīreṣu prītyā me śāśvatī sthitiḥ ।। utsekalobhasaṃtrāsadainyakrodhavinākṛtāḥ ।
kṛtajñāḥ kelisadanaṃ sadācārāḥ sadā mama ।। pativratāmakalahāmalaulyāmakutūhalām । aviprakīrṇabhāṇḍāṃ ca gatanidrāṃ bhaje striyam ।। matteṣu kuñjarendreṣu hayeṣu vṛṣabheṣu ca ।
phullāravindavṛndeṣu śaraccandrakareṣu ca ।। nadīṣu haṃsahāsāsu rājadrājaraṇeṣu ca । vaneṣu munipuṇyeṣu yajñeṣu ca vasāmyaham ।। etacchrutvā punarbhīṣmamapṛcchatpāṇḍunandanaḥ ।
sparśādhikyaṃ kimu strīṇāṃ nṛṇāṃ vā saṃgameṣviti ।। so abravīdabhavadyajvā bhṛṅgāśvo nāma bhūpatiḥ । yaśaḥ kusumavallīṣu yo abhūtsaṃtatamādhavaḥ ।। pratikūlaṃ sa śaktasya yajñamagniṣṭutaṃ punaḥ ।
ājahāra jagāmāsya śatrutāṃ yena vāsavaḥ ।। sa kadācinmṛgaprepsurvājinā vipine vrajan । indreṇa mohito vatsa nājñāsīttṛṣṇayārditaḥ ।। so apaśyadagre vipulaṃ saraḥ sphaṭikanirmalam ।
lolakalloladolāṅkaṃ keliveśma himatviṣaḥ ।। tasminsa sahasā snātaḥ pāyayitvā turaṅgamam । abhavallalanārūpaḥ pīnaśroṇipayodharaḥ ।। sa lajjāduḥkhavivaśo gatvāśvena nijāṃ purīm ।
nivedya nijavṛttāntaṃ rājye putraśataṃ vyadhāt ।। strīrūpaḥ so atha vijanaṃ tyaktarājyastapovanam । prayayau kalayannantarvidherutsāhavāmatām ।। tatra taṃ kāminīrūpamakāmayata tāpasaḥ ।
patanti ṣaṭpadāstatra yatra yatra sarojinī ।। tasmādasūta putrāṇāṃ sa śataṃ balaśālinām । kāntāvapurabhūnnityaṃ teṣu cātyantavatsalaḥ ।। pūrvaputrānathābhyetya puṃstvajātānuvāca saḥ ।
strītvajātaiḥ sutaistaistairvasudhā saha bhujyatām ।। tadgirā miśratāṃ yātaṃ tataḥ putraśatadvayam । bubhuje bhuvamamlānayaśovikramaśāsanām ।। atrāntare samabhyetya viprarūpī śatakratuḥ ।
bhedena rājaputrāṇāṃ vidadhe kalahodayam ।। tataste yudhi saṃnaddhā rājyahetoḥ parasparam । kṛtvā sainyakṣayaṃ ghoraṃ niḥśeṣāḥ pralayaṃ yayuḥ ।। bhedātprayāte nidhanaṃ yudhi putraśatadvaye ।
bhṛṅgāśvo lalanārūpaḥ śuśoca karumasvanam ।। tamindro brāhmaṇavapurdṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca tatkathām । pralīnamanyuḥ kāruṇyāduvāca vihasanmuhuḥ ।। śakro ahaṃ tava putrāste mayā vipriyakāriṇaḥ ।
bheditā nādhunā vairamāpanne tvayi me nṛpa ।। putrāṇāṃ śatamekaṃ te madvarādadya jīvatu । yattvamicchasi jātaṃ prāk puṃsaḥ strīvapuṣo athavā ।। ityukte devarājena bhṛṅgāśvastamayācata ।
jīvitaṃ strītvajātānāṃ putrāṇāṃ praṇatānanaḥ ।। tamabravītsurapatiḥ puṃstvajātānkathaṃ sutān । tyaktvā strītvaprajāteṣu putreṣu snihyati bhavān ।। iti pṛṣṭo maghavatā babhāṣe strīvapurnṛpaḥ ।
snehavātsalyarāgāṇāṃ lalanā eva mandiram ।। śrutvaitadavadacchakraḥ sarve jīvantu te sutāḥ । strīrūpaṃ tu parityajya puruṣo bhava madvarāt ।। ityukto pārthivo avādītstrītvaṃ naiva tyajāmyaham ।
strīṇāṃ sparśeṣu yā prītiḥ sā puṃbhirlabhyate kutaḥ ।। daivātsamanubhūyedaṃ suciraṃ prakṛtidvayam । etāvadeva jāne ahaṃ yatprīterbhājanaṃ striyaḥ ।। kāmasya sāraṃ surataṃ ratasya sparśāmṛtaṃ tacca sulocanānām ।
sarvātmanā nirvṛtijīvaśūnyaṃ bhave bhave jīvitameva kāntāḥ ।। yathārthamiti tenoktaṃ niśamya vibudhādhipaḥ । jagāma jīvayitvāsya prītaḥ putraśatadvayam ।। bhṛṅgāśvopākhyānam ।।
śrutvaitaddharmatanayaḥ punargāṅgeyamabravīt । māhātmyaṃ śrotumicchāmi devasya tripuradviṣaḥ ।। iti pṛṣṭo narendreṇa vyājahāra pitāmahaḥ । māhātmyaṃ devadevasya vaktumarhati keśavaḥ ।।
harireva haraṃ vetti haro vetti tathā harim । ekaiva mūrtiranayoḥ kāraṇāddvaitamāśritā ।। iti devavratenokte murārirdhramajanmanā । pṛṣṭaḥ śaśāṅkacūḍasya prabhāvaṃ prayato avadat ।।
putrārthinī jāmbavatī priyā provāca māṃ purā । pradyumnasadṛśaṃ deva tvattaḥ putraguṇocitam । prāptumicchāmi saṃkalpaḥ pūryatāmeṣa me tvayā ।। ityukto ahaṃ dayitayā tayā bālamṛgīdṛśā ।
dhyātvā muhūrtaṃ putrārthī prayātamupasevanam ।। athāruhya gireḥ śaṅke purā munitapovanam । apaśyaṃ tejasāṃ rāśimupamanyuṃ nijāśrame ।। prahṛṣṭaṃ jyeṣṭhavayasaṃ pinākivarabhūṣitam ।
dīptaṃ tapobhirvividhaiḥ pūrṇalāvaṇyavigraham ।। praśāntaramaṇīyena satvenānandadāyinā । kirantaṃ madhurodāranirvāṇāmṛtavāhinīm ।। taṃ vilokya praṇamyāhaṃ pūjāmādāya tatkṛtām ।
tatsaṃbhāṣaṇasaṃjātaparānandamayo abhavam ।। sa māmuvāca praṇataṃ prītyā jñānavilocanaḥ । devaṃ giriśamārādhya tulyaṃ putramavāpsyasi ।। te te trailokyajayinaḥ sukeśipramukāḥ purā ।
śrūyante śaṃkaravarātprāptāḥ śakrādhikaṃ padam ।। purāsminvyāghrapādasya maharṣeḥ piturāśrame । sakṛdāsvādya gokṣīraṃ yācitā jananī mayā ।। payaso asaṃbhavānmātrā dattaṃ piṣṭarasaṃ tataḥ ।
pītvāhaṃ virasaṃ duḥkhādabhavaṃ sāśrulocanaḥ ।। athābravīnmāṃ jananī vane putra payaḥ kutaḥ । śrīkaṇṭhaṃ na hyanārādhya labhyate abhimataṃ kvacit ।। iti māturvacaḥ śrutvā prayāto asmi tapovane ।
yatnādakaravaṃ tīvraṃ tapo vārṣasahasrikam ।। nānyataḥ prārthaye śakravaraṃ prāptamapi svayam । pīyūṣakiraṇottaṃsāddevādanyatra dhūrjaṭeḥ ।। tenālaṃ surarājyena kiṃ mokṣeṇāpi tena me ।
nirvyājabhaktidayito dātā yasminna śaṃkaraḥ ।। ityukto bahuśaḥ śakro mayā bhargānurāgiṇā । rūpamaindraṃ parityajya babhūva vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ ।। śūlinaṃ jaṭinaṃ devaṃ vīkṣya candrakalādharam ।
abhavaṃ nirbharānandaprasaradbāṣpanirjharaḥ ।। tataḥ stuto mayā śaṃbhurmahyaṃ kṣīrodadhiṃ dadau । ādadhe cāśrame tasminsaṃkalpānmama saṃnidhim ।। taṃ tvamārādhya varadaṃ tapasā pārvatīpatim ।
labhakha tanayaṃ kṛṣṇa tasyātmā tvaṃ sa vā tava ।। uktvaivamupamanyurmāṃ dīkṣitaṃ śivaśāsane । ādideśa tapoyoge rahasyaṃ gṛhyatāmiti ।। mantreṇa tadvitīrṇena tapasā ca samāhitaḥ ।
tato apaśyamahaṃ kāle devaṃ candrārdhaśekharam ।। meghajālasamārūḍhaṃ vyomni somaśatojjvalam । taṃ vilokyābhinandyāhaṃ stutvā harṣaparo abhavam ।। tato yathepsitāndattvā varānmahyaṃ maheśvaraḥ ।
antardadhe sudhāpūrairāpūryeva diśo daśā ।। athopamanyurmāmetya prakṛṣṭaṃ hṛṣṭamabravīt । taṇḍiproktāni nāmāni śṛṇu mādhava dhūrjaṭeḥ ।। taṇḍirnāma muniḥ pūrvaṃ guhyairgītaiḥ svayaṃbhuvā ।
trinetraṃ prayataṃ nāmnāṃ tuṣṭāva daśabhiḥ śataiḥ ।। sthāṇo sthirasthite śaṃbho śarva bhāno varaprada । hara rudra smarārāte viśva viśveśvareśvara ।। bhava bharga śivāśvāsa bhavānīvallabha prabho ।
śaśāṅkaśakalottaṃsa śiva śānta maheśvara ।। namastubhyaṃ jagatsargāsthitisaṃhārakāriṇe । brahmopendrendravapuṣe triguṇāya trimūrtaye ।। iti stutipadairdivyairvedaproktaiśca nāmabhiḥ ।
sahasrasaṃkhyaiḥ sa munistuṣṭāva śaśiśekharam ।। evamīśvarasaṃbaddhāḥ kṛtvāhaṃ muninā kathā । agamaṃ garuḍārūḍho dvārakaṃ harṣanirbharaḥ ।। jāmbavatyāstataḥ śrīmānvaṃśamuktāmaṇiḥ sutaḥ ।
sāmbo abhavadguṇānyasya jānīṣe dharmanandana ।। iti kṛṣṇena kathitaṃ śrutvā bhīṣmasabhāsadaḥ । munayo manasā devaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ vavandire ।। meghavāhanaparva ।।
capalāḥ sahacāriṇyaḥ kathaṃ jāyā nṛṇāmiti । punaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ kṣitibhujā babhāṣe jāhnivīsutaḥ ।। aṣṭāvakro muniḥ pūrvaṃ vivāhārthī sulocanām । apaśyatsuprabhāṃ nāma vadanyasya muneḥ sutām ।।
indukundāṅkurākārasukumāratarākṛtim । sa tāmālokya sumukhīṃ yayāce sotsuko munim ।। taṃ vadanyo avadadgaccha viśālāṃ diśamuttarām । atikramya kuberasya bhavanaṃ bhavasevitam ।।
tataḥ pratinivṛttāya tubhyaṃ dāsyāmi suprabhām । ityuktaḥ sa vadanyena prataśte tāṃ diśaṃ śanaiḥ ।। tato himādrimullaṅkhya bāhudāṃ ca mahānadīm । aśoke vimale snātvā rudrāṇī kūpamāptavān ।।
sa kailāsataṭaṃ prāpya dadarśa dhanadālayam । hemapaṅkajinītīralasatkalpalatāvanam ।। sādaraṃ pūjitastena rājñā vaiśravaṇena saḥ । uvāsa vatsaraṃ sāgraṃ vilāsamaṇiveśmasu ।।
ciramapsarasāṃ nṛttairgītairgandharvayoṣitām । prītimāsādya vipulāmāmantrya dhanadaṃ yayau ।। to girīndrānullaṅghya samāṃ maṇimayīṃ bhuvam । avatīrya ghanacchāyaṃ pāpa ratnalatāvanam ।।
hemapuṣkariṇīśīte sa tasmindivyakānane । maṇimauktikajālāṅgaṃ dadarśodāramandiram ।। so atha dvārāgramabhyetya tasya vaiḍūryaveśmanaḥ । prāpto ahamatithirdūrādityūce saṃśrayāśayā ।।
tataḥ sapta vinirgatya kanyāḥ kamalalocanāḥ । divyabhūṣaṇasaṃpannāstasyātithyaṃ pracakrire ।। gṛhaṃ praveśitastābhirhemaratnāsanojjvalam । dadarśa maṇiparyaṅke vṛddhāṃ bhāsvarabhūṣaṇām ।।
tayā madhuravādinyā prāpya nirdiṣṭamāsanam । gataklamaḥ kṣaṇaṃ tasthau munirvismayaniścalaḥ ।। dinānte so atha tāḥ prāha yāntu sarvāḥ svamālayam । ekaiva śāntahṛdayā paricaryāṃ karotu me ।।
ityukte muninā sarvāḥ prayayustāḥ sulocanāḥ । ekaiva jaratī tatra sthau śaśisitāṃśukā ।। aṣṭāvakro atha suṣvāpa śayane sparśaśālini । vitānālambimandāradāmni svacchottaracchade ।।
dvitīyaśayanādvṛddhā samutthāya tataḥ śanaiḥ । muneḥ śayyāntikaṃ pāyānnibhṛtā brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। kampamānatanuḥ sātha śayyāmāruhya viklavā । muniṃ śītāpadeśena nibiḍaṃ pariṣasvaje ।।
āliṅgyamānaḥ sa tayā tasthau kāṣṭhamivācalaḥ । paradārapariṣvaṅgaśaṅkāsaktacitāśayaḥ ।। sātha taṃ sparśavimukhaṃ praṇayānmañjuvādinī । uvāca bhogasaṃkalpabhaṅgaṃ mā me kṛthāḥ prabho ।।
idaṃ me ratnabhavanaṃ cāruratnalatāvanam । tvadadhīnamakasmānme ceto hi ramate tvayi ।। na te doṣo asti matsaṅge tyājyā naiva tu yoṣitaḥ । durgamaṃ nābhijānanti gaṇayanti na ca śramam ।।
prayānti puruṣāneva rāgavāgurayā striyaḥ । naitāḥ kulānurodhena nivartante na cerṣyayā ।। rāmāsvaruddhaprasaraḥ sarvathā makaradhvajaḥ । strī satīti pravādo ayamekasakteti kā kathā ।।
narāntaraṃ prayāntyetā nimnāmnamivāpagāḥ । manmathapreritā nārī vimarṣaṃ bhajate katham ।। yāsāṃ prāṇapaṇenāpi vallabhaṃ suratāmṛtam । ityarthamāno api tayā nābyanandatsa tāṃ muniḥ ।।
anyedyurapi sā rātrau tathaiva tamabhāṣata । bhajasva svayamāyātāṃ duḥsaho me smarajvaraḥ ।। niṣedho rativāñchāsu nidhanaṃ kila yoṣitām । ityuktvā nirvikāraṃ taṃ sā dṛṣṭvā punarabraravīt ।।
māmuttarāṃ diśaṃ viddhi strīvṛttāntaṃ pradarśitam । adhunā tāṃ vadanyasya gatvā prāpnuhi kanyakām ।। etadākarṇya sa munistāmāmantrya savismayaḥ । śanaiḥ pratiyayau jñānastrīvṛtto nijamāśramam ।।
tato vadanyamabhyetya strīvṛttāntaṃ nivedya tam । avāpodvāhavidhinā vitīrṇāṃ tena suprabhām ।। aṣṭāvakradiksaṃvādaḥ ।। atha vidhyanugaṃ śrāddhaṃ pātrāpātrakramaṃ tathā ।
rājñā gatiṃ ca tīrthaṃ ca pṛṣṭaḥ śāntanavo abravīt ।। yajeta devānpūrvāhṇe śuciḥ śuklo jitendriyaḥ । maṅgalālaṃkṛtaṃ sragvī bhogauḥ suddhairmanoramaiḥ ।। vitryaṃ karmāparāhṇe tu kuryātprayatamānasaḥ ।
teṣu teṣu ca kāleṣu deśeṣu ca yatāvidhi ।। deśakālādirahitaṃ śvāvalīḍhaṃ rasacyutam । kīṭakośāsthisaṃspṛṣṭaṃ śrāddhamaśnanti rākṣasāḥ ।। unmattāḥ kṛpaṇāḥ kāṇāḥ kuṣṭhino vṛṣalīvarāḥ ।
cikitsakā vārdhuṣikā gītanṛtyādijīvinaḥ ।। hīnādhikāṅgā guravo brahmavikrayiṇo anṛtāḥ । anagnayaḥ sattrabhujaḥ kṣattriyāḥ kṣetrajīvinaḥ ।। piśunā vratahīnāśca vedavidyāvivarjitāḥ ।
parihāryāḥ sadā vipāḥ śrāddhāghnā haitukāstathā ।। parasvahāriṇāṃ puṃsāṃ paradārābhigāminām । bhagnavratānāṃ lubdhānāṃ niṣiddhakrayyajīvinām ।। vṛtticchedaṃ suhṛcchedaṃ bhartṛcchedaṃ ca kurvatām ।
vihitācārahīnānāṃ nirayo nilayo akṣayaḥ ।। karuṇāpūrṇamanasāṃ tyāgināṃ pātravarṣiṇām । kṣamāvatāmāśramiṇāṃ prapākūpasabhākṛtām ।। yājināṃ tīrthapūtānāṃ viduṣāṃ satyavādinām ।
madyamāṃsaviraktānāṃ svargamārgo nirargalaḥ ।। gautamena purā pṛṣṭaḥ sarvavinmuniraṅgirāḥ । uvāca puṇyaṃ tīrthānāṃ tapoyogena sasmitam ।। candrabhāgā vitastā ca kaśmīrasaritastathā ।
munitulyāṃ gatiṃ puṃsāṃ prayacchantyeva sevitāḥ ।। bhāgīrathīṃ kauśikīṃ ca rāmaṇīṃ narmadāṃ tathā । prayāgaṃ nandikuṇḍaṃ ca vipāśaṃ mānasaṃ saraḥ ।। puṇyatīrthāni cānyāni naraḥ prāpya jitendriyaḥ ।
sarvatīrthaphalaṃ dātā labhate prāgupoṣitaḥ ।। gaṅgā tu sarvatīrthānāṃ pravaraṃ tīrthamucyate । asthimātre yayā spṛṣṭe nṛṇāṃ svargatirakṣayā ।। na te deśā na te śailā na te janapadāḥ kṣitau ।
patākā yasya puṇyasya jāhnavī na vibhāvyate ।। kimapāyamayairyajñaiḥ kiṃ tapobhiḥ śramapradaiḥ । jahnukanyāpayaḥpūtaṃ yadi puṇyavatāṃ vapuḥ ।। vyomaśrīmauktikalatā śrīkaṇṭhottaṃsamālikā ।
yātā smṛtipadaṃ yeṣāṃ bhaṅgāyaivākhilainasām ।। gaṅgājalena spṛṣṭānāṃ phalamalpaṃ surālayaḥ । śiloñchavṛttinā pūrvaṃ siddhaḥ pṛṣṭo abravīditi ।। etadaṅgirasā proktaṃ niśamya kila gautamaḥ ।
smṛtvā vavande sānandaḥ puṇyāṃ mandākinīṃ muniḥ ।। āṅgirasīyam ।। kathaṃ prāpyaṃ manuṣyeṇa brāhmaṇyamiti bhūbhujā । pṛṣṭo devavrataḥ prāha brāhmaṇyaṃ durlabhaṃ nṛpa ।।
piturniyogādyajñārthaṃ mataṅgakhyo dvijanmanaḥ । vrajanvāhaṃ pratodena kharaṃ gāḍhamatāḍayat ।। gardabhī vyathitaṃ dṛṣṭvā putraṃ duḥkhāduvāca tam । brāhmaṇyaṃ nāsya tenaiṣa jātaścaṇḍālaceṣṭitaḥ ।
vahainamiti tacchrutvā priyaḥ papraccha tāṃ punaḥ ।। tayā niveditāṃ jātiṃ nijāṃ jñātvā sa duḥkhitaḥ । meroḥ śṛṅgādiva śvabhre patito vilalāpa saḥ ।। pitre nivedya tatpāpaṃ mātuḥ sa tapase vanam ।
