gatvā brāhmaṇyakāmo abhūtsthāṇubhūtaḥ śataṃ samāḥ ।। śakrādapi svayaṃ prāptānnaiva brāhmaṇyamāptavān । tato gatvā gayāṃ cakre sahasrābdaṃ paraṃtapaḥ ।। punaḥ punaḥ sa tapasā dhūmāyitajagattrayaḥ ।
indrādavāpa devatvaṃ na tu brāhmaṇyamuttamam ।। chandodeva iti khyātaḥ sa mataṅgābhidhaḥ purā । khecaro abhūnmṛgākṣīṇāṃ pūjyaḥ paramavallabhaḥ ।। indramātaṅgam ।।
vītahavyasya nṛpaterbrāhmaṇyaṃ śrūyate kila । tadvadeti punaḥ pṛṣṭo rājñā prāha pitāmahaḥ ।। vītahavyasutaiḥ pūrvaṃ hehayairbalavattaraiḥ । haryaśvo nāma samare kāśirājo nipātitaḥ ।।
kālena tasya putro api punastaireva saṃgare । sa devaḥ kāśinagare labdhalakṣyairnipātitaḥ ।। tatsuto api divodāsastaireva yudhi nirjitaḥ । bharadvājaprasādātsa lebhe putraṃ pratardanam ।।
sa vītahavyatanayānsarvānabhyetya saṃgare । jaghāna paramāstrajño bharadvājavaro arjitaḥ ।। vītahavyo hatasutaḥ pranaṣṭabalavāhanaḥ । pratardanenānusṛtaḥ prayayau śaraṇaṃ bhṛgum ।।
bhṛgorāśramamāsādya vītahavyavadhodyataḥ । pratardano muniṃ prāha muñcainamiti durmadaḥ ।। tacchrutvā kṣatriyo neha kaścitsarve dvijā vayam । ityuvāca bhṛgurbhītastato asatyādakampata ।।
kṣattrābhidhānātprabhraṣṭaṃ śatruṃ jñātvā pratardane । yāte bhṛgurvītahavyaṃ satyavāgbrāhmaṇaṃ vyadhāt ।। vītahavyopākhyānam ।। ke praṇamyā iti panaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ śāntanavo abravīt ।
svakarmadharmaniratā haṃsārāgavivarjitāḥ ।। praṇamyā brāhmaṇā eva pavitracaritavratāḥ । yaiṣāṃ kopaprasādābhyāṃ śoṣaḥ poṣaśca bhūbhujām ।। bhūmidevāḥ sadā pūjyā yatprasādāddhutāśanaḥ ।
havyaṃ kavyaṃ ca vahati kṛṣṇamityāha nāradaḥ ।। jeya balaṃ bhaye rakṣā bheṣajaṃ vyasanāmaye । paraloke astu vo viprāḥ śakramityāha śambaraḥ ।। brāhmaṇapraśaṃsā ।।
strīṇāṃ nisargalolānāṃ svabhāvaṃ pāṇḍusūnunā । pṛṣṭo durlakṣyacittānāṃ vyājahāra pitāmahaḥ ।। strīsvabhāvaṃ purā pṛṣṭā nāradena surāṅganā । jagāda pañcacūlākhyā yathārthaṃ śāpakampitā ।।
strī satī strīsvabhāvaṃ ca mādṛśī vaktumarhati । śāsanāttava bhītāhaṃ kiṃtu vakṣyāmi tattvataḥ ।। saṃgharṣakṣobhakāriṇyaḥ sodvegāḥ kaluṣāśayāḥ । mattā harantyeva vapurnimnagā iva nimnagāḥ ।।
apyanviṣṭā na labhyante saṃtyaktā na tyajanti ca । vāsanā iva saṃsāre mohanaikaratāḥ striyaḥ ।। prahasanti viṣādinyo hṛṣṭāḥ śocanti helayā । rāgiṇyo api priyaṃ ghnanti ko hi tāṃ vetti yoṣitam ।।
na kulena na mānena na dhanena na sevayā । maryādāmanuvartante lalanāścapalāśayāḥ ।। suveśaṃ subhagaṃ kāntaṃ tyaktvā paricitaṃ ciram । nindyenādṛṣṭapūrveṇa ramante svecchayā striyaḥ ।।
saṃbhāṣitāścenmadhuraṃ sasmitaṃ cedvilokitāḥ । yantritāḥ svajanenāpi tadā sādhyā na yoṣitaḥ ।। arthināmapyalābhena duḥkhadainyaśrameṇa vā । akasmādeva nārīṇāṃ satītvaṃ jāyate kvacit ।।
nānāpuruṣasaṃvāsahāsollāsavilāsinīm । veśyāyoṣāṃ nirīkṣante saspṛhaṃ kulayoṣitaḥ ।। niṣedhādeva nārīṇamabhilāṣo vivardhate । parasaṅgeṣvapathyeṣu bālānāmiva rogiṇām ।।
acchinnaprasaraḥ kāmo naivāsāṃ kṣamate dhṛtim । mitho yāvatpravartante puruṣāsaṃbhave striyaḥ ।। krūṃrāṇāṃ kṣaṇarāgāṇāṃ saṃdhyānāmiva yoṣitām । satatāsannadoṣāṇāṃ dhīmānko nāma viśvaset ।।
sarvathā na bhavatyeva kāruṇyamiva pāpinām । anutseka ivāḍhyānāmārjavaṃ hariṇīdṛśām ।। uparodhairbahuvidhairapi sādhvyo niyantritāḥ । kāntaṃ puruṣamālokya yāntyeva sahasārdratām ।।
suraśaṅkāspadamabhūtpurā vandyo vadhūjanaḥ । tataḥ surārthito dhātā kṛtyāsargādvyadhātstriyaḥ ।। lajjāṃ labhante lalanāḥ puṃsāṃ kautukavṛddhaye । patyurviśvāsanopāyaṃ kṛtakaṃ ca satīvratam ।।
nṛtyanti śocanti patanti yānti hasanti gāyanti vadanti yacca । tadyoṣitaḥ svapnasamānaceṣṭaṃ māyāmayaṃ sarvamasatyameva ।। nāradapañcacūḍāsaṃvādaḥ ।। tāḥ striyo lolamatayaḥ kathaṃ rakṣyā narairiti ।
pṛṣṭo yudhiṣṭhireṇāha punastripathagāsutaḥ ।। devaśarmāṃ muniḥ pūrvaṃ yajñārthaṃ gantumudyataḥ । śaśāsa śiṣyaṃ vipulaṃ bahumāyaṃ śatakratum ।। jñātvā ruciṃ śarīrāntaḥ praviśa tvaṃ samīravat ।
gātrairgātrāṇyavaṣṭabhya tasyāstasthau sa yatnavān ।। atrāntaraṃ samāsādya sahasrākṣaḥ samāyayau । sa dadarśa ruciṃ cārulocanāmacalāṃ punaḥ ।। hemastanorujaghanāṃ kāñcanīmiva putrikām ।
ākhaṇḍalamathāsādya sā saṃjātamanobhavā ।। vaktuṃ vipulasaṃruddhā na śaśāka sulocanā । ākīrṇahāsakusumā vilolālakaṣaṭūpadam । latāmiva nivātasthāṃ sakampakarapallavām ।।
dṛṣṭvā tāṃ vismitaḥ śakraḥ prāyādvipulatarjitaḥ । abhyetya devaśarmātha sarvaṃ tadbubudhe muniḥ ।। tasmādavāpya vipulastatastuṣṭādgurorvarān । cacāra kṛtakṛtyaḥ kṣmāṃ pūjyamāno nṛpairdvijaiḥ ।।
atrāntare svasurbhartrā ruciraṅgamahībhujā । nimantritā gṛhe apaśyadbhaginīṃ puṣpabhūṣitām ।। visṛṣṭastadgirā śiṣyaḥ puṣpārthaṃ devaśarmaṇā । dadarśa mithunaṃ ṣaṭ ca devinaḥ kitavānpathi ।।
teṣāṃ vivāde śuśrāva śapathaṃ vipulārjitān । sa lokānāpnuyādyaśca pracaletsaṃvidamiti ।। tacchrutvā duḥkhito abhyetya gurave sa nyavedayat । śaṅkamāno guruvadhūgātrasaṃsparśapātakam ।।
gurustamūce mithunamahorātraṃ taducyate । ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ ca kitavāste nṛṇāṃ karmasākṣiṇaḥ ।। na śakyā rakṣituṃ nāryo rakṣitā ca tvayā ruciḥ । asatyena tavodīrṇaṃ tasmānnaśyatu pātakam ।।
ityevaṃ rakṣaitā pūrvaṃ vipulena guroḥ priyā । na tvetā rakṣituṃ śaktaḥ kaścillolavilocanāḥ ।। vipulopākhyānam ।। vivāhadharmaṃ pṛṣṭo atha rājñā bhīṣṇo abravītpunaḥ ।
kanyā guṇavate deyā kulīnāyātirūpiṇe ।। śūdrāyeva śrutiḥ kanyā hīnāya pratipāditā । kuladvayaṃ dahatyeva tasmātpātraṃ vicārayet ।। aśāstroktaiḥ pariṇayairjāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ ।
saṃyogairviṣamaiḥ puṃsāṃ patati vyasane kulam ।। vivāhadharmāḥ ।। darśane sahavāse ca satāṃ pṛṣṭo mahībhujā । māhātmyaṃ ca gavāṃ bīṣmaḥ sarvajñaḥ punarabravīt ।।
gaṅgāyamunayormadhye cyavano antarjalavrataḥ । tasthau munīndraḥ suciraṃ sthāṇubhūto mahātapāḥ ।। āghrāya puṇyamāmodaṃ tasya kāruṇyaśālinaḥ । ālīya tasthurgātreṣu matsyā valayalīlayā ।।
tataḥ kālena mahatā jālenākṛṣya dhīvarāḥ । vipulaṃ matsyasaṃghātaṃ tanmadhye dadṛśurmunim ।। śaivālanālavalitaṃ śaṅkhikaṅkaṇamālitam । hariśmaśrujaṭāpiṅgaṃ tejasāmiva saṃcayam ।।
taṃ vīkṣya kampitāḥ sarve sahasā jālajīvinaḥ । nimīlitākṣaṃ jagaduḥ prasīda bhagavanniti ।। tataḥ sa karumāviṣṭo matsyeṣu sahavāsiṣu । niṣādānavadatpaśyandṛśānugrahavāñchayā ।।
vikrīya māṃ vimucyantāṃ yuṣmābhiḥ salilaukasaḥ । dayitāḥ sahavāsānme matsyā yūyaṃ ca darśanāt ।। ityukte muninā dāśāstūrṇaṃ gatvā mahībhuje । vepamānāḥ svavṛttāntaṃ nahuṣāya nyavedayan ।।
tataḥ svayaṃ sa nṛpatiḥ pūjāmādāya satvaraḥ । purohitaṃ puraskṛtya cyavanaṃ draṣṭumāyayau ।। kṛtapraṇāmaṃ nahuṣaṃ munirvīkṣya kṛtāñjalim । yathocitena mūlyena māṃ gṛhāṇetyacodayat ।।
dhīvarebhyaḥ sahasrāṇi koṭikoṭiśatāni ca । rājyārdhamathavā rājyaṃ dadānītyabravīnnṛpaḥ ।। naitanmamocitaṃ mūlyaṃ cintyatāṃ munibhiḥ saha । nṛpaṃ dāśeṣu kāruṇyādityuvācāsakṛnmuniḥ ।।
tato viṣaṇṇaṃ nahuṣaṃ śāpabhītamadhomukham । gavi jāto dvijavaro babhāṣe dhīmatāṃ varaḥ ।। mūlyaṃ munīśvarasyāsya tulyaṃ gaureva yatparam । tasmādenaṃ gavā rājangṛhāṇa bhava nirvṛtaḥ ।।
brāhmaṇenetyabhihite prahṛṣṭaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ । muktaye matsyasaṃghānāṃ gavā jagrāha bhārgavam ।। tato darśanavātsalyāccyavanaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ । dāśebhyaḥ pratijagrāha dhenuṃ tatkuśale sthitaḥ ।।
munīndreṇa gṛhītāyāṃ vidhivadgavi dhīvarāḥ । taddṛṣṭipātānmatsyāśca saśarīrā divaṃ gatāḥ ।। amṛtāyatanaṃ gāvaḥ pavitrā rudramātaraḥ । smṛtimātreṇa muṣṇanti kilbiṣaṃ kila dehinām ।।
cyavanopākhyānam ।। kuśikasya kṣitipaterjāto vipraḥ kathaṃ kule । bhṛgornṛpaśceti rājñā pṛṣṭo avādītsuravrataḥ ।। bhāvikathābhijñaścyavanastejasāṃ nidhiḥ ।
mandire pūjitastasthau kuśikasya mahīpateḥ ।। sa bhūbhujā sabhāryeṇa paricaryāvrate dhṛte । bhuktvā suṣvāpa niśceṣṭaḥ saptarātratrayaṃ muniḥ ।। pādasaṃvāhanaṃ tasya nirāhāro vadhūsakhaḥ ।
rājā cakāra nibhṛto nidrābhaṅgabhayākulaḥ ।। tato muniḥ samutthāya maunī gatvā manojavaḥ । antardadhe sabhāryeṇa nṛpeṇānusṛtaḥ pathi ।। tasminnantarhite rājā nirāhāro atimūrcchitaḥ ।
patitaḥ kṣaṇamāśvāsya viveśa svagṛhaṃ punaḥ ।। tau dampatī dadṛśaturmūkaṃ kāṣṭhamivācalam । ekapārśvena suptasya kṣapāstasyaikaviṃśatim । tasthatustau nirāhārau pādasaṃvāhane punaḥ ।।
pratibuddho atha tailena śatapātena bhubhujā । bhaktyā nirvartitasnāno bheje siṃhāsanaṃ muniḥ ।। tato nānāvidhaṃ bhojyaṃ rājayogyaṃ svayaṃ kṛtam । dattaṃ rājñā sabhāryeṇa dadāha bhṛgunandanaḥ ।।
punarantarhito bhūtvā punaḥ kṛtvāsya saṃnidhim । nirvikāraṃ sabhāryaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvābhūdvismito muniḥ ।। avikriyaṃ nirāhāraṃ sa rājānaṃ vadhūsakham । rathena sāṃyugīnena vaha māmityacodayat ।।
ityuktvā dampatī dhṛtvā tau rathe vicacāra saḥ । trikaṇṭhakakaṣāghātasaṃjātakṛtajokṣitau ।। adarśayattataścitrahemavallīmanoharam । svargaṃ sanandanodyānaṃ munistau mohayanmuhuḥ ।।
dṛṣṭanaṣṭairbahuvidhairmāyācaṭulavibhramaiḥ । muninā vihitairmohaṃ dampatī tau na jagmatuḥ ।। vepamānau nirāhārau dūrādhvaśramakarṣitau । tuṣṭaścirānamunivaro rathānmuktvā jagāda tau ।।
prīto ahaṃ yuvayorbhaktyā gṛhṇītamadhunā varam । pautraste brāhmaṇo rājanbhaviṣyati mahātapāḥ ।। tadvaṃśajairvirodho ayaṃ bhārgavānāmupasthitaḥ । tasmātkṣatriyavicchedadhiyā tvaṃ pīḍito mayā ।।
gataklamo nivṛttaśca pīyūṣairiva pūritaḥ । bhava madvacasā dhanyaḥ sabhāryaḥ pṛthivīpate ।। ityuktvāntarhite tasmiṃstasya kālena bhūpateḥ । ajāyata kule śrīmānvinaśvāmitrastaponidhiḥ ।।
bhārgavaśca yathā jāto rāmaḥ kṣatrakṣayo arjitaḥ । ṛcīkasya prabhāveṇa tanmayā kathitaṃ purā ।। cyavanakuśikasaṃvādaḥ ।। śrutvaitadbhūbhujā pṛthvīkṣayapātakaśaṅkinā ।
punaḥ pṛṣṭo avadadbhīṣṇo dānānāṃ phalamuttamam ।। tapasā labhyate sarvamācāreṇa damena ca । ānṛśaṃsyena satyena dānena ca samīhitam ।। dattvā vibhūṣitāṃ dhenuṃ kapilāṃ kāṃsyadohanīm ।
pṛthivīdānasadṛśaṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।। prayāti vasulokaṃ ca tiladhenuprado naraḥ । kanyābhūmipradaḥ śakralokamāsādya modate ।। bhūtābhayapradānaṃ tu dānānāṃ pravaraṃ smṛtam ।
nijābhimatadānaṃ ca sarvakāmaphalapradam । suvarṇadānena nṛṇāṃ kṣīyate kila pātakam ।। sarvaṃ sūte vasumatī dhatte ca nikhilaṃ jagat । jñeyaḥ sarvapradastasmāddātṝṇāṃ bhūmido varaḥ ।।
annaṃ śarīriṇāṃ prāṇāstasmātprāṇaprado annadaḥ । annadānasamaṃ loke nāstīti prāha nāradaḥ ।। pānīyadānamamṛtaṃ prāṇināṃ saṃpracakṣate । vicchāyatāpajvalitāḥ paraloke hi bhūmayaḥ ।।
tilapradānaṃ śaṃsanti kṣayāya nikhilainasām । tuṣṭo yamaḥ purā vipraṃ tilāndehītyacodayat ।। brahmasvavarjaṃ sarvasvaṃ dattvā durgāṇi saṃtaret । brahmasvaśalyaṃ hi nṛṇāṃ tīvrapātaṃ pracakṣate ।।
dvāravatyāṃ mahākūpe purā gulmatṛṇāvṛte । kṛkalāsaṃ mahākāyaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarvavṛṣṇayaḥ ।। sa taiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ samuddhartumaśaktairavadacchanaiḥ । nṛgo ahaṃ nṛpatirbrahmaśāpādyāto daśāmimām ।।
viprebhyo gṛhamedhibhyo nikharvāṇi purā gavām । hemakoṭiprado dattvā yāto ahaṃ nirvṛtiṃ parām ।। tataḥ kadācinmaddattadhenuṃ viprasya mandire । nijāṃ caurahṛtāṃ dṛṣṭvā jagrāha brāhmaṇo aparaḥ ।।
rājñā mameyaṃ prāgdattā hṛteyaṃ dasyunā paraḥ । evaṃ vivadamānau tau matsabhāmabhijagmatuḥ ।। tadvṛttāntamahaṃ śrutvā prārthanā bahuśastayoḥ । dhanairgobhirnarairaśvairyatnādakaravaṃ pṛthak ।।
tathāpyeko na tatyāja gāṃ pratigrahapālanāt । dvitīyaśca gṛhe jātāṃ tāṃ snehabhayakātaraḥ ।। atha kālena yāto ahaṃ dharmarājaniketanam । bahudānārjitāṃllokāndivyānaśrauṣamātmanaḥ ।।
kiṃtu brahmasvavibhraṃśānmamemāṃ kṛkalāsatām । śauridarśanaparyantāmādideśa svayaṃ yamaḥ ।। iti bruvāṇaḥ kṛṣṇasya daśā vidhvastapātakaḥ । nṛgo jagāma tridivaṃ tyaktvā tāṃ kṛkalāsatām ।।
nṛgopākhyānam ।। uddālakasya brahmarṣeḥ pituḥ kopānmahāmuniḥ । nāsiketābhidhaḥ prāṇāṃstatyājābhihato dṛśā ।। putraṃ nipatitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śāntakrodho muniḥ śanaiḥ ।
ajīvayanmantranidhiḥ kāruṇyātsāśrulocanaḥ ।। tataḥ svapnotthita iva prāptajīvo muneḥ sutaḥ । pitrā pṛṣṭo avadatsarvaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ yadyamamandire ।। ratnastambhaśatodāre pitṛrājasabhātale ।
avāpaṃ vipulāṃ pūjāṃ pādyamardhyaṃ tathāsanam ।। tatrāpaśyaṃ vimāneṣu sūryendudyutikāntiṣu । bhāsvarābharaṇasmerānnarānsukṛtaśālinaḥ ।। ghṛtakṣīrāmṛtajalā dṛṣṭāstatra mayāpagāḥ ।
hemābjapuñjakuñjāgrakūjanmaṇivihaṅgamāḥ ।। divyānbhogānmayā dṛṣṭvā pṛṣṭo vaivasvataḥ smayāt । etāḥ pīyūṣavāhinyaḥ keṣāṃ svecchāparigrahāḥ ।। yamo abravīdgopradānāmetāḥ kṣīraghṛtāpagāḥ ।
nādattvā puruṣo dhenuṃ paramāmṛtamaśnute ।। asaṃbhave gavāṃ yāvatsalilena tilena ca । ghṛtena vā kalpayitvā dhenuṃ dadyātsudhāśayā ।। godānasadṛśaṃ loke dānamanyanna vidyate ।
sādaraṃ māṃ putṛpatirjagādeti punaḥ punaḥ ।। ityukte nāsiketena munirmuniśatairvṛtaḥ । gopradānaṃ mahatpuṇyaṃ praśaśaṃsa muhurmuhuḥ ।। nāsiketopākhyānam ।।
sarvalokānatikramya gavāṃ lokaḥ prakaśate । yatsatyaṃ nirayāyante tatra svargasukhaśriyaḥ ।। gopradā eva golokaṃ prāyanti sukṛtojjvalāḥ । ityuvāca purā pṛṣṭaḥ śakreṇa kamalāsanaḥ ।।
vasiṣṭhādya munivarā nṛpā daśarathādayaḥ । surāśca śakrapramukhā gotulyaṃ na pracakṣate ।। nivāsārthaṃ purā gāvaḥ prārthitā bahuśaḥ śriyā । nigadya capalāsīti pradadurna pratiśrayam ।।
abhāṣata tato lakṣmīrbhavatībhiranādarāt । tyaktā nindyā bhaviṣyāmi tasmādyāce punaḥ punaḥ ।। athādiṣṭā śriyo gobhirhelayā gomaye sthitiḥ । tasmādetāḥ paraṃ puṇyaṃ pavitraṃ nāstyataḥ param ।।
gopradānam ।। hemadānaṃ dahatyevaṃ sarvapāpāni dehinām । tejo hi paramaṃ putra kāñcanaṃ jātavedasaḥ ।। purāhaṃ jāhnavīkūle śrāddhe piṇḍaprada pituḥ ।
apaśyaṃ śantanoḥ pāṇimutthitaṃ ratnakaṅkaṇam ।। piṇḍo mayā kuśeṣveva taṃ vilokya samarpitaḥ । tuṣṭastadā me janakaṃ svapne provāca māmidam ।। śāstrānuvartinā putra tvayā dhanyo asmi sūnunā ।
kanakaṃ dehi viprebhyo dānānāmuttamaṃ hi tat ।। jāmadagnyaḥ purā rāmaḥ kṛtvā niḥkṣatriyaṃ jagat । munibhirdāpito hema tasmātpāpādamucyata ।। tārakoṣaplutā devāḥ purā śītāṃśuśekharam ।
skandotpattimayācanta kathāṃ vijñāya bhāvinīm ।। tato gaurīpativīryaṃ vadane jātavedasaḥ । rativighnakṛto devastatyāja paramaṃ mahaḥ ।। vahninātha dhṛto garbhaḥ śrīmānsaṃvatsarāyutam ।
gaṅgāyāṃ nihitaḥ sāpi nidadhe taṃ girestaṭe ।। sa kārtikeyo bhagavāñjātaḥ śaravane śiśuḥ । surāṇāṃ śaktimānāsītsenānīstārakāntakaḥ ।। tasya janmani yatpūrvaṃ saṃjātaṃ jātavedasaḥ ।
mahī vasumatī yena tatsuvarṇaṃ pracakṣate ।। suvarṇotpattiḥ ।। atha śrāddhavidhiṃ pṛṣṭo rājñā śāntanavo abravīt । tilapradānaṃ vijñeyaṃ śrāddhaṃ madhughṛtāplutam ।।
māṣamatsyaiḍaśaśakacchāgavārāhaśākunaiḥ । pārṣatanyaṅgugavayamāhiṣairvai navairapi ।। māṃsairvivṛddhyā māsānāṃ kramātsaṃvatsaraṃ sadā । tṛptiṃ pitṝṇāṃ śrāddheṣu vadanti śrutikovidāḥ ।।
vāghrīṇasasya māṃsena dvādaśābdamuśanti ca । khaṅgamāṃsairlohapṛṣṭhaiḥ kālaśākaistathā kṣayam ।। na teṣāṃ pitaraḥ śocyāstrayodaśyāṃ madhāsu ca । varṣāsu vihitaṃ śrāddhaṃ pāyase na sasarpiṣā ।।
gāyakūpe vaṭatale chāyāyāṃ kuñjarasya vā । anantaṃ kalayantyeva śrāddhaṃ puṇyadineṣu ca ।। vidhinakṣatrayogeṣu kāmyaṃ śrāddhaṃ vinirdiśet । sadācāror'hati śrāddhaṃ vipro nirdeṣavigrahaḥ ।।
vaiśvadevena vidhinā saṃskṛtenana ca vahninā । rakṣyate brāhmaṇaiḥ śrāddhaṃ viṣṇupūjāpuraḥsaraiḥ ।। śrāddhe niṣiddhaṃ satataṃ saguḍaṃ lavaṇatrayam । ajājīhiṅgusauvīrapalāṇḍulaśunāni ca ।।
śrāddhavidhiḥ ।। dātṛpratigrahītṝṇāṃ viśeṣaṃ jagatībhujā । pṛṣṭaḥ surasaritsūnurdhyātvā punarabhāṣata ।। anāvṛṣṭihate kāle purā nirdagdhapādape ।
arundhatīsakhāśceruḥ śāntāḥ saptarṣayaḥ kṣitau ।। dāsaḥ paśusakho nāma dāsī caṇḍā ca tadvadhūḥ । tānevānuprayayatuḥ kṣuttṛṣṇāparipīḍitau ।। rājye surājñaḥ śaibyasya gatāsuṃ tanayaṃ tataḥ ।
munayaste kṣudhākrāntāḥ sthālyāṃ paktuṃ samudyayuḥ ।। atha rājā vṛṣādarbhirdṛṣṭvā vaiśravaṇopamaḥ । vyagrānmunīnviṣaṇṇātmā tānuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। yathecchaṃ gṛhyatāṃ mattaḥ sarvaṃ vā vividhaṃ vasu ।
jugupsā jananī vṛttirbhavadbhistyajyatāmiyam ।। ityukte bhūmipālena pratyūcurmunipuṃgavāḥ । tapaḥkṣayakaro rājanghoro rājapratigrahaḥ ।। pratigrahāgnigdhānāṃ sakṛdbrāhmaṇaśākhinām ।
kilbiṣājñānaśeṣāṇāṃ punaḥ puṇyaphalaṃ kutaḥ ।। etaduktvā parityajya stālīṃ te kānanaṃ yayuḥ । prāṇapīḍāpaṇenāpi pratigrahaparāṅbhukhāḥ ।। vane teṣāṃ vṛṣādarbhiḥ phalānyaudumbarāṇyatha ।
mantribhirhemagarbhāṇi kārayitvākṣipatpuraḥ ।। tānyapi jvalitānyeva bhītāstyaktvā munīśvarāḥ । yayurmithaḥ praśaṃsantaḥ puṇyasaṃtoṣaśīlatām ।। tatprakopādvṛṣādarbhirhutvā sapadi pāvakam ।
kṛtyāmutpādya bhayadāmādideśa munikṣaye ।। atrāntare te munayaścarantaḥ kānane sukhama । dadṛśuḥ pīvarākāraṃ parivrājaṃ śunaḥsakham ।। vilokya tamarundhatyā pṛṣṭāstatpuṣṭikāraṇam ।
ūcurmunivarā nāyaṃ kriyāvyagro yathā vayam ।। agnihotraṃ na vedāśca śāstrakanthā na duḥsahā । nānendhanaprayatnaśca na kalatraṃ na yācakāḥ ।। śunaḥsakhasya svacchandacāriṇaḥ sukhaśālinaḥ ।
śarīraṃ pīvaramidaṃ cintāśūnyasya vardhate ।। ityuktvā tena saṃjātasauhārdā munayo vane । dadṛśurnalinīṃ phullakamalotpalaśālinīm ।। vṛṣādarbhiprayuktā sā yātudhānībhi sārthinaḥ ।
tatra tānavadaddhorā rakṣāmi nalinīmimām ।। nivedya nijanāmāni gṛhyantāṃ tu mṛṇālikāḥ । ajñātanāmadheyānāṃ neha matsaṃnidhau gatiḥ ।। etadatriprabhṛtayaḥ śrutvā te munayaḥ kramāt ।
gūḍhanirvacanaistaistairnāmānyasyai nyavedayan ।। tulyākṣarapadakṣobhaṃ nāma teṣāṃ niruktataḥ । śrutvā niṣpratibhā kṛtyābhi sarakṣyāmavārayat ।। śunaḥsakhoditaṃ nāma punaḥ papraccha sā yadā ।
tadā kruddhāstu daṇḍena vidadhustāṃ ca bhasmasāt ।। tataḥ śaśikarākārāḥ samuddhṛtya mṛṇālikāḥ । tīre nikṣipya munayaḥ snātvā cakrurjalakriyām ।। athotthāya visāhārasādarāste śramākulāḥ ।
visāni tāni nāpaśyannyastāni nalinītaṭe ।। parasparaṃ śaṅkitāśca cakrire śapathaṃ kramāt । sahasābhimatocchedo mahatāmapi duḥsahaḥ ।। vṛthāpāko vṛthācāraḥ kūṭasākṣī niṣiddhakṛt ।
dṛśaṃsaḥ kāmacaritaścauro vedavivarjitaḥ ।। padā spṛśatu gāṃ vahnimapsu śleṣmābhiyacchatu । paradārābhigāmī ca garadaḥ somavikrayī । piśunaścāstvasau yena hṛtaṃ no visabhojanam ।।
ityukte munibhiḥ paścāttānuvāca śunaḥsakhaḥ । yājine chandasāṃ dhāmne śuddhāya brahmacāriṇe ।। deyātsa kanyakāṃ yena hatānyatra bhi sāni naḥ । śrutvaitadūcurmunayastvayā bhāṣitamīpsitam ।।
tvayaiva hṛtamasmākaṃ sarvathābhi sabhojanam । iti teṣu bruvāṇeṣu hasanprāha śunaḥsakhaḥ ।। mayaiveha visastainyaṃ kṛtaṃ vo hitakāriṇā । sā ca kṛtyā hatā ghoro devo ahaṃ tridaśeśvaraḥ ।।
ityuktvā nijamāsthāya rūpaṃ saptarṣibhiḥ saha । velladvimānamālāṅkaṃ nākaṃ nākapatiryayau ।। pratigrahanivṛttānāmevamujjvalacetasām । vibhātyalaulyābharaṇā vṛttiḥ saṃtoṣaśālinām ।।
visastainyam ।। munayaḥ kaśyapamukhā nṛpāśca nahuṣādayaḥ । śatakratuṃ puraskṛtya tīrthāni prayayuḥ purā ।। te snātvā puṇyatīrtheṣu puṣkarāhariṇīṃ yayuḥ ।
tatrāgastyamunirnyastaṃ nāpaśyannijapuṣkaram ।। tataste śapathaṃ cakruḥ krameṇa gurupātakam । indrastu prāha dhanyo astu sa hṛtaṃ yena puṣkaram ।। puṣkarastainyam ।।
chattropānatpradhā naṃ ca bhīṣmaḥ pṛṣṭo mahībhujā । uvāceha paraṃ puṇyaṃ paratra trāṇamiṣyate ।। jamadagniḥ purā dhanvī lakṣyābhyāsarato vane । sasarja sāyakaśreṇīṃ raśmimālāmivāṃśumān ।।
visṛṣṭānviśikhānbhartrā reṇukā tatra tadgirā । ānināyenduvadanā sukumārā punaḥ punaḥ ।। tāṃ caṇḍakiraṇasphārasaṃtāpāyāsamūrcchitām । sa jāyāṃ vīkṣya madhyāhne kruddhaḥ sūryamudaikṣata ।।
tato divyāstravikaṭaṃ khe prahartuṃ samudyatam । raviḥ prasādayāmāsa bhayādetya kṛtāñjaliḥ ।। gatakrodhasya tasyātha chattramātapavāraṇam । upānahau ca pradadau prītaye vāsareśvaraḥ ।।
chattropānatpradhā naṃ taddānānāmuttamaṃ smṛtam । saṃtāpaśamanaṃ nṝṇāmasmiṃlloke paratra ca ।। chattrotpattiḥ ।। taḍākakūpadānaṃ ca puṇyaṃ śarma śarīriṇām ।
paratra marusaṃtapte pānīyaṃ kila durlabham ।। apāratimire ghore paraloke nirāśraye । ālokadurlabhastasmāddīpaṃ dadyānnaraḥ sadā ।। prīṇāti sakalāṃllokānsumanovalidhūpadaḥ ।
asurendramiti prāha purā śukraḥ kathāntare ।। puṣpadhūpapradaḥ svarge durdharṣo nahuṣo abhavat । ākhaṇḍalasyāsanaṃ ca prāpākhaṇḍitaśāsanaḥ ।। yadā pasparśa pādena sarpeti munipuṃgavam ।
dṛpto agastyaṃ samāviśya bhṛguṇā pātitastadā ।। bhīmabāhugrahakṛto ghorājagararūpiṇaḥ । araṇye bhavatā yasya śāpamokṣaḥ purā kṛtaḥ ।। puṣpādidānam ।।
punaḥ pṛṣṭo nṛpatinā gatiṃ brahmasvahāriṇām । ūce śāntanavo rājanbrahmasvaṃ viṣamaṃ viṣam ।। jātismaraḥ purā kaścidrājaputraḥ sakautukaḥ । kujātihetuṃ paprāccha caṇḍālaṃ so apyabhāṣata ।।
śrūyatāṃ kāraṇaṃ yena prāptaścaṇḍālatāmaham । brāhmaṇasya purā gāvo hṛtāḥ prabaladasyubhiḥ ।। tāsāṃ rajo yajñabhūmau somamadhye apatatkvacit । tatpītvā narakaṃ viprā dīkṣitena sahāyayuḥ ।।
bhikṣāpātre nipatitaṃ tadreṇu brahmacāriṇaḥ । tadreṇu tatsthitaṃ cānnaṃ mohānme bhakṣyatāṃ yayau ।। brāhmaṇaḥ śrotriyaścāhaṃ brahmacārī jitendriyaḥ । tenāvastāmimāṃ prāptaḥ paśya brahmasvagauravam ।।
ityuktvā kṣatriyagirā brāhmaṇārthe raṇānale । hutvā śarīraṃ caṇḍālaḥ prāpa puṇyaṃ punargatim ।। rājanyacaṇḍālasaṃvādaḥ ।। nānā gatīḥ puṇyakṛtāṃ bhīṣmaḥ pṛṣṭo mahībhujā ।
uvāca karmavaicitryātte te lokāḥ śarīriṇām ।। gautamenāśrame pūrvaṃ śiśurhastī vivardhitaḥ । homāvaśeṣapayasā nīvāraprasavena ca ।। tato madajalaśyāmakapolālīnaṣaṭpadaḥ ।
līlālasaḥ sa kālena babhūvācalasaṃnibhaḥ ।। idhmadarbhaphalāhārī nirjarāśramapālakaḥ । muneḥ putra iva prītyā sa babhūva mahāgajaḥ ।। taṃ pravṛddhaṃ tathā nāgaṃ svayametya śatakratuḥ ।
jahāra rūpamāsthāya dhṛtarāṣṭrasya bhūpateḥ ।। punaḥ punaryācyamāno muninā sa yadā nṛpaḥ । na tatyāja gajaṃ darpāttadā taṃ gautamo avadat ।। gatvā yatra śarīrānte narāḥ kālavaśīkṛtāḥ ।
nandanti śocantyathavā tatra dāsyasi me gajam ।। pāpātmāno viśasyante yatra tairbhrakuṭīmukhaiḥ । vaivasvatasamādiṣṭaistatra dāsyasi me gajam ।। samānā bhīravaḥ śūrā durbalā balinastathā ।
yatra mugdhā vidagdhāśca tatra dāsyati me gajam ।। dhanadasya pure ramye merau vā nandane vane । dhāmni śītamayūkhasya sahasrakiraṇasya vā ।। varuṇāsya surendrasya surabhīṇāṃ svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।
loke vā dāsyasi gajaṃ na tatra balavānasi ।। etacchrutvāvadadrājā narakaṃ yānti nāstikāḥ । narā vyāmiśrakarmāṇaḥ prayānti yamamandiram ।। dhanadasya puraṃ yānti vratino atithipūjakāḥ ।
yaṣṭāro nandanaṃ yānti dātāraḥ somamaṇḍalam ।। khādhyāyinaḥ sūryalokaṃ niyatāstīrthasevinaḥ । yānti praśāntāḥ saṃsārātparaṃ dhāma svayaṃbhuvaḥ । nāhaṃ kvacidgamiṣyāmi kva nu dāsyāmi te gajam ।।
ityuktvā kuñjaraṃ tasmai dattvā divyāṃ tathā gatim । svaṃ vapurdarśayitvā ca hasannindro yayau divam ।। hastikūṭīyam ।। saśarīraḥ purā rājā brahmalokaṃ bhagīrathaḥ ।
yayau mahīgovṛṣadaḥ kanyāgrāmapurapradaḥ ।। sadācārāḥ satyavanto jyeṣṭhaśuśrūṣavo narāḥ । gurupūjāratāḥ kṣāntā bhavantīha śatāyuṣaḥ ।। upavāsavratajuṣāṃ tithinakṣatrayogataḥ ।
niyamā divyaphaladā jagādetyaṅgirāḥ purā ।। śrutveti dharmatanaye dehi dehagatiṃ punaḥ । praṣṭuṃ samudyate sākṣādbṛhaspatirathāyayau ।। sa pūjito munivarairbhīṣmeṇa vidureṇa ca ।
dhṛtārāṣṭreṇa kṛṣṇena bheje ratnojjvalāsanam ।। yudhiṣṭhiror'cayitvā taṃ prayāto bhīṣmaśāsanāt । papracchācārasaṃsāramaraṇaṃ dehadehinoḥ ।। tato abravītsuraguruḥ śarīraṃ pāñcabhautikam ।
pañcadhā yātamutsṛjya svapnavacceṣṭate naraḥ ।। dehabhaṅge nirālokaṃ gatvā deśamabāndavam । dehī vāsanayā viddhastattadvetti śubhāśubham ।। tyaktvā kalevaraṃ janturnirmokamiva pannagaḥ ।
dharmādharmayuto yāti sāmoda iva mārutaḥ ।। tattadbhuktvā nirākāraḥ karmapuryaṣṭakāśaśrayaḥ । bhūtaiḥ samāgamaṃ yāti punaḥ śukramukhāccyutaḥ ।। karmabhiḥ śavalaistatra madhuvallipyate punaḥ ।
cakravatpaśukoṭīnāṃ lipto bhrāmyati yoniṣu ।। dattvā ca vipulaṃ dānaṃ modate puṇyavānsukhī । ahiṃsayā yāti divaṃ tṛṣṇayā kaṣṭamaśnute ।। gṛhītvā patito vipraściraṃ bhavati gardabhaḥ ।
sūkaraḥ kṛkavākuśca jambukaḥ śva sa jāyate ।। gurornikāraṃ kṛtvā ca bhavati śvā tato vṛkaḥ । tataśca rāsabho ghoro narakāvartanirgataḥ ।। pitroḥ kṛtāpakāraśca śvā kūrmaḥ śalyakastathā ।
vyāḍo dāsaśca bhavati kramātkarmakṣayāvadhi ।। bhartṛdveṣī kapirbhūtvā mūṣikaḥ śvāpi jāyate । nikṣepahartā duḥkhāya bhrāntvā yoniśataṃ śanaiḥ ।। amedhyāvartakalile jāyate kutsitaḥ krimī ।
paranindārataḥ śārṅgo matsyo viśvastagātakaḥ ।। mṛgaśchāgo atha kīṭaśca kramādbhavati duṣkṛtī । sasyahartā bhavatyākhuḥ kroḍaḥ kauleyakastathā ।। kravyādajātiṃ vividhāṃ bhajate pārajāyikaḥ ।
śūdro vipravadhūṃ gatvā krimirākhuśca jāyate ।। kṛtaghnaḥ kālapuruṣairnarakeṣvāhato bhṛśam । kṛmirbhūtvā tato garbhaśateṣvantarvipadyate ।। kṛmistriḥsaptakṛtvaśca bhavati bhrūṇahā naraḥ ।
makṣikā bhojanaharo mūṣikaśca yavānnahṛt ।। cīrī ca lalanasteno dadhihartā tathā bakaḥ । varhī varṇaharo raktavastrahṛjjīvajīvakaḥ ।। piplastailaharaṇātphalastainyātpipīlakaḥ ।
miṣṭānnacauryāddhūkaśca vastracauryātkapotakaḥ । chacchundarirgandhaharī matsyo bhavati nihnavī ।। evaṃ bahuvidhaistaistaiścitrapākaiḥ kukarmabhiḥ । tāṃ tāṃ tamomayīṃ yoniṃ saṃsaranti śarīriṇaḥ ।।
saṃsāracakram ।। evaṃvidhāni pāpāni prāyāścittairvinā nṛṇām । dānena kila śāmyanti dānaṃ hi paramā gatiḥ ।। annameva paraṃ prāṇā bhūtānāmamṛtodgatiḥ ।
annadānaṃ mahattasmātpātraṃ yatra na gaṇyate ।। annapradaḥ sudhāvarṣī jāyate dhanavānsadā । śrīmānpunardadānyannaṃ prāksaṃskāradhiyaiva saḥ ।। labhate punaraiśvaryamityeva cakralīlayā ।
parivartini kāle asminpuṇyavānnāpacīyate ।। kālacakram ।। ityuktvā bhagavānsākṣātpūjyamāno maharṣibhiḥ । tejorañjitadikcakro divamācakrame guruḥ ।।
ahiṃsālakṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ sarvabhūtābhayapradam । ajātaśatruṇa pṛṣṭaḥ punaḥ śāntanavo abravīt ।। amāṃsabhakṣaṇaṃ nṝṇāmaśvamedhaśataiḥ samam । māṃsaṃ hi jāyate ghorānnānyatra vadhapātakāt ।।
māṃsādeva samutpannaṃ māṃsaṃ māṃsamayo naraḥ । tulyavyathe asminsaṃsāre bhuñjānaḥ kiṃ na lajjate ।। kaṇṭakenāpi saṃspṛṣṭā yānti kāmapi vikriyām । te api śastranikṛttasya paśoraśnanti vigraham ।।
bhayamākampanaṃ tīvraṃ dehināṃ dehasaṃkṣaye । dṛṣṭvā ko nāma māṃsebhyaḥ spṛhāṃ kuryādarākṣasaḥ ।। amāṃsāśī jagadbandhuḥ prāṇināmabhayapradaḥ । prayāti nirbhayaṃ dhāma puṇyakāruṇyasāgaraḥ ।।
kraturnirvighnasaṃbhārastīrthamadhvaśramoñjhitam । ahiṃsā nāma paramaṃ vratamatyaktabhojanam ।। amāṃsabhakṣaṇam ।। prāṇāḥ priyatarāḥ puṃsāṃ yairhutāste raṇānale ।
tadgatiṃ kathayetyukto rājñā bhīṣmo avadatpunaḥ ।। evametatpriyāḥ prāṇā duḥkhināmapi dehinām । śaknoti kastānsahasā tyuktaṃ sattvavato vinā ।। sarvathā jīvitābhraṃśe bhīravo bhayaviklavāḥ ।
tṛṇāñcite api nayane mīlayantyeva kātarāḥ ।। purā śakaṭasaṃtrāsādvidrutaṃ pathi kīṭakam । vyāso vilokya papraccha sasmitaṃ jñānalocanaḥ ।। asminnapi śarīre te rakṣārthaṃ ko ayamāgrahaḥ ।
tatsarvaṃ maraṇaṃ manye tava kutsitajīvinaḥ ।। etacchrutvā munivacastaṃ kīṭaḥ pratyabhāṣata । nāsti kāyasamaṃ kiṃciddehināṃ vallabhaṃ vibho ।। kīṭikāpremabaddhasya sūkṣmakīṭakaputriṇaḥ ।
vivarāntaragehe me śakrasyeva sukhaṃ divi ।। snehasyāyatanaṃ prāṇāḥ kaḥ svayaṃ tyaktumīśvaraḥ । muhūrtamapi labhyante naite meruśatairapi ।। śūdro ahaṃ bahubhiḥ pāpaiḥ kīṭayonimimāṃ śritaḥ ।
pitroḥ śuśrūṣayā kiṃtu mune jātiṃ smarāmyaham ।। tacchrutvā karuṇāmbhodhirbhagavānbhūtabhāvanaḥ । tasmai nṛpapadaṃ vyāso dadau janmāntare kramāt ।। vipro atha tadgirā bhūtvā sa yayau paramāṃ gatim ।
āpatsu mahatāmeva darśanaṃ kalpapādapaḥ ।। tasmādatipriyāḥ prāṇā yaistyaktāḥ saṃmukhairyudhi । dhairyābdhayaste tridive spardhante vibudhādhipam ।। kīṭakopākhyānam ।।
vidyāyāstapaso vāpi dānādvā kiṃ viśiṣyate । iti pṛṣṭaḥ kṣitibhujā babhāṣe jāhanavīsutaḥ ।। vārāṇasyāṃ purā vyāso maitreyeṇa nimantritaḥ । bhuktvā prahṛṣṭaḥ provāca kathānte tapasāṃ nidhiḥ ।।
tejaḥ paraṃ tapo nāma divyameva balaṃ tapaḥ । paśyanti santastapasā jñānaṃ hi tapasaḥ phalam ।। asminbhavamahāmohatapto vyāpte jagattraye । vidyaiva paramaṃ cakṣurakṣuṇṇā lokakāraṇam ।।
kiṃtu sarvamatītyaitaddānameva viśiṣyate । dānātparaṃ na saṃsāre dehināṃ śarma vidyate ।। annadānaiḥ sukṛtinaḥ prayātāḥ paramaṃ padam । muniprāpyamanāyāsalīlayā sattvaśālinaḥ ।।
annaṃ haviḥ sudhā pāṇāstaddātā jīvitapradaḥ । ityuktvā munimāmantrya jagāma munipuṃgavaḥ ।। maitreyabhikṣā ।। pṛṣṭo atha yoṣitāṃ rājñā sadācāraḥ pitāmahaḥ ।
uvāca satataṃ strīṇāṃ sadācāraḥ satīvratam ।। kaikeyī sumanā nāma suralokasthitāṃ purā । papraccha śāṇḍilīṃ dīptatejaḥpuñjajitāmarām ।। subhage kena tapasā dānena caritena vā ।
bhāsi divyavimāne asminmamūrtevāṃśumataḥ prabhā ।। kutūhaleneti tayā pṛṣṭā provāca śāṇḍilī । nāhaṃ vratairna saṃnyāsairna dānena divaṃ śritā ।। pūjitaḥ satataṃ bhaktyā mayā daivatavatpatiḥ ।
na hi santaḥ praśaṃsanti tapaḥ strīṇāmataḥ param ।। niṣkuṭe dvāri harmye vā rājamārgāvalokinī । nābhavaṃ proṣite vāpi patyau vratavivarjitā ।। chāyevānapagā bhartuḥ kope bhītā hitaiṣiṇī ।
bhūtvāhaṃ tridivaṃ prāptā manovākkarmabhiḥ satī ।। ityuktvā śāṇḍilī prāyāttato niṣadhamunnatam । tasmātsatīvratādanyannārīṇāṃ na parāyaṇam ।। śāṇḍilīsumanāsaṃvādaḥ ।।
adhikaṃ prīyate kiṃsvitsāmnā dānena vā janaḥ । pṛṣṭo yudhiṣṭhireṇeti punardevavrato abravīt ।। purā vane dvijaḥ kaścidgṛhīto rakṣasā balāt । sarvopāyavihīnatvātsāmnā muktimacintayat ।।
niśācarastamavadvañcanāya vadhodyataḥ । pāṇḍuro durbalaścāhaṃ kenaitkathyatāmiti ।। viprastamūce nūnaṃ te dūrībhūtaḥ suhṛjjanaḥ । niḥsahāyena cāptā śrīstvayā tenāsi pāṇḍuraḥ ।।
ārādhyamāno yatnena te vyaktamanimittataḥ । viraktaḥ svajano yāsi tena vā pariśuṣyasi ।। tvatto hīnaguṇānanyānvyakte paśyasi pūjitān । aiśvaryamānasubhagāṃstena vā durbalo bhavān ।।
vyaktaṃ tyāgī daridro asi guṇairnūnaṃ na pūjyase । prājñasya te na śṛṇvanti sādhurvā vañcyase khalaiḥ ।। mūrkho vā śāstrarasiko mānī hīnakulo asi vā । duḥkhaṃ svapiṣi manye ahaṃ cintayā hariṇaḥ kṛśaḥ ।।
śrutvaitadāśayagrāhī brāhmaṇoktaṃ niśācaraḥ । prītastatyāja taṃ sāmnā ko hi sāntvairna tuṣyati ।। harimakṛśīyam ।। kṛṣṇaprabhāvaṃ pṛṣṭo ata rājñā śāntanavo abravīt ।
purā tapaḥsthitaṃ śauriṃ munayo draṣṭumāyayuḥ ।। dadṛśuste tatastatra viṣṇuvaktrotthitāgninā । dagdhaṃ vanaṃ mahatpaścāttenaivāpyāyitaṃ dṛśā ।। taddṛṣṭvā nāradamukhāddivyaṃ bubudhire param ।
tadgirā vaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma vipluṣṭācalaśekharam ।। tato nānākathākhyānakovidaḥ kaiṭabhatviṣā । kathānte nāradaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ prastāvocitamabhyadhāt ।। purā himagirau gaurī dhūrjaṭeḥ kila līlayā ।
netre karābhyāṃ pidadhe sa tenābhūttrilocanaḥ ।। tṛtīyanayanodbhūtavahninā so abhavadgiriḥ । pluṣyatsālalatājālajvālāvalayitāmbaraḥ ।। tato gaurīgirā cakre punargaurīguruṃ girim ।
smerapuṣpalatāvṛkṣaṃ dṛśā śītāṃśuśekharaḥ ।। tatra pṛṣṭo bahuvidhāḥ kathāḥ praṇayalālasaḥ । devyā kathānte bhagavānūce dharmārthanirṇayam ।। pravṛttānāṃ sadācāraṃ varṇāśramavibhāgajam ।
nivṛttānāṃ ca niḥsaṅgakriyānirvāṇajaṃ phalam ।। tataḥ śaśāṅkacūḍena pṛṣṭā devī mṛgīdṛśām । śaśaṃsa puṇyaṃ caritaṃ varārādhanadaivatam ।। athābravīnnīlakaṇṭhaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sarvairmunīśvaraiḥ ।
kāraṇaṃ paramaṃ viṣṇuṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhavāpyaye ।। vasudevasya tanayo bhaviṣyati hariḥ kṣitau । aṃśāvatīrṇo vibudhārātisaṃhāratatparaḥ ।। sa sūryaḥ sa ca śītāṃśu so ahaṃ sa ca caturmukhaḥ ।
sarvadevamayaḥ śauriḥ kaṃsakeśiniṣūdanaḥ । umāpaterapi puraḥ śrutamasmābhirīśvarāt ।। etacchrutvā munivaco dvārakāmetya keśavaḥ । avāpa putraṃ rukmiṇyāṃ svecchāsṛṣṭajagattrayaḥ ।।
dhanyo asi yasya te rājankamalāvallabho vibhuḥ । viśvarakṣāmaṇiḥ so ayaṃ goptā garuḍalāñchanaḥ ।। umāmaheśvarasaṃvādaḥ ।। kathayitveti gāṅgeye muhūrtaṃ maunamāsthite ।
ūce munisabhāmadhye śanakairdharmanandanaḥ ।। daivataṃ paramaṃ śarma kimekaṃ sarvadehinām । kasminpratiṣṭhitaṃ viśvaṃ stutyā muktipradaśca kaḥ ।। ityukte dharmaputreṇa babhāṣe jāhnavīsutaḥ ।
manasā puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ natvā viṣṇumanāmayam ।। ananto bhagavānviṣṇurdevadevo jagatprabhuḥ । stuto nāmasahasreṇa mokṣado garuḍadhvajaḥ ।। jagatpratiṣṭhitaṃ tasmindaivataṃ paramaṃ ca saḥ ।
nāmnāṃ sahasraṃ munayo yasya gāyanti muktaye ।। viśvaṃ viṣṇurvaṣaṭkāro bhūtabhavyabhavātmanaḥ । prabhorbhūtabhṛto bhūtabhāvanasya bhavacchidaḥ ।। patyuḥ puṃsaḥ purāṇasya kṣetratretrajñasākṣiṇaḥ ।
bhuvaḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ śaṃbhorvidhāturvedhaso vidheḥ ।। harerhiraṇyagarbhasya śrīpatorviśvakarmaṇaḥ । vṛṣākaperamoghasya sahasrākṣasya gopateḥ ।। sahasraśiraso viṣṇorvyāpinaḥ praṇavātmanaḥ ।
stotraṃ nāmasahasrāṅkaṃ mantrarājaṃ pracakṣate ।। ityuktvā vaidikairdivyairgauṇamukhyaiśca nāmabhiḥ । sahasrasaṃkhyaistuṣṭāva deva bhīṣmaḥ sanātanam ।। śrutvaitatprayataḥ kṛṣṇaṃ vanditvā dharmanandanaḥ ।
prabhāvaṃ bhūmidevānāṃ papraccha dyunadīsutam ।। so avadadbrahmaniṣṭhānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ bhayātkila । udeti somaḥ sūryaśca prayāti ca samīraṇaḥ ।। dattātreyavarāvāptasahasrabhujamunmadam ।
kārtavīryaṃ purā prāha vāyurjitagattrayam ।। brāhmaṇebhyaḥ paro nāsti rājendra balavattaraḥ । bhavādṛśā dṛśā yeṣāṃ bhavanti na bhavanti ca ।। somaputryā vṛtaḥ pūrvamuttasthe yādasāṃ prabhum ।
tatkāmamapibatkopāddayitāmājahāra ca ।। nirjitākhilagīrvāṇagandharvā dānavāḥ purā । sṛṣṭo atriṇā śītakaraḥ śakraṃ ca cyavano ajayat ।। surāṇāṃ daityasamare rakṣitā timire purā ।
sṛṣṭo atriṇā śītakaraḥ śakraṃ ca cyavano ajayat ।। iti brāhmaṇamāhātmyaṃ śrutvā haihayabhūpatiḥ । arjuno apujayannityaṃ bhūmidevānānanyadhīḥ ।। pavanārjunasaṃvādaḥ ।।
ataḥ paraṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ prabhāvaṃ keśavo vibhuḥ । jānāti nābhinalinasvecchāsṛṣṭacaturmukhaḥ ।। iti bhīṣmeṇa kathite hṛṣīkeśaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । papraccha vipramāhātmyaṃ sa ca pṛṣṭastamabhyadhāt ।।
purāhaṃ raukmiṇeyena pṛṣṭaḥ śaktiṃ dvijanmanām । avadaṃ tapasā yeṣāṃ kampante daivatānyapi ।। putra sarvaprayatnena pūjaya brāhmaṇānsadā । ete krodhaprasādābhyāṃ jīvayanti dahanti ca ।।
pratiśrāyarthī durvāsāḥ purā dīptākṣimūrdhajaḥ । uvāsa madgṛhe taistaiḥ sevyamānaḥ priyairmayā ।। sa bhuktvā pāyasaṃ taptamucchiṣṭena ruṣā jvalan । limpāṅgānīti māmāha taccāsmyakaravaṃ bhayāt ।।
rukmiṇīṃ sa rathe kṛtvā babhrāma bahuyojanam । nirvikāraṃ ca māṃ dṛṣṭāva tutoṣa paruṣāśrayaḥ ।। sa māmūce tavocchiṣṭaliptaṃ vajramayaṃ vapuḥ । bhaviṣyati vinā pādau tau niliptau yatastvayā ।।
durvāsaso bhikṣā ।। etatkṛṣṇavacaḥ śrutvā pārthaḥ śāntanavātpunaḥ । śuśrāva devarājarṣivaṃśānkalmaṣanāśanān ।। kaṇvairabhyavakrītavasiṣṭhabhṛgukaśyapān ।
duḥṣyantarāmanahuṣālarkaśvetabhagīrathān ।। kathayitvā kṣaṇaṃ sthitvā tūṣṇīṃ niḥśabdasa । puraṃ vyāsājñayā pārthaṃ visasarja suravrataḥ ।। kṛṣṇena saha kaunteyo bhrātṛbhiśca sahānugaiḥ ।
dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ puraskṛtya prayayau hastināpuram ।। pūjyamānaḥ surairdātā sthitvā tatra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । dṛṣṭvottaraṃ sa saṃprāptaṃ punarāyātpitāmaham ।। sānugaḥ sa samabhyetya gāṅgeyaṃ śaraśāyinam ।
praṇamya pāṇḍavo asmīti nigadya samupāviśat ।। munīndrajuṣṭe sadasi brahmaloka ivāpare । jāte niḥśabdasaṃcāre bhīṣmavaktrāvalokini ।। śanairunmīlya nayane pāṇḍavānvīkṣya sānugān ।
vāggamī gambhīramavadadgāṅgeyaḥ pāṇḍavāgrajam ।। kāle diṣṭyā bhavānprāptaḥ parivṛtte divākaraḥ । māsadvayamatītaṃ me niśātaśaraśāyinaḥ । tvāmāmantrya vrajāmyeṣa putra lokānsanātanān ।।
ityuktvā satyadugdhābdhiḥ kiṃcidāvṛttakaṃdharaḥ । uvāca vidurasyāgre dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ pitāmahaḥ ।। rājanvidyāmayaṃ cakṣurakṣuṇṇāṃ tava lakṣyate । mā gamaḥ putraśokārtyā mohaṃ kālo hi durjayaḥ ।।
putravatpaśya bhūpālamanṛśaṃsaṃ yudhiṣṭhiram । prayātu śeṣaḥ kāle ayaṃ tava saṃtoṣaśālinaḥ ।। etaduktvā hṛṣīkeśaṃ stutvā mūrdhnā praṇamya ca । babhāṣe bhagavangantumanujānīhi māmiti ।।
atha kṛṣṇābhyanujñāto nistaraṅga ivodadhiḥ । muhūrtamabhavadbhīṣmo dadhānaḥ prāṇadhāraṇām ।। antaḥ sparśarasāttasya gātrāṇi tyajato bahiḥ । viśalyāni śanaiḥ sarve dadṛśurvismayākulāḥ ।।
sa galitasakalāntaḥsvāntaviśrāntimūlodgatanijabalaśaktisphoṭitāśeṣacakram । vitatataralatārasphāratejaḥprakāraprasṛtamarududañcanmadhyanāḍikrameṇa ।। lalitadalasarojaproccaṭajjīvahaṃso dṛśamatiśaśisūryāṃ bhrūvibhāge niveśya । galitakaraṇavṛttigrāmaniḥsyanādalakṣyaḥ sapadi kimapi bhīṣmaścintayansaṃbabhūva ।।
bhīṣmotkrāntiḥ ।। atha jyotistaḍitpuñjarāṃśuśatācitam । bhittvā bhīṣmasya mūrdhānaṃ viveśa vimalaṃ nabhaḥ ।। tato asya ratnābharaṇairvāsobhiḥ kusumaistathā ।
dharmarājaḥ saviduraścakre vaimānikaṃ svayam ।। chettraṃ tasya yaśaḥ śubhraṃ yuyutsustūrṇamagrahīt । cāmare sattvadhavale bhīmasenārjunāvapi ।। sabāṣpaṃ bharatastrībhistālavṛntānilena saḥ ।
vījyamānaścitāṃ prāpa śrīkhaṇḍāgurukalpitām ।। sajīva iva saṃlīne gāṅgeye sphāratejasi । yudhiṣṭhiramukhāścakruḥ sāśrunetrā jalakriyām ।। tatra mandākinītīre viṣaṇṇo rājñi sānuge ।
jalamadhyātsamuttasthau jāhnavī sāśrulocanā ।। sā vihvalā śokavatī viṣaṇṇaiḥ paramarṣibhiḥ । vyāsanāradakaṇvādyairmuhurālokitāvadat ।। hā putra tripurārātiśiṣyasya kṣatriyadviṣaḥ ।
jetā tasyāpi rāmasya nihato asi kathaṃ paraiḥ ।। aho nu tvayi kālena yāte astaṃ yaśasāṃ nidhau । śocyeyaṃ pṛthivī śūnyā vīraratnavinā kṛtā ।। kā nāma jananī pāpā madvidhānyā bhaviṣyati ।
nihataṃ tvādṛśaṃ putraṃ yā śrutvāpi na dīryate ।। aho bata varākeṇa hato bhīṣmaḥ śikhaṇḍinā । kupitaḥ kuñjarārātirjambukena nipātitaḥ ।। iti pralāpamukharāṃ jahnukanyāṃ janārdanaḥ ।
śanairāśvāsayannūce meghagambhīraniḥsvanaḥ ।। vijñātaparamārthāpi vasuśāpe api sākṣiṇī । sāmānyajananīva tvaṃ kathaṃ devi vimuhyase ।। na hi śāntanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ tripurāriparākramam ।
hantuṃ śikhaṇḍinaḥ śaktirvinā kālādbalīyasaḥ ।। sa yātaḥ paramaṃ dhāma svacchandanidhanaḥ svayam । aśocyaṃ mā śucaḥ putraṃ ko anyo jāyeta tadvidhaḥ ।। iti vyāsādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ kṛṣṇenāśvāsitā śanaiḥ ।
niḥsyandamīnamakarā kṣaṇaṃ mandākinī babhau ।। tato yudhiṣṭhiramukhāstāṃ samāmantrya sānugāḥ । duḥkhākulā nyavartanta yāte astaṃ vāsareśvare ।। nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam ।
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। yaśaḥ śaśāṅkośeṣe astaṃ prayāte bhīṣmabhāsvati । papāta dharmatanayaḥ śokamlānamukhāmbujaḥ ।। mohamūrcchākule tasminviṣaṇṇe saha bāndhavaiḥ ।
śucaṃ saṃstambhya śanakairdhṛtarāṣṭrastamabravīt ।। uttiṣṭha pṛthivīpāla na dhairyaṃ hātumarhasi । saṃsārāsāracaritaṃ munibhyaḥ śrutavānasi ।। śokasyāvasaro nāyaṃ svadharmādacyutasya te ।
pāhi sattvasudhāsindho prajāpatiriva prajāḥ ।। śocitavyo mamaivāyaṃ kālaḥ samucito adhunā । vidurasya giro yena na śrutāḥ sunayojjvalāḥ ।। ityukte dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa kṛṣṇaḥ kṣmāpālamabhyadhāt ।
mā śucaḥ kṣatradharmeṇa labdhāṃ bhuṅkṣva mahīmimām ।। duḥkhibhyo hi palāyante dhairyāyattā vibhūtayaḥ । yajasva vijayī rājanpāpaśaṅkāpanuttaye ।। aśvamedhena vidhinā yātastadyogyatāmasi ।
etanmunivacaḥ śrutvā yajñe baddhamanorathaḥ ।। dhanamūlāṃ kriyaṃ matvā rājyakośamacintayat । so atha sarvānsamāhūya kośādhyakṣānmakhotsukaḥ ।। tebhyaḥ śuśrāva sarvasvaṃ kṣayitaṃ yudhi kauravaiḥ ।
aśvamedhe nirāśaṃ taṃ vijñāya draviṇaṃ vinā ।। uvāca karuṇāsindhurvyāso nirvāpayanniva । maruttasya kṣitipateryajñaśeṣaṃ himācale ।। kāñcanaṃ vidyate bhūri yajñārthaṃ tadavāpsyasi ।
śrutvaitatpāṇḍuputreṇa maruttasya mahīpateḥ ।। mahāyajñakathāṃ pṛṣṭaḥ provāca munipuṃgavaḥ । mahīyasi manorvaṃśe mahatāṃ yaśasāṃ nidhiḥ ।। karaṃdhamakule śrīmānmarutto abhūnmahīpatiḥ ।
tamandraḥ spardhate nityaṃ na sa śaknoti ceṣṭitaiḥ ।। yadā tadā manyutapto rahaḥ prāha bṛhaspatim । karaṃdhamo abhavadyājyastvatpituḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।। kramāttavāpi tatsūnurmaruttastadguṇādhikaḥ ।
kiṃtu taddarpasaṃgharṣādbhavantamahamarthaye ।। na yājakapadaṃ tasya gantavyaṃ bhavatādhunā । ityarthito maghavatā tathetyūce bṛhaspatiḥ ।। adyaprabhṛti martyo me na yājya iti saṃvidā ।
atrāntare narapatirmarutto vipulaṃ kratum ।। āhartuṃ kṛtasaṃkalpo bṛhaspatimupāyayau । sa tenābhyarthito yatnādyājako astu bhavāniti ।। na cakārābhyupagamaṃ śakrapraṇayayantritaḥ ।
pratyākhyātaḥ sa guruṇā rājā lajjānatānanaḥ ।। vrajanvinaṣṭasaṃkalpo dadarśa pathi nāradam । nārado api tamālokya pṛṣṭvā śrutvā ca tatkathām ।। uvāca tyaja saṃtāpaṃ mā rājanvimanā bhava ।
saṃvartākhyo nidhirdhāmnāmanujo asti bṛhaspateḥ ।। svacchandacārī yogīndro vārāṇasyāṃ sa vartate । saṃvartaḥ sa parijñeyo vrajethāḥ śaraṇaṃ tu tam ।। nivedito ahaṃ keneti pṛṣṭastena tvamānataḥ ।
bravīthā nārado mahyaṃ tvāmihasthaṃ nyavedayat ।। kathayitvā prahṛṣṭaśca jvalitaṃ jātavedasam । ityuktvā prārthayethāstaṃ yājakaṃ yajvanāṃ varaḥ ।। nāradenetyabhihite bhūpālo harṣanirbharaḥ ।
taduktaṃ vidadhe sarvaṃ gatvā vāraṇasīṃ svayam ।। saṃtyaktonmattarūpaṃ sa prāpya taṃ yājakaṃ nṛpaḥ । cakāra tadanujñātastapo himagirestaṭe ।। tapasā yajñavittārthī devamārādhya śaṃkaram ।
anekameruvipulaṃ lebhe hema sa pārthivaḥ ।। haimeṣu sarvabhāṇḍeṣu raciteṣvatha śilpibhiḥ । saṃpūrṇo yajñasaṃbhāraḥ prāvartata mahībhujaḥ ।। samṛddhimatulāṃ tasya yajñe jñātvā bṛhaspatiḥ ।
saṃvartakaṃ yājakaṃ ca saṃtaptastanutāṃ yayau ।। sa śokakāraṇaṃ pṛṣṭaḥ śakreṇa mlānamānasaḥ । maruttayajñavibhavaṃ bhrātṛspardhākulo avadat ।। tataḥ śatakratustasya prītye guruvatsalaḥ ।
uvāca vahnimāhūya maruttaṃ vraja pārthivam ।। gatvā madvacasā vācyaḥ sa ca rājā tvayā kratau । yathā saṃvartakaṃ tyaktvā bhavedyājyo bṛhaspateḥ ।। ityuktaḥ surarājena gatvā vahnirnarādhipam ।
śakrasaṃdeśamavadanna ca rājābhyamanyata ।। tataḥ pratinivṛtto atha punargaccheti vajriṇā । preritaḥ pāvako avādītsaṃvartabhayakampitaḥ ।। sa tatra brahmacārī māmūce saṃvartakaḥ krudhā ।
tejorāśiḥ śapeyaṃ tvāṃ sameṣyasi punaryadi ।। śrutvaitatkātaro asīti taṃ jagāda puraṃdaraḥ । jvalanaḥ pratyuvācātha taṃ kopahaviṣā jvalan ।। aho nu brahmakopāgnirahalyāvallabhasya te ।
pramādādatha kopādvā mohādvā śakra vismṛtaḥ ।। sa yadā cyavanaḥ kopānmahādaṃṣṭraṃ mahāsuram । asṛjattvadvadhāyograṃ tadā dhairyaṃ kva te gatam ।। duḥsahā brāhmaṇaruṣo nirdahanti jagatkṣaṇāt ।
ukte hutāśaneneti na śaktaḥ kiṃcidabravīt ।। visṛṣṭaḥ punarindreṇa gandharvādhipatirnṛpam । ūce guruṃ bhajasveti na ca rājā tamagrahīt ।। tataḥ kruddhaḥ svayaṃ vajrī garjangambhīraniḥsvanaḥ ।
yajñāṅganaṃ narapatervyomnā meghairvṛto yayau ।। prabhāvenātha mahatā saṃvartasyogratejasaḥ । śatamanyusamutsṛṣṭaṃ vajraṃ meghānsamāviśat ।। tanmantraśaktyā vivaśaḥ samāhūto atha vṛtrahā ।
āyayau saha bhāgārhaistridaśaiḥ somapīthibhiḥ ।। pūjito atha maruttena śāntamanyuḥ śatakratuḥ । yajñakriyāparikare paricaryāparo abhavat ।। tadājñayā surāḥ sarve yajñasaṃbhārakāriṇaḥ ।
babhūvurbhūmipālasya nideśavaśagāściram ।। evaṃ tasyendrajayino rājñaḥ saṃvartatejasā । nirvighnaḥ pūrṇatāṃ prāpa yajñaḥ kanakavarṣiṇaḥ ।। taccheṣadviṇena tvaṃ hayamedhamahāmakham ।
prayataḥ prāpnuhītyuktāva virarāma munīśvaraḥ ।। saṃvartamaruttīyam ।। kṛṣṇenāśvārasyamāno atha munibhirbhrātṛbhistathā । aśvamedhadhṛtodyogo dhṛtiṃ lebhe yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।।
draṣṭuṃ tataḥ prajākāryaṃ pravṛtte dharmanandane । antardadhe tamāmantrya sarvaṃ tanmunimaṇḍalam ।। hemaratnalatākānte vikāsikanakāmbuje । atha kṛṣṇau sabhodyāne svairaṃ prītyā vijahvatuḥ ।।
kathānte tatra kaṃsāriṃ subhadrāvallabho avadat । yuddhārambhe tvayoktaṃ yatsarvaṃ tanmama vismṛtam ।। visṛṣṭaṃ paramārthajña jñānaṃ tatpunarucyatām । ityuktaḥ pāṇḍuputreṇa viṣaṇṇaḥ keśavo abravīt ।।
aho tvayāvadhānena na śrutaṃ tadabuddhinā । na śakyate punarvaktuṃ tathāpi śrūyatāmidam ।। brāhmaṇena purā kaścijjīvanmuktadaśāṃ śritaḥ । siddhaḥ pṛṣṭo avadatsarvaṃ vijñāya bhavavibhramam ।।
asminnasatyasaṃghāte bhūtānāṃ pāñcabhautike । guṇairnibaddhaḥ pakṣīva jīvastiṣṭhati pañjare ।। ahaṃkāraikasārāṇāṃ dehināṃ vismṛtātmanām । cakravatparivartante sukhaduḥkhakṣayodayāḥ ।।
dehānte karmasaṃsargājjantavaḥ śubhaduṣkṛtaiḥ । tārārūpā vimānāni bhajante narakāṇi vā ।। tato bhogakṣaye garbhaṃ jarāyupariveṣṭitam । śukrarūpo viśatyātmā yonyāṃ śoṇitasaṃplutaḥ ।।
niḥśvāsāgrairyathā vāri līyate darpaṇodare । nirdhūtasya yathā vahnerūṣmā vyomni prasarpati ।। yathā vā kusumāmodaḥ praviśatyantare anile । rāgaḥ saṃkrāntimāyāti sarandhre sphaṭike yathā ।।
tathā durlakṣyasaṃcāro garbhamātmā pradhāvati । bibhrāṇo vāsanāmantaḥ śītasparśamivānilaḥ ।। jātasya jāyate tasya vardhamānasya vardhate । tṛṣṇātanturbhi sasyeva śuṣyato na tu śuṣyati ।।
vivekādduḥkhasaṃyogādvairāgyaṃ gāḍhamāśritaḥ । nāhamasasmīti mantreṇa mucyate brahmadīkṣitaḥ ।। pūrvaṃ bhāveṣu nirvāṇastataḥ kāraṇavṛttiṣu । nirālambadaśāmetya yogī brahmaṇi līyate ।।
sarvataḥ pāṇicaraṇaṃ sarvavyāpinamavyayam । ātmānaṃ sa parijñāya satyāmetāṃ bhavasthitim ।। ityuktvā brāhmaṇaṃ siddhaḥ sahasāntaradhīyata । idamanyacca kaunteya śreyase prayataḥ śṛṇu ।।
uvāca brāhmaṇī kācidbhartāraṃ vijane purā । gamiṣyāmi gatiṃ sādhvī kāmahaṃ tvatparāyaṇā ।। iti pṛṣṭastayā viprastāmuvāca smitānanaḥ । agnirvaiśvānaro nāma sthito antaḥ kila dehinām ।।
indriyāṇi manobuddhistasya saptārciṣa smṛtāḥ । viṣayāścāsya samidho bhoktāraḥ sapta cartvijaḥ । tasminhate sarvamidaṃ jāyate ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। indriyāṇīva manaso manasteṣāṃ ca sarvadā ।
parasparopakāreṇa prīyate dehasaṃgame ।। manobuddhiprabhṛtayaḥ saptendriyamṛgāḥ purā । atarkeṇaiva nihatā rājñā yogamayaiḥ śaraiḥ ।। jitendriyasya no kiṃcididaṃ tasyaiva cākhilam ।
viṣayā viṣayasyeti janako vipramabhyadāt ।। tasmādasaktamanasā dṛṣṭvā sarvamidaṃ mayā । tyaktaṃ parāvarajñena bhavāvirbhāvaśāntaye ।। gatistavāpi kalyāṇi madbhāvasadṛśī sadā ।
brahmāraṇīsamudbhūtaṃ jānīhi jñānapāvakam ।। etatpatyurvacaḥ śrutvā brāhmaṇī tattvadarśinī । kṣetrakṣetrajñavijñānaṃ paraṃ prāvīṇyamāyayau ।। śrutvaitadarjunaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ babhāṣe vismayākulaḥ ।
yogīndro brāhmaṇaḥ ko asau kvāste vā sā ca tadvadhūḥ ।। ityuktaḥ kaiṭabhārātiḥ punarūce dhanaṃjayam । śiṣyeṇa pṛṣṭaḥ sarvajñaḥ purā gururabhāṣata ।। bṛhaspatiprabhṛtibhirmunīndraiḥ sarvadarśibhiḥ ।
śruteyaṃ bhavavicchedakathā proktā svayaṃbhuvā ।। guṇatrayanibaddhānāṃ karmabhedavikāriṇām । bhāvo ayaṃ prāṇināṃ śaśvadalpo apyāyātyanalpatām ।। vicitraḥ kila sargo ayamahaṃkārādvinirgataḥ ।
tasminneva layaṃ yāti śvabhre puṣpacayo yathā ।। janmāntaraśatābhyāsādantaraṅgatvamāgataḥ । ahaṃkāraḥ sa manaso līlayā kena bhedyate ।। avidyā tānavenaiva śanaiḥ saṃnyastakarmaṇaḥ ।
vikalpadvaṃdvaviratau jñānālokaḥ prajāyate ।। jñānāgninā pravṛddhena dagdhvā bhavaviṣadrumam । sarvagranthivinirmuktaḥ paramāmṛtamaśnute ।। iti brahmoditaṃ jñānaṃ śiṣyāya guruṇā purā ।
nānānidarśanopetaṃ kathitaṃ bhavaśāntaye ।। ahameva guruḥ pārtha śiṣyaśca tvaṃ samo mama । ityuktvā jñānasarvasvaṃ virarāma janārdanaḥ ।। anugītāḥ ।।
tato vihṛtya suciraṃ prītyā kṛṣṇaḥ kirīṭinā । dvārakāgamane cakre matiṃ bandhujanotsukaḥ ।। sa gatvā nṛpamāmantrya dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ ca sānugam । āśvāsya kṛṣṇāṃ kuntīṃ ca praṇamyādāya cānujām ।।
aśvamedhe sameṣyāmi punaḥ kṛtveti saṃvidam । dārukapreritarathaḥ pratasthe garuḍadhvajaḥ ।। sa vrajansātyakisakhastejorañjitadiṅmukhaḥ । uttaṅkaṃ tapasāṃ rāśimāluloke muniḥ pathi ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sādaraṃ śauriḥ praṇamya racitāñjaliḥ । kuśalaṃ vītavairāṇāṃ papracchāśramavāsinām ।। uttaṅko api hariṃ dṛṣṭvā prītipūrvamanāmayam । ūce kaccittvayā sāmnā rakṣitaṃ bhārataṃ kulam ।।
kaccidduryodhano rājā dharmaputraśca sānugau । sthitau vigatasaṃgharṣau tvadbuddhyā paitrike pade ।। ityuttaṅkena govindaḥ pṛṣṭastaṃ pratyabhāṣata । bhāratānāṃ mune yatnaḥ paraḥ saṃdhau kṛto mayā ।।
hitamukto api bahuśaḥ kauravo vidurādibhiḥ । na jagrāha kṛtāntena daivena ca vimohitaḥ ।। nirbandhātkururājasya rādheyamunivartinaḥ । nihatāḥ pārthivāḥ sarve śeṣāḥ pañcaiva pāṇḍavāḥ ।।
etcchrutvā muniḥ kopājjvalitānalasaṃnibhaḥ । tamūce vakramanasā te tvayaiva nipātitāḥ ।। śaktenāpi tvayā kṛṣṇa yasmātpārthahitaiṣiṇā । upekṣitaḥ kṣayo ghorastasmācchāpaṃ dadāni te ।।
uttaṅkenetyabhihite babhāṣe kaiṭabhāntakaḥ । jānāmi tejasāṃ rāśiṃ tvāmuttaṅka taponidhim ।। kiṃtu nārhasi kopena tīvraṃ kartuṃ tapovyayam । tamo hi duḥsahaṃ ghoraṃ krodho mṛtyuḥ śarīriṇām ।।
nādyāpi naṣṭamoho asi nanu nādyāpi paśyasi । kiṃ na jānāsi māṃ sarvaṃ sarvavyāpinamavyayam ।। sarvadevamayaḥ kartā viśvātmā jagatāmaham । ityukte puṣkarākṣeṇa śāntakopo abravīnmuniḥ ।।
jāne tvāṃ kiṃ tu taddivyaṃ draṣṭumicchāmi te vapuḥ । ityarthito munīndreṇa viśvāviṣkāralīlayā ।। śaktiprakāśaparipūritasaṃvidagre rekhāsphuraddruhiṇarudramahendracandram । dhāmatrayottaramanaśvaramaiśvaraṃ ta ddṛṣṭvā vapurmunivaro abhavadastamohaḥ ।।
tataḥ stotrairuttaṅkena viṣṇurbhaktyā namaskṛtaḥ । tadgirā svavapuḥ saumyaṃ tadeva punarādade ।। saṃnidhi te vidhāsyāmi sarvataḥ smaraṇānmune । ityuktvā taṃ samāmantrya prāyādgaruḍaketanaḥ ।।
tataḥ kadācitsa munirjalārthī marudhanvasu । carandadarśa caṇḍālaṃ dhanuṣpāṇiṃ jalapradam ।। gṛhāṇetyasakṛttena prārthito api muniryadā । na jagrāhāśuci jalamuttaṅko antardadhe tadā ।।
tataḥ sametya bhagavānsvayaṃ viṣṇustamabravīt । mune madvacasā śakraḥ sudhāṃ tvāṃ dātumāyayau ।। jalado na sa cāṇḍālo mithyā śaṅkā tavābhavat । pratyākhyātaḥ sa yanmohānna tadyuktaṃ tvayā kṛtam ।।
adhunā madvarātte astu sāmṛtairjalanirjharaiḥ । pūriteyaṃ marumahī nigadyeti yayau hariḥ ।। evaṃ mahāprabhāvo asāvuttaṅko yaśasāṃ nidhiḥ । durlabhaṃ darśanaṃ viṣṇoḥ sānugrahamavāptavān ।।
āsādya paramaṃ jñānaṃ yaḥ purā gurusevayā । taddakṣiṇārthī prayayau rājñaḥ pauṣasya mandiram ।। kuṇḍale prāpya rucire vitīrṇe pauṣabhāryayā । hṛte ca dṛṣṭvā nāśena jīviteśarasātalam ।।
jitvā nāgānsamāsādya te purā ratnakuṇḍale । yo dadau gurubhāryāyai kṛtakṛtyo babhūva ca ।। uttaṅkaviśvarūpadarśanam ।। yāte dvāravatīṃ kṛṣṇe yādavānandadāyini ।
yudhiṣṭhiraḥ sahāmātyo yajñakāryamacintayat ।। sa gatvā sānujaḥ śailaṃ śrīkaṇṭhadayitaṃ śanaiḥ । ārādhya tapasā rudraṃ devadevaṃ pinākinam ।। upahāreṇa vidhinā muhūrte śubhaśaṃsini ।
abhyarcya guhyakādhīśaṃ maṇibhadraṃ ca sānugam ।। munibhistarpite vahnau dhaumyena ca purodhasā । lebhe pāṇaḍusutaḥ śrīmānmaruttanihitaṃ nidhim ।। pṛthupramāṇarūpāṇi bhāsvanti vividhāni ca ।
hemabhāṇḍasahasrāṇi ratnabhāraśatāni ca ।। uṣṭrāṇāṃ śakaṭānāṃ ca hayānāṃ kariṇāṃ tathā । daśalakṣāṇi tadvittamanayaddhastināpuram ।। mahiṣāṇāṃ svarāṇāṃ ca puruṣāṇāṃ gavāṃ tathā ।
na babhūva tadā saṃkhyā vahatāṃ bhūri kāñcanam ।। akṣayyaṃ kośamādāya prāpte atha svapuraṃ nṛpe । sahito vṛṣṇibhiḥ sarvairāyayau madhusūdanaḥ ।। etasminneva samaye saubhadramahiṣī sutam ।
droṇaputrāstranirdagdhamasūta gatajīvitam ।। uttarāyāḥ suto jātaḥ strīṇāmityutsavasvanaḥ । vyasurvyasuścetyabhavatsa eva rodanadhvaniḥ ।। bālapravālakalikākomalāvayave śiśau ।
jāte nirjīvite śokānmumoha jananījanaḥ ।। tataḥ kuntī subhadrā ca sametya karuṇānidhim । bāṣpasaṃdigdhayā vācā rukmiṇīpatimūcatuḥ ।। svasreyasya yaśomūrterabhimanyoḥ priyasya te ।
bālasya bālastanayo jāto adya gatajīvanaḥ ।। karuṇārdre niśamyaitadbhagavānbhūtabhāvanaḥ । viveśa sūtikāveśma śauriḥ kalaśabhūṣitam ।। ratnadīptāṃśukapiśaṃ dīptauṣadhiśatācitam ।
mantrairbhiṣagbhiḥ śikhinā śastrairastraiśca rakṣitam ।। athottarā prāpya saṃjñāṃ śītavāribhirukṣitā । tamaṅke śiśumādāya vilalāpa hareḥ puraḥ ।। tato jaladagambhīraghoṣaḥ śaurirabhāṣata ।
dṛśā pīyūṣavarṣiṇyā vilokya śanakaiḥ śiśum ।। satyāddvijebhyo dharmācca yathā nānyatpriyaṃ mama । tena satyena bālo ayamastramukto adya jīvatu ।। mādhavenetyabhihite labdhajīvaḥ sa bālakaḥ ।
sūryāṃśubhiriva spṛṣṭo babhūvāmbujakorakaḥ ।। tataḥ pravṛtte vipule sahasā nagarotsave । nabhaścarāṇāmapyāsītyasādhu sādhviti niḥsvanaḥ ।। parikṣīṇe kurulaye yasmājjāto ayamarbhakaḥ ।
tasmātparīkṣinnāmnāstu jagādetyatha keśavaḥ ।। pirakṣijjanma ।। vyāsājñayā tato rājño yajñayogyo mahādhanaḥ । prāvartatoruratnāḍhyaḥ saṃbhāro bahukautukaḥ ।।
athotsṛjya vidhānena kṛṣṇaśāraṃ turaṅgamam । rakṣitaṃ pāṇḍuputreṇa svayaṃ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā ।। babhūva caitraśuklānte dīkṣito dharmanandanaḥ । hemamālādharo daṇḍī muṇḍaḥ kṛṣṇājināvṛtaḥ ।।
tatastrigartaviṣayaṃ prāpte yajñaturaṅgame । rājaputrairabhūdyuddhaṃ tumulaṃ savyasācinaḥ ।। yudhiṣṭhirājñā tasyābhūnna hantavyā nṛpā iti । tāṃ smarannāvadhīdbhūpānsa vijigye tu kevalam ।।
prāgjyotiṣeśvaraṃ vīraṃ bhagadattātmajaṃ yudhi । tribhirdinairvajradattaṃ jitvā kuñjarayodhinm ।। saindhavairakarodyuddhaṃ suciraṃ krūrayodhibhiḥ । pādacārī raṇe pārtho rathakuñjaravartibhiḥ ।।
pautraṃ jayadrathasyātha śiśumādāya duḥśalā । savyasācinamāsādya babhāṣe sāśrulocanā ।। bhrātastvayi samāyāte tvannāmaiva niśamya me । putro jāyadrathiryātaḥ pañcatāṃ sphaṭitāśayaḥ ।।
tatsuto mama pautro ayaṃ svasrayatanayastava । rakṣyaḥ sarvātmanetyuktvā ruroda dhṛtarāṣṭrajā ।। viṣaṇṇāstāṃ samāśvāsya pārtho bāṣpārdralocanaḥ । nindannijāṃ kṣattrajātiṃ jagāma turagānugaḥ ।।
śvetāśvamaśvagoptāraṃ maṇipūrapuraṃ tataḥ । prāptaṃ pratyudyayau rājā tatputro babhruvāhanaḥ ।। pūjāmādāya tanayaṃ namraṃ dṛṣṭvā puraḥ sthitam । yuddhārthī śakratanayo nābhyanandatkṛtāñjalim ।।
dṛṣṭvā māṃ sāyudhaṃ prāptaṃ sāmnā pratyudyato asi kim । dhiktvāmakṣattriyaṃ bhīrumityūce taṃ dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। atrāntare mahīṃ bhittvā samutthāyoragāṅganā । bhartuḥ pāṇḍusutasyāgre babhāṣe babhruvāhanam ।।
yuddhena tuṣyati pitā tavāyaṃ subhaṭapriyaḥ । vīrasaṃtānasaphalā śauryaśrīrabhimāninām ।। ityuktaḥ sa tayā dhanvī rathaṃ hemaharidhvajam । āruhyāmuktakavacaḥ pitaraṃ yoddhumāyayau ।।
tataḥ śaraśatairviddhastena śrānto dhanaṃjayaḥ । ānandanirbharastasya praśaśaṃsa parākramam ।। gāṇḍīvadhanvanā muktānnārācānvajragauravān । aprāptāneva ciccheda śaraiścitrāṅgadāsutaḥ ।।
athonmamātha putrasya syandanaṃ śakranandanaḥ । hemapattralatācitramudyānamiva mārutaḥ ।। vilokya virathaṃ putraṃ yudhyamānamasaṃbhramam । mandaprayatnaśithilānprāhiṇodvijayaḥ śarān ।।
atha tīkṣṇena hṛdaye pattriṇā babhruvāhanaḥ । vajreṇevācalabhidā jaghāna śvetavāhanam ।। avadhye sarvabhūtānāṃ putreṇa nihater'june । nādo babhūva gagane hā heti tridivaukasām ।।
pitaraṃ patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā śakraketumiva kṣitau । mumoha nindannātmānaṃ tyaktacāpor'junātmajaḥ ।। atha citrāṅgadābhyetya putreṇa nihataṃ patim । vilokya śokasaṃpannā vilalāpa sumadhyamā ।।
aho bata cirādetya jāyāyā mama mandiram । āryaputra tvayātithyaṃ prāptaṃ putrādbalīyasaḥ ।। aho nu hatabhāgyāhaṃ ciraviproṣitaṃ patim । tvāṃ prāptaṃ nayanānandaṃ paśyāmi nihataṃ kṣitau ।।
ityuktvā gāḍhamāliṅgya sā patiṃ bāṣpagadgadā । ulūpī nāgatanayā bhuvi citrāṅgadāpatat ।। labdhasaṃjño atha śokārtaḥ pralapanbabhruvāhanaḥ । śarīratyāganiyamaṃ cakre kilbiṣakūṇitaḥ ।।
tataḥ pradadhyau manasā nāgī saṃjīvanaṃ maṇim । sa ca dhyātastayā satyā nāgalokātsamāyayau ।। spṛṣṭo atha hṛdaye tena jīvitaṃ prāpya phalguṇaḥ । citrāṅgadā ca sahasā śokaṃ tyaktvā hriyaṃ yayau ।।
tato nivedya vṛttāntaṃ jagāda bhujagātmajā । ulūpī dhairyaladhiṃ suptotthicamivārjunam ।। śāpo bhīṣmavadhādeṣa dattaste vasubhiḥ purā । ko anyathā tvāṃ raṇe śakto jetuṃ nirjitadhūrjaṭim ।।
matpitā mayi vātsalyācchāpitā vasavaśca te । ūcustvacchāpanirvāṇaṃ ratnametanmahāprabham ।। śrutvaitadvismitaḥ pārtho nāgīṃ citrāṅgadāṃ tathā । parisāntvya śanaiḥ pūjāṃ jagrāha tanayārpitām ।।
tatastaṃ dayitaṃ vīraḥ putramāmantrya pāṇḍavaḥ । hayānusārī babhrāma vasudhāmabdhimekhalām ।। sa jitvā magadhādhīśaṃ jarāsaṃdhātmajātmajam । vaṅgānpuṇḍrānkirātāṃśca dākṣiṇātyānsamāgadhān ।।
gāndhārānsaubalasutānrājaputrānprahāriṇaḥ । āgantavyaṃ makhe rājñaḥ sarvairityādideśa tān ।। tataḥ pratinivṛttena turagena sahārjunaḥ । viveśa pūjitaḥ pauraurvijayī hastināpuram ।।
hayotsargaḥ ।। tataḥ pravṛtte vidhivadyajñe kanakavarṣiṇaḥ । rājño munijanākīrṇe prāpteṣvakhilarājasu ।। jananyā saha bhūpāle saṃprāpte babhruvāhane ।
sādaraṃ phalguṇaprītyā pūjite pāṇḍunandanaiḥ ।। niḥśeṣakalmaṣaploṣadivyadīkṣākṛtakṣaṇaḥ । kriyāmahīnāṃ vidadhe svayaṃ satyavatīsutaḥ ।। haimaṃ tatrābhavatsarvamiṣṭakācayanādikam ।
yūpabhāṇḍaghanasthālīparyaṅkagṛhatoraṇam ।। devarṣisiddhagandharvakiṃnarā maṅgalaṃ jaguḥ । karmāntareṣu yajñasya nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। śamite paśusaṅghe ca turagaṃ brāhmaṇottamāḥ ।
ālabhanta yathāśāstramupasaṃrodhya pārṣatīm ।। tataste yājakāstatra vapāmuddhṛtya vājinaḥ । śrapayitvā śubhaṃ dhūmaṃ pāṇḍavebhyo nyavedayan ।। tataḥ pūrṇe na vidhinā vyāsāya pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
catuḥsamudrarasanāṃ pṛthivīṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadhau ।। dattvātha hemakoṭīnāṃ koṭiṃ tadvacasā nṛpaḥ । brāhmaṇebhyaḥ punaḥ kṣoṇīṃ jagrāha muninārpitām ।। pūjayitvā narendreṇa mānārheṣvatha rājasu ।
visṛṣṭeṣvabhavatko api brahmasaṅghamahotsavaḥ ।। babhūvustatra vāhinyo madhunaḥ kṣīrasarpiṣām । babhuśca kulaśailābhā bhakṣyā modakarāśayaḥ ।। dvijebhyo dīyamāneṣu hemaratneṣu bhūbhujā ।
śakrāyudhairiva vyāptā diśo daśa cakāśire ।। dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saviduraḥ sañjayaḥ subalātmajāḥ । tasthurdaivatavattatra pūjyamānā mahībhujā ।। yajñaḥ ।।
atrāntare hemacitrapārśvo bilamukhodgataḥ । nakulo laghusaṃcāro yajñabhūmimupāyayau ।। sa manuṣyagirā prāha janayañjanakautukam । aho nu saktṛprasthena na tulyo ayaṃ mahāmakhaḥ ।।
nūnaṃ dānakaṇaḥ śuddhaḥ kṛśo api prathate nṛṇām । nūnaṃ bahudraviṇatā mithyaivotsavaḍambaraḥ ।। iti bruvāṇaḥ pṛṣṭo asau viprairvismayanirbharaiḥ । uvāca sraktuprasthasya māhātmyaṃ śrūyatāṃ dvijāḥ ।।
śilocchavṛttirabhavatkurukṣetre purā dvijaḥ । viśuddhasattvadraviṇaḥ kṛśo bahukuṭumbakaḥ ।। ghore kadāciddurbhikṣe kṣīṇavṛttiścireṇa saḥ । kṛcchrātkṣetraśataṃ bhrāntvā saktuprasthamavāptavān ।।
baiśvadevena vidhinā sa kṛtvāvaśyakaṃ gṛhe । kalatrasahito bhoktuṃ prasthito apaśyadarthinam ।। kṣutparītaḥ kṣudhākrāntaṃ sa taṃ dṛṣṭvātithiṃ dvijaḥ । dadau svamaśanaṃ tasmai saṃtoṣaviṣadāśayaḥ ।।
tadbhuktvā nābhavattasya kṣunnavṛttiryadārthinaḥ । tadbhāryā tatsutaścāsmai tatsnuṣā ca dadau tadā ।। sarveṣāṃ bhojanenātha tṛptaḥ so atithirabravīt । dharmastuṣṭo asmi sattvena mahatī siddhirastu vaḥ ।।
ityuktvāntarhite tasminvimānaistaraṇiprabhaiḥ । saśarīrā divaṃ prāpuḥ sarve te ślāghyavṛttayaḥ ।। athāhaṃ saktugandhena samāhūto bilāśrayaḥ । tāmucchiṣṭabhuvaṃ prāpto bhuktavānyatra so atithiḥ ।।
tatpātrasalilaspṛṣṭamekaṃ pārśvamidaṃ mama । luṭhitaṃ hemaruciraṃ jātaṃ puṇyairivāplutam ।। dvitīyapārśvacintā me kathaṃ haimaṃ bhavediti । babhūva suciraṃ tasmātprāpto ahaṃ vasudhādhipam ।।
dvijalakṣasahasrāṇāmiha bhojanabhūmiṣu । bhrāntasyāpi na saṃjātaḥ ko api kānto lavastanau ।। tasmānna saktuprasthasya samatāmarhati kratuḥ । ityuktvā nakulaḥ prāyāccitrakāntiradarśanam ।।
evaṃ yajñasahasrebhyaḥ śreyasī bhāvaśuddhatā । manasaḥ kila vaimalyaṃ paraṃ brahma pracakṣate ।। agastyasya purā satre viprā dvādaśavārṣike । śaśaṃsurbhāvinīṃ ghorāmanāvṛṣṭiṃ parasparam ।।
tato agastyaḥ parityajya dravyayajñaṃ mahāmatiḥ । cakāra stabdhamanasā dhyānayajñaṃ taponidhiḥ ।। sa eva vasusaṃpannaḥ sarvavitkṛtasaṃnidhiḥ । kraturbabhūva yenendro vavarṣānandanirbharaḥ ।।
śreyānsattvaviśuddhasya pāṇḍavasyābhavatkratuḥ । kiṃ tu svakāryānnakulastatra cakre vimānanām ।। jijñāsurjamadagniṃ prāksvayaṃ krodhaḥ śvavigrahaḥ । pasparśa jihvayā śrāddhe dhṛtaṃ hi piṭhire payaḥ ।।
krodho ayamiti vijñāya munistaṃ jñānalocanaḥ । na śaśāpa tato bhītaḥ krodhaḥ kampākulo abhavat ।। tataste pitaraḥ kruddhā yeṣāṃ śrāddhe dhṛtaṃ payaḥ । aśapansuciraṃ yena krodho nakulatāṃ yayau ।।
avamānakathāṃ kṛtvā svayaṃ yaudhiṣṭhire kratau । śāpakṣayaṃ prāpsyasīti tairevāsya kṛto avadhiḥ ।। nakulopākhyānam ।। iti sakalanarendrairvandyamānasya rājño dvijajanaparipuṣṭaḥ sattvapuṣpaprakāraḥ ।
śubhaphalanicayādyo yajñasaṃbhāramūlaścaritatarurudāraḥ satyaśākho rarāja ।। nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। ekacchatrāṃ mahīṃ rājñi praśāsati yudhiṣṭhire ।
nāśrūyatārtijaḥ śabdo na cādṛśyata yācakaḥ ।। yaśasā dharmavīrasya tasya vyāpte jagattraye । rāghavādikathābandheṣvabhūnmandācaro janaḥ ।। dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ saviduro gāndhārī ca pativratā ।
satataṃ daivataṃ tasya babhūvuḥ pratimāṃ vinā ।। rāja ṣaḍrasavaicitryaveśavāravidhāyinaḥ । bhojane dhṛtarāṣṭrasya sa sūdānsvayamaikṣata ।। tacchāsanānnāpriyāṇi kuruvṛddhasya pāṇḍavāḥ ।
aślīlaṃ dadataḥ sarve prativādaṃ pracakrire ।। rājārhaṃ bhojanaṃ bhuṅkte sarvamevāmbikāsutaḥ । iti viśrāvya gūḍhaṃ tu so abhavatphalabhojanaḥ ।। aho vratavatastasya jāpinaḥ kṣitiśāyinaḥ ।
jāyāsakhasya vairāgyaṃ bubudhe na yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। evaṃ nivasatāṃ teṣāṃ mithaḥ praṇayaśālinām । kāle pravāhini yayuḥ samaḥ pañcādhikā daśa ।। kadācidatha saṃsmṛtya bhīmaḥ kauravadurnayān ।
cakāra tadvadhakathāṃ bahuśabdaṃ ca durmadaḥ ।। dhṛtarāṣṭro jitakrodhastadākarṇya vadhūsakhaḥ । vidhāyāśrutavatsarvamabhūtsaṃnyāsalālasaḥ ।। tatastasyātinirvedādbhāvabhramaparāṅbhukham ।
babhuva śamakāmasya vairāgyābharaṇaṃ manaḥ ।। viyogaśatadagdhānāmavamānaviṣāśinām । sarvatyāgaḥ sukhāyaiva nirvāṇāmṛtanirjharaḥ ।। sa yudhiṣṭhiramabhyetya vanavāsasamutsukaḥ ।
uvāca niyamakṣāmo damopaśamamanthanam ।। varṇāśramaguro rājannanujānīhi pārtha mām । daśāṃ vṛddhocitāṃ labdhuṃ vrajāmyeṣa tapovanam ।। iyaṃ bhavasukhāsvādaratistatparacetasām ।
nṛṇāmajīrṇatṛṣṇeva satataṃ parivardhate ।। spṛśa māṃ puṇyagandhena vapuṣā dharmanandana । svasti te pāhi pṛthivīṃ putravatpaśya ca prajāḥ ।। kośadurgabalādāne kurvīthā yatnamuttamam ।
gūḍhamantraḥ prajāpāla unmūlā hi nṛpaśriyaḥ ।। ityuktvā mūrdhnyupāghrāya nirāhāraḥ kṛśo nṛpam । kampamānatanurvṛddho babhūva gamanotsukaḥ ।। taṃ sāśrulocano rājā yayāce racitāñjaliḥ ।
māmutsṛjya kathaṃ nāma gantumarhasi kānanam ।। tvatpādasevāsaṃtoṣaṃ tyuktuṃ nāhamihotsahe । vītarāgasya te tāta gṛheṣveva tapovanam ।। iti tenārthyamāno api bubudhe na yadā sa tat ।
tadā satyavatīsūnurmuniḥ svayamupāyayau ।। sa dharmarājamabhyetya babhāṣe jñānalocanaḥ । tyajyatāmeṣa bhūpāla vṛddho yātu tapovanam ।। śrutasya vayaso buddhervivekasya kulasya ca ।
supakvamanasāṃ kāle vairāgyaṃ paramaṃ phalam ।। jarāśubhreṣu keśeṣu praśānte viṣayādare । tapovanātparaṃ manye bhūṣaṇaṃ na śarīriṇām ।। ityuktvāntarhite vyāse viṣaṇṇena mahībhujā ।
kṛcchrādiva tathetyukto jaharṣa kurupuṃgavaḥ ।। sa kṛtvā bhīṣmamukhyānāṃ gurūṇāṃ śrāddhamuttamam । mahārhaḥ vipulaṃ dānaṃ dadau brāhmaṇasaṃmatam ।। dadatastasya no vighnaṃ cakrire pāṇḍunandanāḥ ।
bhamastu kopatāmrākṣo dhanaṃjayamabhāṣata ।। kilbiṣaṃ yaiḥ kṛtaṃ ghoraṃ purāsmāsu bahucchalam । kauravāṇāṃ kathaṃ śrāddhe teṣāṃ vittavyayaṃ sahe ।। yātu duryodhanaḥ pāpo narakaṃ sahito anujaiḥ ।
vayaṃ śrāddhaṃ kariṣyāmaḥ svayaṃ śaṃtanunandane ।। iti bruvāṇamasakṛnnivārya pavanātmajam । naitadvācyaṃ punariti provāca śvetavāhanaḥ ।। atha pratasthe gāndhāryā saha rājāmbikāsutaḥ ।
gāvalganisakhaḥ paurānāmantrya vidurānugaḥ ।। putrairudaśrunayanaiḥ snuṣābhiścārthitā bhṛśam । kuntī tapovanaruciṃ nātyajaddevarānugā ।। athāgre sahitaḥ kuntyā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ sahānujaḥ ।
rājarṣijuṣṭaṃ vipinaṃ viveśa viśadāśayaḥ ।। tatra rājarṣivaryeṇa śatayūpena saṃgataḥ । jaṭāvalkalabhṛccakre sānujaḥ suciraṃ tapaḥ ।। taṃ tīvraniyamakṣāmaṃ nāradādyā maharṣayaḥ ।
kṛtakṛtyatayā prāptaṃ draṣṭavyā draṣṭumāyayuḥ ।। sarvābhirbharatastrībhiḥ sahitāste mahārathāḥ । nidhāya kānanopānte caturaṅge mahadbalam ।। apanītasitacchattracāmarāḥ pādacāriṇaḥ ।
tapovanaṃ praviviśurdhṛtarāṣṭreṇa sevitam ।। te praṇamyāmbikāsūnuṃ jananīṃ saṃjayaṃ tathā । viṣaṇṇāḥ prayayurmūrcchāṃ snāyuśeṣānvilokya tān ।। dhṛtarāṣṭro api rājānaṃ saṃjayena niveditam ।
papraccha kuśalaṃ kośe paure janapade tathā ।। tapovṛddhiṃ tataḥ pṛṣṭvā kuruvṛddhaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ । viduraḥ kveti papraccha sa ca pṛṣṭastamabravīt ।। vāyubhakṣo asthiśeṣāṅgaḥ svecchācārī nirambaraḥ ।
viduro asminvane putra dṛśyate na ca dṛśyate ।। ityukte dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa samabhyāyādyadṛcchayā । viduro dhūlidigdhāṅgo bilvamātramukhaḥ kṛśaḥ ।। āśrame sa janaṃ dṛṣṭvā palāyanaparo abhavat ।
tamanvadhāvadekākī sāśrunetro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। dṛśyaḥ kvacidadṛśyaśca vidurastamanādarāt । apaśyadvītarāgāṇāṃ tṛṇe rājñi ca tulyatā ।। sa vṛkṣamūlamāśritya jñānadeho jvalanniva ।
ukto yudhiṣṭhiro asmīti rājñā saṃbhāṣaṇārthinā ।। nirnimeṣekṣaṇo maunī taṃ vīkṣya kṣapitāśayaḥ । netrapāṇendriyaiḥ kṣipraṃ tameva sahasāviśat ।। dehaṃ nirmokavattyaktvā praviṣṭe vidure nṛpaḥ ।
vihāya rājasaṃ bhāvaṃ babhūva jñānanirbharaḥ ।। dagdhumabhyudyataṃ kṣatturatha tatra kalevaram । yudhiṣṭhiraṃ vyomacarā jñānasiddhā nyavārayan ।। tataḥ sametya tatsarvaṃ dhṛtarāṣṭrāya bhūpatiḥ ।
nivedya tasthau nirduḥkhaḥ sānujo māturantike ।। phalāhāraḥ kṣamāśāyī kṣapayitvātha śarvarīm । prātardatvā yathākāmaṃ dvijebhyo ratnakāñcanam ।। rājarṣibhiḥ sahāsīnaṃ praṇamya kurupuṃgavam ।
dadarśa tejasāṃ rāśiṃ prāptaṃ satyavatīsutam ।। vyāso api dharmatanayaṃ saṃbhāvya racitāñjalim । yatidharmeṇa tāṃ siddhiṃ ślāghyāṃ kṣatturapūjayat ।। arthitaḥ kṣatravṛddhena gāndhāryā pṛthayā tayā ।
paralokagatānsarvānbhūpālānsaha kauravaiḥ ।। adarśayatkurustrīṇāṃ vyāsaḥ svarganadījale । sādhvyo api tānanuyayurvimānaistyaktavigrahāḥ ।। atha dharmātmajo rājā tatra saptarṣisevite ।
māsaṃ sthitvā puraṃ prāyātkuruvṛddhena coditaḥ ।। rathāśvakuñjarānīkaiḥ sa gatvā niḥśvasanmuhuḥ । akāma iva kṛcchreṇa rājadhānīṃ samāviśat ।। atha dharmeṇa vasudhāṃ dharmarājasya śāsataḥ ।
yāti kāle suramunirnāradaḥ samupāyayau ।। dhṛtarāṣṭrakathāṃ pṛṣṭaḥ pūjitaḥ sa mahībhujā । uvāca rājanyāto asau rājarṣiḥ paramāṃ gatim ।। saṃvatsaraṃ vāyubhakṣo varṣaṃ ca tyaktabhojanaḥ ।
kandukākāravadano durlakṣyaḥ so abhavatkṛśaḥ ।। tataḥ sa vahnīṃstatyāja mumukṣurniṣkriyo muniḥ । kānane te apyavartanta jarattarunirantare ।। tatra priyāsakho rājā kuntyā saha mahāmatiḥ ।
vanaṃ prajvalitaṃ dṛṣṭvā samādhi vidadhe param ।। avyāptā vyāpakāḥ svacchāḥ svayaṃ galitavṛttayaḥ । sphucabrahmāṇḍavivarāste dhāma paramaṃ yayuḥ ।। evaṃ śamāṅkurasteṣāṃ sarvasaṃnyāsapallavaḥ ।
svāntaprakāśakusumaḥ phalito jñānapādapaḥ ।। tato dāvāgninā tena dagdhāste bandhunā yathā । saṃjayastu vratakṣāmo yātastuhinabhūdharam ।। śrutvaitatpāṇḍutanayo vyāptaḥ śokakṛṣāṇu nā ।
śuśoca sānujaḥ kuntīṃ sasutaṃ ca kurūdvaham ।। tataḥ prayāte devarṣau rājā kṛtvā jalakriyām । tānevoddiśya vipulaṃ dadau draviṇamakṣayam ।। so atha dhairyaṃ samālambya śokamutsārya dehajam ।
saṃsārāsāratāṃ dhyāyanvivekaśaraṇo abhavat ।। bhāvāḥ svabhāvaviśarārava eva teṣu saktaṃ mano na virahe sahate anutāpam । tatsarvathā priyaviyogaviṣāhatānāṃ śāntyai sudhā tanubhṛtāṃ vipulo vivekaḥ ।। nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam ।
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। mahīṃ mahībhṛtāṃ dhurye dharmarāje praśāsati । ṣaḍviṃśe abde mahābhāgā dvārakāṃ munayo yayuḥ ।। tāndṛṣṭvā kauśikamukhānpraharṣanmadaviplutāḥ ।
sāmbaṃ kṛtvā vadhūveśaṃ papracchurvṛṣṇipuṃgavāḥ ।। api putraḥ sutā vāsyā bhaviṣyati munīśvarāḥ । tacchrutvā te avadannasyāḥ kulamṛtyurbhaviṣyati ।। musalaṃ brahmadaṇḍākhyamityuktvādarśanaṃ yayuḥ ।
lauhaṃ sāmbastato asūta musalaṃ vajrasaṃhatam ।। tadāhvako bhayātpiṣṭvā tūrṇaṃ tatyāja sāgare । sarvajño jñātavṛttānto vṛṣṇikṣayamupasthitam ।। vijñāya kaiṭabhārātistīrthayātrārasādyayau ।
caṇḍāṃśumaṇḍaloccaṇḍaṃ tataścakraṃ suradviṣaḥ ।। ratho dhvajaśca sauvarṇaḥ sahasāntaradhīyata । atha mārjāravicchāye kabandhāvṛtamaṇḍale ।। sūrye vighaṭṭitāśeṣadiktaṭe vāti mārute ।
muṇḍo viṭaṅkavadano yādavānāṃ gṛhe gṛhe ।। saṃdarśya vadanaṃ prāyādvācānviṣṭo apyadṛśyata । cītkārapuruṣaḥ śabdaḥ śārikānāṃ gṛheṣvabhūt ।। gṛdhragomāyunādena rājamārgau'pyapūryata ।
viparītā prasūtiśca paśūnāmabhavattadā ।। kośeṣu kanakābandhe ratnāni svayamasphuṭan । teṣu ghoranimitteṣu jāteṣvapyaviśaṅkitāḥ ।। babhūvurvṛṣṇayo bhānti na hi nāśeṣu buddhayaḥ ।
prabhāsamatha saṃprāpte kṛṣṇe yādavavṛṣṇayaḥ ।। tameva deśamabhyetya cakrire vipulotsavam । udyāneṣu vicitreṣu vijahnustatra te sukham ।। gītanṛtyarasāsaktāḥ kalitāḥ kālacakṣuṣā ।
āpānakelisaṃsakte tato vṛṣṇikule abhavat ।। vivāde yuddhasaṃbaddhaḥ śaineyakṛtavarmaṇoḥ । hārdikyaṃ sātyākiḥ prāha suptahā sauptiko bhavān ।। sa tamūce tvayā prāyagato bhūriśravā hataḥ ।
evaṃ vivādātsaṃgrāmasteṣāmāsītsudāruṇaḥ ।। prāktasmādvajramusalātprajātairvallarīcayaiḥ । tṛṇamapyabhavattatra brahmadaṇḍamadotkaṭam ।। kṣayāya musalībhūtaṃ sahasāndhakavṛṣṇiṣu ।
yā bhūdāpānabhūsteṣāṃ lalanānayanotsavaḥ ।। saiva mṛtyorabhūddhorasaṃhārāhāramaṇḍapaḥ । sāmbe gade cārudoṣṇi pradyumne kṛtavarmaṇi ।। aniruddhe ca śaineye nihate paśyato hareḥ ।
vṛtte vṛṣṇikṣaye ghore strīśeṣā yādave kule ।। dvārakā prarurodeva cchinnahārāśrunirjharaiḥ । tataḥ śaurirhaladharaṃ draṣṭuṃ duḥkhākulo vrajan ।। dārukaṃ tatkathayituṃ prāhiṇotsavyasācine ।
yoṣitāṃ dasturakṣāyai babhrumādāya keśavaḥ ।। gatvā janakamāmantrya rauhiṇeyamupāyayau । athāpaśyanmukhāttasya niḥsṛtaṃ madhusūdanaḥ ।। sahasraśīrṣaṃ bhujagaṃ śvetaṃ śvetācalopamam ।
vāsukipramukhairnāgairatha pratyudyataiḥ saha ।। dṛṣṭvārṇavaṃ praviṣṭaṃ taṃ varuṇenārcitaṃ punaḥ । gatijñaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ na śuśoca janārdanaḥ ।। bhave hyabhāvasadbhāve bhāvānāṃ sthiratā kutaḥ ।
anantadhāmni milite balabhadre sakānane ।। praviśya yogī suṣvāpa nibaddhaprāṇadhāraṇaḥ । taṃ svajyotiṣi saṃsaktaṃ lubdhako mṛgaśaṅkayā ।। jaghāna niśitāgreṇa śareṇa caraṇodare ।
kṛṣṇaśāradhiyā kṛṣṇo lubdhakeneṣuṇā hataḥ ।। nārāyaṇākhyamaviśatparaṃ dhāma sanātanam । surasiddharṣigandharvaiḥ pūjyamāne saha śriyā ।। viṣṇuṃ praviṣṭe govinde babhūva kṣubhitaṃ jagat ।
atrāntare dārukena kathite yādavakṣaye ।। śokaṃ trāsaṃ ca dainyaṃ ca bhejire pāṇḍavāḥ param । tato yudhiṣṭhiragirā dvārakāṃ śvetavāhanaḥ ।। dārukenaiva sahitaḥ prayayau śokamūrcchitaḥ ।
sa prāpa yādavapurīmapadmāmiva padminīm ।। vṛṣṇisiṃhairvirahitā guhāṃ haimavatīmiva । kaṣṭairariṣṭanicayaiḥ spṛṣṭāṃ duḥkhādvilokya tām ।। draṣṭuṃ viveśa śokārtaṃ janakaṃ kaṃsavidviṣaḥ ।
tārapralāpamukharairvṛtaṃ vṛṣṇivadhūjanaiḥ ।। ṣoḍaśastrīsahasrāṇi kalatraṃ kamalāpateḥ । saubhadrajanako dṛṣṭvā mumoha bhayavihvalam ।। śayānaṃ bhuvi pārtho api vasudevaṃ pralāpinam ।
vilokya śokavivaśo vajrabhinna ivāpatat ।। kva rāmaḥ kva ca govindaḥ kva pradyumnaḥ kva sātyakiḥ । aho vidherduranteyaṃ śaktirityarjuno avadat ।। maṇikaṅkaṇajhāṅkārinṛttagītaghanadhvaniḥ ।
aviśrāntamabhūdyatra śravaṇānandanirjharaiḥ ।। tatraiva vṛṣṇinārīṇāṃ śṛṇvannārodanadhvanim । niśāṃ nināya bībhatsurnirapāyamayīṃ śriyam ।। tataḥ prātaḥ priyasuto vasudevaḥ priyāṃ tanum ।
tatyāja devakīmukhyairanuyāto vadhūjanaiḥ ।। tataḥ sāttvatamukhyānāṃ sarveṣāṃ śokavihvalaḥ । pārthaḥ śarīraṃ saṃskṛtya cakāra salilakriyām ।। vajrābhidhānaṃ kṛṣṇasya pautraṃ kuntīsutastataḥ ।
ādāya vṛṣṇikāntāśca pratasthe dārukānugaḥ ।। atha dvāravatīṃ sphārataraṅgabhujamaṇḍalaiḥ । śaṅkhāṭṭahāsavikaṭo jahāra makarākaraḥ ।। hate vṛṣṇipure kṣipraṃ ratnalobhādivābdhinā ।
puruṣānugataṃ sarvamityūce duḥkhito janaḥ ।। kalatraṃ vṛṣṇisiṃhānāmādāya śvetavāhanaḥ । indraprasthaṃ vrajanprāpa durgamāṃ vikaṭāṭavīm ।। dasyavastatra gopālā balinaḥ paśujīvinaḥ ।
adṛṣṭapūrvāḥ svaryoṣitsubhagāḥ sāttvatāṅganāḥ ।। taḍittaralaratnāṃśupuñjaritāmbarāḥ । vilokya lobhavaśagā hartumabhyudyayurbalāt ।। gopānāpatitāndṛṣṭā tānugralaguḍāyudhān ।
gāṇḍīvadhanvā gāṇḍīpamadhijyamakarotkrudhā ।। kālaśaktihatasyāpi tasyāpi kṣapitadviṣaḥ । na śaktirabhavatkācitkṣīṇeṣorjyāvikarṣaṇe ।। cāpayaṣṭiranāyattā tasyābhūdatiduḥkhagā ।
vṛddhasyeva daridrasya taruṇī rūpiṇī vadhūḥ ।। tasya kopāgnitaptasya vṛthā bhrūbhaṅgakāriṇaḥ । bhṛtyā ivāvinītasya babhūvuravaśāḥ śarāḥ ।। te divyāstragaṇāḥ kvāpi jagmurutsṛjya taṃ mṛdhe ।
guṇasaṅgāmanādṛtya dhūrtā mitramivādhanam ।। sa niḥśaśvāsa vipulairmārgaṇaiḥ parivarjitaḥ । kṣīṇakośa iva tyāgī vailakṣyavinatānanaḥ ।। tato niṣpratibhe tatra pārthe sarvāyudhakṣayāt ।
vṛṣṇipaurāṅganā jahrurnirvivekā vanecarāḥ ।। na tu pradhānanārīṣu teṣāmāsītpragalbhatā । anarhasya mahārheṣu nīcasyojasvitā katham ।। taiḥ prasahya hṛte straiṇe bhagnamāno dhanaṃjayaḥ ।
pratasthe nijadordaṇḍe sāsūyāḥ pātayandṛśaḥ ।। aho balavatī devī saṃsāre asminnanityatā । aho niḥsāraparyantā bhāvānāṃ prabhaviṣṇutā ।। aho sarvakaṣaḥ kālaścitrapākamaho jagat ।
vijite vijayo gopairduḥkhādityavadajjanaḥ ।। dhiganityavilāsasya vibhramabhrāntikāriṇaḥ । dhāturadbhutanirmāṇavinodaviśarārutām ।। ākhaṇḍalaprabhṛtayaḥ khāṇḍave yena khaṇḍitāḥ ।
kairāte tripurārātiḥ samare yena toṣitaḥ ।। jitvā tamapi gopālā varākāḥ suhṛdaṃ hareḥ । jahrurviṣṇukalatrāṇi dhikkālasya durantatām ।। revatīṃ rukmiṇīṃ satyabhāmāṃ jāmbavatīṃ tathā ।
vajraṃ pautraṃ ca kaṃsāreranyāśca yaduyoṣitaḥ ।। ādāya phalguṇaḥ śocannindraprasthaṃ samāviśat । sabāṣpaṃ paurasaṃghātairabhitaḥ parivāritaḥ ।। rājye nidhāya tatraiva vajraṃ yāte dhanaṃjaye ।
satyabhāmānugā devyaḥ pāvakaṃ viviśuḥ śucā ।। vrajanvṛṣṇiviyogārtaḥ kirīṭi hastināpuram । parāvarajñaṃ bhāvānāṃ vane vyāsaṃ vyalokayat ।। duḥkhānnyavedayattasmai ghoraṃ vṛṣṇikulakṣayam ।
ātmanaścāttacāpasya gopaiḥ pathi parābhavam ।। tamabravījjñānanidhirmunirāśvāsya mūrcchitam । putra kālavilāsānāṃ sarvametadvijṛmbhitam ।। matirvibhūtayo bhogāḥ prabhāvāḥ śaktayo guṇāḥ ।
sarvathā kālakalayā nīyate smṛtiśeṣatām ।। dhruvaṃ sarvaparityāge na kuryurmunayo matim । avasānaikavirasā yadi na syādbhavasthitiḥ ।। ityukto muninā pārthaḥ prayayau hastināpuram ।
prabhāvaṃ vṛṣṇisiṃhasya kalayanbhṛśavihvalaḥ ।। nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। atha vṛṣṇikṣayaṃ śrutvā dharmasūnurdhanaṃjayāt ।
namaḥ kālāya baline niḥśvasannityabhāṣata ।। sarvatyāgakṛto yogo viveśa bhrātṛbhiḥ saha । rājyaṃ dauryodhanaṃ dattvā guṇāhārya yuyutsave ।। nije parikṣitaṃ rājye sthāpayitvābhimanyujam ।
tatpālane samādiśya subhadraṃ satyaśāsanaḥ ।। prakṛtibhyo vinikṣipya taṃ dvijebhyaśca dharmavit । śrāddhaṃ vidhāya bandhubhyaḥ puṇyāmiṣṭiṃ ca naiṣṭhikīm ।। agnīnutsṛjya salile paurānāśvāsya duḥkhitān ।
devīmāmantrya vasudhāṃ sānujo draupadīsakhaḥ । pratasthe sarvasaṃnyāsī yogayukto yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। tataḥ sametya bhagavānsvayameva hutāśanaḥ । pārthājjagrāha gāṇḍīvaṃ tau cākṣayyau maheṣudhī ।।
śvā tānanuyayāveko vāryamāṇo api yatnataḥ । atha te śanakaiḥ prāpurdiśaṃ dakṣiṇapaścimām ।। dṛṣṭvā tatra samudreṇa bhṛtāṃ dvāravatīṃ jalaiḥ । āśāmudīcīṃ prayayurbhuvaḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam ।।
himācalamatikramya prāptāste vālukārṇavam । dadṛśurmerumuttuṅgaśṛṅgāliṅgitanandanam ।। niragāre nirālambe tasminnadhvani dustare । śirīṣapelavatanuḥ papāta drupadātmajā ।।
tāṃ yātajīvitāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhīmaḥ prāha yudhiṣṭhiram । rājanpāñcālarājasya suteyaṃ patitā bhuvi ।। cintayannapi paśyāmi nāsyāḥ kimapi kilbiṣam । kasmādeṣā tapoyegaṃ tyaktvā pañcatvamāgatā ।।
dharmasūnurniśamyaitadanāvṛttamukho avadat । babhuva pakṣapāto asyāḥ sarvadābhyadhikor'june ।। ityukte bhūmipālena sahadevo apatadbhuvi । tasminnipatite pṛṣṭo bhīmenoce nṛpaḥ punaḥ ।।
eṣa prajñābhimānena jaḍaṃ jagadamanyata । iti dharmasutenokte papāta nakulaḥ kṣitau ।। rājā pṛṣṭo atha bhīmena vrajannevābravītpunaḥ । rūpamānī smareṇāpi spardhāmeṣa na ca kṣamī ।।
ityukte vrajatā rājñā nipapāta dhanaṃjayaḥ । punaśca pṛṣṭo bhīmena jagāda jagatīpatiḥ ।। śūramānī cacāraiṣa śithilaṃ samarāṅgane । iti bruvāṇo bhūpālo jagāmaivāviluptadhīḥ ।।
bhīmastato nipatitaḥ patito asmītyuvāca tam । so abravīdbaladarpo abhūdbhīma bahvaśanasya te ।। tato abhūdeka evātha vrajannanugataḥ śunā । dadarśa sākṣādāyātaṃ rathenendraṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।।
rājanmatpuramehīti śakreṇokto jagāda saḥ । śunā virahitaḥ svargaṃ saśarīro na kāmaye ।। tamabravītsurapatiḥ śunāṃ svarge kuto gatiḥ । dhiṣṇyamārohatu śveti tvadanyaḥ ko anubhāṣate ।।
tatastamūce nṛpatirbhaktatyāgaṃ kathaṃ sahe । bhaktavidveṣiṇaḥ svarge nṛśaṃsasya kuto gatiḥ ।। yadyasti sukutaṃ kiṃcinmama tena sureśvara । yātu svargaṃ sadehaḥ svā nainaṃ tyaktuṃ samutsahe ।।
strīvadhenaiva sadṛśaṃ brahmasvaharaṇena ca । sarvapāpātmakaṃ santo bhaktatyāgaṃ pracakṣate ।। ityukte dharmarājena dharmastyaktvā śvavigraham । tamūce putra tuṣṭo asmi sadvṛttena tavāmunā ।।
dṛṣṭo asi pāthaso hetoḥ purā dvaitavane mayā । svasti te vraja bhūpāla saśarīraḥ surālayam ।। iti pitrā samādiṣṭo vimānaṃ vipulaprabham । āruhya puṇyasopānaṃ viveśa suramandiram ।।
pūjyamānaḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ munibhirnāradādibhiḥ । rājarṣitārakāmadhye sa rarājāṃśumāniva ।। tataḥ sa śakramavadbhrātaro yatra me sthitāḥ । śyāmā ca yatra dayitā tatra vāso mamepsitaḥ ।।
tamabravītsahasrākṣo bhāvaṃ mā mānuṣaṃ gamaḥ । rājarṣibhiranāsādyāṃ prāpto asi gatimuttamām ।। ityukto apyasakṛdyatnādvajriṇā dharmanandanaḥ । bhrātṝnavāptumicchāmītyabhāṣata punaḥ punaḥ ।।
nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। tataḥ svargaśriyā juṣṭaṃ bhrājiṣṇumukuṭāṅgadam । dadarśa śakrasaṃkāśaṃ kururājaṃ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।।
taṃ vīkṣya sānujaṃ tatra jātamanyuḥ śatakratum । uvāca svasti devebhyaḥ svargāyāstvayamañjaliḥ ।। yatra duryodhanaḥ pāpaḥ pṛthivīkṣayakāraṇam । sumerukūṭavikaṭe vibhāti paramāsane ।।
na tatra mama vāso asti vrajāmyeṣa namo astu te । yatra me bhrātaraḥ śūrāstatra vāso mamādhunā ।। iti rājño bruvāṇasya devadūtaṃ surāstataḥ । bhrātṝnprati prayāhīti prāhurvāyumanojavam ।।
sa devadūtādiṣṭena vrajansapadi vartmanā । dadarśa puruṣānghorānnarakāntaravartinaḥ ।। keśaśoṇitamāṃsāsṛgvasāsaṃghātapicchile । praklinnānekakuṇapavyākīrṇakṛmisaṃkule ।।
kākakaṅkabakolūkavadanairabhito vṛte । śavadurgandhanīrandhrasaṃghaṭṭaśatasaṃkule ।। karapattraśilāpākasaṃtaptasikatātaṭe । lohitailavasākumbhakūṭaśalmalidāruṇe ।।
kṣurakaṇṭakakīlograjvālāstambhavibhīṣaṇe । taptavaitaraṇīvisrapūyapūritasaikate ।। asipatravanotkṛttanaranārīkṛtasvane । ghorāndhakāragahane tatra śuśrāva dharmajaḥ ।।
pāpināṃ kvāthyamānānāmākrandaṃ dhṛtidāruṇam । kṣaṇamekamito rājanmā nivartasva śītalaiḥ ।। tvatpuṇyavātaiḥ spṛṣṭānāmasmākaṃ bādhate tamaḥ । vayaṃ bhīmaprabhṛtayaḥ pāṇḍavā bhrātarastava ।।
kṛṣṇā ceyaṃ varārohā mahiṣī vallabhā satī । śrutvaitatkaruṇaṃ rājā vajreṇeva vidāritaḥ ।। tatraiva tasthau nirdvandvo nindandurlalitaṃ vidheḥ । so avadadbata devānāmavicārahataiva dhīḥ ।।
yaireta dharmaniratāḥ kleśe asminsamupekṣitāḥ । ayaṃ mohaḥ prasādo vā viveko nāyamīdṛśaḥ ।। vibudhānāṃ na jānanti ye dharmasya vyatikramam । bhramaḥ svapno atha māyeyaṃ kimetaditi cintayan ।।
devadūta na jānāmi kasyedaṃ durviceṣṭate । ihaivāhaṃ sthito gaccha na me svargeṇa kāraṇam ।। pūjyante yatra durvṛttā viśasyante nu sādhavaḥ । ityukto dharmarājena devadūtaḥ surādhipam ।।
gatvā vyajijñapatsarvaṃ sa ca tūṣṇīṃ samāyayau । prāpte surādhipe tatra saha dharmādibhiḥ suraiḥ ।। nādṛśyatāśubhaṃ kiṃcidvavau puṇyaśca mārutaḥ । tato abravītsurapatirviṣṇaṃ dharmanandanam ।।
asatyametannāyeyaṃ mayaiveha pradarśitā । etadālokanaṃ rājñāmavaśyaṃ miśrakarmaṇām ।। asatyaleśasaṃsparśādetaddroṇavadhāttava । ehi paśya nijānbhrātṝndivyaṃ svapadamāśritān ।।
svargaśriyaṃ ca pāñcālīṃ putrāṃścāmaratāṃ gatān । ityukte devarājena vītaśokī yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।। snātvā dharmagirā svargagaṅgāmbhasi nabhaḥprabhe । utsṛjya mānuṣaṃ bhāvaṃ puṇyāṃ surasabhāṃ yayau ।।
apsaronṛttalalitāngāyangandharvakiṃnarān । tatra svapadamārūḍhānapaśyadanujānnijān ।। maṇḍale ca raveḥ karṇaṃ svayamindreṇa darśitam । abhibhanyuṃ ca rucirākāranirjitamanmatham ।।
varcobhidhānaṃ somasya taṃ sutaṃ somamaṇḍale । gandharvarājaṃ sākṣācca dhṛtarāṣṭraṃ janeśvaram ।। vasuṃ śāntanavaṃ bhīṣmaṃ guruṃ droṇaṃ bṛhaspatim । nārāyaṇaṃ ca viśveśaṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।।
yadaṃśā bhuvi ye jātāstāṃśca dṛṣṭvā tadāśrayān । āsasāda sadānandaṃ vandyaṃ nandanavāsinām । dharmasūnurnidhirdhāmnāṃ hariścandrocitaṃ padam ।। atha nahuṣadilīpadhundhumārasagarabhagīratharāmakārtavīryaiḥ ।
nṛpatibhirabhito abhivandyamānaḥ sitacaritaḥ sa rarāja rājacandraḥ ।। śrutveti bhāratakathāṃ vaiśampāyanakīrtitām । saṃpannasarpasatro abhūnnirvṛtto janamejayaḥ ।। etatsūtena kathitaṃ naimiṣāraṇyavāsinaḥ ।
niśamya śaunakamukhāstasthurānandanirbharāḥ ।। nārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam । devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।। muniḥ punātu vo vyāsaḥ sadā saṃnihitā sukhe ।
trimārgagā madhumatī yasya śuddhā sarasvatī ।। śaunakena punaḥ pṛṣṭo naimiṣe laumaharṣaṇiḥ । abhyadhādadbhutaṃ bhūmau saṃbhavaṃ kaiṭabhadviṣaḥ ।। ākarṇya bhāratakathāṃ prahṛṣṭo janamejayaḥ ।
apṛcchadvaiṣṇavaṃ vaṃśaṃ vaiśampāyanamādarāt ।। sa pṛṣṭaḥ pṛṣuvaṃśena pārthivena kathāṃ hareḥ । jagāda jagatāṃ hetuṃ praṇamya prayataḥ prabhum ।। apa evāsṛjatpūrvaṃ bhagavānviṣṇuravyayaḥ ।
tāsu vīryaṃ narākhyāsu yena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tadaṇḍamabhavadvaimaṃ yasmiñjātaḥ prajāpatiḥ । asṛjanmanumukhyāṃśca kardamādyānprajāpatīn ।। dakṣaṃ ca sarvabhūtāni yasya dauhitrasaṃtatiḥ ।
pṛthakpṛthakca rājyāni somādināmakalpayat ।। kadācidatrivaṃśasya suto aṅgasya prajāpateḥ । mṛtyuputryāṃ sunīthāyāṃ jātaḥ sthitivilopakṛt ।। svarvo nāmābhavadrājā kilbiṣātkaluṣāśayaḥ ।
prajānāṃ vidhivaimukhyānmūrtimāniva viplavaḥ ।। anunīto api bahuśaḥ sa yadā nābhavadvaśī । tadā nigṛhyātibalaṃ munayastamapātayan ।। mamanthurasya te savyamūruṃ krodhānalākulāḥ ।
tataḥ samudabhūtsvarvo naraḥ kṛṣṇo bhayākulaḥ ।। niṣīdetyatriṇokto asau niṣādajanako abhavat । tato mamanthurmunayaḥ pāṇiṃ venasya dakṣiṇam ।। tāmrāṅgulidalātpāṇikamalādudabhūttataḥ ।
pitāmaha iva śrīmānpṛthuḥ pṛthulalocanaḥ ।। dhanurājagavaṃ tasya vibibhau hemavarṣiṇaḥ । nijajvālāvalī dhāma dīptasyeva vibhāvasoḥ ।। tatprasādāddivaṃ yāte vene vainyo atha bhūbhujām ।
ādyo ratnākarairetya ratnaurabhyarcitaḥ svayam ।। jale śaile ca tasyābhūdabhagnapraṇayā gatiḥ । taṃ tuṣṭuvurnavotpannāḥ sūtamāgadhabandinaḥ ।। prajānāṃ vṛttaye bhūmistenādiṣṭā tarasvinā ।
bhītā dudrāva gaurbhūtvā dhanvī tāmādravatsa ca ।। sā lokānbrahmalokāntānaśeṣānvidrutā javāt । tamevāttāyudhaṃ paścādapaśyadvalitānanā ।। paritrāṇamapaśyantī sā tamūce kṛtāñjaliḥ ।
kopaṃ jahi mahīpāla yoṣitaṃ parirakṣa mām ।। vinā dharitrīṃ tiṣṭhanti prajānātha kathaṃ prajāḥ । iti śritivacaḥ śrutvā vītakopo abravīnnṛpaḥ ।। prajāvṛttinimitto ayaṃ samārambho mama tviyi ।
bahūnāṃ prāṇarakṣārthamekahiṃsā praśasyate ।। vistārya svayamātmānaṃ dhārayiṣyāmyahaṃ prajāḥ । na cedvitara lokānāṃ vṛttiṃ putrī ca me bhava ।। iti kṣitibhujādiṣṭā jagāda jagatī natā ।
ahaṃ vṛtti vidhāsyāmi prajānāṃ tvatsutā satī ।। deśānsamīkuru vibho śilākūṭaviśaṅkaṭān । sarvasyāpi bhavatyetadyathā kṣīraṃ struṃta māya ।। niśamyaitatpṛthuyaśāḥ pṛthuḥ pṛthuśiloccayān ।
pṛthakcakre dhanuṣkoṭyā suspaṣṭā yena bhūrabhūt ।। tataḥ sasyāni pṛthivīṃ svanāmāṅkāṃ dudoha saḥ । manuṃ svāyaṃbhuvaṃ vatsaṃ kṛtvā karapuṭodare ।। śrūyate munibhirdugdhā tapo brahma ca būḥ purā ।
vatsaḥ somo gururdegdhā pātramāsīcca kāñcanam ।। rūpyapātre ca pitṛbhirdugdheyaṃ vasudhā sudhām । yamaṃ vatsaṃ samādāya tathā dogdhāramantakam ।। alābupātre nāgaiśca viṣaṃ dugdhā balapradam ।
dhṛtarāṣraṃ ca dogdhāraṃ kṛtvā vatsaṃ ca takṣakam ।। asurairāyase pātre māyāṃ dugdhā vasuṃdharā । vatsastadābhūtprahlādo dogdhā ca danujo madhuḥ ।। yakṣairapi purā dugdhā vatsaṃ kṛtvā dhaneśvaram ।
antardhānakaraṃ kṣīramāmapātre bhayaṃkaram ।। rudhiraṃ rākṣasairdugdhā vatsakena sumālinā । padmapātre śubhāngandhāndugdhā gandharvakiṃnaraiḥ ।। parvatairmerumādāya dogdhāraṃ śailabhājane ।
ratnauṣadhigaṇāndugdhā vatsaṃ kṛtvā himālayam ।। vṛkṣaiḥ pālāśapātre ca dugdhā puṣpaṃ phalaṃ tataḥ । dogdhṛtvamagamatsālastadā plakṣaśca vatsatām ।। sarvadā sarvadā bhūmirityevaṃ śāsanātpṛthoḥ ।
ādirājasya jayinaḥ karma yasyaitadadbhutam ।। pṛthivīdohaḥ ।। śrutveti vainyacaritaṃ vismito janamejayaḥ । muniṃ manvantarakathāmapṛcchatso apyabhāṣata ।।
svāyaṃbhuvo manuḥ pūrvamabhūtsaptarṣayastadā । marīcyatripulastyādyā ।। । devāśca tuṣṭitābhidhāḥ ।।
auttamākhyastṛtīyo abhūnmanuḥ saptarṣayastadā । vasiṣṭhaputrāstasyāsannṛbhavaśca divaukasaḥ ।। tāmaso abhūnmanusturyo yasya saptarṣayo antare । babhūvuḥ pṛthugārgyādyāḥ sabhyāśca tridivaukasaḥ ।।
raivataḥ pañcamo apyāsīnmanuḥ saptarṣayastadā । vedabāhumukhāścāsannabhūtarajasaḥ surāḥ ।। cākṣuṣo atha manuḥ ṣaṣṭho bhṛgumukhyā yadantare । abhavansapta munayo lekhasaṃjñāstathāmarāḥ ।।
eteṣu bahuputreṣu ṣaṭsu yāteṣu sāṃpratam । vartate saptamaḥ śrīmānadya vaivasvato manuḥ ।। kaśyapo atrirvasiṣṭhaśca bhāradvājo atha gautamaḥ । kauśiko jamadagniśca saptaite adya maharṣayaḥ ।।
sāśvirudrāśca maruto vasvādityāśca devatāḥ । ikṣvākupramukhāścāsya manoḥ putrā mahībhujaḥ ।। sāvarṇo atha manurbhāvī tasya saptarṣayo antare । rāmavyāsakṛpātreyadrauṇigālavakāśyapāḥ ।।
catvāro merusāvarṇā bhāvino manavaḥ pare । teṣāṃ nava navāścānye te te saptarṣayaḥ kramāt ।। rocyo nāma manuḥ ṣaṣṭho bhautyākhyaḥ saptamo manuḥ । caturdaśaite manavo yebhyo manvantarāḥ kramāt ।।
caturyugānāṃ pūrṇānāṃ sāgrāṇāmekasaptatiḥ । manvantarāṇāṃ pratyekameṣa saṃkhyākṛto avadhiḥ ।। caturdaśasu yāteṣu teṣu manvantareṣvatha । kalpakṣaye jagadviṣṇorantaḥ sarvaṃ pralīyate ।।
