punaśca bhavatītyevaṃ cakravatparivartate । kalpasaṃkṣayalakṣāṇāmanādinidhanā gatiḥ ।। sāṃpratasya manostāvadasminvaivasvate antare । harivaṃśaprasaṅgena śrūyatāmatha saṃbhavaḥ ।।
manvantaravarṇanam ।। ādityaḥ kaśyapājjāto vivaśvānmahasāṃ nidhiḥ । ugrarūpo abhavaddhoradīptisaṃtānasaṃcayaḥ ।। diṣṭayā nāyaṃ mṛto aṇḍasthaḥ pravṛddhena svatejasā ।
snehādityuditaḥ pitrā mārtaṇḍa iti viśrutaḥ ।। saṃjñā nāmābhavattasya lāvaṇyanalinī priyā । bahukautukanirmātuḥ putrī tvaṣṭuḥ prajāpateḥ ।। tasyāmajījanatputraṃ śrāddhadevaṃ manuṃ raviḥ ।
yamaṃ kanyāṃ ca yamunāṃ yamalatvātkṛtābhidhau ।। tīkṣṇāṃśoratha tadrūpaṃ vikṛtaṃ ghoratejasaḥ । na sehe dhṛtidhairyāpi saṃjñā kāntikumudvatī ।। tulyarūpāṃ nijacchāyāṃ māyāyogavinirmitām ।
sā dhṛtvā svapatergūḍhaṃ jagāma janakāntikam ।। patyuḥ samīpaṃ gaccheti nirastā tena māninā । lajjitā vaḍavā bhūtvā prayayāvuttarānkurūn ।। tataḥ saṃjñāsavarṇāyāṃ sāvarṇākhyaḥ paro manuḥ ।
raverajñātavṛttasya cchāyāyāmabhavatsutaḥ ।। śanaiścaro dvitīyaśca snehamabhyadhikaṃ tayoḥ । chāyā cakāra vātsalyānna tathāparaputrayoḥ ।। kṣamī jyeṣṭho manuḥ sehe tadyamastu na cakṣame ।
bālyāttenāhatā daivādbālena jananī purā ।। sā taṃ śaśāpa kupitā caraṇāste patantviti । tacchrutvā śaṅkito bhāsvānkopāttāṃ śaptumudyataḥ ।। gatvā tvaṣṭurgṛhaṃ tūrmaṃ saṃjñāvṛttāntamabhyadhāt ।
tejastavaitadatyugraṃ saṃjñā na sahate satī ।। pracchannaṃ tatra vaḍavā vane carati śādvalam । iti tvaṣṭurgirā jñātvā tenaivāropito bhramam ।। aśātayannijaṃ tejo dayitādarśanotsukaḥ ।
tejasā tena vidadhe tvaṣṭā cakraṃ sudarśanam ।। daityāndhakārasaṃhārasahāyaṃ kaiṭabhadviṣaḥ । tataḥ kamalinīkāntaḥ kāntarūpo divākaraḥ ।। gatvā dadarśa vipine vaḍavārūpiṇīṃ priyām ।
tatra tena viveṣṭantī hyakrāntā hayarūpiṇā ।। parāvṛttamukhaivāsītparasaṃsparśaśaṅkayā । tato vivasvato vīryaṃ nāsikāthūtkṛtena sā ।। tatsasarja yato jātau nāsatyāvaśvinau yamau ।
atha saṃjñā parijñāya saumyaṃ devaṃ divākaram ।। nijarūpavatī prāyādgṛhaṃ tadanuyāyinī । manuḥ prajāpatisasītpitṝṇāmadhipo yamaḥ ।। tridaśānāṃ ca bhiṣajāvaśvinau yamunā sarit ।
bhāvī prajāpatiścānyaḥ savarṇātanayo manuḥ ।। grahāṇāṃ saptamaścāsīnmandacārī śanaiśvaraḥ । ikṣvākuśibiśaryātinābhāgādyāḥ sutā manoḥ ।। teṣu jāteṣu putrārthī mittrāvaruṇayormanuḥ ।
iṣṭiṃ cakāra tatrāsya sutābhūllalitadyutiḥ ।। iḍā nāma sphuradratnabhūṣaṇoddyotitāmbarā । praṇamya padmavadanā manuṃ tacchāsanānugā ।। mittrāvaruṇayorvāsaṃ tadaṃśāsmīti sā yayau ।
sadācārocitā tābhyāṃ sā putrītyabhinanditā ।। tadvaraṃ prāpa putrastvaṃ bhaviṣyasi manoriti । tataḥ pratinivṛttā sā vrajantī gajagāminī ।। dṛṣṭvā hariṇaśāvākṣī budhena śaśisūnunā ।
tatsaṃgamātsamāsādya purūravasamātmajam ।। strīrūpaṃ sā samutsṛjya pradyumnākhyo abhavannṛpaḥ । utkalo vinatāśvaśca gayaśceti tadātmajaḥ ।। ikṣvākostumupādo abhūtkakutsthastasya cātmajaḥ ।
tadvaṃśe kuvalāśvo abhūduttaṅkavacasā ca yaḥ ।। vālukāntargataṃ ghoraṃ dhundhuṃ nāma mahāsuram । jaghāna yasya niḥśvāsaiḥ pṛthivī samadahyata ।। kuvalāśvasya nṛpaterjātastvayyāruṇiḥ kule ।
tena satyavrato nāma paurakanyāpahārataḥ ।। putraḥ śapto antyajātistvamavāpto vijane avasat । atrāntare vinā varṣaṃ kṛcchre dvādaśavārṣike ।। tatyāja sasutāṃ bhāryāṃ viśvāmitro ambudhestaṭe ।
sāṃ madhyamaṃ gale baddhvā vikretuṃ prastutā sutam ।। satyavratena kṛpayā vāritā vṛttidāyinā । viśvāmitrasutaścābhūdgalabandhaḥ sa gālavaḥ ।। sa tyāgādvāritaḥ kiṃ me na piteti purohite ।
satyavrato rājaputro vasiṣṭhe manyumānabhūt ।। kāmadhenuṃ sa tasyātha carantīṃ śāpamohitaḥ । nihatya gādhiputrāṇāmātmanaścāśanaṃ vyadhāt ।। kopakatvātpiturdhenuvadhādaprokṣitāśanāt ।
śāpaśaṅkutraṃya tasya vaśiṣṭhaḥ samapātayat ।। tasya triśaṅkusaṃjñasya viśvāmitraḥ pituḥ padam । datvābhūdyājako yena sadehastridivaṃ yayau ।। tasya putro hariścandro rājasūye rarāja yaḥ ।
sagarastatkule rājā yatsutaiḥ sāgaraḥ kṛtaḥ ।। mātuḥ sapatnīdattena jātaḥ saha gareṇa yaḥ । pratyantadeśāñjitvāsau pituḥ pūrvāpakāriṇaḥ ।। niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkārānvidadhe lakṣaṇāṅkitān ।
cakāra muṇḍaśirasaḥ kāmbojānvadharakṣaṇāt ।। śaśakordhaśiromuṇḍānmuktakeśāṃśca pāratān । pahlavānyavanādyāṃśca śmaśrucihnānakalpayat ।। vaṃśe tasya dilīpo abhūttasya sūnurbhagīrathaḥ ।
duhitṛtvamagādyasya bhuvi bhāgīrathī nadī ।। kule tasyābhavadrājā rāmo daśarathātmajaḥ । rājarṣivaṃśā bahavo babhūvustatsutātkuśāt ।। ikṣvākorityayaṃ vaṃśastadbhrātustu mariṣyataḥ ।
śakā babhūvustanayā nābhāgasya suto abhavat ।। ambarīṣo mahīpālo vṛṣṇeḥ putrāśca vṛṣṇayaḥ । raṇadhṛṣṭāḥ śibeḥ putrāḥ śaryāterabhavatsutā ।। sukanyā cyavanenoḍhā putraścāntabhūpatiḥ ।
ravetī tasya tanayā sa purā sahitastayā ।। brahmalokaṃ yayau śrotuṃ gāndharva brahmaṇo antike । tato bahuyuge kāle vyatīte kṣaṇaleśavat ।। apaśyatsvapurīmetya dvārakāṃ vṛṣṇibhirvṛtām ।
aspṛṣṭāṃ kālakalayā brahmalokanivāsataḥ ।। pradadau balabhadrāya bālāmeva sa revatīm । dattvā ca tanayāṃ prāyāttapase merukandaram ।। ikṣvākoranujaḥ ṣaṣṭho riṣṭākhyastasya cātmajau ।
vaiśyau brāhmaṇatāṃ prāptau tapoyogādakalmaṣau ।। karūṣaḥ saptamo yastu kāruṣāstatsutā nṛpāḥ । pṛthukaścāṣṭamaḥ śūdro babhūva gurugovadhāt ।। ete babhūvurikṣvākorbhrātaro aṣṭau manoḥ sutāḥ ।
ityete śrāddhadevasya bhuvi vaṃśadharā manoḥ ।। manuvaṃśaḥ ।। pṛṣṭaḥ śrāddhaprasaṅgena pitṛkalpaṃ mahībhujā । muniḥ prāhāvadadbhīṣmaḥ praśnānte yadyudhiṣṭhiram ।।
pitaraḥ pūjitāḥ śrāddhe tribhiḥ piṇḍaistripauruṣaiḥ । devatatvena puṣṇanti jantūnnānāgatiṣvapi ।। śaṃtanorudyate piṇḍe śrāddhakāle mayā pituḥ । uttasthau kaṅkaṇodāraḥ karaḥ kamalakomalaḥ ।।
taṃ vilokya mayā piṇḍe kuśeṣveva samarpite । śāstrākriyānuvartitvāttattoṣajanako mama ।। svacchandamaraṇaṃ tasmādavāpyāhaṃ varaṃ varam । tenopadiṣṭaṃ tatkālaṃ mārkaṇḍeyamupasthitam ।।
apṛcchaṃ daivataṃ śrāddhaṃ phalaṃ ca pitṛyājinām । so abravīnmeruśikhare mayā pṛṣaṣṭastapasyatā ।। sanatkumāre bhagavānprāhaitattejasāṃ nidhiḥ । brahmā purā surāndṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā tānātmayājinaḥ ।।
kathaṃ naite yajante māmiti śāpādamohayat । te naṣṭasaṃvidaḥ sarve prasādya kamalodbhavam ।। prāyaścittaṃ nijānputrānpapracchustasya śāsanāt । prāyaścittaistataḥ pūtāḥ kriyājñānopadeśataḥ ।।
gurutvātsvasutairuktā gamyatāṃ putrakā iti । ta ete pitaraḥ pūjyā devānāṃ tanayā api ।। yeṣāṃ śrāddhaṃ vinā prāhustridaśā niṣphalāḥ kriyāḥ । tadvihīneṣu yāgeṣu phalamaśnanti rākṣasāḥ ।।
anyonyaṃ pitarastasmāddevāḥ pitṛgaṇā api । śrāddhenāpyāyate somaḥ sa puṣṇātyakhilāḥ prajāḥ ।। śrāddhena pitaraḥ prītā nṝṇāṃ pitṛpitāmahān । āpyāyayanti sarvatra tiryagyonigatānapi ।।
catvārastadgaṇā mūrtā mūrtihīnāstrayo gaṇāḥ । sudhābhujo yogajuṣo vairājā iti viśrutāḥ ।। menākhyā mānasī teṣāṃ kanyā himagireḥ priyā । maināko yatsutaḥ śrīmānpitā krauñcamahāgireḥ ।।
menāyāstanayāstisro yāścerurduścaraṃ tapaḥ । jyeṣṭhā tāsāmapārṇākhyā bhavānī bhavavallabhā ।। u meti tapaso mātrā vāritābhūdumeti yā । devalasyaikaparṇākhyā dvitīyābhūnmunervadhūḥ ।।
jaigīṣavyasya bhāryābhūttṛtīyāpyekapāṭalā । putrī marīciputrāṇāṃ pitṝṇāmapi mānasī ।। acchodākhyā varasaritprāgacchodasaraḥsnutā । aparijñāya pitaraṃ sābhilāṣā vilokya sā ।।
bhraṣṭā papāta tacchāpāttatprasādakṛtāvadhiḥ । aṣṭāviṃśe dvāpare sā saṃbhūtā matsyayonijā ।। asūta yā sutaṃ vyāsaṃ gandhakālī parāśarāt । pulastyaputrāḥ pitaro divi barhiṣadaḥ pare ।।
mānasī kanyakā teṣāṃ pīvarī nāma yoginī । janayiṣyatyapatyāni yasyāṃ vyāsasutaḥ śukaḥ ।। putrīṃ ca kṛtvā jananīṃ brahmadattasya bhūpateḥ । amūrtāḥ karmasaṃnyāsādete pitṛgaṇāstrayaḥ ।।
somadevānmānavādīnpūjitā bhāvayanti ye । mūrtāstu somapā nāma pitaro anye sudhābhujaḥ ।। teṣāṃ gaurmānasī kanyā yajante brāhmaṇāśca tām । anye tvaṅgirasaḥ putrāḥ pitaraḥ śraddhavarjitāḥ ।।
yaṣṭāraḥ kṣatriyāsteṣāṃ yaśodākhyā ca kanyakā । sahasrayājino mātrā dilīpasya mahīpateḥ ।। ājyapāḥ pitaraḥ putrāḥ kaśyapasya prajāpateḥ । yajante tānsadā vaiśyā kanyā teṣāṃ ca mānasī ।।
virajā nāma jananī yayāteḥ pṛthivīpateḥ । sukālā nāma pitaro vaśiṣṭhasya muneḥ sutāḥ ।। śūdrāṇāmeva te pūjyāstatputrī narmadā sarit । kurukutsapriyā yasyāstrasaddastuḥ suto nṛpaḥ ।।
ete pitṛgaṇā mūrtāścatvāro varṇadaivatam । yeṣāṃ yuge yuge pūjāṃ śrāddhadevo abhyadhānmanuḥ ।। rājataṃ rājatāṅkaṃ vā yātaṃ teṣāṃ svadhābhujām । śastraṃ śrāddhe somavahnimanupūjāpuraḥ sare ।।
ta ete pitaraḥ pūjyāḥ krodhahīnāḥ prasādinaḥ । saṃkalpakalpalatikā bhaktiryeṣāṃ mahāphalā ।। dharmāpacārādvibhraṣṭā brāhmaṇāḥ pitṛpūjayā । yathā svapadameṣyanti tatsarvaṃ drakṣyasi kratau ।।
śrāddhabhāvaṃ vijānīhi svayamityabhidhāya saḥ । sanatkumāro divyaṃ me cakṣurduttvā tirodadhe ।। tato apaśyaṃ kurukṣetre viprānkālena sapta tān । vāgduṣṭaḥ krodhano hiṃsraḥ piśunaḥ svasṭamaḥ kaviḥ ।।
pitṛvartī ceti nāma sadṛśākārasevinaḥ । atha kauśikadāyādā gurorgārgyasya te purā ।। prasthitāḥ pathi gāṃ mūḍhāḥ kṣudhārtā hantumudyayuḥ । yadā nivāryamāṇāste kavinā svasṭamena ca ।।
na nivṛttāstadā kopātpitṛvartī jagāda tān । sarvathaitadakāryaṃ vo garhitaṃ sarvajantubhiḥ ।। śrāddhapūrvo ayamārambhaḥ kriyatāṃ yadi durgrahaḥ । etadākarṇya te sarve taduktaṃ cakrire vidhim ।।
tataste hiṃsayā kāle śaptājāyanta lubdhakāḥ । daśārṇeṣu svakarmasthāḥ satyaśīlaparāyaṇāḥ ।। janmāntare śrāddhaphalālluptā teṣāṃ na tu smṛtiḥ । nirvairī nirvṛtiḥ kṣānto nirmanyurvaidhasaḥ kṛtiḥ ।।
mātṛvartī ca te vyādhāḥ pitṛsevākṛtakṣaṇāḥ । dhanūṃṣi pitroḥ pānīye vihāya vyasavo abhavan ।। tataḥ phullalatāpuñjakuñje kālāñjane girau । trāsāyāsavivignāste jātā jātismarā mṛgāḥ ।।
unmukho nityacakitaḥ stabdhavarṇaḥ sulocanaḥ । ghasmaraḥ piṇḍito nādī ceti ceṣṭocitābhidhāḥ ।। te brahmacāriṇaḥ kṣāntāḥ pūrvavidyāvivāsitāḥ । vihāriṇo merutaṭī gatvā prāṇānparyatyajan ।।
adyāmi merugāminyaḥ kālāñjanataṭotthitāḥ । teṣāṃ kanakūṭeṣu dṛśyante pādapaṅktayaḥ ।। tataḥ śucisariddvīpe laharīdhaitasaikate । babhūvuścakravākāste taruṇā brahmacāriṇaḥ ।।
nirmamo niḥspṛhaḥ kṣānto nirvairo niṣpratigrahaḥ । nirvṛto nibhṛtaśceti yoginaste vihaṅgamāḥ ।। jātāstatra ca te haṃsāstapoyogaparāyaṇāḥ । vālānilākulotphullakamalotpalamāline ।।
salile vilasantyete vibhrājaṃ nāma bhūpatim । dadṛśuḥ padmavadanāvṛndairjitasarovaram ।। pātuṃ yadṛcchayāyātaṃ tīropāntalatāvane । śacīpatimivālokya taṃ kanīyānvihaṅgamaḥ ।।
tasya rājyaspṛhāṃ cakre tadaiśvaryahṛtāśayaḥ । dvau cābhūtāṃ khagau tasya spṛhānugatamānasau ।। tataḥ kālena te sarve sārasā vyasavo abhavan । vi bhrājaṃ tadvanamabhūtsaraśca nṛpasevitam ।।
vibhrājasyātha putro abhūdaṇuho nāma bhūpatiḥ । tasmai vitṝṇāṃ dauhitrīṃ putrīṃ vyāsasutaḥ śukaḥ ।। kṛtvīṃ nāma dadau divyayogināmadhidevatām । tasyāḥ sa haṃsaḥ putro abhūdyogabhraṣṭo hatasmṛtiḥ ।।
brahmadatta iti khyātaḥ kāmpilye nagare nṛpaḥ । pāñcālapu ṇḍarīkākhyau tasyāstāṃ sacivau nṛpau ।। haṃsau spṛhābhraṣṭayogau yau tau tadanugāśayau । jātismarāstu catvāro jātāḥ sabrahmacāriṇaḥ ।।
brahmadattasya dayitā devalasyātmajā muneḥ । babhūva saṃnatirnāma māninī madirāvaniḥ ।। sa kadācillatālāsyavyālolapavane vane । sevyamānastayā tantryā vijahāra smaropamaḥ ।।
sarvaprāṇirutajño asau tatra praṇayakopataḥ । pipīlakāyāḥ śuśrāva bhartustāṃ tāṃ prasādanām ।। sa tacchrutvā calaccārukapolaphalako nṛpaḥ । jahāsa dayitākaṇṭhe kurvanmuktāvalīmiva ।।
kasmādakasmānme nātho hasatīti vilajjitā । sābhavatpadmavadanā candrodaya ivābjinī ।। pipīlakarutāścarye kathite api mahībhujā । prāṇatyāgaikasaṃkalpā tadasatyamamanyata ।।
dayitādīrghakopena vivigno vasudhādhipaḥ । nirāhāravrato viṣṇuṃ dadarśa prayatāśayaḥ ।। kuśalaṃ bhavitā prātastaveti hariśāsanāt । prabhāte rathamāruhya puraṃ sasacivo aviśat ।।
atrāntare taiścaturbhirdvijairjātismaraiḥ pitā । visṛṣṭaḥ śrāvaya nṛpaṃ ślokamityājagāma tam ।। sa samāsādya bhūpālaṃ sacivābhyāṃ saha sthitam । idamāśrāvayadvipraḥ kimapyutsukamānasam ।।
sapta dāśā daśārṇeṣu girau kālāñjane mṛgāḥ । cakravākā nadīdvīpe haṃsāḥ sarasi mānase ।। vayaṃ te adya kurukṣetre jātā vedavido dvijāḥ । gantāro dūramadhvānaṃ yūyaṃ kimavasādinaḥ ।।
śrutvaitatsmṛtayogātmā niḥspandakaraṇo nṛpaḥ । sacivābhyāṃ saha paraṃ dhāma tacca samāyayau ।। śrāddhaprabhāvādityetatkṣapayitvograpātakam । yātāḥ kauśikadāyādā yoginaḥ paramaṃ padam ।।
śāntanoḥ śāsanādetanmārkaṇḍeyācchrutaṃ mayā । brahmadattasya putro abhūdviśvakseno mahīpatiḥ ।। daṇḍasenaḥ sutastasya bhallāṭaśca tadātmajaḥ । yaḥ karṇena purā vīro digjaye vinipātitaḥ ।।
bhallāṭasyābhavatsūnurdurnayī janamejayaḥ । ugrāyudho atha tatputraḥ pāpācāro niraṅkuśaḥ ।। tridivaṃ śantanau yāte hartuṃ satyavatīṃ balāt । manaścakāra durvṛttastato yadhi mayā hataḥ ।।
iti śrāddhaphalaṃ bhīṣmo babhāṣe dharmanandanam । śrāddhenāpyāyate somo vṛṣṇayo yasya vaṃśajāḥ ।। pitṛkalpaḥ ।। atriścacāra bhagavānmaunī munivaraḥ purā ।
tapo varṣasahasrāṇi divyāni trīṇī niścalaḥ ।। tasyātha nirnimeṣasya śarīraṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ । abhūddivyāmṛtamayaṃ kāntaṃ dugdhodadheriva ।। tataḥ susrāva netrābhyāmatrestaddaśadhā srutam ।
amṛtaṃ dikṣu daśasu prabhāsaṃpūritāmbaram ।। vṛtaṃ taddaśabhirgarbhe digbhiryatnena duḥsaham । somatvamāptaṃ sahasā papāta bhuvi bhāsvaram ।। tasminnipatite tūrṇaṃ kampite bhuvanatraye ।
rathe vedamaye brahmā sahasrāśve tamādadhe ।। taṃ rathasthaṃ munivarā devāstrailokyabhāvanam । tuṣṭuvustejaso vṛddhayo sarvajidyena so abhavat ।। vatsarāṇāṃ cakārāsau pūrṇaṃ padmaśataṃ tapaḥ ।
utpannāstejasā tasya divyauṣadhisudhāgaṇāḥ ।। rājā rājyābhiṣikto atha brahmaṇā brāhmaṇādhipaḥ । vallabho dakṣaputrīṇāṃ rājasūye rarāja saḥ ।। surasiddharṣigandharvasevyastribhuvaneśvaraḥ ।
lokānavinayotsekāścacāra śrīviśṛṅkhalaḥ ।। jahāra tarasā so atha tārāṃ nāma bṛhaspateḥ । vallabhāṃ vibhavodbhūtabhūtenodbhāvyate na kaḥ ।। tridaśairbodhyamāno api na sa tatyāja tāṃ yadā ।
tadā bṛhaspateḥ pakṣaṃ śukro rudrastathāgrahīt ।। tataḥ pravṛtte samare bhairave tārakāmaye । devānāṃ rudramukhyānāṃ vīreṇa tuhinātviṣā ।। astraṃ brahmaśiraḥ spṛ ṣṭaṃ yaśaśchedi divaukasām ।
alpāvaśeṣāmakarodbhagnadhvastahatāṃ camūm ।। trastairatha surairetya yācitaḥ kamalodbhavaḥ । nirvāya sāmnā samaraṃ dadau jāyāṃ bṛhaspateḥ ।। sagarbhāmāgātāmūce sa tāmīrṣyāviṣolbaṇaḥ ।
na dhāryo ayaṃ tvayā garbho madyonāvityadhomukhīm ।। tatastatyāja sā garbhamiṣīkāstambhasaṃstare । tejasā jātamātro asau vibudhānajayadbudhaḥ ।। pṛṣṭā tato ayaṃ kasyeti devairnovāca sā yadā ।
tadā pṛṣṭā viriñcena candrasyetyavadallaghu ।। sa putraḥ śaśinaḥ śrīmānpratikūlodayo divi । śiśiravyajano dhīmānbabhau vibudhanandanaḥ ।। atha kālena śītāṃśurdakṣiṇākṣīṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।
paradāraparāmarṣāttapto atriṃ śaraṇaṃ yayau ।। sa tena putravātsalyānmantraiḥ kṣapitakilbiṣaḥ । rarāja yakṣmaṇā muktaḥ punaryukto nijaśriyā ।। somotpattiḥ ।।
iḍāyāmatha putro abhūdbudhasya sa purūravāḥ । yasyābhūdbhūvanaślāghyā kāntā kīrtirivorvaśī ।। tasya ṣaṭ tanayāstasyāmabhavaṃstridaśālaye । āyurjyeṣṭho nṛpasteṣāṃ nahuṣo apyāyuṣaḥ sutaḥ ।।
rajiprabhṛtayastasya catvāro apyanujāḥ purā । devāsuraraṇe pūrvaṃ sāhāyye vajrapāṇinā ।। rajirvṛtaḥ svarājyena paṇena nahuṣānujaḥ । sa hatvā ditijānvīrānsurendratvaṃ paṇārjitam ।।
tvatputro asmīti śakreṇa dhūrtenābhihito atyajat । atha kālena jayino rajeḥ putrā mahaujasaḥ ।। rājyaṃ tridaśarājasya jahruḥ pitṛbalārjitam । hṛtarājyaḥ sa śakro atha hṛtabhāgaḥ kratuṣvapi ।।
yayāce badarīmātraṃ puroḍāśaṃ bṛhaspatim । tena bālamukhābjena yācito naṣṭacetasā ।। cakāra rajiputrāṇāṃ matimohaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ । tataste rāgiṇo mattā vibhraṣṭā nyāyavartmanaḥ ।।
saṃvṛttā bhṛśamutsekānnaṣṭavīryaparākramāḥ । tena tāndurjayānhatvā vajrī svapadamāptavān ।। śapharotphālacaṭulā durvṛttānāṃ hi saṃpadaḥ । nahṛṣasyābhavatputro yayātiḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।।
divyena yo rathāgryeṇa ṣaḍrātreṇājayajjagat । yo asau kālena tadvaṃśe śāpānnaṣṭo rathottamaḥ ।। jarāsaṃdhena saṃprāpto hṛto yo apyasurāriṇā । yayāteḥ śukrakanyāyāṃ devayānyāṃ babhūvatuḥ ।।
yaduścaturvasuśceti tanayau saṃmatau satām । vṛṣaparvasutāyāśca śarmiṣṭhāyāḥ sutāstrayaḥ ।। druhyānupūrunāmānastasyāsanvaṃśavardhanāḥ । kāle atha vipule yāte yayātiḥ pravayāḥ sutān ।।
yayāce yauvanaṃ kāmī jarayā jagatīpatiḥ । mṛtyusiṃhanakhaśreṇīṃ sukhapadmahimāhatim ।। yadā kaścinna jagrāha jarāṃ purustadāgrahīt । tasmādyauvanamāsādya yadumukhyānatho parān ।।
yayātiraśapadvaṃśyā yenaiṣāmanṛpāḥ sadā । tato didṛkṣuḥ kāmānāṃ pāraṃ taruṇavigrahaḥ ।। viśvasya nākakāminyā nandane vijahāra saḥ । suciraṃ sevamāno api rājā rājīvalocanām ।।
yadā pravardhamānecchaḥ kāmānāṃ nāntamāyayau । tadā rājyaṃ sutasyaiva purordatvā jarāṃ nijām ।। jagrāha jātavairāgyo jagau cedaṃ munivrataḥ । citraṃ bhogābhilāṣo ayaṃ bhogābhyāsena vardhate ।।
vellatkallolajālena salileneva vāḍavaḥ । bata visphārasaṃsārasaroruharajaśchaṭā ।। prītiḥ pratiniśaṃ mugdhānbadhnāti madhupāniva । jīryatāmapyajīryor ayaṃ naśyatāmapi naśvaraḥ ।।
kāmaḥ kāmavatāmantarghuṇaḥ kṣitiruhāmiva । niṣiddho niyamenāpi dhairyeṇāpyavadhīritaḥ ।। rāgo jvalatyaho vastreṇācchādita ivānilaḥ । iti saṃcintya niyato yayātistapasā yutaḥ ।।
kulocitena vidhinā yaśaḥśeṣatvamāyayau । pūroryayātiputrasya vaśe suvipule kṣitau ।। pravartamāne bahudhā kālenābhūnmahīpatiḥ । duṣyanto yasya bharataḥ putro bhāratavaṃśakṛt ।।
avadāte kule yasya jāto asi janamejayaḥ । ityeṣa pauravo vaṃśaḥ pūrvameva mayoditaḥ ।। pūruvaṃśaḥ ।। turvasostu mahānvaṃśo yasmiñjātaḥ karaṃdhamaḥ ।
maruttastatsuto yasmai dadau hema maheśvaraḥ ।। tasyāsanvipule vaṃśe pāṇḍyacaulāḥ sakeralāḥ । rājā marutpatirnāma druhyavaṃśe tvajāyata ।। kṛcchreṇa dīrghasaṃgrāme yauvanāśvena yo hataḥ ।
gāndhārastatsuto yasya vaṃśe jātāsturaṅgamāḥ ।। anostu vaṃśe dharmādyā jātāḥ pratyantabhūmipāḥ । yadostu prasṛte vaṃśe kṛtavīryātmajo nṛpaḥ ।। kārtavīryārjuno jātaḥ sahasrabhujadurmadaḥ ।
hehayānartabhojādyastālajaṅghāśca tatkule ।। kālena jātastadvaṃśe vṛṣo vṛṣasuto madhuḥ । vṛṣaṇastatsuto yasya vaṃśe sāgaravṛṣṇayaḥ ।। andhako apyanvaye teṣāmabhūdandhakavaṃśakṛt ।
bahuśākhe ca tadvaṃśe jāto krūraḥ sahasradaḥ ।। tatpitṛvyakule kāle śūraḥ śrīmānajāyata । vasudevaḥ sutastasya babhūvānakadundubhiḥ ।। yasmiñjāte divi mahānabhūddundubhiniḥsvanaḥ ।
bhrātāsya devabhāgākhyastathā devaśravāḥ paraḥ ।। anādhṛṣṭiḥ kanavako vatsaḥ śyāmo vavṛñja saḥ । pṛthukīrtiḥ pṛthākhyā ca śrutadevī śrutaśravāḥ ।। rājādhidevī pañcaitāḥ śūraputryo asya cānujāḥ ।
pṛthukīrtisuto rājā dantavakro nṛpātmajaḥ ।। pṛthāsutā dharmarājabhīmasenadhanaṃjayāḥ । śrutaśravāyāstanayaḥ śiśupālo mahābalaḥ ।। daityarājo abhavadyo asau hiraṇyakaśipuḥ purā ।
pitṛvyavaṃśe śūrasya śaineyaḥ satyako abhavat ।। sātyakistasya tanayo yuyudhānāparābhidhaḥ । uddhavo vibudhācāryaḥ śatrudevamukhāstathā ।। śatrudevasya naiṣādirekalavyo abhavatkule ।
vatsāvate tvaputrāya vasudevaḥ pratāpavān ।। adbhirdadau sutaṃ vīraṃ śauriḥ kauśikamaurasam । gaṇḍūṣakāyāputrāya cārudoṣṇādikānhariḥ ।। dve bhārye vasudevasya rohiṇī devakī tathā ।
rohiṇītanayo rāmaḥ sāraṇo durdamaḥ subhaḥ ।। śubhrapiṇḍāradamanāste mahāvadanātmajāḥ । anujā ca subhadraiṣā mahiṣī savyasācinaḥ ।। rāmasya niṣadho nāma revatyāmabhavatsutaḥ ।
devakīnandanaḥ kṛṣṇo devo dānavasūdanaḥ ।। vasudevasya cānyāsu bhāryāsu hyabhavansutāḥ । bhojopāsaṅgavijayā vṛṣadevo gadastathā ।। āśāvaho lomapādaḥ kapilo vardhamānakaḥ ।
pauṇḍro niṣādanāthaścetyugravīryaparākramāḥ ।। atrāntare gārgyamunirdhanu kālāyasāśanaḥ । cacāra dvādaśa samā brahmacārī paraṃ tapaḥ ।। trigartarājasutayā parīkṣāyai savibhramam ।
na cacālāyasaprakhyo hriyamāṇaśayo api yaḥ ।। sa manyutapto gopālakanyāyāṃ rudraśāsanāt । asṛjatkālayavanaṃ kālaṃ sarvamahībhujām ।। rathe yasya hayā ghorā vṛṣapūrvārdhavigrahāḥ ।
gṛhīto yavanendreṇa niṣputreṇa sa putrakaḥ ।। yuddhārthī darpasaṃmattaḥ papraccha subhaṭānbhuvi । nāradasya girā jñātvā sa vīrānvṛṣṇiyādavān ।। mathurānilayāñjetumakṣauhiṇyā samādravat ।
te kālayavanākrāntā jarāsaṃdhena cārditāḥ ।। vṛṣṇayo mathurāṃ tyaktvā dvārakāṃ cakrurambudhau । vaṃśaskandheṣu cānyeṣu saṃbhūtā yādavāḥ pare ।। sātvatasyābhavaddaivairudgītacaritaḥ kule ।
yajvā devāvṛdho rājā babhrustasyātmajo abhavat ।। āpagāyāṃ sarvarṇāyāṃ jātaḥ koṭisahasradaḥ । saṃbhūtāstatkule vīrā bhojāste śāntikāvatāḥ ।। andhakātkukkuro jātastadvaṃśyo apyāhuko abhavat ।
praṇetā vṛṣṇivaṃśānāṃ rājā kṛtayugocitaḥ ।। devakaścograsenaśca tatsutau devakasya tu । devavatpramukāḥ putrā devakyādyaśca kanyakāḥ ।। yāḥ sapta vasudevāya vitīrṇā vīramātaraḥ ।
ugrasenasutaḥ kaṃso nyagrodhapramukhāgrajaḥ ।। kaṃsā kaṃsavatī tanvī pālī kahvā ca kanyakāḥ । vidūrathakule bhoje babhūva hṛdikābhidhaḥ ।। kṛtavarmamukhāstasya śatadhanvādayaḥ sutāḥ ।
kroṣṭorvaṃśe praseno abhūtsatrājitsenajittathā । ityete bahavo vaṃśā viśrutā yādavā yadoḥ ।। yaduvaṃśaḥ ।। abdhestaṭe dvāravatyāṃ niveśe viṣadaṃ maṇim ।
divyaṃ syamantakaṃ nāma prasenaḥ kila labdhavān ।। sa maṇiḥ kanakasyandī vyāyidurbhikṣanāśanaḥ । śaktenāpyutsukenāpi na hṛtastasya śauriṇā ।। kālena mṛgayāsaktaḥ praseno maṇibhūṣitaḥ ।
siṃhena nihato yuddhe sahasā maṇihāriṇā ।। yāntaṃ javena taṃ siṃhamṛkṣarājo atha jāmvān । nihatya maṇimādāya balavānbilamāviśat ।। vṛṣṇyandhakahataṃ dṛṣṭvā prasenaṃ vijane vane ।
maṇilobhātkṛtaṃ sarvaṃ kṛṣṇeneti śaśaṅkire ।। viśuddhabhāvaḥ kṛṣṇo api tamanveṣṭuṃ yayau maṇim । mithyākalaṅkaṃ yaśasāmapavādaṃ saheta kaḥ ।। sāsraṃ prasenamālokya sa siṃheta vidāritam ।
tasyāvidūre siṃhaṃ ca dadarśa vinipātitam ।। maṇeralābhe vijñāya padavīmṛkṣaśaṃsinīm । guhāṃ praviśya gambhīraṃ dadarśa vipulaṃ bilam ।। tatra dhātryā sa śuśrāva vacanaṃ bālasāntvane ।
tavaivāsau maṇiḥ putra mā rodīḥ sukumāraka ।। śrutveti jñātavṛttānto jāmbavantaṃ dadarśa saḥ । tenātha yuyudhe kṛṣṇo divasānekaviṃśatim ।। daśagrīvograsaṃgrāmaśastrollikhitavakṣasam ।
jāmbavantaṃ vijityātha dattāṃ tena sutāṃ hariḥ ।। bimbādharāṃ jāmbavatīṃ lebhe taṃ ca syamantakam । tato dvāravatīmetya syamantakamudāradhīḥ ।। sa prasenānujāyaiva dadau sattrajite maṇim ।
satyabhāmāmukhāstisraḥ satrājinmuravairiṇaḥ ।। pradadau kanyakāḥ kāmakumudākāracandrikāḥ । satrājitaṃ ghātayitvā bhojena śatadhanvanā ।। aharanmaṇimakrūro mithaḥ sāhāyyasaṃvidā ।
satyabhāmā svayaṃ gatvā hate pitari duḥkhitā ।। jatuveśmani dagdheṣu pārtheṣu dhṛtarāṣṭrajaiḥ । śārṅgadhanvānamāsādya vāraṇāvatavāsinam ।। hataṃ nyavedayatsāśruḥ pitaraṃ śatadhanvanā ।
tatastūrṇaṃ samabhyetya dvārakāṃ garuḍadhvajaḥ ।। rāmeṇa sahiti gatvā yuyudhe śatadhanvanā । cakre maṇipradasyāpi nākrūro asya sahāyatām ।। svārthakāle vyatīte hi dhūrtā no kasyacinnijāḥ ।
adhiruhyāśu vaḍavāṃ śatayojanagāminīm ।। vidrutaṃ śatadhanvānaṃ mithilābhimukhaṃ javāt । jaghāna kaiṭabhārātirnāsasāda ca taṃ maṇim ।। so apahnuto maṇiriti kruddho asmai lāṅgalī mṛṣā ।
na dvārakāṃ viśāmīti mithilāṃ vimukho yayau ।। tatra duryodhanastasmādgadāśikṣāmavāptavān । tataḥ kṛṣṇānugairetya vṛṣṇivīraiḥ prasāditaḥ ।। dvārakāmāyayau śrīmāñjātatattvo halāyudhaḥ ।
akrūro api maṇisphīto bahuyajño bahupradaḥ ।। sukhaṃ nināya ṣaṣṭyabdīṃ dīkṣākavacarakṣitaḥ । vyaktiṃ yāte maṇau kiṃcidbhīte rāmatsakeśavāt ।। apayāte tato akrūre nāvarṣatpākaśāsanaḥ ।
jñātibhedabhayātpūrvaṃ kṛṣṇenopekṣitaściram ।। prasādya panarānīto durbhikṣārtaiḥ sayādavaiḥ । tasmindānapatau prāpte vavarṣa tridivaveśvaraḥ ।। kālena yācitaḥ sāmnā kṛṣṇena sa dadau maṇim ।
tasmai svasāraṃ cākrūraḥ prītaye cārulocanām ।। vinayārjavatuṣṭastaṃ keśavo api maṇiṃ dadau । akrūrāyaiva mahatāṃ praṇayānto hi durgrahaḥ ।। syamantakālambhaḥ ।।
kulāvalīṃ yādavānāṃ niśamya janamejayaḥ । vismito janmanā viṣṇorvaiśampāyanamabravīt ।। aho nu mahadāścaryamapūrvaṃ pratibhāti me । kathaṃ jagannivāso abhūccarācaragururnaraḥ ।।
yatkukṣikoṭare śete kalpānte bhuvanāvalī । sakathaṃ mānuṣīgarbhaṃ prapede bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।। vaiśvarūpyamidaṃ yasya sarvabhūtāntarātmanaḥ । icchāmātrasamunmeṣadarpaṇe pratibimbitam ।।
iti pṛṣṭaḥ kṣitibhujā jagāda mudito muniḥ । śrūyatāmadbhutaṃ janma viṣṇorjanmabhayacchidaḥ ।। yena yajñavarāheṇa vedayajñamayaṃ vapuḥ । kṛtvoddhṛtā vasumatī caturarṇavamekhalā ।।
babhau kuvalayaśyāmā daṃṣṭāgre yasya medinī । bālaśevalavallīva līnā palvalakeliṣu ।। yena kesariṇā śaṅkhaśubhrābhirnakhaśuktibhiḥ । āyuṣā saha niṣpītaṃ hiraṇyakaśiporyaśaḥ ।।
uraḥsthalāsthinirgharṣānnakhakrakacapañjare । yasya daityavadhe kopaḥ prāpa kalpāgniketutām ।। trailokyakramaṇe yasya vijayadhvajatāṃ yayau । pādo gaṅgājalollāsavyāloladhavalāṃśukaḥ ।।
kharvaḥ pūrvamatha prāṃśuraprameyastato abhavat । yaśca harṣaśca devānāṃ mohaśca tridaśadviṣām ।। yasya kuṇḍalatāṃ karṇe ravirnābhau sarojatām । prāpa pravardhamānasya gulphe kaṭakaratnatām ।।
uccairvilokayantīnāṃ tadvapuḥ surayoṣitām । valividhvaṃsabhītyeva nādṛśyata valitrayam ।। dattātreyāvatāreṇa dharmācārasya majjataḥ । vedānāṃ ca kṛtaṃ yena sthityai hastāvalambanam ।।
jāmadagnyavapurbhūtvā kārtavīryasya karmaṭham । mṛṇālamaṇḍalīlāvaṃ doḥsahasraṃ lulāva yaḥ ।। yaḥ kuṭhāre asthiniṣpeṣakhaṇḍanā dantamālikām । kṣatriyakṣayakālānāṃ babhāra gaṇanāmiva ।।
yaḥ pūrvāṅgavatīṃ cārumadhyadeśāṃ payasvinīm । sapuṇḍrakānanāṃ prādātsavatsāṃ kaśyapāya gām ।। yo abhavadbhuvanābhogabhūṣaṇaṃ raghunandanaḥ । vīraḥ subāhamārīcaghorameghamahānilaḥ ।।
bhrāntaḥ saptasu lokeṣu saptābdhikṣobhasaṃbhṛtaḥ । saptatālabhido yasya dhanvino dhanuṣadhvaniḥ ।। adyāpi setusaṃghaṭṭavisphuṭacchuktisaṃpuṭaḥ । suvyaktamuktādaśano vakti yasyāmbudhiryaśaḥ ।।
kirīṭakoṭiviśrāntaṃ yena śubhrayaśoṃśukaiḥ । unmṛṣṭaṃ lokapālānāmindrijitsainyajaṃ rajaḥ ।। patitotpatitairyasya daśāsyavadanairmuhuḥ । babhūva kandukāmandavinodānandavibhramaḥ ।।
bhuvo bhārāvatārāya kṛṣṇo vṛṣṇikule abhavat । śiśupālādibhūpālakālaḥ śakalitāsuraḥ ।। yadvakṣasi grāvabhidaḥ śṛṅgabhaṅgaparābhavaḥ । asaktiviṣamollekhairariṣṭasyāpyasūcyata ।।
cakre yaścaraṇaḥ śubhrairmūrdhni kāliyabhoginaḥ । nakhakāntiphaṇācakraiḥ śeṣaspardhadhirohaṇam ।। mūlāsthicchedaniṣpeṣajātajvālājaṭājuṣā । bāṇabāhuvane yasya cakreṇa krakacāyitam ।।
karkī viṣṇuyaśā yaśca bhaviṣyati yayugakṣaye । sattvadharmalatodyānanavasaurabhamādhavaḥ ।। tasyāścaryaprabhāvasya śrūyatāmidamujjvalam । caritaṃ puṇyapīyūṣaiḥ kilbiṣakṣālanakṣamam ।।
prabhāvaṃ tasya tattvena vaktuṃ ko nu pragalbhate । yatra vācaspatirmūko dūre bhogipatergiraḥ ।। prādurbhāvasaṃgrahaḥ ।। vṛtte vṛtravadhe pūrvaṃ saṃgrāme tārakāmaye ।
tridaśāḥ śaraṇaṃ jagmurviśvaksenaṃ janārdanam ।। dattaṃ tenābhayaṃ teṣāṃ viṣame daityaje bhaye । saṃhatā dānavāḥ sarve viviśuḥ samarāṅganam ।। mayo māyānidhisteṣāmagraṇīrugravigrahaḥ ।
babhau haimaṃ samārūḍho rathamṛkṣasahasragam ।। tāraḥ krośādhikāyāmamāyasaṃ rathamāsthitaḥ । yuktaṃ svarasahasreṇa dhūmottho agnirivābabhau ।। hayagrīvaḥ samāruhya rathaṃ hayasahasragam ।
mattukuñjarayuktaṃ ca tvaṣṭā mandaragauravam ।। vīrā virocanādyāśca tasthuḥ samarasaṃmukhāḥ । kalpāntajaladabyūhavipulaṃ tadbalārṇavam ।। viṣṇunā vihitāśvāsā vīkṣya devāḥ samādravan ।
airāvaṇagatasteṣāṃ sahasrākṣaḥ puro babhau ।। indrāyudhasahasrāṇi darśayanvajraraśmibhiḥ । yamastāramahāhāraḥ śyāmo mahiṣavāhanaḥ ।। tasthau lambāmbudo nīlaśailo nirjharavāniva ।
śvetāśvo maṇimālāṅko varuṇastaraṇiprabhaḥ ।। rathe rarāja kailāse ratnakūṭa ivodgataḥ । hemarkmā hemaratho hemāṅgadādharaḥ ।। jahāra dhanado meroḥ sūryātapajuṣaḥ śriyam ।
himaraśmirhimaśilāśubhrāśvastuhināyudhaḥ ।। tasthau jaladavāhaśca vāyurāyuḥ śarīriṇām । devaśca svayamabhyāyādbhagavānkaiṭabhāntakaḥ ।। dīptacakragadāśārṅganandano garuḍadhvajaḥ ।
cakraṃ rarāja tasyājau dhārābimbitadānavam ।। antaḥpraviṣṭanihatārātivrātamivābhitaḥ । praśānte jvalite merurivāsya bhujagāntakaḥ ।। babhāse bhāsvaro vāhaḥ pravāhaḥ śatrutejasām ।
tasya dīptataraiḥ pakṣairbabhūva pihitaṃ nabhaḥ ।। antyairdvādaśabhiḥ sūryairivaikaghanatāṃ gataiḥ । virarāja tadārūḍho hariḥ kaustubhabhūṣitaḥ ।। vaḍavānalasaṃyukto maināka iva ratnasūḥ ।
rudrādityamarudviśvasādhyāśvivasucāraṇāḥ ।। udyayuḥ kṣubdhasainyābdheḥ kallolā iva saṃgatāḥ । athoddhūtāmbudhidhvānaḍajīkṛtajagattrayaḥ ।। rarāsa ghoṣagambhīraḥ samarāmbhadundubhiḥ ।
petuḥ parasparaṃ teṣāṃ dehe tejasvināṃ prabhāḥ ।। pravṛtte samare hemanārācanicayā iva । surāsurakarotsṛṣṭaśastrāstranikapotthitāḥ ।। jvālāścakrurdhvajāgreṣu kṣaṇaṃ pītāṃśukabhramam ।
cerustridaśamātaṅgadantollikhitakaṅkaṭāḥ ।। jātadhūmānalā daityā meghā iva savidyutaḥ । teṣāṃ vakṣastaṭe bhugnadantāste divyakuñjarāḥ ।। sikatāsetuniḥsārānamanyanta kulācalān ।
tato daityabhujoddhūtaśastranirvivirā divi ।। babhūvurniścalāḥ kṣipraṃ citranyastā ivāmarāḥ । iyamatyantadurvārā daityamāyā mahīyasī ।। yamo avi niyameneva baddhastannidhaneṣu yat ।
vāyuḥ paṅguriva kṣipramaprakāśa ivāṃśumān ।। jayastu yudhi daityeṣu vahniḥ śīta ivābhavat । tataḥ sahasranayano vajreṇonmya daityajām ।। māyāṃ mayamukhānvīrānsuraiḥ punarayodhayat ।
vajrivajranikṛttānāṃ daityānāṃ patatāṃ bhuvi ।। gurubhirvigrahaiḥ prāpuraikyaṃ saptāpi te abdhayaḥ । te gajendra ivāliptā dānavā dānavāribhiḥ ।। tamobhirāvṛtāḥ petuḥ surendrema vimohitāḥ ।
bahumāyastato māyāṃ mayaḥ samayavartinīm ।। pramayāyaiva devānāmaurvānalavatīṃ vyadhāt । ūrujastanayo vahneḥ saṃkalpādbrahmacāriṇaḥ ।। lokāndidhakṣuḥ kālātmā vārbhakṣo brahmaṇo varāt ।
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ pūrvamaurvo bhaktyā varapradaḥ ।। jajvāla suresanāsu tasminsamarasaṃkaṭe । aurveṇa dahyamānāste jvālājaṭilavigrahāḥ ।। ekībhūtānyamanyanta tejāṃsi ca tamāṃsi ca ।
vivaśāstridaśāḥ sarve tenaurvānalaparvaṇā ।। varuṇaṃ śītaraśmiṃ ca trāṇameva vyacintayan । athākhaṇḍalanirdiṣṭaścandramā varuṇāgragaḥ ।। kṣipanhimaśilāsaṃghānudyayau yudhi dānavān ।
tuṣāravāripūraiste bhṛśaṃ tābhyāṃ samāhatāḥ ।। niśceṣṭā dānavāḥ prāpuḥ kāṣṭhapāṣāṇatulyatām । himasya mahatī śaktiḥ sā kāpi dahanātmikā ।। yayā dānavasaṃghānāmasthibhaṅgo mahānabhūt ।
tuṣārāśanisaṃchannā dānavānāmanīkinī ।। nāsāniḥśvāsavivarairnirvibhāgamasūcyata । māyāvinimayaṃ jñātvā mayaḥ svajanasiddhaye ।। asṛjatpārvatīṃ māyāṃ drumaśastraśilāghanām ।
drumaśailaniruddhānāṃ sphuṭitāyudhavarmaṇām ।। moho jajṛmbhe devānāmṛte cakragadādharam । tataḥ kṣaṇāttadādiṣṭau tadanu pāṇitaujasā ।। samaṃ viviśatuḥ senāṃ daityānāmagnimārutau ।
bhasmakūṭāvalīśeṣānkṛtvā drumaśiloccayān ।। uddhūtāndikṣu vikṣipya tau raṇāgre viceratuḥ । anilollāsitajvālājvalitaśmaśrubhīṣaṇaḥ ।। daityānāṃ dahyamānānāṃ dhūmaḥ kāla ivodyayau ।
mārutasyāgnitaptasya vahnetodyatasya ca ।। abhūtkūtāntahuṃkāraghoraḥ kahakahāravaḥ । vicaṭaccarmaṇāmeṣaṃ chamacchamiti medasām ।। sphuṭassthūlāsthibandhānāṃ ko api vyatikaro abhavat ।
jayatsu surasaṅgheṣu bhaṅge ditijamaṇḍale ।। kālanemiḥ samuttasthau trijagadgrasalālasaḥ । jṛmbhāvispaṣṭadaṃṣṭāgrairugravaktrairbhṛtāmbaraḥ ।। jagatkṣayāyeva rasādahaṃpūrvikayotthitaiḥ ।
tasyāñjanaśilāstambhasaṃbhārairbhujamaṇḍalaiḥ ।। abhavankakubho bhīmabogibhogavṛtā iva । viṭaṅkamukuṭaprāptaghṛṣṭabrahmāṇḍakarpare ।। asṛjaddhūmajālena kṣayajīmūtaḍambarān ।
śatavaktrasya netrebhyastasya jvālā diśo yayuḥ ।। tacchāyayā jagatsarvamadṛśyamabhavatkṣaṇāt । aghoraiḥ kālarajanīsaṅghaiḥ saṃghaṭṭitairiva ।। tasya viśvakṣayākṣepadīkṣāsamayamaṇḍalaiḥ ।
dīptāyuprabhācakrairālokaḥ kakubhāmabhūt ।। ghaṭṭayansarvatejāṃsi sarvabhūtāni kampayan । jahāra jaladavyūhānkopaniḥśvāsamārutaiḥ ।। udymya pavanāskandhasaṃghaṭṭoddhaṭṭanaṃ bhujam ।
ajīvavatsa ditijānkṣubdhābdhidhvānayā girā ।। udāyudhaiḥ pramuditairdānavaistatpuraḥ saraiḥ । tato yuyudhire devāḥ kālanemihataujasaḥ ।। tasminsamarasaṃghaṭṭe tumule prāṇahāriṇi ।
vyavardhata mahānkāyaḥ karālaḥ kālaneminaḥ ।। tadvaktrakuharodvāntajvālāvalayitāḥ surāḥ । tiryagūrdhvaṃ pravṛddhaiśca tadbhujairabhito hatāḥ ।। tacchastravṛṣṭidalitāstatkarākṛṣṭamaulayaḥ ।
peturbhraṣṭā vimānebhyaḥ kṣīṇapuṇyā iva kṣitau ।। bhagne vakramukhe śakre varuṇe karuṇāspade । dhanade nidhanāpanne śaśāṅke grāsaśaṅkite ।। bhagnāyudhadhvajacchattrā chinnasyandanakuñjarāḥ ।
niśceṣṭāstridaśāstasthurdinadīpā ivāprabhāḥ ।। śītasya vahne kā vārtā taraṇistāradarpaṇaḥ । āsthā kiṃ niścale vāyau kiṃ yamena hataujasā ।। kimete mudritā rudrā vasavo vyasavo nu kim ।
iti bruvāṇā nādena nanandurditinandanāḥ ।। tataḥ saṃprāptavijayaḥ kālanemiḥ kṣatāmaraḥ । lokapālapade tasthau vibhajyānekadhā vapuḥ ।। jalaṃ bhūtvābhavadvyāpī vāyurbhūtvā vavau svayam ।
somasūryatanurbhūtvā rātryahāni cakāra saḥ ।। jagrāha sarvalokātmā havyamagnimukhaḥ svayam । sarvadevamayaḥ so abhūditi viṣṇujigīṣayā ।। samastabhuvanādhīśaḥ sarvadevagaṇairyutaḥ ।
vedadharmakṛpāsatyaiḥ śriyā ca na samāśritaḥ ।। sa dadarśātha devādiṃ devaṃ garuḍalāñchanam । upekṣitāgrasaṃmardaṃ raṇakautukalīlayā ।। prabhādāmābhirāmeṇa kaustubhena vibhūṣitam ।
sphuradindrāyudhodāraṃ snigdhaśyāmamivāmbudam ।। bhujairvibhrājitaṃ ratnakeyūradhṛtipallavaiḥ । hārakāntisudhāsiktaiḥ pārijātairivāparaiḥ ।। uhyamānaṃ suparṇena suvarṇacchavihāriṇā ।
mandaroddhārabhītena mūrteneva sumeruṇā ।। daityasaṃhāragaṇanācihnahemāṅgadāṃ gadām । dhārayantaṃ girīndrāṇāṃ gauravairiva nirmitām ।। aruṇairūruyugale ralasūryāṃśubhirvṛtam ।
madhukaiṭabhakaṇṭhāsṛkchaṭābhiriva carcitam ।। śaṅkhakāntivitānena ratnamālātaraṅgiṇā । kṣīrodeneva śayanāyāsatrastena sevitam ।। rāhukaṇṭhāṭavīchedaprocchalacchoṇitāruṇaiḥ ।
vyāptaṃ cakraprabhācakraiḥ sūryāśubhirivāmbaram ।। aho batāyamasmākaṃ śatrurlocanagocaraḥ । nirañjanadaśāṃ yena nītā daityavadhūdṛśaḥ ।। ghnatā hiraṇyakaśipuṃ sutārairnakharāṅkuraiḥ ।
hantā hatānyanenaiva muktābhāni yaśāṃsi naḥ ।। nṛsiṃhacaraṇākrāntirajodigdhāṃ sabhābhuvam । hatvemaṃ kṣālayāmyeṣa daityaharṣāśruvāribhiḥ ।। iti bruvāṇaṃ sāvajñaṃ līlāsmitasitādharaḥ ।
pātinā darpamadhunā matto asmītyabhyadhādvibhuḥ ।। ghorāṭṭahāsavikaṭo dānavādhipatistataḥ । apātayacchastravṛṣṭiṃ devorasi bhujairghanaiḥ ।। akampyata suparṇo api gadayā caṇḍavegayā ।
devorasi bhujairyena niṣkampo akampata kṣaṇam ।। vismitaḥ kopasaṃrambādatha viṣṇurvyavardhata । sahasrabāhucaraṇaḥ sahasravadanekṣamaḥ ।। sa sudarśanamāsādya viṣadaṃ bhayadaṃ dviṣām ।
paryantatejaḥprasaraiḥ kiratkāñcanāvālukam ।। daityāsthikūṭakuṇṭhākaṃ kṣurāgraṃ vajramaṇḍalam । cikṣepa krakacakrūraṃ dānavānanakānane ।। tadviṣṇubhujanirmuktaṃ pratimānaṃ vivasvataḥ ।
cakartāgniśikhodgāraṃ ghoraṃ vaktraśataṃ dviṣaḥ ।। nikṛttabhujavaktrotthasaradrudhiranirjharaḥ । na papāta ciraṃ daityo manyustabdha iva sthitaḥ ।। pakṣavātena tārkṣyasya kṣuṇṇakṣmādharamaulinā ।
saptābdhayaḥ samutpetustaraṅgāliṅgitāmbarāḥ ।। sarvataḥ pāṇipādena sarve sarvatra dānavāḥ । pīḍitā viśvarūpeṇa prayayuḥ smṛtiśeṣatām ।। kālanemivadhaḥ ।।
tato nivṛtte durvṛtte pravṛtte dharmakarmaṇi । brahmaprabhṛtibhirdevaiḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ ।। svapade śakramādāya brahmasadma yayau hariḥ । vanditastrijagadvandyaiḥ siddhaiḥ saṃvinmayātmabhiḥ ।।
tato nijāśramaṃ gatvā svaprabhodbhāsitaṃ vibhuḥ । bheje ambudhau yogānidrāmadabhrābhrottaracchade ।। taṃ śeṣaśāyinaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sahasravadanaṃ śanaiḥ । nidrā siṣeve mattālimāleva kamalākaram ।।
tasya pītāṃśukodāraṃ suptasya vibabhau vapuḥ । nābhebrahmasarojottharajaḥ puñjairivācitam ।। kalayannakṣasūtreṇa laukikīṃ kālakalmaṣām । prajāḥ śvāsāvalīsūtraiḥ saṃjahārotsasarja ca ।।
tasminprasupte vidhinā dakṣaiṇāyanakāriṇā । nidrāpi nidrayevābhūttamaḥpaṭalamīlitā ।। jṛmbālasyavimohāṅkā nṛṇāṃ jīvārthahāriṇī । adīrghapralaye seyaṃ pāvanī viṣṇusaṃgamāt ।।
tato varṣasahasreṣu yāteṣu ca kṛte kate । tretāyāṃ vinivṛttāyāṃ dvāpare tanutāṃ gate ।। kamalākelikamalaprāntavātavibodhitam । pitāmahamukhā devāḥ sahasrākṣapurāḥsarāḥ ।।
ekībhūtāḥ samabhyetya jagatkāryārthamudyatāḥ । taṃ tuṣṭuvurmunigaṇāḥ phullapadmakarāḥ kṣaṇam ।। yoganidrāpadeśena garbhīkṛtajagattraye । tvayi deva na jānīmaḥ kartvayaṃ suptasaṃvidā ।।
trailokyakarmaṇāṃ mudrāṃ nidrāṃ netrābjaṣaṭpadīm । tyaja bhogaparimlānāmiva nīlotpalasrajam ।। sphāreṇa dakṣiṇenākṣṇā janmakṣetreṇa bhāsvataḥ । jaganti kamalānīva vikāsaya jagatpate ।।
savyenendūdayānandaviṣyandāmṛtavarṣiṇā । bhūtāni sarvabhūtātmankumudānīva jīvaya ।। deva devāḥ pratīkṣante tvatprasādāvalokanam । vijñaptiḥ śrūyatāmeṣā jagatāṃ kāryagauravāt ।।
śrutveti devarṣivaco nidrāviṣadalocanaḥ । pārśve valitahārārdhaviśrāntikṛtamaṇḍalaḥ ।। āvṛttakaṃdharo devānavadaddaśanāṃśubhiḥ । kurvanvadanapadmānāṃ mṛṇālīkāṇḍamaṇḍalam ।।
kimayaṃ lokapālānāṃ mantraśaṃsī samāgamaḥ । api nāma na daityendraiḥ krāntāstridaśabhūmayaḥ ।। phullābjapuñjajayinī kiraṇāṅkurakesarā । iyaṃ vo vadanacchāyā na śaṃsati parābhavam ।।
ayaṃ ca svayamāyātaḥ padmajanmā pitāmahaḥ । hitaṃ ca jagatāṃ kāryaṃ nālpametadbhaviṣyati ।। sajjo ahaṃ bhavatāmarthe kartavyamadhunocyatām । iti vādini deveśe babhāṣe caturānanaḥ ।।
sarvaṃ tvameva sarvātsañjānīṣe kāryamātmanā । praśnājñāḥ kiṃtu bhavataḥ pareṇa na vilaṅghyate ।। sahasraśīrṣaḥ śeṣo ayaṃ vaktuṃ jānāti te stutim । tavaiva bhāratī devī yadi vaiṣā sarasvatī ।।
tvaccakrakrakarotkṛttadaityograviṣapādape । dharmasyati jagatyasminnabhagnapraṇayo rathaḥ ।। vivṛddhaḥ sarvabhūpālāḥ sadācārānuvartinaḥ । prabhūtabalasaṃbhārairbhāraḥ kiṃtu mahānkṣiteḥ ।।
seyaṃ mahīyasī cintā mahīmañjanaśaṅkayā । sadvṛttānāṃ narendrāṇāṃ kṣaye yadayamudyamaḥ ।। prajāpateriti vacaḥ śrutvā devaḥ prajāhitam । tathetyuktvā yayau sārdhaṃ tridaśairamarāvatīm ।।
tāṃ kalpapādapavatīṃ ratnamandirasundarām । praviśya bheje prodbhūtaratnastambhaprabhāṃ samabhām ।। candrakāntāsane tatra kṣīrārṇava ivāpare । stite viṣṇau surāḥ prāpurhemaratnāsanānyatha ।।
brahmavākyātpratīhāre vetrapāṇau samīraṇe । nivātasuptadugdhābdhiniḥśabdamabhavatsadaḥ ।। tatastaṃ sūcitābhikhyā svayaṃ tāmarasaukasā । pādapīṭhe puro viṣṇorupaviśyānatānanā ।।
śyāmā padmapalāśākṣī hārāṃśuśabalastanī । nānāratnaprabhābhaṅkena devī rohiṇabhūbhṛtaḥ ।। uvācorvī mukhāmbhojadivyagandhādhivāsinī । harantī bālavallīnāṃ bhṛṅgabhārakadarthanām ।।
deva tvaccaraṇāmbhojamadhyaviśrāntilālitā । na kadācana jāne ahaṃ jagadbhārapariśramama ।। lalanā kva nu nāmāhaṃ kva ceme kulabhūdharāḥ । tadetattvadavaṣṭambhasaṃbhārasya vidṛmbhitam ।।
majjantī salile pūrvaṃ nalinīdalalīlayā । tvayaivādivarāheṇa daṃṣṭrāgreṇāhamuddhṛtā ।। jagatyekārṇave pūrvaṃ nirmathya madhukaiṭabhau । tanmedasā ghanībhūtā tvayāhaṃ medinī kṛtā ।।
bhārgaveṇa kṛte kopādasakṛtkṣattrasaṃkṣaye । kālena punarudbhūtā manorvaṃśe nareśvarāḥ ।। teṣāṃ subhaṭasaṃghāte gajavājisamākule । vṛddhyā nirvivarībhūte bhāreṇāsmi nipīḍitā ।।
kriyatāṃ tatkṣayopāye apyavadhānalavaḥ kṣaṇam । śaraṇyaṃ trideśeśānāṃ tvāmasmi śaraṇaṃ gatā ।। gururagniḥ suvarṇasya tigmāṃśuśca gavāṃ guruḥ । tārakāṇāṃ guruḥ somaḥ sadā mama gururbhavān ।।
śrutveti pṛthivīvākyaṃ viṣṇunā tiryagīkṣitaḥ । tatsamīhitatattvajño devānprāha pitāmahaḥ ।। aṃśāvatāraḥ kriyatāṃ bhavadbhirbhūtaye bhuvaḥ । eṣa viṣṇuḥ kṣitau sākṣādavatāre kṛtakṣaṇaḥ ।।
purā jalanidhestīre kaśyapena saha sthitam । māṃ gaṅgānugataḥ śrīmānāyayau bhūṣito ambudhiḥ ।। tenāhaṃ plāvito vārbhirdṛptaṃ tamavadaṃ ruṣā । bho rājaveśa śānto asītyuraktamātro bhavattanuḥ ।।
sa jātaḥ śaṃtanurnāma macchāpādvasudhādhipaḥ । vasūnāṃ jananī gaṅgā tamevānugatā priyā ।। tadvaṃśe pāṇḍurutpanno dhṛtarāṣṭraśca bhūmipau । dharmānilendrāśvibhāgāḥ pāṇḍorāyānti putratām ।।
kelaraṃśasya putro astu dhṛtarāṣṭrasya sānujaḥ । anyeṣu rājavaṃśeṣu bhavantu ca surāḥ pare ।। rudraśca śiśirāṃśuśca gandharvoragārākṣasāḥ । teṣāṃ parasparaṃ ghore vairāraṇimudbhave ।
raṇānale kṣayaṃ yātu ghanaṃ kṣitipakānanam ।। tānprajāpatirityuktvā visasarja vusaṃdharām । tatoṃ'śaistatsamādiṣṭāstridaśāḥ kṣmāmavātaran ।। atrāntare heraraṃśo bhagavānnārado muniḥ ।
abhyāyāttejasā kurvandiśaḥ kanakapiṅgalāḥ ।। nādaśaktiṃ kuṭilatāṃ bhuvanodarasaṃkaṭe । mūrtāmiva vahanvīṇāṃ svarajñaśchandasāṃ nidhiḥ ।। rahasyabhettā jagatāṃ kalikelikutūhalī ।
āvarjitajaṭābandhaḥ sa viṣṇu praṇato abhyadhāt ।। bhagavanbhuvi bhūpālavaṃśeṣu tridaśeśvarāḥ । avatīrṇā bhavadvākyātkitveṣa viphalaḥ śramaḥ ।। asatāṃ tāvadamarāḥ samuddhatamahoragāḥ ।
tṛṣṇāñcane api kā śaktistvāṃ vinā parameṣṭhinam ।। dānavā bhuvi saṃbhūtā bhavatā ye hatāḥ purā । avatīrya bhavāneva teṣāṃ mūlakṣaye kṣamaḥ ।। lavaṇaṃ dānavaṃ hatvā śatrughno rāghavānujaḥ ।
chittvā madhuvanaṃ cakre yāṃ purīṃ mathurāṃ purā ।। tasyāmadya samutpannaḥ kaṃso yadukule nṛpaḥ । yo asau hatastvayā pūrvaṃ kālanemirmahāsuraḥ ।। hayagrīvādayo ye ca daityāḥ pūrvaṃ harāstvayā ।
te keśidhenukāriṣṭapralambādyā bhuvi sthitāḥ ।। teṣāṃ vadhāya bhagavankriyatāṃ svayamudyamaḥ । nāradenetyabhihite tathetyūce jagatpatiḥ ।। janmadhāmocitaṃ pṛṣṭastena brahmavadattataḥ ।
śrūyatāṃ bhagavanyaste dhanyaḥ samucitaḥ pitā ।। yajñārthe yājñiyāṃ dhenuṃ purā putrasya kaśyapaḥ । aditiḥ surabhiścāsya vallabhe jagatīpateḥ ।। sa yādavakule jāto vasudevo mahāyaśāḥ ।
devakī rohiṇī ceti te tasya dayite ubhe ।। tasya putratvamāsādya gopakrīḍārasākulaḥ । atyadbhutāni karmaṇi darśayañjahi dānavān ।। dhanyaḥ sa jagatāṃ vandyaḥ kasya vā na spṛhāpadam ।
yaḥ śroṣyati tavāvyaktavarṇaṃ tāteti jalpataḥ ।। iti padmodbhavagirā kṛtābhyupagame harau । nāradaḥ prayayau bhedī kautukenārjavena ca ।। vicitrabhāskarāllokalokasaṃcaraṇavrataḥ ।
sa mahīmetya mathurāṃ viveśa viṣadāṃ purīm ।। kautukānāṃ kulagṛhaṃ ko ayaṃ sakalasaṃpadām । udyānaṃ kalpavallīnāṃ vīkṣya tāṃ vismito abhavat ।। tatra siṃhāsanāsīnāṃ kaṃsaṃ bhīmaṃ mahībhujām ।
pratyagraṃ taṃ dadarśogramugrasenajamagrajaḥ ।। tatsabhāṃ pūjitastena ratnasiṃhāsanojjvalām । praviśya kṣaṇamāsīnastamūce balagarvitam ।। lokasaṃcāriṇā kaṃsa mayā surasabhāntare ।
śrutastava vadhopāye mantraḥ suciracintitaḥ ।। pituḥ svasuste devakyā yo garbho bhavitāṣṭamaḥ । sānugasya sa te mṛtyurvihitaḥ śaṅkitaiḥ suraiḥ ।। ityudīrya munau yāte śvasankaṃsaḥ sabhāsthitaḥ ।
jahāsa kāntiṃ śatrūṇāṃ daṃṣṭrābhistarjayannivaḥ ।। so avadatsacivānantaḥkope apyavikṛtānanaḥ । asūyayeva devānāṃ muhurālokayannabhaḥ ।। aho nu bhedaśīlena muninā mūḍhacetasā ।
nākaukasāmaviṣaye kathito mantra eṣa naḥ ।। nitarāṃ pratikūlo ahaṃ devānāmadhunā sthitaḥ । keśimukhyāḥ kṣayāyorvyāṃ vicarantu madāśayā ।। pralambalenukāriṣṭapūtanākāliyādayaḥ ।
kurvanti yajvanāṃ loke devadveṣātparābhavam ।। devakīgarbhanidhane tiṣṭhantvavahitāḥ sadā । āptavādena nāryastu puruṣāśca hitā mama ।। ityuktaḥ sacivānkaṃso nirvikāro abhavadbahiḥ ।
antastu cintāsaṃtāpamuvāha viṣaduḥsaham ।। tasminnavasare kṛṣṇo jagadrakṣākṛtakṣaṇaḥ । pātālametya tāngarbhānapaśyatkālanemijān ।। tapasogreṇa te prāpuḥ purā kamalajādvarāt ।
hiraṇyakaśipuścaitānaśapahbrahmanindakaḥ ।। māmanādṛtya yuṣmābhiryasmādārādhito vidhiḥ । tasmātpūrvaṃ piturvadhyā yūyaṃ garbhānmṛtā bhuvi ।। iti tacchāpavivaśānsalilāntaraniścalān ।
tānsuptānvīkṣya bhagavānnidrāmūce svarūpiṇīm ।। ṣaṭsu garbheṣu devakyā jīvānetānkṣipa svayam । bhaviṣyatyantakastatra teṣāṃ kaṃsaḥ svacintayā ।। saptamo rohiṇīgarbho tyājyo vinimayena tu ।
garbhastadante devakyā bhaviṣyāmyahamaṣṭamaḥ ।। govraje nandagopasya yaśodākhyā kuṭumbinī । majjanma samakālatvaṃ tadgarbhe avatara svayam ।। māse aṣṭame navamyāṃ tu kṛṣṇarātryāṃ mṛgekṣaṇe ।
vyatyāsastatra bhavitā tulye janmanyathāvayoḥ ।। tatastvaṃ kaṃsapuruṣaiḥ śilāyāmāhatā bhṛśam । gamiṣyasi divaṃ devi divyena vapuṣānvitā ।। tatra tvaṃ śakrabhaginī bhūtvā pūjyā divaukasām ।
durgā nisumbhasumbhaghnī padaṃ vindhye kariṣyasi ।। candrānanā kṛṣṇatanuḥ siṃhavāhā śikhidhvajā । vyaktāvyaktā parā śaktiḥ kālarātrirjayā dhṛtiḥ ।। hrīḥ śrīrmāyā matiḥ puṣṭirdevānāmadhidevatā ।
jananī vyāpinī kālī pārvatī dharaṇī prabhā ।। sarvakṣayakarī ghorā śivā pīyūṣavarṣiṇī । navamī saṃnidhiḥ siddhidāyinī tvaṃ bhaviṣyasi ।। ityādiśya harirnidrāmunnidrāmburuhekṣaṇaḥ ।
tatkāryaṃ manasā dhyātvā svadhāma bhagavānyayau ।। atha garbheṣu devakyāḥ ṣaṭsu kaṃsasya śāsanāt । hateṣu teṣu kramaśaḥ kiṃkaraiḥ krūrakāribhiḥ ।। saptame api samākṛṣya nīte saṃkarṣaṇābhidhe ।
vintastarohiṇīgarbhagehe svajananīdhiyā ।। aṣṭamaṃ jagatāṃ nāthaṃ garbhamādatta devakī । yena prabhātaveleva sābhūdāsannabhāskarā ।। tataḥ pūrṇe aṣṭame māsi rātryardhe abhijitā yute ।
asūta devakī viṣṇuṃ hutāśanamivāraṇiḥ ।। tasminneva kṣaṇe kanyāṃ yaśodā viṣadadyutim । ajījanatprasanneṣu lokeṣvacyutajanmanā ।। kampite bhuvane devagaṇe maṅgalabhāṣiṇi ।
puṣpavarṣaiḥ prakāśāsu dikṣu kīrtyā hareriva ।। nidrayā mohite rakṣijane tatpreritāśayaḥ । vasudevo rahaścakre garbhayorvyatyayaṃ svayam ।। nandagopagṛhe putraṃ vinyasyādāya tatsutām ।
devakīgarbhaśayane tatyāja bhayaśaṅkitaḥ ।। tataḥ prabuddhaiḥ kanyeyaṃ jātetyadbhutavādibhiḥ । kaṃsāya darśitā garbhasalilārdraiva rakṣibhiḥ ।। tacchāsanādāhatātha sā taiḥ pṛthuśilātale ।
dīptāyudhānekabhujā śikhevāgneḥ svamāviśat ।। hāranakṣatramālāṅkā śaśāṅkarucirānanā । bhūtasaṃmohajananī rajanīva savigrahā ।। haṃsaratnaprabhādīptakuṇḍalābhyāṃ virājitā ।
dyaurivāstodayāsaktaśaśimārtāṇḍamaṇḍalā ।। mayūrabarhābharaṇā māyūradhvajabhūṣitā । śyāmā saśakracāpeva prāvṛṭpīnapayodharā ।। mukuṭena triśṛṅgeṇa nānāratnāṭṭahāsinā ।
vibhūṣitakacābandhā rohiṇādrivatīva bhūḥ ।। sā bhūtasaṃghānugatā hasantī sakhanaṃ muhuḥ । dārayantī tamaḥ kaṃsaṃ tarjayantī samabhyadhāt ।। kaṃsa kaṃsāntakāle ahaṃ kṛṣyamāṇasya vairiṇā ।
vidārya jīvitaṃ dehe pāsyāmi tava śauṇitam ।। ityuktvābhimataṃ deśaṃ yayau kātyāyanī divaḥ । cakampe viphalodyogalajjitaścograsenajaḥ ।। sa gatvā devakīṃ mūrdhnā praṇipatya prasādya ca ।
garbhāḥ kālena te mātaḥ kṣapitā ityabhāṣata ।। kṛṣṇotpattiḥ ।। śaṅkito vasudevastu rohiṇīsutamatyajat । nandagopagṛheṣveva śītāṃśusubhagadyutim ।।
nyāsīkṛtya yaśodāyāṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ saṃkarṣaṇaṃ śiśum । gūḍhe ca kṛṣṇavṛttānte taccintānirato abhavat ।। prerito nandagopastu tena putrahitaiṣiṇā । tyaktvā vṛndāvanaṃ ghoraṃ daityakaṇṭakapannagaiḥ ।।
govardhanavanopānte yamunāsnigdhapādape । vītavighne vrajaṃ cakre bahubhirgokulairvṛtaḥ ।। gambhīramanthanirghoṣaghanānanditacātake । pākāvartighṛtāmodasaṃpūritasamīraṇe ।।
vanaprāpyapraticchannavatsahuṃkāragogaṇe । gopālīkākalīgītaniścalāṅgakuraṅgake ।। kālindītīravānīralatādolāyitārbhake । bhrātrā sahenduśubhreṇa kṛṣṇo marakatadyutiḥ ।।
vyavardhata vanodbhedaḥ sa gāṅga iva yāmunaḥ । prasuptaṃ śakaṭasyādhastṛpte stanyena niścalam ।। kadācittaṃ samutsṛjya yaśodā yamunāṃ yayau । prabuddhaḥ so atha śanakaiḥ pāṇipādaṃ kṣipanmuhuḥ ।।
ruroda daśanoddyotaiḥ kṣīrapūrairivāṅkitaḥ । caraṇau ca prasāryordhvaṃ jṛmbhāvikasitānanaḥ ।। pādenaikena śakaṭaṃ viparyastamadho vyadhāt । atrāntare sambhyetya yaśodā prasnutastanī ।।
śakaṭaṃ bhagnamālokya cakampe sutavatsalā । sā śiśuṃ svasthamādāyetyūce nando viśaṅkitaḥ ।। kenedaṃ śakaṭaṃ bhagnaṃ vinā mattavṛṣāhatīḥ । teneti pṛṣṭāḥ śiśavaḥ kṛṣṇeneti babhāṣire ।।
śakaṭabhaṅgaḥ ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇotsave loke supte niśi niśācarī । āyayau pūtanā nāma māyayā prasnutastanī ।। sā dadhau vadane tasya śiśornidhanakāṅkṣiṇī ।
stanaṃ prāṇaiḥ sahāsyāśca tamākṛṣyoccakarta saḥ ।। hatāyāṃ vyāghraghoṣāyāṃ tasyāmabhyutthito bhayāt । sabhāryo nandagopoo abhūnmagnonmagna ivāmbudhau ।। tato viditavṛttāntau vismayānandanirbharau ।
tau dampatī bahiḥ kaṃsabhayānno kaṃsabhayānno kiṃcidūcatuḥ ।। pūtanāvadhaḥ ।। śanakaiścaraṇanyāsamakrūraiḥ sagatāgataiḥ । harṣaṃ vavarṣa bandhūnāṃ trailokyākramaṇakṣamaḥ ।।
kālena vardhamānau tau kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇau vane । pūryamāṇau madeneva pañcānanakiśorakau ।। virejatuḥ śiśukrīḍāyāṃ subhūṣitavigrahau । rakṣyamāṇāvivāliṅgya bhuvo bhārakṣayakṣamau ।।
kāntau kamalapattrākṣau calatkuṭilakuntalau । smitena cakratuḥ kaṇṭhe sitamuktāvalīriva ।। tulyalāvaṇyamādhuryadhuryaṃ vapurabhūttayoḥ । mahatāṃ saṃśraye nūnamekakāryavirodhine ।।
svecchāgopatanau tatra deve trailokyagoptari । spṛhā tatsaṅgadhanyebhyo gopebhyo abūddivaukasām ।। dhartuṃ yadā yaśodā taṃ na śaśāka mahājavam । ābabandhodare dhīrā dāmnā dāmodaraṃ tadā ।।
tarasā sa samākṛṣya dāmabaddhamulūkhalam । vicacāra vane kelicaturo vigataśramaḥ ।। vismayaṃ prayayurgopāstasyolūkhalakarṣaṇāt । mandarādhāradhairye api jagadyasminna vismitam ।।
vipulau yamunātīre saṃhātāvarjunadrumau । sa prāpya tanmadhyagataścakarṣolūkhalaṃ balāt ।। tadbalonmūlitau vegātpetaturatha tau drumau । yenābhūtkṣobhagambhīraḥ saṃrambho yamunāmbhasaḥ ।।
gopabālāstadālokya bhayasmayatayākulāḥ । yaśodāmūcire gatvā saṃbhramākulitasvarāḥ ।। ayi pramādaśīle tvaṃ sukhasuptena mohitā । pūjyau tau tava putrasya patitāvupari drumau ।।
devānmahābhayānmuktaṃ gatvā taṃ paśya dārakam । śrutveti svedamagneva yaśodā kampitā yayau ।। sā vilokya tayormadhye mahāpādapayoḥ sutam । saṃtrāsaṃ ca prasādaṃ ca vismayaṃ ca yayau kramāt ।।
tataḥ sarve samabhyetya gopavṛddhāḥ sasaṃbhramam । avadankena ghoṣasya daivatau pātitāvimau ।। nābhavanmeghanirghāto vyabhre kā vidyutāṃ kathā । neha matto dvipaḥ kasmādakasmāddrumayoḥ kṣayaḥ ।।
iti vādini gopālamaṇḍale sutamagrahīt । vimucya nandaḥ sāsūyaṃ yaśodāmavalokayan ।। nindati svavadhūṃ yāte nandagope sahānuge । gṛhe gṛhe bhavatko api drumabhaṅgakathāsmayaḥ ।।
drumanipātaḥ ।। kiṃcidunmuktabālyau tāvatha saṃkarṣaṇācyutau । nīlapītāmbarau kākapakṣāṅkau ceraturvane ।। uttaṃsakusumāpīḍaiḥ phalavibhramakāriṇau ।
rakṣātilakaratnāgrāviva nāgakumārakau ।। mayūrapakṣābharaṇaprabhāpallavaśālinau । lāvaṇyāmṛtaniṣyandau pārijātātmajāviva ।। hrasvaveṇukalakvāṇasvabhāvamadhurasvanau ।
prāṃśuśailaśilāsīnāviva kinnaradārakau ।। utpatatkandukodāragulikācaturabhramau । vicitramālyalalitau vidyādharasutāviva ।। pāṇau dadhānau bāṇāṅkakelikodaṇḍaṇḍikām ।
punarvanamivāyātau vīrau rāghavalakṣmaṇau ।। viharantau madodārau tau rājīvavilocanau । rejatuḥ kiṃcidāsannanavayauvanavibhrāmau ।। cirabhogaparimlānaviralauṣadhipādape ।
nāraṃsta keśavastatra navakānanakautukī ।। sa kṛtvā vrajasaṃtrāsaṃ gūḍhaṃ māyāmayairvṛkaiḥ । rantuṃ vṛndāvanopāntaṃ kālindīsundaraṃ yayau ।। niviṣṭe gokule tatra nirbhaye sevyasaṃśraye ।
navakānanasaṃbhogaḥ ko api gopakule abhavat ।। adṛśyata tataḥ śyāmā navodgatapayodharā । vadhūrnaveva kṛṣṇasya prāvṛḍvihitakautukā ।। navavāridharairvyomni calatkalabhavibhramaiḥ ।
viyoginīmanojanmavahnidhūmodgamāyitam ।। jayinaḥ smararājasya vījayanvyajanairiva । tato virahiṇīcintāniḥśvāsaprasabho anilaḥ ।। bhuvi kāntāsmitasitā babhuḥ ketakasūcayaḥ ।
meghāmardaviśīrṇasya śiśirāṃśoḥ kalā iva ।। balākāvalayāścerurgurugarjaratā divi । mattameghagajendrāṇāṃ dantakānticayā iva ।। ghanānāṃ śakracāpena vanānāṃ śikhitāṇḍavaiḥ ।
parasparaprabhāpuñjaspardheva samajāyata ।। varṣākṣālitasacchāyatamālakadalībharāḥ । snigdhasnāteva yuvatirvirarāja vasuṃdharā ।। tvaṅgatturaṅgabhrūbhaṅgā phenakūṭāhva hāsinī ।
matteva yauvanavatī babhrāma yamunāvane ।। babhau saudāminīdāmakāntiḥ kāpi payomucām । meruśekharalagneva taptajāmbūnadacchaṭā ।। nīlābhracakitāḥ kvāpi rājahaṃsagaṇā yayuḥ ।
ciraṃ naṣṭamivānveṣṭuṃ śaśāṅkaṃ kumudākarāḥ ।। tasminkadambakuṭajāmodapramuda nirbhare । kāle virahiṇāṃ kāle kṛṣṇaṃ saṃkarṣaṇo abravīt ।। pūritaṃ parisarpadbhirbalākāphenahāsibhiḥ ।
paśya kṛṣṇa ghanairvyoma yāmunairiva vāribhiḥ ।। taḍitpītāmbarajuṣāṃ vanamālāvalambinām । vibhāti vārivāhānāṃ taveva śyāmalaṃ vapuḥ ।। ityagrajavacaḥ śrutvā praṇayābharaṇaṃ hariḥ ।
lalāsa līlābharaṇo madhūrābharaṇe vane ।। prāvṛḍvarṇanam ।। varṣacchedaprakāśe atha navībhūta ivākhile । kadācidviharankṛṣṇaḥ kānane bhrātaraṃ vinā ।।
nyagrodhaṃ prāpa vipulaṃ vṛto gopakumārakaiḥ । pravṛddhabhujasaṃbhārairnabho mātumivodgatam ।। vidyādharasanādhāni tridaśādhyuṣitāni ca । kulādriśikharāṇīva kautukāddraṣṭumutthitam ।।
sarvāśāpūraṇodārasacchāyaṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ bhuvaḥ । prāsādaṃ vandevīnāṃ bhāṇḍīraṃ nāma pādapam ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā snigdhamānandabandhuṃ śaurirnirantaram । hṛṣṭaścacāra tanmūle gītavādyavinodakṛt ।।
tato dadarśa kālindīṃ jagaddvipamadacchaṭām । tvaṅgattaraṅgakuṭilāṃ dīrghaveṇīmivāvaneḥ ।। phenabudbudanakṣatramālāṃ puṇyajanocitām । yātāṃ tāpicchasaccāyāṃ dravatāmiva śarvarīm ।।
visphāraśapharotphālasphuratsphītaphaṇāṅkitām । senāmiva bhujaṅgānāṃ taraṅgābhogabhaṅgurām ।। unnidrapadmavadanāṃ vikacotpalalocanām । cakravākakucābhogāṃ śyāmāṃ haṃsasitasmitām ।।
caṇḍāṃśutāpavigalanmaṇiparvatakandarām । saṃpravṛttāmivāvartasphūrjanmarakatadravām ।। kvacitsuptāmivāspandāṃ kvacinmattāmivoddhatām । mūrchitāṃ viṣavegena kvaciddaṣṭāmivāhinā ।।
kvacidbhītāmiva cchannāṃ kvacidvyāgramivākulām । amandavibhramālolāṃ kvacinmānavatīmiva ।। majjadgopāṅganātuṅgakucakumbhonnatodakām । nananda kṛṣṇastāṃ dṛṣṭvā taruṇīmiva hāriṇīm ।।
tato dadarśa pātālatalagambhīrabhīṣaṇam । karālakālabhrūbhaṅgabhaṅgurormiśatākulam ।। tamomalinamatyugramakāraṇabhayapradam । dūrātparihṛtaṃ sarvaiḥ khalaṃ naramiveśvaram ।।
adyāpi na jagadgrastaṃ mayeti jvalitāśayam । dhūmodgamāyitaistoyairniḥśvasantamivāniśam ।। vyāptamāśīrviṣairghoraistīrakoṭaraśāyibhiḥ । vītacandrārkanakṣatraṃ svamivātaṅkadaṃ hradam ।।
nikṣīkṣya dūrākṣobhyaṃ kṣaṇaṃ hariracintayat । asminsa kāliyo nāma kālakūṭotkaṭaḥ phaṇī ।। nivāsatyasitākāraḥ sarvaprāṇibhayaṃkaraḥ । yeneyaṃ viṣaniḥśvāsairdūṣitā yamunātaṭī ।।
so ayaṃ matto atidarpeṇa matto nāśamihārhati । saṃbhavo ayaṃ mama prāyo vināśāya durātmanām ।। vicintyeti hradopāntākadambataruputrakam । baddhakakṣyaḥ samāruhya papāta nabhaso ambhasi ।।
garjatā kṛṣṇameghena sā vegamavapātinā । udyayau kṣobhitāṃ vāri vikarālormiśekharam ।। dūrotpatitaśailābhakallolavinipātajaḥ । tadabhūddhorasaṃghaṭṭaṭāṅkāro ghaṭṭitāmbaraḥ ।।
tataḥ sa dahanodgāraviṣaphūlkārabhīṣaṇaḥ । pañcāsyo raktanayanaḥ kāliyaḥ samadṛśyata ।। añjanācalatulyena tasya bhogena sarvataḥ । vardhamānena saṃruddhaṃ jalaṃ vyoma vyagāhata ।।
tatkopajvalanajvālāvalaye kṣipramambhasām । aparaurvānalabhrāntijanakaḥ praloya'bhavat ।। dantaniṣpeṣajāstasya viṣānalaparamparāḥ । bhasmasātsahasā tīratarumālāṃ pracakrire ।।
bhogenāveṣṭyamāno atha kṛṣṇaḥ kṛṣṇena bhoginā । babhau valayito vārbhistamāla iva yāmunaiḥ ।। sānugenoragendreṇa govindaṃ gopadārakāḥ । daṃṣṭrākoṭiviṣolkabhirvyāptaṃ vīkṣya samantataḥ ।।
saṃtrastā vrajamabhyetya cakranduḥ srastakandukāḥ । eṣa dāmodaro ghore patitaḥ kāliyāmbhasi ।। veṣṭitaḥ kālakalpena bhoginātha viṣetkaṭam । vacaḥ śrutvā yayuḥ sarve nandagopamukhā hradam ।।
pratyagrāyāsaniḥspande saṃdehādolitāśaye । nandagope phaṇivyāptaputravaktrāvalokini ।। tārapralāpamukhare yaśodāduḥsvadārite । strījane atīva saṃtapte pyāpte rāgaviṣairiva ।।
tīraṃ saṃkarṣaṇenaitya saṃjñayaiva vibodhitaḥ । bhujābhyāṃ bhīṣaṇābhogaṃ bhogamāsphālya bhoginaḥ ।। caraṇābhyāṃ samākramya harirbandhādvinirgataḥ । avanāmya phaṇācakraṃ saratnaṃ jvalanolbaṇam ।
āruroha śiraḥsphāraṃ madhyamaṃ madhusūdanaḥ ।। tataḥ sa sarvajagatāṃ carācaragururguruḥ । unmamarda padanyāsairnṛtyanniva savibhramam ।। srastadarpo galaddhairyaḥ prodvāntograviṣastataḥ ।
sa kṛṣṇaṃ rudhirodgāragalitākṣaramabhyadhāt ।। bhītaḥ saṃrakṣaṇīyo ahaṃ nasraḥ sarvātmanā tvayā । añjalivyañjanaṃ dainyaṃ jīvapuṇyamidaṃ mama ।। dāmodaro niśamyaitajjagāda bhujagādhipam ।
hrado ayamaśivācāra sevyo astu bhavatā vinā ।। tatastvamambudhiṃ gaccha yadi vāñchasi jīvitam । tatra matpādamudrā te tārkṣyarakṣā bhaviṣyati ।। iti tacchāsanādyāte sānuge bhujage kṣaṇāt ।
yayuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ praśaṃsanto gopāḥ sānandavismayāḥ ।। kāliyasūdanam ।। tato viviśatuḥ kelikalau haladharācyutau । viśālatālahintālatamālaśyāmalaṃ vanam ।।
pañcatālaphalāsvādananditonmadamānasau । ceratustatra tau ḍimbakrīḍāḍambaratatparau ।। athāyayau dhenukākhyo daityastālavanāśrayaḥ । karālakesarasphāraskandhabandhoddhuraḥ kharaḥ ।।
tasyānugairmahākāyairgardabhairabhito vṛtam । udabhūttālagahanaṃ vyāptaṃ dhūmodgatairiva ।। dhenuko atha bhṛśaṃ kopādrudhirāruṇalocanaḥ । svurairnirdārayanbhūmiṃ rāmakṛṣṇavadhepsayā ।।
āhvānamiva daityānāṃ kurvanpātālavāsinām । ghaṭṭayanniva heṣābhirvajrogradaśanāyudhaḥ ।। abhyadhāvatsamudbhrāntapucchaḥ saṃkarṣaṇaṃ javāt । vātāvadhūtaikaśikhaścandraṃ megha ivākulaḥ ।।
vidār daśanaiḥ so atha rauhiṇeyamasaṃbhramam । babhūva paścimamukhaḥ prahārāya parāṅmukhaḥ ।। tābhyāmeva samādāya taṃ khurābhyāṃ prahāriṇam । cikṣepa tālaśikhare phalārthīva halāyudhaḥ ।।
sa bhagnorutaruskandhasruṭyatkaṭhinakīkasaḥ । papāta niṣlārambhaḥ saha tālaphalairbhuvi ।। sānuge atha hate tasminhate kharaparākrame । vītavighnamabhūtsevyaṃ tattālavanamāyatam ।।
dhenukavadhaḥ ।। bhūyo bhāṇḍīravipinaṃ tau gatvā keliśālinau । dvandvopatanalīlābhirgopaputrairvijahratuḥ ।। atha tāvāyayau vanyakusumottaṃsabhūṣaṇaḥ ।
gopaveṣacchalaccannaḥ pralambo nāma dānavaḥ ।। krīḍābhirāśayagrāhī toṣayitvā sa tau muhuḥ । jahāra skandhamārūḍhaṃ kadācitkeśavāgrajam ।। sa taṃ hṛtvā drutatirnijarūpamadarśayat ।
tamaḥpaṭāvṛtā yena bhītyeva kakubho abhavan ।। tasyāñjanādriśikharākāre mūrdhni parisphuran । dāvānalaśikhāpuñjapiṅgaścūḍāmaṇirbabhau ।। tasyābabhau mukhodgīrṇā sadhūmadahanāvalī ।
nīlapītā patākeva daṃṣṭrātoraṇalambinī ।। nīlaśailaśilākūṭavikaṭe rohiṇīsutaḥ । babhāra dānavaskandhe śaradambhodavibhramam ।। hriyamāmaḥ sa tenāśu mānuṣaṃ bhāvamāśritaḥ ।
saṃmitaṃ keśavenārātpurāṇaṃ smārito vapuḥ ।। yattatparataraṃ dhāma vāgīśaṃ viśvatomukham । sarvadevamayaṃ satyamanantamajamavyayam ।। nijaṃ vipulāmāsthāya balaṃ bhūmidhṛtikṣamam ।
jaghāna muṣṭinā mūrdhni pralambaṃ dhenukāntakaḥ ।। muṣṭipātādvighaṭitasphuṭallālāṭakarparam । kāye viveśa daityasya kīrmaraktacchaṭaṃ śiraḥ ।। skandhādavasrute rāme girisphāraṃ kalevaram ।
nipapāta pralambasya lambamānabhujadvayam ।। pralambavadhaḥ ।। balinā baladevena pralambe vinipātite । prayāte vārṣike tatra śanairmāsacatuṣṭaye ।।
pratyāsanne navautsukyanirbharānandadāyini । kratūtsave samārambho babhūva vanavāsinām ।। tataḥ saptacchadāmodamālinīhaṃsanūpurā । viṣadendumukhī phullanīlotpalavilocanā ।।
nimantriteva pramadā tasminvrajamahotsave । adṛśyata sitāmbhodabhaktismerāmbarā śarat ।। tatra gopagirā jñātvā yāgaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ marutpateḥ । ūce smitasitālokaiḥ pāñcajanyamivāsṛjan ।।
aho nu hāsyajananī mugdheyaṃ bhavatāṃ matiḥ । yāgaḥ śakrāya nārhe ayaṃ gopā hi giridaivatāḥ ।। iti tadvacasā gopairgiriyajñe pravartate । vihitā bhakṣyagirayo ghṛtakṣīrorunirjharāḥ ।।
govardhanagireryajñe tasminbahvannasaṃbhṛte । pāyasaiḥ sadadhicchannairhimacchanneva bhūrabhūt ।। mayūrapattrābharaṇāḥ kusamottaṃsaśekharāḥ । tasminyāge babhurgopā gāvaśca suvibhūṣitāḥ ।।
girimūrdhani viśvātmā pareṇa girivarṣmaṇā । vapuṣā bubhuje kṛṣṇastatsarvaṃ tairniveditam ।। tatpraharṣasmitodāraṃ nijaṃ divyaṃ mahadvapuḥ । praṇanāma svayaṃ kṛṣṇo gopaiḥ saha giriprabham ।।
giriyajñaḥ ।। vṛtte mahotsave tasmiñśatamanyuḥ krudhā jvalan । ādideśa vrajocchittyai ghorānsaṃvartakāmbudān ।। tena te preritāḥ kṣipraṃ nīlaśailaśilāghanāḥ ।
ghanāścakrurjagadvyāptaṃ kālarātriśatairiva ।। bhinnāñjanaghanacchāyairjīmūtairgarjitorjitaiḥ । grastā ivoddhataiḥ kṣipraṃ nādṛśyanta diśo daśa ।। tataḥ karikarākārā stambhasaṃrambhavibhramāḥ ।
peturdharādhare dhārāḥ parihārā dhṛteḥ param ।। kālāṭṭahāsavikaṭā jalodgārāḥ prapātinaḥ । virejuḥ kālameghānāṃ girīṇāmiva nirjharāḥ ।। so abhavadbhīṣaṇābhogameghasaṃghātanirmitaḥ ।
ullasatsthūlakallolalolaḥ salilaviplavaḥ ।। vidyutpiśaṅgakeśānāṃ garjatāṃ megharakṣasām । bhayeneva yayau kvāpī jagatī jalasaṃstutā ।। te śakrādhiṣṭitā ghorā dīptāśakrāyudhāṅkitāḥ ।
varṣāśaninipātena cakrire kadanaṃ gavām ।। vartmavinyastanetrāṇāṃ patantīnāmitastataḥ । trāsaśītaparītānāṃ ghorastasāmabhūtkṣayaḥ ।। ayaṃ sa pralayārambhaḥ puṣkarāvartabhīṣaṇaḥ ।
saṃprāpta iti bhītānāṃ gopānāmabhavadbhavaḥ ।। taddṛṣṭvā vaiśasaṃ ghoraṃ nāśāyopasthitaṃ gavām । govindo jagatāṃ goptā rakṣāṃ kṣaṇamacintayat ।। imamutpāṭya śailendramahaṃ govardhanaṃ balāt ।
chattrīkaromyupastānāṃ saṃśrayaṃ vipulaṃ gavām ।। iti dhyātvā dhiyaṃ dhīro nidadhe bhūdhare dṛśam । utpāṭanakṣaṇakṣāntyai phullapadmāvalīmiva ।। tataḥ sapadi viśvātmā balena mahatānvitaḥ ।
ujjahāra giriṃ dorbhyāṃ sphuṭanmūlaśikhātalam ।। mūlāvalambinaḥ kṣipraṃ pātālamiva nirgatāḥ । uddhṛtasya gireḥ sarpāḥ snāyujālatulāṃ yayuḥ ।। saṃpīḍitaśilāpīḍānibaḍikṛtanirjharaiḥ ।
babhuḥ palitakalloladukūlavalitā diśaḥ ।। haritālarajaḥpuñjaiḥ pavanāvartanartitaiḥ । babhau tatpātitairvyāptaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pītāṃśukairiva ।। vyādhūtāstasya pārśveṣu kṣaṇamutpatato ghanāḥ ।
kṣmābhṛtaḥ pakṣavikṣepabhrāntiṃ cakruḥ svacāriṇām ।। tasmingovindadordaṇḍacchattrībhūte mahībhṛti । phullamālāvalī srastā cakre sragdāmavibhramam ।। svacāriṇo adya sucirādime te girayo vayam ।
jātā vajradhara kṣmābhṛtpakṣacchedamadaṃ tyaja ।। iti trāsotpatantīnāṃ vidyādharamṛgīdṛśām । raśanānūpurārāvaiḥ sa jagādeva bhūdharaḥ ।। paryastaprasarastobhakṣubhyatkesarigarjitaiḥ ।
sa ghoraghanasaṃghātānatarjayadivorjitān ।। sa samunmūlanāyāsasaṃbhrāntadvipayūthapaiḥ । babhau khe śekharollekhapātitairiva vāridaiḥ ।। ghūrṇamānamahāśākhikusumotkarareṇubhiḥ ।
sa rakṣāmaṇḍalānīva dhenūnāṃ vidadhe muhuḥ ।। trāsāpatatsiddhavadhūtārahāraistaraṅgibhiḥ । adhaḥsthāngaganastho adrirjahāseva mahīdharān ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā khecarāḥ prāhuḥ kimayaṃ girirutthitaḥ ।
yadi na pralayārambho yadi nākālaviplavaḥ ।। tataḥ kṛṣṇagirā gopāḥ śailotpāṭanabhūgṛham । vipulaṃ viviśuḥ śāntyai nikhilaiḥ saha godhanaiḥ ।। nivāte nirjale tasminsuviśāle girestaṭe ।
tasthurjagānnivāsena gāvo gopāśca rabhitāḥ ।। vṛṣṭicchanne prayāte atha saptarātre marutpatiḥ । jagāma viphalodyogalajjito jaladaiḥ saha ।। tatastaṃ vipulābhogatuṅgaśṛṅgaṃ guruṃ girim ।
nyaveśayannijapade līlayaiva jagadguruḥ ।। govardhanoddharaṇam ।। saptarātraṃ dhṛte tasmingirau garuḍalakṣmaṇāḥ । taṃ draṣṭumāyayau sākṣātsahasrākṣo ativismitaḥ ।।
jaṅgamādiva kailāsātso avatīrya suradvipāt । govardhanaśilāsīnaṃ dadarśa madhusūdanam ।। antarhitena tārkṣyeṇa pakṣairācchāditātapam । asatyākalitenaiva tejasāpūritāmbaram ।।
mayūrakaṇṭhasacchāyaṃ taptahemaprabhāṃśukam । indranīlagireḥ śṛṅgaṃ taptaṃ bālātapairiva ।। taṃ vīkṣya kamalākāntaṃ gopaveṣadharaṃ harim । sahasranetramātmānaṃ manasā praśaśaṃsa saḥ ।।
maulikuṇḍalakeyūrasphāraratnāṃśusaṃcayaiḥ । indrāyudhasahasrāṇi muhurdikṣu kṣipanniva ।। abhyetya keśavaṃ śakro babhāṣe praṇayocitam । dantatviṣā daśa diśaḥ sudhayā pūrayanniva ।।
atidaivamidaṃ karma tava kṛṣṇa kimadbhutam । śaktiralpīyasī yasya samagrajagatāṃ gatiḥ ।। sarvalokopari paraṃ vartante kāmadhenavaḥ । tāsāṃ tridaśapūjyānāṃ brahmaṇaścāsmi śāsanāt ।।
prāpto abhiṣektuṃ govinda rājye tvāmīpsitaṃ gavām । ityuktvā ratnakumbhena mūrdhni tasya dadau payaḥ ।। upendramabhiṣicyendraḥ prasādya ca punaḥ punaḥ । pālyastvayā sakhā bandhuḥ svasreyo janakasya yaḥ ।।
tvayā daityacchidā kṛṣṇa keśikaṃsavadhe kṛte । bhavatsahāyaḥ pṛthivīṃ sa jeṣyati dhanaṃjayaḥ ।। iti praṇayino vācaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ śrutvā śacīpateḥ । jānanbhāratavṛttāntaṃ tatheti pratyapadyata ।।
evaṃ rahaḥ samābhāṣya jambhahāsurasūdanam । airāvaṇakarālūnameghena nabhasā yayau ।। govindābhiṣekaḥ ।। gopaveṣadharaṃ gopā devaṃ matvā tamadbhutam ।
mudritā iva tacchaktyā mugdhā no kiṃcidūcire ।। tatastaṃ padmapattrākṣaṃ nivṛttāśeṣaśauśavam । janā nirbharatāruṇyalāvaṇyaṃ nayanaiḥ papuḥ ।। śaranniśāsu saṃpūrṇacandrasmitasitāsu saḥ ।
hariṇīhārinetrābhirvijahāra ratipriyaḥ ।। sa rāgavṛṣayuddheṣu niyuddheṣu ca kautukī । vīraśṛṅgārarabhasaḥ sa babhūva manoharaḥ ।। chekoktiṣu kṛtābhyāsā veśakarmasu sādarāḥ ।
babhustā vismito lāpā vibhrameṣu kṛtakṣaṇāḥ ।। tallīlānukṛtau yatnastatkathāśravaṇe rasaḥ । tatsvairabhāṣaṇe harṣaḥ ko apyabhūdgopayoṣitām ।। tāsāmakṛtakasmerasphuritādharapallavam ।
mugdhānāṃ vadanaṃ prītyai babhūvābhyadhikaṃ hareḥ ।। yadgurūṇāmanāyattāyattāstyaktagṛhakriyāḥ । dveṣiṇyaḥ svajane yacca tatkṛṣṇāsyavijṛmbhitam ।। salajjā api māninyaḥ prakaṭasmaravikriyāḥ ।
tanvyo api tanutāṃ prāpustāstadarpitamānasāḥ ।। kampasvedavatī kasmādakasmātsakhi mūrchitā । api kṛṣṇabhujaṅgena na daṣṭāsi pramādinī ।। nāyaṃ tava gṛhe mārgo mārgo ayaṃ vijane vane ।
yamunātīravānīravallarīkeliveśmanaḥ ।। amuṣminkusumārāme kṛṣṇaṣaṭcaraṇena kim । kṛtavraṇā tvamadhare yenāsi vinatānanā ।। gāyanti yadi kṛṣṇasya caritaṃ gopakanyakāḥ ।
tvaṃ na smarasi kiṃ mūḍhe srastaṃ śīlamivāṃśukam ।। dāmodaramatāsmīti madāndhe kiṃ na pasyasi । sa kāntāśatasaṃketasakto hi bahuvallabhaḥ ।। kiṃ nu nāma stanau tanvi sotkampau vinigūhase ।
pulakāṅkakapolasya vadanasya karoṣi kim ।। iyamindīvaraśyāmā śyāmā kusumahāsinī । kṛṣṇaśca gūḍhasaṃcārī carasyekākinī katham ।। iti gopāṅganāḥ serṣyaṃ saṃbhogasubhagā mithaḥ ।
vyāharanti sma sāsūyaṃ svairaṃ smaraśarāturāḥ ।। kāntākararuhālūnabālavañjulapallavam । ratiśayyārase śairevarbabhūva vilalaṃ vanam ।। tasya kāntataraṃ kāntāḥ samadāḥ saṃmadākulam ।
vadanaṃ vadanodārā ghūrṇamānekṣaṇāḥ papuḥ ।। tāsāmabhisarantīnāmavaśaṃ keśavaṃ prati । petuḥ śaśāṅke sāsūyā dṛśo darśanaśaṅkayā ।। mādhave madhurodārasundarīratitatpare ।
saphalaṃ dhanyamātmānaṃ manye mene manobhavaḥ ।। aho nu jayinī śaktiḥ samarasya smayakāriṇī । prajāpatigurau yasyāḥ saṃpūrṇapraṇayā gatiḥ ।। gopīsaṃkrīḍanam ।।
tataḥ kadācillalanākeliśālini keśave । adṛśyata pradoṣānte daityo mattavṛṣākṛtiḥ ।। ariṣṭo duṣṭacaritastīkṣṇaśṛṅgo aruṇekṣaṇaḥ । puñjīkṛtaḥ śaśikaraistamaḥkūṭa ivāsitaḥ ।।
bhāyayanvṛṣabhānbhīmo bherīgambhīraniḥsvanaḥ । nīlaśailaśilāpīṭhakāṭhoraskandhabandhuraḥ ।। prahārābhimukhaṃ kṛṣṇakukṣinikṣiptacakṣuṣaḥ । tasya śṛṅgayugaṃ lebhe kālatoraṇatulyatām ।।
prahāriṇaṃ madodagraṃ jagrāhograṃ tamacyutaḥ । khalaṃ mūrkhaṃ navaiśvaryaṃ priyavādīva vañcakaḥ ।। gṛhītastena balinā baladevānujena saḥ । babhūvodbhrāntasāvegapucchoddhutarajaḥpaṭaḥ ।।
tasyāndolivaktrasya ghorahuṃkārakāriṇaḥ । vyālaghnā saṅkhamāleva sphāraphenāvalī gale ।। tataḥ kaṇṭhaṃ nipīḍyāsya dhṛtvā mūrdhni padaṃ javāt । śṛṅgamekaṃ samutpāṭya jaghāna vadane hariḥ ।।
sa tīkṣṇaśṛṅgābhihataḥ papāta bhuvi dānavaḥ । prastyānarudhirodgāravicaladdhargharāravaḥ ।। ariṣṭavadhaḥ ।। ariṣṭe nihate tasminnariṣṭe tridivaukasām ।
prabhāvaḥ paprathe śairermathurādhipateḥ puraḥ ।। sa vṛṣṇivṛddhānvibudhānvasudevapurogamam । ugrasenaṃ ca pitaraṃ dārdikyākrūrasātyakān ।। acintyatsamānāyya niścayaṃ nayakovidān ।
niḥśabdajanasaṃcāre niśīthe vyastasevakaḥ ।। pradīpapratibimbāṅkaratnābharaṇatejasā । gūḍhacintānalajvālaṃ bahiḥ prakaṭayanniva ।। so abravītkṣaṇamālokya vadanānyabhimāninām ।
dīrghocchvāsena kathayannavaṃ vairiparābhavam ।। iyaṃ prathitasārāṇāṃ viduṣāṃ satvaśālinām । sūcyate bhavatāmagre mānaglānikadarthanā ।। pramādādavalepādvā vismṛtenālpakena naḥ ।
cūḍāmaṇiṣu vinyastaṃ caraṇaprabhavaṃ rajaḥ ।। na sahante suragurorye sāmyaṃ gurukovidāḥ । spardhayā bata lajjante yudhi vajrāyudhena ye ।। te yūyaṃ yasya sacivaḥ sacivāropitaśriyaḥ ।
tasya kā nāma gaṇanā gaṇanāthe api jāyate ।। avajñopekṣitasyāyaṃ vipākaḥ śatrujanmanaḥ । vayamapyadhunā yena yātāścintāvidheyatām ।। śrūyate nandagopasya pravṛddhacaritaḥ śiśuḥ ।
daityānāmapi yaḥ śaṅke śaṅkataṅkagururnavaḥ ।। vinyasya caraṇaṃ yena mūrdhni kāliyabhiginaḥ । svarvīkṛtāni śūrāṇāṃ śirāṃsi ca yaśāṃsi ca ।। sāgrajena hatāstena pralambāriṣṭadhenukāḥ ।
avajñāspadamevābhūdyeṣāṃ śakro api saṃgare ।। girirgovardhano nāma saptāhaṃ pāṇinā dhṛtaḥ । smayāya durnimittāya nāśāya ca na kasya saḥ ।। na jānīmaḥ sa kiṃ tāvadbhūtamatyadbhutaṃ kṣitau ।
samudbhūtamadho yena nīyate naḥ parākramaḥ ।। tasmānmanīṣibhirvīrairbhavadbhiścintyatamayam । yaśaḥkusumavallīnāṃ paraśurvyasanodayaḥ ।। uktaṃ ca nāradenaitatpunaretya purā svayam ।
vasudevasutaḥ kṛṣṇo nandagopagṛhe sthitaḥ ।। nandagopasutā cāsau śilāyāmāhatā tvayā । sā gatvā vindhyagahanaṃ pulindaśabarārcitā ।। niśumbhaśumbhau ditijau jaghāna ghanavikramau ।
vihito vasudevena garbhayorvyatyayastayoḥ ।। kṛṣṇaḥ sa te bhayasthānamityuktvā nārado yayau । so ayaṃ bandhuḥ kṛtaghno me vasudevaḥ sthito antike ।। yena naḥ kṣayasaṃdehatulāmāropitaṃ yaśaḥ ।
narakāvartakalilā yasya kilbiṣavipruṣaḥ ।। sa kṛtaghno adhamaḥ kena pātakenopamīyate । ghorahālāhalāpūrṇaḥ kuṭilo ayaṃ mayā svayam ।। dhṛtaḥ sarpo nijagṛhe yenāptaḥ satkule kaliḥ ।
mithyā dhavalakūrco ayaṃ bandhucchadmā jaḍo ripuḥ ।। vasudevaḥ sadā jihmo vadhārhe apyeṣa rakṣitaḥ । sarvābhiśaṅkitā rājñāṃ sunayajñairudāhṛtā ।। ataḥ saṃcintyate ḍimbo na tu me gaṇanāspadam ।
jagadgrasagariṣṭhasya satpratāpahavirbhujaḥ ।। antera na bhavatyeva śiśurgopapataṅgakaḥ । athavā vartate sādhuryadyasmānprati sāgrajaḥ ।। kā kṣatirbhogabhāgī me bandhumadhye bhaviṣyati ।
akrūro madgirā yātu vrajaṃ dānapatiḥ svayam ।। etena tau samāhūtau draṣṭumicchāmi dārakau । nandagopaprabhṛtayaḥ karadā mama śāsanāt ।। dhanurmakhe samāyāntu prastutādhikadāyinaḥ ।
vīrāṇāṃ harṣajananau kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇau ca tau ।। mallābhyāṃ yudhyamānau me raṅge prītatiṃ kariṣyataḥ । iti divyadṛśākrūraḥ śrutvā kaṃsena bhāṣitam ।। yayau yādavaśārdūlaḥ śauridarsanalālasaḥ ।
akrūre govrajaṃ yāte vṛddhāste vṛṣṇipuṃgavāḥ ।। nindayā vusudevasya kruddhāstasthuradhomukhāḥ । tataḥ pitāmahaḥ kaṃsaṃ pitāmaha ivāparaḥ ।। abhyadhādandhako apīmāndurjayaḥ pratibandhakaḥ ।
vandhyāḥ kule api satataṃ mayanye dhanyatarāḥ striyaḥ ।। na kulaghnaḥ suto yāsāṃ kadācidapi jāyate । na jātu vajrajihveṣu tīkṣṇeṣu krūrakāriṣu ।। sudhālayā tiṣṭhati śrīḥ kamalāṅkurakomalā ।
aho nu śocyatāṃ yātāścirādyādavavṛṣṇayaḥ ।। vṛddhāvamānakṛdbālo yeṣāṃ kaṃsa tvamagraṇīḥ । ka evaṃ nāma jaḍadhīranunmattaḥ prabhāṣate ।। rakṣito vasudevena pitrā putraḥ kimapyaho ।
neha putrātpriyataraṃ kiṃcidasti śarīriṇām ।। putra svajanakaṃ pṛccha putrasnehasya gauravam । paralokaparitrāṇāṃ pitrā cedrakṣitaḥ sutaḥ ।। tasyāsya vācyatā keyaṃ yūyaṃ sarve api putriṇaḥ ।
vasudevātmajo vīraḥ kṛṣṇaḥ saṃkarṣaṇānujaḥ ।। bandhubuddhyā praṇayinā saṃdheyaḥ sarvathā tvayā । hitaṃ pathyaṃ ca me mohānna kariṣyasi cedvacaḥ ।। tadaiśvaryaprabhāvo adya saṃpūrṇāvadhireṣa te ।
dṛśyante kṣayasaṃsinyo durnimittaparamparāḥ ।। anyatra kṛṣṇasaṃdhānāttāsu śāntirna te parā । ityandhakavacaḥ śrutvā niḥśvasanbhrakuṭīmukhaḥ ।। nirjagāma tataḥ kaṃsaḥ parāṅmukha iva śriyaḥ ।
nāyamastīti vṛddheṣu bhāṣamāṇeṣu vṛṣṇiṣu ।। ādideśāśu śvetāṅgaṃ kaṃsaḥ keśituraṅgamam । sa kṛṣṇanidhanāyograḥ preritastena dānavaḥ ।। jagāma govrajaṃ ghorasaṃdhyāsṛksaṃplute ahani ।
sa kopādrudhireṇeva pūritākṣaḥ śvasanmuhuḥ ।। uraḥsthalamilatprothaḥkuñcitoruśirodharaḥ । vajrasārasvurāghātanirdāritaśilātalaḥ ।। visphārakesarasaṭākarālaskandhakandharaḥ ।
ghaṭṭayanniva heṣābhiḥ pibanniva diśo daśa ।। nirmāṃsacarvaṇāsvādaprasravatsṛkviśoṇitaḥ । kṛtāntacāmarākāravalitoddhūtavaladhiḥ ।। vivṛttānanavispaṣṭaniryaddantāṃśumaṇḍalaḥ ।
dikṣu mānuṣamāṃsādaḥ kṣipannasthicayāniva ।। so abhidudrāva vegena kṛṣṇamāpāṇḍuracchaviḥ । pavanāpreritasphāraḥ śaranmegha ivācalam ।। samutkṣiptāgracaraṇaṃ keśavaḥ keśinaṃ puraḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā nivāryamāṇo api gaupaiḥ krodhāttamādravat ।। khurābhyāṃ kṛtaśalyābhyāṃ balādvakṣasi tāḍitaḥ । ghoraheṣāravogreṇa tena nākampatācyutaḥ ।। kesarādhūnanoddhūtarajasastasya valgitaiḥ ।
babhūvuḥ kakubhaśchannā dhūmaketuśatairiva ।। tasya prahārato vaktrakuhare vivare hariḥ । dāruṇe dāruṇāyeva dviguṇaṃ bhujamādade ।। keśidantāntarāsaktaḥ sa rarāja harerbhujaḥ ।
phenāvalīparikṣiptaḥ pārijāta ivārṇave ।। keśīśailaśilāstambhadṛḍhe doṣṇi muradviṣaḥ । bhagnadantaściraṃ cakre vaktrāñjanakadarthanāḥ ।। prasravatsavedasalilaḥ srotaḥ proddhāntaśoṇitaḥ ।
vyāvṛttanayanaḥ keśī niḥśvasanniścalo abhavat ।। sphārite doṣṇi kṛṣṇena gaṇḍakūṭataṭāntare । sphuṭasthūlāsthiṭāṅkāraṃ tadvaktramabhavaddvidhā ।। sa dāmodaradurvāradordaṇḍadalitākṛtiḥ ।
papāta rudhirodgāraghorasturagadānavaḥ ।। keśivadhaḥ ।। hate keśini kaṃsasya priye suhṛdi dānave । bhuvaneṣvabhavatko api harṣotsāhamahotsavaḥ ।।
antarhito muniḥ prītyā nāradaḥ kṛṣṇamabravīt । sādhu mādhava niḥśalyaṃ tvāyā kṛtmidaṃ jagat ।। keśinirdāraṇātsvayātaḥ keśavastvaṃ bhaviṣyasi । ityuktvā prayayau harṣānnārado abhimatāṃ diśam ।।
prādurāsīttataḥ śaurernimittanicayaḥ śubhaḥ । bandhunā pitṛtulyena yaḥ śaṃsati samāgamam ।। merupārśvāntaraṃ prāyāddinānte vāsareśvaraḥ । kṛṣṇakeśivadhāścaryakathāṃ vaktumivādarāt ।।
tataḥ pītāṃśukodāradāmodaramanoharam । babhūva sahajaśyāmaṃ saṃdhyāṃśuśabalaṃ nabhaḥ ।। śanaiḥ saṃghaṭṭitāḥ śyāmāstamobhirabhavaddiśaḥ । tārakāṃśusrutakṣīrā gopālairiva dhenavaḥ ।।
vyomābdhipāñcajanyo atha niśānāthaḥ samudyayau । yāminīkāminīkelimaṇḍano maṇidarpaṇaḥ ।। śaśāṅkakarasāreṇa vihāreṇa suraśriyaḥ । tamasaḥ parihāreṇa hāraiṇaiva nabho babhau ।।
netrapremṇi sudhāsīmni sitimni vyomni gāḍhatām । yaśasīvāśrite śaurerniśākarakaracchalāt ।। praharṣayannīlakaṇṭhānrathena ghananādinā । śekharo vṛṣṇivīrāṇāmaktūraḥ pratyapadyata ।।
nandagopasya sadanaṃ sa samāsādya gokule । dadarśa śatapattrākṣaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ keśinisūdanam ।। ayaṃ sa kaiṭabhārātirbhagavānmadhusūdanaḥ । bhuvo bhārāvatārāya jāto yādavanandanaḥ ।।
śrīvatsalakṣaṇo vakṣo bibhrāṇaḥ kustubhocitam । niḥspandāliṅgane yogyaṃ kamalākucakumbhayoḥ ।। meghaśyāmena vapuṣā nayanāmṛtavarṣiṇā । dhatte saudāminīdāmaramyaṃ pītāṃśukadvayam ।।
anena nṛtyati manaḥsphāraṃ prasarato dṛśau । etadāliṅganāyeva bhujau me paridhāvataḥ ।। ehi mādhava kṛṣṇeti vyāharanprītinirbharaḥ । pūjito nandagopena kṛṣṇena ca viveśa saḥ ।।
prāptapūjāsanaḥ so atha sasaṃkarṣaṇamacyutam । uvāca puṇḍarīkākṣamāpibanniva cakṣuṣā ।। iyaṃ te dhīragambhīrā harṣapīyūṣavarṣiṇī । prayāti nā puṇyavatāṃ mūrtirlocanagocaram ।।
mohāttvadbhaktivimukhastvāṃ dṛṣṭvā prātarāgatam । vāñchitaḥ kṛtakṛtyaśca bhavitā mathureśvaraḥ ।। draṣṭumicchati kaṃsastvāṃ prātargantāsi tatpurīm । tvadvapuḥ pūrṇapūṇyena dhanyāḥ paśyantu yādavāḥ ।।
tatra kaṃsasya saṃbhāradhanādhāmni dhanurmahīm । upatiṣṭhantu dhaninaḥ sarve gopāḥ karapradāḥ ।। etāvadeva pracuraṃ mamāgamanakāraṇam । idaṃ tu bāndhavasnohādyatkiṃcidabhidhīyate ।।
vṛddhaḥ sa sukṛtī tatra putra putravatāṃ varaḥ । vilokya vasudevastvāṃ phalaṃ prāpnotu janmanaḥ ।। tvatkṛte satataṃ yasya kaṃsavākyaśarāḥ svarāḥ । tvāmavāpnotu māhātmyaṃ rohaṇādrivasuṃdharā ।।
api kaṃsabhayātputrairasaṃpītapayodharā । kṛṣṇeti nāmnā satataṃ sīdati prasnustanī ।। gūḍhacintāviniḥśvāsadhūsarādharapallavā । dūrīkṛtasutasnehavaiklavyāptavipallavām ।।
rahitāmiva rāmeṇa kausalyāṃ kulamaulinā । darśanāmṛtavarṣeṇa nirvāpaya sametya tām ।। aho tṛṣṇeva sahajācchāyeva sahacāriṇī । vāsanevāparikṣīṇā sarvathā bhavitavyatā ।।
viśvoddharaṇadakṣasya jagadrakṣāśikhāmaṇeḥ । tavāpi janma savudhācintayā yatpraśuṣyati ।। kaṃsanirbhartsanānamrastvāṃ prāpya janakaścirāt । vahatu trijagatpūjya putra mānonnataṃ śiraḥ ।।
akrūrasaṃdeśaḥ ।। ityukte dānapatinā snehavātsalyaśālinā । sarvaṃ karomīti vadannirvikārānano abhavat ।। gantuṃ kṛtābhyupagame kṛṣṇe gopamṛgīdṛśām ।
cintāsaṃtaptaniḥśvāsairivendurmlānatāṃ yayau ।। dugdhā niśīthatsena jyotsnā pūrapayasvinī । prātardyaiḥ sāṃdhyarāgeṇa kapilā gaurivābabhau ।। athodayācalaśiroratnatāmāgate ravau ।
udyatpradīptacakrasya śobhāṃ lebhe harernabhaḥ ।। karopanayasaṃpūrṇaiḥ śakaṭairatha bhūribhiḥ । gantumabhyudyayurgopapatayaḥ kaṃsaśāsanāt ।। rathaiḥ prayayurakrūrarauhiṇeyācyutādayaḥ ।
arghyamānā ivottālagopālīlocanotpalaiḥ ।। avāpya yamunātīramakrūraḥ kṛṣṇamabravīt । asminhrade bhogivṛte kṛṣṇa śeṣaṃ phaṇīśvaram ।। nimajjya bhagavanmantraiḥ pūjayāmyamṛtāśanaḥ ।
ityuktvā kṛṣṇanikṣiptarathastatra mamajja saḥ ।। nimagnaḥ so atha pātālaṃ divyakhastikalāñchanam । śeṣaṃ sahasramūrdhānaṃ dadarśāsīnamīśvaram ।। hemābjamālābharaṇaṃ sarvaratnābhūṣitam ।
sahasraśikharasphāratuṣāragirivibhramam ।। āsevyamānaṃ praṇatairnikhilaiḥ kulabhogibhiḥ । nīlāmbaraṃ nālaketuṃ halinaṃ musalāyudham ।। utsaṅge tasya kṛṣṇaṃ ca śītāṃśoriva lāñchanam ।
niṣaṇṇaṃ vismito apaśyañjapanbrahya sanātanam ।। rauhiṇeyācyutau matvā tāvevonmajjaya satvaraḥ । dṛṣṭvā rathasthau tāveva mamajja punarādarāt ।। punastathaiva tau dṛṣṭvā samunmajjyāstasaṃśayaḥ ।
tvameva sarvamityūce pṛṣṭaḥ kṛṣṇena sasmitam ।। hradadarśanam ।। dinānte prāpya mathurāmakrūraḥ svagṛhāntare । svairaṃ jagāda govindaṃ kaṃsadurnayaśaṅkitaḥ ।।
vasudevagṛhaṃ tāta na gantavyaṃ tvayādhunā । na ca rāmeṇa nitarāṃ kaṃsādāpnoti bhartsanām ।। ityukte dānapatinā kṛṣṇaḥ sasmitamabravīt । satyaṃ tatra na gacchāvaḥ paśyāvaḥ kautukātpurīm ।।
ityābhāṣya madodārau rāmakṛṣṇau viceratuḥ । avatīrṇau vimānābhyāṃ vīrau vidyādharāviva ।। tau rājarajakaṃ prāpya yayācāte mahābhujau । vāsāṃsi rucirābhāṃsi na dadāvadhamaśca saḥ ।।
krodhadarpāvaliptaṃ taṃ rajakaṃ krūravādinam । hatvā jahāra vāsāṃsi baladevānujo balāt ।। svayaṃ mālyopanayanaṃ mālākārī valīmatī । śrīpateḥ śrīpradaṃ prādātprītyā praṇayavādinī ।।
krameṇa līlayā kṛṣṇaḥ suspaṣṭāvayavāṃ kṣaṇāt । tāṃ cakre yauvanodyānapūrṇalāvaṇyavallarīm ।। tataḥ prāpyāyudhāgāraṃ pūjitaṃ daityadānavaiḥ । utsāhārhaṃ śilāstambhasāraṃ dadṛśaturdhanuḥ ।।
dāmodarastadādāya dorbhyāmākṛṣya durdharam । babhañja sphāriṭāṅkāraṃ mṛṇālīnālalīlayā ।। tena śabdena pavanaskandhasaṃghaṭṭakāriṇā । rarāsa dāriteva dyauścakampe ca vasuṃdharā ।।
āyudhāgāriko apyāśu dhanurbhaṅgaṃ nyavedayat । kaṃsāyākampitamanāścakre darpātsa cāśrutam ।। bhagnaṃ kenāpi mallena śrutvā cāpaṃ nareśvaraḥ । dideśa sarvamallānāṃ yuddhaprekṣāmahotsavam ।।
svairaṃ tataḥ samāhūya mallau cāṇūramauṣṭikau । cirasaṃdhāritau cakre vadhasajjau muradviṣaḥ ।। gajaśālādhipaṃ kaṃsaḥ saṃgrāmasacivaṃ rahaḥ । ūce mohe api saṃprāptasukṛtaḥ śauricintayā ।।
prātardhanurmahīraṅgamāgantā vasudevajaḥ । sāgrajo darpasaṃmatto mattaḥ sa vadharmahati ।। raṅgadvāri tvayā cāsau nirghātī vyālakuñjaraḥ । kāryaḥ kuvalayāpīḍaḥ krodhāttannidhanodyataḥ ।।
hataputraṃ karomyeva vasudevaṃ niraṃśakam । bandhucchadmapraticchannānnṛpāṃścāndhakayādavān ।। purā mamārtavavatī jananī navakautukāt । priyāsanādikaṭake cacāra kusumojjvale ।।
tatra vālānilollāsavellitāśokapallave । sphūrjadbakulakiñjalkapiñjarīkṛtaṣaṭpade ।। puñjīkṛtalatākuñjamañjuguñjadvihaṅgame । ratirāgarasodārasmarasaṃjīvane vane ।।
dadarśa tāṃ saurapatirdrumilo dānaveśvaraḥ । latāṃ stanastabakinīṃ kāmakalpataroriva ।। mayo yogīśvaraḥ so atha rūpaṃ kṛtvā piturmama । bheje tāṃ manmathāviṣṭaḥ satīṃ premanirargalām ।।
tataḥ sā vṛttakartavyā śaṅkitā vīkṣya dānavam । pāpaṃ śaśāpa kupitā dūṣitāsmīti duḥkhitā ।। vadhaṃ prāpsyasi durvṛtta madbhartṛkulajādyudhi । ayaṃ ca mama garbhe adya tvayā yastanayo dhṛtaḥ ।।
ityuktvā śanakaiḥ prāyāditi māmāha nāradaḥ । tasmādahaṃ daityapaterdrumilasyātmajo mataḥ ।। suto ahaṃ nograsenasya yādavā me na bāndhavāḥ । te hir ve mamocchedyāḥ kṛṣṇotsāhapratīkṣiṇaḥ ।।
saṃdiśyeti mahāmātyaṃ saṃkḷptamape ahani । saṃgataprekṣakaṃ raṅgaṃ viveśa viṣadāṃśukaḥ ।। valabhītuṅgaratnāṃśuṃtaraṅgāliṅgitāmbare । saṃgatānantasāmantasamāgamanirantera ।।
bhojavṛṣṇyandhakaistatra vīraiḥ parivṛto babhau । hemasiṃhāsanāsīnaḥ pīnāṃsaḥ kaṃsabhūpatiḥ ।। molikuṇḍalakeyūraratnāṃśuśabaladyutiḥ । kāntābhiścāmaraprāntakampitoṣṇīṣapallavaḥ ।।
nānādeśāgatāstasya śāsanādatha durmadāḥ । samutpeturmahāmallā bhujāsphālanaśālinaḥ ।। saṃkarṣaṇācyutau vīrau nīlapītāmbarau tataḥ । sitāsitaghanacchāyau raṅgadvāramavāpatuḥ ।।
gātraiḥ kuvālayāpīḍākāriṇaṃ tatra gauravāt । punaḥ kuvalayīpīḍaṃ sajjaṃ dadṛśaturgajam ।। bhogīndrābhogasaṃbhrāntikaraṃ kajjalamecakam । kālakūṭacchaṭāṭopanirdagdhamiva mandiram ।।
ādhoraṇena durvāradarpapreritamojasā । taṃ yuddhasaṃmukhaṃ dṛṣṭvā dantāghātakṣatācalam ।। punaḥ kuṇḍalitoddaṇḍaghoraśuṇḍālamaṇḍalam । trailokyakavalīkāravikarālamivāntakam ।।
maṇḍalāni carankṛṣṇaḥ savyadakṣiṇapārśavayoḥ । svasahastālambanaṃ kurvanvegena tamamohayat ।। āghatākulitaḥ so atha vivalatparvatākṛtiḥ । pravṛddaśramaśūtkāraśīkarāpuritāmbaraḥ ।।
dantābhighāvaiphalyājjānubhyāmavaniṃ gataḥ । sahasotthāya govindaṃ laghucitraparākramam ।। carantaṃ karadantāgracaraṇābhyantare api saḥ । na prāpa kṛtayatno api bhāgyahīna ivopsitam ।।
harirdadatsukaṭakaṃ datvāsya caraṇaṃ mukhe । saṃgrāmatoraṇastambhaṃ pāṇibhyāṃ dantamagrahīt ।। kaṃsaśrīnalinīmūlamivotpāṭya dvipānanāt । tīkṣṇāgraṃ dantamusalaṃ tenaiva nijaghāna tam ।।
nijadantaprahāreṇa raktodgārī vidāritaḥ । hastī srutaśakṛnmūtraścacālācalasaṃnibhaḥ ।। ākṛṣṭapṛccho rāmeṇa hatārohaḥ sa śauriṇā । dantanirdāritakaṭaḥ papāta vikaṭaḥ kṣitau ।।
kuvalayāpīḍavadhaḥ ।। hatvā kuvalayāpīḍaṃ jagatpīḍākṣayodyataḥ । raṅgaṃ viveśa govindaḥ kāminīkautukapradaḥ ।। gajaraktacchaṭāṅkasya līlāvalgitavāsasaḥ ।
rūpaṃ tasya babhau raṅge meghasyeva savidyutaḥ ।। dantidantaḥ sa śuśubhe kare kāliyavidviṣaḥ । aṣṭamīśītakiraṇaḥ prabhādīpta ivāmbare ।। tataḥ kaṃsājñayā mallo balavānandhradeśajaḥ ।
cāṇūraḥ parvatākārastatra kṛṣṇamayodhayat ।। tayorjānubhujābandhaiḥ preraṇākarṣaṇāccanaiḥ । pīḍanāsphālanāghātaiḥ pṛthivī samakampataḥ ।। putraḥ pīyūṣavarṣīti harṣabāṣpārdracakṣuṣā ।
sakampaṃ vasudevena mātrā ca jayasaṃśraye ।। śrīkānta ityapsarobhirdaityacchedīti khecaraiḥ । bandhurityādarādgopaiḥ pravīra iti yādavaiḥ ।। mallo varāko asya kiyāniti saṃkarṣaṇena ca ।
tarasvī vīkṣyamāṇo asau mallānāṃ vismayaṃ vyadhāt ।। tataḥ kopākulaḥ kaṃsaḥ kṛṣṇotsāhavivardhanam । bhujamudyamya vipulaṃ tūryasvanamavārayat ।। utsāhavādye kaṃsena kṛṣṇadveṣānnivārite ।
devadundubhayo nedustāratūryaravairdivi ।। mallaṃ kṛṣṇa jahītyāśu saptarṣibhirudīrite । papātoddyotitākāśaḥ kaṃsasya mukuṭānmaṇiḥ ।। atha daityāvatārasya mallasyādbhutavikramaḥ ।
muṣṭiprahāreṇa śiraścakāra dalitendriyam ।। tasya sphuṭallalāṭasya locane dīpasaṃnibhe । nipetatuḥ kṣititale tārāyugalaśobhane ।। tato nipatitāśeṣamalle malle nipātite ।
abhūtkṣubdhābdhigambhīro raṅgakṣobhabhavaḥ svanaḥ ।। saṃkarṣaṇo api jagrāha mallaṃ maṇḍalakovidaḥ । mauṣṭikaṃ nāma vikaṭaṃ tāmarākhyaṃ ca keśavaḥ ।। janmāvartaṃ paribhrāmya tomalaṃ kāliyāntakaḥ ।
papāta bhuvi niṣpiṣya mauṣṭikaṃ ca halāyudhaḥ ।। hateṣu teṣu malleṣu śalyeṣu tridivaukasām । vismite yādavakule lulite raṅgamaṇḍale ।। sudhāsārairivāsikte vasudeva vadhūsakhe ।
cukopa bhrukuṭībhīṣmaḥ kaṃsaḥ kampitamānasaḥ ।। sāvegaistasya niḥśvāsairiva pralayatāṃ gate । kopāgnau sarvabhūtānāṃ ghoramāvirabhūdbhayam ।। tasya gaṇḍataṭe spaṣṭaṃ khedabindulatā babhau ।
laḍatkuṇḍalasakteva bimbitā mauktikāvalī ।। bhrūbhaṅgena nivāryaiva raṅgakolāhalasvanam । vetriprotsāritajano jagāda jagatīpatiḥ ।। iyaṃ saralatā jātu jātā sārakṣayāya naḥ ।
kathaṃ prathitasārāṇāṃ madhye gopaḥ pradṛśyate ।। jambukena hatāḥ siṃhā yadi tatkriyate atra kim । niṣkāsyantāmito gopā nandagopaśca badhyatām ।। bāndhavavyasanaścāyaṃ vasudevaḥ kulādhamaḥ ।
nidhīyatāṃ kṣayamukhe svapakṣaiḥ saha yādavaiḥ ।। ugrasenasutasyeti śāsanādugravikramaḥ । samudyayuryathādiṣṭaṃ kartuṃ tanmativartinaḥ ।। tatastrāsākulānvīkṣya gopāngoptā divaukasām ।
devīṃ ca devakīṃ putrasnehavaiklavyaviklavām ।। hemasaṃhāsanopāntamabhipatya trivikramaḥ । jagrāha lolamālyeṣu kaṃsaṃ keśeṣu keśavaḥ ।। agre digbhiriva nyastamavatīrṇamivāmbarāt ।
sahasā patitaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ kaṃsaḥ kālamamanyata ।। kṛṣṇenākṛṣyamāṇeṣu mālyavatsu mahīpateḥ । keśeṣu vilalāpeva rājaśrīrbhaṅgaśiñjitaiḥ ।। nāmyamānānanaḥ kaṃsaḥ śauriṇā bhārapīḍitām ।
vadhe nimittatāṃ yātāmāluloke mahīmiva ।। vaktrāmbararavirlakṣmīvihāramaṇiparvataḥ । maulistasyāpatatsrastamuktāsrukaṇasaṃtatiḥ ।। tamākṛṣya sphuṭanmuktāhārakeyūrakuṇḍalam ।
sphāraiśvaryādiva mahāhemasiṃhāsanāccyutam ।। raktakuṭṭimanirghṛṣṭagātraprasrutaśoṇitam । utsasarja viśīrṇāsuṃ kaṃsaṃ dūre harirvyasum । ajitaṃ sarvabhūpālairabhagnaṃ vajrisaṃgare ।।
taṃ vīkṣya sarvabhūtānāmavaśyaṃ śauriṇā hatam । raṅge samudabhūddhoraḥ kṣaṇaṃ halahalāravaḥ ।। kaṃsavadhaḥ ।। tasminvīrakulottaṃse hate kaṃse murāriṇā ।
kaṃsānujaṃ sunāmānaṃ nijaghāna halāyudhaḥ ।। devo atha devakīsūnurvavande devavanditaḥ । vasudevasya pādābjo mātuścānandanirbharaḥ ।। sahasā hatamākarṇya kaṃsaṃ kaṃsavadhūjanaḥ ।
akāṇḍavajrapātena nirdārita ivāyayau ।। taṃ pāṃsurūṣitaṃ bhūmau siṃhāhatamiva dvipam । saṃvīkṣyonmathitaṃ vegādvāteneva mahādrumam ।। krośantyastārakaruṇaṃ chinnahāravibūṣaṇāḥ ।
